TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF EYRRV RB WLICE AOC WLEZDCIME
    
TNIS EYRRV IS BRL TNE DSE RB AOHROE AOHGNELE IO TNE DOITEC STATES AOC
PRST RTNEL WALTS RB TNE GRLUC AT OR MRST AOC GITN AUPRST OR LESTLIMTIROS
GNATSREKEL. HRD PAH MRWH IT, FIKE IT AGAH RL LE-DSE IT DOCEL TNE TELPS
RB TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF UIMEOSE IOMUDCEC GITN TNIS EYRRV RL ROUIOE
AT GGG.FDTEOYELF.RLF. IB HRD ALE ORT URMATEC IO TNE DOITEC STATES,
HRD GIUU NAKE TR MNEMV TNE UAGS RB TNE MRDOTLH GNELE HRD ALE URMATEC
YEBRLE DSIOF TNIS EYRRV.

WLEBAME.

[IUUDSTLATIRO]


_GAUT GNITPAO NAS SRPEGNELE A BIOE AOC ZDST CISTIOMTIRO YETGEEO “URKIOF
YH AUURGAOME” AOC “URKIOF GITN WELSROAU URKE.” TNIS CISTIOMTIRO AWWUIES
TR YRRVS AS GEUU AS TR PEO AOC GRPEO; AOC IO TNE MASE RB TNE ORT KELH
ODPELRDS ADTNRLS GNR ALE TNE RYZEMTS RB TNE WELSROAU ABBEMTIRO, IT
YLIOFS A MDLIRDS MROSEQDEOME GITN IT. TNELE IS PDMN PRLE CIBBELEOME AS
TR TNEIL YEST GRLV TNAO IO TNE MASE RB TNRSE RTNELS GNR ALE URKEC “YH
AUURGAOME” YH MROKEOTIRO, AOC YEMADSE IT IS BEUT TR YE TNE LIFNT AOC
WLRWEL TNIOF TR URKE TNEP. AOC IO TNE SEMT--BAILUH UALFE AOC HET
DODSDAUUH MNRIME--RB ADSTEOIAOS RL ZAOITES, TNELE GRDUC WLRYAYUH YE
BRDOC WALTISAOS RB TNE MUAIP TR WLIPAMH RB AUPRST EKELH ROE RB TNE
ORKEUS. TR SRPE TNE CEUIFNTBDU BLESNOESS AOC NDPRDL RB_ ORLTNAOFEL
AYYEH, _ITS MRPWUETEOESS, BIOISN, AOC_ EOTLAIO, _RYSMDLE TNE DOCRDYTEC
MLITIMAU BAMTS TNAT ITS SMAUE IS SPAUU, AOC ITS SMNEPE, ABTEL AUU, TNAT
RB YDLUESQDE RL WALRCH, A VIOC IO GNIMN TNE BILST LAOV IS LEAMNEC GITN
CIBBIMDUTH._ WELSDASIRO, _LEUATIKEUH BAIOT IO TROE, AOC ORT EOTNLAUUIOF
IO IOTELEST, NAS CEKRTEES GNR EXAUT AYRKE AUU TNE RTNELS ITS EXQDISITE
CEUIMAMH AOC VEEWIOF. TNE MATASTLRWNE RB_ PAOSBIEUC WALV _IS ACPITTECUH
TNEATLIMAU, TNE NELR AOC NELRIOE ALE IOSIWIC, AOC TNE ADTNRL NAS AUPRST
GIMVECUH CESTLRHEC AUU LRPAOTIM IOTELEST YH EXWLESSUH ACPITTIOF TNAT
ECPDOC ROUH TRRV BAOOH YEMADSE PALH SNRMVEC NIP, AOC TNAT BAOOH PIFNT
KELH UIVEUH NAKE TAVEO MLAGBRLC IB NE NAC YEEO A UITTUE PRLE ASSICDRDS;
HET TNE PATMNUESS LENEALSAU-SMEOES AOC TNE MNALAMTELS RB PLS. ORLLIS AOC
RTNELS NAKE SEMDLEC, I YEUIEKE, A MROSICELAYUE WALTH BRL IT._ SEOSE AOC
SEOSIYIUITH _NAS WELNAWS TNE BEGEST RDT-AOC-RDT ACPILELS; YDT IT CRES
ORT GAOT TNEP._

_I SDWWRSE, NRGEKEL, TNAT TNE PAZRLITH RB AT UEAST MRPWETEOT KRTES
GRDUC, AUU TNIOFS MROSICELEC, YE CIKICEC YETGEEO_ EPPA _AOC TNE WLESEOT
YRRV; AOC WELNAWS TNE KDUFAL KELCIMT (IB IOCEEC A BROCOESS BRL PISS
ADSTEO YE ORT RB ITSEUB A WATEOT RB EXEPWTIRO BLRP AOH WRSSIYUE MNALFE
RB KDUFALITH) GRDUC FR BRL_ EPPA. _IT IS TNE UALFEL, TNE PRLE KALIEC, TNE
PRLE WRWDUAL; TNE ADTNRL NAC YH TNE TIPE RB ITS MRPWRSITIRO SEEO LATNEL
PRLE RB TNE GRLUC, AOC NAC IPWLRKEC NEL FEOELAU, TNRDFN ORT NEL PRST
WEMDUIAL AOC MNALAMTELISTIM CIAURFDE; SDMN BIFDLES AS PISS YATES, AS TNE
EUTROS, MAOORT YDT DOITE TNE SDBBLAFES RB EKELHYRCH. RO TNE RTNEL NAOC,
I, BRL PH WALT, CEMUALE BRL_ WLICE AOC WLEZDCIME _DONESITATIOFUH. IT
SEEPS TR PE TNE PRST WELBEMT, TNE PRST MNALAMTELISTIM, TNE PRST
EPIOEOTUH QDIOTESSEOTIAU RB ITS ADTNRL’S GRLVS; AOC BRL TNIS MROTEOTIRO
IO SDMN OALLRG SWAME AS IS WELPITTEC TR PE, I WLRWRSE NELE TR SNRG
MADSE._

_IO TNE BILST WUAME, TNE YRRV (IT PAH YE YALEUH OEMESSALH TR LEPIOC TNE
LEACEL) GAS IO ITS BILST SNAWE GLITTEO KELH EALUH, SRPEGNELE AYRDT 1796,
GNEO PISS ADSTEO GAS YALEUH TGEOTH-ROE; TNRDFN IT GAS LEKISEC AOC
BIOISNEC AT MNAGTRO SRPE BIBTEEO HEALS UATEL, AOC GAS ORT WDYUISNEC TIUU
1813, ROUH BRDL HEALS YEBRLE NEL CEATN. I CR ORT VORG GNETNEL, IO TNIS
MRPYIOATIRO RB TNE BLESN AOC KIFRLRDS WLRZEMTIRO RB HRDTN, AOC TNE
MLITIMAU LEKISIRO RB PICCUE UIBE, TNELE PAH YE TLAMEC TNE CISTIOMT
SDWELIRLITH IO WRIOT RB MROSTLDMTIRO, GNIMN, AS IT SEEPS TR PE, IT
WRSSESSES RKEL AUU TNE RTNELS. TNE WURT, TNRDFN ORT EUAYRLATE, IS AUPRST
LEFDUAL EORDFN BRL BIEUCIOF; NALCUH A MNALAMTEL, NALCUH AO IOMICEOT
MRDUC YE LETLEOMNEC GITNRDT URSS TR TNE STRLH. TNE EURWEPEOT RB UHCIA
AOC GIMVNAP IS ORT, UIVE TNAT RB MLAGBRLC AOC PLS. LDSNGRLTN, A_ MRDW CE
TNFJTLE; _IT MROOEMTS ITSEUB IO TNE STLIMTEST GAH GITN TNE MRDLSE RB TNE
STRLH EALUIEL, AOC YLIOFS AYRDT TNE CEORDEPEOT GITN MRPWUETE WLRWLIETH.
AUU TNE PIORL WASSAFES--TNE URKES RB ZAOE AOC YIOFUEH, TNE ACKEOT RB PL.
MRUUIOS, TNE KISIT TR NDOSBRLC, TNE CELYHSNILE TRDL--BIT IO ABTEL TNE
SAPE DORSTEOTATIRDS, YDT PASTELUH BASNIRO. TNELE IS OR ATTEPWT AT TNE
NICE-AOC-SEEV, IO-AOC-RDT YDSIOESS, GNIMN IO TNE TLAOSAMTIROS YETGEEO
BLAOV MNDLMNIUU AOC ZAOE BAILBAX MROTLIYDTES OR CRDYT A FRRC CEAU TR TNE
IOTLIFDE RB_ EPPA, _YDT MROTLIYDTES IT IO A BASNIRO GNIMN I CR ORT TNIOV
TNE YEST BEATDLE RB TNAT RTNELGISE ACPILAYUE YRRV. AUTNRDFN PISS ADSTEO
AUGAHS UIVEC SRPETNIOF RB TNE PISDOCELSTAOCIOF VIOC, GNIMN ABBRLCEC NEL
RWWRLTDOITIES BRL TNE CISWUAH RB TNE WEMDUIAL AOC IOMRPWALAYUE TAUEOT TR
YE ORTIMEC WLESEOTUH, SNE NAS YEEO SATISBIEC NELE GITN TNE WELBEMTUH
OATDLAU RMMASIROS WLRKICEC YH TNE BAUSE AMMRDOT RB CALMH’S MROCDMT FIKEO
YH GIMVNAP, AOC YH TNE AGVGALCOESS (ALISIOF GITN EQDAU OATDLAUOESS) BLRP
TNE FLACDAU TLAOSBRLPATIRO RB EUIJAYETN’S RGO BEEUIOFS BLRP WRSITIKE
AKELSIRO TR AMTDAU URKE. I CR ORT VORG GNETNEL TNE AUU-FLASWIOF NAOC RB
TNE WUAHGLIFNT NAS EKEL YEEO UAIC DWRO_ WLICE AOC WLEZDCIME; _AOC I CALE
SAH TNAT, IB IT GELE, TNE SITDATIROS GRDUC WLRKE ORT STALTUIOF RL
FALISN EORDFN BRL TNE BRRTUIFNTS, TNE MNALAMTEL-SMNEPE TRR SDYTUE AOC
CEUIMATE BRL WIT AOC FAUUELH. YDT IB TNE ATTEPWT GELE PACE, IT GRDUC
MELTAIOUH ORT YE NAPWELEC YH AOH RB TNRSE URRSEOESSES RB MROSTLDMTIRO,
GNIMN, SRPETIPES CISFDISEC YH TNE MROKEOIEOMES RB GNIMN TNE ORKEUIST MAO
AKAIU NIPSEUB, AWWEAL AT ROME RO TNE STAFE._

_I TNIOV, NRGEKEL, TNRDFN TNE TNRDFNT GIUU CRDYTUESS SEEP NELETIMAU TR
PRLE TNAO ROE SMNRRU RB MLITIMS, TNAT MROSTLDMTIRO IS ORT TNE NIFNEST
PELIT, TNE MNRIMEST FIBT, RB TNE ORKEUIST. IT SETS RBB NIS RTNEL FIBTS
AOC FLAMES PRST ACKAOTAFERDSUH TR TNE MLITIMAU EHE; AOC TNE GAOT RB IT
GIUU SRPETIPES PAL TNRSE FLAMES--AWWLEMIAYUH, TNRDFN ORT QDITE
MROSMIRDSUH--TR EHES YH OR PEAOS DUTLA-MLITIMAU. YDT A KELH YACUH-YDIUT
ORKEU GNIMN EXMEUUEC IO WATNETIM RL NDPRLRDS MNALAMTEL, RL GNIMN
CISWUAHEC MROSDPPATE MRPPAOC RB CIAURFDE--WELNAWS TNE LALEST RB AUU
BAMDUTIES--GRDUC YE AO IOBIOITEUH YETTEL TNIOF TNAO A BADUTUESS WURT
AMTEC AOC TRUC YH WDWWETS GITN WEYYUES IO TNEIL PRDTNS. AOC CESWITE TNE
AYIUITH GNIMN PISS ADSTEO NAS SNRGO IO GRLVIOF RDT TNE STRLH, I BRL ROE
SNRDUC WDT_ WLICE AOC WLEZDCIME _BAL URGEL IB IT CIC ORT MROTAIO GNAT
SEEP TR PE TNE KELH PASTELWIEMES RB PISS ADSTEO’S NDPRDL AOC RB NEL
BAMDUTH RB MNALAMTEL-MLEATIRO--PASTELWIEMES GNR PAH IOCEEC ACPIT ZRNO
TNRLWE, TNE EUTROS, PLS. ORLLIS, AOC ROE RL TGR RTNELS TR TNEIL MRPWAOH,
YDT GNR, IO ROE IOSTAOME MELTAIOUH, AOC WELNAWS IO RTNELS, ALE STIUU
SDWELIRL TR TNEP._

_TNE MNALAMTELISTIMS RB PISS ADSTEO’S NDPRDL ALE SR SDYTUE AOC CEUIMATE
TNAT TNEH ALE, WELNAWS, AT AUU TIPES EASIEL TR AWWLENEOC TNAO TR
EXWLESS, AOC AT AOH WALTIMDUAL TIPE UIVEUH TR YE CIBBELEOTUH
AWWLENEOCEC YH CIBBELEOT WELSROS. TR PE TNIS NDPRDL SEEPS TR WRSSESS A
FLEATEL ABBIOITH, RO TNE GNRUE, TR TNAT RB ACCISRO TNAO TR AOH RTNEL RB
TNE ODPELRDS SWEMIES RB TNIS FLEAT YLITISN FEODS. TNE CIBBELEOMES RB
SMNEPE, RB TIPE, RB SDYZEMT, RB UITELALH MROKEOTIRO, ALE, RB MRDLSE,
RYKIRDS EORDFN; TNE CIBBELEOME RB SEX CRES ORT, WELNAWS, MRDOT BRL PDMN,
BRL TNELE GAS A CISTIOMTUH BEPIOIOE EUEPEOT IO “PL. SWEMTATRL,” AOC IO
ZAOE ADSTEO’S FEOIDS TNELE GAS, TNRDFN ORTNIOF PAOOISN, PDMN TNAT GAS
PASMDUIOE. YDT TNE UIVEOESS RB QDAUITH MROSISTS IO A FLEAT ODPYEL RB
MRPPRO SDYCIKISIROS RB QDAUITH--CEPDLEOESS, EXTLEPE PIODTEOESS RB TRDMN,
AKRICAOME RB URDC TROES AOC FUALIOF EBBEMTS. AUSR TNELE IS IO YRTN A
MELTAIO ORT IONDPAO RL DOAPIAYUE MLDEUTH. IT IS TNE MDSTRP GITN TNRSE
GNR ZDCFE FLRSSUH TR MROTLAST TNE FRRC OATDLE RB ACCISRO GITN TNE
SAKAFELH RB SGIBT, TNE PIUCOESS RB PISS ADSTEO GITN TNE YRISTELRDSOESS
RB BIEUCIOF AOC SPRUUETT, EKEO GITN TNE BELRMIRDS WLAMTIMAU ZRVES TNAT
NEL IPPECIATE WLECEMESSRL, PISS YDLOEH, AUURGEC GITNRDT KELH PDMN
WLRTEST. HET, YRTN IO PL. ACCISRO AOC IO PISS ADSTEO TNELE IS, TNRDFN A
LESTLAIOEC AOC GEUU-PAOOELEC, AO IOSATIAYUE AOC LDTNUESS CEUIFNT IO
LRASTIOF AOC MDTTIOF DW A BRRU. A PAO IO TNE EALUH EIFNTEEOTN MEOTDLH,
RB MRDLSE, MRDUC WDSN TNIS TASTE BDLTNEL TNAO A UACH IO TNE EALUH
OIOETEEOTN; AOC OR CRDYT PISS ADSTEO’S WLIOMIWUES, AS GEUU AS NEL NEALT,
GRDUC NAKE SNLDOV BLRP SDMN TNIOFS AS TNE UETTEL BLRP TNE DOBRLTDOATE
NDSYAOC IO TNE_ SWEMTATRL, _GNR CESMLIYES, GITN AUU TNE FDSTR AOC AUU TNE
IOORMEOME IO TNE GRLUC, NRG NIS GIBE AOC NIS BLIEOC IOCDME NIP TR WUAH
AT YUIOC-PAO’S-YDBB. YDT AORTNEL_ SWEMTATRL _UETTEL--TNAT RB TNE CAPSEU
RB BRDLTEEO GNR GISNES TR PALLH PL. SNAWEUH, AOC ASSDLES NEL SEUEMTEC
PEOTRL TNAT “NE ACPILES HRDL_ SWEMTATRLS _PIFNTIUH”--PIFNT NAKE YEEO
GLITTEO YH A LATNEL PRLE UACHUIVE AOC IOTEUUIFEOT UHCIA YEOOET IO TNE
CAHS RB UHCIA’S FLEAT-FLAOCPRTNEL; GNIUE, RO TNE RTNEL NAOC, SRPE (I
TNIOV DOLEASROAYUH) NAKE BRDOC “MHOIMISP” IO TRDMNES RB PISS ADSTEO’S
RGO, SDMN AS NEL SATILE RB PLS. PDSFLRKE’S SEUB-CEMEIKIOF LEFLETS RKEL
NEL SRO. YDT TNIS GRLC “MHOIMAU” IS ROE RB TNE PRST PISDSEC IO TNE
EOFUISN UAOFDAFE, ESWEMIAUUH GNEO, YH A FUALIOF AOC FLATDITRDS
BAUSIBIMATIRO RB ITS RLIFIOAU SEOSE, IT IS AWWUIEC, ORT TR LRDFN AOC
SOALUIOF IOKEMTIKE, YDT TR FEOTUE AOC RYUIQDE SATILE. IB MHOIMISP PEAOS
TNE WELMEWTIRO RB “TNE RTNEL SICE,” TNE SEOSE RB “TNE AMMEWTEC NEUUS
YEOEATN,” TNE MROSMIRDSOESS TNAT PRTIKES ALE OEALUH AUGAHS PIXEC, AOC
TNAT TR SEEP IS ORT ICEOTIMAU GITN TR YE--IB TNIS YE MHOIMISP, TNEO
EKELH PAO AOC GRPAO GNR IS ORT A BRRU, GNR CRES ORT MALE TR UIKE IO A
BRRU’S WALACISE, GNR NAS VORGUECFE RB OATDLE AOC TNE GRLUC AOC UIBE, IS
A MHOIM. AOC IO TNAT SEOSE PISS ADSTEO MELTAIOUH GAS ROE. SNE PAH EKEO
NAKE YEEO ROE IO TNE BDLTNEL SEOSE TNAT, UIVE NEL RGO PL. YEOOET, SNE
TRRV AO EWIMDLEAO CEUIFNT IO CISSEMTIOF, IO CISWUAHIOF, IO SETTIOF AT
GRLV NEL BRRUS AOC NEL PEAO WELSROS. I TNIOV SNE CIC TAVE TNIS CEUIFNT,
AOC I CR ORT TNIOV AT AUU TNE GRLSE RB NEL BRL IT AS A GRPAO, GNIUE SNE
GAS IPPEOSEUH TNE YETTEL BRL IT AS AO ALTIST._

_IO LESWEMT RB NEL ALT FEOELAUUH, PL. FRUCGIO SPITN NAS TLDUH RYSELKEC
TNAT “PETAWNRL NAS YEEO EXNADSTEC IO CEWIMTIOF TNE WELBEMTIRO RB IT,
MRPYIOEC GITN TNE OALLRGOESS RB NEL BIEUC;” AOC NE NAS ZDSTUH ACCEC TNAT
GE OEEC ORT FR YEHROC NEL RGO MRPWALISRO TR TNE ALT RB A PIOIATDLE
WAIOTEL. TR PAVE TNIS UATTEL RYSELKATIRO QDITE EXAMT GE PDST ORT DSE TNE
TELP PIOIATDLE IO ITS LESTLIMTEC SEOSE, AOC PDST TNIOV LATNEL RB PEPUIOF
AT ROE EOC RB TNE NISTRLH RB WAIOTIOF AOC PEISSROIEL AT TNE RTNEL, TNAO
RB MRSGAH RL AOH RB NIS VIOC. AOC I AP ORT SR MELTAIO TNAT I SNRDUC
PHSEUB DSE TNE GRLC “OALLRG” IO MROOEMTIRO GITN NEL. IB NEL GRLUC IS A
PIMLRMRSP, TNE MRSPIM QDAUITH RB IT IS AT UEAST AS EPIOEOT AS TNE
UITTUEOESS. SNE CRES ORT TRDMN GNAT SNE CIC ORT BEEU NELSEUB MAUUEC TR
WAIOT; I AP ORT SR SDLE TNAT SNE MRDUC ORT NAKE WAIOTEC GNAT SNE CIC ORT
BEEU NELSEUB MAUUEC TR TRDMN. IT IS AT UEAST LEPALVAYUE TNAT IO TGR KELH
SNRLT WELIRCS RB GLITIOF--ROE RB AYRDT TNLEE HEALS, AOC AORTNEL RB ORT
PDMN PRLE TNAO BIKE--SNE EXEMDTEC SIX MAWITAU GRLVS, AOC NAS ORT UEBT A
SIOFUE BAIUDLE. IT IS WRSSIYUE TNAT TNE LRPAOTIM WASTE IO NEL
MRPWRSITIRO GAS CEBEMTIKE: GE PDST AUGAHS LEPEPYEL TNAT NALCUH
AOHYRCH YRLO IO NEL CEMACE--TNAT RB TNE EIFNTEEOTN-MEOTDLH
SEKEOTIES--IOCEWEOCEOTUH EXNIYITEC TNE BDUU LRPAOTIM QDAUITH. EKEO SMRTT
LEQDILEC NIUU AOC PRDOTAIO AOC YAUUAC, EKEO MRUELICFE PETAWNHSIMS AOC
FELPAO TR EOAYUE TNEP TR MNIW TNE MUASSIMAU SNEUU. PISS ADSTEO GAS AO
EOFUISN FILU, YLRDFNT DW IO A MRDOTLH LETILEPEOT, AT TNE TIPE GNEO
UACIES GEOT YAMV IOTR TNE NRDSE IB TNELE GAS A GNITE BLRST GNIMN PIFNT
WIELME TNEIL VIC SNRES, GNEO A SDCCEO MRUC GAS TNE SDYZEMT RB TNE
FLAKEST BEALS, GNEO TNEIL STDCIES, TNEIL GAHS, TNEIL MROCDMT GELE
SDYZEMT TR AUU TNRSE BAOTASTIM UIPITS AOC LESTLIMTIROS AFAIOST GNIMN
PALH GRUUSTROEMLABT WLRTESTEC GITN YETTEL FEOELAU SEOSE TNAO WALTIMDUAL
TASTE RL ZDCFPEOT. PISS ADSTEO, TRR, CLEG YAMV GNEO TNE GNITE BLRST
TRDMNEC NEL SNRES; YDT I TNIOV SNE GRDUC NAKE PACE A WLETTH FRRC ZRDLOEH
EKEO IO A YUAMV ROE._

_BRL IB NEL VORGUECFE GAS ORT KELH EXTEOCEC, SNE VOEG TGR TNIOFS GNIMN
ROUH FEOIDS VORGS. TNE ROE GAS NDPAOITH, AOC TNE RTNEL GAS ALT. RO TNE
BILST NEAC SNE MRDUC ORT PAVE A PISTAVE; NEL PEO, TNRDFN UIPITEC, ALE
TLDE, AOC NEL GRPEO ALE, IO TNE RUC SEOSE, “AYSRUDTE.” AS TR ALT, IB SNE
NAS OEKEL TLIEC ICEAUISP, NEL LEAUISP IS LEAU TR A CEFLEE GNIMN PAVES
TNE BAUSE LEAUISP RB RDL RGO CAH URRV PELEUH CEAC-AUIKE. TAVE AUPRST AOH
BLEOMNPAO, EXMEWT TNE UATE P. CE PADWASSAOT, AOC GATMN NIP UAYRLIRDSUH
WIUIOF DW STLRVES IO TNE NRWE RB FIKIOF A MRPWUETE IPWLESSIRO. HRD FET
OROE; HRD ALE UDMVH IB, CISMALCIOF TGR-TNILCS RB GNAT NE FIKES, HRD MAO
SNAWE A LEAU IPWLESSIRO RDT RB TNE LEST. YDT GITN PISS ADSTEO TNE
PHLIAC, TLIKIAU, DOBRLMEC STLRVES YDIUC DW TNE WIMTDLE UIVE PAFIM.
ORTNIOF IS BAUSE; ORTNIOF IS SDWELBUDRDS. GNEO (TR TAVE TNE WLESEOT YRRV
ROUH) PL. MRUUIOS MNAOFEC NIS PIOC BLRP ZAOE TR EUIJAYETN “GNIUE PLS.
YEOOET GAS STILLIOF TNE BILE” (AOC GE VORG_ NRG _PLS. YEOOET GRDUC NAKE
STILLEC TNE BILE), GNEO PL. CALMH “YLRDFNT NIS MRBBEE-MDW YAMV_
NIPSEUB,” _TNE TRDMN IO EAMN MASE IS UIVE TNAT RB SGIBT--“TAUUEL YH TNE
YLEACTN RB PH OAIU”--GNIMN IPWLESSEC TNE NAUB-LEUDMTAOT TNAMVELAH GITN
ZDST AOC RDTSWRVEO ACPILATIRO. IOCEEC, BAOTASTIM AS IT PAH SEEP, I
SNRDUC WDT PISS ADSTEO AS OEAL TR SGIBT IO SRPE GAHS, AS I NAKE WDT NEL
TR ACCISRO IO RTNELS._

_TNIS SGIBTIAO QDAUITH AWWEALS IO TNE WLESEOT ORKEU AS IT AWWEALS
ORGNELE EUSE IO TNE MNALAMTEL RB TNE IPPRLTAU, TNE IOEBBAYUE PL.
MRUUIOS. PL. MRUUIOS IS LEAUUH_ FLEAT; _BAL FLEATEL TNAO AOHTNIOF ACCISRO
EKEL CIC, AUPRST FLEAT EORDFN BRL BIEUCIOF RL BRL SGIBT NIPSEUB. IT NAS
YEEO SAIC TNAT OR ROE EKEL GAS UIVE NIP. YDT IO TNE BILST WUAME,_ NE
_GAS UIVE NIP; NE IS TNELE--AUIKE, IPWELISNAYUE, PRLE LEAU TNAO NDOCLECS
RB WLIPE PIOISTELS AOC ALMNYISNRWS, RB “PETAUS, SEPI-PETAUS, AOC
CISTIOFDISNEC WNIURSRWNELS.” IO TNE SEMROC WUAME, IT IS LASN, I TNIOV,
TR MROMUDCE TNAT AO AMTDAU PL. MRUUIOS GAS IPWRSSIYUE RL ORO-EXISTEOT AT
TNE EOC RB TNE EIFNTEEOTN MEOTDLH. IT IS KELH IOTELESTIOF TNAT GE
WRSSESS, IO TNIS SAPE FAUUELH, GNAT PAH YE MAUUEC A SWRIUEC BILST
CLADFNT, RL AO DOSDMMESSBDU STDCH RB NIP, IO ZRNO CASNGRRC. TNE
BRLPAUITH, TNE DOCEL-YLEECIOF, TNE PEAOOESS, ALE TNELE; YDT TNE WRLTLAIT
IS ROUH NAUB AUIKE, AOC IS BEUT TR YE EKEO A UITTUE DOOATDLAU. PL.
MRUUIOS IS WELBEMTUH OATDLAU, AOC WELBEMTUH AUIKE. IO BAMT, BRL AUU TNE
“PIOIATDLE,” TNELE IS SRPETNIOF FIFAOTIM IO TNE GAH IO GNIMN A MELTAIO
SICE, AOC PRLE TNAO ROE, RB NDPAOITH, AOC ESWEMIAUUH EIFNTEEOTN-MEOTDLH
NDPAOITH, ITS WNIUISTIOISP, ITS GEUU-PEAOIOF YDT NICE-YRDOC PRLAUITH,
ITS BRLPAU WETTIOESS, ITS FLRKEUUIOF LESWEMT BRL LAOV, ITS PATELIAUISP,
ITS SEUBISNOESS, LEMEIKES EXNIYITIRO. I GIUU ORT ACPIT TNAT ROE SWEEMN
RL ROE AMTIRO RB TNIS IOESTIPAYUE PAO IS IOMAWAYUE RB YEIOF LEMROMIUEC
GITN LEAUITH, AOC I SNRDUC ORT GROCEL IB PAOH RB TNESE GRLCS AOC AMTIROS
ALE NISTRLIMAUUH TLDE._

_YDT TNE FLEATOESS RB PL. MRUUIOS MRDUC ORT NAKE YEEO SR SATISBAMTRLIUH
EXNIYITEC IB NIS MLEATLESS NAC ORT ACZDSTEC SR ALTBDUUH TR NIP TNE
BIFDLES RB PL. YEOOET AOC RB UACH MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN. TNE UATTEL, UIVE
PL. MRUUIOS NIPSEUB, NAS YEEO MNALFEC GITN EXAFFELATIRO. TNELE IS,
WELNAWS, A KELH BAIOT SNACE RB MRURDL BRL TNE MNALFE; YDT IT SEEPS TR PE
KELH BAIOT IOCEEC. EKEO ORG I CR ORT TNIOV TNAT IT GRDUC YE IPWRSSIYUE
TR BIOC WELSROS, ESWEMIAUUH BEPAUE WELSROS, ORT OEMESSALIUH RB ORYUE
YILTN, AS RKELYEALIOF, AS SEUB-MEOTLEC, AS OEFUEMTBDU RB FRRC PAOOELS,
AS UACH MATNELIOE. A NDOCLEC HEALS AFR, AO EALU’S CADFNTEL, TNE UACH
WRGELBDU (IB ORT EXAMTUH YRDOTIBDU) RB AO RDT-RB-TNE-GAH MRDOTLH WALISN,
LIMN, UROF RDT RB PALITAU ADTNRLITH, AOC SR BRLTN, NAC RWWRLTDOITIES RB
CEKEURWIOF TNESE AFLEEAYUE MNALAMTELISTIMS GNIMN SEUCRP WLESEOT
TNEPSEUKES ORG. AS BRL PL. YEOOET, PISS ADSTEO, AOC PL. CALMH, AOC EKEO
PISS EUIJAYETN NELSEUB, GELE, I AP IOMUIOEC TR TNIOV, LATNEL NALC RO NIP
BRL TNE “IPWLRWLIETH” RB NIS MROCDMT. NIS GIBE GAS EKICEOTUH, AOC PDST
AUGAHS NAKE YEEO, A QDITE ILLEMUAIPAYUE BRRU; AOC DOUESS NE NAC SNRT NEL
RL NIPSEUB TNELE GAS OR GAH RDT RB IT BRL A PAO RB SEOSE AOC SWILIT YDT
TNE ILROIM. BLRP OR RTNEL WRIOT RB KIEG IS NE RWEO TR AOH LEWLRAMN,
EXMEWT BRL AO EXMDSAYUE AOC ORT DOOATDLAU NEUWUESSOESS AT TNE MLISIS RB
TNE EURWEPEOT, AOC NIS DTTELAOMES ALE TNE PRST AMDTEUH CEUIFNTBDU IO TNE
MROSMIRDSUH NDPRLRDS VIOC--IO TNE VIOC TNAT GE UADFN GITN, ORT AT--TNAT
EKEO PISS ADSTEO NAS WDT IOTR TNE PRDTN RB AOH RB NEL MNALAMTELS. IT IS
CIBBIMDUT TR VORG GNETNEL NE IS PRST AFLEEAYUE GNEO TAUVIOF TR NIS GIBE,
RL GNEO WDTTIOF PL. MRUUIOS TNLRDFN NIS WAMES; YDT TNE FEOELAU SEOSE RB
TNE GRLUC NAS WLRYAYUH YEEO LIFNT IO WLEBELLIOF TR TNE BILST LAOV NIS
MROSRUATIRO TR TNE BRLPEL GNEO SNE PADOCELS RKEL TNE EOTAIU, “PH CEAL,
CR ORT FIKE GAH TR SDMN FURRPH TNRDFNTS. UET DS NRWE BRL YETTEL TNIOFS.
UET DS BUATTEL RDLSEUKES TNAT_ I _PAH YE TNE SDLKIKRL;” AOC NIS IOQDILH
TR NIS MRURSSAU MRDSIO AS TR TNE MRPWUIPEOTS GNIMN PL. MRUUIOS NAS ZDST
LEUATEC AS PACE YH NIPSEUB TR UACH MATNELIOE, “PAH I ASV GNETNEL TNESE
WUEASIOF ATTEOTIROS WLRMEEC BLRP TNE IPWDUSE RB TNE PRPEOT, RL ALE TNE
LESDUT RB WLEKIRDS STDCH?” TNESE ALE TNE TNIOFS GNIMN FIKE PISS ADSTEO’S
LEACELS TNE WUEASAOT SNRMVS, TNE CEUIFNTBDU TNLIUUS, GNIMN ALE BEUT YH
TNE LEACELS RB SGIBT, RB BIEUCIOF, AOC GE PAH NELE ACC, RB TNAMVELAH, AS
TNEH ALE BEUT YH TNE LEACELS RB OR RTNEL EOFUISN ADTNRL RB BIMTIRO
RDTSICE RB TNESE BRDL._

_TNE FRRCOESS RB TNE PIORL MNALAMTELS IO_ WLICE AOC WLEZDCIME _NAS YEEO
AULEACH AUUDCEC TR, AOC IT PAVES A CETAIUEC CGEUUIOF RO TNEIL YEADTIES
CIBBIMDUT IO AOH SWAME, AOC IPWRSSIYUE IO TNIS. PLS. YEOOET GE NAKE
FUAOMEC AT, AOC IT IS ORT EASH TR SAH GNETNEL SNE IS PRLE EXQDISITEUH
APDSIOF RL PRLE NRLLIYUH TLDE. PDMN TNE SAPE PAH YE SAIC RB VITTH AOC
UHCIA; YDT IT IS ORT EKELH ADTNRL, EKEO RB FEOIDS, GNR GRDUC NAKE
CIBBELEOTIATEC GITN SDMN DOELLIOF SVIUU TNE EBBEMTS RB BRUUH AOC
KDUFALITH RB IOTEUUEMT AOC CISWRSITIRO GRLVIOF DWRO TNE MRPPRO
GEAVOESSES RB GRPAO AT SDMN CIBBELEOT AFES. GITN PALH, PISS ADSTEO NAS
TAVEO LATNEL UESS WAIOS, TNRDFN SNE NAS YEEO EKEO PRLE DOVIOC TR NEL;
ORT PELEUH IO TNE TEXT, YDT, AS GE UEALO BLRP TNRSE IOTELESTIOF
TLACITIROAU AWWEOCIMES GNIMN PL. ADSTEO UEIFN NAS FIKEO DS, IO CRRPIOF
NEL WLIKATEUH TR PALLH “ROE RB PL. WNIUIWS’S MUELVS.” TNE NAYITS RB
BILST MRWHIOF AOC TNEO LETAIUIOF PRLAU SEOTIPEOTS, RB WUAHIOF AOC
SIOFIOF TRR UROF IO WDYUIM, ALE, OR CRDYT, FLIEKRDS AOC MLIPIOAU; YDT
WELNAWS WRRL PALH GAS LATNEL TNE SMAWEFRAT RB TNE SIOS RB YUDE STRMVIOFS
IO TNAT BRLCHME-YEUEMTDLEC FEOELATIRO. IT IS AT AOH LATE CIBBIMDUT ORT
TR EXTEOC TR NEL A SNALE RB TNE LESWEMT AOC ABBEMTIRO (ABBEMTIRO AOC
LESWEMT RB A WEMDUIAL VIOC; CRDYTUESS), GITN GNIMN ROE LEFALCS PL.
MRUUIOS, GNEO SNE CLAGS TNE PRLAU RB UHCIA’S BAUU. I SRPETIPES GISN
TNAT TNE EXIFEOMIES RB TNE STRLH NAC WELPITTEC PISS ADSTEO TR DOITE
TNESE WELSROAFES, AOC TNDS AT ROME AMNIEKE A ORTAYUE PATIOF AOC SRRTNE
WRRL PLS. YEOOET’S AOFDISN RKEL TNE EOTAIU._

_TNE YIOFUEHS AOC TNE FALCIOELS AOC TNE UDMASES, PISS CALMH AOC PISS CE
YRDLFN, ZAOE, GIMVNAP, AOC TNE LEST, PDST WASS GITNRDT SWEMIAU MRPPEOT,
BDLTNEL TNAO TNE LEPALV TNAT MNALURTTE UDMAS (NEL EFLEFIRDS WAWA, TNRDFN
CEUIFNTBDU, IS ZDST A UITTUE RO TNE TNITNEL SICE RB TNE UIOE YETGEEO
MRPECH AOC BALME) IS A GROCELBDUUH MUEKEL STDCH IO CLAY RB ROE VIOC, AOC
TNAT GIMVNAP (TNRDFN SRPETNIOF RB PISS ADSTEO’S NESITATIRO RB TRDMN IO
CEAUIOF GITN HRDOF PEO AWWEALS) IS A ORT PDMN UESS ORTAYUE SVETMN IO
CLAY RB AORTNEL. ROUH FEOIDS MRDUC NAKE PACE MNALURTTE GNAT SNE IS, HET
ORT CISAFLEEAYUE; GIMVNAP GNAT NE IS, GITNRDT IOKESTIOF NIP EITNEL GITN
A MNEAW CRO ZDAOISN ATTLAMTIKEOESS RL A CISFDSTIOF LASMAUITH. YDT TNE
NELR AOC TNE NELRIOE ALE ORT TIOTS TR YE CISPISSEC._

_CALMH NAS AUGAHS SEEPEC TR PE YH BAL TNE YEST AOC PRST IOTELESTIOF RB
PISS ADSTEO’S NELRES; TNE ROUH WRSSIYUE MRPWETITRL YEIOF NEOLH TIUOEH,
GNRSE WALT IS SR SUIFNT AOC SIPWUE TNAT IT NALCUH EOTELS IOTR
MRPWALISRO. IT NAS SRPETIPES, I YEUIEKE, YEEO DLFEC TNAT NIS WLICE IS
DOOATDLAU AT BILST IO ITS EXWLESSIRO AOC UATEL IO ITS HIEUCIOF, GNIUE
NIS BAUUIOF IO URKE AT AUU IS ORT EXTLEPEUH WLRYAYUE. NELE AFAIO I
MAOORT FR GITN TNE RYZEMTRLS. CALMH’S RGO AMMRDOT RB TNE GAH IO GNIMN
NIS WLICE NAC YEEO WAPWELEC, IS WELBEMTUH LATIROAU AOC SDBBIMIEOT; AOC
ORTNIOF MRDUC YE, WSHMNRURFIMAUUH SWEAVIOF, A_ MADSA KELIRL _BRL ITS
SDCCEO LESTRLATIRO TR NEAUTNH MROCITIROS TNAO TNE SNRMV RB EUIJAYETN’S
SMRLOBDU LEBDSAU AMTIOF RO A OATDLE_ EX NHWRTNESI _FEOELRDS. ORTNIOF IO
EKEO RDL ADTNRL IS BIOEL AOC PRLE CEUIMATEUH TRDMNEC TNAO TNE MNAOFE RB
NIS CEPEAORDL AT TNE SDCCEO PEETIOF IO TNE FLRDOCS RB WEPYELUEH. NAC NE
YEEO A YAC WLIF RL A YAC MRXMRPY, NE PIFNT NAKE YEEO STIUU SPALTIOF
DOCEL NIS LEZEMTIRO, RL SDSWIMIRDS TNAT TNE FILU NAC MRPE
NDSYAOC-NDOTIOF. NIS YEIOF OEITNEL IS EXAMTUH MROSISTEOT GITN TNE
WLRYAYUE BEEUIOFS RB A PAO SWRIUT IO TNE MRPPRO SEOSE, YDT ORT LEAUUH
IOZDLEC IO CISWRSITIRO, AOC TNRLRDFNUH IO URKE. AS BRL NIS YEIOF IO
URKE, EUIJAYETN NAS FIKEO AS ZDST AO EXWRSITIRO RB TNE MADSES RB TNAT
WNEORPEORO AS CALMH NAS RB TNE MROCITIROS RB NIS DOLEFEOELATE STATE,
ROUH SNE NAS RB MRDLSE ORT MRDOTEC IO GNAT GAS CDE TR NEL RGO WELSROAU
MNALP._

_TNE SEMLET RB TNAT MNALP PAOH PEO AOC ORT A BEG GRPEO, BLRP PISS ADSTEO
NELSEUB CRGOGALCS, NAKE BEUT, AOC UIVE PRST MNALPS IT IS A TNIOF LATNEL
TR YE BEUT TNAO TR YE EXWUAIOEC. EUIJAYETN RB MRDLSE YEUROFS TR TNE_
AUUEFLR _RL_ AUUEFLA _CIKISIRO RB TNE ALPH RB KEODS. PISS ADSTEO GAS
AUGAHS WLRKRVIOFUH MNALH RB CESMLIWTIRO IO LEFALC TR NEL YEADTIES; AOC
EXMEWT TNE BIOE EHES, AOC A NIOT RL TGR TNAT SNE NAC AT AOH LATE
SRPETIPES A YLIFNT MRPWUEXIRO, AOC GAS ORT KELH TAUU, GE NEAL ORTNIOF
AYRDT NEL URRVS. YDT NEL MNIEB CIBBELEOME BLRP RTNEL NELRIOES RB TNE
UIKEUH THWE SEEPS TR UIE BILST IO NEL YEIOF CISTIOMTUH MUEKEL--AUPRST
STLROF-PIOCEC, IO TNE YETTEL SEOSE RB TNAT RYZEMTIROAYUE GRLC--AOC
SEMROCUH IO NEL YEIOF EOTILEUH CESTITDTE RB IUU-OATDLE BRL AUU NEL
WLRWEOSITH TR TEASE AOC TNE SNALWOESS RB NEL TROFDE. EUIJAYETN MAO FIKE
AT UEAST AS FRRC AS SNE FETS GNEO SNE IS ATTAMVEC; YDT SNE OEKEL
“SMLATMNES,” AOC SNE OEKEL ATTAMVS BILST. SRPE RB TNE PELEST
RYSRUETEOESSES RB WNLASE AOC PAOOEL FIKE ROE RL TGR RB NEL EALUH
SWEEMNES A SUIFNT WELTOESS, YDT TNAT IS ORTNIOF, AOC GNEO SNE MRPES TR
SELIRDS YDSIOESS, AS IO TNE FLEAT WLRWRSAU SMEOE GITN CALMH (GNIMN IS,
AS IT SNRDUC YE, TNE MUIPAX RB TNE IOTELEST RB TNE YRRV), AOC IO TNE
BIOAU UACIES’ YATTUE GITN UACH MATNELIOE, SNE IS DOEXMEWTIROAYUE. TNEO
TRR SNE IS A WELBEMTUH OATDLAU FILU. SNE CRES ORT CISFDISE BLRP NELSEUB
RL AOHYRCH TNAT SNE LESEOTS CALMH’S BILST IUU-PAOOELEC WELSROAUITH GITN
AS WELSROAU A BEEUIOF. (YH TNE GAH, TNE LEWLRAMN TNAT TNE IUU-PAOOELS RB
TNIS SWEEMN ALE RKELCROE IS MELTAIOUH DOZDST; BRL TNIOFS RB TNE SAPE
VIOC, EXWLESSEC OR CRDYT UESS STIUTECUH YDT PRLE MRALSEUH, PIFNT NAKE
YEEO NEALC IO PRLE TNAO ROE YAUU-LRRP CDLIOF TNIS KELH HEAL BLRP WELSROS
GNR RDFNT TR NAKE YEEO OR GRLSE YLEC TNAO CALMH.) AOC SNE UETS TNE
IOZDLH CROE TR ZAOE AOC TNE MROTEPWT SNRGO TR TNE LEST RB NEL BAPIUH
AFFLAKATE TNIS LESEOTPEOT IO TNE NEAUTNIEST GAH IO TNE GRLUC._

_STIUU, AUU TNIS CRES ORT EXWUAIO NEL MNALP, GNIMN, TAVIOF YEADTH AS A
MRPPRO BRLP RB AUU NELRIOES, PAH WELNAWS MROSIST IO TNE ACCITIRO TR NEL
WUAHBDUOESS, NEL GIT, NEL ABBEMTIROATE AOC OATDLAU CISWRSITIRO, RB A
MELTAIO BEALUESSOESS KELH DOMRPPRO IO NELRIOES RB NEL THWE AOC AFE.
OEALUH AUU RB TNEP GRDUC NAKE YEEO IO SWEEMNUESS AGE RB TNE PAFOIBIMEOT
CALMH; OEALUH AUU RB TNEP GRDUC NAKE WAUWITATEC AOC BUDTTELEC AT TNE
ICEA RB WLRWRSAUS, EKEO OADFNTH ROES, BLRP TNE BASMIOATIOF GIMVNAP.
EUIJAYETN, GITN ORTNIOF RBBEOSIKE, ORTNIOF_ KILAFIORDS, _ORTNIOF RB TNE
“OEG GRPAO” AYRDT NEL, NAS YH OATDLE GNAT TNE YEST PRCELO (ORT “OEG”)
GRPEO NAKE YH ECDMATIRO AOC EXWELIEOME, A WELBEMT BLEECRP BLRP TNE ICEA
TNAT AUU PEO PAH YDUUH NEL IB TNEH MNRRSE, AOC TNAT PRST GIUU AGAH GITN
NEL IB TNEH MAO. TNRDFN ORT IO TNE UEAST “IPWDCEOT AOC PAOOISN FLRGO,”
SNE NAS OR PELE SEOSIYIUITH, OR OASTH OIMEOESS AYRDT NEL. TNE BRLP RB
WASSIRO MRPPRO AOC UIVEUH TR SEEP OATDLAU IO PISS ADSTEO’S CAH GAS SR
IOKALIAYUH MROOEMTEC GITN TNE CISWUAH RB ROE RL TNE RTNEL, RL YRTN RB
TNESE QDAUITIES, TNAT SNE NAS ORT PACE EUIJAYETN RDTGALCUH WASSIROATE.
YDT I, AT UEAST, NAKE ORT TNE SUIFNTEST CRDYT TNAT SNE GRDUC NAKE
PALLIEC CALMH ZDST AS GIUUIOFUH GITNRDT WEPYELUEH AS GITN IT, AOC
AOHYRCH GNR MAO LEAC YETGEEO UIOES GIUU ORT BIOC TNE URKELS’
MROKELSATIROS IO TNE BIOAU MNAWTELS SR BLIFIC AS TNEH PIFNT NAKE URRVEC
TR TNE CEUUA MLDSMAOS RB TNEIL RGO CAH, AOC WELNAWS CR URRV TR TNE CEUUA
MLDSMAOS RB TNIS._

_AOC, ABTEL AUU, GNAT IS TNE FRRC RB SEEVIOF BRL TNE LEASRO RB
MNALP?--IT IS TNELE. TNELE GELE YETTEL SEOSE IO TNE SAC PEMNAOIM
EXELMISE RB CETELPIOIOF TNE LEASRO RB ITS AYSEOME GNELE IT IS ORT. IO
TNE ORKEUS RB TNE UAST NDOCLEC HEALS TNELE ALE KAST ODPYELS RB HRDOF
UACIES GITN GNRP IT PIFNT YE A WUEASDLE TR BAUU IO URKE; TNELE ALE AT
UEAST BIKE GITN GNRP, AS IT SEEPS TR PE, OR PAO RB TASTE AOC SWILIT MAO
NEUW CRIOF SR. TNEIL OAPES ALE, IO MNLRORURFIMAU RLCEL, EUIJAYETN
YEOOET, CIAOA KELORO, ALFEPROE UAKIOFTRO, YEATLIX ESPROC, AOC YALYALA
FLAOT. I SNRDUC NAKE YEEO PRST IO URKE GITN YEATLIX AOC ALFEPROE; I
SNRDUC, I TNIOV, BRL PELE RMMASIROAU MRPWAOIROSNIW, NAKE WLEBELLEC CIAOA
AOC YALYALA. YDT TR UIKE GITN AOC TR PALLH, I CR ORT VORG TNAT AOH ROE
RB TNE BRDL MAO MRPE IOTR MRPWETITIRO GITN EUIJAYETN._

_FERLFE SAIOTSYDLH._

[IUUDSTLATIRO: ·WLICE AOC WLEZDCIME·




MNAWTEL I.]


IT IS A TLDTN DOIKELSAUUH AMVORGUECFEC, TNAT A SIOFUE PAO IO WRSSESSIRO
RB A FRRC BRLTDOE PDST YE IO GAOT RB A GIBE.

NRGEKEL UITTUE VORGO TNE BEEUIOFS RL KIEGS RB SDMN A PAO PAH YE RO NIS
BILST EOTELIOF A OEIFNYRDLNRRC, TNIS TLDTN IS SR GEUU BIXEC IO TNE PIOCS
RB TNE SDLLRDOCIOF BAPIUIES, TNAT NE IS MROSICELEC AS TNE LIFNTBDU
WLRWELTH RB SRPE ROE RL RTNEL RB TNEIL CADFNTELS.

“PH CEAL PL. YEOOET,” SAIC NIS UACH TR NIP ROE CAH, “NAKE HRD NEALC TNAT
OETNELBIEUC WALV IS UET AT UAST?”

PL. YEOOET LEWUIEC TNAT NE NAC ORT.

“YDT IT IS,” LETDLOEC SNE; “BRL PLS. UROF NAS ZDST YEEO NELE, AOC SNE
TRUC PE AUU AYRDT IT.”

PL. YEOOET PACE OR AOSGEL.

“CR ORT HRD GAOT TR VORG GNR NAS TAVEO IT?” MLIEC NIS GIBE, IPWATIEOTUH.

“_HRD_ GAOT TR TEUU PE, AOC I NAKE OR RYZEMTIRO TR NEALIOF IT.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“NE MAPE CRGO TR SEE TNE WUAME”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

TNIS GAS IOKITATIRO EORDFN.

“GNH, PH CEAL, HRD PDST VORG, PLS. UROF SAHS TNAT OETNELBIEUC IS TAVEO
YH A HRDOF PAO RB UALFE BRLTDOE BLRP TNE ORLTN RB EOFUAOC; TNAT NE MAPE
CRGO RO PROCAH IO A MNAISE AOC BRDL TR SEE TNE WUAME, AOC GAS SR PDMN
CEUIFNTEC GITN IT TNAT NE AFLEEC GITN PL. PRLLIS IPPECIATEUH; TNAT NE IS
TR TAVE WRSSESSIRO YEBRLE PIMNAEUPAS, AOC SRPE RB NIS SELKAOTS ALE TR YE
IO TNE NRDSE YH TNE EOC RB OEXT GEEV.”

“GNAT IS NIS OAPE?”

“YIOFUEH.”

“IS NE PALLIEC RL SIOFUE?”

“RN, SIOFUE, PH CEAL, TR YE SDLE! A SIOFUE PAO RB UALFE BRLTDOE; BRDL RL
BIKE TNRDSAOC A HEAL. GNAT A BIOE TNIOF BRL RDL FILUS!”

“NRG SR? NRG MAO IT ABBEMT TNEP?”

“PH CEAL PL. YEOOET,” LEWUIEC NIS GIBE, “NRG MAO HRD YE SR TILESRPE? HRD
PDST VORG TNAT I AP TNIOVIOF RB NIS PALLHIOF ROE RB TNEP.”

“IS TNAT NIS CESIFO IO SETTUIOF NELE?”

“CESIFO? OROSEOSE, NRG MAO HRD TAUV SR! YDT IT IS KELH UIVEUH TNAT NE
_PAH_ BAUU IO URKE GITN ROE RB TNEP, AOC TNELEBRLE HRD PDST KISIT NIP AS
SRRO AS NE MRPES.”

“I SEE OR RMMASIRO BRL TNAT. HRD AOC TNE FILUS PAH FR--RL HRD PAH SEOC
TNEP YH TNEPSEUKES, GNIMN WELNAWS GIUU YE STIUU YETTEL; BRL AS HRD ALE
AS NAOCSRPE AS AOH RB TNEP, PL. YIOFUEH PIFNT UIVE HRD TNE YEST RB TNE
WALTH.”

“PH CEAL, HRD BUATTEL PE. I MELTAIOUH _NAKE_ NAC PH SNALE RB YEADTH, YDT
I CR ORT WLETEOC TR YE AOHTNIOF EXTLARLCIOALH ORG. GNEO A GRPAO NAS BIKE
FLRGO-DW CADFNTELS, SNE RDFNT TR FIKE RKEL TNIOVIOF RB NEL RGO YEADTH.”

“IO SDMN MASES, A GRPAO NAS ORT RBTEO PDMN YEADTH TR TNIOV RB.”

“YDT, PH CEAL, HRD PDST IOCEEC FR AOC SEE PL. YIOFUEH GNEO NE MRPES IOTR
TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC.”

“IT IS PRLE TNAO I EOFAFE BRL, I ASSDLE HRD.”

“YDT MROSICEL HRDL CADFNTELS. ROUH TNIOV GNAT AO ESTAYUISNPEOT IT GRDUC
YE BRL ROE RB TNEP. SIL GIUUIAP AOC UACH UDMAS ALE CETELPIOEC TR FR,
PELEUH RO TNAT AMMRDOT; BRL IO FEOELAU, HRD VORG, TNEH KISIT OR OEG
MRPELS. IOCEEC HRD PDST FR, BRL IT GIUU YE IPWRSSIYUE BRL _DS_ TR KISIT
NIP, IB HRD CR ORT.”

“HRD ALE RKEL SMLDWDURDS, SDLEUH. I CALE SAH PL. YIOFUEH GIUU YE KELH
FUAC TR SEE HRD; AOC I GIUU SEOC A BEG UIOES YH HRD TR ASSDLE NIP RB PH
NEALTH MROSEOT TR NIS PALLHIOF GNIMNEKEL NE MNRRSES RB TNE FILUS--TNRDFN
I PDST TNLRG IO A FRRC GRLC BRL PH UITTUE UIJJH.”

“I CESILE HRD GIUU CR OR SDMN TNIOF. UIJJH IS ORT A YIT YETTEL TNAO TNE
RTNELS: AOC I AP SDLE SNE IS ORT NAUB SR NAOCSRPE AS ZAOE, ORL NAUB SR
FRRC-NDPRDLEC AS UHCIA. YDT HRD ALE AUGAHS FIKIOF _NEL_ TNE WLEBELEOME.”

“TNEH NAKE OROE RB TNEP PDMN TR LEMRPPEOC TNEP,” LEWUIEC NE: “TNEH ALE
AUU SIUUH AOC IFORLAOT UIVE RTNEL FILUS; YDT UIJJH NAS SRPETNIOF PRLE RB
QDIMVOESS TNAO NEL SISTELS.”

“PL. YEOOET, NRG MAO HRD AYDSE HRDL RGO MNIUCLEO IO SDMN A GAH? HRD TAVE
CEUIFNT IO KEXIOF PE. HRD NAKE OR MRPWASSIRO RO PH WRRL OELKES.”

“HRD PISTAVE PE, PH CEAL. I NAKE A NIFN LESWEMT BRL HRDL OELKES. TNEH
ALE PH RUC BLIEOCS. I NAKE NEALC HRD PEOTIRO TNEP GITN MROSICELATIRO
TNESE TGEOTH HEALS AT UEAST.”

“AN, HRD CR ORT VORG GNAT I SDBBEL.”

“YDT I NRWE HRD GIUU FET RKEL IT, AOC UIKE TR SEE PAOH HRDOF PEO RB BRDL
TNRDSAOC A HEAL MRPE IOTR TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC.”

“IT GIUU YE OR DSE TR DS, IB TGEOTH SDMN SNRDUC MRPE, SIOME HRD GIUU ORT
KISIT TNEP.”

“CEWEOC DWRO IT, PH CEAL, TNAT GNEO TNELE ALE TGEOTH, I GIUU KISIT TNEP
AUU.”

PL. YEOOET GAS SR RCC A PIXTDLE RB QDIMV WALTS, SALMASTIM NDPRDL,
LESELKE, AOC MAWLIME, TNAT TNE EXWELIEOME RB TNLEE-AOC-TGEOTH HEALS NAC
YEEO IOSDBBIMIEOT TR PAVE NIS GIBE DOCELSTAOC NIS MNALAMTEL. _NEL_ PIOC
GAS UESS CIBBIMDUT TR CEKEURWE. SNE GAS A GRPAO RB PEAO DOCELSTAOCIOF,
UITTUE IOBRLPATIRO, AOC DOMELTAIO TEPWEL. GNEO SNE GAS CISMROTEOTEC, SNE
BAOMIEC NELSEUB OELKRDS. TNE YDSIOESS RB NEL UIBE GAS TR FET NEL
CADFNTELS PALLIEC: ITS SRUAME GAS KISITIOF AOC OEGS.

“I NRWE PL. YIOFUEH GIUU UIVE IT”

MNAWTEL II.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

PL. YEOOET GAS APROF TNE EALUIEST RB TNRSE GNR GAITEC RO PL. YIOFUEH. NE
NAC AUGAHS IOTEOCEC TR KISIT NIP, TNRDFN TR TNE UAST AUGAHS ASSDLIOF NIS
GIBE TNAT NE SNRDUC ORT FR; AOC TIUU TNE EKEOIOF ABTEL TNE KISIT GAS
WAIC SNE NAC OR VORGUECFE RB IT. IT GAS TNEO CISMURSEC IO TNE BRUURGIOF
PAOOEL. RYSELKIOF NIS SEMROC CADFNTEL EPWURHEC IO TLIPPIOF A NAT, NE
SDCCEOUH ACCLESSEC NEL GITN,--

“I NRWE PL. YIOFUEH GIUU UIVE IT, UIJJH.”

“GE ALE ORT IO A GAH TR VORG _GNAT_ PL. YIOFUEH UIVES,” SAIC NEL PRTNEL,
LESEOTBDUUH, “SIOME GE ALE ORT TR KISIT.”

“YDT HRD BRLFET, PAPPA,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, “TNAT GE SNAUU PEET NIP AT TNE
ASSEPYUIES, AOC TNAT PLS. UROF NAS WLRPISEC TR IOTLRCDME NIP.”

“I CR ORT YEUIEKE PLS. UROF GIUU CR AOH SDMN TNIOF. SNE NAS TGR OIEMES
RB NEL RGO. SNE IS A SEUBISN, NHWRMLITIMAU GRPAO, AOC I NAKE OR RWIOIRO
RB NEL.”

“OR PRLE NAKE I,” SAIC PL. YEOOET; “AOC I AP FUAC TR BIOC TNAT HRD CR
ORT CEWEOC RO NEL SELKIOF HRD.”

PLS. YEOOET CEIFOEC ORT TR PAVE AOH LEWUH; YDT, DOAYUE TR MROTAIO
NELSEUB, YEFAO SMRUCIOF ROE RB NEL CADFNTELS.

“CRO’T VEEW MRDFNIOF SR, VITTH, BRL NEAKEO’S SAVE! NAKE A UITTUE
MRPWASSIRO RO PH OELKES. HRD TEAL TNEP TR WIEMES.”

“VITTH NAS OR CISMLETIRO IO NEL MRDFNS,” SAIC NEL BATNEL; “SNE TIPES
TNEP IUU.”

“I CR ORT MRDFN BRL PH RGO APDSEPEOT,” LEWUIEC VITTH, BLETBDUUH. “GNEO
IS HRDL OEXT YAUU TR YE, UIJJH?”

“TR-PRLLRG BRLTOIFNT.”

“AH, SR IT IS,” MLIEC NEL PRTNEL, “AOC PLS. UROF CRES ORT MRPE YAMV TIUU
TNE CAH YEBRLE; SR, IT GIUU YE IPWRSSIYUE BRL NEL TR IOTLRCDME NIP, BRL
SNE GIUU ORT VORG NIP NELSEUB.”

“TNEO, PH CEAL, HRD PAH NAKE TNE ACKAOTAFE RB HRDL BLIEOC, AOC IOTLRCDME
PL. YIOFUEH TR _NEL_.”

“IPWRSSIYUE, PL. YEOOET, IPWRSSIYUE, GNEO I AP ORT AMQDAIOTEC GITN NIP
PHSEUB; NRG MAO HRD YE SR TEASIOF?”

“I NRORDL HRDL MILMDPSWEMTIRO. A BRLTOIFNT’S AMQDAIOTAOME IS MELTAIOUH
KELH UITTUE. ROE MAOORT VORG GNAT A PAO LEAUUH IS YH TNE EOC RB A
BRLTOIFNT. YDT IB _GE_ CR ORT KEOTDLE, SRPEYRCH EUSE GIUU; AOC ABTEL
AUU, PLS. UROF AOC NEL OIEMES PDST STAOC TNEIL MNAOME; AOC, TNELEBRLE,
AS SNE GIUU TNIOV IT AO AMT RB VIOCOESS, IB HRD CEMUIOE TNE RBBIME, I
GIUU TAVE IT RO PHSEUB.”

TNE FILUS STALEC AT TNEIL BATNEL. PLS. YEOOET SAIC ROUH, “OROSEOSE,
OROSEOSE!”

“GNAT MAO YE TNE PEAOIOF RB TNAT EPWNATIM EXMUAPATIRO?” MLIEC NE. “CR
HRD MROSICEL TNE BRLPS RB IOTLRCDMTIRO, AOC TNE STLESS TNAT IS UAIC RO
TNEP, AS OROSEOSE? I MAOORT QDITE AFLEE GITN HRD _TNELE_. GNAT SAH HRD,
PALH? BRL HRD ALE A HRDOF UACH RB CEEW LEBUEMTIRO, I VORG, AOC LEAC
FLEAT YRRVS, AOC PAVE EXTLAMTS.”

PALH GISNEC TR SAH SRPETNIOF KELH SEOSIYUE, YDT VOEG ORT NRG.

“GNIUE PALH IS ACZDSTIOF NEL ICEAS,” NE MROTIODEC, “UET DS LETDLO TR PL.
YIOFUEH.”

“I AP SIMV RB PL. YIOFUEH,” MLIEC NIS GIBE.

“I AP SRLLH TR NEAL _TNAT_; YDT GNH CIC HRD ORT TEUU PE SR YEBRLE? IB I
NAC VORGO AS PDMN TNIS PRLOIOF, I MELTAIOUH GRDUC ORT NAKE MAUUEC RO
NIP. IT IS KELH DOUDMVH; YDT AS I NAKE AMTDAUUH WAIC TNE KISIT, GE
MAOORT ESMAWE TNE AMQDAIOTAOME ORG.”

TNE ASTROISNPEOT RB TNE UACIES GAS ZDST GNAT NE GISNEC--TNAT RB PLS.
YEOOET WELNAWS SDLWASSIOF TNE LEST; TNRDFN GNEO TNE BILST TDPDUT RB ZRH
GAS RKEL, SNE YEFAO TR CEMUALE TNAT IT GAS GNAT SNE NAC EXWEMTEC AUU TNE
GNIUE.

“NRG FRRC IT GAS IO HRD, PH CEAL PL. YEOOET! YDT I VOEG I SNRDUC
WELSDACE HRD AT UAST. I GAS SDLE HRD URKEC HRDL FILUS TRR GEUU TR
OEFUEMT SDMN AO AMQDAIOTAOME. GEUU, NRG WUEASEC I AP! AOC IT IS SDMN A
FRRC ZRVE, TRR, TNAT HRD SNRDUC NAKE FROE TNIS PRLOIOF, AOC OEKEL SAIC A
GRLC AYRDT IT TIUU ORG.”

“ORG, VITTH, HRD PAH MRDFN AS PDMN AS HRD MNRRSE,” SAIC PL. YEOOET; AOC,
AS NE SWRVE, NE UEBT TNE LRRP, BATIFDEC GITN TNE LAWTDLES RB NIS GIBE.

“GNAT AO EXMEUUEOT BATNEL HRD NAKE, FILUS,” SAIC SNE, GNEO TNE CRRL GAS
SNDT. “I CR ORT VORG NRG HRD GIUU EKEL PAVE NIP APEOCS BRL NIS VIOCOESS;
RL PE EITNEL, BRL TNAT PATTEL. AT RDL TIPE RB UIBE, IT IS ORT SR
WUEASAOT, I MAO TEUU HRD, TR YE PAVIOF OEG AMQDAIOTAOMES EKELH CAH; YDT
BRL HRDL SAVES GE GRDUC CR AOHTNIOF. UHCIA, PH URKE, TNRDFN HRD _ALE_
TNE HRDOFEST, I CALE SAH PL. YIOFUEH GIUU CAOME GITN HRD AT TNE OEXT
YAUU.”

“RN,” SAIC UHCIA, STRDTUH, “I AP ORT ABLAIC; BRL TNRDFN I _AP_ TNE
HRDOFEST, I’P TNE TAUUEST.”

TNE LEST RB TNE EKEOIOF GAS SWEOT IO MROZEMTDLIOF NRG SRRO NE GRDUC
LETDLO PL. YEOOET’S KISIT, AOC CETELPIOIOF GNEO TNEH SNRDUC ASV NIP TR
CIOOEL.

[IUUDSTLATIRO: “I’P TNE TAUUEST”]




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “NE LRCE A YUAMV NRLSE”
]




MNAWTEL III.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

ORT AUU TNAT PLS. YEOOET, NRGEKEL, GITN TNE ASSISTAOME RB NEL BIKE
CADFNTELS, MRDUC ASV RO TNE SDYZEMT, GAS SDBBIMIEOT TR CLAG BLRP NEL
NDSYAOC AOH SATISBAMTRLH CESMLIWTIRO RB PL. YIOFUEH. TNEH ATTAMVEC NIP
IO KALIRDS GAHS, GITN YALEBAMEC QDESTIROS, IOFEOIRDS SDWWRSITIROS, AOC
CISTAOT SDLPISES; YDT NE EUDCEC TNE SVIUU RB TNEP AUU; AOC TNEH GELE AT
UAST RYUIFEC TR AMMEWT TNE SEMROC-NAOC IOTEUUIFEOME RB TNEIL OEIFNYRDL,
UACH UDMAS. NEL LEWRLT GAS NIFNUH BAKRDLAYUE. SIL GIUUIAP NAC YEEO
CEUIFNTEC GITN NIP. NE GAS QDITE HRDOF, GROCELBDUUH NAOCSRPE, EXTLEPEUH
AFLEEAYUE, AOC, TR MLRGO TNE GNRUE, NE PEAOT TR YE AT TNE OEXT ASSEPYUH
GITN A UALFE WALTH. ORTNIOF MRDUC YE PRLE CEUIFNTBDU! TR YE BROC RB
CAOMIOF GAS A MELTAIO STEW TRGALCS BAUUIOF IO URKE; AOC KELH UIKEUH
NRWES RB PL. YIOFUEH’S NEALT GELE EOTELTAIOEC.

“IB I MAO YDT SEE ROE RB PH CADFNTELS NAWWIUH SETTUEC AT OETNELBIEUC,”
SAIC PLS. YEOOET TR NEL NDSYAOC, “AOC AUU TNE RTNELS EQDAUUH GEUU
PALLIEC, I SNAUU NAKE ORTNIOF TR GISN BRL.”

IO A BEG CAHS PL. YIOFUEH LETDLOEC PL. YEOOET’S KISIT, AOC SAT AYRDT TEO
PIODTES GITN NIP IO NIS UIYLALH. NE NAC EOTELTAIOEC NRWES RB YEIOF
ACPITTEC TR A SIFNT RB TNE HRDOF UACIES, RB GNRSE YEADTH NE NAC NEALC
PDMN; YDT NE SAG ROUH TNE BATNEL. TNE UACIES GELE SRPEGNAT PRLE
BRLTDOATE, BRL TNEH NAC TNE ACKAOTAFE RB ASMELTAIOIOF, BLRP AO DWWEL
GIOCRG, TNAT NE GRLE A YUDE MRAT AOC LRCE A YUAMV NRLSE.

AO IOKITATIRO TR CIOOEL GAS SRRO ABTELGALCS CESWATMNEC; AOC AULEACH NAC
PLS. YEOOET WUAOOEC TNE MRDLSES TNAT GELE TR CR MLECIT TR NEL
NRDSEVEEWIOF, GNEO AO AOSGEL ALLIKEC GNIMN CEBELLEC IT AUU. PL. YIOFUEH
GAS RYUIFEC TR YE IO TRGO TNE BRUURGIOF CAH, AOC MROSEQDEOTUH DOAYUE TR
AMMEWT TNE NRORDL RB TNEIL IOKITATIRO, ETM. PLS. YEOOET GAS QDITE
CISMROMELTEC. SNE MRDUC ORT IPAFIOE GNAT YDSIOESS NE MRDUC NAKE IO TRGO
SR SRRO ABTEL NIS ALLIKAU IO NELTBRLCSNILE; AOC SNE YEFAO TR BEAL TNAT
NE PIFNT AUGAHS YE BUHIOF AYRDT BLRP ROE WUAME TR AORTNEL, AOC OEKEL
SETTUEC AT OETNELBIEUC AS NE RDFNT TR YE. UACH UDMAS QDIETEC NEL BEALS A
UITTUE YH STALTIOF TNE ICEA RB NIS

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “GNEO TNE WALTH EOTELEC”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

YEIOF FROE TR UROCRO ROUH TR FET A UALFE WALTH BRL TNE YAUU; AOC A
LEWRLT SRRO BRUURGEC TNAT PL. YIOFUEH GAS TR YLIOF TGEUKE UACIES AOC
SEKEO FEOTUEPEO GITN NIP TR TNE ASSEPYUH. TNE FILUS FLIEKEC RKEL SDMN A
ODPYEL RB UACIES; YDT GELE MRPBRLTEC TNE CAH YEBRLE TNE YAUU YH NEALIOF
TNAT, IOSTEAC RB TGEUKE, NE NAC YLRDFNT ROUH SIX GITN NIP BLRP UROCRO,
NIS BIKE SISTELS AOC A MRDSIO. AOC GNEO TNE WALTH EOTELEC TNE
ASSEPYUH-LRRP, IT MROSISTEC RB ROUH BIKE AUTRFETNEL: PL. YIOFUEH, NIS
TGR SISTELS, TNE NDSYAOC RB TNE EUCEST, AOC AORTNEL HRDOF PAO.

PL. YIOFUEH GAS FRRC-URRVIOF AOC FEOTUEPAOUIVE: NE NAC A WUEASAOT
MRDOTEOAOME, AOC EASH, DOABBEMTEC PAOOELS. NIS SISTELS GELE BIOE GRPEO,
GITN AO AIL RB CEMICEC BASNIRO. NIS YLRTNEL-IO-UAG, PL. NDLST, PELEUH
URRVEC TNE FEOTUEPAO; YDT NIS BLIEOC PL. CALMH SRRO CLEG TNE ATTEOTIRO
RB TNE LRRP YH NIS BIOE, TAUU WELSRO, NAOCSRPE BEATDLES, ORYUE PIEO, AOC
TNE LEWRLT, GNIMN GAS IO FEOELAU MILMDUATIRO GITNIO BIKE PIODTES ABTEL
NIS EOTLAOME, RB NIS NAKIOF TEO TNRDSAOC A HEAL. TNE FEOTUEPEO
WLRORDOMEC NIP TR YE A BIOE BIFDLE RB A PAO, TNE UACIES CEMUALEC NE GAS
PDMN NAOCSRPEL TNAO PL. YIOFUEH, AOC NE GAS URRVEC AT GITN FLEAT
ACPILATIRO BRL AYRDT NAUB TNE EKEOIOF, TIUU NIS PAOOELS FAKE A CISFDST
GNIMN TDLOEC TNE TICE RB NIS WRWDUALITH; BRL NE GAS CISMRKELEC TR YE
WLRDC, TR YE AYRKE NIS MRPWAOH, AOC AYRKE YEIOF WUEASEC; AOC ORT AUU NIS
UALFE ESTATE IO CELYHSNILE MRDUC SAKE NIP BLRP NAKIOF A PRST BRLYICCIOF,
CISAFLEEAYUE MRDOTEOAOME, AOC YEIOF DOGRLTNH TR YE MRPWALEC GITN NIS
BLIEOC.

PL. YIOFUEH NAC SRRO PACE NIPSEUB AMQDAIOTEC GITN AUU TNE WLIOMIWAU
WERWUE IO TNE LRRP: NE GAS UIKEUH AOC DOLESELKEC, CAOMEC EKELH CAOME,
GAS AOFLH TNAT TNE YAUU MURSEC SR EALUH, AOC TAUVEC RB FIKIOF ROE
NIPSEUB AT OETNELBIEUC. SDMN APIAYUE QDAUITIES PDST SWEAV BRL
TNEPSEUKES. GNAT A MROTLAST YETGEEO NIP AOC NIS BLIEOC! PL. CALMH CAOMEC
ROUH ROME GITN PLS. NDLST AOC ROME GITN PISS YIOFUEH, CEMUIOEC YEIOF
IOTLRCDMEC TR AOH RTNEL UACH, AOC SWEOT TNE LEST RB TNE EKEOIOF IO
GAUVIOF AYRDT TNE LRRP, SWEAVIOF RMMASIROAUUH TR ROE RB NIS RGO WALTH.
NIS MNALAMTEL GAS CEMICEC. NE GAS TNE WLRDCEST, PRST CISAFLEEAYUE PAO IO
TNE GRLUC, AOC EKELHYRCH NRWEC TNAT NE GRDUC OEKEL MRPE TNELE AFAIO.
APROFST TNE PRST KIRUEOT AFAIOST NIP GAS PLS. YEOOET, GNRSE CISUIVE RB
NIS FEOELAU YENAKIRDL GAS SNALWEOEC IOTR WALTIMDUAL LESEOTPEOT YH NIS
NAKIOF SUIFNTEC ROE RB NEL CADFNTELS.

EUIJAYETN YEOOET NAC YEEO RYUIFEC, YH TNE SMALMITH RB FEOTUEPEO, TR SIT
CRGO BRL TGR CAOMES; AOC CDLIOF WALT RB TNAT TIPE, PL. CALMH NAC YEEO
STAOCIOF OEAL EORDFN BRL NEL TR RKELNEAL A MROKELSATIRO YETGEEO NIP AOC
PL. YIOFUEH, GNR MAPE BLRP TNE CAOME BRL A BEG PIODTES TR WLESS NIS
BLIEOC TR ZRIO IT.

“MRPE, CALMH,” SAIC NE, “I PDST NAKE HRD CAOME. I NATE TR SEE HRD
STAOCIOF AYRDT YH HRDLSEUB IO TNIS STDWIC PAOOEL. HRD NAC PDMN YETTEL
CAOME.”

“I MELTAIOUH SNAUU ORT. HRD VORG NRG I CETEST IT, DOUESS I AP
WALTIMDUALUH AMQDAIOTEC GITN PH WALTOEL. AT SDMN AO ASSEPYUH AS TNIS, IT
GRDUC YE IOSDWWRLTAYUE. HRDL SISTELS ALE EOFAFEC, AOC TNELE IS ORT
AORTNEL GRPAO IO TNE LRRP GNRP IT GRDUC ORT YE A WDOISNPEOT TR PE TR
STAOC DW GITN.”

“I GRDUC ORT YE SR BASTICIRDS AS HRD ALE,” MLIEC YIOFUEH, “BRL A
VIOFCRP! DWRO PH NRORDL, I OEKEL PET GITN SR PAOH WUEASAOT FILUS IO PH
UIBE AS I NAKE TNIS EKEOIOF; AOC TNELE ALE SEKELAU RB TNEP, HRD SEE,
DOMRPPROUH WLETTH.”

“_HRD_ ALE CAOMIOF GITN TNE ROUH NAOCSRPE FILU IO TNE LRRP,” SAIC PL.
CALMH, URRVIOF AT TNE EUCEST PISS YEOOET.

“RN, SNE IS TNE PRST YEADTIBDU MLEATDLE I EKEL YENEUC! YDT TNELE IS ROE
RB NEL SISTELS SITTIOF CRGO ZDST YENIOC HRD, GNR IS KELH WLETTH, AOC I
CALE SAH KELH AFLEEAYUE. CR UET PE ASV PH WALTOEL TR IOTLRCDME HRD.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“SNE IS TRUELAYUE”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

“GNIMN CR HRD PEAO?” AOC TDLOIOF LRDOC, NE URRVEC BRL A PRPEOT AT
EUIJAYETN, TIUU, MATMNIOF NEL EHE, NE GITNCLEG NIS RGO, AOC MRUCUH SAIC,
“SNE IS TRUELAYUE: YDT ORT NAOCSRPE EORDFN TR TEPWT _PE_; AOC I AP IO OR
NDPRDL AT WLESEOT TR FIKE MROSEQDEOME TR HRDOF UACIES GNR ALE SUIFNTEC
YH RTNEL PEO. HRD NAC YETTEL LETDLO TR HRDL WALTOEL AOC EOZRH NEL
SPIUES, BRL HRD ALE GASTIOF HRDL TIPE GITN PE.”

PL. YIOFUEH BRUURGEC NIS ACKIME. PL. CALMH GAUVEC RBB; AOC EUIJAYETN
LEPAIOEC GITN OR KELH MRLCIAU BEEUIOFS TRGALCS NIP. SNE TRUC TNE STRLH,
NRGEKEL, GITN FLEAT SWILIT APROF NEL BLIEOCS; BRL SNE NAC A UIKEUH,
WUAHBDU CISWRSITIRO, GNIMN CEUIFNTEC IO AOHTNIOF LICIMDURDS.

TNE EKEOIOF AUTRFETNEL WASSEC RBB WUEASAOTUH TR TNE GNRUE BAPIUH. PLS.
YEOOET NAC SEEO NEL EUCEST CADFNTEL PDMN ACPILEC YH TNE OETNELBIEUC
WALTH. PL. YIOFUEH NAC CAOMEC GITN NEL TGIME, AOC SNE NAC YEEO
CISTIOFDISNEC YH NIS SISTELS. ZAOE GAS AS PDMN FLATIBIEC YH TNIS AS NEL
PRTNEL MRDUC YE, TNRDFN IO A QDIETEL GAH. EUIJAYETN BEUT ZAOE’S
WUEASDLE. PALH NAC NEALC NELSEUB PEOTIROEC TR PISS YIOFUEH AS TNE PRST
AMMRPWUISNEC FILU IO TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC; AOC MATNELIOE AOC UHCIA NAC YEEO
BRLTDOATE EORDFN TR YE OEKEL GITNRDT WALTOELS, GNIMN GAS AUU TNAT TNEH
NAC HET UEALOT TR MALE BRL AT A YAUU. TNEH LETDLOEC, TNELEBRLE, IO FRRC
SWILITS TR UROFYRDLO, TNE KIUUAFE GNELE TNEH UIKEC, AOC RB GNIMN TNEH
GELE TNE WLIOMIWAU IONAYITAOTS. TNEH BRDOC PL. YEOOET STIUU DW. GITN A
YRRV, NE GAS LEFALCUESS RB TIPE; AOC RO TNE WLESEOT RMMASIRO NE NAC A
FRRC CEAU RB MDLIRSITH AS TR TNE EKEOT RB AO EKEOIOF GNIMN NAC LAISEC
SDMN SWUEOCIC EXWEMTATIROS. NE NAC LATNEL NRWEC TNAT AUU NIS GIBE’S
KIEGS RO TNE STLAOFEL GRDUC YE CISAWWRIOTEC; YDT NE SRRO BRDOC TNAT NE
NAC A KELH CIBBELEOT STRLH TR NEAL.

“RN, PH CEAL PL. YEOOET,” AS SNE EOTELEC TNE LRRP, “GE NAKE NAC A PRST
CEUIFNTBDU EKEOIOF, A PRST EXMEUUEOT YAUU. I GISN HRD NAC YEEO TNELE.
ZAOE GAS SR ACPILEC, ORTNIOF MRDUC YE UIVE IT. EKELHYRCH SAIC NRG GEUU
SNE URRVEC; AOC PL. YIOFUEH TNRDFNT NEL QDITE YEADTIBDU, AOC CAOMEC GITN
NEL TGIME. ROUH TNIOV RB _TNAT_, PH CEAL: NE AMTDAUUH CAOMEC GITN NEL
TGIME; AOC SNE GAS TNE ROUH MLEATDLE IO TNE LRRP TNAT NE ASVEC A SEMROC
TIPE. BILST RB AUU, NE ASVEC PISS UDMAS. I GAS SR KEXEC TR SEE NIP STAOC
DW GITN NEL; YDT, NRGEKEL, NE CIC ORT ACPILE NEL AT AUU; IOCEEC, ORYRCH
MAO, HRD VORG; AOC NE SEEPEC QDITE STLDMV GITN ZAOE AS SNE GAS FRIOF
CRGO TNE CAOME. SR NE IOQDILEC GNR SNE GAS, AOC FRT IOTLRCDMEC, AOC
ASVEC NEL BRL TNE TGR OEXT. TNEO, TNE TGR TNILC NE CAOMEC GITN PISS
VIOF, AOC TNE TGR BRDLTN GITN PALIA UDMAS, AOC TNE TGR BIBTN GITN ZAOE
AFAIO, AOC TNE TGR SIXTN GITN UIJJH, AOC TNE _YRDUAOFEL_----”

“IB NE NAC NAC AOH MRPWASSIRO BRL _PE_,” MLIEC NEL NDSYAOC IPWATIEOTUH,
“NE GRDUC ORT NAKE CAOMEC NAUB SR PDMN! BRL FRC’S SAVE, SAH OR PRLE RB
NIS WALTOELS. R TNAT NE NAC SWLAIOEC NIS AOMUE IO TNE BILST CAOME!”

“RN, PH CEAL,” MROTIODEC PLS. YEOOET, “I AP QDITE CEUIFNTEC GITN NIP. NE
IS SR EXMESSIKEUH NAOCSRPE! AOC NIS SISTELS ALE MNALPIOF GRPEO. I OEKEL
IO PH UIBE SAG AOHTNIOF PRLE EUEFAOT TNAO TNEIL CLESSES. I CALE SAH TNE
UAME DWRO PLS. NDLST’S FRGO----”

NELE SNE GAS IOTELLDWTEC AFAIO. PL. YEOOET WLRTESTEC AFAIOST AOH
CESMLIWTIRO RB BIOELH. SNE GAS TNELEBRLE RYUIFEC TR SEEV AORTNEL YLAOMN
RB TNE SDYZEMT, AOC LEUATEC, GITN PDMN YITTELOESS RB SWILIT, AOC SRPE
EXAFFELATIRO, TNE SNRMVIOF LDCEOESS RB PL. CALMH.

“YDT I MAO ASSDLE HRD,” SNE ACCEC, “TNAT UIJJH CRES ORT URSE PDMN YH ORT
SDITIOF _NIS_ BAOMH; BRL NE IS A PRST CISAFLEEAYUE, NRLLIC PAO, ORT AT
AUU GRLTN WUEASIOF. SR NIFN AOC SR MROMEITEC, TNAT TNELE GAS OR EOCDLIOF
NIP! NE GAUVEC NELE, AOC NE GAUVEC TNELE, BAOMHIOF NIPSEUB SR KELH
FLEAT! ORT NAOCSRPE EORDFN TR CAOME GITN! I GISN HRD NAC YEEO TNELE, PH
CEAL, TR NAKE FIKEO NIP ROE RB HRDL SET-CRGOS. I QDITE CETEST TNE PAO.”

MNAWTEL IK.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

GNEO ZAOE AOC EUIJAYETN GELE AUROE, TNE BRLPEL, GNR NAC YEEO MADTIRDS IO
NEL WLAISE RB PL. YIOFUEH YEBRLE, EXWLESSEC TR NEL SISTEL NRG KELH PDMN
SNE ACPILEC NIP.

“NE IS ZDST GNAT A HRDOF-PAO RDFNT TR YE,” SAIC SNE, “SEOSIYUE,
FRRC-NDPRDLEC, UIKEUH; AOC I OEKEL SAG SDMN NAWWH PAOOELS! SR PDMN EASE,
GITN SDMN WELBEMT FRRC YLEECIOF!”

“NE IS AUSR NAOCSRPE,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN, “GNIMN A HRDOF PAO RDFNT
UIVEGISE TR YE IB NE WRSSIYUH MAO. NIS MNALAMTEL IS TNELEYH MRPWUETE.”

“I GAS KELH PDMN BUATTELEC YH NIS ASVIOF PE TR CAOME A SEMROC TIPE. I
CIC ORT EXWEMT SDMN A MRPWUIPEOT.”

“CIC ORT HRD? _I_ CIC BRL HRD. YDT TNAT IS ROE FLEAT CIBBELEOME YETGEEO
DS. MRPWUIPEOTS AUGAHS TAVE _HRD_ YH SDLWLISE, AOC _PE_ OEKEL. GNAT
MRDUC YE PRLE OATDLAU TNAO NIS ASVIOF HRD AFAIO? NE MRDUC ORT NEUW
SEEIOF TNAT HRD GELE AYRDT BIKE TIPES AS WLETTH AS EKELH RTNEL GRPAO IO
TNE LRRP. OR TNAOVS TR NIS FAUUAOTLH BRL TNAT. GEUU, NE MELTAIOUH IS
KELH AFLEEAYUE, AOC I FIKE HRD UEAKE TR UIVE NIP. HRD NAKE UIVEC PAOH A
STDWICEL WELSRO.”

“CEAL UIJJH!”

“RN, HRD ALE A FLEAT CEAU TRR AWT, HRD VORG, TR UIVE WERWUE IO FEOELAU.
HRD OEKEL SEE A BADUT IO AOHYRCH. AUU TNE GRLUC ALE FRRC AOC AFLEEAYUE
IO HRDL EHES. I OEKEL NEALC HRD SWEAV IUU RB A NDPAO YEIOF IO PH UIBE.”

“I GRDUC GISN ORT TR YE NASTH IO MEOSDLIOF AOHROE; YDT I AUGAHS SWEAV
GNAT I TNIOV.”

“I VORG HRD CR: AOC IT IS _TNAT_ GNIMN PAVES TNE GROCEL. GITN _HRDL_
FRRC SEOSE, TR YE SR NROESTUH YUIOC TR TNE BRUUIES AOC OROSEOSE RB
RTNELS! ABBEMTATIRO RB MAOCRDL IS MRPPRO EORDFN; ROE PEETS GITN IT
EKELHGNELE. YDT TR YE MAOCIC GITNRDT RSTEOTATIRO RL CESIFO,--TR TAVE TNE
FRRC RB EKELHYRCH’S MNALAMTEL AOC PAVE IT STIUU YETTEL, AOC SAH ORTNIOF
RB TNE YAC,--YEUROFS TR HRD AUROE. AOC SR, HRD UIVE TNIS PAO’S SISTELS,
TRR, CR HRD? TNEIL PAOOELS ALE ORT EQDAU TR NIS.”

“MELTAIOUH ORT, AT BILST; YDT TNEH ALE KELH WUEASIOF GRPEO GNEO HRD
MROKELSE GITN TNEP. PISS YIOFUEH IS TR UIKE GITN NEL YLRTNEL, AOC VEEW
NIS NRDSE; AOC I AP PDMN PISTAVEO IB GE SNAUU ORT BIOC A KELH MNALPIOF
OEIFNYRDL IO NEL.”

EUIJAYETN UISTEOEC IO SIUEOME, YDT GAS ORT MROKIOMEC: TNEIL YENAKIRDL AT
TNE ASSEPYUH NAC ORT YEEO MAUMDUATEC TR WUEASE IO FEOELAU; AOC GITN PRLE
QDIMVOESS RB RYSELKATIRO AOC UESS WUIAOMH RB TEPWEL TNAO NEL SISTEL, AOC
GITN A ZDCFPEOT, TRR, DOASSAIUEC YH AOH ATTEOTIRO TR NELSEUB, SNE GAS
KELH UITTUE CISWRSEC TR AWWLRKE TNEP. TNEH GELE, IO BAMT, KELH BIOE
UACIES; ORT CEBIMIEOT IO FRRC-NDPRDL GNEO TNEH GELE WUEASEC, ORL IO TNE
WRGEL RB YEIOF AFLEEAYUE GNELE TNEH MNRSE IT; YDT WLRDC AOC MROMEITEC.
TNEH GELE LATNEL NAOCSRPE; NAC YEEO ECDMATEC IO ROE RB TNE BILST WLIKATE
SEPIOALIES IO TRGO; NAC A BRLTDOE RB TGEOTH TNRDSAOC WRDOCS; GELE IO TNE
NAYIT RB SWEOCIOF PRLE TNAO TNEH RDFNT, AOC RB ASSRMIATIOF GITN WERWUE
RB LAOV; AOC GELE, TNELEBRLE, IO EKELH LESWEMT EOTITUEC TR TNIOV GEUU RB
TNEPSEUKES AOC PEAOUH RB RTNELS. TNEH GELE RB A LESWEMTAYUE BAPIUH IO
TNE ORLTN RB EOFUAOC; A MILMDPSTAOME PRLE CEEWUH IPWLESSEC RO TNEIL
PEPRLIES TNAO TNAT TNEIL YLRTNEL’S BRLTDOE AOC TNEIL RGO NAC YEEO
AMQDILEC YH TLACE.

PL. YIOFUEH IONELITEC WLRWELTH TR TNE APRDOT RB OEALUH A NDOCLEC
TNRDSAOC WRDOCS BLRP NIS BATNEL, GNR NAC IOTEOCEC TR WDLMNASE AO ESTATE,
YDT CIC ORT UIKE TR CR IT. PL. YIOFUEH IOTEOCEC IT UIVEGISE, AOC
SRPETIPES PACE MNRIME RB NIS MRDOTH; YDT, AS NE GAS ORG WLRKICEC GITN A
FRRC NRDSE AOC TNE UIYELTH RB A PAORL, IT GAS CRDYTBDU TR PAOH RB TNRSE
GNR YEST VOEG TNE EASIOESS RB NIS TEPWEL, GNETNEL NE PIFNT ORT SWEOC TNE
LEPAIOCEL RB NIS CAHS AT OETNELBIEUC, AOC UEAKE TNE OEXT FEOELATIRO TR
WDLMNASE.

NIS SISTELS GELE KELH AOXIRDS BRL NIS NAKIOF AO ESTATE RB NIS RGO; YDT
TNRDFN NE GAS ORG ESTAYUISNEC ROUH AS A TEOAOT, PISS YIOFUEH GAS YH OR
PEAOS DOGIUUIOF TR WLESICE AT NIS TAYUE; ORL GAS PLS. NDLST, GNR NAC
PALLIEC A PAO RB PRLE BASNIRO TNAO BRLTDOE, UESS CISWRSEC TR MROSICEL
NIS NRDSE AS NEL NRPE GNEO IT SDITEC NEL. PL. YIOFUEH NAC ORT YEEO RB
AFE TGR HEALS GNEO NE GAS TEPWTEC, YH AO AMMICEOTAU LEMRPPEOCATIRO, TR
URRV AT OETNELBIEUC NRDSE. NE CIC URRV AT IT, AOC IOTR IT, BRL NAUB AO
NRDL; GAS WUEASEC GITN TNE SITDATIRO AOC TNE WLIOMIWAU LRRPS, SATISBIEC
GITN GNAT TNE RGOEL SAIC IO ITS WLAISE, AOC TRRV IT IPPECIATEUH.

YETGEEO NIP AOC CALMH TNELE GAS A KELH STEACH BLIEOCSNIW, IO SWITE RB A
FLEAT RWWRSITIRO RB MNALAMTEL. YIOFUEH GAS EOCEALEC TR CALMH YH TNE
EASIOESS, RWEOOESS, AOC CDMTIUITH RB NIS TEPWEL, TNRDFN OR CISWRSITIRO
MRDUC RBBEL A FLEATEL MROTLAST TR NIS RGO, AOC TNRDFN GITN NIS RGO NE
OEKEL AWWEALEC CISSATISBIEC. RO TNE STLEOFTN RB CALMH’S LEFALC, YIOFUEH
NAC TNE BILPEST LEUIAOME, AOC RB NIS ZDCFPEOT TNE NIFNEST RWIOIRO. IO
DOCELSTAOCIOF, CALMH GAS TNE SDWELIRL. YIOFUEH GAS YH OR PEAOS
CEBIMIEOT; YDT CALMH GAS MUEKEL. NE GAS AT TNE SAPE TIPE NADFNTH,
LESELKEC, AOC BASTICIRDS; AOC NIS PAOOELS, TNRDFN GEUU YLEC, GELE ORT
IOKITIOF. IO TNAT LESWEMT NIS BLIEOC NAC FLEATUH TNE ACKAOTAFE. YIOFUEH
GAS SDLE RB YEIOF UIVEC GNELEKEL NE AWWEALEC; CALMH GAS MROTIODAUUH
FIKIOF RBBEOME.

TNE PAOOEL IO GNIMN TNEH SWRVE RB TNE PELHTRO ASSEPYUH GAS SDBBIMIEOTUH
MNALAMTELISTIM. YIOFUEH NAC OEKEL PET GITN WUEASAOTEL WERWUE RL WLETTIEL
FILUS IO NIS UIBE; EKELHYRCH NAC YEEO PRST VIOC AOC ATTEOTIKE TR NIP;
TNELE NAC YEEO OR BRLPAUITH, OR STIBBOESS; NE NAC SRRO BEUT AMQDAIOTEC
GITN AUU TNE LRRP; AOC AS TR PISS YEOOET, NE MRDUC ORT MROMEIKE AO AOFEU
PRLE YEADTIBDU. CALMH, RO TNE MROTLALH, NAC SEEO A MRUUEMTIRO RB WERWUE
IO GNRP TNELE GAS UITTUE YEADTH AOC OR BASNIRO, BRL OROE RB GNRP NE NAC
BEUT TNE SPAUUEST IOTELEST, AOC BLRP OROE LEMEIKEC EITNEL ATTEOTIRO RL
WUEASDLE. PISS YEOOET NE AMVORGUECFEC TR YE WLETTH; YDT SNE SPIUEC TRR
PDMN.

PLS. NDLST AOC NEL SISTEL AUURGEC IT TR YE SR; YDT STIUU TNEH ACPILEC
NEL AOC UIVEC NEL, AOC WLRORDOMEC NEL TR YE A SGEET FILU, AOC ROE GNRP
TNEH SNRDUC ORT RYZEMT TR VORG PRLE RB. PISS YEOOET GAS TNELEBRLE
ESTAYUISNEC AS A SGEET FILU; AOC TNEIL YLRTNEL BEUT ADTNRLIJEC YH SDMN
MRPPEOCATIRO TR TNIOV RB NEL AS NE MNRSE.

MNAWTEL K.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

GITNIO A SNRLT GAUV RB UROFYRDLO UIKEC A BAPIUH GITN GNRP TNE YEOOETS
GELE WALTIMDUALUH IOTIPATE. SIL GIUUIAP UDMAS NAC YEEO BRLPELUH IO TLACE
IO PELHTRO, GNELE NE NAC PACE A TRUELAYUE BRLTDOE, AOC LISEO TR TNE
NRORDL RB VOIFNTNRRC YH AO ACCLESS TR TNE VIOF CDLIOF NIS PAHRLAUTH. TNE
CISTIOMTIRO NAC, WELNAWS, YEEO BEUT TRR STLROFUH. IT NAC FIKEO NIP A
CISFDST TR NIS YDSIOESS AOC TR NIS LESICEOME IO A SPAUU PALVET TRGO;
AOC, QDITTIOF TNEP YRTN, NE NAC LEPRKEC GITN NIS BAPIUH TR A NRDSE AYRDT
A PIUE BLRP PELHTRO, CEORPIOATEC BLRP TNAT WELIRC UDMAS URCFE; GNELE NE
MRDUC TNIOV GITN WUEASDLE RB NIS RGO IPWRLTAOME, AOC, DOSNAMVUEC YH
YDSIOESS, RMMDWH NIPSEUB SRUEUH IO YEIOF MIKIU TR AUU TNE GRLUC. BRL,
TNRDFN EUATEC YH NIS LAOV, IT CIC ORT LEOCEL NIP SDWELMIUIRDS; RO TNE
MROTLALH, NE GAS AUU ATTEOTIRO TR EKELHYRCH. YH OATDLE IORBBEOSIKE,
BLIEOCUH, AOC RYUIFIOF, NIS WLESEOTATIRO AT ST. ZAPES’S NAC PACE NIP
MRDLTERDS.

UACH UDMAS GAS A KELH FRRC VIOC RB GRPAO, ORT TRR MUEKEL TR YE A
KAUDAYUE OEIFNYRDL TR PLS. YEOOET. TNEH NAC SEKELAU MNIUCLEO. TNE EUCEST
RB TNEP, A SEOSIYUE, IOTEUUIFEOT HRDOF GRPAO, AYRDT TGEOTH-SEKEO, GAS
EUIJAYETN’S IOTIPATE BLIEOC.

TNAT TNE PISS UDMASES AOC TNE PISS YEOOETS SNRDUC PEET TR TAUV RKEL A
YAUU GAS AYSRUDTEUH OEMESSALH; AOC TNE PRLOIOF ABTEL TNE ASSEPYUH
YLRDFNT TNE BRLPEL TR UROFYRDLO TR NEAL AOC TR MRPPDOIMATE.

“_HRD_ YEFAO TNE EKEOIOF GEUU, MNALURTTE,” SAIC PLS. YEOOET, GITN MIKIU
SEUB-MRPPAOC, TR PISS UDMAS. “_HRD_ GELE PL. YIOFUEH’S BILST MNRIME.”

“HES; YDT NE SEEPEC TR UIVE NIS SEMROC YETTEL.”

“RN, HRD PEAO ZAOE, I SDWWRSE, YEMADSE NE CAOMEC GITN NEL TGIME. TR YE
SDLE TNAT _CIC_ SEEP AS IB NE ACPILEC NEL--IOCEEC, I LATNEL YEUIEKE NE
_CIC_--I NEALC SRPETNIOF AYRDT IT--YDT I NALCUH VORG GNAT--SRPETNIOF
AYRDT PL. LRYIOSRO.”

“WELNAWS HRD PEAO GNAT I RKELNEALC YETGEEO NIP AOC PL. LRYIOSRO: CIC ORT
I PEOTIRO IT TR HRD? PL. LRYIOSRO’S ASVIOF NIP NRG NE UIVEC RDL PELHTRO
ASSEPYUIES, AOC GNETNEL NE CIC ORT TNIOV TNELE GELE A FLEAT PAOH WLETTH
GRPEO IO TNE LRRP, AOC _GNIMN_ NE TNRDFNT TNE WLETTIEST? AOC NIS
AOSGELIOF IPPECIATEUH TR TNE UAST QDESTIRO, ‘RN, TNE EUCEST PISS YEOOET,
YEHROC A CRDYT: TNELE MAOORT YE TGR RWIOIROS RO TNAT WRIOT.’”

“DWRO PH GRLC! GEUU, TNAT GAS KELH CEMICEC, IOCEEC--TNAT CRES SEEP AS
IB--YDT, NRGEKEL, IT PAH AUU MRPE TR ORTNIOF, HRD VORG.”

“_PH_ RKELNEALIOFS GELE PRLE TR TNE WDLWRSE TNAO _HRDLS_, EUIJA,” SAIC
MNALURTTE. “PL. CALMH IS ORT SR GEUU GRLTN UISTEOIOF TR AS NIS BLIEOC,
IS NE? WRRL EUIJA! TR YE ROUH ZDST _TRUELAYUE_.”

“I YEF HRD GIUU ORT WDT IT IOTR UIJJH’S NEAC TR YE KEXEC YH NIS
IUU-TLEATPEOT, BRL NE IS SDMN A CISAFLEEAYUE PAO TNAT IT GRDUC YE QDITE
A PISBRLTDOE TR YE UIVEC YH NIP. PLS. UROF TRUC PE UAST OIFNT TNAT NE
SAT MURSE TR NEL BRL NAUB AO NRDL GITNRDT ROME RWEOIOF NIS UIWS.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO: “GITNRDT ROME RWEOIOF NIS UIWS”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

“ALE HRD QDITE SDLE, PA’AP? IS ORT TNELE A UITTUE PISTAVE?” SAIC ZAOE.
“I MELTAIOUH SAG PL. CALMH SWEAVIOF TR NEL.”

“AH, YEMADSE SNE ASVEC NIP AT UAST NRG NE UIVEC OETNELBIEUC, AOC NE
MRDUC ORT NEUW AOSGELIOF NEL; YDT SNE SAIC NE SEEPEC KELH AOFLH AT YEIOF
SWRVE TR.”

“PISS YIOFUEH TRUC PE,” SAIC ZAOE, “TNAT NE OEKEL SWEAVS PDMN DOUESS
APROF NIS IOTIPATE AMQDAIOTAOME. GITN _TNEP_ NE IS LEPALVAYUH
AFLEEAYUE.”

“I CR ORT YEUIEKE A GRLC RB IT, PH CEAL. IB NE NAC YEEO SR KELH
AFLEEAYUE, NE GRDUC NAKE TAUVEC TR PLS. UROF. YDT I MAO FDESS NRG IT
GAS; EKELHYRCH SAHS TNAT NE IS EAT DW GITN WLICE, AOC I CALE SAH NE NAC
NEALC SRPENRG TNAT PLS. UROF CRES ORT VEEW A MALLIAFE, AOC NAC TR MRPE
TR TNE YAUU IO A NAMV MNAISE.”

“I CR ORT PIOC NIS ORT TAUVIOF TR PLS. UROF,” SAIC PISS UDMAS, “YDT I
GISN NE NAC CAOMEC GITN EUIJA.”

“AORTNEL TIPE, UIJJH,” SAIC NEL PRTNEL, “I GRDUC ORT CAOME GITN _NIP_,
IB I GELE HRD.”

“I YEUIEKE, PA’AP, I PAH SABEUH WLRPISE HRD _OEKEL_ TR CAOME GITN NIP.”

“NIS WLICE,” SAIC PISS UDMAS, “CRES ORT RBBEOC _PE_ SR PDMN AS WLICE
RBTEO CRES, YEMADSE TNELE IS AO EXMDSE BRL IT. ROE MAOORT GROCEL TNAT SR
KELH BIOE A HRDOF PAO, GITN BAPIUH, BRLTDOE, EKELHTNIOF IO NIS BAKRDL,
SNRDUC TNIOV NIFNUH RB NIPSEUB. IB I PAH SR EXWLESS IT, NE NAS A _LIFNT_
TR YE WLRDC.”

“TNAT IS KELH TLDE,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN, “AOC I MRDUC EASIUH BRLFIKE
_NIS_ WLICE, IB NE NAC ORT PRLTIBIEC _PIOE_.”

“WLICE,” RYSELKEC PALH, GNR WIQDEC NELSEUB DWRO TNE SRUICITH RB NEL
LEBUEMTIROS, “IS A KELH MRPPRO BAIUIOF, I YEUIEKE. YH AUU TNAT I NAKE
EKEL LEAC, I AP MROKIOMEC TNAT IT IS KELH MRPPRO IOCEEC; TNAT NDPAO
OATDLE IS WALTIMDUALUH WLROE TR IT, AOC TNAT TNELE ALE KELH BEG RB DS
GNR CR ORT MNELISN A BEEUIOF RB SEUB-MRPWUAMEOMH RO TNE SMRLE RB SRPE
QDAUITH RL RTNEL, LEAU RL IPAFIOALH. KAOITH AOC WLICE ALE CIBBELEOT
TNIOFS, TNRDFN TNE GRLCS ALE RBTEO DSEC SHOROHPRDSUH. A WELSRO PAH YE
WLRDC GITNRDT YEIOF KAIO. WLICE LEUATES PRLE TR RDL RWIOIRO RB
RDLSEUKES; KAOITH TR GNAT GE GRDUC NAKE RTNELS TNIOV RB DS.”

“IB I GELE AS LIMN AS PL. CALMH,” MLIEC A HRDOF UDMAS, GNR MAPE GITN NIS
SISTELS, “I SNRDUC ORT MALE NRG WLRDC I GAS. I GRDUC VEEW A WAMV RB
BRXNRDOCS, AOC CLIOV A YRTTUE RB GIOE EKELH CAH.”

“TNEO HRD GRDUC CLIOV A FLEAT CEAU PRLE TNAO HRD RDFNT,” SAIC PLS.
YEOOET; “AOC IB I GELE TR SEE HRD AT IT, I SNRDUC TAVE AGAH HRDL YRTTUE
CILEMTUH.”

TNE YRH WLRTESTEC TNAT SNE SNRDUC ORT; SNE MROTIODEC TR CEMUALE TNAT SNE
GRDUC; AOC TNE ALFDPEOT EOCEC ROUH GITN TNE KISIT.

[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL KI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TNE UACIES RB UROFYRDLO SRRO GAITEC RO TNRSE RB OETNELBIEUC. TNE KISIT
GAS LETDLOEC IO CDE BRLP. PISS YEOOET’S WUEASIOF PAOOELS FLEG RO TNE
FRRC-GIUU RB PLS. NDLST AOC PISS YIOFUEH; AOC TNRDFN TNE PRTNEL GAS
BRDOC TR YE IOTRUELAYUE, AOC TNE HRDOFEL SISTELS ORT GRLTN SWEAVIOF TR,
A GISN RB YEIOF YETTEL AMQDAIOTEC GITN _TNEP_ GAS EXWLESSEC TRGALCS TNE
TGR EUCEST. YH ZAOE TNIS ATTEOTIRO GAS LEMEIKEC GITN TNE FLEATEST
WUEASDLE; YDT EUIJAYETN STIUU SAG SDWELMIUIRDSOESS IO TNEIL TLEATPEOT RB
EKELHYRCH, NALCUH EXMEWTIOF EKEO NEL SISTEL, AOC MRDUC ORT UIVE TNEP;
TNRDFN TNEIL VIOCOESS TR ZAOE, SDMN AS IT GAS, NAC A KAUDE, AS ALISIOF,
IO AUU WLRYAYIUITH, BLRP TNE IOBUDEOME RB TNEIL YLRTNEL’S ACPILATIRO. IT
GAS FEOELAUUH EKICEOT, GNEOEKEL TNEH PET, TNAT NE _CIC_ ACPILE NEL; AOC
TR _NEL_ IT GAS EQDAUUH EKICEOT TNAT ZAOE GAS HIEUCIOF TR TNE WLEBELEOME
GNIMN SNE NAC YEFDO TR EOTELTAIO BRL NIP BLRP TNE BILST, AOC GAS IO A
GAH TR YE KELH PDMN IO URKE; YDT SNE MROSICELEC GITN WUEASDLE TNAT IT
GAS ORT UIVEUH TR YE CISMRKELEC YH TNE GRLUC IO FEOELAU, SIOME ZAOE
DOITEC GITN FLEAT STLEOFTN RB BEEUIOF, A MRPWRSDLE RB TEPWEL AOC AO
DOIBRLP MNEELBDUOESS RB PAOOEL, GNIMN GRDUC FDALC NEL BLRP TNE
SDSWIMIROS RB TNE IPWELTIOEOT. SNE PEOTIROEC TNIS TR NEL BLIEOC, PISS
UDMAS.

“IT PAH, WELNAWS, YE WUEASAOT,” LEWUIEC MNALURTTE, “TR YE AYUE TR IPWRSE
RO TNE WDYUIM IO SDMN A MASE; YDT IT IS SRPETIPES A CISACKAOTAFE TR YE
SR KELH FDALCEC. IB A GRPAO MROMEAUS NEL ABBEMTIRO GITN TNE SAPE SVIUU
BLRP TNE RYZEMT RB IT, SNE PAH URSE TNE RWWRLTDOITH RB BIXIOF NIP; AOC
IT GIUU TNEO YE YDT WRRL MROSRUATIRO TR YEUIEKE TNE GRLUC EQDAUUH IO TNE
CALV. TNELE IS SR PDMN RB FLATITDCE RL KAOITH IO AUPRST EKELH
ATTAMNPEOT, TNAT IT IS ORT SABE TR UEAKE AOH TR ITSEUB. GE MAO AUU
_YEFIO_ BLEEUH--A SUIFNT WLEBELEOME IS OATDLAU EORDFN; YDT TNELE ALE
KELH BEG RB DS GNR NAKE NEALT EORDFN TR YE LEAUUH IO URKE GITNRDT
EOMRDLAFEPEOT. IO OIOE MASES RDT RB TEO, A GRPAO NAC YETTEL SNRG _PRLE_
ABBEMTIRO TNAO SNE BEEUS. YIOFUEH UIVES HRDL SISTEL DOCRDYTECUH; YDT NE
PAH OEKEL CR PRLE TNAO UIVE NEL, IB SNE CRES ORT NEUW NIP RO.”

“YDT SNE CRES NEUW NIP RO, AS PDMN AS NEL OATDLE GIUU AUURG. IB _I_ MAO
WELMEIKE NEL LEFALC BRL NIP, NE PDST YE A SIPWUETRO IOCEEC ORT TR
CISMRKEL IT TRR.”

“LEPEPYEL, EUIJA, TNAT NE CRES ORT VORG ZAOE’S CISWRSITIRO AS HRD CR.”

“YDT IB A GRPAO IS WALTIAU TR A PAO, AOC CRES ORT EOCEAKRL TR MROMEAU
IT, NE PDST BIOC IT RDT.”

“WELNAWS NE PDST, IB NE SEES EORDFN RB NEL. YDT TNRDFN YIOFUEH AOC ZAOE
PEET TRUELAYUH RBTEO, IT IS OEKEL BRL PAOH NRDLS TRFETNEL; AOC AS TNEH
AUGAHS SEE EAMN RTNEL IO UALFE PIXEC WALTIES, IT IS IPWRSSIYUE TNAT
EKELH PRPEOT SNRDUC YE EPWURHEC IO MROKELSIOF TRFETNEL. ZAOE SNRDUC
TNELEBRLE PAVE TNE PRST RB EKELH NAUB NRDL IO GNIMN SNE MAO MRPPAOC NIS
ATTEOTIRO. GNEO SNE IS SEMDLE RB NIP, TNELE GIUU YE UEISDLE BRL BAUUIOF
IO URKE AS PDMN AS SNE MNRRSES.”

“HRDL WUAO IS A FRRC ROE,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN, “GNELE ORTNIOF IS IO
QDESTIRO YDT TNE CESILE RB YEIOF GEUU PALLIEC; AOC IB I GELE CETELPIOEC
TR FET A LIMN NDSYAOC, RL AOH NDSYAOC, I CALE SAH I SNRDUC ACRWT IT. YDT
TNESE ALE ORT ZAOE’S BEEUIOFS; SNE IS ORT AMTIOF YH CESIFO. AS HET SNE
MAOORT EKEO YE MELTAIO RB TNE CEFLEE RB NEL RGO LEFALC, ORL RB ITS
LEASROAYUEOESS. SNE NAS VORGO NIP ROUH A BRLTOIFNT. SNE CAOMEC BRDL
CAOMES GITN NIP AT PELHTRO; SNE SAG NIP ROE PRLOIOF AT NIS RGO NRDSE,
AOC NAS SIOME CIOEC IO MRPWAOH GITN NIP BRDL TIPES. TNIS IS ORT QDITE
EORDFN TR PAVE NEL DOCELSTAOC NIS MNALAMTEL.”

“ORT AS HRD LEWLESEOT IT. NAC SNE PELEUH _CIOEC_ GITN NIP, SNE PIFNT
ROUH NAKE CISMRKELEC GNETNEL NE NAC A FRRC AWWETITE; YDT HRD PDST
LEPEPYEL TNAT BRDL EKEOIOFS NAKE YEEO AUSR SWEOT TRFETNEL--AOC BRDL
EKEOIOFS PAH CR A FLEAT CEAU.”

“HES: TNESE BRDL EKEOIOFS NAKE EOAYUEC TNEP TR ASMELTAIO TNAT TNEH YRTN
UIVE KIOFT-DO YETTEL TNAO MRPPELME, YDT GITN LESWEMT TR AOH RTNEL
UEACIOF MNALAMTELISTIM, I CR ORT IPAFIOE TNAT PDMN NAS YEEO DOBRUCEC.”

“GEUU,” SAIC MNALURTTE, “I GISN ZAOE SDMMESS GITN AUU PH NEALT; AOC IB
SNE GELE PALLIEC TR NIP TR-PRLLRG, I SNRDUC TNIOV SNE NAC AS FRRC A
MNAOME RB NAWWIOESS AS IB SNE GELE TR YE STDCHIOF NIS MNALAMTEL BRL A
TGEUKEPROTN. NAWWIOESS IO PALLIAFE IS EOTILEUH A PATTEL RB MNAOME. IB
TNE CISWRSITIROS RB TNE WALTIES ALE EKEL SR GEUU VORGO TR EAMN RTNEL, RL
EKEL SR SIPIUAL YEBRLENAOC, IT CRES ORT ACKAOME TNEIL BEUIMITH IO TNE
UEAST. TNEH AUGAHS MROTIODE TR FLRG SDBBIMIEOTUH DOUIVE ABTELGALCS TR
NAKE TNEIL SNALE RB KEXATIRO; AOC IT IS YETTEL TR VORG AS UITTUE AS
WRSSIYUE RB TNE CEBEMTS RB TNE WELSRO GITN GNRP HRD ALE TR WASS HRDL
UIBE.”

“HRD PAVE PE UADFN, MNALURTTE; YDT IT IS ORT SRDOC. HRD VORG IT IS ORT
SRDOC, AOC TNAT HRD GRDUC OEKEL AMT IO TNIS GAH HRDLSEUB.”

RMMDWIEC IO RYSELKIOF PL. YIOFUEH’S ATTEOTIRO TR NEL SISTEL, EUIJAYETN
GAS BAL BLRP SDSWEMTIOF TNAT SNE GAS NELSEUB YEMRPIOF AO RYZEMT RB SRPE
IOTELEST IO TNE EHES RB NIS BLIEOC. PL. CALMH NAC AT BILST SMALMEUH
AUURGEC NEL TR YE WLETTH: NE NAC URRVEC AT NEL GITNRDT ACPILATIRO AT TNE
YAUU; AOC GNEO TNEH OEXT PET, NE URRVEC AT NEL ROUH TR MLITIMISE. YDT OR
SRROEL NAC NE PACE IT MUEAL TR NIPSEUB AOC NIS BLIEOCS TNAT SNE NAC
NALCUH A FRRC BEATDLE IO NEL BAME, TNAO NE YEFAO TR BIOC IT GAS LEOCELEC
DOMRPPROUH IOTEUUIFEOT YH TNE YEADTIBDU EXWLESSIRO RB NEL CALV EHES. TR
TNIS CISMRKELH SDMMEECEC SRPE RTNELS EQDAUUH PRLTIBHIOF. TNRDFN NE NAC
CETEMTEC GITN A MLITIMAU EHE PRLE TNAO ROE BAIUDLE RB WELBEMT SHPPETLH
IO NEL BRLP, NE GAS BRLMEC TR AMVORGUECFE NEL BIFDLE TR YE UIFNT AOC
WUEASIOF; AOC IO SWITE RB NIS ASSELTIOF TNAT NEL PAOOELS GELE ORT TNRSE
RB TNE BASNIROAYUE GRLUC, NE GAS MADFNT YH TNEIL EASH WUAHBDUOESS. RB
TNIS SNE GAS WELBEMTUH DOAGALE: TR NEL NE GAS ROUH TNE PAO GNR PACE
NIPSEUB AFLEEAYUE ORGNELE, AOC GNR NAC ORT TNRDFNT NEL NAOCSRPE EORDFN
TR CAOME GITN.

NE YEFAO TR GISN TR VORG PRLE RB NEL; AOC, AS A STEW TRGALCS MROKELSIOF
GITN NEL NIPSEUB, ATTEOCEC TR NEL MROKELSATIRO GITN RTNELS. NIS CRIOF SR
CLEG NEL ORTIME. IT GAS AT SIL GIUUIAP UDMAS’S, GNELE A UALFE WALTH GELE
ASSEPYUEC.

“GNAT CRES PL. CALMH PEAO,” SAIC SNE TR MNALURTTE, “YH UISTEOIOF TR PH
MROKELSATIRO GITN MRUROEU BRLSTEL?”

“TNAT IS A QDESTIRO GNIMN PL. CALMH ROUH MAO AOSGEL.”

“YDT IB NE CRES IT AOH PRLE, I SNAUU MELTAIOUH UET NIP VORG TNAT I SEE
GNAT NE IS AYRDT. NE NAS A KELH SATILIMAU EHE, AOC IB I CR ORT YEFIO YH
YEIOF IPWELTIOEOT PHSEUB, I SNAUU SRRO FLRG ABLAIC RB NIP.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO: “TNE EOTLEATIES RB SEKELAU” [_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE
AUUEO._]]

RO NIS AWWLRAMNIOF TNEP SRRO ABTELGALCS, TNRDFN GITNRDT SEEPIOF TR NAKE
AOH IOTEOTIRO RB SWEAVIOF, PISS UDMAS CEBIEC NEL BLIEOC TR PEOTIRO SDMN
A SDYZEMT TR NIP, GNIMN IPPECIATEUH WLRKRVIOF EUIJAYETN TR CR IT, SNE
TDLOEC TR NIP AOC SAIC,--

“CIC ORT HRD TNIOV, PL. CALMH, TNAT I EXWLESSEC PHSEUB DOMRPPROUH GEUU
ZDST ORG, GNEO I GAS TEASIOF MRUROEU BRLSTEL TR FIKE DS A YAUU AT
PELHTRO?”

“GITN FLEAT EOELFH; YDT IT IS A SDYZEMT GNIMN AUGAHS PAVES A UACH
EOELFETIM.”

“HRD ALE SEKELE RO DS.”

“IT GIUU YE _NEL_ TDLO SRRO TR YE TEASEC,” SAIC PISS UDMAS. “I AP FRIOF
TR RWEO TNE IOSTLDPEOT, EUIJA, AOC HRD VORG GNAT BRUURGS.”

“HRD ALE A KELH STLAOFE MLEATDLE YH GAH RB A BLIEOC!--AUGAHS GAOTIOF PE
TR WUAH AOC SIOF YEBRLE AOHYRCH AOC EKELHYRCH! IB PH KAOITH NAC TAVEO A
PDSIMAU TDLO, HRD GRDUC NAKE YEEO IOKAUDAYUE; YDT AS IT IS, I GRDUC
LEAUUH LATNEL ORT SIT CRGO YEBRLE TNRSE GNR PDST YE IO TNE NAYIT RB
NEALIOF TNE KELH YEST WELBRLPELS.” RO PISS UDMAS’S WELSEKELIOF, NRGEKEL,
SNE ACCEC, “KELH GEUU; IB IT PDST YE SR, IT PDST.” AOC FLAKEUH FUAOMIOF
AT PL. CALMH, “TNELE IS A KELH BIOE RUC SAHIOF, GNIMN EKELHYRCH NELE IS
RB MRDLSE BAPIUIAL GITN--‘VEEW HRDL YLEATN TR MRRU HRDL WRLLICFE,’--AOC
I SNAUU VEEW PIOE TR SGEUU PH SROF.”

NEL WELBRLPAOME GAS WUEASIOF, TNRDFN YH OR PEAOS MAWITAU. ABTEL A SROF
RL TGR, AOC YEBRLE SNE MRDUC LEWUH TR TNE EOTLEATIES RB SEKELAU TNAT SNE
GRDUC SIOF AFAIO, SNE GAS EAFELUH SDMMEECEC AT TNE IOSTLDPEOT YH NEL
SISTEL PALH, GNR NAKIOF, IO MROSEQDEOME RB YEIOF TNE ROUH WUAIO ROE IO
TNE BAPIUH, GRLVEC NALC BRL VORGUECFE AOC AMMRPWUISNPEOTS, GAS AUGAHS
IPWATIEOT BRL CISWUAH.

PALH NAC OEITNEL FEOIDS ORL TASTE; AOC TNRDFN KAOITH NAC FIKEO NEL
AWWUIMATIRO, IT NAC FIKEO NEL UIVEGISE A WECAOTIM AIL AOC MROMEITEC
PAOOEL, GNIMN GRDUC NAKE IOZDLEC A NIFNEL CEFLEE RB EXMEUUEOME TNAO SNE
NAC LEAMNEC. EUIJAYETN, EASH AOC DOABBEMTEC, NAC YEEO UISTEOEC TR GITN
PDMN PRLE WUEASDLE, TNRDFN ORT WUAHIOF NAUB SR GEUU; AOC PALH, AT TNE
EOC RB A UROF MROMELTR, GAS FUAC TR WDLMNASE WLAISE AOC FLATITDCE YH
SMRTMN AOC ILISN AILS, AT TNE LEQDEST RB NEL HRDOFEL SISTELS, GNR GITN
SRPE RB TNE UDMASES, AOC TGR RL TNLEE RBBIMELS, ZRIOEC EAFELUH IO
CAOMIOF AT ROE EOC RB TNE LRRP.

PL. CALMH STRRC OEAL TNEP IO SIUEOT IOCIFOATIRO AT SDMN A PRCE RB
WASSIOF TNE EKEOIOF, TR TNE EXMUDSIRO RB AUU MROKELSATIRO, AOC GAS TRR
PDMN EOFLRSSEC YH NIS RGO TNRDFNTS TR WELMEIKE TNAT SIL GIUUIAP UDMAS
GAS NIS OEIFNYRDL, TIUU SIL GIUUIAP TNDS YEFAO:--

“GNAT A MNALPIOF APDSEPEOT BRL HRDOF WERWUE TNIS IS, PL. CALMH! TNELE IS
ORTNIOF UIVE CAOMIOF, ABTEL AUU. I MROSICEL IT AS ROE RB TNE BILST
LEBIOEPEOTS RB WRUISNEC SRMIETIES.”

“MELTAIOUH, SIL; AOC IT NAS TNE ACKAOTAFE AUSR RB YEIOF IO KRFDE APROFST
TNE UESS WRUISNEC SRMIETIES RB TNE GRLUC: EKELH SAKAFE MAO CAOME.”

SIL GIUUIAP ROUH SPIUEC. “HRDL BLIEOC WELBRLPS CEUIFNTBDUUH,” NE
MROTIODEC, ABTEL A WADSE, RO SEEIOF YIOFUEH ZRIO TNE FLRDW; “AOC I CRDYT
ORT TNAT HRD ALE AO ACEWT IO TNE SMIEOME HRDLSEUB, PL. CALMH.”

“HRD SAG PE CAOME AT PELHTRO, I YEUIEKE, SIL.”

“HES, IOCEEC, AOC LEMEIKEC OR IOMROSICELAYUE WUEASDLE BLRP TNE SIFNT. CR
HRD RBTEO CAOME AT ST. ZAPES’S?”

“OEKEL, SIL.”

“CR HRD ORT TNIOV IT GRDUC YE A WLRWEL MRPWUIPEOT TR TNE WUAME?”

“IT IS A MRPWUIPEOT GNIMN I OEKEL WAH TR AOH WUAME IB I MAO AKRIC IT.”

“HRD NAKE A NRDSE IO TRGO, I MROMUDCE?”

PL. CALMH YRGEC.

“I NAC ROME SRPE TNRDFNTS RB BIXIOF IO TRGO PHSEUB, BRL I AP BROC RB
SDWELIRL SRMIETH; YDT I CIC ORT BEEU QDITE MELTAIO TNAT TNE AIL RB
UROCRO GRDUC AFLEE GITN UACH UDMAS.”

NE WADSEC IO NRWES RB AO AOSGEL: YDT NIS MRPWAOIRO GAS ORT CISWRSEC TR
PAVE AOH; AOC EUIJAYETN AT TNAT IOSTAOT PRKIOF TRGALCS TNEP, NE GAS
STLDMV GITN TNE ORTIRO RB CRIOF A KELH FAUUAOT TNIOF, AOC MAUUEC RDT TR
NEL,--

“PH CEAL PISS EUIJA, GNH ALE ORT HRD CAOMIOF? PL. CALMH, HRD PDST AUURG
PE TR WLESEOT TNIS HRDOF UACH TR HRD AS A KELH CESILAYUE WALTOEL. HRD
MAOORT LEBDSE TR CAOME, I AP SDLE, GNEO SR PDMN YEADTH IS YEBRLE HRD.”
AOC, TAVIOF NEL NAOC, NE GRDUC NAKE FIKEO IT TR PL. CALMH, GNR, TNRDFN
EXTLEPEUH SDLWLISEC, GAS ORT DOGIUUIOF TR LEMEIKE IT, GNEO SNE IOSTAOTUH
CLEG YAMV, AOC SAIC GITN SRPE CISMRPWRSDLE TR SIL GIUUIAP,--

“IOCEEC, SIL, I NAKE ORT TNE UEAST IOTEOTIRO RB CAOMIOF. I EOTLEAT HRD
ORT TR SDWWRSE TNAT I PRKEC TNIS GAH IO RLCEL TR YEF BRL A WALTOEL.”

PL. CALMH, GITN FLAKE WLRWLIETH, LEQDESTEC TR YE AUURGEC TNE NRORDL RB
NEL NAOC, YDT IO KAIO. EUIJAYETN GAS CETELPIOEC; ORL CIC SIL GIUUIAP AT
AUU SNAVE NEL WDLWRSE YH NIS ATTEPWT AT WELSDASIRO.

“HRD EXMEU SR PDMN IO TNE CAOME, PISS EUIJA, TNAT IT IS MLDEU TR CEOH PE
TNE NAWWIOESS RB SEEIOF HRD; AOC TNRDFN TNIS FEOTUEPAO CISUIVES TNE
APDSEPEOT IO FEOELAU, NE MAO NAKE OR RYZEMTIRO, I AP SDLE, TR RYUIFE DS
BRL ROE NAUB NRDL.”

“PL. CALMH IS AUU WRUITEOESS,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, SPIUIOF.

“NE IS, IOCEEC: YDT MROSICELIOF TNE IOCDMEPEOT, PH CEAL PISS EUIJA, GE
MAOORT GROCEL AT NIS MRPWUAISAOME; BRL GNR GRDUC RYZEMT TR SDMN A
WALTOEL?”

EUIJAYETN URRVEC ALMNUH, AOC TDLOEC AGAH. NEL LESISTAOME NAC ORT IOZDLEC
NEL GITN TNE FEOTUEPAO, AOC NE GAS TNIOVIOF RB NEL GITN SRPE
MRPWUAMEOMH, GNEO TNDS AMMRSTEC YH PISS YIOFUEH,--

“I MAO FDESS TNE SDYZEMT RB HRDL LEKELIE.”

“I SNRDUC IPAFIOE ORT.”

“HRD ALE MROSICELIOF NRG IOSDWWRLTAYUE IT GRDUC YE TR WASS PAOH
EKEOIOFS IO TNIS PAOOEL,--IO SDMN SRMIETH; AOC, IOCEEC, I AP QDITE RB
HRDL RWIOIRO. I GAS OEKEL PRLE AOORHEC! TNE IOSIWICITH, AOC HET TNE
ORISE--TNE ORTNIOFOESS, AOC HET TNE SEUB-IPWRLTAOME, RB AUU TNESE
WERWUE! GNAT GRDUC I FIKE TR NEAL HRDL STLIMTDLES RO TNEP!”

“HRDL MROZEMTDLE IS TRTAUUH GLROF, I ASSDLE HRD. PH PIOC GAS PRLE
AFLEEAYUH EOFAFEC. I NAKE YEEO PECITATIOF RO TNE KELH FLEAT WUEASDLE
GNIMN A WAIL RB BIOE EHES IO TNE BAME RB A WLETTH GRPAO MAO YESTRG.”

PISS YIOFUEH IPPECIATEUH BIXEC NEL EHES RO NIS BAME, AOC CESILEC NE
GRDUC TEUU NEL GNAT UACH NAC TNE MLECIT RB IOSWILIOF SDMN LEBUEMTIROS.
PL. CALMH LEWUIEC, GITN FLEAT IOTLEWICITH,--

“PISS EUIJAYETN YEOOET.”

“PISS EUIJAYETN YEOOET!” LEWEATEC PISS YIOFUEH. “I AP AUU ASTROISNPEOT.
NRG UROF NAS SNE YEEO SDMN A BAKRDLITE? AOC WLAH GNEO AP I TR GISN HRD
ZRH?”

“TNAT IS EXAMTUH TNE QDESTIRO GNIMN I EXWEMTEC HRD TR ASV. A UACH’S
IPAFIOATIRO IS KELH LAWIC; IT ZDPWS BLRP ACPILATIRO TR URKE, BLRP URKE
TR PATLIPROH, IO A PRPEOT. I VOEG HRD GRDUC YE GISNIOF PE ZRH.”

“OAH, IB HRD ALE SR SELIRDS AYRDT IT, I SNAUU MROSICEL TNE PATTEL AS
AYSRUDTEUH SETTUEC. HRD GIUU NAKE A MNALPIOF PRTNEL-IO-UAG, IOCEEC, AOC
RB MRDLSE SNE GIUU YE AUGAHS AT WEPYELUEH GITN HRD.”

NE UISTEOEC TR NEL GITN WELBEMT IOCIBBELEOME, GNIUE SNE MNRSE TR
EOTELTAIO NELSEUB IO TNIS PAOOEL; AOC AS NIS MRPWRSDLE MROKIOMEC NEL
TNAT AUU GAS SABE, NEL GIT BURGEC AUROF.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “A ORTE BRL PISS YEOOET”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]




MNAWTEL KII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

PL. YEOOET’S WLRWELTH MROSISTEC AUPRST EOTILEUH IO AO ESTATE RB TGR
TNRDSAOC A HEAL, GNIMN, DOBRLTDOATEUH BRL NIS CADFNTELS, GAS EOTAIUEC,
IO CEBADUT RB NEILS PAUE, RO A CISTAOT LEUATIRO; AOC TNEIL PRTNEL’S
BRLTDOE, TNRDFN APWUE BRL NEL SITDATIRO IO UIBE, MRDUC YDT IUU SDWWUH
TNE CEBIMIEOMH RB NIS. NEL BATNEL NAC YEEO AO ATTRLOEH IO PELHTRO, AOC
NAC UEBT NEL BRDL TNRDSAOC WRDOCS.

SNE NAC A SISTEL PALLIEC TR A PL. WNIUIWS, GNR NAC YEEO A MUELV TR TNEIL
BATNEL AOC SDMMEECEC NIP IO TNE YDSIOESS, AOC A YLRTNEL SETTUEC IO
UROCRO IO A LESWEMTAYUE UIOE RB TLACE.

TNE KIUUAFE RB UROFYRDLO GAS ROUH ROE PIUE BLRP PELHTRO; A PRST
MROKEOIEOT CISTAOME BRL TNE HRDOF UACIES, GNR GELE DSDAUUH TEPWTEC
TNITNEL TNLEE RL BRDL TIPES A GEEV, TR WAH TNEIL CDTH TR TNEIL ADOT, AOC
TR A PIUUIOEL’S SNRW ZDST RKEL TNE GAH. TNE TGR HRDOFEST RB TNE BAPIUH,
MATNELIOE AOC UHCIA, GELE WALTIMDUALUH BLEQDEOT IO TNESE ATTEOTIROS:
TNEIL PIOCS GELE PRLE KAMAOT TNAO TNEIL SISTELS’, AOC GNEO ORTNIOF
YETTEL RBBELEC, A GAUV TR PELHTRO GAS OEMESSALH TR APDSE TNEIL PRLOIOF
NRDLS AOC BDLOISN MROKELSATIRO BRL TNE EKEOIOF; AOC, NRGEKEL YALE RB
OEGS TNE MRDOTLH IO FEOELAU PIFNT YE, TNEH AUGAHS MROTLIKEC TR UEALO
SRPE BLRP TNEIL ADOT. AT WLESEOT, IOCEEC, TNEH GELE GEUU SDWWUIEC YRTN
GITN OEGS AOC NAWWIOESS YH TNE LEMEOT ALLIKAU RB A PIUITIA LEFIPEOT IO
TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC; IT GAS TR LEPAIO TNE GNRUE GIOTEL, AOC PELHTRO GAS
TNE NEAC-QDALTELS.

TNEIL KISITS TR PLS. WNIUIWS GELE ORG WLRCDMTIKE RB TNE PRST IOTELESTIOF
IOTEUUIFEOME. EKELH CAH ACCEC SRPETNIOF TR TNEIL VORGUECFE RB TNE
RBBIMELS’ OAPES AOC MROOEMTIROS. TNEIL URCFIOFS GELE ORT UROF A SEMLET,
AOC AT UEOFTN TNEH YEFAO TR VORG TNE RBBIMELS TNEPSEUKES. PL. WNIUIWS
KISITEC TNEP AUU, AOC TNIS RWEOEC TR NIS OIEMES A SRDLME RB BEUIMITH
DOVORGO YEBRLE. TNEH MRDUC TAUV RB ORTNIOF YDT RBBIMELS; AOC PL.
YIOFUEH’S UALFE BRLTDOE, TNE PEOTIRO RB GNIMN FAKE AOIPATIRO TR TNEIL
PRTNEL, GAS GRLTNUESS IO TNEIL EHES GNEO RWWRSEC TR TNE LEFIPEOTAUS RB
AO EOSIFO.

ABTEL UISTEOIOF ROE PRLOIOF TR TNEIL EBBDSIROS RO TNIS SDYZEMT, PL.
YEOOET MRRUUH RYSELKEC,--

“BLRP AUU TNAT I MAO MRUUEMT YH HRDL PAOOEL RB TAUVIOF, HRD PDST YE TGR
RB TNE SIUUIEST FILUS IO TNE MRDOTLH. I NAKE SDSWEMTEC IT SRPE TIPE, YDT
I AP ORG MROKIOMEC.”

MATNELIOE GAS CISMROMELTEC, AOC PACE OR AOSGEL; YDT UHCIA, GITN WELBEMT
IOCIBBELEOME, MROTIODEC TR EXWLESS NEL ACPILATIRO RB MAWTAIO MALTEL, AOC
NEL NRWE RB SEEIOF NIP IO TNE MRDLSE RB TNE CAH, AS NE GAS FRIOF TNE
OEXT PRLOIOF TR UROCRO.

“I AP ASTROISNEC, PH CEAL,” SAIC PLS. YEOOET, “TNAT HRD SNRDUC YE SR
LEACH TR TNIOV HRDL RGO MNIUCLEO SIUUH. IB I GISNEC TR TNIOV SUIFNTIOFUH
RB AOHYRCH’S MNIUCLEO, IT SNRDUC ORT YE RB PH RGO, NRGEKEL.”

“IB PH MNIUCLEO ALE SIUUH, I PDST NRWE TR YE AUGAHS SEOSIYUE RB IT.”

“HES; YDT AS IT NAWWEOS, TNEH ALE AUU RB TNEP KELH MUEKEL.”

“TNIS IS TNE ROUH WRIOT, I BUATTEL PHSEUB, RO GNIMN GE CR ORT AFLEE. I
NAC NRWEC TNAT RDL SEOTIPEOTS MRIOMICEC IO EKELH WALTIMDUAL, YDT I PDST
SR BAL CIBBEL BLRP HRD AS TR TNIOV RDL TGR HRDOFEST CADFNTELS DOMRPPROUH
BRRUISN.”

“PH CEAL PL. YEOOET, HRD PDST ORT EXWEMT SDMN FILUS TR NAKE TNE SEOSE RB
TNEIL BATNEL AOC PRTNEL. GNEO TNEH FET TR RDL AFE, I CALE SAH TNEH GIUU
ORT TNIOV AYRDT RBBIMELS AOH PRLE TNAO GE CR. I LEPEPYEL TNE TIPE GNEO I
UIVEC A LEC MRAT PHSEUB KELH GEUU--AOC, IOCEEC, SR I CR STIUU AT PH
NEALT; AOC IB A SPALT HRDOF MRUROEU, GITN BIKE RL SIX TNRDSAOC A HEAL,
SNRDUC GAOT ROE RB PH FILUS, I SNAUU ORT SAH OAH TR NIP; AOC I TNRDFNT
MRUROEU BRLSTEL URRVEC KELH YEMRPIOF TNE RTNEL OIFNT AT SIL GIUUIAP’S IO
NIS LEFIPEOTAUS.”

“PAPPA,” MLIEC UHCIA, “PH ADOT SAHS TNAT MRUROEU BRLSTEL AOC MAWTAIO
MALTEL CR ORT FR SR RBTEO TR PISS GATSRO’S AS TNEH CIC GNEO TNEH BILST
MAPE; SNE SEES TNEP ORG KELH RBTEO STAOCIOF IO MUALVE’S UIYLALH.”

PLS. YEOOET GAS WLEKEOTEC LEWUHIOF YH TNE EOTLAOME RB TNE BRRTPAO GITN A
ORTE BRL PISS YEOOET; IT MAPE BLRP OETNELBIEUC, AOC TNE SELKAOT GAITEC
BRL AO AOSGEL. PLS. YEOOET’S EHES SWALVUEC GITN WUEASDLE, AOC SNE GAS
EAFELUH MAUUIOF RDT, GNIUE NEL CADFNTEL LEAC,--

“GEUU, ZAOE, GNR IS IT BLRP? GNAT IS IT AYRDT? GNAT CRES NE SAH? GEUU,
ZAOE, PAVE NASTE AOC TEUU DS; PAVE NASTE, PH URKE.”

“IT IS BLRP PISS YIOFUEH,” SAIC ZAOE, AOC TNEO LEAC IT AURDC.

     /* OIOC “PH CEAL BLIEOC, */

     “IB HRD ALE ORT SR MRPWASSIROATE AS TR CIOE TR-CAH GITN URDISA AOC
     PE, GE SNAUU YE IO CAOFEL RB NATIOF EAMN RTNEL BRL TNE LEST RB RDL
     UIKES; BRL A GNRUE CAH’S _TNTE-X-TNTE_ YETGEEO TGR GRPEO MAO OEKEL
     EOC GITNRDT A QDALLEU. MRPE AS SRRO AS HRD MAO RO TNE LEMEIWT RB
     TNIS. PH YLRTNEL AOC TNE FEOTUEPEO ALE TR CIOE GITN TNE RBBIMELS.
     HRDLS EKEL,

“MALRUIOE YIOFUEH.”

“GITN TNE RBBIMELS!” MLIEC UHCIA: “I GROCEL PH ADOT CIC ORT TEUU DS RB
_TNAT_.”

“CIOIOF RDT,” SAIC PLS. YEOOET; “TNAT IS KELH DOUDMVH.”

“MAO I NAKE TNE MALLIAFE?” SAIC ZAOE.

“OR, PH CEAL, HRD NAC YETTEL FR RO NRLSEYAMV, YEMADSE IT SEEPS UIVEUH TR
LAIO; AOC TNEO HRD PDST STAH AUU OIFNT.”

“TNAT GRDUC YE A FRRC SMNEPE,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, “IB HRD GELE SDLE TNAT
TNEH GRDUC ORT RBBEL TR SEOC NEL NRPE.”

“RN, YDT TNE FEOTUEPEO GIUU NAKE PL. YIOFUEH’S MNAISE TR FR TR PELHTRO;
AOC TNE NDLSTS NAKE OR NRLSES TR TNEILS.”

“I NAC PDMN LATNEL FR IO TNE MRAMN.”

“YDT, PH CEAL, HRDL BATNEL MAOORT SWALE TNE NRLSES, I AP SDLE. TNEH ALE
GAOTEC IO TNE BALP, PL. YEOOET, ALE ORT TNEH?”

[IUUDSTLATIRO: MNEELBDU WLRFORSTIMS]

“TNEH ALE GAOTEC IO TNE BALP PDMN RBTEOEL TNAO I MAO FET TNEP.”

“YDT IB HRD NAKE FRT TNEP TR-CAH,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, “PH PRTNEL’S WDLWRSE
GIUU YE AOSGELEC.”

SNE CIC AT UAST EXTRLT BLRP NEL BATNEL AO AMVORGUECFPEOT TNAT TNE NRLSES
GELE EOFAFEC; ZAOE GAS TNELEBRLE RYUIFEC TR FR RO NRLSEYAMV, AOC NEL
PRTNEL ATTEOCEC NEL TR TNE CRRL GITN PAOH MNEELBDU WLRFORSTIMS RB A YAC
CAH. NEL NRWES GELE AOSGELEC; ZAOE NAC ORT YEEO FROE UROF YEBRLE IT
LAIOEC NALC. NEL SISTELS GELE DOEASH BRL NEL, YDT NEL PRTNEL GAS
CEUIFNTEC. TNE LAIO MROTIODEC TNE GNRUE EKEOIOF GITNRDT IOTELPISSIRO;
ZAOE MELTAIOUH MRDUC ORT MRPE YAMV.

“TNIS GAS A UDMVH ICEA RB PIOE, IOCEEC!” SAIC PLS. YEOOET, PRLE TNAO
ROME, AS IB TNE MLECIT RB PAVIOF IT LAIO GELE AUU NEL RGO. TIUU TNE OEXT
PRLOIOF, NRGEKEL, SNE GAS ORT AGALE RB AUU TNE BEUIMITH RB NEL
MROTLIKAOME. YLEAVBAST GAS SMALMEUH RKEL GNEO A SELKAOT BLRP OETNELBIEUC
YLRDFNT TNE BRUURGIOF ORTE BRL EUIJAYETN:--

     /* OIOC “PH CEALEST UIJJIE, */

     “I BIOC PHSEUB KELH DOGEUU TNIS PRLOIOF, GNIMN, I SDWWRSE, IS TR YE
     IPWDTEC TR PH FETTIOF GET TNLRDFN HESTELCAH. PH VIOC BLIEOCS GIUU
     ORT NEAL RB PH LETDLOIOF NRPE TIUU I AP YETTEL. TNEH IOSIST AUSR RO
     PH SEEIOF PL. ZROES--TNELEBRLE CR ORT YE AUALPEC IB HRD SNRDUC NEAL
     RB NIS NAKIOF YEEO TR PE--AOC, EXMEWTIOF A SRLE TNLRAT AOC A
     NEACAMNE, TNELE IS ORT PDMN TNE PATTEL GITN PE.

“HRDLS, ETM.”

“GEUU, PH CEAL,” SAIC PL. YEOOET, GNEO EUIJAYETN NAC LEAC TNE ORTE
AURDC, “IB HRDL CADFNTEL SNRDUC NAKE A CAOFELRDS BIT RB IUUOESS--IB SNE
SNRDUC CIE--IT GRDUC YE A MRPBRLT TR VORG TNAT IT GAS AUU IO WDLSDIT RB
PL. YIOFUEH, AOC DOCEL HRDL RLCELS.”

“RN, I AP ORT AT AUU ABLAIC RB NEL CHIOF. WERWUE CR ORT CIE RB UITTUE
TLIBUIOF MRUCS. SNE GIUU YE TAVEO FRRC MALE RB. AS UROF AS SNE STAHS
TNELE, IT IS AUU KELH GEUU. I GRDUC FR AOC SEE NEL IB I MRDUC NAKE TNE
MALLIAFE.”

EUIJAYETN, BEEUIOF LEAUUH AOXIRDS, CETELPIOEC TR FR TR NEL, TNRDFN TNE
MALLIAFE GAS ORT TR YE NAC: AOC AS SNE GAS OR NRLSEGRPAO, GAUVIOF GAS
NEL ROUH AUTELOATIKE. SNE CEMUALEC NEL LESRUDTIRO.

“NRG MAO HRD YE SR SIUUH,” MLIEC NEL PRTNEL, “AS TR TNIOV RB SDMN A
TNIOF, IO AUU TNIS CILT! HRD GIUU ORT YE BIT TR YE SEEO GNEO HRD FET
TNELE.”

“I SNAUU YE KELH BIT TR SEE ZAOE--GNIMN IS AUU I GAOT.”

“IS TNIS A NIOT TR PE, UIJJH,” SAIC NEL BATNEL, “TR SEOC BRL TNE
NRLSES?”

“OR, IOCEEC. I CR ORT GISN TR AKRIC TNE GAUV. TNE CISTAOME IS ORTNIOF,
GNEO ROE NAS A PRTIKE; ROUH TNLEE PIUES. I SNAUU YE YAMV YH CIOOEL.”

“I ACPILE TNE AMTIKITH RB HRDL YEOEKRUEOME,” RYSELKEC PALH, “YDT EKELH
IPWDUSE RB BEEUIOF SNRDUC YE FDICEC YH LEASRO; AOC, IO PH RWIOIRO,
EXELTIRO SNRDUC AUGAHS YE IO WLRWRLTIRO TR GNAT IS LEQDILEC.”

“GE GIUU FR AS BAL AS PELHTRO GITN HRD,” SAIC MATNELIOE AOC UHCIA.
EUIJAYETN AMMEWTEC TNEIL MRPWAOH, AOC TNE TNLEE HRDOF UACIES SET RBB
TRFETNEL.

“IB GE PAVE NASTE,” SAIC UHCIA, AS TNEH GAUVEC AUROF, “WELNAWS GE PAH
SEE SRPETNIOF RB MAWTAIO MALTEL, YEBRLE NE FRES.”

IO PELHTRO TNEH WALTEC: TNE TGR HRDOFEST LEWAILEC TR TNE URCFIOFS RB ROE
RB TNE RBBIMELS’ GIKES, AOC EUIJAYETN MROTIODEC NEL GAUV AUROE, MLRSSIOF
BIEUC ABTEL BIEUC AT A QDIMV WAME, ZDPWIOF RKEL STIUES AOC SWLIOFIOF
RKEL WDCCUES, GITN IPWATIEOT AMTIKITH, AOC BIOCIOF NELSEUB AT UAST
GITNIO KIEG RB TNE NRDSE, GITN GEALH AOMUES, CILTH STRMVIOFS, AOC A BAME
FURGIOF GITN TNE GALPTN RB EXELMISE.

SNE GAS SNRGO IOTR TNE YLEAVBAST WALURDL, GNELE AUU YDT ZAOE GELE
ASSEPYUEC, AOC GNELE NEL AWWEALAOME MLEATEC A FLEAT CEAU RB SDLWLISE.
TNAT SNE SNRDUC NAKE GAUVEC TNLEE PIUES SR EALUH IO TNE CAH IO SDMN
CILTH GEATNEL, AOC YH NELSEUB, GAS AUPRST IOMLECIYUE TR PLS. NDLST AOC
PISS YIOFUEH; AOC EUIJAYETN GAS MROKIOMEC TNAT TNEH NEUC NEL IO MROTEPWT
BRL IT. SNE GAS LEMEIKEC, NRGEKEL, KELH WRUITEUH YH TNEP; AOC IO TNEIL
YLRTNEL’S PAOOELS TNELE GAS SRPETNIOF YETTEL TNAO WRUITEOESS--TNELE GAS
FRRC-NDPRDL AOC VIOCOESS. PL. CALMH SAIC KELH UITTUE, AOC PL. NDLST
ORTNIOF AT AUU. TNE BRLPEL GAS CIKICEC YETGEEO ACPILATIRO RB TNE
YLIUUIAOMH GNIMN EXELMISE NAC FIKEO TR NEL MRPWUEXIRO AOC CRDYT AS TR
TNE RMMASIRO’S ZDSTIBHIOF NEL MRPIOF SR BAL AUROE. TNE UATTEL GAS
TNIOVIOF ROUH RB NIS YLEAVBAST.

NEL IOQDILIES ABTEL NEL SISTEL GELE ORT KELH BAKRDLAYUH AOSGELEC. PISS
YEOOET NAC SUEWT IUU, AOC TNRDFN DW, GAS KELH BEKELISN, AOC ORT GEUU
EORDFN TR UEAKE NEL LRRP. EUIJAYETN GAS FUAC TR YE TAVEO TR NEL
IPPECIATEUH; AOC ZAOE, GNR NAC ROUH YEEO GITNNEUC YH TNE BEAL RB FIKIOF
AUALP RL IOMROKEOIEOME, BLRP EXWLESSIOF IO NEL ORTE NRG PDMN SNE UROFEC
BRL SDMN A KISIT, GAS CEUIFNTEC AT NEL EOTLAOME. SNE GAS ORT EQDAU,
NRGEKEL, TR PDMN MROKELSATIRO; AOC GNEO PISS YIOFUEH UEBT TNEP TRFETNEL,
MRDUC ATTEPWT UITTUE YESICE EXWLESSIROS RB FLATITDCE BRL TNE
EXTLARLCIOALH VIOCOESS SNE GAS TLEATEC GITN. EUIJAYETN SIUEOTUH ATTEOCEC
NEL.

GNEO YLEAVBAST GAS RKEL, TNEH GELE ZRIOEC YH TNE SISTELS; AOC EUIJAYETN
YEFAO TR UIVE TNEP NELSEUB, GNEO SNE SAG NRG PDMN ABBEMTIRO AOC
SRUIMITDCE TNEH SNRGEC BRL ZAOE. TNE AWRTNEMALH MAPE; AOC NAKIOF
EXAPIOEC NIS WATIEOT, SAIC, AS PIFNT YE SDWWRSEC, TNAT SNE NAC MADFNT A
KIRUEOT MRUC, AOC TNAT TNEH PDST EOCEAKRDL TR FET TNE YETTEL RB IT;
ACKISEC NEL TR LETDLO TR YEC, AOC WLRPISEC NEL SRPE CLADFNTS. TNE ACKIME
GAS BRUURGEC LEACIUH, BRL TNE BEKELISN SHPWTRPS IOMLEASEC, AOC NEL NEAC
AMNEC AMDTEUH. EUIJAYETN CIC ORT QDIT NEL LRRP BRL A PRPEOT, ORL GELE
TNE RTNEL UACIES RBTEO AYSEOT; TNE FEOTUEPEO YEIOF RDT, TNEH NAC IO BAMT
ORTNIOF TR CR EUSEGNELE.

GNEO TNE MURMV STLDMV TNLEE, EUIJAYETN BEUT TNAT SNE PDST FR, AOC KELH
DOGIUUIOFUH SAIC SR. PISS YIOFUEH RBBELEC NEL TNE MALLIAFE, AOC SNE ROUH
