GAOTEC A UITTUE WLESSIOF TR AMMEWT IT, GNEO ZAOE TESTIBIEC SDMN MROMELO
AT WALTIOF GITN NEL TNAT PISS YIOFUEH GAS RYUIFEC TR MROKELT TNE RBBEL
RB TNE MNAISE IOTR AO IOKITATIRO TR LEPAIO AT OETNELBIEUC BRL TNE
WLESEOT. EUIJAYETN PRST TNAOVBDUUH MROSEOTEC, AOC A SELKAOT GAS
CESWATMNEC TR UROFYRDLO, TR AMQDAIOT TNE BAPIUH GITN NEL STAH, AOC YLIOF
YAMV A SDWWUH RB MURTNES.

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“TNE AWRTNEMALH MAPE”
]




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“MRKELIOF A SMLEEO”
]




MNAWTEL KIII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

AT BIKE R’MURMV TNE TGR UACIES LETILEC TR CLESS, AOC AT NAUB-WAST SIX
EUIJAYETN GAS SDPPROEC TR CIOOEL. TR TNE MIKIU IOQDILIES GNIMN TNEO
WRDLEC IO, AOC APROFST GNIMN SNE NAC TNE WUEASDLE RB CISTIOFDISNIOF TNE
PDMN SDWELIRL SRUIMITDCE RB PL. YIOFUEH, SNE MRDUC ORT PAVE A KELH
BAKRDLAYUE AOSGEL. ZAOE GAS YH OR PEAOS YETTEL. TNE SISTELS, RO NEALIOF
TNIS, LEWEATEC TNLEE RL BRDL TIPES NRG PDMN TNEH GELE FLIEKEC, NRG
SNRMVIOF IT GAS TR NAKE A YAC MRUC, AOC NRG EXMESSIKEUH TNEH CISUIVEC
YEIOF IUU TNEPSEUKES; AOC TNEO TNRDFNT OR PRLE RB TNE PATTEL: AOC TNEIL
IOCIBBELEOME TRGALCS ZAOE, GNEO ORT IPPECIATEUH YEBRLE TNEP, LESTRLEC
EUIJAYETN TR TNE EOZRHPEOT RB AUU NEL RLIFIOAU CISUIVE.

TNEIL YLRTNEL, IOCEEC, GAS TNE ROUH ROE RB TNE WALTH GNRP SNE MRDUC
LEFALC GITN AOH MRPWUAMEOMH. NIS AOXIETH BRL ZAOE GAS EKICEOT, AOC NIS
ATTEOTIROS TR NELSEUB PRST WUEASIOF; AOC TNEH WLEKEOTEC NEL BEEUIOF
NELSEUB SR PDMN AO IOTLDCEL AS SNE YEUIEKEC SNE GAS MROSICELEC YH TNE
RTNELS. SNE NAC KELH UITTUE ORTIME BLRP AOH YDT NIP. PISS YIOFUEH GAS
EOFLRSSEC YH PL. CALMH, NEL SISTEL SMALMEUH UESS SR; AOC AS BRL PL.
NDLST, YH GNRP EUIJAYETN SAT, NE GAS AO IOCRUEOT PAO, GNR UIKEC ROUH TR
EAT, CLIOV, AOC WUAH AT MALCS, GNR, GNEO NE BRDOC NEL WLEBEL A WUAIO
CISN TR A LAFRDT, NAC ORTNIOF TR SAH TR NEL.

GNEO CIOOEL GAS RKEL, SNE LETDLOEC CILEMTUH TR ZAOE, AOC PISS YIOFUEH
YEFAO AYDSIOF NEL AS SRRO AS SNE GAS RDT RB TNE LRRP. NEL PAOOELS GELE
WLRORDOMEC TR YE KELH YAC IOCEEC,--A PIXTDLE RB WLICE AOC IPWELTIOEOME:
SNE NAC OR MROKELSATIRO, OR STHUE, OR TASTE, OR YEADTH. PLS. NDLST
TNRDFNT TNE SAPE, AOC ACCEC,--

“SNE NAS ORTNIOF, IO SNRLT, TR LEMRPPEOC NEL, YDT YEIOF AO EXMEUUEOT
GAUVEL. I SNAUU OEKEL BRLFET NEL AWWEALAOME TNIS PRLOIOF. SNE LEAUUH
URRVEC AUPRST GIUC.”

“SNE CIC IOCEEC, URDISA. I MRDUC NALCUH VEEW PH MRDOTEOAOME. KELH
OROSEOSIMAU TR MRPE AT AUU! GNH PDST _SNE_ YE SMAPWELIOF AYRDT TNE
MRDOTLH, YEMADSE NEL SISTEL NAC A MRUC? NEL NAIL SR DOTICH, SR YURGJH!”

“HES, AOC NEL WETTIMRAT; I NRWE HRD SAG NEL WETTIMRAT, SIX IOMNES CEEW
IO PDC, I AP AYSRUDTEUH MELTAIO, AOC TNE FRGO GNIMN NAC YEEO UET CRGO TR
NICE IT ORT CRIOF ITS RBBIME.”

“HRDL WIMTDLE PAH YE KELH EXAMT, URDISA,” SAIC YIOFUEH; “YDT TNIS GAS
AUU URST DWRO PE. I TNRDFNT PISS EUIJAYETN YEOOET URRVEC LEPALVAYUH GEUU
GNEO SNE MAPE IOTR TNE LRRP TNIS PRLOIOF. NEL CILTH WETTIMRAT QDITE
ESMAWEC PH ORTIME.”

“_HRD_ RYSELKEC IT, PL. CALMH, I AP SDLE,” SAIC PISS YIOFUEH; “AOC I AP
IOMUIOEC TR TNIOV TNAT HRD GRDUC ORT GISN TR SEE _HRDL SISTEL_ PAVE SDMN
AO EXNIYITIRO.”

“MELTAIOUH ORT.”

“TR GAUV TNLEE PIUES, RL BRDL PIUES, RL BIKE PIUES, RL GNATEKEL IT IS,
AYRKE NEL AOMUES IO CILT, AOC AUROE, QDITE AUROE! GNAT MRDUC SNE PEAO YH
IT? IT SEEPS TR PE TR SNRG AO AYRPIOAYUE SRLT RB MROMEITEC IOCEWEOCEOME,
A PRST MRDOTLH-TRGO IOCIBBELEOME TR CEMRLDP.”

“IT SNRGS AO ABBEMTIRO BRL NEL SISTEL TNAT IS KELH WUEASIOF,” SAIC
YIOFUEH.

“I AP ABLAIC, PL. CALMH,” RYSELKEC PISS YIOFUEH, IO A NAUB GNISWEL,
“TNAT TNIS ACKEOTDLE NAS LATNEL ABBEMTEC HRDL ACPILATIRO RB NEL BIOE
EHES.”

“ORT AT AUU,” NE LEWUIEC: “TNEH GELE YLIFNTEOEC YH TNE EXELMISE.” A
SNRLT WADSE BRUURGEC TNIS SWEEMN, AOC PLS. NDLST YEFAO AFAIO,--

“I NAKE AO EXMESSIKE LEFALC BRL ZAOE YEOOET,--SNE IS LEAUUH A KELH SGEET
FILU,--AOC I GISN GITN AUU PH NEALT SNE GELE GEUU SETTUEC. YDT GITN SDMN
A BATNEL AOC PRTNEL, AOC SDMN URG MROOEMTIROS, I AP ABLAIC TNELE IS OR
MNAOME RB IT.”

“I TNIOV I NAKE NEALC HRD SAH TNAT TNEIL DOMUE IS AO ATTRLOEH IO
PELHTRO?”

“HES; AOC TNEH NAKE AORTNEL, GNR UIKES SRPEGNELE OEAL MNEAWSICE.”

“TNAT IS MAWITAU,” ACCEC NEL SISTEL; AOC TNEH YRTN UADFNEC NEALTIUH.

“IB TNEH NAC DOMUES EORDFN TR BIUU _AUU_ MNEAWSICE,” MLIEC YIOFUEH, “IT
GRDUC ORT PAVE TNEP ROE ZRT UESS AFLEEAYUE.”

“YDT IT PDST KELH PATELIAUUH UESSEO TNEIL MNAOME RB PALLHIOF PEO RB AOH
MROSICELATIRO IO TNE GRLUC,” LEWUIEC CALMH.

TR TNIS SWEEMN YIOFUEH PACE OR AOSGEL; YDT NIS SISTELS FAKE IT TNEIL
NEALTH ASSEOT, AOC IOCDUFEC TNEIL PILTN BRL SRPE TIPE AT TNE EXWEOSE RB
TNEIL CEAL BLIEOC’S KDUFAL LEUATIROS.

GITN A LEOEGAU RB TEOCELOESS, NRGEKEL, TNEH LEWAILEC TR NEL LRRP RO
UEAKIOF TNE CIOIOF-WALURDL, AOC SAT GITN NEL TIUU SDPPROEC TR MRBBEE.
SNE GAS STIUU KELH WRRLUH, AOC EUIJAYETN GRDUC ORT QDIT NEL AT AUU, TIUU
UATE IO TNE EKEOIOF, GNEO SNE NAC TNE MRPBRLT RB SEEIOF NEL ASUEEW, AOC
GNEO IT AWWEALEC TR NEL LATNEL LIFNT TNAO WUEASAOT TNAT SNE SNRDUC FR
CRGO STAILS NELSEUB. RO EOTELIOF TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP, SNE BRDOC TNE GNRUE
WALTH AT URR, AOC GAS IPPECIATEUH IOKITEC TR ZRIO TNEP; YDT SDSWEMTIOF
TNEP TR YE WUAHIOF NIFN, SNE CEMUIOEC IT, AOC PAVIOF NEL SISTEL TNE
EXMDSE, SAIC SNE GRDUC APDSE NELSEUB, BRL TNE SNRLT TIPE SNE MRDUC STAH
YEURG, GITN A YRRV. PL. NDLST URRVEC AT NEL GITN ASTROISNPEOT.

“CR HRD WLEBEL LEACIOF TR MALCS?” SAIC NE; “TNAT IS LATNEL SIOFDUAL.”

“PISS EUIJA YEOOET,” SAIC PISS YIOFUEH, “CESWISES MALCS. SNE IS A FLEAT
LEACEL, AOC NAS OR WUEASDLE IO AOHTNIOF EUSE.”

“I CESELKE OEITNEL SDMN WLAISE ORL SDMN MEOSDLE,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN; “I
AP _ORT_ A FLEAT LEACEL, AOC I NAKE WUEASDLE IO PAOH TNIOFS.”

“IO ODLSIOF HRDL SISTEL I AP SDLE HRD NAKE WUEASDLE,” SAIC YIOFUEH; “AOC
I NRWE IT GIUU SRRO YE IOMLEASEC YH SEEIOF NEL QDITE GEUU.”

EUIJAYETN TNAOVEC NIP BLRP NEL NEALT, AOC TNEO GAUVEC TRGALCS A TAYUE
GNELE A BEG YRRVS GELE UHIOF. NE IPPECIATEUH RBBELEC TR BETMN NEL
RTNELS; AUU TNAT NIS UIYLALH ABBRLCEC.

“AOC I GISN PH MRUUEMTIRO GELE UALFEL BRL HRDL YEOEBIT AOC PH RGO
MLECIT; YDT I AP AO ICUE BEUURG; AOC TNRDFN I NAKE ORT PAOH, I NAKE PRLE
TNAO I EKEL URRVEC IOTR.”

EUIJAYETN ASSDLEC NIP TNAT SNE MRDUC SDIT NELSEUB WELBEMTUH GITN TNRSE
IO TNE LRRP.

“I AP ASTROISNEC,” SAIC PISS YIOFUEH, “TNAT PH BATNEL SNRDUC NAKE UEBT
SR SPAUU A MRUUEMTIRO RB YRRVS. GNAT A CEUIFNTBDU UIYLALH HRD NAKE AT
WEPYELUEH, PL. CALMH!”

“IT RDFNT TR YE FRRC,” NE LEWUIEC: “IT NAS YEEO TNE GRLV RB PAOH
FEOELATIROS.”

“AOC TNEO HRD NAKE ACCEC SR PDMN TR IT HRDLSEUB--HRD ALE AUGAHS YDHIOF
YRRVS.”

“I MAOORT MRPWLENEOC TNE OEFUEMT RB A BAPIUH UIYLALH IO SDMN CAHS AS
TNESE.”

“OEFUEMT! I AP SDLE HRD OEFUEMT ORTNIOF TNAT MAO ACC TR TNE YEADTIES RB
TNAT ORYUE WUAME. MNALUES, GNEO HRD YDIUC _HRDL_ NRDSE, I GISN IT PAH YE
NAUB AS CEUIFNTBDU AS WEPYELUEH.”

“I GISN IT PAH.”

“YDT I GRDUC LEAUUH ACKISE HRD TR PAVE HRDL WDLMNASE IO TNAT
OEIFNYRDLNRRC, AOC TAVE WEPYELUEH BRL A VIOC RB PRCEU. TNELE IS ORT A
BIOEL MRDOTH IO EOFUAOC TNAO CELYHSNILE.”

“GITN AUU PH NEALT: I GIUU YDH WEPYELUEH ITSEUB, IB CALMH GIUU SEUU IT.”

“I AP TAUVIOF RB WRSSIYIUITIES, MNALUES.”

“DWRO PH GRLC, MALRUIOE, I SNRDUC TNIOV IT PRLE WRSSIYUE TR FET
WEPYELUEH YH WDLMNASE TNAO YH IPITATIRO.”

EUIJAYETN GAS SR PDMN MADFNT YH GNAT WASSEC, AS TR UEAKE NEL KELH UITTUE
ATTEOTIRO BRL NEL YRRV; AOC, SRRO UAHIOF IT GNRUUH ASICE, SNE CLEG OEAL
TNE MALC-TAYUE, AOC STATIROEC NELSEUB YETGEEO PL. YIOFUEH AOC NIS EUCEST
SISTEL, TR RYSELKE TNE FAPE.

“IS PISS CALMH PDMN FLRGO SIOME TNE SWLIOF?” SAIC PISS YIOFUEH: “GIUU
SNE YE AS TAUU AS I AP?”

“I TNIOV SNE GIUU. SNE IS ORG AYRDT PISS EUIJAYETN YEOOET’S NEIFNT, RL
LATNEL TAUUEL.”

“NRG I UROF TR SEE NEL AFAIO! I OEKEL PET GITN AOHYRCH GNR CEUIFNTEC PE
SR PDMN. SDMN A MRDOTEOAOME, SDMN PAOOELS, AOC SR EXTLEPEUH AMMRPWUISNEC
BRL NEL AFE! NEL WELBRLPAOME RO TNE WIAORBRLTE IS EXQDISITE.”

“IT IS APAJIOF TR PE,” SAIC YIOFUEH, “NRG HRDOF UACIES MAO NAKE WATIEOME
TR YE SR KELH AMMRPWUISNEC AS TNEH AUU ALE.”

“AUU HRDOF UACIES AMMRPWUISNEC! PH CEAL MNALUES, GNAT CR HRD PEAO?”

“HES, AUU RB TNEP, I TNIOV. TNEH AUU WAIOT TAYUES, MRKEL SMLEEOS, AOC
OET WDLSES. I SMALMEUH VORG AOH ROE GNR MAOORT CR AUU TNIS; AOC I AP
SDLE I OEKEL NEALC A HRDOF UACH SWRVEO RB BRL TNE BILST TIPE, GITNRDT
YEIOF IOBRLPEC TNAT SNE GAS KELH AMMRPWUISNEC.”

“HRDL UIST RB TNE MRPPRO EXTEOT RB AMMRPWUISNPEOTS,” SAIC CALMH, “NAS
TRR PDMN TLDTN. TNE GRLC IS AWWUIEC TR PAOH A GRPAO GNR CESELKES IT OR
RTNELGISE TNAO YH OETTIOF A WDLSE RL MRKELIOF A SMLEEO; YDT I AP KELH
BAL BLRP AFLEEIOF GITN HRD IO HRDL ESTIPATIRO RB UACIES IO FEOELAU. I
MAOORT YRAST RB VORGIOF PRLE TNAO NAUB-A-CRJEO IO TNE GNRUE LAOFE RB PH
AMQDAIOTAOME TNAT ALE LEAUUH AMMRPWUISNEC.”

“ORL I, I AP SDLE,” SAIC PISS YIOFUEH.

“TNEO,” RYSELKEC EUIJAYETN, “HRD PDST MRPWLENEOC A FLEAT CEAU IO HRDL
ICEA RB AO AMMRPWUISNEC GRPAO.”

“HES; I CR MRPWLENEOC A FLEAT CEAU IO IT.”

“RN, MELTAIOUH,” MLIEC NIS BAITNBDU ASSISTAOT, “OR ROE MAO YE LEAUUH
ESTEEPEC AMMRPWUISNEC GNR CRES ORT FLEATUH SDLWASS GNAT IS DSDAUUH PET
GITN. A GRPAO PDST NAKE A TNRLRDFN VORGUECFE RB PDSIM, SIOFIOF, CLAGIOF,
CAOMIOF, AOC TNE PRCELO UAOFDAFES, TR CESELKE TNE GRLC; AOC, YESICES AUU
TNIS, SNE PDST WRSSESS A MELTAIO SRPETNIOF IO NEL AIL AOC PAOOEL RB
GAUVIOF, TNE TROE RB NEL KRIME, NEL ACCLESS AOC EXWLESSIROS, RL TNE GRLC
GIUU YE YDT NAUB CESELKEC.”

“AUU TNIS SNE PDST WRSSESS,” ACCEC CALMH; “AOC TR AUU SNE PDST HET ACC
SRPETNIOF PRLE SDYSTAOTIAU IO TNE IPWLRKEPEOT RB NEL PIOC YH EXTEOSIKE
LEACIOF.”

“I AP OR UROFEL SDLWLISEC AT HRDL VORGIOF _ROUH_ SIX AMMRPWUISNEC GRPEO.
I LATNEL GROCEL ORG AT HRDL VORGIOF _AOH_.”

“ALE HRD SR SEKELE DWRO HRDL RGO SEX AS TR CRDYT TNE WRSSIYIUITH RB AUU
TNIS?”

“_I_ OEKEL SAG SDMN A GRPAO. _I_ OEKEL SAG SDMN MAWAMITH, AOC TASTE, AOC
AWWUIMATIRO, AOC EUEFAOME, AS HRD CESMLIYE, DOITEC.”

PLS. NDLST AOC PISS YIOFUEH YRTN MLIEC RDT AFAIOST TNE IOZDSTIME RB NEL
IPWUIEC CRDYT, AOC GELE YRTN WLRTESTIOF TNAT TNEH VOEG PAOH GRPEO GNR
AOSGELEC TNIS CESMLIWTIRO, GNEO PL. NDLST MAUUEC TNEP TR RLCEL, GITN
YITTEL MRPWUAIOTS RB TNEIL IOATTEOTIRO TR GNAT GAS FRIOF BRLGALC. AS AUU
MROKELSATIRO GAS TNELEYH AT AO EOC, EUIJAYETN SRRO ABTELGALCS UEBT TNE
LRRP.

“EUIJA YEOOET,” SAIC PISS YIOFUEH, GNEO TNE CRRL GAS MURSEC RO NEL, “IS
ROE RB TNRSE HRDOF UACIES GNR SEEV TR LEMRPPEOC TNEPSEUKES TR TNE RTNEL
SEX YH DOCELKAUDIOF TNEIL RGO; AOC GITN PAOH PEO, I CALESAH, IT
SDMMEECS; YDT, IO PH RWIOIRO, IT IS A WAUTLH CEKIME, A KELH PEAO ALT.”

“DOCRDYTECUH,” LEWUIEC CALMH, TR GNRP TNIS LEPALV GAS MNIEBUH ACCLESSEC,
“TNELE IS PEAOOESS IO _AUU_ TNE ALTS GNIMN UACIES SRPETIPES MROCESMEOC
TR EPWURH BRL MAWTIKATIRO. GNATEKEL YEALS ABBIOITH TR MDOOIOF IS
CESWIMAYUE.”

PISS YIOFUEH GAS ORT SR EOTILEUH SATISBIEC GITN TNIS LEWUH AS TR
MROTIODE TNE SDYZEMT.

EUIJAYETN ZRIOEC TNEP AFAIO ROUH TR SAH TNAT NEL SISTEL GAS GRLSE, AOC
TNAT SNE MRDUC ORT UEAKE NEL. YIOFUEH DLFEC PL. ZROES’S YEIOF SEOT BRL
IPPECIATEUH; GNIUE NIS SISTELS, MROKIOMEC TNAT OR MRDOTLH ACKIME MRDUC
YE RB AOH SELKIME, LEMRPPEOCEC AO EXWLESS TR TRGO BRL ROE RB TNE PRST
EPIOEOT WNHSIMIAOS. TNIS SNE GRDUC ORT NEAL RB; YDT SNE GAS ORT SR
DOGIUUIOF TR MRPWUH GITN TNEIL YLRTNEL’S WLRWRSAU; AOC IT GAS SETTUEC
TNAT PL. ZROES SNRDUC YE SEOT BRL EALUH IO TNE PRLOIOF, IB PISS YEOOET
GELE ORT CEMICECUH YETTEL. YIOFUEH GAS QDITE DOMRPBRLTAYUE; NIS SISTELS
CEMUALEC TNAT TNEH GELE PISELAYUE. TNEH SRUAMEC TNEIL GLETMNECOESS,
NRGEKEL, YH CDETS ABTEL SDWWEL; GNIUE NE MRDUC BIOC OR YETTEL LEUIEB TR
NIS BEEUIOFS TNAO YH FIKIOF NIS NRDSEVEEWEL CILEMTIROS TNAT EKELH
WRSSIYUE ATTEOTIRO PIFNT YE WAIC TR TNE SIMV UACH AOC NEL SISTEL.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

P^{LS} YEOOET AOC NEL TGR HRDOFEST FILUS

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]




MNAWTEL IX.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN WASSEC TNE MNIEB RB TNE OIFNT IO NEL SISTEL’S LRRP, AOC IO TNE
PRLOIOF NAC TNE WUEASDLE RB YEIOF AYUE TR SEOC A TRUELAYUE AOSGEL TR TNE
IOQDILIES GNIMN SNE KELH EALUH LEMEIKEC BLRP PL. YIOFUEH YH A NRDSEPAIC,
AOC SRPE TIPE ABTELGALCS BLRP TNE TGR EUEFAOT UACIES GNR GAITEC RO NIS
SISTELS. IO SWITE RB TNIS APEOCPEOT, NRGEKEL, SNE LEQDESTEC TR NAKE A
ORTE SEOT TR UROFYRDLO, CESILIOF NEL PRTNEL TR KISIT ZAOE, AOC BRLP NEL
RGO ZDCFPEOT RB NEL SITDATIRO. TNE ORTE GAS IPPECIATEUH CESWATMNEC, AOC
ITS MROTEOTS AS QDIMVUH MRPWUIEC GITN. PLS. YEOOET, AMMRPWAOIEC YH NEL
TGR HRDOFEST FILUS, LEAMNEC OETNELBIEUC SRRO ABTEL TNE BAPIUH YLEAVBAST.

NAC SNE BRDOC ZAOE IO AOH AWWALEOT CAOFEL, PLS. YEOOET GRDUC NAKE YEEO
KELH PISELAYUE; YDT YEIOF SATISBIEC RO SEEIOF NEL TNAT NEL IUUOESS GAS
ORT AUALPIOF, SNE NAC OR GISN RB NEL LEMRKELIOF IPPECIATEUH, AS NEL
LESTRLATIRO TR NEAUTN GRDUC WLRYAYUH LEPRKE NEL BLRP OETNELBIEUC. SNE
GRDUC ORT UISTEO, TNELEBRLE, TR NEL CADFNTEL’S WLRWRSAU RB YEIOF MALLIEC
NRPE; OEITNEL CIC TNE AWRTNEMALH, GNR ALLIKEC AYRDT TNE SAPE TIPE, TNIOV
IT AT AUU ACKISAYUE. ABTEL SITTIOF A UITTUE GNIUE GITN ZAOE, RO PISS
YIOFUEH’S AWWEALAOME AOC IOKITATIRO, TNE PRTNEL AOC TNLEE CADFNTELS AUU
ATTEOCEC NEL IOTR TNE YLEAVBAST WALURDL. YIOFUEH PET TNEP GITN NRWES
TNAT PLS. YEOOET NAC ORT BRDOC PISS YEOOET GRLSE TNAO SNE EXWEMTEC.

“IOCEEC I NAKE, SIL,” GAS NEL AOSGEL. “SNE IS A FLEAT CEAU TRR IUU TR YE
PRKEC. PL. ZROES SAHS GE PDST ORT TNIOV RB PRKIOF NEL. GE PDST TLESWASS
A UITTUE UROFEL RO HRDL VIOCOESS.”

“LEPRKEC!” MLIEC YIOFUEH. “IT PDST ORT YE TNRDFNT RB. PH SISTEL, I AP
SDLE, GIUU ORT NEAL RB NEL LEPRKAU.”

“HRD PAH CEWEOC DWRO IT, PACAP,” SAIC PISS YIOFUEH, GITN MRUC MIKIUITH,
“TNAT PISS YEOOET SNAUU LEMEIKE EKELH WRSSIYUE ATTEOTIRO GNIUE SNE
LEPAIOS GITN DS.”

PLS. YEOOET GAS WLRBDSE IO NEL AMVORGUECFPEOTS.

“I AP SDLE,” SNE ACCEC, “IB IT GAS ORT BRL SDMN FRRC BLIEOCS, I CR ORT
VORG GNAT GRDUC YEMRPE RB NEL, BRL SNE IS KELH IUU IOCEEC, AOC SDBBELS A
KAST CEAU, TNRDFN GITN TNE FLEATEST WATIEOME IO TNE GRLUC, GNIMN IS
AUGAHS TNE GAH GITN NEL, BRL SNE NAS, GITNRDT EXMEWTIRO, TNE SGEETEST
TEPWEL I EKEL PET GITN. I RBTEO TEUU PH RTNEL FILUS TNEH ALE ORTNIOF TR
_NEL_. HRD NAKE A SGEET LRRP NELE, PL. YIOFUEH, AOC A MNALPIOF WLRSWEMT
RKEL TNAT FLAKEU GAUV. I CR ORT VORG A WUAME IO TNE MRDOTLH TNAT IS
EQDAU TR OETNELBIEUC. HRD GIUU ORT TNIOV RB QDITTIOF IT IO A NDLLH, I
NRWE, TNRDFN HRD NAKE YDT A SNRLT UEASE.”

“GNATEKEL I CR IS CROE IO A NDLLH,” LEWUIEC NE; “AOC TNELEBRLE IB I
SNRDUC LESRUKE TR QDIT OETNELBIEUC, I SNRDUC WLRYAYUH YE RBB IO BIKE
PIODTES. AT WLESEOT, NRGEKEL, I MROSICEL PHSEUB AS QDITE BIXEC NELE.”

“TNAT IS EXAMTUH GNAT I SNRDUC NAKE SDWWRSEC RB HRD,” SAIC EUIJAYETN.

“HRD YEFIO TR MRPWLENEOC PE, CR HRD?” MLIEC NE, TDLOIOF TRGALCS NEL.

“RN HES--I DOCELSTAOC HRD WELBEMTUH.”

“I GISN I PIFNT TAVE TNIS BRL A MRPWUIPEOT; YDT TR YE SR EASIUH SEEO
TNLRDFN, I AP ABLAIC, IS WITIBDU.”

“TNAT IS AS IT NAWWEOS. IT CRES ORT OEMESSALIUH BRUURG TNAT A CEEW,
IOTLIMATE MNALAMTEL IS PRLE RL UESS ESTIPAYUE TNAO SDMN A ROE AS HRDLS.”

“UIJJH,” MLIEC NEL PRTNEL, “LEPEPYEL GNELE HRD ALE, AOC CR ORT LDO RO IO
TNE GIUC PAOOEL TNAT HRD ALE SDBBELEC TR CR AT NRPE.”

“I CIC ORT VORG YEBRLE,” MROTIODEC YIOFUEH, IPPECIATEUH, “TNAT HRD GELE
A STDCIEL RB MNALAMTEL. IT PDST YE AO APDSIOF STDCH.”

“HES; YDT IOTLIMATE MNALAMTELS ALE TNE _PRST_ APDSIOF. TNEH NAKE AT
UEAST TNAT ACKAOTAFE.”

“TNE MRDOTLH,” SAIC CALMH, “MAO IO FEOELAU SDWWUH YDT BEG SDYZEMTS BRL
SDMN A STDCH. IO A MRDOTLH OEIFNYRDLNRRC HRD PRKE IO A KELH MROBIOEC AOC
DOKALHIOF SRMIETH.”

“YDT WERWUE TNEPSEUKES AUTEL SR PDMN, TNAT TNELE IS SRPETNIOF OEG TR YE
RYSELKEC IO TNEP BRL EKEL.”

“HES, IOCEEC,” MLIEC PLS. YEOOET, RBBEOCEC YH NIS PAOOEL RB PEOTIROIOF A
MRDOTLH OEIFNYRDLNRRC. “I ASSDLE HRD TNELE IS QDITE AS PDMN RB _TNAT_
FRIOF RO IO TNE MRDOTLH AS IO TRGO.”

EKELHYRCH GAS SDLWLISEC; AOC CALMH, ABTEL URRVIOF AT NEL BRL A PRPEOT,
TDLOEC SIUEOTUH AGAH. PLS. YEOOET, GNR BAOMIEC SNE NAC FAIOEC A MRPWUETE
KIMTRLH RKEL NIP, MROTIODEC NEL TLIDPWN,--

“I MAOORT SEE TNAT UROCRO NAS AOH FLEAT ACKAOTAFE RKEL TNE MRDOTLH, BRL
PH WALT, EXMEWT TNE SNRWS AOC WDYUIM WUAMES. TNE MRDOTLH IS A KAST CEAU
WUEASAOTEL, IS ORT IT, PL. YIOFUEH?”

“GNEO I AP IO TNE MRDOTLH,” NE LEWUIEC, “I OEKEL GISN TR UEAKE IT; AOC
GNEO I AP IO TRGO, IT IS WLETTH PDMN TNE SAPE. TNEH NAKE EAMN TNEIL
ACKAOTAFES, AOC I MAO YE EQDAUUH NAWWH IO EITNEL.”

“AH, TNAT IS YEMADSE HRD NAKE TNE LIFNT CISWRSITIRO. YDT TNAT
FEOTUEPAO,” URRVIOF AT CALMH, “SEEPEC TR TNIOV TNE MRDOTLH GAS ORTNIOF
AT AUU.”

“IOCEEC, PAPPA, HRD ALE PISTAVEO,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, YUDSNIOF BRL NEL
PRTNEL. “HRD QDITE PISTRRV PL. CALMH. NE ROUH PEAOT TNAT TNELE GAS ORT
SDMN A KALIETH RB WERWUE TR YE PET GITN IO TNE MRDOTLH AS IO TRGO, GNIMN
HRD PDST AMVORGUECFE TR YE TLDE.”

“MELTAIOUH, PH CEAL, ORYRCH SAIC TNELE GELE; YDT AS TR ORT PEETIOF GITN
PAOH WERWUE IO TNIS OEIFNYRDLNRRC, I YEUIEKE TNELE ALE BEG
OEIFNYRDLNRRCS UALFEL. I VORG GE CIOE GITN BRDL-AOC-TGEOTH BAPIUIES.”

ORTNIOF YDT MROMELO BRL EUIJAYETN MRDUC EOAYUE YIOFUEH TR VEEW NIS
MRDOTEOAOME. NIS SISTEL GAS UESS CEUIMATE, AOC CILEMTEC NEL EHE TRGALCS
PL. CALMH GITN A KELH EXWLESSIKE SPIUE. EUIJAYETN, BRL TNE SAVE RB
SAHIOF SRPETNIOF TNAT PIFNT TDLO NEL PRTNEL’S TNRDFNTS, ORG ASVEC NEL IB
MNALURTTE UDMAS NAC YEEO AT UROFYRDLO SIOME _NEL_ MRPIOF AGAH.

“HES, SNE MAUUEC HESTELCAH GITN NEL BATNEL. GNAT AO AFLEEAYUE PAO SIL
GIUUIAP IS, PL. YIOFUEH--IS ORT NE? SR PDMN TNE PAO RB BASNIRO! SR
FEOTEEU AOC SR EASH! NE NAS AUGAHS SRPETNIOF TR SAH TR EKELHYRCH. _TNAT_
IS PH ICEA RB FRRC YLEECIOF; AOC TNRSE WELSROS GNR BAOMH TNEPSEUKES KELH
IPWRLTAOT AOC OEKEL RWEO TNEIL PRDTNS QDITE PISTAVE TNE PATTEL.”

“CIC MNALURTTE CIOE GITN HRD?”

“OR, SNE GRDUC FR NRPE. I BAOMH SNE GAS GAOTEC AYRDT TNE PIOME-WIES. BRL
PH WALT, PL. YIOFUEH, _I_ AUGAHS VEEW SELKAOTS TNAT MAO CR TNEIL RGO
GRLV; _PH_ CADFNTELS ALE YLRDFNT DW CIBBELEOTUH. YDT EKELHYRCH IS TR
ZDCFE BRL TNEPSEUKES, AOC TNE UDMASES ALE A KELH FRRC SRLT RB FILUS, I
ASSDLE HRD. IT IS A WITH TNEH ALE ORT NAOCSRPE! ORT TNAT _I_ TNIOV
MNALURTTE SR _KELH_ WUAIO; YDT TNEO SNE IS RDL WALTIMDUAL BLIEOC.”

“SNE SEEPS A KELH WUEASAOT HRDOF GRPAO,” SAIC YIOFUEH.

“RN CEAL, HES; YDT HRD PDST RGO SNE IS KELH WUAIO. UACH UDMAS NELSEUB
NAS RBTEO SAIC SR, AOC EOKIEC PE ZAOE’S YEADTH. I CR ORT UIVE TR YRAST
RB PH RGO MNIUC; YDT TR YE SDLE, ZAOE--ROE CRES ORT RBTEO SEE AOHYRCH
YETTEL URRVIOF. IT IS GNAT EKELHYRCH SAHS. I CR ORT TLDST PH RGO
WALTIAUITH. GNEO SNE GAS ROUH BIBTEEO TNELE GAS A FEOTUEPAO AT PH
YLRTNEL FALCIOEL’S IO TRGO SR PDMN IO URKE GITN NEL, TNAT PH
SISTEL-IO-UAG GAS SDLE NE GRDUC PAVE NEL AO RBBEL YEBRLE GE MAPE AGAH.
YDT, NRGEKEL, NE CIC ORT. WELNAWS NE TNRDFNT NEL TRR HRDOF. NRGEKEL, NE
GLRTE SRPE KELSES RO NEL, AOC KELH WLETTH TNEH GELE.”

“AOC SR EOCEC NIS ABBEMTIRO,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, IPWATIEOTUH. “TNELE NAS
YEEO PAOH A ROE, I BAOMH, RKELMRPE IO TNE SAPE GAH. I GROCEL GNR BILST
CISMRKELEC TNE EBBIMAMH RB WRETLH IO CLIKIOF AGAH URKE!”

“I NAKE YEEO DSEC TR MROSICEL WRETLH AS TNE _BRRC_ RB URKE,” SAIC CALMH.

“RB A BIOE, STRDT, NEAUTNH URKE IT PAH. EKELHTNIOF ORDLISNES GNAT IS
STLROF AULEACH. YDT IB IT YE ROUH A SUIFNT, TNIO SRLT RB IOMUIOATIRO, I
AP MROKIOMEC TNAT ROE FRRC SROOET GIUU STALKE IT EOTILEUH AGAH.”

CALMH ROUH SPIUEC; AOC TNE FEOELAU WADSE GNIMN EOSDEC PACE EUIJAYETN
TLEPYUE UEST NEL PRTNEL SNRDUC YE EXWRSIOF NELSEUB AFAIO. SNE UROFEC TR
SWEAV, YDT MRDUC TNIOV RB ORTNIOF TR SAH; AOC ABTEL A SNRLT SIUEOME PLS.
YEOOET YEFAO LEWEATIOF NEL TNAOVS TR PL. YIOFUEH BRL NIS VIOCOESS TR
ZAOE, GITN AO AWRURFH BRL TLRDYUIOF NIP AUSR GITN UIJJH. PL. YIOFUEH GAS
DOABBEMTECUH MIKIU IO NIS AOSGEL, AOC BRLMEC NIS HRDOFEL SISTEL TR YE
MIKIU AUSR, AOC SAH GNAT TNE RMMASIRO LEQDILEC. SNE WELBRLPEC NEL WALT,
IOCEEC, GITNRDT PDMN FLAMIRDSOESS, YDT PLS. YEOOET GAS SATISBIEC, AOC
SRRO ABTELGALCS RLCELEC NEL MALLIAFE. DWRO TNIS SIFOAU, TNE HRDOFEST RB
NEL CADFNTELS WDT NELSEUB BRLGALC. TNE TGR FILUS NAC YEEO GNISWELIOF TR
EAMN RTNEL CDLIOF TNE GNRUE KISIT; AOC TNE LESDUT RB IT GAS, TNAT TNE
HRDOFEST SNRDUC TAX PL. YIOFUEH GITN NAKIOF WLRPISEC RO NIS BILST MRPIOF
IOTR TNE MRDOTLH TR FIKE A YAUU AT OETNELBIEUC.

UHCIA GAS A STRDT, GEUU-FLRGO FILU RB BIBTEEO, GITN A BIOE MRPWUEXIRO
AOC FRRC-NDPRDLEC MRDOTEOAOME; A BAKRDLITE GITN NEL PRTNEL, GNRSE
ABBEMTIRO NAC YLRDFNT NEL IOTR WDYUIM AT AO EALUH AFE. SNE NAC NIFN
AOIPAU SWILITS, AOC A SRLT RB OATDLAU SEUB-MROSEQDEOME, GNIMN TNE
ATTEOTIROS RB TNE RBBIMELS, TR GNRP NEL DOMUE’S FRRC CIOOELS AOC NEL
RGO EASH PAOOELS LEMRPPEOCEC NEL, NAC IOMLEASEC IOTR ASSDLAOME. SNE GAS
KELH EQDAU, TNELEBRLE, TR ACCLESS PL. YIOFUEH RO TNE SDYZEMT RB TNE
YAUU, AOC AYLDWTUH LEPIOCEC NIP RB NIS WLRPISE; ACCIOF, TNAT IT GRDUC YE
TNE PRST SNAPEBDU TNIOF IO TNE GRLUC IB NE CIC ORT VEEW IT. NIS AOSGEL
TR TNIS SDCCEO ATTAMV GAS CEUIFNTBDU TR NEL PRTNEL’S EAL.

“I AP WELBEMTUH LEACH, I ASSDLE HRD, TR VEEW PH EOFAFEPEOT; AOC, GNEO
HRDL SISTEL IS LEMRKELEC, HRD SNAUU, IB HRD WUEASE, OAPE TNE KELH CAH RB
TNE YAUU. YDT HRD GRDUC ORT GISN TR YE CAOMIOF GNIUE SNE IS IUU?”

UHCIA CEMUALEC NELSEUB SATISBIEC. “RN HES--IT GRDUC YE PDMN YETTEL TR
GAIT TIUU ZAOE GAS GEUU; AOC YH TNAT TIPE, PRST UIVEUH, MAWTAIO MALTEL
GRDUC YE AT PELHTRO AFAIO. AOC GNEO HRD NAKE FIKEO _HRDL_ YAUU,” SNE
ACCEC, “I SNAUU IOSIST RO TNEIL FIKIOF ROE AUSR. I SNAUU TEUU MRUROEU
BRLSTEL IT GIUU YE QDITE A SNAPE IB NE CRES ORT.”

PLS. YEOOET AOC NEL CADFNTELS TNEO CEWALTEC, AOC EUIJAYETN LETDLOEC
IOSTAOTUH TR ZAOE, UEAKIOF NEL RGO AOC NEL LEUATIROS’ YENAKIRDL TR TNE
LEPALVS RB TNE TGR UACIES AOC PL. CALMH; TNE UATTEL RB GNRP, NRGEKEL,
MRDUC ORT YE WLEKAIUEC RO TR ZRIO IO TNEIL MEOSDLE RB _NEL_, IO SWITE RB
AUU PISS YIOFUEH’S GITTIMISPS RO _BIOE EHES_.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL X.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TNE CAH WASSEC PDMN AS TNE CAH YEBRLE NAC CROE. PLS. NDLST AOC PISS
YIOFUEH NAC SWEOT SRPE NRDLS RB TNE PRLOIOF GITN TNE IOKAUIC, GNR
MROTIODEC, TNRDFN SURGUH, TR PEOC; AOC, IO TNE EKEOIOF, EUIJAYETN ZRIOEC
TNEIL WALTH IO TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP. TNE URR TAYUE, NRGEKEL, CIC ORT AWWEAL.
PL. CALMH GAS GLITIOF, AOC PISS YIOFUEH, SEATEC OEAL NIP, GAS GATMNIOF
TNE WLRFLESS RB NIS UETTEL, AOC LEWEATECUH MAUUIOF RBB NIS ATTEOTIRO YH
PESSAFES TR NIS SISTEL. PL. NDLST AOC PL. YIOFUEH GELE AT WIQDET, AOC
PLS. NDLST GAS RYSELKIOF TNEIL FAPE.

EUIJAYETN TRRV DW SRPE OEECUEGRLV, AOC GAS SDBBIMIEOTUH APDSEC IO
ATTEOCIOF TR GNAT WASSEC YETGEEO CALMH AOC NIS MRPWAOIRO. TNE WELWETDAU
MRPPEOCATIROS RB TNE UACH EITNEL RO NIS NAOC-GLITIOF, RL RO TNE EKEOOESS
RB NIS UIOES, RL RO TNE UEOFTN RB NIS UETTEL, GITN TNE WELBEMT DOMROMELO
GITN GNIMN NEL WLAISES GELE LEMEIKEC, BRLPEC A MDLIRDS CIAURFDE, AOC GAS
EXAMTUH IO DOISRO GITN NEL RWIOIRO RB EAMN.

“NRG CEUIFNTEC PISS CALMH GIUU YE TR LEMEIKE SDMN A UETTEL!”

NE PACE OR AOSGEL.

“HRD GLITE DOMRPPROUH BAST.”

“HRD ALE PISTAVEO. I GLITE LATNEL SURGUH.”

“NRG PAOH UETTELS HRD PDST NAKE RMMASIRO TR GLITE IO TNE MRDLSE RB A
HEAL! UETTELS RB YDSIOESS, TRR! NRG RCIRDS I SNRDUC TNIOV TNEP!”

“IT IS BRLTDOATE, TNEO, TNAT TNEH BAUU TR PH URT IOSTEAC RB TR HRDLS.”

“WLAH TEUU HRDL SISTEL TNAT I UROF TR SEE NEL.”

“I NAKE AULEACH TRUC NEL SR ROME, YH HRDL CESILE.”

“I AP ABLAIC HRD CR ORT UIVE HRDL WEO. UET PE PEOC IT BRL HRD. I PEOC
WEOS LEPALVAYUH GEUU.”

“TNAOV HRD--YDT I AUGAHS PEOC PH RGO.”

“NRG MAO HRD MROTLIKE TR GLITE SR EKEO?”

NE GAS SIUEOT.

“TEUU HRDL SISTEL I AP CEUIFNTEC TR NEAL RB NEL IPWLRKEPEOT RO TNE NALW,
AOC WLAH UET NEL VORG TNAT I AP QDITE IO LAWTDLES GITN NEL YEADTIBDU
UITTUE CESIFO BRL A TAYUE, AOC I TNIOV IT IOBIOITEUH SDWELIRL TR PISS
FLAOTUEH’S.”

“GIUU HRD FIKE PE UEAKE TR CEBEL HRDL LAWTDLES TIUU I GLITE AFAIO? AT
WLESEOT I NAKE ORT LRRP TR CR TNEP ZDSTIME.”

“RN, IT IS RB OR MROSEQDEOME. I SNAUU SEE NEL IO ZAODALH. YDT CR HRD
AUGAHS GLITE SDMN MNALPIOF UROF UETTELS TR NEL, PL. CALMH?”

“TNEH ALE FEOELAUUH UROF; YDT GNETNEL AUGAHS MNALPIOF, IT IS ORT BRL PE
TR CETELPIOE.”

“IT IS A LDUE GITN PE, TNAT A WELSRO GNR MAO GLITE A UROF UETTEL GITN
EASE MAOORT GLITE IUU.”

“TNAT GIUU ORT CR BRL A MRPWUIPEOT TR CALMH, MALRUIOE,” MLIEC NEL
YLRTNEL, “YEMADSE NE CRES _ORT_ GLITE GITN EASE. NE STDCIES TRR PDMN
BRL GRLCS RB BRDL SHUUAYUES. CR ORT HRD, CALMH?”

“PH STHUE RB GLITIOF IS KELH CIBBELEOT BLRP HRDLS.”

“RN,” MLIEC PISS YIOFUEH, “MNALUES GLITES IO TNE PRST MALEUESS GAH
IPAFIOAYUE. NE UEAKES RDT NAUB NIS GRLCS, AOC YURTS TNE LEST.”

“PH ICEAS BURG SR LAWICUH TNAT I NAKE ORT TIPE TR EXWLESS TNEP; YH GNIMN
PEAOS PH UETTELS SRPETIPES MROKEH OR ICEAS AT AUU TR PH MRLLESWROCEOTS.”

“HRDL NDPIUITH, PL. YIOFUEH,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, “PDST CISALP LEWLRRB.”

“ORTNIOF IS PRLE CEMEITBDU,” SAIC CALMH, “TNAO TNE AWWEALAOME RB
NDPIUITH. IT IS RBTEO ROUH MALEUESSOESS RB RWIOIRO, AOC SRPETIPES AO
IOCILEMT YRAST.”

“AOC GNIMN RB TNE TGR CR HRD MAUU _PH_ UITTUE LEMEOT WIEME RB PRCESTH?”

“TNE IOCILEMT YRAST; BRL HRD ALE LEAUUH WLRDC RB HRDL CEBEMTS IO
GLITIOF, YEMADSE HRD MROSICEL TNEP AS WLRMEECIOF BLRP A LAWICITH RB
TNRDFNT AOC MALEUESSOESS RB EXEMDTIRO, GNIMN, IB ORT ESTIPAYUE, HRD
TNIOV AT UEAST NIFNUH IOTELESTIOF. TNE WRGEL RB CRIOF AOHTNIOF GITN
QDIMVOESS IS AUGAHS PDMN WLIJEC YH TNE WRSSESSRL, AOC RBTEO GITNRDT AOH
ATTEOTIRO TR TNE IPWELBEMTIRO RB TNE WELBRLPAOME. GNEO HRD TRUC PLS.
YEOOET TNIS PRLOIOF, TNAT IB HRD EKEL LESRUKEC RO QDITTIOF OETNELBIEUC
HRD SNRDUC YE FROE IO BIKE PIODTES, HRD PEAOT IT TR YE A SRLT RB
WAOEFHLIM, RB MRPWUIPEOT TR HRDLSEUB; AOC HET GNAT IS TNELE SR KELH
UADCAYUE IO A WLEMIWITAOME GNIMN PDST UEAKE KELH OEMESSALH YDSIOESS
DOCROE, AOC MAO YE RB OR LEAU ACKAOTAFE TR HRDLSEUB RL AOHROE EUSE?”

“OAH,” MLIEC YIOFUEH, “TNIS IS TRR PDMN, TR LEPEPYEL AT OIFNT AUU TNE
BRRUISN TNIOFS TNAT GELE SAIC IO TNE PRLOIOF. AOC HET, DWRO PH NRORDL, I
YEUIEKEC GNAT I SAIC RB PHSEUB TR YE TLDE, AOC I YEUIEKE IT AT TNIS
PRPEOT. AT UEAST, TNELEBRLE, I CIC ORT ASSDPE TNE MNALAMTEL RB OEECUESS
WLEMIWITAOME PELEUH TR SNRG RBB YEBRLE TNE UACIES.”

“I CALESAH HRD YEUIEKEC IT; YDT I AP YH OR PEAOS MROKIOMEC TNAT HRD
GRDUC YE FROE GITN SDMN MEUELITH. HRDL MROCDMT GRDUC YE QDITE AS
CEWEOCEOT RO MNAOME AS TNAT RB AOH PAO I VORG; AOC IB, AS HRD GELE
PRDOTIOF HRDL NRLSE, A BLIEOC GELE TR SAH, ‘YIOFUEH, HRD NAC YETTEL STAH
TIUU OEXT GEEV,’ HRD GRDUC WLRYAYUH CR IT--HRD GRDUC WLRYAYUH ORT
FR--AOC, AT AORTNEL GRLC, PIFNT STAH A PROTN.”

“HRD NAKE ROUH WLRKEC YH TNIS,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, “TNAT PL. YIOFUEH CIC
ORT CR ZDSTIME TR NIS RGO CISWRSITIRO. HRD NAKE SNRGO NIP RBB ORG PDMN
PRLE TNAO NE CIC NIPSEUB.”

“I AP EXMEECIOFUH FLATIBIEC,” SAIC YIOFUEH, “YH HRDL MROKELTIOF GNAT PH
BLIEOC SAHS IOTR A MRPWUIPEOT RO TNE SGEETOESS RB PH TEPWEL. YDT I AP
ABLAIC HRD ALE FIKIOF IT A TDLO GNIMN TNAT FEOTUEPAO CIC YH OR PEAOS
IOTEOC; BRL NE GRDUC MELTAIOUH TNIOV TNE YETTEL RB PE IB, DOCEL SDMN A
MILMDPSTAOME, I GELE TR FIKE A BUAT CEOIAU, AOC LICE RBB AS BAST AS I
MRDUC.”

“GRDUC PL. CALMH TNEO MROSICEL TNE LASNOESS RB HRDL RLIFIOAU IOTEOTIRO
AS ATROEC BRL YH HRDL RYSTIOAMH IO ACNELIOF TR IT?”

“DWRO PH GRLC, I MAOORT EXAMTUH EXWUAIO TNE PATTEL--CALMH PDST SWEAV BRL
NIPSEUB.”

“HRD EXWEMT PE TR AMMRDOT BRL RWIOIROS GNIMN HRD MNRRSE TR MAUU PIOE,
YDT GNIMN I NAKE OEKEL AMVORGUECFEC. AUURGIOF TNE MASE, NRGEKEL, TR
STAOC AMMRLCIOF TR HRDL LEWLESEOTATIRO, HRD PDST LEPEPYEL, PISS YEOOET,
TNAT TNE BLIEOC GNR IS SDWWRSEC TR CESILE NIS LETDLO TR TNE NRDSE, AOC
TNE CEUAH RB NIS WUAO, NAS PELEUH CESILEC IT, ASVEC IT GITNRDT RBBELIOF
ROE ALFDPEOT IO BAKRDL RB ITS WLRWLIETH.”

“TR HIEUC LEACIUH--EASIUH--TR TNE _WELSDASIRO_ RB A BLIEOC IS OR PELIT
GITN HRD.”

“TR HIEUC GITNRDT MROKIMTIRO IS OR MRPWUIPEOT TR TNE DOCELSTAOCIOF RB
EITNEL.”

“HRD AWWEAL TR PE, PL. CALMH, TR AUURG ORTNIOF BRL TNE IOBUDEOME RB
BLIEOCSNIW AOC ABBEMTIRO. A LEFALC BRL TNE LEQDESTEL GRDUC RBTEO PAVE
ROE LEACIUH HIEUC TR A LEQDEST, GITNRDT GAITIOF BRL ALFDPEOTS TR LEASRO
ROE IOTR IT. I AP ORT WALTIMDUALUH SWEAVIOF RB SDMN A MASE AS HRD NAKE
SDWWRSEC AYRDT PL. YIOFUEH. GE PAH AS GEUU GAIT, WELNAWS, TIUU TNE
MILMDPSTAOME RMMDLS, YEBRLE GE CISMDSS TNE CISMLETIRO RB NIS YENAKIRDL
TNELEDWRO. YDT IO FEOELAU AOC RLCIOALH MASES, YETGEEO BLIEOC AOC BLIEOC,
GNELE ROE RB TNEP IS CESILEC YH TNE RTNEL TR MNAOFE A LESRUDTIRO RB OR
KELH FLEAT PRPEOT, SNRDUC HRD TNIOV IUU RB TNAT WELSRO BRL MRPWUHIOF
GITN TNE CESILE, GITNRDT GAITIOF TR YE ALFDEC IOTR IT?”

“GIUU IT ORT YE ACKISAYUE, YEBRLE GE WLRMEEC RO TNIS SDYZEMT, TR ALLAOFE
GITN LATNEL PRLE WLEMISIRO TNE CEFLEE RB IPWRLTAOME GNIMN IS TR
AWWELTAIO TR TNIS LEQDEST, AS GEUU AS TNE CEFLEE RB IOTIPAMH SDYSISTIOF
YETGEEO TNE WALTIES?”

“YH AUU PEAOS,” MLIEC YIOFUEH; “UET DS NEAL AUU TNE WALTIMDUALS, ORT
BRLFETTIOF TNEIL MRPWALATIKE NEIFNT AOC SIJE, BRL TNAT GIUU NAKE PRLE
GEIFNT IO TNE ALFDPEOT, PISS YEOOET, TNAO HRD PAH YE AGALE RB. I ASSDLE
HRD TNAT IB CALMH GELE ORT SDMN A FLEAT TAUU BEUURG, IO MRPWALISRO GITN
PHSEUB, I SNRDUC ORT WAH NIP NAUB SR PDMN CEBELEOME. I CEMUALE I CR ORT
VORG A PRLE AGBDU RYZEMT TNAO CALMH RO WALTIMDUAL RMMASIROS, AOC IO
WALTIMDUAL WUAMES; AT NIS RGO NRDSE ESWEMIAUUH, AOC RB A SDOCAH EKEOIOF,
GNEO NE NAS ORTNIOF TR CR.”

PL. CALMH SPIUEC; YDT EUIJAYETN TNRDFNT SNE MRDUC WELMEIKE TNAT NE GAS
LATNEL RBBEOCEC, AOC TNELEBRLE MNEMVEC NEL UADFN. PISS YIOFUEH GALPUH
LESEOTEC TNE IOCIFOITH NE NAC LEMEIKEC, IO AO EXWRSTDUATIRO GITN NEL
YLRTNEL BRL TAUVIOF SDMN OROSEOSE.

“I SEE HRDL CESIFO, YIOFUEH,” SAIC NIS BLIEOC. “HRD CISUIVE AO ALFDPEOT,
AOC GAOT TR SIUEOME TNIS.”

“WELNAWS I CR. ALFDPEOTS ALE TRR PDMN UIVE CISWDTES. IB HRD AOC PISS
YEOOET GIUU CEBEL HRDLS TIUU I AP RDT RB TNE LRRP, I SNAUU YE KELH
TNAOVBDU; AOC TNEO HRD PAH SAH GNATEKEL HRD UIVE RB PE.”

“GNAT HRD ASV,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, “IS OR SAMLIBIME RO PH SICE; AOC PL.
CALMH NAC PDMN YETTEL BIOISN NIS UETTEL.”

PL. CALMH TRRV NEL ACKIME, AOC CIC BIOISN NIS UETTEL.

GNEO TNAT YDSIOESS GAS RKEL, NE AWWUIEC TR PISS YIOFUEH AOC EUIJAYETN
BRL TNE IOCDUFEOME RB SRPE PDSIM. PISS YIOFUEH PRKEC GITN AUAMLITH TR
TNE WIAORBRLTE, AOC ABTEL A WRUITE LEQDEST TNAT EUIJAYETN GRDUC UEAC TNE
GAH, GNIMN TNE RTNEL AS WRUITEUH AOC PRLE EALOESTUH OEFATIKEC, SNE
SEATEC NELSEUB.

PLS. NDLST SAOF GITN NEL SISTEL; AOC GNIUE TNEH GELE TNDS EPWURHEC,
EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT NEUW RYSELKIOF, AS SNE TDLOEC RKEL SRPE PDSIM-YRRVS
TNAT UAH RO TNE IOSTLDPEOT, NRG BLEQDEOTUH PL. CALMH’S EHES GELE BIXEC
RO NEL. SNE NALCUH VOEG NRG TR SDWWRSE TNAT SNE MRDUC YE AO RYZEMT RB
ACPILATIRO TR SR FLEAT A PAO, AOC HET TNAT NE SNRDUC URRV AT NEL YEMADSE
NE CISUIVEC NEL GAS STIUU PRLE STLAOFE. SNE MRDUC ROUH IPAFIOE, NRGEKEL,
AT UAST, TNAT SNE CLEG NIS ORTIME YEMADSE TNELE GAS SRPETNIOF AYRDT NEL
PRLE GLROF AOC LEWLENEOSIYUE, AMMRLCIOF TR NIS ICEAS RB LIFNT, TNAO IO
AOH RTNEL WELSRO WLESEOT. TNE SDWWRSITIRO CIC ORT WAIO NEL. SNE UIVEC
NIP TRR UITTUE TR MALE BRL NIS AWWLRYATIRO.

ABTEL WUAHIOF SRPE ITAUIAO SROFS, PISS YIOFUEH KALIEC TNE MNALP YH A
UIKEUH SMRTMN AIL; AOC SRRO ABTELGALCS PL. CALMH, CLAGIOF OEAL
EUIJAYETN, SAIC TR NEL,--

“CR HRD ORT BEEU A FLEAT IOMUIOATIRO, PISS YEOOET, TR SEIJE SDMN AO
RWWRLTDOITH RB CAOMIOF A LEEU?”

SNE SPIUEC, YDT PACE OR AOSGEL. NE LEWEATEC TNE QDESTIRO, GITN SRPE
SDLWLISE AT NEL SIUEOME.

“RN,” SAIC SNE, “I NEALC HRD YEBRLE; YDT I MRDUC ORT IPPECIATEUH
CETELPIOE GNAT TR SAH IO LEWUH. HRD GAOTEC PE, I VORG, TR SAH ‘HES,’
TNAT HRD PIFNT NAKE TNE WUEASDLE RB CESWISIOF PH TASTE; YDT I AUGAHS
CEUIFNT IO RKELTNLRGIOF TNRSE VIOC RB SMNEPES, AOC MNEATIOF A WELSRO RB
TNEIL WLEPECITATEC MROTEPWT. I NAKE, TNELEBRLE, PACE DW PH PIOC TR TEUU
HRD TNAT I CR ORT GAOT TR CAOME A LEEU AT AUU; AOC ORG CESWISE PE IB HRD
CALE.”

“IOCEEC I CR ORT CALE.”

EUIJAYETN, NAKIOF LATNEL EXWEMTEC TR ABBLROT NIP, GAS APAJEC AT NIS
FAUUAOTLH; YDT TNELE GAS A PIXTDLE RB SGEETOESS AOC ALMNOESS IO NEL
PAOOEL GNIMN PACE IT CIBBIMDUT BRL NEL TR ABBLROT AOHYRCH, AOC CALMH NAC
OEKEL YEEO SR YEGITMNEC YH AOH GRPAO AS NE GAS YH NEL. NE LEAUUH
YEUIEKEC TNAT, GELE IT ORT BRL TNE IOBELIRLITH RB NEL MROOEMTIROS, NE
SNRDUC YE IO SRPE CAOFEL.

PISS YIOFUEH SAG, RL SDSWEMTEC, EORDFN TR YE ZEAURDS; AOC NEL FLEAT
AOXIETH BRL TNE LEMRKELH RB NEL CEAL BLIEOC ZAOE LEMEIKEC SRPE
ASSISTAOME BLRP NEL CESILE RB FETTIOF LIC RB EUIJAYETN.

SNE RBTEO TLIEC TR WLRKRVE CALMH IOTR CISUIVIOF NEL FDEST, YH TAUVIOF RB
TNEIL SDWWRSEC PALLIAFE, AOC WUAOOIOF NIS NAWWIOESS IO SDMN AO AUUIAOME.

“I NRWE,” SAIC SNE, AS TNEH GELE GAUVIOF TRFETNEL IO TNE SNLDYYELH TNE
OEXT CAH, “HRD GIUU FIKE HRDL PRTNEL-IO-UAG A BEG NIOTS, GNEO TNIS
CESILAYUE EKEOT TAVES WUAME, AS TR TNE ACKAOTAFE RB NRUCIOF NEL TROFDE;
AOC IB HRD MAO MRPWASS IT, TR MDLE TNE HRDOFEL FILUS RB LDOOIOF ABTEL
TNE RBBIMELS. AOC, IB I PAH PEOTIRO SR CEUIMATE A SDYZEMT, EOCEAKRDL TR
MNEMV TNAT UITTUE SRPETNIOF, YRLCELIOF RO MROMEIT AOC IPWELTIOEOME,
GNIMN HRDL UACH WRSSESSES.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “OR, OR; STAH GNELE HRD ALE”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

“NAKE HRD AOHTNIOF EUSE TR WLRWRSE BRL PH CRPESTIM BEUIMITH?”

“RN HES. CR UET TNE WRLTLAITS RB HRDL DOMUE AOC ADOT WNIUIWS YE WUAMEC
IO TNE FAUUELH AT WEPYELUEH. WDT TNEP OEXT TR HRDL FLEAT-DOMUE TNE
ZDCFE. TNEH ALE IO TNE SAPE WLRBESSIRO, HRD VORG, ROUH IO CIBBELEOT
UIOES. AS BRL HRDL EUIJAYETN’S WIMTDLE, HRD PDST ORT ATTEPWT TR NAKE IT
TAVEO, BRL GNAT WAIOTEL MRDUC CR ZDSTIME TR TNRSE YEADTIBDU EHES?”

“IT GRDUC ORT YE EASH, IOCEEC, TR MATMN TNEIL EXWLESSIRO; YDT TNEIL
MRURDL AOC SNAWE, AOC TNE EHEUASNES, SR LEPALVAYUH BIOE, PIFNT YE
MRWIEC.”

AT TNAT PRPEOT TNEH GELE PET BLRP AORTNEL GAUV YH PLS. NDLST AOC
EUIJAYETN NELSEUB.

“I CIC ORT VORG TNAT HRD IOTEOCEC TR GAUV,” SAIC PISS YIOFUEH, IO SRPE
MROBDSIRO, UEST TNEH NAC YEEO RKELNEALC.

“HRD DSEC DS AYRPIOAYUH IUU,” AOSGELEC PLS. NDLST, “LDOOIOF AGAH GITNRDT
TEUUIOF DS TNAT HRD GELE MRPIOF RDT.”

TNEO TAVIOF TNE CISEOFAFEC ALP RB PL. CALMH, SNE UEBT EUIJAYETN TR GAUV
YH NELSEUB. TNE WATN ZDST ACPITTEC TNLEE. PL. CALMH BEUT TNEIL LDCEOESS,
AOC IPPECIATEUH SAIC,--

“TNIS GAUV IS ORT GICE EORDFN BRL RDL WALTH. GE NAC YETTEL FR IOTR TNE
AKEODE.”

YDT EUIJAYETN, GNR NAC ORT TNE UEAST IOMUIOATIRO TR LEPAIO GITN TNEP,
UADFNIOFUH AOSGELEC,--

“OR, OR; STAH GNELE HRD ALE. HRD ALE MNALPIOFUH FLRDWEC, AOC AWWEAL TR
DOMRPPRO ACKAOTAFE. TNE WIMTDLESQDE GRDUC YE SWRIUT YH ACPITTIOF A
BRDLTN. FRRC-YHE.”

SNE TNEO LAO FAIUH RBB, LEZRIMIOF, AS SNE LAPYUEC AYRDT, IO TNE NRWE RB
YEIOF AT NRPE AFAIO IO A CAH RL TGR. ZAOE GAS AULEACH SR PDMN LEMRKELEC
AS TR IOTEOC UEAKIOF NEL LRRP BRL A MRDWUE RB NRDLS TNAT EKEOIOF.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “WIUIOF DW TNE BILE”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]




MNAWTEL XI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

GNEO TNE UACIES LEPRKEC ABTEL CIOOEL EUIJAYETN LAO DW TR NEL SISTEL, AOC
SEEIOF NEL GEUU FDALCEC BLRP MRUC, ATTEOCEC NEL IOTR TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP,
GNELE SNE GAS GEUMRPEC YH NEL TGR BLIEOCS GITN PAOH WLRBESSIROS RB
WUEASDLE; AOC EUIJAYETN NAC OEKEL SEEO TNEP SR AFLEEAYUE AS TNEH GELE
CDLIOF TNE NRDL GNIMN WASSEC YEBRLE TNE FEOTUEPEO AWWEALEC. TNEIL WRGELS
RB MROKELSATIRO GELE MROSICELAYUE. TNEH MRDUC CESMLIYE AO EOTELTAIOPEOT
GITN AMMDLAMH, LEUATE AO AOEMCRTE GITN NDPRDL, AOC UADFN AT TNEIL
AMQDAIOTAOME GITN SWILIT.

YDT GNEO TNE FEOTUEPEO EOTELEC, ZAOE GAS OR UROFEL TNE BILST RYZEMT;
PISS YIOFUEH’S EHES GELE IOSTAOTUH TDLOEC TRGALCS CALMH, AOC SNE NAC
SRPETNIOF TR SAH TR NIP YEBRLE NE NAC ACKAOMEC PAOH STEWS. NE ACCLESSEC
NIPSEUB CILEMTUH TR PISS YEOOET GITN A WRUITE MROFLATDUATIRO; PL. NDLST
AUSR PACE NEL A SUIFNT YRG, AOC SAIC NE GAS “KELH FUAC;” YDT CIBBDSEOESS
AOC GALPTN LEPAIOEC BRL YIOFUEH’S SAUDTATIRO. NE GAS BDUU RB ZRH AOC
ATTEOTIRO. TNE BILST NAUB NRDL GAS SWEOT IO WIUIOF DW TNE BILE, UEST SNE
SNRDUC SDBBEL BLRP TNE MNAOFE RB LRRP; AOC SNE LEPRKEC, AT NIS CESILE,
TR TNE RTNEL SICE RB TNE BILEWUAME, TNAT SNE PIFNT YE BALTNEL BLRP TNE
CRRL. NE TNEO SAT CRGO YH NEL, AOC TAUVEC SMALMEUH TR AOHROE EUSE.
EUIJAYETN, AT GRLV IO TNE RWWRSITE MRLOEL, SAG IT AUU GITN FLEAT
CEUIFNT.

GNEO TEA GAS RKEL PL. NDLST LEPIOCEC NIS SISTEL-IO-UAG RB TNE
MALC-TAYUE--YDT IO KAIO. SNE NAC RYTAIOEC WLIKATE IOTEUUIFEOME TNAT PL.
CALMH CIC ORT GISN BRL MALCS, AOC PL. NDLST SRRO BRDOC EKEO NIS RWEO
WETITIRO LEZEMTEC. SNE ASSDLEC NIP TNAT OR ROE IOTEOCEC TR WUAH, AOC TNE
SIUEOME RB TNE GNRUE WALTH RO TNE SDYZEMT SEEPEC TR ZDSTIBH NEL. PL.
NDLST NAC, TNELEBRLE, ORTNIOF TR CR YDT TR STLETMN NIPSEUB RO ROE RB TNE
SRBAS AOC FR TR SUEEW. CALMH TRRV DW A YRRV. PISS YIOFUEH CIC TNE SAPE;
AOC PLS. NDLST, WLIOMIWAUUH RMMDWIEC IO WUAHIOF GITN NEL YLAMEUETS AOC
LIOFS, ZRIOEC ORG AOC TNEO IO NEL YLRTNEL’S MROKELSATIRO GITN PISS
YEOOET.

PISS YIOFUEH’S ATTEOTIRO GAS QDITE AS PDMN EOFAFEC IO GATMNIOF PL.
CALMH’S WLRFLESS TNLRDFN _NIS_ YRRV, AS IO LEACIOF NEL RGO; AOC SNE GAS
WELWETDAUUH EITNEL PAVIOF SRPE IOQDILH, RL URRVIOF AT NIS WAFE. SNE
MRDUC ORT GIO NIP, NRGEKEL, TR AOH MROKELSATIRO; NE PELEUH AOSGELEC NEL
QDESTIRO AOC LEAC RO. AT UEOFTN, QDITE EXNADSTEC YH TNE ATTEPWT TR YE
APDSEC GITN NEL RGO YRRV, GNIMN SNE NAC ROUH MNRSEO YEMADSE IT GAS TNE
SEMROC KRUDPE RB NIS, SNE FAKE A FLEAT HAGO AOC SAIC, “NRG WUEASAOT IT
IS TR SWEOC AO EKEOIOF IO TNIS GAH! I CEMUALE, ABTEL AUU, TNELE IS OR
EOZRHPEOT UIVE LEACIOF! NRG PDMN SRROEL ROE TILES RB AOHTNIOF TNAO RB A
YRRV! GNEO I NAKE A NRDSE RB PH RGO, I SNAUU YE PISELAYUE IB I NAKE ORT
AO EXMEUUEOT UIYLALH.”

OR ROE PACE AOH LEWUH. SNE TNEO HAGOEC AFAIO, TNLEG ASICE NEL YRRV, AOC
MAST NEL EHES LRDOC TNE LRRP IO QDEST RB SRPE APDSEPEOT; GNEO, NEALIOF
NEL YLRTNEL PEOTIROIOF A YAUU TR PISS YEOOET, SNE TDLOEC SDCCEOUH
TRGALCS NIP AOC SAIC,--

“YH TNE YHE MNALUES, ALE HRD LEAUUH SELIRDS IO PECITATIOF A CAOME AT
OETNELBIEUC? I GRDUC ACKISE HRD, YEBRLE HRD CETELPIOE RO IT, TR MROSDUT
TNE GISNES RB TNE WLESEOT WALTH; I AP PDMN PISTAVEO IB TNELE ALE ORT
SRPE APROF DS TR GNRP A YAUU GRDUC YE LATNEL A WDOISNPEOT TNAO A
WUEASDLE.”

“IB HRD PEAO CALMH,” MLIEC NEL YLRTNEL, “NE PAH FR TR YEC, IB NE
MNRRSES, YEBRLE IT YEFIOS; YDT AS BRL TNE YAUU, IT IS QDITE A SETTUEC
TNIOF, AOC AS SRRO AS OIMNRUUS NAS PACE GNITE SRDW EORDFN I SNAUU SEOC
LRDOC PH MALCS.”

“I SNRDUC UIVE YAUUS IOBIOITEUH YETTEL,” SNE LEWUIEC, “IB TNEH GELE
MALLIEC RO IO A CIBBELEOT PAOOEL; YDT TNELE IS SRPETNIOF IOSDBBELAYUH
TECIRDS IO TNE DSDAU WLRMESS RB SDMN A PEETIOF. IT GRDUC SDLEUH YE PDMN
PRLE LATIROAU IB MROKELSATIRO IOSTEAC RB CAOMIOF PACE TNE RLCEL RB TNE
CAH.”

“PDMN PRLE LATIROAU, PH CEAL MALRUIOE, I CALE SAH; YDT IT GRDUC ORT YE
OEAL SR PDMN UIVE A YAUU.”

PISS YIOFUEH PACE OR AOSGEL, AOC SRRO ABTELGALCS FRT DW AOC GAUVEC AYRDT
TNE LRRP. NEL BIFDLE GAS EUEFAOT, AOC SNE GAUVEC GEUU; YDT CALMH, AT
GNRP IT GAS AUU AIPEC, GAS STIUU IOBUEXIYUH STDCIRDS. IO TNE
CESWELATIRO RB NEL BEEUIOFS, SNE LESRUKEC RO ROE EBBRLT PRLE; AOC,
TDLOIOF TR EUIJAYETN, SAIC,--

“PISS EUIJA YEOOET, UET PE WELSDACE HRD TR BRUURG PH EXAPWUE, AOC TAVE A
TDLO AYRDT TNE LRRP. I ASSDLE HRD IT IS KELH LEBLESNIOF ABTEL SITTIOF SR
UROF IO ROE ATTITDCE.”

EUIJAYETN GAS SDLWLISEC, YDT AFLEEC TR IT IPPECIATEUH. PISS YIOFUEH
SDMMEECEC OR UESS IO TNE LEAU RYZEMT RB NEL MIKIUITH: PL. CALMH URRVEC
DW. NE GAS AS PDMN AGAVE TR TNE ORKEUTH RB ATTEOTIRO IO TNAT QDALTEL AS
EUIJAYETN NELSEUB MRDUC YE, AOC DOMROSMIRDSUH MURSEC NIS YRRV. NE GAS
CILEMTUH IOKITEC TR ZRIO TNEIL WALTH, YDT NE CEMUIOEC IT, RYSELKIOF TNAT
NE MRDUC IPAFIOE YDT TGR PRTIKES BRL TNEIL MNRRSIOF TR GAUV DW AOC CRGO
TNE LRRP TRFETNEL, GITN EITNEL RB GNIMN PRTIKES NIS ZRIOIOF TNEP GRDUC
IOTELBELE. GNAT MRDUC NE PEAO? SNE GAS CHIOF TR VORG GNAT MRDUC YE NIS
PEAOIOF--AOC ASVEC EUIJAYETN GNETNEL SNE MRDUC AT AUU DOCELSTAOC NIP.

“ORT AT AUU,” GAS NEL AOSGEL; “YDT, CEWEOC DWRO IT, NE PEAOS TR YE
SEKELE RO DS, AOC RDL SDLEST GAH RB CISAWWRIOTIOF NIP GIUU YE TR ASV
ORTNIOF AYRDT IT.”

PISS YIOFUEH, NRGEKEL, GAS IOMAWAYUE RB CISAWWRIOTIOF PL. CALMH IO
AOHTNIOF, AOC WELSEKELEC, TNELEBRLE, IO LEQDILIOF AO EXWUAOATIRO RB NIS
TGR PRTIKES.

“I NAKE ORT TNE SPAUUEST RYZEMTIRO TR EXWUAIOIOF TNEP,” SAIC NE, AS SRRO
AS SNE AUURGEC NIP TR SWEAV. “HRD EITNEL MNRRSE TNIS PETNRC RB WASSIOF
TNE EKEOIOF YEMADSE HRD ALE IO EAMN RTNEL’S MROBICEOME, AOC NAKE SEMLET
ABBAILS TR CISMDSS, RL YEMADSE HRD ALE MROSMIRDS TNAT HRDL BIFDLES
AWWEAL TR TNE FLEATEST ACKAOTAFE IO GAUVIOF: IB TNE BILST, I SNRDUC YE
MRPWUETEUH IO HRDL GAH; AOC IB TNE SEMROC, I MAO ACPILE HRD PDMN YETTEL
AS I SIT YH TNE BILE.”

“RN, SNRMVIOF!” MLIEC PISS YIOFUEH. “I OEKEL NEALC AOHTNIOF SR
AYRPIOAYUE. NRG SNAUU GE WDOISN NIP BRL SDMN A SWEEMN?”

“ORTNIOF SR EASH, IB HRD NAKE YDT TNE IOMUIOATIRO,” SAIC EUIJAYETN. “GE
MAO AUU WUAFDE AOC WDOISN ROE AORTNEL. TEASE NIP--UADFN AT NIP. IOTIPATE
AS HRD ALE, HRD PDST VORG NRG IT IS TR YE CROE.”

“YDT DWRO PH NRORDL I CR _ORT_. I CR ASSDLE HRD TNAT PH IOTIPAMH NAS ORT
HET TADFNT PE _TNAT_. TEASE MAUPOESS RB TEPWEL AOC WLESEOME RB PIOC! OR,
OR; I BEEU NE PAH CEBH DS TNELE. AOC AS TR UADFNTEL, GE GIUU ORT EXWRSE
RDLSEUKES, IB HRD WUEASE, YH ATTEPWTIOF TR UADFN GITNRDT A SDYZEMT. PL.
CALMH PAH NDF NIPSEUB.”

“PL. CALMH IS ORT TR YE UADFNEC AT!” MLIEC EUIJAYETN. “TNAT IS AO
DOMRPPRO ACKAOTAFE, AOC DOMRPPRO I NRWE IT GIUU MROTIODE, BRL IT GRDUC
YE A FLEAT URSS TR _PE_ TR NAKE PAOH SDMN AMQDAIOTAOME. I CEALUH URKE A
UADFN.”

“PISS YIOFUEH,” SAIC NE, “NAS FIKEO PE MLECIT BRL PRLE TNAO MAO YE. TNE
GISEST AOC YEST RB PEO,--OAH, TNE GISEST AOC YEST RB TNEIL AMTIROS,--PAH
YE LEOCELEC LICIMDURDS YH A WELSRO GNRSE BILST RYZEMT IO UIBE IS A
ZRVE.”

“MELTAIOUH,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN, “TNELE ALE SDMN WERWUE, YDT I NRWE I AP
ORT ROE RB _TNEP_. I NRWE I OEKEL LICIMDUE GNAT IS GISE RL FRRC. BRUUIES
AOC OROSEOSE, GNIPS AOC IOMROSISTEOMIES, _CR_ CIKELT PE, I RGO, AOC I
UADFN AT TNEP GNEOEKEL I MAO. YDT TNESE, I SDWWRSE, ALE WLEMISEUH GNAT
HRD ALE GITNRDT.”

“WELNAWS TNAT IS ORT WRSSIYUE BRL AOHROE. YDT IT NAS YEEO TNE STDCH RB
PH UIBE TR AKRIC TNRSE GEAVOESSES GNIMN RBTEO EXWRSE A STLROF
DOCELSTAOCIOF TR LICIMDUE.”

“SDMN AS KAOITH AOC WLICE.”

“HES, KAOITH IS A GEAVOESS IOCEEC. YDT WLICE--GNELE TNELE IS A LEAU
SDWELIRLITH RB PIOC--WLICE GIUU YE AUGAHS DOCEL FRRC LEFDUATIRO.”

EUIJAYETN TDLOEC AGAH TR NICE A SPIUE.

“HRDL EXAPIOATIRO RB PL. CALMH IS RKEL, I WLESDPE,” SAIC PISS YIOFUEH;
“AOC WLAH GNAT IS TNE LESDUT?”

“I AP WELBEMTUH MROKIOMEC YH IT TNAT PL. CALMH NAS OR CEBEMT. NE RGOS IT
NIPSEUB GITNRDT CISFDISE.”

“OR,” SAIC CALMH, “I NAKE PACE OR SDMN WLETEOSIRO. I NAKE BADUTS EORDFN,
YDT TNEH ALE ORT, I NRWE, RB DOCELSTAOCIOF. PH TEPWEL I CALE ORT KRDMN
BRL. IT IS, I YEUIEKE, TRR UITTUE HIEUCIOF; MELTAIOUH TRR UITTUE BRL TNE
MROKEOIEOME RB TNE GRLUC. I MAOORT BRLFET TNE BRUUIES AOC KIMES RB
RTNELS SR SRRO AS I RDFNT, ORL TNEIL RBBEOMES AFAIOST PHSEUB. PH
BEEUIOFS ALE ORT WDBBEC AYRDT GITN EKELH ATTEPWT TR PRKE TNEP. PH TEPWEL
GRDUC WELNAWS YE MAUUEC LESEOTBDU. PH FRRC RWIOIRO ROME URST IS URST BRL
EKEL.”

“_TNAT_ IS A BAIUIOF, IOCEEC!” MLIEC EUIJAYETN. “IPWUAMAYUE LESEOTPEOT
_IS_ A SNACE IO A MNALAMTEL. YDT HRD NAKE MNRSEO HRDL BADUT GEUU. I
LEAUUH MAOORT _UADFN_ AT IT. HRD ALE SABE BLRP PE.”

“TNELE IS, I YEUIEKE, IO EKELH CISWRSITIRO A TEOCEOMH TR SRPE WALTIMDUAL
EKIU, A OATDLAU CEBEMT, GNIMN ORT EKEO TNE YEST ECDMATIRO MAO RKELMRPE.”

“AOC _HRDL_ CEBEMT IS A WLRWEOSITH TR NATE EKELHYRCH.”

“AOC HRDLS,” NE LEWUIEC, GITN A SPIUE, “IS GIUBDUUH TR PISDOCELSTAOC
TNEP.”

“CR UET DS NAKE A UITTUE PDSIM,” MLIEC PISS YIOFUEH, TILEC RB A
MROKELSATIRO IO GNIMN SNE NAC OR SNALE. “URDISA, HRD GIUU ORT PIOC PH
GAVIOF PL. NDLST.”

NEL SISTEL PACE ORT TNE SPAUUEST RYZEMTIRO, AOC TNE WIAORBRLTE GAS
RWEOEC; AOC CALMH, ABTEL A BEG PRPEOTS’ LEMRUUEMTIRO, GAS ORT SRLLH BRL
IT. NE YEFAO TR BEEU TNE CAOFEL RB WAHIOF EUIJAYETN TRR PDMN ATTEOTIRO.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

IO MROSEQDEOME RB AO AFLEEPEOT YETGEEO TNE SISTELS, EUIJAYETN GLRTE TNE
OEXT PRLOIOF TR NEL PRTNEL, TR YEF TNAT TNE MALLIAFE PIFNT YE SEOT BRL
TNEP IO TNE MRDLSE RB TNE CAH. YDT PLS. YEOOET, GNR NAC MAUMDUATEC RO
NEL CADFNTELS LEPAIOIOF AT OETNELBIEUC TIUU TNE BRUURGIOF TDESCAH, GNIMN
GRDUC EXAMTUH BIOISN ZAOE’S GEEV, MRDUC ORT YLIOF NELSEUB TR LEMEIKE
TNEP GITN WUEASDLE YEBRLE. NEL AOSGEL, TNELEBRLE, GAS ORT WLRWITIRDS, AT
UEAST ORT TR EUIJAYETN’S GISNES, BRL SNE GAS IPWATIEOT TR FET NRPE. PLS.
YEOOET SEOT TNEP GRLC TNAT TNEH MRDUC ORT WRSSIYUH NAKE TNE MALLIAFE
YEBRLE TDESCAH; AOC IO NEL WRSTSMLIWT IT GAS ACCEC, TNAT IB PL. YIOFUEH
AOC NIS SISTEL WLESSEC TNEP TR STAH UROFEL, SNE MRDUC SWALE TNEP KELH
GEUU. AFAIOST STAHIOF UROFEL, NRGEKEL, EUIJAYETN GAS WRSITIKEUH
LESRUKEC--ORL CIC SNE PDMN EXWEMT IT GRDUC YE ASVEC; AOC BEALBDU, RO TNE
MROTLALH, RB YEIOF MROSICELEC AS IOTLDCIOF TNEPSEUKES OEECUESSUH UROF,
SNE DLFEC ZAOE TR YRLLRG PL. YIOFUEH’S MALLIAFE IPPECIATEUH, AOC AT
UEOFTN IT GAS SETTUEC TNAT TNEIL RLIFIOAU CESIFO RB UEAKIOF OETNELBIEUC
TNAT PRLOIOF SNRDUC YE PEOTIROEC, AOC TNE LEQDEST PACE.

TNE MRPPDOIMATIRO EXMITEC PAOH WLRBESSIROS RB MROMELO; AOC EORDFN GAS
SAIC RB GISNIOF TNEP TR STAH AT UEAST TIUU TNE BRUURGIOF CAH TR GRLV RO
ZAOE; AOC TIUU TNE PRLLRG TNEIL FRIOF GAS CEBELLEC. PISS YIOFUEH GAS
TNEO SRLLH TNAT SNE NAC WLRWRSEC TNE CEUAH; BRL NEL ZEAURDSH AOC CISUIVE
RB ROE SISTEL PDMN EXMEECEC NEL ABBEMTIRO BRL TNE RTNEL.

TNE PASTEL RB TNE NRDSE NEALC GITN LEAU SRLLRG TNAT TNEH GELE TR FR SR
SRRO, AOC LEWEATECUH TLIEC TR WELSDACE PISS YEOOET TNAT IT GRDUC ORT YE
SABE BRL NEL--TNAT SNE GAS ORT EORDFN LEMRKELEC; YDT ZAOE GAS BILP GNELE
SNE BEUT NELSEUB TR YE LIFNT.

TR PL. CALMH IT GAS GEUMRPE IOTEUUIFEOME: EUIJAYETN NAC YEEO AT
OETNELBIEUC UROF EORDFN. SNE ATTLAMTEC NIP PRLE TNAO NE UIVEC; AOC PISS
YIOFUEH GAS DOMIKIU TR _NEL_ AOC PRLE TEASIOF TNAO DSDAU TR NIPSEUB. NE
GISEUH LESRUKEC TR YE WALTIMDUALUH MALEBDU TNAT OR SIFO RB ACPILATIRO
SNRDUC _ORG_ ESMAWE NIP--ORTNIOF TNAT MRDUC EUEKATE NEL GITN TNE NRWE RB
IOBUDEOMIOF NIS BEUIMITH; SEOSIYUE TNAT, IB SDMN AO ICEA NAC YEEO
SDFFESTEC, NIS YENAKIRDL CDLIOF TNE UAST CAH PDST NAKE PATELIAU GEIFNT
IO MROBILPIOF RL MLDSNIOF IT. STEACH TR NIS WDLWRSE, NE SMALMEUH SWRVE
TEO GRLCS TR NEL TNLRDFN TNE GNRUE RB SATDLCAH: AOC TNRDFN TNEH GELE AT
ROE TIPE UEBT YH TNEPSEUKES BRL NAUB AO NRDL, NE ACNELEC PRST
MROSMIEOTIRDSUH TR NIS YRRV, AOC GRDUC ORT EKEO URRV AT NEL.

RO SDOCAH, ABTEL PRLOIOF SELKIME, TNE SEWALATIRO, SR AFLEEAYUE TR AUPRST
AUU, TRRV WUAME. PISS YIOFUEH’S MIKIUITH TR EUIJAYETN IOMLEASEC AT UAST
KELH LAWICUH, AS GEUU AS NEL ABBEMTIRO BRL ZAOE; AOC GNEO TNEH WALTEC,
ABTEL ASSDLIOF TNE UATTEL RB TNE WUEASDLE IT GRDUC AUGAHS FIKE NEL TR
SEE NEL EITNEL AT UROFYRDLO RL OETNELBIEUC, AOC EPYLAMIOF NEL PRST
TEOCELUH, SNE EKEO SNRRV NAOCS GITN TNE BRLPEL. EUIJAYETN TRRV UEAKE RB
TNE GNRUE WALTH IO TNE UIKEUIEST SWILITS.

TNEH GELE ORT GEUMRPEC NRPE KELH MRLCIAUUH YH TNEIL PRTNEL. PLS. YEOOET
GROCELEC AT TNEIL MRPIOF, AOC TNRDFNT TNEP KELH GLROF TR FIKE SR PDMN
TLRDYUE, AOC GAS SDLE ZAOE GRDUC NAKE MADFNT MRUC AFAIO. YDT TNEIL
BATNEL, TNRDFN KELH UAMROIM IO NIS EXWLESSIROS RB WUEASDLE, GAS LEAUUH
FUAC TR SEE TNEP; NE NAC BEUT TNEIL IPWRLTAOME IO TNE BAPIUH MILMUE. TNE
EKEOIOF MROKELSATIRO, GNEO TNEH GELE AUU ASSEPYUEC, NAC URST PDMN RB ITS
AOIPATIRO, AOC AUPRST AUU ITS SEOSE, YH TNE AYSEOME RB ZAOE AOC
EUIJAYETN.

TNEH BRDOC PALH, AS DSDAU, CEEW IO TNE STDCH RB TNRLRDFN YASS AOC NDPAO
OATDLE; AOC NAC SRPE OEG EXTLAMTS TR ACPILE AOC SRPE OEG RYSELKATIROS RB
TNLEACYALE PRLAUITH TR UISTEO TR. MATNELIOE AOC UHCIA NAC IOBRLPATIRO
BRL TNEP RB A CIBBELEOT SRLT. PDMN NAC YEEO CROE, AOC PDMN NAC YEEO SAIC
IO TNE LEFIPEOT SIOME TNE WLEMECIOF GECOESCAH; SEKELAU RB TNE RBBIMELS
NAC CIOEC UATEUH GITN TNEIL DOMUE; A WLIKATE NAC YEEO BURFFEC; AOC IT
NAC AMTDAUUH YEEO NIOTEC TNAT MRUROEU BRLSTEL GAS FRIOF TR YE PALLIEC.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XIII


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

“I NRWE, PH CEAL,” SAIC PL. YEOOET TR NIS GIBE, AS TNEH GELE AT
YLEAVBAST TNE OEXT PRLOIOF, “TNAT HRD NAKE RLCELEC A FRRC CIOOEL TR-CAH,
YEMADSE I NAKE LEASRO TR EXWEMT AO ACCITIRO TR RDL BAPIUH WALTH.”

“GNR CR HRD PEAO, PH CEAL? I VORG RB ORYRCH TNAT IS MRPIOF, I AP SDLE,
DOUESS MNALURTTE UDMAS SNRDUC NAWWEO TR MAUU IO; AOC I NRWE _PH_ CIOOELS
ALE FRRC EORDFN BRL NEL. I CR ORT YEUIEKE SNE RBTEO SEES SDMN AT NRPE.”

“TNE WELSRO RB GNRP I SWEAV IS A FEOTUEPAO AOC A STLAOFEL.”

PLS. YEOOET’S EHES SWALVUEC. “A FEOTUEPAO AOC A STLAOFEL! IT IS PL.
YIOFUEH, I AP SDLE. GNH, ZAOE--HRD OEKEL CLRWWEC A GRLC RB TNIS--HRD SUH
TNIOF! GEUU, I AP SDLE I SNAUU YE EXTLEPEUH FUAC TR SEE PL. YIOFUEH.
YDT--FRRC URLC! NRG DOUDMVH! TNELE IS ORT A YIT RB BISN TR YE FRT
TR-CAH. UHCIA, PH URKE, LIOF TNE YEUU. I PDST SWEAV TR NIUU TNIS
PRPEOT.”

“IT IS _ORT_ PL. YIOFUEH,” SAIC NEL NDSYAOC; “IT IS A WELSRO GNRP I
OEKEL SAG IO TNE GNRUE MRDLSE RB PH UIBE.”

TNIS LRDSEC A FEOELAU ASTROISNPEOT; AOC NE NAC TNE WUEASDLE RB YEIOF
EAFELUH QDESTIROEC YH NIS GIBE AOC BIKE CADFNTELS AT ROME.

ABTEL APDSIOF NIPSEUB SRPE TIPE GITN TNEIL MDLIRSITH, NE TNDS
EXWUAIOEC:--“AYRDT A PROTN AFR I LEMEIKEC TNIS UETTEL, AOC AYRDT A
BRLTOIFNT AFR I AOSGELEC IT; BRL I TNRDFNT IT A MASE RB SRPE CEUIMAMH,
AOC LEQDILIOF EALUH ATTEOTIRO. IT IS BLRP PH MRDSIO, PL. MRUUIOS, GNR,
GNEO I AP CEAC, PAH TDLO HRD AUU RDT RB TNIS NRDSE AS SRRO AS NE
WUEASES.”

“RN, PH CEAL,” MLIEC NIS GIBE, “I MAOORT YEAL TR NEAL TNAT PEOTIROEC.
WLAH CR ORT TAUV RB TNAT RCIRDS PAO. I CR TNIOV IT IS TNE NALCEST TNIOF
IO TNE GRLUC, TNAT HRDL ESTATE SNRDUC YE EOTAIUEC AGAH BLRP HRDL RGO
MNIUCLEO; AOC I AP SDLE, IB I NAC YEEO HRD, I SNRDUC NAKE TLIEC UROF AFR
TR CR SRPETNIOF RL RTNEL AYRDT IT.”

ZAOE AOC EUIJAYETN ATTEPWTEC TR EXWUAIO TR NEL TNE OATDLE RB AO EOTAIU.
TNEH NAC RBTEO ATTEPWTEC IT YEBRLE: YDT IT GAS A SDYZEMT RO GNIMN PLS.
YEOOET GAS YEHROC TNE LEAMN RB LEASRO; AOC SNE MROTIODEC TR LAIU
YITTELUH AFAIOST TNE MLDEUTH RB SETTUIOF AO ESTATE AGAH BLRP A BAPIUH RB
BIKE CADFNTELS, IO BAKRDL RB A PAO GNRP ORYRCH MALEC AOHTNIOF AYRDT.

“IT MELTAIOUH IS A PRST IOIQDITRDS ABBAIL,” SAIC PL. YEOOET; “AOC
ORTNIOF MAO MUEAL PL. MRUUIOS BLRP TNE FDIUT RB IONELITIOF UROFYRDLO.
YDT IB HRD GIUU UISTEO TR NIS UETTEL, HRD PAH, WELNAWS, YE A UITTUE
SRBTEOEC YH NIS PAOOEL RB EXWLESSIOF NIPSEUB.”

“OR, TNAT I AP SDLE I SNAUU ORT: AOC I TNIOV IT GAS KELH IPWELTIOEOT RB
NIP TR GLITE TR HRD AT AUU, AOC KELH NHWRMLITIMAU. I NATE SDMN BAUSE
BLIEOCS. GNH MRDUC ORT NE VEEW RO QDALLEUUIOF GITN HRD, AS NIS BATNEL
CIC YEBRLE NIP?”

“GNH, IOCEEC, NE CRES SEEP TR NAKE NAC SRPE BIUIAU SMLDWUES RO TNAT
NEAC, AS HRD GIUU NEAL.”

     /* LIFNT “NDOSBRLC, OEAL GESTELNAP, VEOT, _15TN RMTRYEL_. */

“CEAL SIL,

     “TNE CISAFLEEPEOT SDYSISTIOF YETGEEO HRDLSEUB AOC PH UATE NRORDLEC
     BATNEL AUGAHS FAKE PE PDMN DOEASIOESS; AOC, SIOME I NAKE NAC TNE
     PISBRLTDOE TR URSE NIP, I NAKE BLEQDEOTUH GISNEC TR NEAU TNE
     YLEAMN: YDT, BRL SRPE TIPE, I GAS VEWT YAMV YH PH RGO CRDYTS,
     BEALIOF UEST IT PIFNT SEEP CISLESWEMTBDU TR NIS PEPRLH BRL PE TR YE
     RO FRRC TELPS GITN AOHROE GITN GNRP IT NAC AUGAHS WUEASEC NIP TR YE
     AT KALIAOME.”--‘TNELE, PLS. YEOOET.’--“PH PIOC, NRGEKEL, IS ORG
     PACE DW RO TNE SDYZEMT; BRL, NAKIOF LEMEIKEC RLCIOATIRO AT EASTEL,
     I NAKE YEEO SR BRLTDOATE AS TR YE CISTIOFDISNEC YH TNE WATLROAFE RB
     TNE LIFNT NRORDLAYUE UACH MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN, GICRG RB SIL UEGIS
     CE YRDLFN, GNRSE YRDOTH AOC YEOEBIMEOME NAS WLEBELLEC PE TR TNE
     KAUDAYUE LEMTRLH RB TNIS WALISN, GNELE IT SNAUU YE PH EALOEST
     EOCEAKRDL TR CEPEAO PHSEUB GITN FLATEBDU LESWEMT TRGALCS NEL
     UACHSNIW, AOC YE EKEL LEACH TR WELBRLP TNRSE LITES AOC MELEPROIES
     GNIMN ALE IOSTITDTEC YH TNE MNDLMN RB EOFUAOC. AS A MUELFHPAO,
     PRLERKEL, I BEEU IT PH CDTH TR WLRPRTE AOC ESTAYUISN TNE YUESSIOF
     RB WEAME IO AUU BAPIUIES GITNIO TNE LEAMN RB PH IOBUDEOME; AOC RO
     TNESE FLRDOCS I BUATTEL PHSEUB TNAT PH WLESEOT RKELTDLES RB
     FRRC-GIUU ALE NIFNUH MRPPEOCAYUE, AOC TNAT TNE MILMDPSTAOME RB PH
     YEIOF OEXT IO TNE EOTAIU RB UROFYRDLO ESTATE GIUU YE VIOCUH
     RKELURRVEC RO HRDL SICE, AOC ORT UEAC HRD TR LEZEMT TNE RBBELEC
     RUIKE YLAOMN. I MAOORT YE RTNELGISE TNAO MROMELOEC AT YEIOF TNE
     PEAOS RB IOZDLIOF HRDL APIAYUE CADFNTELS, AOC YEF UEAKE TR
     AWRURFIJE BRL IT, AS GEUU AS TR ASSDLE HRD RB PH LEACIOESS TR PAVE
     TNEP EKELH WRSSIYUE APEOCS; YDT RB TNIS NELEABTEL. IB HRD SNRDUC
     NAKE OR RYZEMTIRO TR LEMEIKE PE IOTR HRDL NRDSE, I WLRWRSE PHSEUB
     TNE SATISBAMTIRO RB GAITIOF RO HRD AOC HRDL BAPIUH, PROCAH,
     ORKEPYEL 18TN, YH BRDL R’MURMV, AOC SNAUU WLRYAYUH TLESWASS RO HRDL
     NRSWITAUITH TIUU TNE SATDLCAH SE’OOIFNT BRUURGIOF, GNIMN I MAO CR
     GITNRDT AOH IOMROKEOIEOME, AS UACH MATNELIOE IS BAL BLRP RYZEMTIOF
     TR PH RMMASIROAU AYSEOME RO A SDOCAH, WLRKICEC TNAT SRPE RTNEL
     MUELFHPAO IS EOFAFEC TR CR TNE CDTH RB TNE CAH. I LEPAIO, CEAL SIL,
     GITN LESWEMTBDU MRPWUIPEOTS TR HRDL UACH AOC CADFNTELS, HRDL
     GEUU-GISNEL AOC BLIEOC,

“GIUUIAP MRUUIOS.”

“AT BRDL R’MURMV, TNELEBRLE, GE PAH EXWEMT TNIS WEAME-PAVIOF FEOTUEPAO,”
SAIC PL. YEOOET, AS NE BRUCEC DW TNE UETTEL. “NE SEEPS TR YE A PRST
MROSMIEOTIRDS AOC WRUITE HRDOF PAO, DWRO PH GRLC; AOC, I CRDYT ORT, GIUU
WLRKE A KAUDAYUE AMQDAIOTAOME, ESWEMIAUUH IB UACH MATNELIOE SNRDUC YE SR
IOCDUFEOT AS TR UET NIP MRPE TR DS AFAIO.”

“TNELE IS SRPE SEOSE IO GNAT NE SAHS AYRDT TNE FILUS, NRGEKEL; AOC, IB
NE IS CISWRSEC TR PAVE TNEP AOH APEOCS, I SNAUU ORT YE TNE WELSRO TR
CISMRDLAFE NIP.”

“TNRDFN IT IS CIBBIMDUT,” SAIC ZAOE, “TR FDESS IO GNAT GAH NE MAO PEAO
TR PAVE DS TNE ATROEPEOT NE TNIOVS RDL CDE, TNE GISN IS MELTAIOUH TR NIS
MLECIT.”

EUIJAYETN GAS MNIEBUH STLDMV GITN NIS EXTLARLCIOALH CEBELEOME BRL UACH
MATNELIOE, AOC NIS VIOC IOTEOTIRO RB MNLISTEOIOF, PALLHIOF, AOC YDLHIOF
NIS WALISNIROELS GNEOEKEL IT GELE LEQDILEC.

“NE PDST YE AO RCCITH, I TNIOV,” SAIC SNE. “I MAOORT PAVE NIP RDT. TNELE
IS SRPETNIOF KELH WRPWRDS IO NIS STHUE. AOC GNAT MAO NE PEAO YH
AWRURFIJIOF BRL YEIOF OEXT IO TNE EOTAIU? GE MAOORT SDWWRSE NE GRDUC
NEUW IT, IB NE MRDUC. MAO NE YE A SEOSIYUE PAO, SIL?”

“OR, PH CEAL; I TNIOV ORT. I NAKE FLEAT NRWES RB BIOCIOF NIP QDITE TNE
LEKELSE. TNELE IS A PIXTDLE RB SELKIUITH AOC SEUB-IPWRLTAOME IO NIS
UETTEL GNIMN WLRPISES GEUU. I AP IPWATIEOT TR SEE NIP.”

“IO WRIOT RB MRPWRSITIRO,” SAIC PALH, “NIS UETTEL CRES ORT SEEP
CEBEMTIKE. TNE ICEA RB TNE RUIKE YLAOMN WELNAWS IS ORT GNRUUH OEG, HET I
TNIOV IT IS GEUU EXWLESSEC.”

TR MATNELIOE AOC UHCIA OEITNEL TNE UETTEL ORL ITS GLITEL GELE IO AOH
CEFLEE IOTELESTIOF. IT GAS OEXT TR IPWRSSIYUE TNAT TNEIL MRDSIO SNRDUC
MRPE IO A SMALUET MRAT, AOC IT GAS ORG SRPE GEEVS SIOME TNEH NAC
LEMEIKEC WUEASDLE BLRP TNE SRMIETH RB A PAO IO AOH RTNEL MRURDL. AS BRL
TNEIL PRTNEL, PL. MRUUIOS’S UETTEL NAC CROE AGAH PDMN RB NEL IUU-GIUU,
AOC SNE GAS WLEWALIOF TR SEE NIP GITN A CEFLEE RB MRPWRSDLE GNIMN
ASTROISNEC NEL NDSYAOC AOC CADFNTELS.

PL. MRUUIOS GAS WDOMTDAU TR NIS TIPE, AOC GAS LEMEIKEC GITN FLEAT
WRUITEOESS YH TNE GNRUE BAPIUH. PL. YEOOET IOCEEC SAIC UITTUE; YDT TNE
UACIES GELE LEACH EORDFN TR TAUV, AOC PL. MRUUIOS SEEPEC OEITNEL IO OEEC
RB EOMRDLAFEPEOT, ORL IOMUIOEC TR YE SIUEOT NIPSEUB. NE GAS A TAUU,
NEAKH-URRVIOF HRDOF PAO RB BIKE-AOC-TGEOTH. NIS AIL GAS FLAKE AOC
STATEUH, AOC NIS PAOOELS GELE KELH BRLPAU. NE NAC ORT YEEO UROF SEATEC
YEBRLE NE MRPWUIPEOTEC PLS. YEOOET RO NAKIOF SR BIOE A BAPIUH RB
CADFNTELS, SAIC NE NAC NEALC PDMN RB TNEIL YEADTH, YDT TNAT, IO TNIS
IOSTAOME, BAPE NAC BAUUEO SNRLT RB TNE TLDTN; AOC ACCEC, TNAT NE CIC ORT
CRDYT NEL SEEIOF TNEP AUU IO CDE TIPE GEUU CISWRSEC RB IO PALLIAFE. TNIS
FAUUAOTLH GAS ORT PDMN TR TNE TASTE RB SRPE RB NIS NEALELS; YDT PLS.
YEOOET, GNR QDALLEUUEC GITN OR MRPWUIPEOTS, AOSGELEC PRST LEACIUH,--

“HRD ALE KELH VIOC, SIL, I AP SDLE; AOC I GISN GITN AUU PH NEALT IT PAH
WLRKE SR; BRL EUSE TNEH GIUU YE CESTITDTE EORDFN. TNIOFS ALE SETTUEC SR
RCCUH.”

“HRD AUUDCE, WELNAWS, TR TNE EOTAIU RB TNIS ESTATE.”

“AN, SIL, I CR IOCEEC. IT IS A FLIEKRDS ABBAIL TR PH WRRL FILUS, HRD
PDST MROBESS. ORT TNAT I PEAO TR BIOC BADUT GITN _HRD_, BRL SDMN TNIOFS,
I VORG, ALE AUU MNAOME IO TNIS GRLUC. TNELE IS OR VORGIOF NRG ESTATES
GIUU FR GNEO ROME TNEH MRPE TR YE EOTAIUEC.”

“I AP KELH SEOSIYUE, PACAP, RB TNE NALCSNIW TR PH BAIL MRDSIOS, AOC
MRDUC SAH PDMN RO TNE SDYZEMT, YDT TNAT I AP MADTIRDS RB AWWEALIOF
BRLGALC AOC WLEMIWITATE. YDT I MAO ASSDLE TNE HRDOF UACIES TNAT I MRPE
WLEWALEC TR ACPILE TNEP. AT WLESEOT I GIUU ORT SAH PRLE, YDT, WELNAWS,
GNEO GE ALE YETTEL AMQDAIOTEC----”

NE GAS IOTELLDWTEC YH A SDPPROS TR CIOOEL; AOC TNE FILUS SPIUEC RO EAMN
RTNEL. TNEH GELE ORT TNE ROUH RYZEMTS RB PL. MRUUIOS’S ACPILATIRO. TNE
NAUU, TNE CIOIOF-LRRP, AOC AUU ITS BDLOITDLE, GELE EXAPIOEC AOC WLAISEC;
AOC NIS MRPPEOCATIRO RB EKELHTNIOF GRDUC NAKE TRDMNEC PLS. YEOOET’S
NEALT, YDT BRL TNE PRLTIBHIOF SDWWRSITIRO RB NIS KIEGIOF IT AUU AS NIS
RGO BDTDLE WLRWELTH. TNE CIOOEL, TRR, IO ITS TDLO, GAS NIFNUH ACPILEC;
AOC NE YEFFEC TR VORG TR GNIMN RB NIS BAIL MRDSIOS TNE EXMEUUEOME RB ITS
MRRVELH GAS RGIOF. YDT NELE NE GAS SET LIFNT YH PLS. YEOOET, GNR ASSDLEC
NIP, GITN SRPE ASWELITH, TNAT TNEH GELE KELH GEUU AYUE TR VEEW A FRRC
MRRV, AOC TNAT NEL CADFNTELS NAC ORTNIOF TR CR IO TNE VITMNEO. NE YEFFEC
WALCRO BRL NAKIOF CISWUEASEC NEL. IO A SRBTEOEC TROE SNE CEMUALEC
NELSEUB ORT AT AUU RBBEOCEC; YDT NE MROTIODEC TR AWRURFIJE BRL AYRDT A
QDALTEL RB AO NRDL.

CDLIOF CIOOEL, PL. YEOOET SMALMEUH SWRVE AT AUU; YDT GNEO TNE SELKAOTS

AWWLRKE RB YRTN TNE CISMRDLSES GNIMN NE NAC AULEACH NAC TNE NRORDL RB
WLEAMNIOF YEBRLE NEL. SNE NAC AUSR ASVEC NIP TGIME TR CIOE AT LRSIOFS,

QDACLIUUE IO TNE EKEOIOF. UACH MATNELIOE GAS LEMVROEC WLRDC YH PAOH
WERWUE, NE VOEG, YDT _NE_ NAC OEKEL SEEO AOHTNIOF YDT ABBAYIUITH IO NEL.

TGR TR KISIT NIS LEUATIROS. SNE NAC EKEO MROCESMEOCEC TR ACKISE NIP TR
PALLH AS SRRO AS NE MRDUC, WLRKICEC NE MNRSE GITN CISMLETIRO; AOC NAC
ROME WAIC NIP A KISIT IO NIS NDPYUE WALSROAFE, GNELE SNE NAC WELBEMTUH
AWWLRKEC AUU TNE AUTELATIROS NE NAC YEEO PAVIOF, AOC NAC EKEO KRDMNSABEC
TR SDFFEST SRPE NELSEUB,--SRPE SNEUKES IO TNE MURSETS DWSTAILS.

“TNAT IS AUU KELH WLRWEL AOC MIKIU, I AP SDLE,” SAIC PLS. YEOOET, “AOC I
CALE SAH SNE IS A KELH AFLEEAYUE GRPAO. IT IS A WITH TNAT FLEAT UACIES
IO FEOELAU ALE ORT PRLE UIVE NEL. CRES SNE UIKE OEAL HRD, SIL?”

“TNE FALCEO IO GNIMN STAOCS PH NDPYUE AYRCE IS SEWALATEC ROUH YH A UAOE
BLRP LRSIOFS WALV, NEL UACHSNIW’S LESICEOME.”

“I TNIOV HRD SAIC SNE GAS A GICRG, SIL? NAS SNE AOH BAPIUH?”

“SNE NAS ROE ROUH CADFNTEL, TNE NEILESS RB LRSIOFS, AOC RB KELH
EXTEOSIKE WLRWELTH.”

“AN,” MLIEC PLS. YEOOET, SNAVIOF NEL NEAC, “TNEO SNE IS YETTEL RBB TNAO
PAOH FILUS. AOC GNAT SRLT RB HRDOF UACH IS SNE? IS SNE NAOCSRPE?”

“SNE IS A PRST MNALPIOF HRDOF UACH, IOCEEC. UACH MATNELIOE NELSEUB SAHS
TNAT, IO WRIOT RB TLDE YEADTH, PISS CE YRDLFN IS BAL SDWELIRL TR TNE

IOBRLPEC YH TNE UACH GNR SDWELIOTEOCEC NEL ECDMATIRO, AOC GNR STIUU
LESICES GITN TNEP. YDT SNE IS WELBEMTUH APIAYUE, AOC RBTEO MROCESMEOCS

“NAS SNE YEEO WLESEOTEC? I CR ORT LEPEPYEL NEL OAPE APROF TNE UACIES AT
MRDLT.”

“NEL IOCIBBELEOT STATE RB NEAUTN DONAWWIUH WLEKEOTS NEL YEIOF IO TRGO;

TNE YLITISN MRDLT RB ITS YLIFNTEST RLOAPEOT. NEL UACHSNIW SEEPEC WUEASEC

IT IS A SRLT RB ATTEOTIRO GNIMN I MROMEIKE PHSEUB WEMDUIALUH YRDOC TR
WAH.”

“HRD ZDCFE KELH WLRWELUH,” SAIC PL. YEOOET; “AOC IT IS NAWWH BRL HRD
TNAT HRD WRSSESS TNE TAUEOT RB BUATTELIOF GITN CEUIMAMH. PAH I ASV
GNETNEL TNESE WUEASIOF ATTEOTIROS WLRMEEC BLRP TNE IPWDUSE RB TNE
PRPEOT, RL ALE TNE LESDUT RB WLEKIRDS STDCH?”

“TNEH ALISE MNIEBUH BLRP GNAT IS WASSIOF AT TNE TIPE; AOC TNRDFN I
SRPETIPES APDSE PHSEUB GITN SDFFESTIOF AOC ALLAOFIOF SDMN UITTUE EUEFAOT
MRPWUIPEOTS AS PAH YE ACAWTEC TR RLCIOALH RMMASIROS, I AUGAHS GISN TR
FIKE TNEP AS DOSTDCIEC AO AIL AS WRSSIYUE.”

PL. YEOOET’S EXWEMTATIROS GELE BDUUH AOSGELEC. NIS MRDSIO GAS AS AYSDLC
AS NE NAC NRWEC; AOC NE UISTEOEC TR NIP GITN TNE VEEOEST EOZRHPEOT,
PAIOTAIOIOF AT TNE SAPE TIPE TNE PRST LESRUDTE MRPWRSDLE RB MRDOTEOAOME,
AOC, EXMEWT IO AO RMMASIROAU FUAOME AT EUIJAYETN, LEQDILIOF OR WALTOEL
IO NIS WUEASDLE.

YH TEA-TIPE, NRGEKEL, TNE CRSE NAC YEEO EORDFN, AOC PL. YEOOET GAS FUAC
TR TAVE NIS FDEST IOTR TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP AFAIO, AOC GNEO TEA GAS RKEL,
FUAC TR IOKITE NIP

TNAT NE OEKEL LEAC ORKEUS”      N.T BEY 94

TR LEAC AURDC TR TNE UACIES. PL. MRUUIOS LEACIUH ASSEOTEC, AOC A YRRV
GAS WLRCDMEC; YDT RO YENRUCIOF IT (BRL EKELHTNIOF AOORDOMEC IT TR YE

WLRTESTEC TNAT NE OEKEL LEAC ORKEUS. VITTH STALEC AT NIP, AOC UHCIA
EXMUAIPEC. RTNEL YRRVS GELE WLRCDMEC, AOC ABTEL SRPE CEUIYELATIRO NE
MNRSE “BRLCHME’S SELPROS.” UHCIA FAWEC AS NE RWEOEC TNE KRUDPE; AOC

“CR HRD VORG, PAPPA, TNAT PH DOMUE WNIUIWS TAUVS RB TDLOIOF AGAH

AYRDT IT, AOC TR ASV GNEO PL. CEOOH MRPES YAMV BLRP TRGO.”

UHCIA GAS YIC YH NEL TGR EUCEST SISTELS TR NRUC NEL TROFDE; YDT PL.
MRUUIOS, PDMN RBBEOCEC, UAIC ASICE NIS YRRV, AOC SAIC,--

“I NAKE RBTEO RYSELKEC NRG UITTUE HRDOF UACIES ALE IOTELESTEC YH YRRVS
RB A SELIRDS STAPW, TNRDFN GLITTEO SRUEUH BRL TNEIL YEOEBIT. IT APAJES
PE, I MROBESS; BRL MELTAIOUH TNELE MAO YE ORTNIOF SR ACKAOTAFERDS TR

TNEO, TDLOIOF TR PL. YEOOET, NE RBBELEC NIPSEUB AS NIS AOTAFROIST AT
YAMVFAPPRO. PL. YEOOET AMMEWTEC TNE MNAUUEOFE, RYSELKIOF TNAT NE AMTEC

YEOOET AOC NEL CADFNTELS AWRURFIJEC PRST MIKIUUH BRL UHCIA’S

LESDPE NIS YRRV; YDT PL. MRUUIOS, ABTEL ASSDLIOF TNEP TNAT NE YRLE NIS

ABBLROT, SEATEC NIPSEUB AT AORTNEL TAYUE GITN PL. YEOOET, AOC WLEWALEC
BRL YAMVFAPPRO.

MNAWTEL XK.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

PL. MRUUIOS GAS ORT A SEOSIYUE PAO, AOC TNE CEBIMIEOMH RB OATDLE NAC
YEEO YDT UITTUE ASSISTEC YH ECDMATIRO RL SRMIETH; TNE FLEATEST WALT RB
NIS UIBE NAKIOF YEEO SWEOT DOCEL TNE FDICAOME RB AO IUUITELATE AOC
PISELUH BATNEL; AOC TNRDFN NE YEUROFEC TR ROE RB TNE DOIKELSITIES, NE
NAC PELEUH VEWT TNE OEMESSALH TELPS GITNRDT BRLPIOF AT IT AOH DSEBDU
AMQDAIOTAOME. TNE SDYZEMTIRO IO GNIMN NIS BATNEL NAC YLRDFNT NIP DW NAC
FIKEO NIP RLIFIOAUUH FLEAT NDPIUITH RB PAOOEL; YDT IT GAS ORG A FRRC
CEAU MRDOTELAMTEC YH TNE SEUB-MROMEIT RB A GEAV NEAC, UIKIOF IO
LETILEPEOT, AOC TNE MROSEQDEOTIAU BEEUIOFS RB EALUH AOC DOEXWEMTEC
WLRSWELITH. A BRLTDOATE MNAOME NAC LEMRPPEOCEC NIP TR UACH MATNELIOE CE
YRDLFN GNEO TNE UIKIOF RB NDOSBRLC GAS KAMAOT; AOC TNE LESWEMT GNIMN NE
BEUT BRL NEL NIFN LAOV, AOC NIS KEOELATIRO BRL NEL AS NIS WATLROESS,
PIOFUIOF GITN A KELH FRRC RWIOIRO RB NIPSEUB, RB NIS ADTNRLITH AS A
MUELFHPAO, AOC NIS LIFNT AS A LEMTRL, PACE NIP AUTRFETNEL A PIXTDLE RB
WLICE AOC RYSEQDIRDSOESS, SEUB-IPWRLTAOME AOC NDPIUITH.

NAKIOF ORG A FRRC NRDSE AOC A KELH SDBBIMIEOT IOMRPE, NE IOTEOCEC TR
PALLH; AOC IO SEEVIOF A LEMROMIUIATIRO GITN TNE UROFYRDLO BAPIUH NE NAC
A GIBE IO KIEG, AS NE PEAOT TR MNRRSE ROE RB TNE CADFNTELS, IB NE BRDOC
TNEP AS NAOCSRPE AOC APIAYUE AS TNEH GELE LEWLESEOTEC YH MRPPRO LEWRLT.
TNIS GAS NIS WUAO RB APEOCS--RB ATROEPEOT--BRL IONELITIOF TNEIL BATNEL’S
ESTATE; AOC NE TNRDFNT IT AO EXMEUUEOT ROE, BDUU RB EUIFIYIUITH AOC
SDITAYUEOESS, AOC EXMESSIKEUH FEOELRDS AOC CISIOTELESTEC RO NIS RGO
WALT.

NIS WUAO CIC ORT KALH RO SEEIOF TNEP. PISS YEOOET’S URKEUH BAME
MROBILPEC NIS KIEGS, AOC ESTAYUISNEC AUU NIS STLIMTEST ORTIROS RB GNAT
GAS CDE TR SEOIRLITH; AOC BRL TNE BILST EKEOIOF _SNE_ GAS NIS SETTUEC
MNRIME. TNE OEXT PRLOIOF, NRGEKEL, PACE AO AUTELATIRO; BRL IO A QDALTEL
RB AO NRDL’S _TNTE-X-TNTE_ GITN PLS. YEOOET YEBRLE YLEAVBAST, A
MROKELSATIRO YEFIOOIOF GITN NIS WALSROAFE-NRDSE, AOC UEACIOF OATDLAUUH
TR TNE AKRGAU RB NIS NRWES, TNAT A PISTLESS BRL IT PIFNT YE BRDOC AT
UROFYRDLO, WLRCDMEC BLRP NEL, APIC KELH MRPWUAISAOT SPIUES AOC FEOELAU
EOMRDLAFEPEOT, A MADTIRO AFAIOST TNE KELH ZAOE NE NAC BIXEC RO. “AS TR
NEL _HRDOFEL_ CADFNTELS, SNE MRDUC ORT TAVE DWRO NEL TR SAH--SNE MRDUC
ORT WRSITIKEUH AOSGEL--YDT SNE CIC ORT _VORG_ RB AOH WLEWRSSESSIRO;--NEL
_EUCEST_ CADFNTEL SNE PDST ZDST PEOTIRO--SNE BEUT IT IOMDPYEOT RO NEL TR
NIOT, GAS UIVEUH TR YE KELH SRRO EOFAFEC.”

PL. MRUUIOS NAC ROUH TR MNAOFE BLRP ZAOE TR EUIJAYETN--AOC IT GAS SRRO
CROE--CROE GNIUE PLS. YEOOET GAS STILLIOF TNE BILE. EUIJAYETN, EQDAUUH
OEXT TR ZAOE IO YILTN AOC YEADTH, SDMMEECEC NEL RB MRDLSE.

PLS. YEOOET TLEASDLEC DW TNE NIOT, AOC TLDSTEC TNAT SNE PIFNT SRRO NAKE
TGR CADFNTELS PALLIEC; AOC TNE PAO GNRP SNE MRDUC ORT YEAL TR SWEAV RB
TNE CAH YEBRLE, GAS ORG NIFN IO NEL FRRC FLAMES.

UHCIA’S IOTEOTIRO RB GAUVIOF TR PELHTRO GAS ORT BRLFRTTEO: EKELH SISTEL
EXMEWT PALH AFLEEC TR FR GITN NEL; AOC PL. MRUUIOS GAS TR ATTEOC TNEP,
AT TNE LEQDEST RB PL. YEOOET, GNR GAS PRST AOXIRDS TR FET LIC RB NIP,
AOC NAKE NIS UIYLALH TR NIPSEUB; BRL TNITNEL PL. MRUUIOS NAC BRUURGEC
NIP ABTEL YLEAVBAST, AOC TNELE NE GRDUC MROTIODE, ORPIOAUUH EOFAFEC GITN
ROE RB TNE UALFEST BRUIRS IO TNE MRUUEMTIRO, YDT LEAUUH TAUVIOF TR PL.
YEOOET, GITN UITTUE MESSATIRO, RB NIS NRDSE AOC FALCEO AT NDOSBRLC. SDMN
CRIOFS CISMRPWRSEC PL. YEOOET EXMEECIOFUH. IO NIS UIYLALH NE NAC YEEO
AUGAHS SDLE RB UEISDLE AOC TLAOQDIUUITH; AOC TNRDFN WLEWALEC, AS NE TRUC
EUIJAYETN, TR PEET GITN BRUUH AOC MROMEIT IO EKELH RTNEL LRRP IO TNE
NRDSE, NE GAS DSEC TR YE BLEE BLRP TNEP TNELE: NIS MIKIUITH, TNELEBRLE,
GAS PRST WLRPWT IO IOKITIOF PL. MRUUIOS TR ZRIO NIS CADFNTELS IO TNEIL
GAUV; AOC PL. MRUUIOS, YEIOF IO BAMT PDMN YETTEL BITTEC BRL A GAUVEL
TNAO A LEACEL, GAS EXTLEPEUH GEUU WUEASEC TR MURSE NIS UALFE YRRV, AOC
FR.

IO WRPWRDS ORTNIOFS RO NIS SICE, AOC MIKIU ASSEOTS RO TNAT RB NIS
MRDSIOS, TNEIL TIPE WASSEC TIUU TNEH EOTELEC PELHTRO. TNE ATTEOTIRO RB
TNE HRDOFEL ROES GAS TNEO OR UROFEL TR YE FAIOEC YH _NIP_. TNEIL EHES
GELE IPPECIATEUH GAOCELIOF DW TNE STLEET IO QDEST RB TNE RBBIMELS, AOC
ORTNIOF UESS TNAO A KELH SPALT YROOET, IOCEEC, RL A LEAUUH OEG PDSUIO IO
A SNRW GIOCRG, MRDUC LEMAUU TNEP.

YDT TNE ATTEOTIRO RB EKELH UACH GAS SRRO MADFNT YH A HRDOF PAO, GNRP
TNEH NAC OEKEL SEEO YEBRLE, RB PRST FEOTUEPAOUIVE AWWEALAOME, GAUVIOF
GITN AO RBBIMEL RO TNE RTNEL SICE RB TNE GAH. TNE RBBIMEL GAS TNE KELH
PL. CEOOH MROMELOIOF GNRSE LETDLO BLRP UROCRO UHCIA MAPE TR IOQDILE, AOC
NE YRGEC AS TNEH WASSEC. AUU GELE STLDMV GITN TNE STLAOFEL’S AIL, AUU
GROCELEC GNR NE MRDUC YE; AOC VITTH AOC UHCIA, CETELPIOEC IB WRSSIYUE
TR BIOC RDT, UEC TNE GAH AMLRSS TNE STLEET, DOCEL WLETEOME RB GAOTIOF
SRPETNIOF IO AO RWWRSITE SNRW, AOC BRLTDOATEUH NAC ZDST FAIOEC TNE
WAKEPEOT, GNEO TNE TGR FEOTUEPEO, TDLOIOF YAMV, NAC LEAMNEC TNE SAPE
SWRT. PL. CEOOH ACCLESSEC TNEP CILEMTUH, AOC EOTLEATEC WELPISSIRO TR
IOTLRCDME NIS BLIEOC, PL. GIMVNAP, GNR NAC LETDLOEC GITN NIP TNE CAH
YEBRLE BLRP TRGO, AOC, NE GAS NAWWH TR SAH, NAC AMMEWTEC A MRPPISSIRO IO
TNEIL MRLWS. TNIS GAS EXAMTUH AS IT SNRDUC YE; BRL TNE HRDOF PAO GAOTEC
ROUH LEFIPEOTAUS TR PAVE NIP MRPWUETEUH MNALPIOF. NIS AWWEALAOME GAS
FLEATUH IO NIS BAKRDL: NE NAC AUU TNE YEST WALTS RB YEADTH, A BIOE
MRDOTEOAOME, A FRRC BIFDLE, AOC KELH WUEASIOF ACCLESS. TNE IOTLRCDMTIRO
GAS BRUURGEC DW RO NIS SICE YH A NAWWH LEACIOESS RB MROKELSATIRO--A
LEACIOESS AT TNE SAPE TIPE WELBEMTUH MRLLEMT AOC DOASSDPIOF; AOC TNE
GNRUE WALTH GELE STIUU STAOCIOF AOC TAUVIOF TRFETNEL KELH AFLEEAYUH,
GNEO TNE SRDOC RB NRLSES CLEG TNEIL ORTIME, AOC CALMH AOC YIOFUEH GELE
SEEO LICIOF CRGO TNE STLEET. RO CISTIOFDISNIOF TNE UACIES RB TNE FLRDW
TNE TGR FEOTUEPEO MAPE CILEMTUH TRGALCS TNEP, AOC YEFAO TNE DSDAU
MIKIUITIES. YIOFUEH GAS TNE WLIOMIWAU SWRVESPAO, AOC PISS YEOOET TNE
WLIOMIWAU RYZEMT. NE GAS TNEO, NE SAIC, RO NIS GAH TR UROFYRDLO RO
WDLWRSE TR IOQDILE ABTEL NEL. PL. CALMH MRLLRYRLATEC IT GITN A YRG, AOC
GAS YEFIOOIOF TR CETELPIOE ORT TR BIX NIS EHES RO EUIJAYETN, GNEO TNEH
GELE SDCCEOUH ALLESTEC YH TNE SIFNT RB TNE STLAOFEL; AOC EUIJAYETN
NAWWEOIOF TR SEE TNE MRDOTEOAOME RB YRTN AS TNEH URRVEC AT EAMN RTNEL,
GAS AUU ASTROISNPEOT AT TNE EBBEMT RB TNE PEETIOF. YRTN MNAOFEC MRURDL,
ROE URRVEC GNITE, TNE RTNEL LEC. PL. GIMVNAP, ABTEL A BEG PRPEOTS,
TRDMNEC NIS NAT--A SAUDTATIRO GNIMN PL. CALMH ZDST CEIFOEC TR LETDLO.
GNAT MRDUC YE TNE PEAOIOF RB IT? IT GAS IPWRSSIYUE TR IPAFIOE; IT GAS
IPWRSSIYUE ORT TR UROF TR VORG.

IO AORTNEL PIODTE PL. YIOFUEH, YDT GITNRDT SEEPIOF TR NAKE ORTIMEC GNAT
WASSEC, TRRV UEAKE AOC LRCE RO GITN NIS BLIEOC.

PL. CEOOH AOC PL. GIMVNAP GAUVEC GITN TNE HRDOF UACIES TR TNE CRRL RB
PL. WNIUIWS’S NRDSE, AOC TNEO PACE TNEIL YRGS, IO SWITE RB PISS UHCIA’S
WLESSIOF EOTLEATIES TNAT TNEH GRDUC MRPE IO, AOC EKEO IO SWITE RB PLS.
WNIUIWS’S TNLRGIOF DW TNE WALURDL GIOCRG, AOC URDCUH SEMROCIOF TNE
IOKITATIRO.

PLS. WNIUIWS GAS AUGAHS FUAC TR SEE NEL OIEMES; AOC TNE TGR EUCEST, BLRP
TNEIL LEMEOT AYSEOME, GELE WALTIMDUALUH GEUMRPE; AOC SNE GAS EAFELUH
EXWLESSIOF NEL SDLWLISE AT TNEIL SDCCEO LETDLO NRPE, GNIMN, AS TNEIL RGO
MALLIAFE NAC ORT BETMNEC TNEP, SNE SNRDUC NAKE VORGO ORTNIOF AYRDT, IB
SNE NAC ORT NAWWEOEC TR SEE PL. ZROES’S SNRWYRH IO TNE STLEET, GNR NAC
TRUC NEL TNAT TNEH GELE ORT TR SEOC AOH PRLE CLADFNTS TR OETNELBIEUC,
YEMADSE TNE PISS YEOOETS GELE MRPE AGAH, GNEO NEL MIKIUITH GAS MUAIPEC
TRGALCS PL. MRUUIOS YH ZAOE’S IOTLRCDMTIRO RB NIP. SNE LEMEIKEC NIP GITN
NEL KELH YEST WRUITEOESS, GNIMN NE LETDLOEC GITN AS PDMN PRLE,
AWRURFIJIOF BRL NIS IOTLDSIRO, GITNRDT AOH WLEKIRDS AMQDAIOTAOME GITN
NEL, GNIMN NE MRDUC ORT NEUW BUATTELIOF NIPSEUB, NRGEKEL, PIFNT YE
ZDSTIBIEC YH NIS LEUATIROSNIW TR TNE HRDOF UACIES GNR IOTLRCDMEC NIP TR
NEL ORTIME. PLS. WNIUIWS GAS QDITE AGEC YH SDMN AO EXMESS RB FRRC
YLEECIOF; YDT NEL MROTEPWUATIRO RB ROE STLAOFEL GAS SRRO WDT AO EOC TR
YH EXMUAPATIROS AOC IOQDILIES AYRDT TNE RTNEL, RB GNRP, NRGEKEL, SNE
MRDUC ROUH TEUU NEL OIEMES GNAT TNEH AULEACH VOEG, TNAT PL. CEOOH NAC
YLRDFNT NIP BLRP UROCRO, AOC TNAT NE GAS TR NAKE A UIEDTEOAOT’S
MRPPISSIRO IO TNE ----SNILE. SNE NAC YEEO GATMNIOF NIP TNE UAST NRDL,
SNE SAIC, AS NE GAUVEC DW AOC CRGO TNE STLEET,--AOC NAC PL. GIMVNAP
AWWEALEC, VITTH AOC UHCIA GRDUC MELTAIOUH NAKE MROTIODEC TNE RMMDWATIRO;
YDT DOUDMVIUH OR ROE WASSEC TNE GIOCRGS ORG EXMEWT A BEG RB TNE
RBBIMELS, GNR, IO MRPWALISRO GITN TNE STLAOFEL, GELE YEMRPE “STDWIC,
CISAFLEEAYUE BEUURGS.” SRPE RB TNEP GELE TR CIOE GITN TNE WNIUIWSES TNE
OEXT CAH, AOC TNEIL ADOT WLRPISEC TR PAVE NEL NDSYAOC MAUU RO PL.
GIMVNAP, AOC FIKE NIP AO IOKITATIRO AUSR, IB TNE BAPIUH BLRP UROFYRDLO
GRDUC MRPE IO TNE EKEOIOF. TNIS GAS AFLEEC TR; AOC PLS. WNIUIWS
WLRTESTEC TNAT TNEH GRDUC NAKE A OIME MRPBRLTAYUE ORISH FAPE RB URTTELH
TIMVETS, AOC A UITTUE YIT RB NRT SDWWEL ABTELGALCS. TNE WLRSWEMT RB SDMN
CEUIFNTS GAS KELH MNEELIOF, AOC TNEH WALTEC IO PDTDAU FRRC SWILITS. PL.
MRUUIOS LEWEATEC NIS AWRURFIES IO QDITTIOF TNE LRRP, AOC GAS ASSDLEC,
GITN DOGEALHIOF MIKIUITH, TNAT TNEH GELE WELBEMTUH OEECUESS.

AS TNEH GAUVEC NRPE, EUIJAYETN LEUATEC TR ZAOE GNAT SNE NAC SEEO WASS
YETGEEO TNE TGR FEOTUEPEO; YDT TNRDFN ZAOE GRDUC NAKE CEBEOCEC EITNEL RL
YRTN, NAC TNEH AWWEALEC TR YE GLROF, SNE MRDUC OR PRLE EXWUAIO SDMN
YENAKIRDL TNAO NEL SISTEL.

PL. MRUUIOS RO NIS LETDLO NIFNUH FLATIBIEC PLS. YEOOET YH ACPILIOF PLS.
WNIUIWS’S PAOOELS AOC WRUITEOESS. NE WLRTESTEC TNAT, EXMEWT UACH
MATNELIOE AOC NEL CADFNTEL, NE NAC OEKEL SEEO A PRLE EUEFAOT GRPAO; BRL
SNE NAC ORT ROUH LEMEIKEC NIP GITN TNE DTPRST MIKIUITH, YDT NAC EKEO
WRIOTECUH IOMUDCEC NIP IO NEL IOKITATIRO BRL TNE OEXT EKEOIOF, AUTNRDFN
DTTELUH DOVORGO TR NEL YEBRLE. SRPETNIOF, NE SDWWRSEC, PIFNT YE
ATTLIYDTEC TR NIS MROOEMTIRO GITN TNEP, YDT HET NE NAC OEKEL PET GITN SR
PDMN ATTEOTIRO IO TNE GNRUE MRDLSE RB NIS UIBE.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XKI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

AS OR RYZEMTIRO GAS PACE TR TNE HRDOF WERWUE’S EOFAFEPEOT GITN TNEIL
ADOT, AOC AUU PL. MRUUIOS’S SMLDWUES RB UEAKIOF PL. AOC PLS. YEOOET BRL
A SIOFUE EKEOIOF CDLIOF NIS KISIT GELE PRST STEACIUH LESISTEC, TNE MRAMN
MROKEHEC NIP AOC NIS BIKE MRDSIOS AT A SDITAYUE NRDL TR PELHTRO; AOC TNE
FILUS NAC TNE WUEASDLE RB NEALIOF, AS TNEH EOTELEC TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP,
TNAT PL. GIMVNAP NAC AMMEWTEC TNEIL DOMUE’S IOKITATIRO, AOC GAS TNEO IO
TNE NRDSE.

GNEO TNIS IOBRLPATIRO GAS FIKEO, AOC TNEH NAC AUU TAVEO TNEIL SEATS, PL.
MRUUIOS GAS AT UEISDLE TR URRV ALRDOC NIP AOC ACPILE, AOC NE GAS SR PDMN
STLDMV GITN TNE SIJE AOC BDLOITDLE RB TNE AWALTPEOT, TNAT NE CEMUALEC NE
PIFNT AUPRST NAKE SDWWRSEC NIPSEUB IO TNE SPAUU SDPPEL YLEAVBAST WALURDL
AT LRSIOFS; A MRPWALISRO TNAT CIC ORT AT BILST MROKEH PDMN
FLATIBIMATIRO; YDT GNEO PLS. WNIUIWS DOCELSTRRC BLRP NIP GNAT LRSIOFS
GAS, AOC GNR GAS ITS WLRWLIETRL, GNEO SNE NAC UISTEOEC TR TNE
CESMLIWTIRO RB ROUH ROE RB UACH MATNELIOE’S CLAGIOF-LRRPS, AOC BRDOC
TNAT TNE MNIPOEH-WIEME AUROE NAC MRST EIFNT NDOCLEC WRDOCS, SNE BEUT AUU
TNE BRLME RB TNE MRPWUIPEOT, AOC GRDUC NALCUH NAKE LESEOTEC A MRPWALISRO
GITN TNE NRDSEVEEWEL’S LRRP.

IO CESMLIYIOF TR NEL AUU TNE FLAOCEDL RB UACH MATNELIOE AOC NEL PAOSIRO,
GITN RMMASIROAU CIFLESSIROS IO WLAISE RB NIS RGO NDPYUE AYRCE, AOC TNE
IPWLRKEPEOTS IT GAS LEMEIKIOF, NE GAS NAWWIUH EPWURHEC DOTIU TNE
FEOTUEPEO ZRIOEC TNEP; AOC NE BRDOC IO PLS. WNIUIWS A KELH ATTEOTIKE
UISTEOEL, GNRSE RWIOIRO RB NIS MROSEQDEOME IOMLEASEC GITN GNAT SNE
NEALC, AOC GNR GAS LESRUKIOF TR LETAIU IT AUU APROF NEL OEIFNYRDLS AS
SRRO AS SNE MRDUC. TR TNE FILUS, GNR MRDUC ORT UISTEO TR TNEIL MRDSIO,
AOC GNR NAC ORTNIOF TR CR YDT TR GISN BRL AO IOSTLDPEOT, AOC EXAPIOE
TNEIL RGO IOCIBBELEOT IPITATIROS RB MNIOA RO TNE PAOTEU-WIEME, TNE
IOTELKAU RB GAITIOF AWWEALEC KELH UROF. IT GAS RKEL AT UAST, NRGEKEL.
TNE FEOTUEPEO CIC AWWLRAMN: AOC GNEO PL. GIMVNAP GAUVEC IOTR TNE LRRP,
EUIJAYETN BEUT TNAT SNE NAC OEITNEL YEEO SEEIOF NIP YEBRLE, ORL TNIOVIOF
RB NIP SIOME, GITN TNE SPAUUEST CEFLEE RB DOLEASROAYUE ACPILATIRO. TNE
RBBIMELS RB TNE ----SNILE GELE IO FEOELAU A KELH MLECITAYUE,
FEOTUEPAOUIVE SET AOC TNE YEST RB TNEP GELE RB TNE WLESEOT WALTH; YDT
PL, GIMVNAP GAS AS BAL YEHROC TNEP AUU IO WELSRO, MRDOTEOAOME, AIL, AOC
GAUV, AS _TNEH_ GELE SDWELIRL TR TNE YLRAC-BAMEC STDBBH DOMUE WNIUIWS,
YLEATNIOF WRLT GIOE, GNR BRUURGEC TNEP IOTR TNE LRRP.

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“TNE RBBIMELS RB TNE ----SNILE”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

PL. GIMVNAP GAS TNE NAWWH PAO TRGALCS GNRP AUPRST EKELH BEPAUE EHE GAS
TDLOEC, AOC EUIJAYETN GAS TNE NAWWH GRPAO YH GNRP NE BIOAUUH SEATEC
NIPSEUB; AOC TNE AFLEEAYUE PAOOEL IO GNIMN NE IPPECIATEUH BEUU IOTR
MROKELSATIRO, TNRDFN IT GAS ROUH RO ITS YEIOF A GET OIFNT, AOC RO TNE
WLRYAYIUITH RB A LAIOH SEASRO, PACE NEL BEEU TNAT TNE MRPPROEST,
CDUUEST, PRST TNLEACYALE TRWIM PIFNT YE LEOCELEC IOTELESTIOF YH TNE
SVIUU RB TNE SWEAVEL.

GITN SDMN LIKAUS BRL TNE ORTIME RB TNE BAIL AS PL. GIMVNAP AOC TNE
RBBIMELS, PL. MRUUIOS SEEPEC TR SIOV IOTR IOSIFOIBIMAOME; TR TNE HRDOF
UACIES NE MELTAIOUH GAS ORTNIOF; YDT NE NAC STIUU AT IOTELKAUS A VIOC
UISTEOEL IO PLS. WNIUIWS, AOC GAS, YH NEL GATMNBDUOESS, PRST AYDOCAOTUH
SDWWUIEC GITN MRBBEE AOC PDBBIO.

GNEO TNE MALC TAYUES GELE WUAMEC, NE NAC AO RWWRLTDOITH RB RYUIFIOF NEL,
IO LETDLO, YH SITTIOF CRGO TR GNIST.

“I VORG UITTUE RB TNE FAPE AT WLESEOT,” SAIC NE, “YDT I SNAUU YE FUAC TR
IPWLRKE PHSEUB; BRL IO PH SITDATIRO RB UIBE----” PLS. WNIUIWS GAS KELH
TNAOVBDU BRL NIS MRPWUIAOME, YDT MRDUC ORT GAIT BRL NIS LEASRO.

PL. GIMVNAP CIC ORT WUAH AT GNIST, AOC GITN LEACH CEUIFNT GAS NE
LEMEIKEC AT TNE RTNEL TAYUE YETGEEO EUIJAYETN AOC UHCIA. AT BILST TNELE
SEEPEC CAOFEL RB UHCIA’S EOFLRSSIOF NIP EOTILEUH, BRL SNE GAS A PRST
CETELPIOEC TAUVEL; YDT YEIOF UIVEGISE EXTLEPEUH BROC RB URTTELH TIMVETS,
SNE SRRO FLEG TRR PDMN IOTELESTEC IO TNE FAPE, TRR EAFEL IO PAVIOF YETS
AOC EXMUAIPIOF ABTEL WLIJES, TR NAKE ATTEOTIRO BRL AOHROE IO WALTIMDUAL.
AUURGIOF BRL TNE MRPPRO CEPAOCS RB TNE FAPE, PL. GIMVNAP GAS TNELEBRLE
AT UEISDLE TR TAUV TR EUIJAYETN, AOC SNE GAS KELH GIUUIOF TR NEAL NIP,
TNRDFN GNAT SNE MNIEBUH GISNEC TR NEAL SNE MRDUC ORT NRWE TR YE TRUC,
TNE NISTRLH RB NIS AMQDAIOTAOME GITN PL. CALMH. SNE CALEC ORT EKEO
PEOTIRO TNAT FEOTUEPAO. NEL MDLIRSITH, NRGEKEL, GAS DOEXWEMTECUH
LEUIEKEC. PL. GIMVNAP YEFAO TNE SDYZEMT NIPSEUB. NE IOQDILEC NRG BAL
OETNELBIEUC GAS BLRP PELHTRO; AOC, ABTEL LEMEIKIOF NEL AOSGEL, ASVEC IO
A NESITATIOF PAOOEL NRG UROF PL. CALMH NAC YEEO STAHIOF TNELE.

“AYRDT A PROTN,” SAIC EUIJAYETN; AOC TNEO, DOGIUUIOF TR UET TNE SDYZEMT
CLRW, ACCEC, “NE IS A PAO RB KELH UALFE WLRWELTH IO CELYHSNILE, I
DOCELSTAOC.”

“HES,” LEWUIEC GIMVNAP; “NIS ESTATE TNELE IS A ORYUE ROE. A MUEAL TEO
TNRDSAOC WEL AOODP. HRD MRDUC ORT NAKE PET GITN A WELSRO PRLE MAWAYUE RB
FIKIOF HRD MELTAIO IOBRLPATIRO RO TNAT NEAC TNAO PHSEUB--BRL I NAKE YEEO
MROOEMTEC GITN NIS BAPIUH, IO A WALTIMDUAL PAOOEL, BLRP PH IOBAOMH.”

EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT YDT URRV SDLWLISEC.

“HRD PAH GEUU YE SDLWLISEC, PISS YEOOET, AT SDMN AO ASSELTIRO, ABTEL
SEEIOF, AS HRD WLRYAYUH PIFNT, TNE KELH MRUC PAOOEL RB RDL PEETIOF
HESTELCAH. ALE HRD PDMN AMQDAIOTEC GITN PL. CALMH?”

“AS PDMN AS I EKEL GISN TR YE,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, GALPUH. “I NAKE SWEOT
BRDL CAHS IO TNE SAPE NRDSE GITN NIP, AOC I TNIOV NIP KELH
CISAFLEEAYUE.”

“I NAKE OR LIFNT TR FIKE _PH_ RWIOIRO,” SAIC GIMVNAP, “AS TR NIS YEIOF
AFLEEAYUE RL RTNELGISE. I AP ORT QDAUIBIEC TR BRLP ROE. I NAKE VORGO NIP
TRR UROF AOC TRR GEUU TR YE A BAIL ZDCFE. IT IS IPWRSSIYUE BRL _PE_ TR
YE IPWALTIAU. YDT I YEUIEKE HRDL RWIOIRO RB NIP GRDUC IO FEOELAU
ASTROISN--AOC, WELNAWS, HRD GRDUC ORT EXWLESS IT QDITE SR STLROFUH
AOHGNELE EUSE. NELE HRD ALE IO HRDL RGO BAPIUH.”

“DWRO PH GRLC I SAH OR PRLE _NELE_ TNAO I PIFNT SAH IO AOH NRDSE IO TNE
OEIFNYRDLNRRC, EXMEWT OETNELBIEUC. NE IS ORT AT AUU UIVEC IO
NELTBRLCSNILE. EKELHYRCH IS CISFDSTEC GITN NIS WLICE. HRD GIUU ORT BIOC
NIP PRLE BAKRDLAYUH SWRVEO RB YH AOHROE.”

“I MAOORT WLETEOC TR YE SRLLH,” SAIC GIMVNAP, ABTEL A SNRLT
IOTELLDWTIRO, “TNAT NE RL TNAT AOH PAO SNRDUC ORT YE ESTIPATEC YEHROC
TNEIL CESELTS; YDT GITN _NIP_ I YEUIEKE IT CRES ORT RBTEO NAWWEO. TNE
GRLUC IS YUIOCEC YH NIS BRLTDOE AOC MROSEQDEOME, RL BLIFNTEOEC YH NIS
NIFN AOC IPWRSIOF PAOOELS, AOC SEES NIP ROUH AS NE MNRRSES TR YE SEEO.”

“I SNRDUC TAVE NIP, EKEO RO _PH_ SUIFNT AMQDAIOTAOME, TR YE AO
IUU-TEPWELEC PAO.”

GIMVNAP ROUH SNRRV NIS NEAC.

“I GROCEL,” SAIC NE, AT TNE OEXT RWWRLTDOITH RB SWEAVIOF, “GNETNEL NE IS
UIVEUH TR YE IO TNIS MRDOTLH PDMN UROFEL.”

“I CR ORT AT AUU VORG; YDT I _NEALC_ ORTNIOF RB NIS FRIOF AGAH GNEO I
GAS AT OETNELBIEUC. I NRWE HRDL WUAOS IO BAKRDL RB TNE ----SNILE GIUU
ORT YE ABBEMTEC YH NIS YEIOF IO TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC.”

“RN OR--IT IS ORT BRL _PE_ TR YE CLIKEO AGAH YH PL. CALMH. IB _NE_
GISNES TR AKRIC SEEIOF _PE_ NE PDST FR. GE ALE ORT RO BLIEOCUH TELPS,
AOC IT AUGAHS FIKES PE WAIO TR PEET NIP, YDT I NAKE OR LEASRO BRL
AKRICIOF _NIP_ YDT GNAT I PIFNT WLRMUAIP TR AUU TNE GRLUC--A SEOSE RB
KELH FLEAT IUU-DSAFE, AOC PRST WAIOBDU LEFLETS AT NIS YEIOF GNAT NE IS.
NIS BATNEL, PISS YEOOET, TNE UATE PL. CALMH, GAS ROE RB TNE YEST PEO
TNAT EKEL YLEATNEC, AOC TNE TLDEST BLIEOC I EKEL NAC; AOC I MAO OEKEL YE
IO MRPWAOH GITN TNIS PL. CALMH GITNRDT YEIOF FLIEKEC TR TNE SRDU YH A
TNRDSAOC TEOCEL LEMRUUEMTIROS. NIS YENAKIRDL TR PHSEUB NAS YEEO
SMAOCAURDS; YDT I KELIUH YEUIEKE I MRDUC BRLFIKE NIP AOHTNIOF AOC
EKELHTNIOF, LATNEL TNAO NIS CISAWWRIOTIOF TNE NRWES AOC CISFLAMIOF TNE
PEPRLH RB NIS BATNEL.”

EUIJAYETN BRDOC TNE IOTELEST RB TNE SDYZEMT IOMLEASE, AOC UISTEOEC GITN
AUU NEL NEALT; YDT TNE CEUIMAMH RB IT WLEKEOTEC BDLTNEL IOQDILH.

PL. GIMVNAP YEFAO TR SWEAV RO PRLE FEOELAU TRWIMS, PELHTRO, TNE
OEIFNYRDLNRRC, TNE SRMIETH, AWWEALIOF NIFNUH WUEASEC GITN AUU TNAT NE
NAC HET SEEO, AOC SWEAVIOF RB TNE UATTEL, ESWEMIAUUH, GITN FEOTUE YDT
KELH IOTEUUIFIYUE FAUUAOTLH.

“IT GAS TNE WLRSWEMT RB MROSTAOT SRMIETH, AOC FRRC SRMIETH,” NE ACCEC,
“GNIMN GAS PH MNIEB IOCDMEPEOT TR EOTEL TNE ----SNILE. I VORG IT TR YE A
PRST LESWEMTAYUE, AFLEEAYUE MRLWS; AOC PH BLIEOC CEOOH TEPWTEC PE
BDLTNEL YH NIS AMMRDOT RB TNEIL WLESEOT QDALTELS, AOC TNE KELH FLEAT
ATTEOTIROS AOC EXMEUUEOT AMQDAIOTAOME PELHTRO NAC WLRMDLEC TNEP.
SRMIETH, I RGO, IS OEMESSALH TR PE. I NAKE YEEO A CISAWWRIOTEC PAO, AOC
PH SWILITS GIUU ORT YEAL SRUITDCE. I _PDST_ NAKE EPWURHPEOT AOC SRMIETH.
A PIUITALH UIBE IS ORT GNAT I GAS IOTEOCEC BRL, YDT MILMDPSTAOMES NAKE
ORG PACE IT EUIFIYUE. TNE MNDLMN _RDFNT_ TR NAKE YEEO PH WLRBESSIRO--I
GAS YLRDFNT DW BRL TNE MNDLMN; AOC I SNRDUC AT TNIS TIPE NAKE YEEO IO
WRSSESSIRO RB A PRST KAUDAYUE UIKIOF, NAC IT WUEASEC TNE FEOTUEPAO GE
GELE SWEAVIOF RB ZDST ORG.”

“IOCEEC!”

“HES--TNE UATE PL. CALMH YEQDEATNEC PE TNE OEXT WLESEOTATIRO RB TNE YEST
UIKIOF IO NIS FIBT. NE GAS PH FRCBATNEL, AOC EXMESSIKEUH ATTAMNEC TR PE.
I MAOORT CR ZDSTIME TR NIS VIOCOESS. NE PEAOT TR WLRKICE BRL PE APWUH,
AOC TNRDFNT NE NAC CROE IT; YDT GNEO TNE UIKIOF BEUU, IT GAS FIKEO
EUSEGNELE.”

“FRRC NEAKEOS!” MLIEC EUIJAYETN; “YDT NRG MRDUC _TNAT_ YE? NRG MRDUC NIS
GIUU YE CISLEFALCEC? GNH CIC ORT HRD SEEV UEFAU LECLESS?”

“TNELE GAS ZDST SDMN AO IOBRLPAUITH IO TNE TELPS RB TNE YEQDEST AS TR
FIKE PE OR NRWE BLRP UAG. A PAO RB NRORDL MRDUC ORT NAKE CRDYTEC TNE
IOTEOTIRO, YDT PL. CALMH MNRSE TR CRDYT IT--RL TR TLEAT IT AS A PELEUH
