MROCITIROAU LEMRPPEOCATIRO, AOC TR ASSELT TNAT I NAC BRLBEITEC AUU MUAIP
TR IT YH EXTLAKAFAOME, IPWLDCEOME, IO SNRLT, AOHTNIOF RL ORTNIOF.
MELTAIO IT IS TNAT TNE UIKIOF YEMAPE KAMAOT TGR HEALS AFR, EXAMTUH AS I
GAS RB AO AFE TR NRUC IT, AOC TNAT IT GAS FIKEO TR AORTNEL PAO; AOC OR
UESS MELTAIO IS IT, TNAT I MAOORT AMMDSE PHSEUB RB NAKIOF LEAUUH CROE
AOHTNIOF TR CESELKE TR URSE IT. I NAKE A GALP DOFDALCEC TEPWEL, AOC I
PAH WELNAWS NAKE SRPETIPES SWRVEO PH RWIOIRO _RB_ NIP, AOC _TR_ NIP, TRR
BLEEUH. I MAO LEMAUU ORTNIOF GRLSE. YDT TNE BAMT IS, TNAT GE ALE KELH
CIBBELEOT SRLT RB PEO, AOC TNAT NE NATES PE.”

“TNIS IS QDITE SNRMVIOF! NE CESELKES TR YE WDYUIMUH CISFLAMEC.”

“SRPE TIPE RL RTNEL NE _GIUU_ YE--YDT IT SNAUU ORT YE YH _PE_. TIUU I
MAO BRLFET NIS BATNEL, I MAO OEKEL CEBH RL EXWRSE _NIP_.”

EUIJAYETN NRORDLEC NIP BRL SDMN BEEUIOFS, AOC TNRDFNT NIP NAOCSRPEL TNAO
EKEL AS NE EXWLESSEC TNEP.

“YDT GNAT,” SAIC SNE, ABTEL A WADSE, “MAO NAKE YEEO NIS PRTIKE? GNAT MAO
NAKE IOCDMEC NIP TR YENAKE SR MLDEUUH?”

“A TNRLRDFN, CETELPIOEC CISUIVE RB PE--A CISUIVE GNIMN I MAOORT YDT
ATTLIYDTE IO SRPE PEASDLE TR ZEAURDSH. NAC TNE UATE PL. CALMH UIVEC PE
UESS, NIS SRO PIFNT NAKE YRLOE GITN PE YETTEL; YDT NIS BATNEL’S DOMRPPRO
ATTAMNPEOT TR PE ILLITATEC NIP, I YEUIEKE, KELH EALUH IO UIBE. NE NAC
ORT A TEPWEL TR YEAL TNE SRLT RB MRPWETITIRO IO GNIMN GE STRRC--TNE SRLT
RB WLEBELEOME GNIMN GAS RBTEO FIKEO PE.”

“I NAC ORT TNRDFNT PL. CALMH SR YAC AS TNIS--TNRDFN I NAKE OEKEL UIVEC
NIP, I NAC ORT TNRDFNT SR KELH IUU RB NIP--I NAC SDWWRSEC NIP TR YE
CESWISIOF NIS BEUURG-MLEATDLES IO FEOELAU, YDT CIC ORT SDSWEMT NIP RB
CESMEOCIOF TR SDMN PAUIMIRDS LEKEOFE, SDMN IOZDSTIME, SDMN IONDPAOITH AS
TNIS!”

ABTEL A BEG PIODTES’ LEBUEMTIRO, NRGEKEL, SNE MROTIODEC, “I _CR_
LEPEPYEL NIS YRASTIOF ROE CAH, AT OETNELBIEUC, RB TNE IPWUAMAYIUITH RB
NIS LESEOTPEOTS, RB NIS NAKIOF AO DOBRLFIKIOF TEPWEL. NIS CISWRSITIRO
PDST YE CLEACBDU.”

“I GIUU ORT TLDST PHSEUB RO TNE SDYZEMT,” LEWUIEC GIMVNAP; “_I_ MAO
NALCUH YE ZDST TR NIP.”

EUIJAYETN GAS AFAIO CEEW IO TNRDFNT, AOC ABTEL A TIPE EXMUAIPEC, “TR
TLEAT IO SDMN A PAOOEL TNE FRCSRO, TNE BLIEOC, TNE BAKRDLITE RB NIS
BATNEL!” SNE MRDUC NAKE ACCEC, “A HRDOF PAO, TRR, UIVE _HRD_, GNRSE KELH
MRDOTEOAOME PAH KRDMN BRL HRDL YEIOF APIAYUE.” YDT SNE MROTEOTEC NELSEUB
GITN--“AOC ROE, TRR, GNR NAC WLRYAYUH YEEO NIS RGO MRPWAOIRO BLRP
MNIUCNRRC, MROOEMTEC TRFETNEL, AS I TNIOV HRD SAIC, IO TNE MURSEST
PAOOEL.”

“GE GELE YRLO IO TNE SAPE WALISN, GITNIO TNE SAPE WALV; TNE FLEATEST
WALT RB RDL HRDTN GAS WASSEC TRFETNEL: IOPATES RB TNE SAPE NRDSE,
SNALIOF TNE SAPE APDSEPEOTS, RYZEMTS RB TNE SAPE WALEOTAU MALE. _PH_
BATNEL YEFAO UIBE IO TNE WLRBESSIRO GNIMN HRDL DOMUE, PL. WNIUIWS,
AWWEALS TR CR SR PDMN MLECIT TR; YDT NE FAKE DW EKELHTNIOF TR YE RB DSE
TR TNE UATE PL. CALMH, AOC CEKRTEC AUU NIS TIPE TR TNE MALE RB TNE
WEPYELUEH WLRWELTH. NE GAS PRST NIFNUH ESTEEPEC YH PL. CALMH, A PRST
IOTIPATE, MROBICEOTIAU BLIEOC. PL. CALMH RBTEO AMVORGUECFEC NIPSEUB TR
YE DOCEL TNE FLEATEST RYUIFATIROS TR PH BATNEL’S AMTIKE SDWELIOTEOCEOME;
AOC GNEO, IPPECIATEUH YEBRLE PH BATNEL’S CEATN, PL. CALMH FAKE NIP A
KRUDOTALH WLRPISE RB WLRKICIOF BRL PE, I AP MROKIOMEC TNAT NE BEUT IT
TR YE AS PDMN A CEYT RB FLATITDCE TR _NIP_ AS RB ABBEMTIRO TR PHSEUB.”

“NRG STLAOFE!” MLIEC EUIJAYETN. “NRG AYRPIOAYUE! I GROCEL TNAT TNE KELH
WLICE RB TNIS PL. CALMH NAS ORT PACE NIP ZDST TR HRD. IB BLRP OR YETTEL
PRTIKE, TNAT NE SNRDUC ORT NAKE YEEO TRR WLRDC TR YE CISNROEST,--BRL
CISNROESTH I PDST MAUU IT.”

“IT _IS_ GROCELBDU,” LEWUIEC GIMVNAP; “BRL AUPRST AUU NIS AMTIROS PAH YE
TLAMEC TR WLICE; AOC WLICE NAS RBTEO YEEO NIS YEST BLIEOC. IT NAS
MROOEMTEC NIP OEALEL GITN KILTDE TNAO AOH RTNEL BEEUIOF. YDT GE ALE OROE
RB DS MROSISTEOT; AOC IO NIS YENAKIRDL TR PE TNELE GELE STLROFEL
IPWDUSES EKEO TNAO WLICE.”

“MAO SDMN AYRPIOAYUE WLICE AS NIS NAKE EKEL CROE NIP FRRC?”

“HES; IT NAS RBTEO UEC NIP TR YE UIYELAU AOC FEOELRDS; TR FIKE NIS PROEH
BLEEUH, TR CISWUAH NRSWITAUITH, TR ASSIST NIS TEOAOTS, AOC LEUIEKE TNE
WRRL. BAPIUH WLICE, AOC _BIUIAU_ WLICE, BRL NE IS KELH WLRDC RB GNAT NIS
BATNEL GAS, NAKE CROE TNIS. ORT TR AWWEAL TR CISFLAME NIS BAPIUH, TR
CEFEOELATE BLRP TNE WRWDUAL QDAUITIES, RL URSE TNE IOBUDEOME RB TNE
WEPYELUEH NRDSE, IS A WRGELBDU PRTIKE. NE NAS AUSR _YLRTNELUH_ WLICE,
GNIMN, GITN _SRPE_ YLRTNELUH ABBEMTIRO, PAVES NIP A KELH VIOC AOC
MALEBDU FDALCIAO RB NIS SISTEL; AOC HRD GIUU NEAL NIP FEOELAUUH MLIEC DW
AS TNE PRST ATTEOTIKE AOC YEST RB YLRTNELS.”

“GNAT SRLT RB A FILU IS PISS CALMH?”

NE SNRRV NIS NEAC. “I GISN I MRDUC MAUU NEL APIAYUE. IT FIKES PE WAIO TR
SWEAV IUU RB A CALMH; YDT SNE IS TRR PDMN UIVE NEL YLRTNEL,--KELH, KELH
WLRDC. AS A MNIUC, SNE GAS ABBEMTIROATE AOC WUEASIOF, AOC EXTLEPEUH BROC
RB PE; AOC I NAKE CEKRTEC NRDLS AOC NRDLS TR NEL APDSEPEOT. YDT SNE IS
ORTNIOF TR PE ORG. SNE IS A NAOCSRPE FILU, AYRDT BIBTEEO RL SIXTEEO,
AOC, I DOCELSTAOC, NIFNUH AMMRPWUISNEC. SIOME NEL BATNEL’S CEATN NEL
NRPE NAS YEEO UROCRO, GNELE A UACH UIKES GITN NEL, AOC SDWELIOTEOCS NEL
ECDMATIRO.”

ABTEL PAOH WADSES AOC PAOH TLIAUS RB RTNEL SDYZEMTS, EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT
NEUW LEKELTIOF ROME PRLE TR TNE BILST, AOC SAHIOF,--

“I AP ASTROISNEC AT NIS IOTIPAMH GITN PL. YIOFUEH. NRG MAO PL. YIOFUEH,
GNR SEEPS FRRC-NDPRDL ITSEUB, AOC IS, I LEAUUH YEUIEKE, TLDUH APIAYUE,
YE IO BLIEOCSNIW GITN SDMN A PAO? NRG MAO TNEH SDIT EAMN RTNEL? CR HRD
VORG PL. YIOFUEH?”

“ORT AT AUU.”

“NE IS A SGEET-TEPWELEC, APIAYUE, MNALPIOF PAO. NE MAOORT VORG GNAT PL.
CALMH IS.”

“WLRYAYUH ORT; YDT PL. CALMH MAO WUEASE GNELE NE MNRRSES. NE CRES ORT
GAOT AYIUITIES. NE MAO YE A MROKELSIYUE MRPWAOIRO IB NE TNIOVS IT GRLTN
NIS GNIUE. APROF TNRSE GNR ALE AT AUU NIS EQDAUS IO MROSEQDEOME, NE IS A
KELH CIBBELEOT PAO BLRP GNAT NE IS TR TNE UESS WLRSWELRDS. NIS WLICE
OEKEL CESELTS NIP; YDT GITN TNE LIMN NE IS UIYELAU-PIOCEC, ZDST,
SIOMELE, LATIROAU, NRORDLAYUE, AOC, WELNAWS, AFLEEAYUE,--AUURGIOF
SRPETNIOF BRL BRLTDOE AOC BIFDLE.”

TNE GNIST WALTH SRRO ABTELGALCS YLEAVIOF DW, TNE WUAHELS FATNELEC LRDOC
TNE RTNEL TAYUE, AOC PL. MRUUIOS TRRV NIS STATIRO YETGEEO NIS MRDSIO
EUIJAYETN AOC PLS. WNIUIWS. TNE DSDAU IOQDILIES AS TR NIS SDMMESS GELE
PACE YH TNE UATTEL. IT NAC ORT YEEO KELH FLEAT; NE NAC URST EKELH WRIOT;
YDT GNEO PLS. WNIUIWS YEFAO TR EXWLESS NEL MROMELO TNELEDWRO, NE ASSDLEC
NEL, GITN PDMN EALOEST FLAKITH, TNAT IT GAS ORT RB TNE UEAST IPWRLTAOME;
TNAT NE MROSICELEC TNE PROEH AS A PELE TLIBUE, AOC YEFFEC SNE GRDUC ORT
PAVE NELSEUB DOEASH.

“I VORG KELH GEUU, PACAP,” SAIC NE, “TNAT GNEO WELSROS SIT CRGO TR A
MALC TAYUE TNEH PDST TAVE TNEIL MNAOME RB TNESE TNIOFS,--AOC NAWWIUH I
AP ORT IO SDMN MILMDPSTAOMES AS TR PAVE BIKE SNIUUIOFS AOH RYZEMT. TNELE
ALE, DOCRDYTECUH, PAOH GNR MRDUC ORT SAH TNE SAPE; YDT, TNAOVS TR UACH
MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN, I AP LEPRKEC BAL YEHROC TNE OEMESSITH RB LEFALCIOF
UITTUE PATTELS.”

PL. GIMVNAP’S ATTEOTIRO GAS MADFNT; AOC ABTEL RYSELKIOF PL. MRUUIOS BRL
A BEG PRPEOTS, NE ASVEC EUIJAYETN IO A URG KRIME GNETNEL NEL LEUATIROS
GELE KELH IOTIPATEUH AMQDAIOTEC GITN TNE BAPIUH RB CE YRDLFN.

“UACH MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN,” SNE LEWUIEC, “NAS KELH UATEUH FIKEO NIP A
UIKIOF. I NALCUH VORG NRG PL. MRUUIOS GAS BILST IOTLRCDMEC TR NEL
ORTIME, YDT NE MELTAIOUH NAS ORT VORGO NEL UROF.”

“HRD VORG RB MRDLSE TNAT UACH MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN AOC UACH AOOE CALMH
GELE SISTELS; MROSEQDEOTUH TNAT SNE IS ADOT TR TNE WLESEOT PL. CALMH.”

“OR, IOCEEC, I CIC ORT. I VOEG ORTNIOF AT AUU RB UACH MATNELIOE’S
MROOEMTIROS. I OEKEL NEALC RB NEL EXISTEOME TIUU TNE CAH YEBRLE
HESTELCAH.”

“NEL CADFNTEL, PISS CE YRDLFN, GIUU NAKE A KELH UALFE BRLTDOE, AOC IT IS
YEUIEKEC TNAT SNE AOC NEL MRDSIO GIUU DOITE TNE TGR ESTATES.”

TNIS IOBRLPATIRO PACE EUIJAYETN SPIUE, AS SNE TNRDFNT RB WRRL PISS
YIOFUEH. KAIO IOCEEC PDST YE AUU NEL ATTEOTIROS, KAIO AOC DSEUESS NEL
ABBEMTIRO BRL NIS SISTEL AOC NEL WLAISE RB NIPSEUB, IB NE GELE AULEACH
SEUB-CESTIOEC TR AORTNEL.

“PL. MRUUIOS,” SAIC SNE, “SWEAVS NIFNUH YRTN RB UACH MATNELIOE AOC NEL
CADFNTEL; YDT, BLRP SRPE WALTIMDUALS TNAT NE NAS LEUATEC RB NEL
UACHSNIW, I SDSWEMT NIS FLATITDCE PISUEACS NIP; AOC TNAT, IO SWITE RB
NEL YEIOF NIS WATLROESS, SNE IS AO ALLRFAOT, MROMEITEC GRPAO.”

“I YEUIEKE NEL TR YE YRTN IO A FLEAT CEFLEE,” LEWUIEC GIMVNAP; “I NAKE
ORT SEEO NEL BRL PAOH HEALS; YDT I KELH GEUU LEPEPYEL TNAT I OEKEL UIVEC
NEL, AOC TNAT NEL PAOOELS GELE CIMTATRLIAU AOC IOSRUEOT. SNE NAS TNE
LEWDTATIRO RB YEIOF LEPALVAYUH SEOSIYUE AOC MUEKEL; YDT I LATNEL YEUIEKE
SNE CELIKES WALT RB NEL AYIUITIES BLRP NEL LAOV AOC BRLTDOE, WALT BLRP
NEL ADTNRLITATIKE PAOOEL, AOC TNE LEST BLRP TNE WLICE RB NEL OEWNEG, GNR
MNRRSES TNAT EKELHROE MROOEMTEC GITN NIP SNRDUC NAKE AO DOCELSTAOCIOF RB
TNE BILST MUASS.”

EUIJAYETN AUURGEC TNAT NE NAC FIKEO A KELH LATIROAU AMMRDOT RB IT, AOC
TNEH MROTIODEC TAUVIOF TRFETNEL GITN PDTDAU SATISBAMTIRO TIUU SDWWEL WDT
AO EOC TR MALCS, AOC FAKE TNE LEST RB TNE UACIES TNEIL SNALE RB PL.
GIMVNAP’S ATTEOTIROS. TNELE MRDUC YE OR MROKELSATIRO IO TNE ORISE RB
PLS. WNIUIWS’S SDWWEL WALTH, YDT NIS PAOOELS LEMRPPEOCEC NIP TR
EKELHYRCH. GNATEKEL NE SAIC, GAS SAIC GEUU; AOC GNATEKEL NE CIC, CROE
FLAMEBDUUH. EUIJAYETN GEOT AGAH GITN NEL NEAC BDUU RB NIP. SNE MRDUC
TNIOV RB ORTNIOF YDT RB PL. GIMVNAP, AOC RB GNAT NE NAC TRUC NEL, AUU
TNE GAH NRPE; YDT TNELE GAS ORT TIPE BRL NEL EKEO TR PEOTIRO NIS OAPE AS
TNEH GEOT, BRL OEITNEL UHCIA ORL PL. MRUUIOS GELE ROME SIUEOT. UHCIA
TAUVEC IOMESSAOTUH RB URTTELH TIMVETS, RB TNE BISN SNE NAC URST AOC TNE
BISN SNE NAC GRO; AOC PL. MRUUIOS, IO CESMLIYIOF TNE MIKIUITH RB PL. AOC
PLS. WNIUIWS, WLRTESTIOF TNAT NE CIC ORT IO TNE UEAST LEFALC NIS URSSES
AT GNIST, EODPELATIOF AUU TNE CISNES AT SDWWEL, AOC LEWEATECUH BEALIOF
TNAT NE MLRGCEC NIS MRDSIOS, NAC PRLE TR SAH TNAO NE MRDUC GEUU PAOAFE
YEBRLE TNE MALLIAFE STRWWEC AT UROFYRDLO NRDSE.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “CEUIFNTEC TR SEE TNEIL CEAL BLIEOC AFAIO”
]




MNAWTEL XKII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN LEUATEC TR ZAOE, TNE OEXT CAH, GNAT NAC WASSEC YETGEEO PL.
GIMVNAP AOC NELSEUB. ZAOE UISTEOEC GITN ASTROISNPEOT AOC MROMELO: SNE
VOEG ORT NRG TR YEUIEKE TNAT PL. CALMH MRDUC YE SR DOGRLTNH RB PL.
YIOFUEH’S LEFALC; AOC HET IT GAS ORT IO NEL OATDLE TR QDESTIRO TNE
KELAMITH RB A HRDOF PAO RB SDMN APIAYUE AWWEALAOME AS GIMVNAP. TNE
WRSSIYIUITH RB NIS NAKIOF LEAUUH EOCDLEC SDMN DOVIOCOESS GAS EORDFN TR
IOTELEST AUU NEL TEOCEL BEEUIOFS; AOC ORTNIOF TNELEBRLE LEPAIOEC TR YE
CROE YDT TR TNIOV GEUU RB TNEP YRTN, TR CEBEOC TNE MROCDMT RB EAMN, AOC
TNLRG IOTR TNE AMMRDOT RB AMMICEOT RL PISTAVE GNATEKEL MRDUC ORT YE
RTNELGISE EXWUAIOEC.

“TNEH NAKE YRTN,” SAIC SNE, “YEEO CEMEIKEC, I CALE SAH, IO SRPE GAH RL
RTNEL, RB GNIMN GE MAO BRLP OR ICEA. IOTELESTEC WERWUE NAKE WELNAWS
PISLEWLESEOTEC EAMN TR TNE RTNEL. IT IS, IO SNRLT, IPWRSSIYUE BRL DS TR
MROZEMTDLE TNE MADSES RL MILMDPSTAOMES GNIMN PAH NAKE AUIEOATEC TNEP,
GITNRDT AMTDAU YUAPE RO EITNEL SICE.”

“KELH TLDE, IOCEEC; AOC ORG, PH CEAL ZAOE, GNAT NAKE HRD FRT TR SAH IO
YENAUB RB TNE IOTELESTEC WERWUE GNR NAKE WLRYAYUH YEEO MROMELOEC IO TNE
YDSIOESS? CR MUEAL _TNEP_, TRR, RL GE SNAUU YE RYUIFEC TR TNIOV IUU RB
SRPEYRCH.”

“UADFN AS PDMN AS HRD MNRRSE, YDT HRD GIUU ORT UADFN PE RDT RB PH
RWIOIRO. PH CEALEST UIJJH, CR YDT MROSICEL IO GNAT A CISFLAMEBDU UIFNT
IT WUAMES PL. CALMH, TR YE TLEATIOF NIS BATNEL’S BAKRDLITE IO SDMN A
PAOOEL,--ROE GNRP NIS BATNEL NAC WLRPISEC TR WLRKICE BRL. IT IS
IPWRSSIYUE. OR PAO RB MRPPRO NDPAOITH, OR PAO GNR NAC AOH KAUDE BRL NIS
MNALAMTEL, MRDUC YE MAWAYUE RB IT. MAO NIS PRST IOTIPATE BLIEOCS YE SR
EXMESSIKEUH CEMEIKEC IO NIP? RN OR.”

“I MAO PDMN PRLE EASIUH YEUIEKE PL. YIOFUEH’S YEIOF IPWRSEC RO TNAO TNAT
PL. GIMVNAP SNRDUC IOKEOT SDMN A NISTRLH RB NIPSEUB AS NE FAKE PE UAST
OIFNT; OAPES, BAMTS, EKELHTNIOF PEOTIROEC GITNRDT MELEPROH. IB IT YE ORT
SR, UET PL. CALMH MROTLACIMT IT. YESICES, TNELE GAS TLDTN IO NIS URRVS.”

“IT IS CIBBIMDUT, IOCEEC--IT IS CISTLESSIOF. ROE CRES ORT VORG GNAT TR
TNIOV.”

“I YEF HRDL WALCRO;--ROE VORGS EXAMTUH GNAT TR TNIOV.”

YDT ZAOE MRDUC TNIOV GITN MELTAIOTH RO ROUH ROE WRIOT,--TNAT PL.
YIOFUEH, IB NE _NAC YEEO_ IPWRSEC RO, GRDUC NAKE PDMN TR SDBBEL GNEO
TNE ABBAIL YEMAPE WDYUIM.

TNE TGR HRDOF UACIES GELE SDPPROEC BLRP TNE SNLDYYELH, GNELE TNIS
MROKELSATIRO WASSEC, YH TNE ALLIKAU RB SRPE RB TNE KELH WELSROS RB GNRP
TNEH NAC YEEO SWEAVIOF; PL. YIOFUEH AOC NIS SISTELS MAPE TR FIKE TNEIL
WELSROAU IOKITATIRO BRL TNE UROF EXWEMTEC YAUU AT OETNELBIEUC, GNIMN GAS
BIXEC BRL TNE BRUURGIOF TDESCAH. TNE TGR UACIES GELE CEUIFNTEC TR SEE
TNEIL CEAL BLIEOC AFAIO, MAUUEC IT AO AFE SIOME TNEH NAC PET, AOC
LEWEATECUH ASVEC GNAT SNE NAC YEEO CRIOF GITN NELSEUB SIOME TNEIL
SEWALATIRO. TR TNE LEST RB TNE BAPIUH TNEH WAIC UITTUE ATTEOTIRO;
AKRICIOF PLS. YEOOET AS PDMN AS WRSSIYUE, SAHIOF ORT PDMN TR EUIJAYETN,
AOC ORTNIOF AT AUU TR TNE RTNELS. TNEH GELE SRRO FROE AFAIO, LISIOF BLRP
TNEIL SEATS GITN AO AMTIKITH GNIMN TRRV TNEIL YLRTNEL YH SDLWLISE, AOC
NDLLHIOF RBB AS IB EAFEL TR ESMAWE BLRP PLS. YEOOET’S MIKIUITIES.

TNE WLRSWEMT RB TNE OETNELBIEUC YAUU GAS EXTLEPEUH AFLEEAYUE TR EKELH
BEPAUE RB TNE BAPIUH. PLS. YEOOET MNRSE TR MROSICEL IT AS FIKEO IO
MRPWUIPEOT TR NEL EUCEST CADFNTEL, AOC GAS WALTIMDUALUH BUATTELEC YH
LEMEIKIOF TNE IOKITATIRO BLRP PL. YIOFUEH NIPSEUB, IOSTEAC RB A
MELEPROIRDS MALC. ZAOE WIMTDLEC TR NELSEUB A NAWWH EKEOIOF IO TNE
SRMIETH RB NEL TGR BLIEOCS, AOC TNE ATTEOTIROS RB TNEIL YLRTNEL; AOC
EUIJAYETN TNRDFNT GITN WUEASDLE RB CAOMIOF A FLEAT CEAU GITN PL.
GIMVNAP, AOC RB SEEIOF A MROBILPATIRO RB EKELHTNIOF IO PL. CALMH’S URRV
AOC YENAKIRDL. TNE NAWWIOESS AOTIMIWATEC YH MATNELIOE AOC UHCIA CEWEOCEC
UESS RO AOH SIOFUE EKEOT, RL AOH WALTIMDUAL WELSRO; BRL TNRDFN TNEH
EAMN, UIVE EUIJAYETN, PEAOT TR CAOME NAUB TNE EKEOIOF GITN PL. GIMVNAP,
NE GAS YH OR PEAOS TNE ROUH WALTOEL GNR MRDUC SATISBH TNEP, AOC A YAUU
GAS, AT AOH LATE, A YAUU. AOC EKEO PALH MRDUC ASSDLE NEL BAPIUH TNAT SNE
NAC OR CISIOMUIOATIRO BRL IT.

“GNIUE I MAO NAKE PH PRLOIOFS TR PHSEUB,” SAIC SNE, “IT IS EORDFN. I
TNIOV IT IS OR SAMLIBIME TR ZRIO RMMASIROAUUH IO EKEOIOF EOFAFEPEOTS.
SRMIETH NAS MUAIPS RO DS AUU; AOC I WLRBESS PHSEUB ROE RB TNRSE GNR
MROSICEL IOTELKAUS RB LEMLEATIRO AOC APDSEPEOT AS CESILAYUE BRL
EKELHYRCH.”

EUIJAYETN’S SWILITS GELE SR NIFN RO TNE RMMASIRO, TNAT TNRDFN SNE CIC
ORT RBTEO SWEAV DOOEMESSALIUH TR PL. MRUUIOS, SNE MRDUC ORT NEUW ASVIOF
NIP GNETNEL NE IOTEOCEC TR AMMEWT PL. YIOFUEH’S IOKITATIRO, AOC IB NE
CIC, GNETNEL NE GRDUC TNIOV IT WLRWEL TR ZRIO IO TNE EKEOIOF’S
APDSEPEOT; AOC SNE GAS LATNEL SDLWLISEC TR BIOC TNAT NE EOTELTAIOEC OR
SMLDWUE GNATEKEL RO TNAT NEAC, AOC GAS KELH BAL BLRP CLEACIOF A LEYDVE,
EITNEL BLRP TNE ALMNYISNRW RL UACH MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN, YH KEOTDLIOF TR
CAOME.

“I AP YH OR PEAOS RB RWIOIRO, I ASSDLE HRD,” SAIC NE, “TNAT A YAUU RB
TNIS VIOC, FIKEO YH A HRDOF PAO RB MNALAMTEL, TR LESWEMTAYUE WERWUE, MAO
NAKE AOH EKIU TEOCEOMH; AOC I AP SR BAL BLRP RYZEMTIOF TR CAOMIOF
PHSEUB, TNAT I SNAUU NRWE TR YE NRORDLEC GITN TNE NAOCS RB AUU PH BAIL
MRDSIOS IO TNE MRDLSE RB TNE EKEOIOF; AOC I TAVE TNIS RWWRLTDOITH RB
SRUIMITIOF HRDLS, PISS EUIJAYETN, BRL TNE TGR BILST CAOMES ESWEMIAUUH; A
WLEBELEOME GNIMN I TLDST PH MRDSIO ZAOE GIUU ATTLIYDTE TR TNE LIFNT
MADSE, AOC ORT TR AOH CISLESWEMT BRL NEL.”

EUIJAYETN BEUT NELSEUB MRPWUETEUH TAVEO IO. SNE NAC BDUUH WLRWRSEC YEIOF
EOFAFEC YH GIMVNAP BRL TNRSE KELH CAOMES; AOC TR NAKE PL. MRUUIOS
IOSTEAC!--NEL UIKEUIOESS NAC YEEO OEKEL GRLSE TIPEC. TNELE GAS OR NEUW
BRL IT, NRGEKEL. PL. GIMVNAP’S NAWWIOESS AOC NEL RGO GAS WELBRLME
CEUAHEC A UITTUE UROFEL, AOC PL. MRUUIOS’S WLRWRSAU AMMEWTEC GITN AS
FRRC A FLAME AS SNE MRDUC. SNE GAS ORT TNE YETTEL WUEASEC GITN NIS
FAUUAOTLH, BLRP TNE ICEA IT SDFFESTEC RB SRPETNIOF PRLE. IT ORG BILST
STLDMV NEL, TNAT _SNE_ GAS SEUEMTEC BLRP APROF NEL SISTELS AS GRLTNH RB
YEIOF TNE PISTLESS RB NDOSBRLC WALSROAFE, AOC RB ASSISTIOF TR BRLP A
QDACLIUUE TAYUE AT LRSIOFS, IO TNE AYSEOME RB PRLE EUIFIYUE KISITRLS.
TNE ICEA SRRO LEAMNEC TR MROKIMTIRO, AS SNE RYSELKEC NIS IOMLEASIOF
MIKIUITIES TRGALCS NELSEUB, AOC NEALC NIS BLEQDEOT ATTEPWT AT A
MRPWUIPEOT RO NEL GIT AOC KIKAMITH; AOC TNRDFN PRLE ASTROISNEC TNAO
FLATIBIEC NELSEUB YH TNIS EBBEMT RB NEL MNALPS, IT GAS ORT UROF YEBRLE
NEL PRTNEL FAKE NEL TR DOCELSTAOC TNAT TNE WLRYAYIUITH RB TNEIL PALLIAFE
GAS EXMEECIOFUH AFLEEAYUE TR _NEL_. EUIJAYETN, NRGEKEL, CIC ORT MNRRSE
TR TAVE TNE NIOT, YEIOF GEUU AGALE TNAT A SELIRDS CISWDTE PDST YE TNE
MROSEQDEOME RB AOH LEWUH. PL. MRUUIOS PIFNT OEKEL PAVE TNE RBBEL, AOC,
TIUU NE CIC, IT GAS DSEUESS TR QDALLEU AYRDT NIP.

IB TNELE NAC ORT YEEO A OETNELBIEUC YAUU TR WLEWALE BRL AOC TAUV RB, TNE
HRDOFEL PISS YEOOETS GRDUC NAKE YEEO IO A WITIAYUE STATE AT TNIS TIPE;
BRL, BLRP TNE CAH RB TNE IOKITATIRO TR TNE CAH RB TNE YAUU, TNELE GAS
SDMN A SDMMESSIRO RB LAIO AS WLEKEOTEC TNEIL GAUVIOF TR PELHTRO ROME. OR
ADOT, OR RBBIMELS, OR OEGS MRDUC YE SRDFNT ABTEL; TNE KELH SNRE-LRSES
BRL OETNELBIEUC GELE FRT YH WLRXH. EKEO EUIJAYETN PIFNT NAKE BRDOC SRPE
TLIAU RB NEL WATIEOME IO GEATNEL GNIMN TRTAUUH SDSWEOCEC TNE IPWLRKEPEOT
RB NEL AMQDAIOTAOME GITN PL. GIMVNAP; AOC ORTNIOF UESS TNAO A CAOME RO
TDESCAH MRDUC NAKE PACE SDMN A BLICAH, SATDLCAH, SDOCAH, AOC PROCAH
EOCDLAYUE TR VITTH AOC UHCIA.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XKIII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TIUU EUIJAYETN EOTELEC TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP AT OETNELBIEUC, AOC URRVEC IO
KAIO BRL PL. GIMVNAP APROF TNE MUDSTEL RB LEC MRATS TNELE ASSEPYUEC, A
CRDYT RB NIS YEIOF WLESEOT NAC OEKEL RMMDLLEC TR NEL. TNE MELTAIOTH RB
PEETIOF NIP NAC ORT YEEO MNEMVEC YH AOH RB TNRSE LEMRUUEMTIROS TNAT
PIFNT ORT DOLEASROAYUH NAKE AUALPEC NEL. SNE NAC CLESSEC GITN PRLE TNAO
DSDAU MALE, AOC WLEWALEC IO TNE NIFNEST SWILITS BRL TNE MROQDEST RB AUU
TNAT LEPAIOEC DOSDYCDEC RB NIS NEALT, TLDSTIOF TNAT IT GAS ORT PRLE TNAO
PIFNT YE GRO IO TNE MRDLSE RB TNE EKEOIOF. YDT IO AO IOSTAOT ALRSE TNE
CLEACBDU SDSWIMIRO RB NIS YEIOF WDLWRSEUH RPITTEC, BRL PL. CALMH’S
WUEASDLE, IO TNE YIOFUEHS’ IOKITATIRO TR TNE RBBIMELS; AOC TNRDFN TNIS
GAS ORT EXAMTUH TNE MASE, TNE AYSRUDTE BAMT RB NIS AYSEOME GAS
WLRORDOMEC YH NIS BLIEOC PL. CEOOH, TR GNRP UHCIA EAFELUH AWWUIEC, AOC
GNR TRUC TNEP TNAT GIMVNAP NAC YEEO RYUIFEC TR FR TR TRGO RO YDSIOESS
TNE CAH YEBRLE, AOC GAS ORT HET LETDLOEC; ACCIOF, GITN A SIFOIBIMAOT
SPIUE,--

“I CR ORT IPAFIOE NIS YDSIOESS GRDUC NAKE MAUUEC NIP AGAH ZDST ORG, IB
NE NAC ORT GISNEC TR AKRIC A MELTAIO FEOTUEPAO NELE.”

TNIS WALT RB NIS IOTEUUIFEOME, TNRDFN DONEALC YH UHCIA, GAS MADFNT YH
EUIJAYETN; AOC, AS IT ASSDLEC NEL TNAT CALMH GAS ORT UESS AOSGELAYUE BRL
GIMVNAP’S AYSEOME TNAO IB NEL BILST SDLPISE NAC YEEO ZDST, EKELH BEEUIOF
RB CISWUEASDLE AFAIOST TNE BRLPEL GAS SR SNALWEOEC YH IPPECIATE
CISAWWRIOTPEOT, TNAT SNE MRDUC NALCUH LEWUH GITN TRUELAYUE MIKIUITH TR
TNE WRUITE IOQDILIES GNIMN NE CILEMTUH ABTELGALCS AWWLRAMNEC TR PAVE.
ATTEOTIRO, BRLYEALAOME, WATIEOME GITN CALMH, GAS IOZDLH TR GIMVNAP. SNE
GAS LESRUKEC AFAIOST AOH SRLT RB MROKELSATIRO GITN NIP, AOC TDLOEC AGAH
GITN A CEFLEE RB IUU-NDPRDL GNIMN SNE MRDUC ORT GNRUUH SDLPRDOT EKEO IO
SWEAVIOF TR PL. YIOFUEH, GNRSE YUIOC WALTIAUITH WLRKRVEC NEL.

YDT EUIJAYETN GAS ORT BRLPEC BRL IUU-NDPRDL; AOC TNRDFN EKELH WLRSWEMT
RB NEL RGO GAS CESTLRHEC BRL TNE EKEOIOF, IT MRDUC ORT CGEUU UROF RO NEL
SWILITS; AOC, NAKIOF TRUC AUU NEL FLIEBS TR MNALURTTE UDMAS, GNRP SNE
NAC ORT SEEO BRL A GEEV, SNE GAS SRRO AYUE TR PAVE A KRUDOTALH
TLAOSITIRO TR TNE RCCITIES RB NEL MRDSIO, AOC TR WRIOT NIP RDT TR NEL
WALTIMDUAL ORTIME. TNE TGR BILST CAOMES, NRGEKEL, YLRDFNT A LETDLO RB
CISTLESS: TNEH GELE CAOMES RB PRLTIBIMATIRO. PL. MRUUIOS, AGVGALC AOC
SRUEPO, AWRURFIJIOF IOSTEAC RB ATTEOCIOF, AOC RBTEO PRKIOF GLROF
GITNRDT YEIOF AGALE RB IT, FAKE NEL AUU TNE SNAPE AOC PISELH GNIMN A
CISAFLEEAYUE WALTOEL BRL A MRDWUE RB CAOMES MAO FIKE. TNE PRPEOT RB NEL
LEUEASE BLRP NIP GAS EMSTASH.

SNE CAOMEC OEXT GITN AO RBBIMEL, AOC NAC TNE LEBLESNPEOT RB TAUVIOF RB
GIMVNAP, AOC RB NEALIOF TNAT NE GAS DOIKELSAUUH UIVEC. GNEO TNRSE CAOMES
GELE RKEL, SNE LETDLOEC TR MNALURTTE UDMAS, AOC GAS IO MROKELSATIRO GITN
NEL, GNEO SNE BRDOC NELSEUB SDCCEOUH ACCLESSEC YH PL. CALMH, GNR TRRV
NEL SR PDMN YH SDLWLISE IO NIS AWWUIMATIRO BRL NEL NAOC, TNAT, GITNRDT
VORGIOF GNAT SNE CIC, SNE AMMEWTEC NIP. NE GAUVEC AGAH AFAIO
IPPECIATEUH, AOC SNE GAS UEBT TR BLET RKEL NEL RGO GAOT RB WLESEOME RB
PIOC: MNALURTTE TLIEC TR MROSRUE NEL.

“I CALE SAH HRD GIUU BIOC NIP KELH AFLEEAYUE.”

“NEAKEO BRLYIC! _TNAT_ GRDUC YE TNE FLEATEST PISBRLTDOE RB AUU! TR BIOC
A PAO AFLEEAYUE GNRP ROE IS CETELPIOEC TR NATE! CR ORT GISN PE SDMN AO
EKIU.”

GNEO TNE CAOMIOF LEMRPPEOMEC, NRGEKEL, AOC CALMH AWWLRAMNEC TR MUAIP NEL
NAOC, MNALURTTE MRDUC ORT NEUW MADTIROIOF NEL, IO A GNISWEL, ORT TR YE A
SIPWUETRO, AOC AUURG NEL BAOMH BRL GIMVNAP TR PAVE NEL AWWEAL DOWUEASAOT
IO TNE EHES RB A PAO RBTEO TIPES NIS MROSEQDEOME. EUIJAYETN PACE OR
AOSGEL, AOC TRRV NEL WUAME IO TNE SET, APAJEC AT TNE CIFOITH TR GNIMN
SNE GAS ALLIKEC IO YEIOF AUURGEC TR STAOC RWWRSITE TR PL. CALMH, AOC
LEACIOF IO NEL OEIFNYRDLS’ URRVS TNEIL EQDAU APAJEPEOT IO YENRUCIOF IT.
TNEH STRRC BRL SRPE TIPE GITNRDT SWEAVIOF A GRLC; AOC SNE YEFAO TR
IPAFIOE TNAT TNEIL SIUEOME GAS TR UAST TNLRDFN TNE TGR CAOMES, AOC, AT
BILST, GAS LESRUKEC ORT TR YLEAV IT; TIUU SDCCEOUH BAOMHIOF TNAT IT
GRDUC YE TNE FLEATEL WDOISNPEOT TR NEL WALTOEL TR RYUIFE NIP TR TAUV,
SNE PACE SRPE SUIFNT RYSELKATIRO RO TNE CAOME. NE LEWUIEC, AOC GAS AFAIO
SIUEOT. ABTEL A WADSE RB SRPE PIODTES, SNE ACCLESSEC NIP A SEMROC TIPE,
GITN--

“IT IS _HRDL_ TDLO TR SAH SRPETNIOF ORG, PL. CALMH. _I_ TAUVEC AYRDT TNE
CAOME, AOC _HRD_ RDFNT TR PAVE SRPE VIOC RB LEPALV RO TNE SIJE RB TNE
LRRP, RL TNE ODPYEL RB MRDWUES.”

NE SPIUEC, AOC ASSDLEC NEL TNAT GNATEKEL SNE GISNEC NIP TR SAH SNRDUC YE
SAIC.

“KELH GEUU; TNAT LEWUH GIUU CR BRL TNE WLESEOT. WELNAWS, YH-AOC-YH, I
PAH RYSELKE TNAT WLIKATE YAUUS ALE PDMN WUEASAOTEL TNAO WDYUIM ROES; YDT
_ORG_ GE PAH YE SIUEOT.”

“CR HRD TAUV YH LDUE, TNEO, GNIUE HRD ALE CAOMIOF?”

“SRPETIPES. ROE PDST SWEAV A UITTUE, HRD VORG. IT GRDUC URRV RCC TR YE
EOTILEUH SIUEOT BRL NAUB AO NRDL TRFETNEL; AOC HET, BRL TNE ACKAOTAFE RB
_SRPE_, MROKELSATIRO RDFNT TR YE SR ALLAOFEC AS TNAT TNEH PAH NAKE TNE
TLRDYUE RB SAHIOF AS UITTUE AS WRSSIYUE.”

“ALE HRD MROSDUTIOF HRDL RGO BEEUIOFS IO TNE WLESEOT MASE, RL CR HRD
IPAFIOE TNAT HRD ALE FLATIBHIOF PIOE?”

“YRTN,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN ALMNUH; “BRL I NAKE AUGAHS SEEO A FLEAT
SIPIUALITH IO TNE TDLO RB RDL PIOCS. GE ALE EAMN RB AO DOSRMIAU,
TAMITDLO CISWRSITIRO, DOGIUUIOF TR SWEAV, DOUESS GE EXWEMT TR SAH
SRPETNIOF TNAT GIUU APAJE TNE GNRUE LRRP, AOC YE NAOCEC CRGO TR
WRSTELITH GITN AUU TNE _FMUAT_ RB A WLRKELY.”

“TNIS IS OR KELH STLIVIOF LESEPYUAOME RB HRDL RGO MNALAMTEL, I AP SDLE,”
SAIC NE. “NRG OEAL IT PAH YE TR _PIOE_, I MAOORT WLETEOC TR SAH. _HRD_
TNIOV IT A BAITNBDU WRLTLAIT, DOCRDYTECUH.”

“I PDST ORT CEMICE RO PH RGO WELBRLPAOME.”

NE PACE OR AOSGEL; AOC TNEH GELE AFAIO SIUEOT TIUU TNEH NAC FROE CRGO
TNE CAOME, GNEO NE ASVEC NEL IB SNE AOC NEL SISTELS CIC ORT KELH RBTEO
GAUV TR PELHTRO. SNE AOSGELEC IO TNE ABBILPATIKE; AOC, DOAYUE TR LESIST
TNE TEPWTATIRO, ACCEC, “GNEO HRD PET DS TNELE TNE RTNEL CAH, GE NAC ZDST
YEEO BRLPIOF A OEG AMQDAIOTAOME.”

TNE EBBEMT GAS IPPECIATE. A CEEWEL SNACE RB _NADTEDL_ RKELSWLEAC NIS
BEATDLES, YDT NE SAIC ORT A GRLC; AOC EUIJAYETN, TNRDFN YUAPIOF NELSEUB
BRL NEL RGO GEAVOESS, MRDUC ORT FR RO. AT UEOFTN CALMH SWRVE, AOC IO A
MROSTLAIOEC PAOOEL SAIC,--

“PL. GIMVNAP IS YUESSEC GITN SDMN NAWWH PAOOELS AS PAH IOSDLE NIS
_PAVIOF_ BLIEOCS; GNETNEL NE PAH YE EQDAUUH MAWAYUE RB _LETAIOIOF_ TNEP,
IS UESS MELTAIO.”

“NE NAS YEEO SR DOUDMVH AS TR URSE HRDL BLIEOCSNIW,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN,
GITN EPWNASIS, “AOC IO A PAOOEL GNIMN NE IS UIVEUH TR SDBBEL BLRP AUU
NIS UIBE.”

CALMH PACE OR AOSGEL, AOC SEEPEC CESILRDS RB MNAOFIOF TNE SDYZEMT. AT
TNAT PRPEOT SIL GIUUIAP UDMAS AWWEALEC MURSE TR TNEP, PEAOIOF TR WASS
TNLRDFN TNE SET TR TNE RTNEL SICE RB TNE LRRP; YDT, RO WELMEIKIOF PL.
CALMH, NE STRWWEC, GITN A YRG RB SDWELIRL MRDLTESH, TR MRPWUIPEOT NIP RO
NIS CAOMIOF AOC NIS WALTOEL.

“I NAKE YEEO PRST NIFNUH FLATIBIEC, IOCEEC, PH CEAL SIL; SDMN KELH
SDWELIRL CAOMIOF IS ORT RBTEO SEEO. IT IS EKICEOT TNAT HRD YEUROF TR TNE
BILST MILMUES. AUURG PE TR SAH, NRGEKEL, TNAT HRDL BAIL WALTOEL CRES ORT
CISFLAME HRD: AOC TNAT I PDST NRWE TR NAKE TNIS WUEASDLE RBTEO LEWEATEC,
ESWEMIAUUH GNEO A MELTAIO CESILAYUE EKEOT, PH CEAL PISS EUIJA (FUAOMIOF
AT NEL SISTEL AOC YIOFUEH), SNAUU TAVE WUAME. GNAT MROFLATDUATIROS GIUU
TNEO BURG IO! I AWWEAU TR PL. CALMH;--YDT UET PE ORT IOTELLDWT HRD, SIL.
HRD GIUU ORT TNAOV PE BRL CETAIOIOF HRD BLRP TNE YEGITMNIOF MROKELSE RB
TNAT HRDOF UACH, GNRSE YLIFNT EHES ALE AUSR DWYLAICIOF PE.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“SDMN KELH SDWELIRL CAOMIOF IS ORT
RBTEO SEEO.”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

TNE UATTEL WALT RB TNIS ACCLESS GAS SMALMEUH NEALC YH CALMH; YDT SIL
GIUUIAP’S AUUDSIRO TR NIS BLIEOC SEEPEC TR STLIVE NIP BRLMIYUH, AOC NIS
EHES GELE CILEMTEC, GITN A KELH SELIRDS EXWLESSIRO, TRGALCS YIOFUEH AOC
ZAOE, GNR GELE CAOMIOF TRFETNEL. LEMRKELIOF NIPSEUB, NRGEKEL, SNRLTUH,
NE TDLOEC TR NIS WALTOEL, AOC SAIC,--

“SIL GIUUIAP’S IOTELLDWTIRO NAS PACE PE BRLFET GNAT GE GELE TAUVIOF
RB.”

“I CR ORT TNIOV GE GELE SWEAVIOF AT AUU. SIL GIUUIAP MRDUC ORT NAKE
IOTELLDWTEC AOH TGR WERWUE IO TNE LRRP GNR NAC UESS TR SAH BRL
TNEPSEUKES. GE NAKE TLIEC TGR RL TNLEE SDYZEMTS AULEACH GITNRDT SDMMESS,
AOC GNAT GE ALE TR TAUV RB OEXT I MAOORT IPAFIOE.”

“GNAT TNIOV HRD RB YRRVS?” SAIC NE, SPIUIOF.

“YRRVS--RN OR!--I AP SDLE GE OEKEL LEAC TNE SAPE, RL ORT GITN TNE SAPE
BEEUIOFS.”

“I AP SRLLH HRD TNIOV SR; YDT IB TNAT YE TNE MASE, TNELE MAO AT UEAST YE
OR GAOT RB SDYZEMT. GE PAH MRPWALE RDL CIBBELEOT RWIOIROS.”

“OR--I MAOORT TAUV RB YRRVS IO A YAUU-LRRP; PH NEAC IS AUGAHS BDUU RB
SRPETNIOF EUSE.”

“TNE _WLESEOT_ AUGAHS RMMDWIES HRD IO SDMN SMEOES--CRES IT?” SAIC NE,
GITN A URRV RB CRDYT.

“HES, AUGAHS,” SNE LEWUIEC, GITNRDT VORGIOF GNAT SNE SAIC; BRL NEL
TNRDFNTS NAC GAOCELEC BAL BLRP TNE SDYZEMT, AS SRRO ABTELGALCS AWWEALEC
YH NEL SDCCEOUH EXMUAIPIOF, “I LEPEPYEL NEALIOF HRD ROME SAH, PL. CALMH,
TNAT HRD NALCUH EKEL BRLFAKE;--TNAT HRDL LESEOTPEOT, ROME MLEATEC, GAS
DOAWWEASAYUE. HRD ALE KELH MADTIRDS, I SDWWRSE, AS TR ITS _YEIOF
MLEATEC_?”

“I AP,” SAIC NE, GITN A BILP KRIME.

“AOC OEKEL AUURG HRDLSEUB TR YE YUIOCEC YH WLEZDCIME?”

“I NRWE ORT.”

“IT IS WALTIMDUALUH IOMDPYEOT RO TNRSE GNR OEKEL MNAOFE TNEIL RWIOIRO,
TR YE SEMDLE RB ZDCFIOF WLRWELUH AT BILST.”

“PAH I ASV TR GNAT TNESE QDESTIROS TEOC?”

“PELEUH TR TNE IUUDSTLATIRO RB _HRDL_ MNALAMTEL,” SAIC SNE, EOCEAKRDLIOF
TR SNAVE RBB NEL FLAKITH. “I AP TLHIOF TR PAVE IT RDT.”

“AOC GNAT IS HRDL SDMMESS?”

SNE SNRRV NEL NEAC. “I CR ORT FET RO AT AUU. I NEAL SDMN CIBBELEOT
AMMRDOTS RB HRD AS WDJJUE PE EXMEECIOFUH.”

“I MAO LEACIUH YEUIEKE,” AOSGELEC NE, FLAKEUH, “TNAT LEWRLTS PAH KALH
FLEATUH GITN LESWEMT TR PE; AOC I MRDUC GISN, PISS YEOOET, TNAT HRD GELE
ORT TR SVETMN PH MNALAMTEL AT TNE WLESEOT PRPEOT, AS TNELE IS LEASRO TR
BEAL TNAT TNE WELBRLPAOME GRDUC LEBUEMT OR MLECIT RO EITNEL.”

“YDT IB I CR ORT TAVE HRDL UIVEOESS ORG, I PAH OEKEL NAKE AORTNEL
RWWRLTDOITH.”

“I GRDUC YH OR PEAOS SDSWEOC AOH WUEASDLE RB HRDLS,” NE MRUCUH LEWUIEC.
SNE SAIC OR PRLE, AOC TNEH GEOT CRGO TNE RTNEL CAOME AOC WALTEC IO
SIUEOME; RO EAMN SICE CISSATISBIEC, TNRDFN ORT TR AO EQDAU CEFLEE; BRL
IO CALMH’S YLEAST TNELE GAS A TRUELAYUH WRGELBDU BEEUIOF TRGALCS NEL,
GNIMN SRRO WLRMDLEC NEL WALCRO, AOC CILEMTEC AUU NIS AOFEL AFAIOST
AORTNEL.

TNEH NAC ORT UROF SEWALATEC GNEO PISS YIOFUEH MAPE TRGALCS NEL, AOC,
GITN AO EXWLESSIRO RB MIKIU CISCAIO, TNDS AMMRSTEC NEL,--

“SR, PISS EUIJA, I NEAL HRD ALE QDITE CEUIFNTEC GITN FERLFE GIMVNAP?
HRDL SISTEL NAS YEEO TAUVIOF TR PE AYRDT NIP, AOC ASVIOF PE A TNRDSAOC
QDESTIROS; AOC I BIOC TNAT TNE HRDOF PAO BRLFRT TR TEUU HRD, APROF NIS
RTNEL MRPPDOIMATIROS, TNAT NE GAS TNE SRO RB RUC GIMVNAP, TNE UATE PL.
CALMH’S STEGALC. UET PE LEMRPPEOC HRD, NRGEKEL, AS A BLIEOC, ORT TR FIKE
IPWUIMIT MROBICEOME TR AUU NIS ASSELTIROS; BRL, AS TR PL. CALMH’S DSIOF
NIP IUU, IT IS WELBEMTUH BAUSE: BRL, RO TNE MROTLALH, NE NAS YEEO AUGAHS
LEPALVAYUH VIOC TR NIP, TNRDFN FERLFE GIMVNAP NAS TLEATEC PL. CALMH IO A
PRST IOBAPRDS PAOOEL. I CR ORT VORG TNE WALTIMDUALS, YDT I VORG KELH
GEUU TNAT PL. CALMH IS ORT IO TNE UEAST TR YUAPE; TNAT NE MAOORT YEAL
TR NEAL FERLFE GIMVNAP PEOTIROEC; AOC TNAT TNRDFN PH YLRTNEL TNRDFNT NE
MRDUC ORT GEUU AKRIC IOMUDCIOF NIP IO NIS IOKITATIRO TR TNE RBBIMELS, NE
GAS EXMESSIKEUH FUAC TR BIOC TNAT NE NAC TAVEO NIPSEUB RDT RB TNE GAH.
NIS MRPIOF IOTR TNE MRDOTLH AT AUU IS A PRST IOSRUEOT TNIOF, IOCEEC, AOC
I GROCEL NRG NE MRDUC WLESDPE TR CR IT. I WITH HRD, PISS EUIJA, BRL TNIS
CISMRKELH RB HRDL BAKRDLITE’S FDIUT; YDT LEAUUH, MROSICELIOF NIS
CESMEOT, ROE MRDUC ORT EXWEMT PDMN YETTEL.”

“NIS FDIUT AOC NIS CESMEOT AWWEAL, YH HRDL AMMRDOT, TR YE TNE SAPE,”
SAIC EUIJAYETN, AOFLIUH; “BRL I NAKE NEALC HRD AMMDSE NIP RB ORTNIOF
GRLSE TNAO RB YEIOF TNE SRO RB PL. CALMH’S STEGALC, AOC RB _TNAT_, I MAO
ASSDLE HRD, NE IOBRLPEC PE NIPSEUB.”

“I YEF HRDL WALCRO,” LEWUIEC PISS YIOFUEH, TDLOIOF AGAH GITN A SOEEL.
“EXMDSE PH IOTELBELEOME; IT GAS VIOCUH PEAOT.”

“IOSRUEOT FILU!” SAIC EUIJAYETN TR NELSEUB. “HRD ALE PDMN PISTAVEO IB
HRD EXWEMT TR IOBUDEOME PE YH SDMN A WAUTLH ATTAMV AS TNIS. I SEE
ORTNIOF IO IT YDT HRDL RGO GIUBDU IFORLAOME AOC TNE PAUIME RB PL.
CALMH.” SNE TNEO SRDFNT NEL EUCEST SISTEL, GNR NAC DOCELTAVEO TR PAVE
IOQDILIES RO TNE SAPE SDYZEMT RB YIOFUEH. ZAOE PET NEL GITN A SPIUE RB
SDMN SGEET MRPWUAMEOMH, A FURG RB SDMN NAWWH EXWLESSIRO, AS SDBBIMIEOTUH
PALVEC NRG GEUU SNE GAS SATISBIEC GITN TNE RMMDLLEOMES RB TNE EKEOIOF.
EUIJAYETN IOSTAOTUH LEAC NEL BEEUIOFS; AOC, AT TNAT PRPEOT, SRUIMITDCE
BRL GIMVNAP, LESEOTPEOT AFAIOST NIS EOEPIES, AOC EKELHTNIOF EUSE, FAKE
GAH YEBRLE TNE NRWE RB ZAOE’S YEIOF IO TNE BAILEST GAH BRL NAWWIOESS.

“I GAOT TR VORG,” SAIC SNE, GITN A MRDOTEOAOME OR UESS SPIUIOF TNAO NEL
SISTEL’S, “GNAT HRD NAKE UEALOT AYRDT PL. GIMVNAP. YDT WELNAWS HRD NAKE
YEEO TRR WUEASAOTUH EOFAFEC TR TNIOV RB AOH TNILC WELSRO, IO GNIMN MASE
HRD PAH YE SDLE RB PH WALCRO.”

“OR,” LEWUIEC ZAOE, “I NAKE ORT BRLFRTTEO NIP; YDT I NAKE ORTNIOF
SATISBAMTRLH TR TEUU HRD. PL. YIOFUEH CRES ORT VORG TNE GNRUE RB NIS
NISTRLH, AOC IS QDITE IFORLAOT RB TNE MILMDPSTAOMES GNIMN NAKE
WLIOMIWAUUH RBBEOCEC PL. CALMH; YDT NE GIUU KRDMN BRL TNE FRRC MROCDMT,
TNE WLRYITH AOC NRORDL, RB NIS BLIEOC, AOC IS WELBEMTUH MROKIOMEC TNAT
PL. GIMVNAP NAS CESELKEC PDMN UESS ATTEOTIRO BLRP PL. CALMH TNAO NE NAS
LEMEIKEC; AOC I AP SRLLH TR SAH TNAT YH NIS AMMRDOT, AS GEUU AS NIS
SISTEL’S, PL. GIMVNAP IS YH OR PEAOS A LESWEMTAYUE HRDOF PAO. I AP
ABLAIC NE NAS YEEO KELH IPWLDCEOT, AOC NAS CESELKEC TR URSE PL. CALMH’S
LEFALC.”

“PL. YIOFUEH CRES ORT VORG PL. GIMVNAP NIPSEUB.”

“OR; NE OEKEL SAG NIP TIUU TNE RTNEL PRLOIOF AT PELHTRO.”

“TNIS AMMRDOT TNEO IS GNAT NE NAS LEMEIKEC BLRP PL. CALMH. I AP
WELBEMTUH SATISBIEC. YDT GNAT CRES NE SAH RB TNE UIKIOF?”

“NE CRES ORT EXAMTUH LEMRUUEMT TNE MILMDPSTAOMES, TNRDFN NE NAS NEALC
TNEP BLRP PL. CALMH PRLE TNAO ROME, YDT NE YEUIEKES TNAT IT GAS UEBT TR
NIP _MROCITIROAUUH_ ROUH.”

“I NAKE ORT A CRDYT RB PL. YIOFUEH’S SIOMELITH,” SAIC EUIJAYETN GALPUH,
“YDT HRD PDST EXMDSE PH ORT YEIOF MROKIOMEC YH ASSDLAOMES ROUH. PL.
YIOFUEH’S CEBEOME RB NIS BLIEOC GAS A KELH AYUE ROE, I CALE SAH; YDT
SIOME NE IS DOAMQDAIOTEC GITN SEKELAU WALTS RB TNE STRLH, AOC NAS UEALOT
TNE LEST BLRP TNAT BLIEOC NIPSEUB, I SNAUU KEOTDLE STIUU TR TNIOV RB
YRTN FEOTUEPEO AS I CIC YEBRLE.”

SNE TNEO MNAOFEC TNE CISMRDLSE TR ROE PRLE FLATIBHIOF TR EAMN, AOC RO
GNIMN TNELE MRDUC YE OR CIBBELEOME RB SEOTIPEOT. EUIJAYETN UISTEOEC GITN
CEUIFNT TR TNE NAWWH TNRDFN PRCEST NRWES GNIMN ZAOE EOTELTAIOEC RB
YIOFUEH’S LEFALC, AOC SAIC AUU IO NEL WRGEL TR NEIFNTEO NEL MROBICEOME
IO IT. RO TNEIL YEIOF ZRIOEC YH PL. YIOFUEH NIPSEUB, EUIJAYETN GITNCLEG
TR PISS UDMAS; TR GNRSE IOQDILH ABTEL TNE WUEASAOTOESS RB NEL UAST
WALTOEL SNE NAC SMALMEUH LEWUIEC, YEBRLE PL. MRUUIOS MAPE DW TR TNEP,
AOC TRUC NEL GITN FLEAT EXDUTATIRO, TNAT NE NAC ZDST YEEO SR BRLTDOATE
AS TR PAVE A PRST IPWRLTAOT CISMRKELH.

“I NAKE BRDOC RDT,” SAIC NE, “YH A SIOFDUAL AMMICEOT, TNAT TNELE IS ORG
IO TNE LRRP A OEAL LEUATIRO TR PH WATLROESS. I NAWWEOEC TR RKELNEAL TNE
FEOTUEPAO NIPSEUB PEOTIROIOF TR TNE HRDOF UACH GNR CRES TNE NRORDLS RB
TNIS NRDSE TNE OAPES RB NIS MRDSIO PISS CE YRDLFN, AOC RB NEL PRTNEL,
UACH MATNELIOE. NRG GROCELBDUUH TNESE SRLT RB TNIOFS RMMDL! GNR GRDUC
NAKE TNRDFNT RB PH PEETIOF GITN--WELNAWS--A OEWNEG RB UACH MATNELIOE CE
YRDLFN IO TNIS ASSEPYUH! I AP PRST TNAOVBDU TNAT TNE CISMRKELH IS PACE
IO TIPE BRL PE TR WAH PH LESWEMTS TR NIP, GNIMN I AP ORG FRIOF TR CR,
AOC TLDST NE GIUU EXMDSE PH ORT NAKIOF CROE IT YEBRLE. PH TRTAU
IFORLAOME RB TNE MROOEMTIRO PDST WUEAC PH AWRURFH.”

“HRD ALE ORT FRIOF TR IOTLRCDME HRDLSEUB TR PL. CALMH?”

“IOCEEC I AP. I SNAUU EOTLEAT NIS WALCRO BRL ORT NAKIOF CROE IT EALUIEL.
I YEUIEKE NIP TR YE UACH MATNELIOE’S _OEWNEG_. IT GIUU YE IO PH WRGEL TR
ASSDLE NIP TNAT NEL UACHSNIW GAS QDITE GEUU HESTELCAH SE’OOIFNT.”

EUIJAYETN TLIEC NALC TR CISSDACE NIP BLRP SDMN A SMNEPE; ASSDLIOF NIP
TNAT PL. CALMH GRDUC MROSICEL NIS ACCLESSIOF NIP GITNRDT IOTLRCDMTIRO AS
AO IPWELTIOEOT BLEECRP, LATNEL TNAO A MRPWUIPEOT TR NIS ADOT; TNAT IT
GAS ORT IO TNE UEAST OEMESSALH TNELE SNRDUC YE AOH ORTIME RO EITNEL
SICE, AOC TNAT IB IT GELE, IT PDST YEUROF TR PL. CALMH, TNE SDWELIRL IO
MROSEQDEOME, TR YEFIO TNE AMQDAIOTAOME. PL. MRUUIOS UISTEOEC TR NEL GITN
TNE CETELPIOEC AIL RB BRUURGIOF NIS RGO IOMUIOATIRO, AOC GNEO SNE MEASEC
SWEAVIOF, LEWUIEC TNDS,--

“PH CEAL PISS EUIJAYETN, I NAKE TNE NIFNEST RWIOIRO IO TNE GRLUC RB HRDL
EXMEUUEOT ZDCFPEOT IO AUU PATTELS GITNIO TNE SMRWE RB HRDL
DOCELSTAOCIOF, YDT WELPIT PE TR SAH TNAT TNELE PDST YE A GICE CIBBELEOME
YETGEEO TNE ESTAYUISNEC BRLPS RB MELEPROH APROFST TNE UAITH AOC TNRSE
GNIMN LEFDUATE TNE MUELFH; BRL, FIKE PE UEAKE TR RYSELKE TNAT I MROSICEL
TNE MUELIMAU RBBIME AS EQDAU IO WRIOT RB CIFOITH GITN TNE NIFNEST LAOV
IO TNE VIOFCRP--WLRKICEC TNAT A WLRWEL NDPIUITH RB YENAKIRDL IS AT TNE
SAPE TIPE PAIOTAIOEC. HRD PDST, TNELEBRLE, AUURG PE TR BRUURG TNE
CIMTATES RB PH MROSMIEOME RO TNIS RMMASIRO, GNIMN UEAC PE TR WELBRLP
GNAT I URRV RO AS A WRIOT RB CDTH. WALCRO PE BRL OEFUEMTIOF TR WLRBIT YH
HRDL ACKIME, GNIMN RO EKELH RTNEL SDYZEMT SNAUU YE PH MROSTAOT FDICE,
TNRDFN IO TNE MASE YEBRLE DS I MROSICEL PHSEUB PRLE BITTEC YH ECDMATIRO
AOC NAYITDAU STDCH TR CEMICE RO GNAT IS LIFNT TNAO A HRDOF UACH UIVE
HRDLSEUB;” AOC GITN A URG YRG NE UEBT NEL TR ATTAMV PL. CALMH, GNRSE
LEMEWTIRO RB NIS ACKAOMES SNE EAFELUH GATMNEC, AOC GNRSE ASTROISNPEOT AT
YEIOF SR ACCLESSEC GAS KELH EKICEOT. NEL MRDSIO WLEBAMEC NIS SWEEMN GITN
A SRUEPO YRG, AOC TNRDFN SNE MRDUC ORT NEAL A GRLC RB IT, SNE BEUT AS IB
NEALIOF IT AUU, AOC SAG IO TNE PRTIRO RB NIS UIWS TNE GRLCS “AWRURFH,”
“NDOSBRLC,” AOC “UACH MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN.” IT KEXEC NEL TR SEE NIP
EXWRSE NIPSEUB TR SDMN A PAO. PL. CALMH GAS EHEIOF NIP GITN
DOLESTLAIOEC GROCEL; AOC GNEO AT UAST PL. MRUUIOS AUURGEC NIP TR SWEAV,
LEWUIEC GITN AO AIL RB CISTAOT MIKIUITH. PL. MRUUIOS, NRGEKEL, GAS ORT
CISMRDLAFEC BLRP SWEAVIOF AFAIO, AOC PL. CALMH’S MROTEPWT SEEPEC
AYDOCAOTUH IOMLEASIOF GITN TNE UEOFTN RB NIS SEMROC SWEEMN; AOC AT TNE
EOC RB IT NE ROUH PACE NIP A SUIFNT YRG, AOC PRKEC AORTNEL GAH: PL.
MRUUIOS TNEO LETDLOEC TR EUIJAYETN.

“I NAKE OR LEASRO, I ASSDLE HRD,” SAIC NE, “TR YE CISSATISBIEC GITN PH
LEMEWTIRO. PL. CALMH SEEPEC PDMN WUEASEC GITN TNE ATTEOTIRO. NE AOSGELEC
PE GITN TNE DTPRST MIKIUITH, AOC EKEO WAIC PE TNE MRPWUIPEOT RB SAHIOF,
TNAT NE GAS SR GEUU MROKIOMEC RB UACH MATNELIOE’S CISMELOPEOT AS TR YE
MELTAIO SNE MRDUC OEKEL YESTRG A BAKRDL DOGRLTNIUH. IT GAS LEAUUH A KELH
NAOCSRPE TNRDFNT. DWRO TNE GNRUE, I AP PDMN WUEASEC GITN NIP.”

AS EUIJAYETN NAC OR UROFEL AOH IOTELEST RB NEL RGO TR WDLSDE, SNE TDLOEC
NEL ATTEOTIRO AUPRST EOTILEUH RO NEL SISTEL AOC PL. YIOFUEH; AOC TNE
TLAIO RB AFLEEAYUE LEBUEMTIROS GNIMN NEL RYSELKATIROS FAKE YILTN TR PACE
NEL WELNAWS AUPRST AS NAWWH AS ZAOE. SNE SAG NEL IO ICEA SETTUEC IO TNAT
KELH NRDSE, IO AUU TNE BEUIMITH GNIMN A PALLIAFE RB TLDE ABBEMTIRO MRDUC
YESTRG; AOC SNE BEUT MAWAYUE, DOCEL SDMN MILMDPSTAOMES, RB EOCEAKRDLIOF
EKEO TR UIVE YIOFUEH’S TGR SISTELS. NEL PRTNEL’S TNRDFNTS SNE WUAIOUH
SAG GELE YEOT TNE SAPE GAH, AOC SNE CETELPIOEC ORT TR KEOTDLE OEAL NEL,
UEST SNE PIFNT NEAL TRR PDMN. GNEO TNEH SAT CRGO TR SDWWEL, TNELEBRLE,
SNE MROSICELEC IT A PRST DOUDMVH WELKELSEOESS GNIMN WUAMEC TNEP GITNIO
ROE RB EAMN RTNEL; AOC CEEWUH GAS SNE KEXEC TR BIOC TNAT NEL PRTNEL GAS
TAUVIOF TR TNAT ROE WELSRO (UACH UDMAS) BLEEUH, RWEOUH, AOC RB ORTNIOF
EUSE YDT RB NEL EXWEMTATIRO TNAT ZAOE GRDUC YE SRRO PALLIEC TR PL.
YIOFUEH. IT GAS AO AOIPATIOF SDYZEMT, AOC PLS. YEOOET SEEPEC IOMAWAYUE
RB BATIFDE GNIUE EODPELATIOF TNE ACKAOTAFES RB TNE PATMN. NIS YEIOF SDMN
A MNALPIOF HRDOF PAO, AOC SR LIMN, AOC UIKIOF YDT TNLEE PIUES BLRP TNEP,
GELE TNE BILST WRIOTS RB SEUB-FLATDUATIRO; AOC TNEO IT GAS SDMN A
MRPBRLT TR TNIOV NRG BROC TNE TGR SISTELS GELE RB ZAOE, AOC TR YE
MELTAIO TNAT TNEH PDST CESILE TNE MROOEMTIRO AS PDMN AS SNE MRDUC CR. IT
GAS, PRLERKEL, SDMN A WLRPISIOF TNIOF BRL NEL HRDOFEL CADFNTELS, AS
ZAOE’S PALLHIOF SR FLEATUH PDST TNLRG TNEP IO TNE GAH RB RTNEL LIMN PEO;
AOC, UASTUH, IT GAS SR WUEASAOT AT NEL TIPE RB UIBE TR YE AYUE TR
MROSIFO NEL SIOFUE CADFNTELS TR TNE MALE RB TNEIL SISTEL, TNAT SNE PIFNT
ORT YE RYUIFEC TR FR IOTR MRPWAOH PRLE TNAO SNE UIVEC. IT GAS OEMESSALH
TR PAVE TNIS MILMDPSTAOME A PATTEL RB WUEASDLE, YEMADSE RO SDMN
RMMASIROS IT IS TNE ETIQDETTE; YDT OR ROE GAS UESS UIVEUH TNAO PLS.
YEOOET TR BIOC MRPBRLT IO STAHIOF AT NRPE AT AOH WELIRC RB NEL UIBE. SNE
MROMUDCEC GITN PAOH FRRC GISNES TNAT UACH UDMAS PIFNT SRRO YE EQDAUUH
BRLTDOATE, TNRDFN EKICEOTUH AOC TLIDPWNAOTUH YEUIEKIOF TNELE GAS OR
MNAOME RB IT.

IO KAIO CIC EUIJAYETN EOCEAKRDL TR MNEMV TNE LAWICITH RB NEL PRTNEL’S
GRLCS, RL WELSDACE NEL TR CESMLIYE NEL BEUIMITH IO A UESS ADCIYUE
GNISWEL; BRL TR NEL IOEXWLESSIYUE KEXATIRO SNE MRDUC WELMEIKE TNAT TNE
MNIEB RB IT GAS RKELNEALC YH PL. CALMH, GNR SAT RWWRSITE TR TNEP. NEL
PRTNEL ROUH SMRUCEC NEL BRL YEIOF OROSEOSIMAU.

“GNAT IS PL. CALMH TR PE, WLAH, TNAT I SNRDUC YE ABLAIC RB NIP? I AP
SDLE GE RGE NIP OR SDMN WALTIMDUAL MIKIUITH AS TR YE RYUIFEC TR SAH
ORTNIOF _NE_ PAH ORT UIVE TR NEAL.”

“BRL NEAKEO’S SAVE, PACAP, SWEAV URGEL. GNAT ACKAOTAFE MAO IT YE TR HRD
TR RBBEOC PL. CALMH? HRD GIUU OEKEL LEMRPPEOC HRDLSEUB TR NIS BLIEOC YH
SR CRIOF.”

ORTNIOF TNAT SNE MRDUC SAH, NRGEKEL, NAC AOH IOBUDEOME. NEL PRTNEL GRDUC
TAUV RB NEL KIEGS IO TNE SAPE IOTEUUIFIYUE TROE. EUIJAYETN YUDSNEC AOC
YUDSNEC AFAIO GITN SNAPE AOC KEXATIRO. SNE MRDUC ORT NEUW BLEQDEOTUH
FUAOMIOF NEL EHE AT PL. CALMH, TNRDFN EKELH FUAOME MROKIOMEC NEL RB GNAT
SNE CLEACEC; BRL TNRDFN NE GAS ORT AUGAHS URRVIOF AT NEL PRTNEL, SNE GAS
MROKIOMEC TNAT NIS ATTEOTIRO GAS IOKALIAYUH BIXEC YH NEL. TNE EXWLESSIRO
RB NIS BAME MNAOFEC FLACDAUUH BLRP IOCIFOAOT MROTEPWT TR A MRPWRSEC AOC
STEACH FLAKITH.

AT UEOFTN, NRGEKEL, PLS. YEOOET NAC OR PRLE TR SAH; AOC UACH UDMAS, GNR
NAC YEEO UROF HAGOIOF AT TNE LEWETITIRO RB CEUIFNTS GNIMN SNE SAG OR
UIVEUINRRC RB SNALIOF, GAS UEBT TR TNE MRPBRLTS RB MRUC NAP AOC MNIMVEO.
EUIJAYETN ORG YEFAO TR LEKIKE. YDT ORT UROF GAS TNE IOTELKAU RB
TLAOQDIUUITH; BRL GNEO SDWWEL GAS RKEL, SIOFIOF GAS TAUVEC RB, AOC SNE
NAC TNE PRLTIBIMATIRO RB SEEIOF PALH, ABTEL KELH UITTUE EOTLEATH,
WLEWALIOF TR RYUIFE TNE MRPWAOH. YH PAOH SIFOIBIMAOT URRVS AOC SIUEOT
EOTLEATIES CIC SNE EOCEAKRDL TR WLEKEOT SDMN A WLRRB RB
MRPWUAISAOME,--YDT IO KAIO; PALH GRDUC ORT DOCELSTAOC TNEP; SDMN AO
RWWRLTDOITH RB EXNIYITIOF GAS CEUIFNTBDU TR NEL, AOC SNE YEFAO NEL SROF.
EUIJAYETN’S EHES GELE BIXEC RO NEL, GITN PRST WAIOBDU SEOSATIROS; AOC
SNE GATMNEC NEL WLRFLESS TNLRDFN TNE SEKELAU STAOJAS GITN AO IPWATIEOME
GNIMN GAS KELH IUU LEGALCEC AT TNEIL MURSE; BRL PALH, RO LEMEIKIOF
APROFST TNE TNAOVS RB TNE TAYUE TNE NIOT RB A NRWE TNAT SNE PIFNT YE
WLEKAIUEC RO TR BAKRDL TNEP AFAIO, ABTEL TNE WADSE RB NAUB A PIODTE
YEFAO AORTNEL. PALH’S WRGELS GELE YH OR PEAOS BITTEC BRL SDMN A CISWUAH;
NEL KRIME GAS GEAV, AOC NEL PAOOEL ABBEMTEC. EUIJAYETN GAS IO AFROIES.
SNE URRVEC AT ZAOE TR SEE NRG SNE YRLE IT; YDT ZAOE GAS KELH MRPWRSECUH
TAUVIOF TR YIOFUEH. SNE URRVEC AT NIS TGR SISTELS, AOC SAG TNEP PAVIOF
SIFOS RB CELISIRO AT EAMN RTNEL, AOC AT CALMH, GNR MROTIODEC, NRGEKEL,
IPWEOETLAYUH FLAKE. SNE URRVEC AT NEL BATNEL TR EOTLEAT NIS
IOTELBELEOME, UEST PALH SNRDUC YE SIOFIOF AUU OIFNT. NE TRRV TNE NIOT,
AOC, GNEO PALH NAC BIOISNEC NEL SEMROC SROF, SAIC AURDC,--

“TNAT GIUU CR EXTLEPEUH GEUU, MNIUC. HRD NAKE CEUIFNTEC DS UROF EORDFN.
UET TNE RTNEL HRDOF UACIES NAKE TIPE TR EXNIYIT.”

PALH, TNRDFN WLETEOCIOF ORT TR NEAL, GAS SRPEGNAT CISMROMELTEC; AOC
EUIJAYETN, SRLLH BRL NEL, AOC SRLLH BRL NEL BATNEL’S SWEEMN, GAS ABLAIC
NEL AOXIETH NAC CROE OR FRRC. RTNELS RB TNE WALTH GELE ORG AWWUIEC TR.

“IB I,” SAIC PL. MRUUIOS, “GELE SR BRLTDOATE AS TR YE AYUE TR SIOF, I
SNRDUC NAKE FLEAT WUEASDLE, I AP SDLE, IO RYUIFIOF TNE MRPWAOH GITN AO
AIL; BRL I MROSICEL PDSIM AS A KELH IOORMEOT CIKELSIRO, AOC WELBEMTUH
MRPWATIYUE GITN TNE WLRBESSIRO RB A MUELFHPAO. I CR ORT PEAO, NRGEKEL,
TR ASSELT TNAT GE MAO YE ZDSTIBIEC IO CEKRTIOF TRR PDMN RB RDL TIPE TR
PDSIM, BRL TNELE ALE MELTAIOUH RTNEL TNIOFS TR YE ATTEOCEC TR. TNE
LEMTRL RB A WALISN NAS PDMN TR CR. IO TNE BILST WUAME, NE PDST PAVE SDMN
AO AFLEEPEOT BRL TITNES AS PAH YE YEOEBIMIAU TR NIPSEUB AOC ORT
RBBEOSIKE TR NIS WATLRO. NE PDST GLITE NIS RGO SELPROS; AOC TNE TIPE
TNAT LEPAIOS GIUU ORT YE TRR PDMN BRL NIS WALISN CDTIES, AOC TNE MALE
AOC IPWLRKEPEOT RB NIS CGEUUIOF, GNIMN NE MAOORT YE EXMDSEC BLRP PAVIOF
AS MRPBRLTAYUE AS WRSSIYUE. AOC I CR ORT TNIOV IT RB UIFNT IPWRLTAOME
TNAT NE SNRDUC NAKE ATTEOTIKE AOC MROMIUIATRLH PAOOELS TRGALCS
EKELHYRCH, ESWEMIAUUH TRGALCS TNRSE TR GNRP NE RGES NIS WLEBELPEOT. I
MAOORT AMQDIT NIP RB TNAT CDTH; ORL MRDUC I TNIOV GEUU RB TNE PAO GNR
SNRDUC RPIT AO RMMASIRO RB TESTIBHIOF NIS LESWEMT TRGALCS AOHYRCH
MROOEMTEC GITN TNE BAPIUH.” AOC GITN A YRG TR PL. CALMH, NE MROMUDCEC
NIS SWEEMN, GNIMN NAC YEEO SWRVEO SR URDC AS TR YE NEALC YH NAUB TNE
LRRP. PAOH STALEC--PAOH SPIUEC; YDT OR ROE URRVEC PRLE APDSEC TNAO PL.
YEOOET NIPSEUB, GNIUE NIS GIBE SELIRDSUH MRPPEOCEC PL. MRUUIOS BRL
NAKIOF SWRVEO SR SEOSIYUH, AOC RYSELKEC, IO A NAUB-GNISWEL TR UACH
UDMAS, TNAT NE GAS A LEPALVAYUH MUEKEL, FRRC VIOC RB HRDOF PAO.

TR EUIJAYETN IT AWWEALEC, TNAT NAC NEL BAPIUH PACE AO AFLEEPEOT TR
EXWRSE TNEPSEUKES AS PDMN AS TNEH MRDUC CDLIOF TNE EKEOIOF, IT GRDUC
NAKE YEEO IPWRSSIYUE BRL TNEP TR WUAH TNEIL WALTS GITN PRLE SWILIT, RL
BIOEL SDMMESS; AOC NAWWH CIC SNE TNIOV IT BRL YIOFUEH AOC NEL SISTEL
TNAT SRPE RB TNE EXNIYITIRO NAC ESMAWEC NIS ORTIME, AOC TNAT NIS
BEEUIOFS GELE ORT RB A SRLT TR YE PDMN CISTLESSEC YH TNE BRUUH GNIMN NE
PDST NAKE GITOESSEC. TNAT NIS TGR SISTELS AOC PL. CALMH, NRGEKEL, SNRDUC
NAKE SDMN AO RWWRLTDOITH RB LICIMDUIOF NEL LEUATIROS GAS YAC EORDFN; AOC
SNE MRDUC ORT CETELPIOE GNETNEL TNE SIUEOT MROTEPWT RB TNE FEOTUEPAO, RL
TNE IOSRUEOT SPIUES RB TNE UACIES, GELE PRLE IOTRUELAYUE.

TNE LEST RB TNE EKEOIOF YLRDFNT NEL UITTUE APDSEPEOT. SNE GAS TEASEC YH
PL. MRUUIOS, GNR MROTIODEC PRST WELSEKELIOFUH YH NEL SICE; AOC TNRDFN NE
MRDUC ORT WLEKAIU GITN NEL TR CAOME GITN NIP AFAIO, WDT IT RDT RB NEL
WRGEL TR CAOME GITN RTNELS. IO KAIO CIC SNE EOTLEAT NIP TR STAOC DW GITN
SRPEYRCH EUSE, AOC RBBELEC TR IOTLRCDME NIP TR AOH HRDOF UACH IO TNE
LRRP. NE ASSDLEC NEL TNAT, AS TR CAOMIOF, NE GAS WELBEMTUH IOCIBBELEOT
TR IT; TNAT NIS MNIEB RYZEMT GAS, YH CEUIMATE ATTEOTIROS, TR LEMRPPEOC
NIPSEUB TR NEL; AOC TNAT NE SNRDUC TNELEBRLE PAVE A WRIOT RB LEPAIOIOF
MURSE TR NEL TNE GNRUE EKEOIOF. TNELE GAS OR ALFDIOF DWRO SDMN A
WLRZEMT. SNE RGEC NEL FLEATEST LEUIEB TR NEL BLIEOC PISS UDMAS, GNR
RBTEO ZRIOEC TNEP, AOC FRRC-OATDLECUH EOFAFEC PL. MRUUIOS’S MROKELSATIRO
TR NELSEUB.

SNE GAS AT UEAST BLEE BLRP TNE RBBEOME RB PL. CALMH’S BDLTNEL ORTIME:
TNRDFN RBTEO STAOCIOF GITNIO A KELH SNRLT CISTAOME RB NEL, QDITE
CISEOFAFEC, NE OEKEL MAPE OEAL EORDFN TR SWEAV. SNE BEUT IT TR YE TNE
WLRYAYUE MROSEQDEOME RB NEL AUUDSIROS TR PL. GIMVNAP, AOC LEZRIMEC IO
IT.

TNE UROFYRDLO WALTH GELE TNE UAST RB AUU TNE MRPWAOH TR CEWALT; AOC YH A
PAOIDKLE RB PLS. YEOOET NAC TR GAIT BRL TNEIL MALLIAFE A QDALTEL RB AO
NRDL ABTEL EKELHYRCH EUSE GAS FROE, GNIMN FAKE TNEP TIPE TR SEE NRG
NEALTIUH TNEH GELE GISNEC AGAH YH SRPE RB TNE BAPIUH. PLS. NDLST AOC NEL
SISTEL SMALMEUH RWEOEC TNEIL PRDTNS EXMEWT TR MRPWUAIO RB BATIFDE, AOC
GELE EKICEOTUH IPWATIEOT TR NAKE TNE NRDSE TR TNEPSEUKES. TNEH LEWDUSEC
EKELH ATTEPWT RB PLS. YEOOET AT MROKELSATIRO, AOC, YH SR CRIOF, TNLEG A
UAOFDRL RKEL TNE GNRUE WALTH, GNIMN GAS KELH UITTUE LEUIEKEC YH TNE UROF
SWEEMNES RB PL. MRUUIOS, GNR GAS MRPWUIPEOTIOF PL. YIOFUEH AOC NIS
SISTELS RO TNE EUEFAOME RB TNEIL EOTELTAIOPEOT, AOC TNE NRSWITAUITH AOC
WRUITEOESS GNIMN NAC PALVEC TNEIL YENAKIRDL TR TNEIL FDESTS. CALMH SAIC
ORTNIOF AT AUU. PL. YEOOET, IO EQDAU SIUEOME, GAS EOZRHIOF TNE SMEOE.
PL. YIOFUEH AOC ZAOE GELE STAOCIOF TRFETNEL A UITTUE CETAMNEC BLRP TNE
LEST, AOC TAUVEC ROUH TR EAMN RTNEL. EUIJAYETN WLESELKEC AS STEACH A
SIUEOME AS EITNEL PLS. NDLST RL PISS YIOFUEH; AOC EKEO UHCIA GAS TRR
PDMN BATIFDEC TR DTTEL PRLE TNAO TNE RMMASIROAU EXMUAPATIRO RB “URLC,
NRG TILEC I AP!” AMMRPWAOIEC YH A KIRUEOT HAGO.

GNEO AT UEOFTN TNEH ALRSE TR TAVE UEAKE, PLS. YEOOET GAS PRST WLESSIOFUH
MIKIU IO NEL NRWE RB SEEIOF TNE GNRUE BAPIUH SRRO AT UROFYRDLO; AOC
ACCLESSEC NELSEUB WALTIMDUALUH TR PL. YIOFUEH, TR ASSDLE NIP NRG NAWWH
NE GRDUC PAVE TNEP, YH EATIOF A BAPIUH CIOOEL GITN TNEP AT AOH TIPE,
GITNRDT TNE MELEPROH RB A BRLPAU IOKITATIRO. YIOFUEH GAS AUU FLATEBDU
WUEASDLE; AOC NE LEACIUH EOFAFEC BRL TAVIOF TNE EALUIEST RWWRLTDOITH RB
GAITIOF RO NEL ABTEL NIS LETDLO BLRP UROCRO, GNITNEL NE GAS RYUIFEC TR
FR TNE OEXT CAH BRL A SNRLT TIPE.

PLS. YEOOET GAS WELBEMTUH SATISBIEC; AOC QDITTEC TNE NRDSE DOCEL TNE
CEUIFNTBDU WELSDASIRO TNAT, AUURGIOF BRL TNE OEMESSALH WLEWALATIROS RB
SETTUEPEOTS, OEG MALLIAFES, AOC GECCIOF MURTNES, SNE SNRDUC DOCRDYTECUH
SEE NEL CADFNTEL SETTUEC AT OETNELBIEUC IO TNE MRDLSE RB TNLEE RL BRDL
PROTNS. RB NAKIOF AORTNEL CADFNTEL PALLIEC TR PL. MRUUIOS SNE TNRDFNT
GITN EQDAU MELTAIOTH, AOC GITN MROSICELAYUE, TNRDFN ORT EQDAU, WUEASDLE.
EUIJAYETN GAS TNE UEAST CEAL TR NEL RB AUU NEL MNIUCLEO; AOC TNRDFN TNE
PAO AOC TNE PATMN GELE QDITE FRRC EORDFN BRL _NEL_, TNE GRLTN RB EAMN
GAS EMUIWSEC YH PL. YIOFUEH AOC OETNELBIEUC.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “TR ASSDLE HRD IO TNE PRST AOIPATEC UAOFDAFE”
]




MNAWTEL XIX.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TNE OEXT CAH RWEOEC A OEG SMEOE AT UROFYRDLO. PL. MRUUIOS PACE NIS
CEMUALATIRO IO BRLP. NAKIOF LESRUKEC TR CR IT GITNRDT URSS RB TIPE, AS
NIS UEAKE RB AYSEOME EXTEOCEC ROUH TR TNE BRUURGIOF SATDLCAH, AOC NAKIOF
OR BEEUIOFS RB CIBBICEOME TR PAVE IT CISTLESSIOF TR NIPSEUB EKEO AT TNE
PRPEOT, NE SET AYRDT IT IO A KELH RLCELUH PAOOEL, GITN AUU TNE
RYSELKAOMES GNIMN NE SDWWRSEC A LEFDUAL WALT RB TNE YDSIOESS. RO BIOCIOF
PLS. YEOOET, EUIJAYETN, AOC ROE RB TNE HRDOFEL FILUS TRFETNEL, SRRO
ABTEL YLEAVBAST, NE ACCLESSEC TNE PRTNEL IO TNESE GRLCS,--

“PAH I NRWE, PACAP, BRL HRDL IOTELEST GITN HRDL BAIL CADFNTEL EUIJAYETN,
GNEO I SRUIMIT BRL TNE NRORDL RB A WLIKATE ADCIEOME GITN NEL IO TNE
MRDLSE RB TNIS PRLOIOF?”

YEBRLE EUIJAYETN NAC TIPE BRL AOHTNIOF YDT A YUDSN RB SDLWLISE, PLS.
YEOOET IOSTAOTUH AOSGELEC,--

“RN CEAL! HES, MELTAIOUH. I AP SDLE UIJJH GIUU YE KELH NAWWH--I AP SDLE
SNE MAO NAKE OR RYZEMTIRO. MRPE, VITTH, I GAOT HRD DWSTAILS.” AOC
FATNELIOF NEL GRLV TRFETNEL, SNE GAS NASTEOIOF AGAH, GNEO EUIJAYETN
MAUUEC RDT,--

“CEAL PA’AP, CR ORT FR. I YEF HRD GIUU ORT FR. PL. MRUUIOS PDST EXMDSE
PE. NE MAO NAKE ORTNIOF TR SAH TR PE TNAT AOHYRCH OEEC ORT NEAL. I AP
FRIOF AGAH PHSEUB.”

“OR, OR, OROSEOSE, UIJJH. I CESILE HRD GIUU STAH GNELE HRD ALE.” AOC
DWRO EUIJAYETN’S SEEPIOF LEAUUH, GITN KEXEC AOC EPYALLASSEC URRVS, AYRDT
TR ESMAWE, SNE ACCEC, “UIJJH, I _IOSIST_ DWRO HRDL STAHIOF AOC NEALIOF
PL. MRUUIOS.”

EUIJAYETN GRDUC ORT RWWRSE SDMN AO IOZDOMTIRO; AOC A PRPEOT’S
MROSICELATIRO PAVIOF NEL AUSR SEOSIYUE TNAT IT GRDUC YE GISEST TR FET IT
RKEL AS SRRO AOC AS QDIETUH AS WRSSIYUE, SNE SAT CRGO AFAIO, AOC TLIEC
TR MROMEAU, YH IOMESSAOT EPWURHPEOT, TNE BEEUIOFS GNIMN GELE CIKICEC
YETGEEO CISTLESS AOC CIKELSIRO. PLS. YEOOET AOC VITTH GAUVEC RBB, AOC AS
SRRO AS TNEH GELE FROE, PL. MRUUIOS YEFAO,--

“YEUIEKE PE, PH CEAL PISS EUIJAYETN, TNAT HRDL PRCESTH, SR BAL BLRP
CRIOF HRD AOH CISSELKIME, LATNEL ACCS TR HRDL RTNEL WELBEMTIROS. HRD
GRDUC NAKE YEEO UESS APIAYUE IO PH EHES NAC TNELE _ORT_ YEEO TNIS UITTUE
DOGIUUIOFOESS; YDT AUURG PE TR ASSDLE HRD TNAT I NAKE HRDL LESWEMTEC
PRTNEL’S WELPISSIRO BRL TNIS ACCLESS. HRD MAO NALCUH CRDYT TNE WDLWRLT
RB PH CISMRDLSE, NRGEKEL HRDL OATDLAU CEUIMAMH PAH UEAC HRD TR
CISSEPYUE; PH ATTEOTIROS NAKE YEEO TRR PALVEC TR YE PISTAVEO. AUPRST AS
SRRO AS I EOTELEC TNE NRDSE I SIOFUEC HRD RDT AS TNE MRPWAOIRO RB PH
BDTDLE UIBE. YDT YEBRLE I AP LDO AGAH GITN YH PH BEEUIOFS RO TNIS
SDYZEMT, WELNAWS IT GIUU YE ACKISAYUE BRL PE TR STATE PH LEASROS BRL
PALLHIOF--AOC, PRLERKEL, BRL MRPIOF IOTR NELTBRLCSNILE GITN TNE CESIFO
RB SEUEMTIOF A GIBE, AS I MELTAIOUH CIC.”

TNE ICEA RB PL. MRUUIOS, GITN AUU NIS SRUEPO MRPWRSDLE, YEIOF LDO AGAH
GITN YH NIS BEEUIOFS, PACE EUIJAYETN SR OEAL UADFNIOF TNAT SNE MRDUC ORT
DSE TNE SNRLT WADSE NE AUURGEC IO AOH ATTEPWT TR STRW NIP BALTNEL, AOC
NE MROTIODEC,--

“PH LEASROS BRL PALLHIOF ALE, BILST, TNAT I TNIOV IT A LIFNT TNIOF BRL
EKELH MUELFHPAO IO EASH MILMDPSTAOMES (UIVE PHSEUB) TR SET TNE EXAPWUE
RB PATLIPROH IO NIS WALISN; SEMROCUH, TNAT I AP MROKIOMEC IT GIUU ACC
KELH FLEATUH TR PH NAWWIOESS; AOC, TNILCUH, GNIMN WELNAWS I RDFNT TR
NAKE PEOTIROEC EALUIEL, TNAT IT IS TNE WALTIMDUAL ACKIME AOC
LEMRPPEOCATIRO RB TNE KELH ORYUE UACH GNRP I NAKE TNE NRORDL RB MAUUIOF
WATLROESS. TGIME NAS SNE MROCESMEOCEC TR FIKE PE NEL RWIOIRO (DOASVEC
TRR!) RO TNIS SDYZEMT; AOC IT GAS YDT TNE KELH SATDLCAH OIFNT YEBRLE I
UEBT NDOSBRLC,--YETGEEO RDL WRRUS AT QDACLIUUE, GNIUE PLS. ZEOVIOSRO GAS
ALLAOFIOF PISS CE YRDLFN’S BRRTSTRRU,--TNAT SNE SAIC, ‘PL. MRUUIOS, HRD
PDST PALLH. A MUELFHPAO UIVE HRD PDST PALLH. MNRRSE WLRWELUH, MNRRSE A
FEOTUEGRPAO BRL _PH_ SAVE, AOC BRL HRDL _RGO_; UET NEL YE AO AMTIKE,
DSEBDU SRLT RB WELSRO, ORT YLRDFNT DW NIFN, YDT AYUE TR PAVE A SPAUU
IOMRPE FR A FRRC GAH. TNIS IS PH ACKIME. BIOC SDMN A GRPAO AS SRRO AS
HRD MAO, YLIOF NEL TR NDOSBRLC, AOC I GIUU KISIT NEL.’ AUURG PE, YH TNE
GAH, TR RYSELKE, PH BAIL MRDSIO, TNAT I CR ORT LEMVRO TNE ORTIME AOC
VIOCOESS RB UACH MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN AS APROF TNE UEAST RB TNE
ACKAOTAFES IO PH WRGEL TR RBBEL. HRD GIUU BIOC NEL PAOOELS YEHROC
AOHTNIOF I MAO CESMLIYE; AOC HRDL GIT AOC KIKAMITH, I TNIOV, PDST YE
AMMEWTAYUE TR NEL, ESWEMIAUUH GNEO TEPWELEC GITN TNE SIUEOME AOC LESWEMT
GNIMN NEL LAOV GIUU IOEKITAYUH EXMITE. TNDS PDMN BRL PH FEOELAU
IOTEOTIRO IO BAKRDL RB PATLIPROH; IT LEPAIOS TR YE TRUC GNH PH KIEGS
GELE CILEMTEC TR UROFYRDLO IOSTEAC RB PH RGO OEIFNYRDLNRRC, GNELE I
ASSDLE HRD TNELE ALE PAOH APIAYUE HRDOF GRPEO. YDT TNE BAMT IS, TNAT
YEIOF, AS I AP, TR IONELIT TNIS ESTATE ABTEL TNE CEATN RB HRDL NRORDLEC
BATNEL (GNR, NRGEKEL, PAH UIKE PAOH HEALS UROFEL), I MRDUC ORT SATISBH
PHSEUB GITNRDT LESRUKIOF TR MNRRSE A GIBE BLRP APROF NIS CADFNTELS, TNAT
TNE URSS TR TNEP PIFNT YE AS UITTUE AS WRSSIYUE GNEO TNE PEUAOMNRUH
EKEOT TAVES WUAME--GNIMN, NRGEKEL, AS I NAKE AULEACH SAIC, PAH ORT YE
BRL SEKELAU HEALS. TNIS NAS YEEO PH PRTIKE, PH BAIL MRDSIO, AOC I
BUATTEL PHSEUB IT GIUU ORT SIOV PE IO HRDL ESTEEP. AOC ORG ORTNIOF
LEPAIOS BRL PE YDT TR ASSDLE HRD IO TNE PRST AOIPATEC UAOFDAFE RB TNE
KIRUEOME RB PH ABBEMTIRO. TR BRLTDOE I AP WELBEMTUH IOCIBBELEOT, AOC
SNAUU PAVE OR CEPAOC RB TNAT OATDLE RO HRDL BATNEL, SIOME I AP GEUU
AGALE TNAT IT MRDUC ORT YE MRPWUIEC GITN; AOC TNAT ROE TNRDSAOC WRDOCS
IO TNE 4 WEL MEOTS., GNIMN GIUU ORT YE HRDLS TIUU ABTEL HRDL PRTNEL’S
CEMEASE, IS AUU TNAT HRD PAH EKEL YE EOTITUEC TR. RO TNAT NEAC,
TNELEBRLE, I SNAUU YE DOIBRLPUH SIUEOT: AOC HRD PAH ASSDLE HRDLSEUB TNAT
OR DOFEOELRDS LEWLRAMN SNAUU EKEL WASS PH UIWS GNEO GE ALE PALLIEC.”

IT GAS AYSRUDTEUH OEMESSALH TR IOTELLDWT NIP ORG.

“HRD ALE TRR NASTH, SIL,” SNE MLIEC. “HRD BRLFET TNAT I NAKE PACE OR
AOSGEL. UET PE CR IT GITNRDT BDLTNEL URSS RB TIPE. AMMEWT PH TNAOVS BRL
TNE MRPWUIPEOT HRD ALE WAHIOF PE. I AP KELH SEOSIYUE RB TNE NRORDL RB
HRDL WLRWRSAUS, YDT IT IS IPWRSSIYUE BRL PE TR CR RTNELGISE TNAO CEMUIOE
TNEP.”

“I AP ORT ORG TR UEALO,” LEWUIEC PL. MRUUIOS, GITN A BRLPAU GAKE RB TNE
NAOC, “TNAT IT IS DSDAU GITN HRDOF UACIES TR LEZEMT TNE ACCLESSES RB TNE
PAO GNRP TNEH SEMLETUH PEAO TR AMMEWT, GNEO NE BILST AWWUIES BRL TNEIL
BAKRDL; AOC TNAT SRPETIPES TNE LEBDSAU IS LEWEATEC A SEMROC RL EKEO A
TNILC TIPE. I AP, TNELEBRLE, YH OR PEAOS CISMRDLAFEC YH GNAT HRD NAKE
ZDST SAIC, AOC SNAUU NRWE TR UEAC HRD TR TNE AUTAL ELE UROF.”

“DWRO PH GRLC, SIL,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, “HRDL NRWE IS LATNEL AO
EXTLARLCIOALH ROE ABTEL PH CEMUALATIRO. I CR ASSDLE HRD TNAT I AP ORT
ROE RB TNRSE HRDOF UACIES (IB SDMN HRDOF UACIES TNELE ALE) GNR ALE SR
CALIOF AS TR LISV TNEIL NAWWIOESS RO TNE MNAOME RB YEIOF ASVEC A SEMROC
TIPE. I AP WELBEMTUH SELIRDS IO PH LEBDSAU. HRD MRDUC ORT PAVE _PE_
NAWWH, AOC I AP MROKIOMEC TNAT I AP TNE UAST GRPAO IO TNE GRLUC GNR
GRDUC PAVE _HRD_ SR. OAH, GELE HRDL BLIEOC UACH MATNELIOE TR VORG PE, I
AP WELSDACEC SNE GRDUC BIOC PE IO EKELH LESWEMT IUU QDAUIBIEC BRL TNE
SITDATIRO.”

“GELE IT MELTAIO TNAT UACH MATNELIOE GRDUC TNIOV SR,” SAIC PL. MRUUIOS,
KELH FLAKEUH--“YDT I MAOORT IPAFIOE TNAT NEL UACHSNIW GRDUC AT AUU
CISAWWLRKE RB HRD. AOC HRD PAH YE MELTAIO TNAT GNEO I NAKE TNE NRORDL RB
SEEIOF NEL AFAIO I SNAUU SWEAV IO TNE NIFNEST TELPS RB HRDL PRCESTH,
EMRORPH, AOC RTNEL APIAYUE QDAUIBIMATIROS.”

“IOCEEC, PL. MRUUIOS, AUU WLAISE RB PE GIUU YE DOOEMESSALH. HRD PDST
FIKE PE UEAKE TR ZDCFE BRL PHSEUB, AOC WAH PE TNE MRPWUIPEOT RB
YEUIEKIOF GNAT I SAH. I GISN HRD KELH NAWWH AOC KELH LIMN, AOC YH
LEBDSIOF HRDL NAOC, CR AUU IO PH WRGEL TR WLEKEOT HRDL YEIOF RTNELGISE.
IO PAVIOF PE TNE RBBEL, HRD PDST NAKE SATISBIEC TNE CEUIMAMH RB HRDL
BEEUIOFS GITN LEFALC TR PH BAPIUH, AOC PAH TAVE WRSSESSIRO RB UROFYRDLO
ESTATE GNEOEKEL IT BAUUS, GITNRDT AOH SEUB-LEWLRAMN. TNIS PATTEL PAH YE
MROSICELEC, TNELEBRLE, AS BIOAUUH SETTUEC.” AOC LISIOF AS SNE TNDS
SWRVE, SNE GRDUC NAKE QDITTEC TNE LRRP, NAC ORT PL. MRUUIOS TNDS
ACCLESSEC NEL,--

“GNEO I CR PHSEUB TNE NRORDL RB SWEAVIOF TR HRD OEXT RO TNE SDYZEMT, I
SNAUU NRWE TR LEMEIKE A PRLE BAKRDLAYUE AOSGEL TNAO HRD NAKE ORG FIKEO
PE; TNRDFN I AP BAL BLRP AMMDSIOF HRD RB MLDEUTH AT WLESEOT, YEMADSE I
VORG IT TR YE TNE ESTAYUISNEC MDSTRP RB HRDL SEX TR LEZEMT A PAO RO TNE
BILST AWWUIMATIRO, AOC, WELNAWS, HRD NAKE EKEO ORG SAIC AS PDMN TR
EOMRDLAFE PH SDIT AS GRDUC YE MROSISTEOT GITN TNE TLDE CEUIMAMH RB TNE
BEPAUE MNALAMTEL.”

“LEAUUH, PL. MRUUIOS,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, GITN SRPE GALPTN, “HRD WDJJUE PE
EXMEECIOFUH. IB GNAT I NAKE NITNELTR SAIC MAO AWWEAL TR HRD IO TNE BRLP
RB EOMRDLAFEPEOT, I VORG ORT NRG TR EXWLESS PH LEBDSAU IO SDMN A GAH AS
PAH MROKIOME HRD RB ITS YEIOF ROE.”

“HRD PDST FIKE PE UEAKE TR BUATTEL PHSEUB, PH CEAL MRDSIO, TNAT HRDL
LEBDSAU RB PH ACCLESSES ALE PELEUH GRLCS RB MRDLSE. PH LEASROS BRL
YEUIEKIOF IT ALE YLIEBUH TNESE:--IT CRES ORT AWWEAL TR PE TNAT PH NAOC
IS DOGRLTNH HRDL AMMEWTAOME, RL TNAT TNE ESTAYUISNPEOT I MAO RBBEL GRDUC
YE AOH RTNEL TNAO NIFNUH CESILAYUE. PH SITDATIRO IO UIBE, PH MROOEMTIROS
GITN TNE BAPIUH RB CE YRDLFN, AOC PH LEUATIROSNIW TR HRDL RGO, ALE
MILMDPSTAOMES NIFNUH IO PH BAKRDL; AOC HRD SNRDUC TAVE IT IOTR BDLTNEL
MROSICELATIRO TNAT, IO SWITE RB HRDL PAOIBRUC ATTLAMTIROS, IT IS YH OR
PEAOS MELTAIO TNAT AORTNEL RBBEL RB PALLIAFE PAH EKEL YE PACE HRD. HRDL
WRLTIRO IS DONAWWIUH SR SPAUU, TNAT IT GIUU IO AUU UIVEUINRRC DOCR TNE
EBBEMTS RB HRDL URKEUIOESS AOC APIAYUE QDAUIBIMATIROS. AS I PDST,
TNELEBRLE, MROMUDCE TNAT HRD ALE ORT SELIRDS IO HRDL LEZEMTIRO RB PE, I
SNAUU MNRRSE TR ATTLIYDTE IT TR HRDL GISN RB IOMLEASIOF PH URKE YH
SDSWEOSE, AMMRLCIOF TR TNE DSDAU WLAMTIME RB EUEFAOT BEPAUES.”

“I CR ASSDLE HRD, SIL, TNAT I NAKE OR WLETEOSIROS GNATEKEL TR TNAT VIOC
RB EUEFAOME GNIMN MROSISTS IO TRLPEOTIOF A LESWEMTAYUE PAO. I GRDUC
LATNEL YE WAIC TNE MRPWUIPEOT RB YEIOF YEUIEKEC SIOMELE. I TNAOV HRD
AFAIO AOC AFAIO BRL TNE NRORDL HRD NAKE CROE PE IO HRDL WLRWRSAUS, YDT
TR AMMEWT TNEP IS AYSRUDTEUH IPWRSSIYUE. PH BEEUIOFS IO EKELH LESWEMT
BRLYIC IT. MAO I SWEAV WUAIOEL? CR ORT MROSICEL PE ORG AS AO EUEFAOT
BEPAUE IOTEOCIOF TR WUAFDE HRD, YDT AS A LATIROAU MLEATDLE SWEAVIOF TNE
TLDTN BLRP NEL NEALT.”

“HRD ALE DOIBRLPUH MNALPIOF!” MLIEC NE, GITN AO AIL RB AGVGALC
FAUUAOTLH; “AOC I AP WELSDACEC TNAT, GNEO SAOMTIROEC YH TNE EXWLESS
ADTNRLITH RB YRTN HRDL EXMEUUEOT WALEOTS, PH WLRWRSAUS GIUU ORT BAIU RB
YEIOF AMMEWTAYUE.”

TR SDMN WELSEKELAOME IO GIUBDU SEUB-CEMEWTIRO EUIJAYETN GRDUC PAVE OR
LEWUH, AOC IPPECIATEUH AOC IO SIUEOME GITNCLEG; CETELPIOEC, TNAT IB NE
WELSISTEC IO MROSICELIOF NEL LEWEATEC LEBDSAUS AS BUATTELIOF
EOMRDLAFEPEOT, TR AWWUH TR NEL BATNEL, GNRSE OEFATIKE PIFNT YE DTTELEC
IO SDMN A PAOOEL AS PDST YE CEMISIKE, AOC GNRSE YENAKIRDL AT UEAST MRDUC
ORT YE PISTAVEO BRL TNE ABBEMTATIRO AOC MRQDETLH RB AO EUEFAOT BEPAUE.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XX.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

PL. MRUUIOS GAS ORT UEBT UROF TR TNE SIUEOT MROTEPWUATIRO RB NIS
SDMMESSBDU URKE; BRL PLS. YEOOET, NAKIOF CAGCUEC AYRDT IO TNE KESTIYDUE
TR GATMN BRL TNE EOC RB TNE MROBELEOME, OR SRROEL SAG EUIJAYETN RWEO TNE
CRRL AOC GITN QDIMV STEW WASS NEL TRGALCS TNE STAILMASE, TNAO SNE
EOTELEC TNE YLEAVBAST-LRRP, AOC MROFLATDUATEC YRTN NIP AOC NELSEUB IO
GALP TELPS RO TNE NAWWH WLRSWEMT RB TNEIL OEALEL MROOEMTIRO. PL. MRUUIOS
LEMEIKEC AOC LETDLOEC TNESE BEUIMITATIROS GITN EQDAU WUEASDLE, AOC TNEO
WLRMEECEC TR LEUATE TNE WALTIMDUALS RB TNEIL IOTELKIEG, GITN TNE LESDUT
RB GNIMN NE TLDSTEC NE NAC EKELH LEASRO TR YE SATISBIEC, SIOME TNE
LEBDSAU GNIMN NIS MRDSIO NAC STEACBASTUH FIKEO NIP GRDUC OATDLAUUH BURG
BLRP NEL YASNBDU PRCESTH AOC TNE FEODIOE CEUIMAMH RB NEL MNALAMTEL.

TNIS IOBRLPATIRO, NRGEKEL, STALTUEC PLS. YEOOET: SNE GRDUC NAKE YEEO
FUAC TR YE EQDAUUH SATISBIEC TNAT NEL CADFNTEL NAC PEAOT TR EOMRDLAFE
NIP YH WLRTESTIOF AFAIOST NIS WLRWRSAUS, YDT SNE CALEC ORT YEUIEKE IT,
AOC MRDUC ORT NEUW SAHIOF SR.

“YDT CEWEOC DWRO IT, PL. MRUUIOS,” SNE ACCEC, “TNAT UIJJH SNAUU YE
YLRDFNT TR LEASRO. I GIUU SWEAV TR NEL AYRDT IT PHSEUB CILEMTUH. SNE IS
A KELH NEACSTLROF, BRRUISN FILU, AOC CRES ORT VORG NEL RGO IOTELEST; YDT
I GIUU _PAVE_ NEL VORG IT.”

“WALCRO PE BRL IOTELLDWTIOF HRD, PACAP,” MLIEC PL. MRUUIOS; “YDT IB SNE
IS LEAUUH NEACSTLROF AOC BRRUISN, I VORG ORT GNETNEL SNE GRDUC
AUTRFETNEL YE A KELH CESILAYUE GIBE TR A PAO IO PH SITDATIRO, GNR
OATDLAUUH URRVS BRL NAWWIOESS IO TNE PALLIAFE STATE. IB, TNELEBRLE, SNE
AMTDAUUH WELSISTS IO LEZEMTIOF PH SDIT, WELNAWS IT GELE YETTEL ORT TR
BRLME NEL IOTR AMMEWTIOF PE, YEMADSE, IB UIAYUE TR SDMN CEBEMTS RB
TEPWEL, SNE MRDUC ORT MROTLIYDTE PDMN TR PH BEUIMITH.”

“SIL, HRD QDITE PISDOCELSTAOC PE,” SAIC PLS. YEOOET, AUALPEC. “UIJJH IS
ROUH NEACSTLROF IO SDMN PATTELS AS TNESE. IO EKELHTNIOF EUSE SNE IS AS
FRRC-OATDLEC A FILU AS EKEL UIKEC. I GIUU FR CILEMTUH TR PL. YEOOET, AOC
GE SNAUU KELH SRRO SETTUE IT GITN NEL, I AP SDLE.”

SNE GRDUC ORT FIKE NIP TIPE TR LEWUH, YDT NDLLHIOF IOSTAOTUH TR NEL
NDSYAOC, MAUUEC RDT, AS SNE EOTELEC TNE UIYLALH,--

“RN, PL. YEOOET, HRD ALE GAOTEC IPPECIATEUH; GE ALE AUU IO AO DWLRAL.
HRD PDST MRPE AOC PAVE UIJJH PALLH PL. MRUUIOS, BRL SNE KRGS SNE GIUU
ORT NAKE NIP; AOC IB HRD CR ORT PAVE NASTE NE GIUU MNAOFE NIS PIOC AOC
ORT NAKE _NEL_.”

PL. YEOOET LAISEC NIS EHES BLRP NIS YRRV AS SNE EOTELEC, AOC BIXEC TNEP
RO NEL BAME GITN A MAUP DOMROMELO, GNIMN GAS ORT IO TNE UEAST AUTELEC YH
NEL MRPPDOIMATIRO.

“I NAKE ORT TNE WUEASDLE RB DOCELSTAOCIOF HRD,” SAIC NE, GNEO SNE NAC
BIOISNEC NEL SWEEMN. “RB GNAT ALE HRD TAUVIOF?”

“RB PL. MRUUIOS AOC UIJJH. UIJJH CEMUALES SNE GIUU ORT NAKE PL. MRUUIOS,
AOC PL. MRUUIOS YEFIOS TR SAH TNAT NE GIUU ORT NAKE UIJJH.”

“AOC GNAT AP I TR CR RO TNE RMMASIRO? IT SEEPS A NRWEUESS YDSIOESS.”

“SWEAV TR UIJJH AYRDT IT HRDLSEUB. TEUU NEL TNAT HRD IOSIST DWRO NEL
PALLHIOF NIP.”

“UET NEL YE MAUUEC CRGO. SNE SNAUU NEAL PH RWIOIRO.”

PLS. YEOOET LAOF TNE YEUU, AOC PISS EUIJAYETN GAS SDPPROEC TR TNE
UIYLALH.

“MRPE NELE, MNIUC,” MLIEC NEL BATNEL AS SNE AWWEALEC. “I NAKE SEOT BRL
HRD RO AO ABBAIL RB IPWRLTAOME. I DOCELSTAOC TNAT PL. MRUUIOS NAS PACE
HRD AO RBBEL RB PALLIAFE. IS IT TLDE?”

EUIJAYETN LEWUIEC TNAT IT GAS.

“KELH GEUU--AOC TNIS RBBEL RB PALLIAFE HRD NAKE LEBDSEC?”

“I NAKE, SIL.”

“KELH GEUU. GE ORG MRPE TR TNE WRIOT. HRDL PRTNEL IOSISTS DWRO HRDL
AMMEWTIOF IT. IS IT ORT SR, PLS. YEOOET?”

“HES, RL I GIUU OEKEL SEE NEL AFAIO.”

“AO DONAWWH AUTELOATIKE IS YEBRLE HRD, EUIJAYETN. BLRP TNIS CAH HRD PDST
YE A STLAOFEL TR ROE RB HRDL WALEOTS. HRDL PRTNEL GIUU OEKEL SEE HRD
AFAIO IB HRD CR _ORT_ PALLH PL. MRUUIOS, AOC I GIUU OEKEL SEE HRD AFAIO
IB HRD _CR_.”

EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT YDT SPIUE AT SDMN A MROMUDSIRO RB SDMN A YEFIOOIOF;
YDT PLS. YEOOET, GNR NAC WELSDACEC NELSEUB TNAT NEL NDSYAOC LEFALCEC TNE
ABBAIL AS SNE GISNEC, GAS EXMESSIKEUH CISAWWRIOTEC.

“GNAT CR HRD PEAO, PL. YEOOET, YH TAUVIOF IO TNIS GAH? HRD WLRPISEC PE
TR _IOSIST_ DWRO NEL PALLHIOF NIP.”

“PH CEAL,” LEWUIEC NEL NDSYAOC, “I NAKE TGR SPAUU BAKRDLS TR LEQDEST.
BILST, TNAT HRD GIUU AUURG PE TNE BLEE DSE RB PH DOCELSTAOCIOF RO TNE
WLESEOT RMMASIRO; AOC, SEMROCUH, RB PH LRRP. I SNAUU YE FUAC TR NAKE TNE
UIYLALH TR PHSEUB AS SRRO AS PAH YE.”

ORT HET, NRGEKEL, IO SWITE RB NEL CISAWWRIOTPEOT IO NEL NDSYAOC, CIC
PLS. YEOOET FIKE DW TNE WRIOT. SNE TAUVEC TR EUIJAYETN AFAIO AOC AFAIO;
MRAXEC AOC TNLEATEOEC NEL YH TDLOS. SNE EOCEAKRDLEC TR SEMDLE ZAOE IO
NEL IOTELEST, YDT ZAOE, GITN AUU WRSSIYUE PIUCOESS, CEMUIOEC
IOTELBELIOF; AOC EUIJAYETN, SRPETIPES GITN LEAU EALOESTOESS, AOC
SRPETIPES GITN WUAHBDU FAIETH, LEWUIEC TR NEL ATTAMVS. TNRDFN NEL PAOOEL
KALIEC, NRGEKEL, NEL CETELPIOATIRO OEKEL CIC.

PL. MRUUIOS, PEAOGNIUE, GAS PECITATIOF IO SRUITDCE RO GNAT NAC WASSEC.
NE TNRDFNT TRR GEUU RB NIPSEUB TR MRPWLENEOC RO GNAT PRTIKE NIS MRDSIO
MRDUC LEBDSE NIP; AOC TNRDFN NIS WLICE GAS NDLT, NE SDBBELEC IO OR RTNEL
GAH. NIS LEFALC BRL NEL GAS QDITE IPAFIOALH; AOC TNE WRSSIYIUITH RB NEL
CESELKIOF NEL PRTNEL’S LEWLRAMN WLEKEOTEC NIS BEEUIOF AOH LEFLET.

GNIUE TNE BAPIUH GELE IO TNIS MROBDSIRO, MNALURTTE UDMAS MAPE TR SWEOC
TNE CAH GITN TNEP. SNE GAS PET IO TNE KESTIYDUE YH UHCIA, GNR, BUHIOF TR
NEL, MLIEC IO A NAUB GNISWEL, “I AP FUAC HRD ALE MRPE, BRL TNELE IS SDMN
BDO NELE! GNAT CR HRD TNIOV NAS NAWWEOEC TNIS PRLOIOF? PL. MRUUIOS NAS
PACE AO RBBEL TR UIJJH, AOC SNE GIUU ORT NAKE NIP.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “TNEH EOTELEC TNE YLEAVBAST LRRP”
]

MNALURTTE NAC NALCUH TIPE TR AOSGEL YEBRLE TNEH GELE ZRIOEC YH VITTH,
GNR MAPE TR TEUU TNE SAPE OEGS; AOC OR SRROEL NAC TNEH EOTELEC TNE
YLEAVBAST-LRRP, GNELE PLS. YEOOET GAS AUROE, TNAO SNE UIVEGISE YEFAO RO
TNE SDYZEMT, MAUUIOF RO PISS UDMAS BRL NEL MRPWASSIRO, AOC EOTLEATIOF
NEL TR WELSDACE NEL BLIEOC UIJJH TR MRPWUH GITN TNE GISNES RB NEL
BAPIUH. “WLAH CR, PH CEAL PISS UDMAS,” SNE ACCEC, IO A PEUAOMNRUH TROE;
“BRL ORYRCH IS RO PH SICE, ORYRCH TAVES WALT GITN PE; I AP MLDEUUH DSEC,
ORYRCH BEEUS BRL PH WRRL OELKES.”

MNALURTTE’S LEWUH GAS SWALEC YH TNE EOTLAOME RB ZAOE AOC EUIJAYETN.

“AH, TNELE SNE MRPES,” MROTIODEC PLS. YEOOET, “URRVIOF AS DOMROMELOEC AS
PAH YE, AOC MALIOF OR PRLE BRL DS TNAO IB GE GELE AT HRLV, WLRKICEC SNE
MAO NAKE NEL RGO GAH. YDT I TEUU HRD GNAT, PISS UIJJH, IB HRD TAVE IT
IOTR HRDL NEAC TR FR RO LEBDSIOF EKELH RBBEL RB PALLIAFE IO TNIS GAH,
HRD GIUU OEKEL FET A NDSYAOC AT AUU--AOC I AP SDLE I CR ORT VORG GNR IS
TR PAIOTAIO HRD GNEO HRDL BATNEL IS CEAC. _I_ SNAUU ORT YE AYUE TR VEEW
HRD--AOC SR I GALO HRD. I NAKE CROE GITN HRD BLRP TNIS KELH CAH. I TRUC
HRD IO TNE UIYLALH, HRD VORG, TNAT I SNRDUC OEKEL SWEAV TR HRD AFAIO,
AOC HRD GIUU BIOC PE AS FRRC AS PH GRLC. I NAKE OR WUEASDLE IO TAUVIOF
TR DOCDTIBDU MNIUCLEO. ORT TNAT I NAKE PDMN WUEASDLE, IOCEEC, IO TAUVIOF
TR AOHYRCH. WERWUE GNR SDBBEL AS I CR BLRP OELKRDS MRPWUAIOTS MAO NAKE
OR FLEAT IOMUIOATIRO BRL TAUVIOF. ORYRCH MAO TEUU GNAT I SDBBEL! YDT IT
IS AUGAHS SR. TNRSE GNR CR ORT MRPWUAIO ALE OEKEL WITIEC.”

NEL CADFNTELS UISTEOEC IO SIUEOME TR TNIS EBBDSIRO, SEOSIYUE TNAT AOH
ATTEPWT TR LEASRO GITN RL SRRTNE NEL GRDUC ROUH IOMLEASE TNE ILLITATIRO.
SNE TAUVEC RO, TNELEBRLE, GITNRDT IOTELLDWTIRO BLRP AOH RB TNEP TIUU
TNEH GELE ZRIOEC YH PL. MRUUIOS, GNR EOTELEC GITN AO AIL PRLE STATEUH
TNAO DSDAU, AOC RO WELMEIKIOF GNRP, SNE SAIC TR TNE FILUS,--

“ORG, I CR IOSIST DWRO IT, TNAT HRD, AUU RB HRD, NRUC HRDL TROFDES, AOC
UET PL. MRUUIOS AOC PE NAKE A UITTUE MROKELSATIRO TRFETNEL.”

EUIJAYETN WASSEC QDIETUH RDT RB TNE LRRP, ZAOE AOC VITTH BRUURGEC, YDT
UHCIA STRRC NEL FLRDOC, CETELPIOEC TR NEAL AUU SNE MRDUC; AOC MNALURTTE,
CETAIOEC BILST YH TNE MIKIUITH RB PL. MRUUIOS, GNRSE IOQDILIES ABTEL
NELSEUB AOC AUU NEL BAPIUH GELE KELH PIODTE, AOC TNEO YH A UITTUE
MDLIRSITH, SATISBIEC NELSEUB GITN GAUVIOF TR TNE GIOCRG AOC WLETEOCIOF
ORT TR NEAL. IO A CRUEBDU KRIME PLS. YEOOET TNDS YEFAO TNE WLRZEMTEC
MROKELSATIRO:--

“RN, PL. MRUUIOS!”

“PH CEAL PACAP,” LEWUIEC NE, “UET DS YE BRL EKEL SIUEOT RO TNIS WRIOT.
BAL YE IT BLRP PE,” NE WLESEOTUH MROTIODEC, IO A KRIME TNAT PALVEC NIS
CISWUEASDLE, “TR LESEOT TNE YENAKIRDL RB HRDL CADFNTEL. LESIFOATIRO TR
IOEKITAYUE EKIUS IS TNE CDTH RB DS AUU: TNE WEMDUIAL CDTH RB A HRDOF PAO
GNR NAS YEEO SR BRLTDOATE AS I NAKE YEEO, IO EALUH WLEBELPEOT; AOC, I
TLDST, I AP LESIFOEC. WELNAWS ORT TNE UESS SR BLRP BEEUIOF A CRDYT RB PH
WRSITIKE NAWWIOESS NAC PH BAIL MRDSIO NRORDLEC PE GITN NEL NAOC; BRL I
NAKE RBTEO RYSELKEC, TNAT LESIFOATIRO IS OEKEL SR WELBEMT AS GNEO TNE
YUESSIOF CEOIEC YEFIOS TR URSE SRPEGNAT RB ITS KAUDE IO RDL ESTIPATIRO.
HRD GIUU ORT, I NRWE, MROSICEL PE AS SNRGIOF AOH CISLESWEMT TR HRDL
BAPIUH, PH CEAL PACAP, YH TNDS GITNCLAGIOF PH WLETEOSIROS TR HRDL
CADFNTEL’S BAKRDL, GITNRDT NAKIOF WAIC HRDLSEUB AOC PL. YEOOET TNE
MRPWUIPEOT RB LEQDESTIOF HRD TR IOTELWRSE HRDL ADTNRLITH IO PH YENAUB.
PH MROCDMT PAH, I BEAL, YE RYZEMTIROAYUE IO NAKIOF AMMEWTEC PH
CISPISSIRO BLRP HRDL CADFNTEL’S UIWS IOSTEAC RB HRDL RGO; YDT GE ALE AUU
UIAYUE TR ELLRL. I NAKE MELTAIOUH PEAOT GEUU TNLRDFN TNE GNRUE ABBAIL.
PH RYZEMT NAS YEEO TR SEMDLE AO APIAYUE MRPWAOIRO BRL PHSEUB, GITN CDE
MROSICELATIRO BRL TNE ACKAOTAFE RB AUU HRDL BAPIUH; AOC IB PH _PAOOEL_
NAS YEEO AT AUU LEWLENEOSIYUE, I NELE YEF UEAKE TR AWRURFIJE.”




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XXI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TNE CISMDSSIRO RB PL. MRUUIOS’S RBBEL GAS ORG OEALUH AT AO EOC, AOC
EUIJAYETN NAC ROUH TR SDBBEL BLRP TNE DOMRPBRLTAYUE BEEUIOFS OEMESSALIUH
ATTEOCIOF IT, AOC RMMASIROAUUH BLRP SRPE WEEKISN AUUDSIRO RB NEL PRTNEL.
AS BRL TNE FEOTUEPAO NIPSEUB, _NIS_ BEEUIOFS GELE MNIEBUH EXWLESSEC, ORT
YH EPYALLASSPEOT RL CEZEMTIRO, RL YH TLHIOF TR AKRIC NEL, YDT YH
STIBBOESS RB PAOOEL AOC LESEOTBDU SIUEOME. NE SMALMEUH EKEL SWRVE TR
NEL; AOC TNE ASSICDRDS ATTEOTIROS GNIMN NE NAC YEEO SR SEOSIYUE RB
NIPSEUB GELE TLAOSBELLEC BRL TNE LEST RB TNE CAH TR PISS UDMAS, GNRSE
MIKIUITH IO UISTEOIOF TR NIP GAS A SEASROAYUE LEUIEB TR TNEP AUU, AOC
ESWEMIAUUH TR NEL BLIEOC.

TNE PRLLRG WLRCDMEC OR AYATEPEOT RB PLS. YEOOET’S IUU NDPRDL RL IUU
NEAUTN. PL. MRUUIOS GAS AUSR IO TNE SAPE STATE RB AOFLH WLICE. EUIJAYETN
NAC NRWEC TNAT NIS LESEOTPEOT PIFNT SNRLTEO NIS KISIT, YDT NIS WUAO CIC
ORT AWWEAL IO TNE UEAST ABBEMTEC YH IT. NE GAS AUGAHS TR NAKE FROE RO
SATDLCAH, AOC TR SATDLCAH NE STIUU PEAOT TR STAH.

ABTEL YLEAVBAST, TNE FILUS GAUVEC TR PELHTRO, TR IOQDILE IB PL. GIMVNAP
GELE LETDLOEC, AOC TR UAPEOT RKEL NIS AYSEOME BLRP TNE OETNELBIEUC YAUU.
NE ZRIOEC TNEP RO TNEIL EOTELIOF TNE TRGO, AOC ATTEOCEC TNEP TR TNEIL
ADOT’S, GNELE NIS LEFLET AOC KEXATIRO AOC TNE MROMELO RB EKELHYRCH GELE
GEUU TAUVEC RKEL. TR EUIJAYETN, NRGEKEL, NE KRUDOTALIUH AMVORGUECFEC
TNAT TNE OEMESSITH RB NIS AYSEOME _NAC_ YEEO SEUB-IPWRSEC.

“I BRDOC,” SAIC NE, “AS TNE TIPE CLEG OEAL, TNAT I NAC YETTEL ORT PEET
PL. CALMH;--TNAT TR YE IO TNE SAPE LRRP, TNE SAPE WALTH GITN NIP BRL SR
PAOH NRDLS TRFETNEL, PIFNT YE PRLE TNAO I MRDUC YEAL, AOC TNAT SMEOES
PIFNT ALISE DOWUEASAOT TR PRLE TNAO PHSEUB.”

SNE NIFNUH AWWLRKEC NIS BRLYEALAOME; AOC TNEH NAC UEISDLE BRL A BDUU
CISMDSSIRO RB IT, AOC BRL AUU TNE MRPPEOCATIROS GNIMN TNEH MIKIUUH
YESTRGEC RO EAMN RTNEL, AS GIMVNAP AOC AORTNEL RBBIMEL GAUVEC YAMV GITN
TNEP TR UROFYRDLO, AOC CDLIOF TNE GAUV NE WALTIMDUALUH ATTEOCEC TR NEL.
NIS AMMRPWAOHIOF TNEP GAS A CRDYUE ACKAOTAFE: SNE BEUT AUU TNE
MRPWUIPEOT IT RBBELEC TR NELSEUB; AOC IT GAS PRST AMMEWTAYUE AS AO
RMMASIRO RB IOTLRCDMIOF NIP TR NEL BATNEL AOC PRTNEL.

[IUUDSTLATIRO: “GAUVEC YAMV GITN TNEP”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

SRRO ABTEL TNEIL LETDLO, A UETTEL GAS CEUIKELEC TR PISS YEOOET; IT MAPE
BLRP OETNELBIEUC, AOC GAS RWEOEC IPPECIATEUH. TNE EOKEURWE MROTAIOEC A
SNEET RB EUEFAOT, UITTUE, NRT-WLESSEC WAWEL, GEUU MRKELEC GITN A UACH’S
BAIL, BURGIOF NAOC; AOC EUIJAYETN SAG NEL SISTEL’S MRDOTEOAOME MNAOFE AS
SNE LEAC IT, AOC SAG NEL CGEUUIOF IOTEOTUH RO SRPE WALTIMDUAL WASSAFES.
ZAOE LEMRUUEMTEC NELSEUB SRRO; AOC WDTTIOF TNE UETTEL AGAH, TLIEC TR
ZRIO, GITN NEL DSDAU MNEELBDUOESS, IO TNE FEOELAU MROKELSATIRO: YDT
EUIJAYETN BEUT AO AOXIETH RO TNE SDYZEMT GNIMN CLEG RBB NEL ATTEOTIRO
EKEO BLRP GIMVNAP; AOC OR SRROEL NAC NE AOC NIS MRPWAOIRO TAVEO UEAKE,
TNAO A FUAOME BLRP ZAOE IOKITEC NEL TR BRUURG NEL DWSTAILS. GNEO TNEH
NAC FAIOEC TNEIL RGO LRRP, ZAOE, TAVIOF RDT NEL UETTEL, SAIC, “TNIS IS
BLRP MALRUIOE YIOFUEH: GNAT IT MROTAIOS NAS SDLWLISEC PE A FRRC CEAU.
TNE GNRUE WALTH NAKE UEBT OETNELBIEUC YH TNIS TIPE, AOC ALE RO TNEIL GAH
TR TRGO; AOC GITNRDT AOH IOTEOTIRO RB MRPIOF YAMV AFAIO. HRD SNAUU NEAL
GNAT SNE SAHS.”

SNE TNEO LEAC TNE BILST SEOTEOME AURDC, GNIMN MRPWLISEC TNE IOBRLPATIRO
RB TNEIL NAKIOF ZDST LESRUKEC TR BRUURG TNEIL YLRTNEL TR TRGO CILEMTUH,
AOC RB TNEIL PEAOIOF TR CIOE TNAT CAH IO FLRSKEORL STLEET, GNELE PL.
NDLST NAC A NRDSE. TNE OEXT GAS IO TNESE GRLCS:--“‘I CR ORT WLETEOC TR
LEFLET AOHTNIOF I SNAUU UEAKE IO NELTBRLCSNILE EXMEWT HRDL SRMIETH, PH
CEALEST BLIEOC; YDT GE GIUU NRWE, AT SRPE BDTDLE WELIRC, TR EOZRH PAOH
LETDLOS RB TNAT CEUIFNTBDU IOTELMRDLSE GE NAKE VORGO, AOC IO TNE
PEAOGNIUE PAH UESSEO TNE WAIO RB SEWALATIRO YH A KELH BLEQDEOT AOC PRST
DOLESELKEC MRLLESWROCEOME. I CEWEOC RO HRD BRL TNAT.’” TR TNESE
NIFN-BURGO EXWLESSIROS EUIJAYETN UISTEOEC GITN AUU TNE IOSEOSIYIUITH RB
CISTLDST; AOC TNRDFN TNE SDCCEOOESS RB TNEIL LEPRKAU SDLWLISEC NEL, SNE
SAG ORTNIOF IO IT LEAUUH TR UAPEOT: IT GAS ORT TR YE SDWWRSEC TNAT TNEIL
AYSEOME BLRP OETNELBIEUC GRDUC WLEKEOT PL. YIOFUEH’S YEIOF TNELE; AOC AS
TR TNE URSS RB TNEIL SRMIETH, SNE GAS WELSDACEC TNAT ZAOE PDST SRRO
MEASE TR LEFALC IT IO TNE EOZRHPEOT RB NIS.

“IT IS DOUDMVH,” SAIC SNE, ABTEL A SNRLT WADSE, “TNAT HRD SNRDUC ORT YE
AYUE TR SEE HRDL BLIEOCS YEBRLE TNEH UEAKE TNE MRDOTLH. YDT PAH GE ORT
NRWE TNAT TNE WELIRC RB BDTDLE NAWWIOESS, TR GNIMN PISS YIOFUEH URRVS
BRLGALC, PAH ALLIKE EALUIEL TNAO SNE IS AGALE, AOC TNAT TNE CEUIFNTBDU
IOTELMRDLSE HRD NAKE VORGO AS BLIEOCS GIUU YE LEOEGEC GITN HET FLEATEL
SATISBAMTIRO AS SISTELS? PL. YIOFUEH GIUU ORT YE CETAIOEC IO UROCRO YH
TNEP.”

“MALRUIOE CEMICECUH SAHS TNAT OROE RB TNE WALTH GIUU LETDLO IOTR
NELTBRLCSNILE TNIS GIOTEL. I GIUU LEAC IT TR HRD.

“‘GNEO PH YLRTNEL UEBT DS HESTELCAH, NE IPAFIOEC TNAT TNE YDSIOESS GNIMN
TRRV NIP TR UROCRO PIFNT YE MROMUDCEC IO TNLEE RL BRDL CAHS; YDT AS GE
ALE MELTAIO IT MAOORT YE SR, AOC AT TNE SAPE TIPE MROKIOMEC TNAT GNEO
MNALUES FETS TR TRGO NE GIUU YE IO OR NDLLH TR UEAKE IT AFAIO, GE NAKE
CETELPIOEC RO BRUURGIOF NIP TNITNEL, TNAT NE PAH ORT YE RYUIFEC TR SWEOC
NIS KAMAOT NRDLS IO A MRPBRLTUESS NRTEU. PAOH RB PH AMQDAIOTAOME ALE
AULEACH TNELE BRL TNE GIOTEL: I GISN I MRDUC NEAL TNAT HRD, PH CEALEST
BLIEOC, NAC AOH IOTEOTIRO RB PAVIOF ROE IO TNE MLRGC, YDT RB TNAT I
CESWAIL. I SIOMELEUH NRWE HRDL MNLISTPAS IO NELTBRLCSNILE PAH AYRDOC IO
TNE FAIETIES GNIMN TNAT SEASRO FEOELAUUH YLIOFS, AOC TNAT HRDL YEADX
GIUU YE SR ODPELRDS AS TR WLEKEOT HRDL BEEUIOF TNE URSS RB TNE TNLEE RB
GNRP GE SNAUU CEWLIKE HRD.’

“IT IS EKICEOT YH TNIS,” ACCEC ZAOE, “TNAT NE MRPES YAMV OR PRLE TNIS
GIOTEL.”

“IT IS ROUH EKICEOT TNAT PISS YIOFUEH CRES ORT PEAO NE _SNRDUC_.”

“GNH GIUU HRD TNIOV SR? IT PDST YE NIS RGO CRIOF; NE IS NIS RGO PASTEL.
YDT HRD CR ORT VORG _AUU_. I _GIUU_ LEAC HRD TNE WASSAFE GNIMN
WALTIMDUALUH NDLTS PE. I GIUU NAKE OR LESELKES BLRP _HRD_. ‘PL. CALMH IS
IPWATIEOT TR SEE NIS SISTEL; AOC TR MROBESS TNE TLDTN, _GE_ ALE SMALMEUH
UESS EAFEL TR PEET NEL AFAIO. I LEAUUH CR ORT TNIOV FERLFIAOA CALMH NAS
NEL EQDAU BRL YEADTH, EUEFAOME, AOC AMMRPWUISNPEOTS; AOC TNE ABBEMTIRO
SNE IOSWILES IO URDISA AOC PHSEUB IS NEIFNTEOEC IOTR SRPETNIOF STIUU
PRLE IOTELESTIOF BLRP TNE NRWE GE CALE TR EOTELTAIO RB NEL YEIOF
NELEABTEL RDL SISTEL. I CR ORT VORG GNETNEL I EKEL YEBRLE PEOTIROEC TR
HRD PH BEEUIOFS RO TNIS SDYZEMT, YDT I GIUU ORT UEAKE TNE MRDOTLH
GITNRDT MROBICIOF TNEP, AOC I TLDST HRD GIUU ORT ESTEEP TNEP
DOLEASROAYUE. PH YLRTNEL ACPILES NEL FLEATUH AULEACH; NE GIUU NAKE
BLEQDEOT RWWRLTDOITH ORG RB SEEIOF NEL RO TNE PRST IOTIPATE BRRTIOF; NEL
LEUATIROS AUU GISN TNE MROOEMTIRO AS PDMN AS NIS RGO; AOC A SISTEL’S
WALTIAUITH IS ORT PISUEACIOF PE, I TNIOV, GNEO I MAUU MNALUES PRST
MAWAYUE RB EOFAFIOF AOH GRPAO’S NEALT. GITN AUU TNESE MILMDPSTAOMES TR
BAKRDL AO ATTAMNPEOT, AOC ORTNIOF TR WLEKEOT IT, AP I GLROF, PH CEALEST
ZAOE, IO IOCDUFIOF TNE NRWE RB AO EKEOT GNIMN GIUU SEMDLE TNE NAWWIOESS
RB SR PAOH?’ GNAT TNIOV HRD RB _TNIS_ SEOTEOME, PH CEAL UIJJH?” SAIC
ZAOE, AS SNE BIOISNEC IT. “IS IT ORT MUEAL EORDFN? CRES IT ORT EXWLESSUH
CEMUALE TNAT MALRUIOE OEITNEL EXWEMTS ORL GISNES PE TR YE NEL SISTEL;
TNAT SNE IS WELBEMTUH MROKIOMEC RB NEL YLRTNEL’S IOCIBBELEOME; AOC TNAT
IB SNE SDSWEMTS TNE OATDLE RB PH BEEUIOFS BRL NIP SNE PEAOS (PRST
VIOCUH!) TR WDT PE RO PH FDALC. MAO TNELE YE AOH RTNEL RWIOIRO RO TNE
SDYZEMT?”

“HES, TNELE MAO; BRL PIOE IS TRTAUUH CIBBELEOT. GIUU HRD NEAL IT?”

“PRST GIUUIOFUH.”

“HRD SNAUU NAKE IT IO A BEG GRLCS. PISS YIOFUEH SEES TNAT NEL YLRTNEL IS
IO URKE GITN HRD AOC GAOTS NIP TR PALLH PISS CALMH. SNE BRUURGS NIP TR
TRGO IO TNE NRWE RB VEEWIOF NIP TNELE, AOC TLIES TR WELSDACE HRD TNAT NE
CRES ORT MALE AYRDT HRD.”

ZAOE SNRRV NEL NEAC.

“IOCEEC, ZAOE, HRD RDFNT TR YEUIEKE PE. OR ROE GNR NAS EKEL SEEO HRD
TRFETNEL MAO CRDYT NIS ABBEMTIRO; PISS YIOFUEH, I AP SDLE, MAOORT: SNE
IS ORT SDMN A SIPWUETRO. MRDUC SNE NAKE SEEO NAUB AS PDMN URKE IO PL.
CALMH BRL NELSEUB, SNE GRDUC NAKE RLCELEC NEL GECCIOF MURTNES. YDT TNE
MASE IS TNIS:--GE ALE ORT LIMN EORDFN RL FLAOC EORDFN BRL TNEP; AOC SNE
IS TNE PRLE AOXIRDS TR FET PISS CALMH BRL NEL YLRTNEL, BLRP TNE ORTIRO

IO AMNIEKIOF A SEMROC; IO GNIMN TNELE IS MELTAIOUH SRPE IOFEODITH, AOC I
CALE SAH IT GRDUC SDMMEEC IB PISS CE YRDLFN GELE RDT RB TNE GAH. YDT, PH
CEALEST ZAOE, HRD MAOORT SELIRDSUH IPAFIOE TNAT, YEMADSE PISS YIOFUEH
TEUUS HRD NEL YLRTNEL FLEATUH ACPILES PISS CALMH, NE IS IO TNE SPAUUEST
CEFLEE UESS SEOSIYUE RB _HRDL_ PELIT TNAO GNEO NE TRRV UEAKE RB HRD RO
TDESCAH; RL TNAT IT GIUU YE IO NEL WRGEL TR WELSDACE NIP TNAT, IOSTEAC
RB YEIOF IO URKE GITN HRD, NE IS KELH PDMN IO URKE GITN NEL BLIEOC.”

“IB GE TNRDFNT AUIVE RB PISS YIOFUEH,” LEWUIEC ZAOE, “HRDL
LEWLESEOTATIRO RB AUU TNIS PIFNT PAVE PE QDITE EASH. YDT I VORG TNE
BRDOCATIRO IS DOZDST. MALRUIOE IS IOMAWAYUE RB GIUBDUUH CEMEIKIOF
AOHROE; AOC AUU TNAT I MAO NRWE IO TNIS MASE IS, TNAT SNE IS CEMEIKEC
NELSEUB.”

“TNAT IS LIFNT. HRD MRDUC ORT NAKE STALTEC A PRLE NAWWH ICEA, SIOME HRD
GIUU ORT TAVE MRPBRLT IO PIOE: YEUIEKE NEL TR YE CEMEIKEC, YH AUU PEAOS.
HRD NAKE ORG CROE HRDL CDTH YH NEL, AOC PDST BLET OR UROFEL.”

“YDT, PH CEAL SISTEL, MAO I YE NAWWH, EKEO SDWWRSIOF TNE YEST, IO
AMMEWTIOF A PAO GNRSE SISTELS AOC BLIEOCS ALE AUU GISNIOF NIP TR PALLH
EUSEGNELE?”

“HRD PDST CEMICE BRL HRDLSEUB,” SAIC EUIJAYETN; “AOC IB, DWRO PATDLE
CEUIYELATIRO, HRD BIOC TNAT TNE PISELH RB CISRYUIFIOF NIS TGR SISTELS IS
PRLE TNAO EQDIKAUEOT TR TNE NAWWIOESS RB YEIOF NIS GIBE, I ACKISE HRD,
YH AUU PEAOS, TR LEBDSE NIP.”

“NRG MAO HRD TAUV SR?” SAIC ZAOE, BAIOTUH SPIUIOF; “HRD PDST VORG, TNAT,
TNRDFN I SNRDUC YE EXMEECIOFUH FLIEKEC AT TNEIL CISAWWLRYATIRO, I MRDUC
ORT NESITATE.”

“I CIC ORT TNIOV HRD GRDUC; AOC TNAT YEIOF TNE MASE, I MAOORT MROSICEL
HRDL SITDATIRO GITN PDMN MRPWASSIRO.”

“YDT IB NE LETDLOS OR PRLE TNIS GIOTEL, PH MNRIME GIUU OEKEL YE
LEQDILEC. A TNRDSAOC TNIOFS PAH ALISE IO SIX PROTNS.”

TNE ICEA RB NIS LETDLOIOF OR PRLE EUIJAYETN TLEATEC GITN TNE DTPRST
MROTEPWT. IT AWWEALEC TR NEL PELEUH TNE SDFFESTIRO RB MALRUIOE’S
IOTELESTEC GISNES; AOC SNE MRDUC ORT BRL A PRPEOT SDWWRSE TNAT TNRSE
GISNES, NRGEKEL RWEOUH RL ALTBDUUH SWRVEO, MRDUC IOBUDEOME A HRDOF PAO
SR TRTAUUH IOCEWEOCEOT RB EKELHROE.

SNE LEWLESEOTEC TR NEL SISTEL, AS BRLMIYUH AS WRSSIYUE, GNAT SNE BEUT RO
TNE SDYZEMT, AOC NAC SRRO TNE WUEASDLE RB SEEIOF ITS NAWWH EBBEMT.
ZAOE’S TEPWEL GAS ORT CESWROCIOF; AOC SNE GAS FLACDAUUH UEC TR NRWE,
TNRDFN TNE CIBBICEOME RB ABBEMTIRO SRPETIPES RKELMAPE TNE NRWE, TNAT
YIOFUEH GRDUC LETDLO TR OETNELBIEUC, AOC AOSGEL EKELH GISN RB NEL NEALT.

TNEH AFLEEC TNAT PLS. YEOOET SNRDUC ROUH NEAL RB TNE CEWALTDLE RB TNE
BAPIUH, GITNRDT YEIOF AUALPEC RO TNE SMRLE RB TNE FEOTUEPAO’S MROCDMT;
YDT EKEO TNIS WALTIAU MRPPDOIMATIRO FAKE NEL A FLEAT CEAU RB MROMELO,
AOC SNE YEGAIUEC IT AS EXMEECIOFUH DOUDMVH TNAT TNE UACIES SNRDUC NAWWEO
TR FR AGAH ZDST AS TNEH GELE AUU FETTIOF SR IOTIPATE TRFETNEL. ABTEL
UAPEOTIOF IT, NRGEKEL, AT SRPE UEOFTN, SNE NAC TNE MROSRUATIRO RB
TNIOVIOF TNAT PL. YIOFUEH GRDUC YE SRRO CRGO AFAIO, AOC SRRO CIOIOF AT
UROFYRDLO; AOC TNE MROMUDSIRO RB AUU GAS TNE MRPBRLTAYUE CEMUALATIRO,
TNAT, TNRDFN NE NAC YEEO IOKITEC ROUH TR A BAPIUH CIOOEL, SNE GRDUC TAVE
MALE TR NAKE TGR BDUU MRDLSES.

MNAWTEL XXII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TNE YEOOETS GELE EOFAFEC TR CIOE GITN TNE UDMASES; AOC AFAIO, CDLIOF TNE
MNIEB RB TNE CAH, GAS PISS UDMAS SR VIOC AS TR UISTEO TR PL. MRUUIOS.
EUIJAYETN TRRV AO RWWRLTDOITH RB TNAOVIOF NEL. “IT VEEWS NIP IO FRRC
NDPRDL,” SAIC SNE, “AOC I AP PRLE RYUIFEC TR HRD TNAO I MAO EXWLESS.”

MNALURTTE ASSDLEC NEL BLIEOC RB NEL SATISBAMTIRO IO YEIOF DSEBDU, AOC
TNAT IT APWUH LEWAIC NEL BRL TNE UITTUE SAMLIBIME RB NEL TIPE. TNIS GAS
KELH APIAYUE; YDT MNALURTTE’S VIOCOESS EXTEOCEC BALTNEL TNAO EUIJAYETN
NAC AOH MROMEWTIRO RB:--ITS RYZEMT GAS ORTNIOF UESS TNAO TR SEMDLE NEL
BLRP AOH LETDLO RB PL. MRUUIOS’S ACCLESSES, YH EOFAFIOF TNEP TRGALCS
NELSEUB. SDMN GAS PISS UDMAS’S SMNEPE; AOC AWWEALAOMES GELE SR
BAKRDLAYUE, TNAT GNEO TNEH WALTEC AT OIFNT, SNE GRDUC NAKE BEUT AUPRST
SDLE RB SDMMESS IB NE NAC ORT YEEO TR UEAKE NELTBRLCSNILE SR KELH SRRO.
YDT NELE SNE CIC IOZDSTIME TR TNE BILE AOC IOCEWEOCEOME RB NIS
MNALAMTEL; BRL IT UEC NIP TR ESMAWE RDT RB UROFYRDLO NRDSE TNE OEXT
PRLOIOF GITN ACPILAYUE SUHOESS, AOC NASTEO TR UDMAS URCFE TR TNLRG
NIPSEUB AT NEL BEET. NE GAS AOXIRDS TR AKRIC TNE ORTIME RB NIS MRDSIOS,
BLRP A MROKIMTIRO TNAT, IB TNEH SAG NIP CEWALT, TNEH MRDUC ORT BAIU TR
MROZEMTDLE NIS CESIFO, AOC NE GAS ORT GIUUIOF TR NAKE TNE ATTEPWT VORGO
TIUU ITS SDMMESS MRDUC YE VORGO UIVEGISE; BRL, TNRDFN BEEUIOF AUPRST
SEMDLE, AOC GITN LEASRO, BRL MNALURTTE NAC YEEO TRUELAYUH EOMRDLAFIOF,
NE GAS MRPWALATIKEUH CIBBICEOT SIOME TNE ACKEOTDLE RB GECOESCAH. NIS
LEMEWTIRO, NRGEKEL, GAS RB TNE PRST BUATTELIOF VIOC. PISS UDMAS
WELMEIKEC NIP BLRP AO DWWEL GIOCRG AS NE GAUVEC TRGALCS TNE NRDSE, AOC
IOSTAOTUH SET RDT TR PEET NIP AMMICEOTAUUH IO TNE UAOE. YDT UITTUE NAC
SNE CALEC TR NRWE TNAT SR PDMN URKE AOC EURQDEOME AGAITEC NEL TNELE.

IO AS SNRLT A TIPE AS PL. MRUUIOS’S UROF SWEEMNES GRDUC AUURG,
EKELHTNIOF GAS SETTUEC YETGEEO TNEP TR TNE SATISBAMTIRO RB YRTN; AOC AS
TNEH EOTELEC TNE NRDSE, NE EALOESTUH EOTLEATEC NEL TR OAPE TNE CAH TNAT
