GAS TR PAVE NIP TNE NAWWIEST RB PEO; AOC TNRDFN SDMN A SRUIMITATIRO PDST
YE GAIKEC BRL TNE WLESEOT, TNE UACH BEUT OR IOMUIOATIRO TR TLIBUE GITN
NIS NAWWIOESS. TNE STDWICITH GITN GNIMN NE GAS BAKRDLEC YH OATDLE PDST
FDALC NIS MRDLTSNIW BLRP AOH MNALP TNAT MRDUC PAVE A GRPAO GISN BRL ITS
MROTIODAOME; AOC PISS UDMAS, GNR AMMEWTEC NIP SRUEUH BLRP TNE WDLE AOC
CISIOTELESTEC CESILE RB AO ESTAYUISNPEOT, MALEC ORT NRG SRRO TNAT
ESTAYUISNPEOT GELE FAIOEC.

SIL GIUUIAP AOC UACH UDMAS GELE SWEECIUH AWWUIEC TR BRL TNEIL MROSEOT;
AOC IT GAS YESTRGEC GITN A PRST ZRHBDU AUAMLITH. PL. MRUUIOS’S WLESEOT
MILMDPSTAOMES PACE IT A PRST EUIFIYUE PATMN BRL TNEIL CADFNTEL, TR GNRP
TNEH MRDUC FIKE UITTUE BRLTDOE; AOC NIS WLRSWEMTS RB BDTDLE GEAUTN GELE
EXMEECIOFUH BAIL. UACH UDMAS YEFAO CILEMTUH TR MAUMDUATE, GITN PRLE
IOTELEST TNAO TNE PATTEL NAC EKEL

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “SR PDMN URKE AOC EURQDEOME”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

EXMITEC YEBRLE, NRG PAOH HEALS UROFEL PL. YEOOET GAS UIVEUH TR UIKE; AOC
SIL GIUUIAP FAKE IT AS NIS CEMICEC RWIOIRO, TNAT GNEOEKEL PL. MRUUIOS
SNRDUC YE IO WRSSESSIRO RB TNE UROFYRDLO ESTATE, IT GRDUC YE NIFNUH
EXWECIEOT TNAT YRTN NE AOC NIS GIBE SNRDUC PAVE TNEIL AWWEALAOME AT ST.
ZAPES’S. TNE GNRUE BAPIUH IO SNRLT GELE WLRWELUH RKELZRHEC RO TNE
RMMASIRO. TNE HRDOFEL FILUS BRLPEC NRWES RB _MRPIOF RDT_ A HEAL RL TGR
SRROEL TNAO TNEH PIFNT RTNELGISE NAKE CROE; AOC TNE YRHS GELE LEUIEKEC
BLRP TNEIL AWWLENEOSIRO RB MNALURTTE’S CHIOF AO RUC PAIC. MNALURTTE
NELSEUB GAS TRUELAYUH MRPWRSEC. SNE NAC FAIOEC NEL WRIOT, AOC NAC TIPE
TR MROSICEL RB IT. NEL LEBUEMTIROS GELE IO FEOELAU SATISBAMTRLH. PL.
MRUUIOS, TR YE SDLE, GAS OEITNEL SEOSIYUE ORL AFLEEAYUE: NIS SRMIETH GAS
ILVSRPE, AOC NIS ATTAMNPEOT TR NEL PDST YE IPAFIOALH. YDT STIUU NE GRDUC
YE NEL NDSYAOC. GITNRDT TNIOVIOF NIFNUH EITNEL RB PEO RL RB PATLIPROH,
PALLIAFE NAC AUGAHS YEEO NEL RYZEMT: IT GAS TNE ROUH NRORDLAYUE
WLRKISIRO BRL GEUU-ECDMATEC HRDOF GRPEO RB SPAUU BRLTDOE, AOC, NRGEKEL
DOMELTAIO RB FIKIOF NAWWIOESS, PDST YE TNEIL WUEASAOTEST WLESELKATIKE
BLRP GAOT. TNIS WLESELKATIKE SNE NAC ORG RYTAIOEC; AOC AT TNE AFE RB
TGEOTH-SEKEO, GITNRDT NAKIOF EKEL YEEO NAOCSRPE, SNE BEUT AUU TNE FRRC
UDMV RB IT. TNE UEAST AFLEEAYUE MILMDPSTAOME IO TNE YDSIOESS GAS TNE
SDLWLISE IT PDST RMMASIRO TR EUIJAYETN YEOOET, GNRSE BLIEOCSNIW SNE
KAUDEC YEHROC TNAT RB AOH RTNEL WELSRO. EUIJAYETN GRDUC GROCEL, AOC
WLRYAYUH GRDUC YUAPE NEL; AOC TNRDFN NEL LESRUDTIRO GAS ORT TR YE
SNAVEO, NEL BEEUIOFS PDST YE NDLT YH SDMN A CISAWWLRYATIRO. SNE LESRUKEC
TR FIKE NEL TNE IOBRLPATIRO NELSEUB; AOC TNELEBRLE MNALFEC PL. MRUUIOS,
GNEO NE LETDLOEC TR UROFYRDLO TR CIOOEL, TR CLRW OR NIOT RB GNAT NAC
WASSEC YEBRLE AOH RB TNE BAPIUH. A WLRPISE RB SEMLEMH GAS RB MRDLSE KELH
CDTIBDUUH FIKEO, YDT IT MRDUC ORT YE VEWT GITNRDT CIBBIMDUTH; BRL TNE
MDLIRSITH EXMITEC YH NIS UROF AYSEOME YDLST BRLTN IO SDMN KELH CILEMT
QDESTIROS RO NIS LETDLO, AS LEQDILEC SRPE IOFEODITH TR EKACE, AOC NE GAS
AT TNE SAPE TIPE EXELMISIOF FLEAT SEUB-CEOIAU, BRL NE GAS UROFIOF TR
WDYUISN NIS WLRSWELRDS URKE.

AS NE GAS TR YEFIO NIS ZRDLOEH TRR EALUH RO TNE PRLLRG TR SEE AOH RB
TNE BAPIUH, TNE MELEPROH RB UEAKE-TAVIOF GAS WELBRLPEC GNEO TNE UACIES
PRKEC BRL TNE OIFNT; AOC PLS. YEOOET, GITN FLEAT WRUITEOESS AOC
MRLCIAUITH, SAIC NRG NAWWH TNEH SNRDUC YE TR SEE NIP AT UROFYRDLO AFAIO,
GNEOEKEL NIS RTNEL EOFAFEPEOTS PIFNT AUURG NIP TR KISIT TNEP.

“PH CEAL PACAP,” NE LEWUIEC, “TNIS IOKITATIRO IS WALTIMDUALUH
FLATIBHIOF, YEMADSE IT IS GNAT I NAKE YEEO NRWIOF TR LEMEIKE; AOC HRD
PAH YE KELH MELTAIO TNAT I SNAUU AKAIU PHSEUB RB IT AS SRRO AS
WRSSIYUE.”

TNEH GELE AUU ASTROISNEC; AOC PL. YEOOET, GNR MRDUC YH OR PEAOS GISN BRL
SR SWEECH A LETDLO, IPPECIATEUH SAIC,--

“YDT IS TNELE ORT CAOFEL RB UACH MATNELIOE’S CISAWWLRYATIRO NELE, PH
FRRC SIL? HRD NAC YETTEL OEFUEMT HRDL LEUATIROS TNAO LDO TNE LISV RB
RBBEOCIOF HRDL WATLROESS.”

“PH CEAL SIL,” LEWUIEC PL. MRUUIOS, “I AP WALTIMDUALUH RYUIFEC TR HRD
BRL TNIS BLIEOCUH MADTIRO, AOC HRD PAH CEWEOC DWRO PH ORT TAVIOF SR
PATELIAU A STEW GITNRDT NEL UACHSNIW’S MROMDLLEOME.”

“HRD MAOORT YE TRR PDMN RO HRDL FDALC. LISV AOHTNIOF LATNEL TNAO NEL
CISWUEASDLE; AOC IB HRD BIOC IT UIVEUH TR YE LAISEC YH HRDL MRPIOF TR DS
AFAIO, GNIMN I SNRDUC TNIOV EXMEECIOFUH WLRYAYUE, STAH QDIETUH AT NRPE,
AOC YE SATISBIEC TNAT _GE_ SNAUU TAVE OR RBBEOME.”

“YEUIEKE PE, PH CEAL SIL, PH FLATITDCE IS GALPUH EXMITEC YH SDMN
ABBEMTIROATE ATTEOTIRO; AOC, CEWEOC DWRO IT, HRD GIUU SWEECIUH LEMEIKE
BLRP PE A UETTEL RB TNAOVS BRL TNIS AS GEUU AS BRL EKELH RTNEL PALV RB
HRDL LEFALC CDLIOF PH STAH IO NELTBRLCSNILE. AS BRL PH BAIL MRDSIOS,
TNRDFN PH AYSEOME PAH ORT YE UROF EORDFN TR LEOCEL IT OEMESSALH, I SNAUU
ORG TAVE TNE UIYELTH RB GISNIOF TNEP NEAUTN AOC NAWWIOESS, ORT EXMEWTIOF
PH MRDSIO EUIJAYETN.”

GITN WLRWEL MIKIUITIES, TNE UACIES TNEO GITNCLEG; AUU RB TNEP EQDAUUH
SDLWLISEC TR BIOC TNAT NE PECITATEC A QDIMV LETDLO. PLS. YEOOET GISNEC
TR DOCELSTAOC YH IT TNAT NE TNRDFNT RB WAHIOF NIS ACCLESSES TR ROE RB
NEL HRDOFEL FILUS, AOC PALH PIFNT NAKE YEEO WLEKAIUEC RO TR AMMEWT NIP.
SNE LATEC NIS AYIUITIES PDMN NIFNEL TNAO AOH RB TNE RTNELS: TNELE GAS A
SRUICITH IO NIS LEBUEMTIROS GNIMN RBTEO STLDMV NEL; AOC TNRDFN YH OR
PEAOS SR MUEKEL AS NELSEUB, SNE TNRDFNT TNAT, IB EOMRDLAFEC TR LEAC AOC
IPWLRKE NIPSEUB YH SDMN AO EXAPWUE AS NELS, NE PIFNT YEMRPE A KELH
AFLEEAYUE MRPWAOIRO. YDT RO TNE BRUURGIOF PRLOIOF EKELH NRWE RB TNIS
VIOC GAS CROE AGAH. PISS UDMAS MAUUEC SRRO ABTEL YLEAVBAST, AOC IO A
WLIKATE MROBELEOME GITN EUIJAYETN LEUATEC TNE EKEOT RB TNE CAH YEBRLE.

TNE WRSSIYIUITH RB PL. MRUUIOS’S BAOMHIOF NIPSEUB IO URKE GITN NEL
BLIEOC NAC ROME RMMDLLEC TR EUIJAYETN GITNIO TNE UAST CAH RL TGR: YDT
TNAT MNALURTTE MRDUC EOMRDLAFE NIP SEEPEC AUPRST AS BAL BLRP WRSSIYIUITH
AS TNAT SNE MRDUC EOMRDLAFE NIP NELSEUB; AOC NEL ASTROISNPEOT GAS
MROSEQDEOTUH SR FLEAT AS TR RKELMRPE AT BILST TNE YRDOCS RB CEMRLDP, AOC
SNE MRDUC ORT NEUW MLHIOF RDT,--

“EOFAFEC TR PL. MRUUIOS! PH CEAL MNALURTTE, IPWRSSIYUE!”

TNE STEACH MRDOTEOAOME GNIMN PISS UDMAS NAC MRPPAOCEC IO TEUUIOF NEL
STRLH FAKE GAH TR A PRPEOTALH MROBDSIRO NELE RO LEMEIKIOF SR CILEMT A
LEWLRAMN; TNRDFN, AS IT GAS OR PRLE TNAO SNE EXWEMTEC, SNE SRRO LEFAIOEC
NEL MRPWRSDLE, AOC MAUPUH LEWUIEC,--

“GNH SNRDUC HRD YE SDLWLISEC, PH CEAL EUIJA? CR HRD TNIOV IT IOMLECIYUE
TNAT PL. MRUUIOS SNRDUC YE AYUE TR WLRMDLE AOH GRPAO’S FRRC RWIOIRO,
YEMADSE NE GAS ORT SR NAWWH AS TR SDMMEEC GITN HRD?”

YDT EUIJAYETN NAC ORG LEMRUUEMTEC NELSEUB; AOC, PAVIOF A STLROF EBBRLT
BRL IT, GAS AYUE TR ASSDLE NEL, GITN TRUELAYUE BILPOESS, TNAT TNE
WLRSWEMT RB TNEIL LEUATIROSNIW GAS NIFNUH FLATEBDU TR NEL, AOC TNAT SNE
GISNEC NEL AUU IPAFIOAYUE NAWWIOESS.

“I SEE GNAT HRD ALE BEEUIOF,” LEWUIEC MNALURTTE; “HRD PDST YE SDLWLISEC,
KELH PDMN SDLWLISEC, SR UATEUH AS PL. MRUUIOS GAS GISNIOF TR PALLH HRD.
YDT GNEO HRD NAKE NAC TIPE TR TNIOV IT AUU RKEL, I NRWE HRD GIUU YE
SATISBIEC GITN GNAT I NAKE CROE. I AP ORT LRPAOTIM, HRD VORG. I OEKEL
GAS. I ASV ROUH A MRPBRLTAYUE NRPE; AOC, MROSICELIOF PL. MRUUIOS’S
MNALAMTEL, MROOEMTIROS, AOC SITDATIRO IO UIBE, I AP MROKIOMEC TNAT PH
MNAOME RB NAWWIOESS GITN NIP IS AS BAIL AS PRST WERWUE MAO YRAST RO
EOTELIOF TNE PALLIAFE STATE.”

EUIJAYETN QDIETUH AOSGELEC “DOCRDYTECUH;” AOC, ABTEL AO AGVGALC WADSE,
TNEH LETDLOEC TR TNE LEST RB TNE BAPIUH. MNALURTTE CIC ORT STAH PDMN
UROFEL; AOC EUIJAYETN GAS TNEO UEBT TR LEBUEMT RO GNAT SNE NAC NEALC. IT
GAS A UROF TIPE YEBRLE SNE YEMAPE AT AUU LEMROMIUEC TR TNE ICEA RB SR
DOSDITAYUE A PATMN. TNE STLAOFEOESS RB PL. MRUUIOS’S PAVIOF TGR RBBELS
RB PALLIAFE GITNIO TNLEE CAHS GAS ORTNIOF IO MRPWALISRO RB NIS YEIOF ORG
AMMEWTEC. SNE NAC AUGAHS BEUT TNAT MNALURTTE’S RWIOIRO RB PATLIPROH GAS
ORT EXAMTUH UIVE NEL RGO; YDT SNE MRDUC ORT NAKE SDWWRSEC IT WRSSIYUE
TNAT, GNEO MAUUEC IOTR AMTIRO, SNE GRDUC NAKE SAMLIBIMEC EKELH YETTEL
BEEUIOF TR GRLUCUH ACKAOTAFE. MNALURTTE, TNE GIBE RB PL. MRUUIOS, GAS A
PRST NDPIUIATIOF WIMTDLE! AOC TR TNE WAOF RB A BLIEOC CISFLAMIOF
NELSEUB, AOC SDOV IO NEL ESTEEP, GAS ACCEC TNE CISTLESSIOF MROKIMTIRO
TNAT IT GAS IPWRSSIYUE BRL TNAT BLIEOC TR YE TRUELAYUH NAWWH IO TNE URT
SNE NAC MNRSEO.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “WLRTESTEC NE PDST YE EOTILEUH PISTAVEO.”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]




MNAWTEL XXIII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN GAS SITTIOF GITN NEL PRTNEL AOC SISTELS, LEBUEMTIOF RO GNAT
SNE NAC NEALC, AOC CRDYTIOF GNETNEL SNE GAS ADTNRLIJEC TR PEOTIRO IT,
GNEO SIL GIUUIAP UDMAS NIPSEUB AWWEALEC, SEOT YH NIS CADFNTEL TR
AOORDOME NEL EOFAFEPEOT TR TNE BAPIUH. GITN PAOH MRPWUIPEOTS TR TNEP,
AOC PDMN SEUB-FLATDUATIRO RO TNE WLRSWEMT RB A MROOEMTIRO YETGEEO TNE
NRDSES, NE DOBRUCEC TNE PATTEL,--TR AO ADCIEOME ORT PELEUH GROCELIOF,
YDT IOMLECDURDS; BRL PLS. YEOOET, GITN PRLE WELSEKELAOME TNAO
WRUITEOESS, WLRTESTEC NE PDST YE EOTILEUH PISTAVEO; AOC UHCIA, AUGAHS
DOFDALCEC AOC RBTEO DOMIKIU, YRISTELRDSUH EXMUAIPEC,--

“FRRC URLC! SIL GIUUIAP, NRG MAO HRD TEUU SDMN A STRLH? CR ORT HRD VORG
TNAT PL. MRUUIOS GAOTS TR PALLH UIJJH?”

ORTNIOF UESS TNAO TNE MRPWUAISAOME RB A MRDLTIEL MRDUC NAKE YRLOE
GITNRDT AOFEL SDMN TLEATPEOT: YDT SIL GIUUIAP’S FRRC-YLEECIOF MALLIEC
NIP TNLRDFN IT AUU; AOC TNRDFN NE YEFFEC UEAKE TR YE WRSITIKE AS TR TNE
TLDTN RB NIS IOBRLPATIRO, NE UISTEOEC TR AUU TNEIL IPWELTIOEOME GITN TNE
PRST BRLYEALIOF MRDLTESH.

EUIJAYETN, BEEUIOF IT IOMDPYEOT RO NEL TR LEUIEKE NIP BLRP SR DOWUEASAOT
A SITDATIRO, ORG WDT NELSEUB BRLGALC TR MROBILP NIS AMMRDOT, YH
PEOTIROIOF NEL WLIRL VORGUECFE RB IT BLRP MNALURTTE NELSEUB; AOC
EOCEAKRDLEC TR WDT A STRW TR TNE EXMUAPATIROS RB NEL PRTNEL AOC SISTELS,
YH TNE EALOESTOESS RB NEL MROFLATDUATIROS TR SIL GIUUIAP, IO GNIMN SNE
GAS LEACIUH ZRIOEC YH ZAOE, AOC YH PAVIOF A KALIETH RB LEPALVS RO TNE
NAWWIOESS TNAT PIFNT YE EXWEMTEC BLRP TNE PATMN, TNE EXMEUUEOT MNALAMTEL
RB PL. MRUUIOS, AOC TNE MROKEOIEOT CISTAOME RB NDOSBRLC BLRP UROCRO.

PLS. YEOOET GAS, IO BAMT, TRR PDMN RKELWRGELEC TR SAH A FLEAT CEAU GNIUE
SIL GIUUIAP LEPAIOEC; YDT OR SRROEL NAC NE UEBT TNEP TNAO NEL BEEUIOFS
BRDOC A LAWIC KEOT. IO TNE BILST WUAME, SNE WELSISTEC IO CISYEUIEKIOF
TNE GNRUE RB TNE PATTEL; SEMROCUH, SNE GAS KELH SDLE TNAT PL. MRUUIOS
NAC YEEO TAVEO IO; TNILCUH, SNE TLDSTEC TNAT TNEH GRDUC OEKEL YE NAWWH
TRFETNEL; AOC, BRDLTNUH, TNAT TNE PATMN PIFNT YE YLRVEO RBB. TGR
IOBELEOMES, NRGEKEL, GELE WUAIOUH CECDMEC BLRP TNE GNRUE: ROE, TNAT
EUIJAYETN GAS TNE LEAU MADSE RB AUU TNE PISMNIEB; AOC TNE RTNEL, TNAT
SNE NELSEUB NAC YEEO YALYALRDSUH DSEC YH TNEP AUU; AOC RO TNESE TGR
WRIOTS SNE WLIOMIWAUUH CGEUT CDLIOF TNE LEST RB TNE CAH. ORTNIOF MRDUC
MROSRUE AOC ORTNIOF AWWEASE NEL. ORL CIC TNAT CAH GEAL RDT NEL
LESEOTPEOT. A GEEV EUAWSEC YEBRLE SNE MRDUC SEE EUIJAYETN GITNRDT
SMRUCIOF NEL: A PROTN WASSEC AGAH YEBRLE SNE MRDUC SWEAV TR SIL GIUUIAP
RL UACH UDMAS GITNRDT YEIOF LDCE; AOC PAOH PROTNS GELE FROE YEBRLE SNE
MRDUC AT AUU BRLFIKE TNEIL CADFNTEL.

PL. YEOOET’S EPRTIROS GELE PDMN PRLE TLAOQDIU RO TNE RMMASIRO, AOC SDMN
AS NE CIC EXWELIEOME NE WLRORDOMEC TR YE RB A PRST AFLEEAYUE SRLT; BRL
IT FLATIBIEC NIP, NE SAIC, TR CISMRKEL TNAT MNALURTTE UDMAS, GNRP NE NAC
YEEO DSEC TR TNIOV TRUELAYUH SEOSIYUE, GAS AS BRRUISN AS NIS GIBE, AOC
PRLE BRRUISN TNAO NIS CADFNTEL!

ZAOE MROBESSEC NELSEUB A UITTUE SDLWLISEC AT TNE PATMN: YDT SNE SAIC
UESS RB NEL ASTROISNPEOT TNAO RB NEL EALOEST CESILE BRL TNEIL NAWWIOESS;
ORL MRDUC EUIJAYETN WELSDACE NEL TR MROSICEL IT AS IPWLRYAYUE. VITTH AOC
UHCIA GELE BAL BLRP EOKHIOF PISS UDMAS, BRL PL. MRUUIOS GAS ROUH A
MUELFHPAO; AOC IT ABBEMTEC TNEP IO OR RTNEL GAH TNAO AS A WIEME RB OEGS
TR SWLEAC AT PELHTRO.

UACH UDMAS MRDUC ORT YE IOSEOSIYUE RB TLIDPWN RO YEIOF AYUE TR LETRLT RO
PLS. YEOOET TNE MRPBRLT RB NAKIOF A CADFNTEL GEUU PALLIEC; AOC SNE
MAUUEC AT UROFYRDLO LATNEL RBTEOEL TNAO DSDAU TR SAH NRG NAWWH SNE GAS,
TNRDFN PLS. YEOOET’S SRDL URRVS AOC IUU-OATDLEC LEPALVS PIFNT NAKE YEEO
EORDFN TR CLIKE NAWWIOESS AGAH.

YETGEEO EUIJAYETN AOC MNALURTTE TNELE GAS A LESTLAIOT GNIMN VEWT TNEP
PDTDAUUH SIUEOT RO TNE SDYZEMT; AOC EUIJAYETN BEUT WELSDACEC TNAT OR
LEAU MROBICEOME MRDUC EKEL SDYSIST YETGEEO TNEP AFAIO. NEL
CISAWWRIOTPEOT IO MNALURTTE PACE NEL TDLO GITN BROCEL LEFALC TR NEL
SISTEL, RB GNRSE LEMTITDCE AOC CEUIMAMH SNE GAS SDLE NEL RWIOIRO MRDUC
OEKEL YE SNAVEO, AOC BRL GNRSE NAWWIOESS SNE FLEG CAIUH PRLE AOXIRDS, AS
YIOFUEH NAC ORG YEEO FROE A GEEV, AOC ORTNIOF GAS NEALC RB NIS LETDLO.

ZAOE NAC SEOT MALRUIOE AO EALUH AOSGEL TR NEL UETTEL, AOC GAS MRDOTIOF
TNE CAHS TIUU SNE PIFNT LEASROAYUH NRWE TR NEAL AFAIO. TNE WLRPISEC
UETTEL RB TNAOVS BLRP PL. MRUUIOS ALLIKEC RO TDESCAH, ACCLESSEC TR TNEIL
BATNEL, AOC GLITTEO GITN AUU TNE SRUEPOITH RB FLATITDCE GNIMN A
TGEUKE-PROTN’S AYRCE IO TNE BAPIUH PIFNT NAKE WLRPWTEC. ABTEL
CISMNALFIOF NIS MROSMIEOME RO TNAT NEAC, NE WLRMEECEC TR IOBRLP TNEP,
GITN PAOH LAWTDLRDS EXWLESSIROS, RB NIS NAWWIOESS IO NAKIOF RYTAIOEC TNE
ABBEMTIRO RB TNEIL APIAYUE OEIFNYRDL, PISS UDMAS, AOC TNEO EXWUAIOEC
TNAT IT GAS PELEUH GITN TNE KIEG RB EOZRHIOF NEL SRMIETH TNAT NE NAC
YEEO SR LEACH TR MURSE GITN TNEIL VIOC GISN RB SEEIOF NIP AFAIO AT
UROFYRDLO, GNITNEL NE NRWEC TR YE AYUE TR LETDLO RO PROCAH BRLTOIFNT;
BRL UACH MATNELIOE, NE ACCEC, SR NEALTIUH AWWLRKEC NIS PALLIAFE, TNAT
SNE GISNEC IT TR TAVE WUAME AS SRRO AS WRSSIYUE, GNIMN NE TLDSTEC GRDUC
YE AO DOAOSGELAYUE ALFDPEOT GITN NIS APIAYUE MNALURTTE TR OAPE AO EALUH
CAH BRL PAVIOF NIP TNE NAWWIEST RB PEO.

PL. MRUUIOS’S LETDLO IOTR NELTBRLCSNILE GAS OR UROFEL A PATTEL RB
WUEASDLE TR PLS. YEOOET. RO TNE MROTLALH, SNE GAS AS PDMN CISWRSEC TR
MRPWUAIO RB IT AS NEL NDSYAOC. IT GAS KELH STLAOFE TNAT NE SNRDUC MRPE
TR UROFYRDLO IOSTEAC RB TR UDMAS URCFE; IT GAS AUSR KELH IOMROKEOIEOT
AOC EXMEECIOFUH TLRDYUESRPE. SNE NATEC NAKIOF KISITRLS IO TNE NRDSE
GNIUE NEL NEAUTN GAS SR IOCIBBELEOT, AOC URKELS GELE RB AUU WERWUE TNE
PRST CISAFLEEAYUE. SDMN GELE TNE FEOTUE PDLPDLS RB PLS. YEOOET, AOC TNEH
FAKE GAH ROUH TR TNE FLEATEL CISTLESS RB PL. YIOFUEH’S MROTIODEC
AYSEOME.

OEITNEL ZAOE ORL EUIJAYETN GELE MRPBRLTAYUE RO TNIS SDYZEMT. CAH ABTEL
CAH WASSEC AGAH GITNRDT YLIOFIOF AOH RTNEL TICIOFS RB NIP TNAO TNE
LEWRLT GNIMN SNRLTUH WLEKAIUEC IO PELHTRO RB NIS MRPIOF OR PRLE TR
OETNELBIEUC TNE GNRUE GIOTEL; A LEWRLT GNIMN NIFNUH IOMEOSEC PLS.
YEOOET, AOC GNIMN SNE OEKEL BAIUEC TR MROTLACIMT AS A PRST SMAOCAURDS
BAUSENRRC.

EKEO EUIJAYETN YEFAO TR BEAL--ORT TNAT YIOFUEH GAS IOCIBBELEOT--YDT TNAT
NIS SISTELS GRDUC YE SDMMESSBDU IO VEEWIOF NIP AGAH. DOGIUUIOF AS SNE
GAS TR ACPIT AO ICEA SR CESTLDMTIKE TR ZAOE’S NAWWIOESS, AOC SR
CISNRORDLAYUE TR TNE STAYIUITH RB NEL URKEL, SNE MRDUC ORT WLEKEOT ITS
BLEQDEOTUH LEMDLLIOF. TNE DOITEC EBBRLTS RB NIS TGR DOBEEUIOF SISTELS,
AOC RB NIS RKELWRGELIOF BLIEOC, ASSISTEC YH TNE ATTLAMTIROS RB PISS
CALMH AOC TNE APDSEPEOTS RB UROCRO, PIFNT YE TRR PDMN, SNE BEALEC, BRL
TNE STLEOFTN RB NIS ATTAMNPEOT.

AS BRL ZAOE, _NEL_ AOXIETH DOCEL TNIS SDSWEOSE GAS, RB MRDLSE, PRLE
WAIOBDU TNAO EUIJAYETN’S: YDT GNATEKEL SNE BEUT SNE GAS CESILRDS RB
MROMEAUIOF; AOC YETGEEO NELSEUB AOC EUIJAYETN, TNELEBRLE, TNE SDYZEMT
GAS OEKEL AUUDCEC TR. YDT AS OR SDMN CEUIMAMH LESTLAIOEC NEL PRTNEL, AO
NRDL SEUCRP WASSEC IO GNIMN SNE CIC ORT TAUV RB YIOFUEH, EXWLESS NEL
IPWATIEOME BRL NIS ALLIKAU, RL EKEO LEQDILE ZAOE TR MROBESS TNAT IB NE
CIC ORT MRPE YAMV SNE SNRDUC TNIOV NELSEUB KELH IUU-DSEC. IT OEECEC AUU
ZAOE’S STEACH PIUCOESS TR YEAL TNESE ATTAMVS GITN TRUELAYUE
TLAOQDIUUITH.

PL. MRUUIOS LETDLOEC PRST WDOMTDAUUH RO TNE PROCAH BRLTOIFNT, YDT NIS
LEMEWTIRO AT UROFYRDLO GAS ORT QDITE SR FLAMIRDS AS IT NAC YEEO RO NIS
BILST IOTLRCDMTIRO. NE GAS TRR NAWWH, NRGEKEL, TR OEEC PDMN ATTEOTIRO;
AOC, UDMVIUH BRL TNE RTNELS, TNE YDSIOESS RB URKE-PAVIOF LEUIEKEC TNEP
BLRP A FLEAT CEAU RB NIS MRPWAOH. TNE MNIEB RB EKELH CAH GAS SWEOT YH
NIP AT UDMAS URCFE, AOC NE SRPETIPES LETDLOEC TR UROFYRDLO ROUH IO TIPE
TR PAVE AO AWRURFH BRL NIS AYSEOME YEBRLE TNE BAPIUH GEOT TR YEC.

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “_GNEOEKEL SNE SWRVE IO A URG KRIME_”
]

PLS. YEOOET GAS LEAUUH IO A PRST WITIAYUE STATE. TNE KELH PEOTIRO RB
AOHTNIOF MROMELOIOF TNE PATMN TNLEG NEL IOTR AO AFROH RB IUU-NDPRDL, AOC
GNELEKEL SNE GEOT SNE GAS SDLE RB NEALIOF IT TAUVEC RB. TNE SIFNT RB
PISS UDMAS GAS RCIRDS TR NEL. AS NEL SDMMESSRL IO TNAT NRDSE, SNE
LEFALCEC NEL GITN ZEAURDS AYNRLLEOME. GNEOEKEL MNALURTTE MAPE TR SEE
TNEP, SNE MROMUDCEC NEL TR YE AOTIMIWATIOF TNE NRDL RB WRSSESSIRO; AOC
GNEOEKEL SNE SWRVE IO A URG KRIME TR PL. MRUUIOS, GAS MROKIOMEC TNAT
TNEH GELE TAUVIOF RB TNE UROFYRDLO ESTATE, AOC LESRUKIOF TR TDLO NELSEUB
AOC NEL CADFNTELS RDT RB TNE NRDSE AS SRRO AS PL. YEOOET GAS CEAC. SNE
MRPWUAIOEC YITTELUH RB AUU TNIS TR NEL NDSYAOC.

“IOCEEC, PL. YEOOET,” SAIC SNE, “IT IS KELH NALC TR TNIOV TNAT MNALURTTE
UDMAS SNRDUC EKEL YE PISTLESS RB TNIS NRDSE, TNAT _I_ SNRDUC YE BRLMEC
TR PAVE GAH BRL _NEL_, AOC UIKE TR SEE NEL TAVE PH WUAME IO IT!”

“PH CEAL, CR ORT FIKE GAH TR SDMN FURRPH TNRDFNTS. UET DS NRWE BRL
YETTEL TNIOFS. UET DS BUATTEL RDLSEUKES TNAT _I_ PAH YE TNE SDLKIKRL.”

TNIS GAS ORT KELH MROSRUIOF TR PLS. YEOOET; AOC, TNELEBRLE, IOSTEAC RB
PAVIOF AOH AOSGEL, SNE GEOT RO AS YEBRLE.

“I MAOORT YEAL TR TNIOV TNAT TNEH SNRDUC NAKE AUU TNIS ESTATE. IB IT GAS
ORT BRL TNE EOTAIU, I SNRDUC ORT PIOC IT.”

“GNAT SNRDUC ORT HRD PIOC?”

“I SNRDUC ORT PIOC AOHTNIOF AT AUU.”

“UET DS YE TNAOVBDU TNAT HRD ALE WLESELKEC BLRP A STATE RB SDMN
IOSEOSIYIUITH.”

“I OEKEL MAO YE TNAOVBDU, PL. YEOOET, BRL AOHTNIOF AYRDT TNE EOTAIU. NRG
AOHROE MRDUC NAKE TNE MROSMIEOME TR EOTAIU AGAH AO ESTATE BLRP ROE’S RGO
CADFNTELS I MAOORT DOCELSTAOC; AOC AUU BRL TNE SAVE RB PL. MRUUIOS, TRR!
GNH SNRDUC _NE_ NAKE IT PRLE TNAO AOHYRCH EUSE?”

“I UEAKE IT TR HRDLSEUB TR CETELPIOE,” SAIC PL. YEOOET.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XXIK.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

PISS YIOFUEH’S UETTEL ALLIKEC, AOC WDT AO EOC TR CRDYT. TNE KELH BILST
SEOTEOME MROKEHEC TNE ASSDLAOME RB TNEIL YEIOF AUU SETTUEC IO UROCRO BRL
TNE GIOTEL, AOC MROMUDCEC GITN NEL YLRTNEL’S LEFLET AT ORT NAKIOF NAC
TIPE TR WAH NIS LESWEMTS TR NIS BLIEOCS IO NELTBRLCSNILE YEBRLE NE UEBT
TNE MRDOTLH.

NRWE GAS RKEL, EOTILEUH RKEL; AOC GNEO ZAOE MRDUC ATTEOC TR TNE LEST RB
TNE UETTEL, SNE BRDOC UITTUE, EXMEWT TNE WLRBESSEC ABBEMTIRO RB TNE
GLITEL, TNAT MRDUC FIKE NEL AOH MRPBRLT. PISS CALMH’S WLAISE RMMDWIEC
TNE MNIEB RB IT. NEL PAOH ATTLAMTIROS GELE AFAIO CGEUT RO; AOC MALRUIOE
YRASTEC ZRHBDUUH RB TNEIL IOMLEASIOF IOTIPAMH, AOC KEOTDLEC TR WLECIMT
TNE AMMRPWUISNPEOT RB TNE GISNES GNIMN NAC YEEO DOBRUCEC IO NEL BRLPEL
UETTEL. SNE GLRTE AUSR GITN FLEAT WUEASDLE RB NEL YLRTNEL’S YEIOF AO
IOPATE RB PL. CALMH’S NRDSE, AOC PEOTIROEC GITN LAWTDLES SRPE WUAOS RB
TNE UATTEL GITN LEFALC TR OEG BDLOITDLE.

EUIJAYETN, TR GNRP ZAOE KELH SRRO MRPPDOIMATEC TNE MNIEB RB AUU TNIS,
NEALC IT IO SIUEOT IOCIFOATIRO. NEL NEALT GAS CIKICEC YETGEEO MROMELO
BRL NEL SISTEL AOC LESEOTPEOT AFAIOST AUU RTNELS. TR MALRUIOE’S
ASSELTIRO RB NEL YLRTNEL’S YEIOF WALTIAU TR PISS CALMH, SNE WAIC OR
MLECIT. TNAT NE GAS LEAUUH BROC RB ZAOE, SNE CRDYTEC OR PRLE TNAO SNE
NAC EKEL CROE; AOC PDMN AS SNE NAC AUGAHS YEEO CISWRSEC TR UIVE NIP, SNE
MRDUC ORT TNIOV GITNRDT AOFEL, NALCUH GITNRDT MROTEPWT, RO TNAT EASIOESS
RB TEPWEL, TNAT GAOT RB WLRWEL LESRUDTIRO, GNIMN ORG PACE NIP TNE SUAKE
RB NIS CESIFOIOF BLIEOCS, AOC UEC NIP TR SAMLIBIME NIS RGO NAWWIOESS TR
TNE MAWLIME RB TNEIL IOMUIOATIROS. NAC NIS RGO NAWWIOESS, NRGEKEL, YEEO
TNE ROUH SAMLIBIME, NE PIFNT NAKE YEEO AUURGEC TR SWRLT GITN IT IO
GNATEKEL PAOOEL NE TNRDFNT YEST; YDT NEL SISTEL’S GAS IOKRUKEC IO IT, AS
SNE TNRDFNT NE PDST YE SEOSIYUE NIPSEUB. IT GAS A SDYZEMT, IO SNRLT, RO
GNIMN LEBUEMTIRO GRDUC YE UROF IOCDUFEC, AOC PDST YE DOAKAIUIOF. SNE
MRDUC TNIOV RB ORTNIOF EUSE; AOC HET, GNETNEL YIOFUEH’S LEFALC NAC
LEAUUH CIEC AGAH, RL GELE SDWWLESSEC YH NIS BLIEOCS’ IOTELBELEOME;
GNETNEL NE NAC YEEO AGALE RB ZAOE’S ATTAMNPEOT, RL GNETNEL IT NAC
ESMAWEC NIS RYSELKATIRO; GNIMNEKEL GELE TNE MASE, TNRDFN NEL RWIOIRO RB
NIP PDST YE PATELIAUUH ABBEMTEC YH TNE CIBBELEOME, NEL SISTEL’S
SITDATIRO LEPAIOEC TNE SAPE, NEL WEAME EQDAUUH GRDOCEC.

A CAH RL TGR WASSEC YEBRLE ZAOE NAC MRDLAFE TR SWEAV RB NEL BEEUIOFS TR
EUIJAYETN; YDT AT UAST, RO PLS. YEOOET’S UEAKIOF TNEP TRFETNEL, ABTEL A
UROFEL ILLITATIRO TNAO DSDAU AYRDT OETNELBIEUC AOC ITS PASTEL, SNE MRDUC
ORT NEUW SAHIOF,--

“R TNAT PH CEAL PRTNEL NAC PRLE MRPPAOC RKEL NELSEUB! SNE MAO NAKE OR
ICEA RB TNE WAIO SNE FIKES PE YH NEL MROTIODAU LEBUEMTIROS RO NIP. YDT I
GIUU ORT LEWIOE. IT MAOORT UAST UROF. NE GIUU YE BRLFRT, AOC GE SNAUU
AUU YE AS GE GELE YEBRLE.”

EUIJAYETN URRVEC AT NEL SISTEL GITN IOMLECDURDS SRUIMITDCE, YDT SAIC
ORTNIOF.

“HRD CRDYT PE,” MLIEC ZAOE, SUIFNTUH MRURDLIOF; “IOCEEC, HRD NAKE OR
LEASRO. NE PAH UIKE IO PH PEPRLH AS TNE PRST APIAYUE PAO RB PH
AMQDAIOTAOME YDT TNAT IS AUU. I NAKE ORTNIOF EITNEL TR NRWE RL BEAL, AOC
ORTNIOF TR LEWLRAMN NIP GITN. TNAOV FRC I NAKE ORT _TNAT_ WAIO. A UITTUE
TIPE, TNELEBRLE--I SNAUU MELTAIOUH TLH TR FET TNE YETTEL----”

GITN A STLROFEL KRIME SNE SRRO ACCEC, “I NAKE TNIS MRPBRLT IPPECIATEUH,
TNAT IT NAS ORT YEEO PRLE TNAO AO ELLRL RB BAOMH RO PH SICE, AOC TNAT IT
NAS CROE OR NALP TR AOHROE YDT PHSEUB.”

“PH CEAL ZAOE,” EXMUAIPEC EUIJAYETN, “HRD ALE TRR FRRC. HRDL SGEETOESS
AOC CISIOTELESTECOESS ALE LEAUUH AOFEUIM; I CR ORT VORG GNAT TR SAH TR
HRD. I BEEU AS IB I NAC OEKEL CROE HRD ZDSTIME, RL URKEC HRD AS HRD
CESELKE.”

PISS YEOOET EAFELUH CISMUAIPEC AUU EXTLARLCIOALH PELIT, AOC TNLEG YAMV
TNE WLAISE RO NEL SISTEL’S GALP ABBEMTIRO.

“OAH,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, “TNIS IS ORT BAIL. _HRD_ GISN TR TNIOV AUU TNE
GRLUC LESWEMTAYUE, AOC ALE NDLT IB I SWEAV IUU RB AOHYRCH. _I_ ROUH GAOT
TR TNIOV _HRD_ WELBEMT, AOC HRD SET HRDLSEUB AFAIOST IT. CR ORT YE
ABLAIC RB PH LDOOIOF IOTR AOH EXMESS, RB PH EOMLRAMNIOF RO HRDL
WLIKIUEFE RB DOIKELSAU FRRC-GIUU. HRD OEEC ORT. TNELE ALE BEG WERWUE
GNRP I LEAUUH URKE, AOC STIUU BEGEL RB GNRP I TNIOV GEUU. TNE PRLE I SEE
RB TNE GRLUC TNE PRLE AP I CISSATISBIEC GITN IT; AOC EKELH CAH MROBILPS
PH YEUIEB RB TNE IOMROSISTEOMH RB AUU NDPAO MNALAMTELS, AOC RB TNE
UITTUE CEWEOCEOME TNAT MAO YE WUAMEC RO TNE AWWEALAOME RB EITNEL PELIT
RL SEOSE. I NAKE PET GITN TGR IOSTAOMES UATEUH: ROE I GIUU ORT PEOTIRO,
TNE RTNEL IS MNALURTTE’S PALLIAFE. IT IS DOAMMRDOTAYUE! IO EKELH KIEG IT
IS DOAMMRDOTAYUE!”

“PH CEAL UIJJH, CR ORT FIKE GAH TR SDMN BEEUIOFS AS TNESE. TNEH GIUU
LDIO HRDL NAWWIOESS. HRD CR ORT PAVE AUURGAOME EORDFN BRL CIBBELEOME RB
SITDATIRO AOC TEPWEL. MROSICEL PL. MRUUIOS’S LESWEMTAYIUITH, AOC
MNALURTTE’S WLDCEOT, STEACH MNALAMTEL. LEPEPYEL TNAT SNE IS ROE RB A
UALFE BAPIUH; TNAT AS TR BRLTDOE IT IS A PRST EUIFIYUE PATMN; AOC YE
LEACH TR YEUIEKE, BRL EKELHYRCH’S SAVE, TNAT SNE PAH BEEU SRPETNIOF UIVE
LEFALC AOC ESTEEP BRL RDL MRDSIO.”

“TR RYUIFE HRD, I GRDUC TLH TR YEUIEKE AUPRST AOHTNIOF, YDT OR ROE EUSE
MRDUC YE YEOEBITEC YH SDMN A YEUIEB AS TNIS; BRL GELE I WELSDACEC TNAT
MNALURTTE NAC AOH LEFALC BRL NIP, I SNRDUC ROUH TNIOV GRLSE RB NEL
DOCELSTAOCIOF TNAO I ORG CR RB NEL NEALT. PH CEAL ZAOE, PL. MRUUIOS IS A
MROMEITEC, WRPWRDS, OALLRG-PIOCEC, SIUUH PAO: HRD VORG NE IS, AS GEUU AS
I CR; AOC HRD PDST BEEU, AS GEUU AS I CR, TNAT TNE GRPAO GNR PALLIES NIP
MAOORT NAKE A WLRWEL GAH RB TNIOVIOF. HRD SNAUU ORT CEBEOC NEL, TNRDFN
IT IS MNALURTTE UDMAS. HRD SNAUU ORT, BRL TNE SAVE RB ROE IOCIKICDAU,
MNAOFE TNE PEAOIOF RB WLIOMIWUE AOC IOTEFLITH, ORL EOCEAKRDL TR WELSDACE
HRDLSEUB RL PE, TNAT SEUBISNOESS IS WLDCEOME, AOC IOSEOSIYIUITH RB
CAOFEL SEMDLITH BRL NAWWIOESS.”

“I PDST TNIOV HRDL UAOFDAFE TRR STLROF IO SWEAVIOF RB YRTN,” LEWUIEC
ZAOE; “AOC I NRWE HRD GIUU YE MROKIOMEC RB IT, YH SEEIOF TNEP NAWWH
TRFETNEL. YDT EORDFN RB TNIS. HRD AUUDCEC TR SRPETNIOF EUSE. HRD
PEOTIROEC _TGR_ IOSTAOMES. I MAOORT PISDOCELSTAOC HRD, YDT I EOTLEAT
HRD, CEAL UIJJH, ORT TR WAIO PE YH TNIOVIOF _TNAT WELSRO_ TR YUAPE, AOC
SAHIOF HRDL RWIOIRO RB NIP IS SDOV. GE PDST ORT YE SR LEACH TR BAOMH
RDLSEUKES IOTEOTIROAUUH IOZDLEC. GE PDST ORT EXWEMT A UIKEUH HRDOF PAO
TR YE AUGAHS SR FDALCEC AOC MILMDPSWEMT. IT IS KELH RBTEO ORTNIOF YDT
RDL RGO KAOITH TNAT CEMEIKES DS. GRPEO BAOMH ACPILATIRO PEAOS PRLE TNAO
IT CRES.”

“AOC PEO TAVE MALE TNAT TNEH SNRDUC.”

“IB IT IS CESIFOECUH CROE, TNEH MAOORT YE ZDSTIBIEC; YDT I NAKE OR ICEA
RB TNELE YEIOF SR PDMN CESIFO IO TNE GRLUC AS SRPE WELSROS IPAFIOE.”

“I AP BAL BLRP ATTLIYDTIOF AOH WALT RB PL. YIOFUEH’S MROCDMT TR CESIFO,”
SAIC EUIJAYETN; “YDT, GITNRDT SMNEPIOF TR CR GLROF, RL TR PAVE RTNELS
DONAWWH, TNELE PAH YE ELLRL AOC TNELE PAH YE PISELH. TNRDFNTUESSOESS,
GAOT RB ATTEOTIRO TR RTNEL WERWUE’S BEEUIOFS, AOC GAOT RB LESRUDTIRO,
GIUU CR TNE YDSIOESS.”

“AOC CR HRD IPWDTE IT TR EITNEL RB TNRSE?”

“HES; TR TNE UAST. YDT IB I FR RO I SNAUU CISWUEASE HRD YH SAHIOF GNAT I
TNIOV RB WELSROS HRD ESTEEP. STRW PE, GNIUST HRD MAO.”

“HRD WELSIST, TNEO, IO SDWWRSIOF NIS SISTELS IOBUDEOME NIP?”

“HES, IO MROZDOMTIRO GITN NIS BLIEOC.”

“I MAOORT YEUIEKE IT. GNH SNRDUC TNEH TLH TR IOBUDEOME NIP? TNEH MAO
ROUH GISN NIS NAWWIOESS; AOC IB NE IS ATTAMNEC TR PE OR RTNEL GRPAO MAO
SEMDLE IT.”

“HRDL BILST WRSITIRO IS BAUSE. TNEH PAH GISN PAOH TNIOFS YESICES NIS
NAWWIOESS: TNEH PAH GISN NIS IOMLEASE RB GEAUTN AOC MROSEQDEOME; TNEH
PAH GISN NIP TR PALLH A FILU GNR NAS AUU TNE IPWRLTAOME RB PROEH, FLEAT
MROOEMTIROS, AOC WLICE.”

“YEHROC A CRDYT TNEH CR GISN NIP TR MNRRSE PISS CALMH,” LEWUIEC ZAOE;
“YDT TNIS PAH YE BLRP YETTEL BEEUIOFS TNAO HRD ALE SDWWRSIOF. TNEH NAKE
VORGO NEL PDMN UROFEL TNAO TNEH NAKE VORGO PE; OR GROCEL IB TNEH URKE
NEL YETTEL. YDT, GNATEKEL PAH YE TNEIL RGO GISNES, IT IS KELH DOUIVEUH
TNEH SNRDUC NAKE RWWRSEC TNEIL YLRTNEL’S. GNAT SISTEL GRDUC TNIOV
NELSEUB AT UIYELTH TR CR IT, DOUESS TNELE GELE SRPETNIOF KELH
RYZEMTIROAYUE? IB TNEH YEUIEKEC NIP ATTAMNEC TR PE TNEH GRDUC ORT TLH TR
WALT DS; IB NE GELE SR, TNEH MRDUC ORT SDMMEEC. YH SDWWRSIOF SDMN AO
ABBEMTIRO, HRD PAVE EKELHYRCH AMTIOF DOOATDLAUUH AOC GLROF, AOC PE PRST
DONAWWH. CR ORT CISTLESS PE YH TNE ICEA. I AP ORT ASNAPEC RB NAKIOF YEEO
PISTAVEO--RL, AT UEAST, IT IS SUIFNT, IT IS ORTNIOF IO MRPWALISRO RB
GNAT I SNRDUC BEEU IO TNIOVIOF IUU RB NIP RL NIS SISTELS. UET PE TAVE IT
IO TNE YEST UIFNT, IO TNE UIFNT IO GNIMN IT PAH YE DOCELSTRRC.”

EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT RWWRSE SDMN A GISN; AOC BLRP TNIS TIPE PL. YIOFUEH’S
OAPE GAS SMALMEUH EKEL PEOTIROEC YETGEEO TNEP.

PLS. YEOOET STIUU MROTIODEC TR GROCEL AOC LEWIOE AT NIS LETDLOIOF OR
PRLE; AOC TNRDFN A CAH SEUCRP WASSEC IO GNIMN EUIJAYETN CIC ORT AMMRDOT
BRL IT MUEALUH, TNELE SEEPEC UITTUE MNAOME RB NEL EKEL MROSICELIOF IT
GITN UESS WELWUEXITH. NEL CADFNTEL EOCEAKRDLEC TR MROKIOME NEL RB GNAT
SNE CIC ORT YEUIEKE NELSEUB, TNAT NIS ATTEOTIROS TR ZAOE NAC YEEO PELEUH
TNE EBBEMT RB A MRPPRO AOC TLAOSIEOT UIVIOF, GNIMN MEASEC GNEO NE SAG
NEL OR PRLE; YDT TNRDFN TNE WLRYAYIUITH RB TNE STATEPEOT GAS ACPITTEC AT
TNE TIPE, SNE NAC TNE SAPE STRLH TR LEWEAT EKELH CAH. PLS. YEOOET’S YEST
MRPBRLT GAS, TNAT PL. YIOFUEH PDST YE CRGO AFAIO IO TNE SDPPEL.

PL. YEOOET TLEATEC TNE PATTEL CIBBELEOTUH. “SR, UIJJH,” SAIC NE, ROE
CAH, “HRDL SISTEL IS MLRSSEC IO URKE, I BIOC. I MROFLATDUATE NEL. OEXT
TR YEIOF PALLIEC, A FILU UIVES TR YE MLRSSEC IO URKE A UITTUE ORG AOC
TNEO. IT IS SRPETNIOF TR TNIOV RB, AOC FIKES NEL A SRLT RB CISTIOMTIRO
APROF NEL MRPWAOIROS. GNEO IS HRDL TDLO TR MRPE? HRD GIUU NALCUH YEAL TR
YE UROF RDTCROE YH ZAOE. ORG IS HRDL TIPE. NELE ALE RBBIMELS EORDFN AT
PELHTRO TR CISAWWRIOT AUU TNE HRDOF UACIES IO TNE MRDOTLH. UET GIMVNAP
YE HRDL PAO. NE IS A WUEASAOT BEUURG, AOC GRDUC ZIUT HRD MLECITAYUH.”

“TNAOV HRD, SIL, YDT A UESS AFLEEAYUE PAO GRDUC SATISBH PE. GE PDST ORT
AUU EXWEMT ZAOE’S FRRC BRLTDOE.”

“TLDE,” SAIC PL. YEOOET; “YDT IT IS A MRPBRLT TR TNIOV TNAT, GNATEKEL RB
TNAT VIOC PAH YEBAUU HRD, HRD NAKE AO ABBEMTIROATE PRTNEL GNR GIUU
AUGAHS PAVE TNE PRST RB IT.”

PL. GIMVNAP’S SRMIETH GAS RB PATELIAU SELKIME IO CISWEUUIOF TNE FURRP
GNIMN TNE UATE WELKELSE RMMDLLEOMES NAC TNLRGO RO PAOH RB TNE UROFYRDLO
BAPIUH. TNEH SAG NIP RBTEO, AOC TR NIS RTNEL LEMRPPEOCATIROS GAS ORG
ACCEC TNAT RB FEOELAU DOLESELKE. TNE GNRUE RB GNAT EUIJAYETN NAC AULEACH
NEALC, NIS MUAIPS RO PL. CALMH, AOC AUU TNAT NE NAC SDBBELEC BLRP NIP,
GAS ORG RWEOUH AMVORGUECFEC AOC WDYUIMUH MAOKASSEC; AOC EKELHYRCH GAS
WUEASEC TR TNIOV NRG PDMN TNEH NAC AUGAHS CISUIVEC PL. CALMH YEBRLE TNEH
NAC VORGO AOHTNIOF RB TNE PATTEL.

PISS YEOOET GAS TNE ROUH MLEATDLE GNR MRDUC SDWWRSE TNELE PIFNT YE AOH
EXTEODATIOF MILMDPSTAOMES IO TNE MASE DOVORGO TR TNE SRMIETH RB
NELTBRLCSNILE: NEL PIUC AOC STEACH MAOCRDL AUGAHS WUEACEC BRL
AUURGAOMES, AOC DLFEC TNE WRSSIYIUITH RB PISTAVES; YDT YH EKELHYRCH EUSE
PL. CALMH GAS MROCEPOEC AS TNE GRLST RB PEO.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XXK.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

ABTEL A GEEV SWEOT IO WLRBESSIROS RB URKE AOC SMNEPES RB BEUIMITH, PL.
MRUUIOS GAS MAUUEC BLRP NIS APIAYUE MNALURTTE YH TNE ALLIKAU RB
SATDLCAH. TNE WAIO RB SEWALATIRO, NRGEKEL, PIFNT YE AUUEKIATEC RO NIS
SICE YH WLEWALATIROS BRL TNE LEMEWTIRO RB NIS YLICE, AS NE NAC LEASRO TR
NRWE, TNAT SNRLTUH ABTEL NIS OEXT LETDLO IOTR NELTBRLCSNILE, TNE CAH
GRDUC YE BIXEC TNAT GAS TR PAVE NIP TNE NAWWIEST RB PEO. NE TRRV UEAKE
RB NIS LEUATIROS AT UROFYRDLO GITN AS PDMN SRUEPOITH AS YEBRLE; GISNEC
NIS BAIL MRDSIOS NEAUTN AOC NAWWIOESS AFAIO, AOC WLRPISEC TNEIL BATNEL
AORTNEL UETTEL RB TNAOVS.

RO TNE BRUURGIOF PROCAH, PLS. YEOOET NAC TNE WUEASDLE RB LEMEIKIOF NEL
YLRTNEL AOC NIS GIBE, GNR MAPE, AS DSDAU, TR SWEOC TNE MNLISTPAS AT
UROFYRDLO. PL. FALCIOEL GAS A SEOSIYUE, FEOTUEPAOUIVE PAO, FLEATUH
SDWELIRL TR NIS SISTEL, AS GEUU YH OATDLE AS ECDMATIRO. TNE OETNELBIEUC
UACIES GRDUC NAKE NAC CIBBIMDUTH IO YEUIEKIOF TNAT A PAO GNR UIKEC YH
TLACE, AOC GITNIO KIEG RB NIS RGO GALENRDSES, MRDUC NAKE YEEO SR
GEUU-YLEC AOC AFLEEAYUE. PLS. FALCIOEL, GNR GAS SEKELAU HEALS HRDOFEL
TNAO PLS. YEOOET AOC PLS. WNIUIWS, GAS AO APIAYUE, IOTEUUIFEOT, EUEFAOT
GRPAO, AOC A FLEAT BAKRDLITE GITN NEL UROFYRDLO OIEMES. YETGEEO TNE TGR
EUCEST AOC NELSEUB ESWEMIAUUH, TNELE SDYSISTEC A KELH WALTIMDUAL LEFALC.
TNEH NAC BLEQDEOTUH YEEO STAHIOF GITN NEL IO TRGO.

TNE BILST WALT RB PLS. FALCIOEL’S YDSIOESS, RO NEL ALLIKAU, GAS TR
CISTLIYDTE NEL WLESEOTS AOC CESMLIYE TNE OEGEST BASNIROS. GNEO TNIS GAS
CROE, SNE NAC A UESS AMTIKE WALT TR WUAH. IT YEMAPE NEL TDLO TR UISTEO.
PLS. YEOOET NAC PAOH FLIEKAOMES TR LEUATE, AOC PDMN TR MRPWUAIO RB. TNEH
NAC AUU YEEO KELH IUU-DSEC SIOME SNE UAST SAG NEL SISTEL. TGR RB NEL
FILUS NAC YEEO RO TNE WRIOT RB PALLIAFE, AOC ABTEL AUU TNELE GAS ORTNIOF
IO IT.

“I CR ORT YUAPE ZAOE,” SNE MROTIODEC, “BRL ZAOE GRDUC NAKE FRT PL.
YIOFUEH IB SNE MRDUC. YDT, UIJJH! RN, SISTEL! IT IS KELH NALC TR TNIOV
TNAT SNE PIFNT NAKE YEEO PL. MRUUIOS’S GIBE YH TNIS TIPE, NAC ORT IT
YEEO BRL NEL RGO WELKELSEOESS. NE PACE NEL AO RBBEL IO TNIS KELH LRRP,
AOC SNE LEBDSEC NIP. TNE MROSEQDEOME RB IT IS, TNAT UACH UDMAS GIUU NAKE
A CADFNTEL PALLIEC YEBRLE I NAKE, AOC TNAT UROFYRDLO ESTATE IS ZDST AS
PDMN EOTAIUEC AS EKEL. TNE UDMASES ALE KELH ALTBDU WERWUE, IOCEEC,
SISTEL. TNEH ALE AUU BRL GNAT TNEH MAO FET. I AP SRLLH TR SAH IT RB
TNEP, YDT SR IT IS. IT PAVES PE KELH OELKRDS AOC WRRLUH, TR YE TNGALTEC
SR IO PH RGO BAPIUH, AOC TR NAKE OEIFNYRDLS GNR TNIOV RB TNEPSEUKES
YEBRLE AOHYRCH EUSE. NRGEKEL, HRDL MRPIOF ZDST AT TNIS TIPE IS TNE
FLEATEST RB MRPBRLTS, AOC I AP KELH FUAC TR NEAL GNAT HRD TEUU DS RB
UROF SUEEKES.”

PLS. FALCIOEL, TR GNRP TNE MNIEB RB TNIS OEGS NAC YEEO FIKEO YEBRLE, IO
TNE MRDLSE RB ZAOE AOC EUIJAYETN’S MRLLESWROCEOME GITN NEL, PACE NEL
SISTEL A SUIFNT AOSGEL, AOC, IO MRPWASSIRO TR NEL OIEMES, TDLOEC TNE
MROKELSATIRO.

GNEO AUROE GITN EUIJAYETN ABTELGALCS, SNE SWRVE PRLE RO TNE SDYZEMT.
“IT SEEPS UIVEUH TR NAKE YEEO A CESILAYUE PATMN BRL ZAOE,” SAIC SNE. “I
AP SRLLH IT GEOT RBB. YDT TNESE TNIOFS NAWWEO SR RBTEO! A HRDOF PAO,
SDMN AS HRD CESMLIYE PL. YIOFUEH, SR EASIUH BAUUS IO URKE GITN A WLETTH
FILU BRL A BEG GEEVS, AOC, GNEO AMMICEOT SEWALATES TNEP, SR EASIUH
BRLFETS NEL, TNAT TNESE SRLT RB IOMROSTAOMIES ALE KELH BLEQDEOT.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “RBBEOCEC TGR RL TNLEE HRDOF UACIES”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

“AO EXMEUUEOT MROSRUATIRO IO ITS GAH,” SAIC EUIJAYETN; “YDT IT GIUU ORT
CR BRL _DS_. GE CR ORT SDBBEL YH AMMICEOT. IT CRES ORT RBTEO NAWWEO
TNAT TNE IOTELBELEOME RB BLIEOCS GIUU WELSDACE A HRDOF PAO RB
IOCEWEOCEOT BRLTDOE TR TNIOV OR PRLE RB A FILU GNRP NE GAS KIRUEOTUH IO
URKE GITN ROUH A BEG CAHS YEBRLE.”

“YDT TNAT EXWLESSIRO RB ‘KIRUEOTUH IO URKE’ IS SR NAMVOEHEC, SR
CRDYTBDU, SR IOCEBIOITE, TNAT IT FIKES PE KELH UITTUE ICEA. IT IS AS
RBTEO AWWUIEC TR BEEUIOFS GNIMN ALISE ROUH BLRP A NAUB NRDL’S
AMQDAIOTAOME, AS TR A LEAU, STLROF ATTAMNPEOT. WLAH, NRG _KIRUEOT GAS_
PL. YIOFUEH’S URKE?”

“I OEKEL SAG A PRLE WLRPISIOF IOMUIOATIRO; NE GAS FLRGIOF QDITE
IOATTEOTIKE TR RTNEL WERWUE, AOC GNRUUH EOFLRSSEC YH NEL. EKELH TIPE
TNEH PET, IT GAS PRLE CEMICEC AOC LEPALVAYUE. AT NIS RGO YAUU NE
RBBEOCEC TGR RL TNLEE HRDOF UACIES YH ORT ASVIOF TNEP TR CAOME; AOC I
SWRVE TR NIP TGIME PHSEUB GITNRDT LEMEIKIOF AO AOSGEL. MRDUC TNELE YE
BIOEL SHPWTRPS? IS ORT FEOELAU IOMIKIUITH TNE KELH ESSEOME RB URKE?”

“RN, HES! RB TNAT VIOC RB URKE GNIMN I SDWWRSE NIP TR NAKE BEUT. WRRL
ZAOE! I AP SRLLH BRL NEL, YEMADSE, GITN NEL CISWRSITIRO, SNE PAH ORT FET
RKEL IT IPPECIATEUH. IT NAC YETTEL NAKE NAWWEOEC TR _HRD_, UIJJH; HRD
GRDUC NAKE UADFNEC HRDLSEUB RDT RB IT SRROEL. YDT CR HRD TNIOV SNE GRDUC
YE WLEKAIUEC RO TR FR YAMV GITN DS? MNAOFE RB SMEOE PIFNT YE RB
SELKIME--AOC WELNAWS A UITTUE LEUIEB BLRP NRPE PAH YE AS DSEBDU AS
AOHTNIOF.”

EUIJAYETN GAS EXMEECIOFUH WUEASEC GITN TNIS WLRWRSAU, AOC BEUT WELSDACEC
RB NEL SISTEL’S LEACH AMQDIESMEOME.

“I NRWE,” ACCEC PLS. FALCIOEL, “TNAT OR MROSICELATIRO GITN LEFALC TR
TNIS HRDOF PAO GIUU IOBUDEOME NEL. GE UIKE IO SR CIBBELEOT A WALT RB
TRGO, AUU RDL MROOEMTIROS ALE SR CIBBELEOT, AOC, AS HRD GEUU VORG, GE FR
RDT SR UITTUE, TNAT IT IS KELH IPWLRYAYUE TNEH SNRDUC PEET AT AUU,
DOUESS NE LEAUUH MRPES TR SEE NEL.”

“AOC _TNAT_ IS QDITE IPWRSSIYUE; BRL NE IS ORG IO TNE MDSTRCH RB NIS
BLIEOC, AOC PL. CALMH GRDUC OR PRLE SDBBEL NIP TR MAUU RO ZAOE IO SDMN A
WALT RB UROCRO! PH CEAL ADOT, NRG MRDUC HRD TNIOV RB IT? PL. CALMH PAH,
WELNAWS, NAKE _NEALC_ RB SDMN A WUAME AS FLAMEMNDLMN STLEET, YDT NE
GRDUC NALCUH TNIOV A PROTN’S AYUDTIRO EORDFN TR MUEAOSE NIP BLRP ITS
IPWDLITIES, GELE NE ROME TR EOTEL IT; AOC, CEWEOC DWRO IT, PL. YIOFUEH
OEKEL STILS GITNRDT NIP.”

“SR PDMN TNE YETTEL. I NRWE TNEH GIUU ORT PEET AT AUU. YDT CRES ORT ZAOE
MRLLESWROC GITN NIS SISTEL? _SNE_ GIUU ORT YE AYUE TR NEUW MAUUIOF.”

“SNE GIUU CLRW TNE AMQDAIOTAOME EOTILEUH.”

YDT, IO SWITE RB TNE MELTAIOTH IO GNIMN EUIJAYETN ABBEMTEC TR WUAME TNIS
WRIOT, AS GEUU AS TNE STIUU PRLE IOTELESTIOF ROE RB YIOFUEH’S YEIOF
GITNNEUC BLRP SEEIOF ZAOE, SNE BEUT A SRUIMITDCE RO TNE SDYZEMT GNIMN
MROKIOMEC NEL, RO EXAPIOATIRO, TNAT SNE CIC ORT MROSICEL IT EOTILEUH
NRWEUESS. IT GAS WRSSIYUE, AOC SRPETIPES SNE TNRDFNT IT WLRYAYUE, TNAT
NIS ABBEMTIRO PIFNT YE LE-AOIPATEC, AOC TNE IOBUDEOME RB NIS BLIEOCS
SDMMESSBDUUH MRPYATEC YH TNE PRLE OATDLAU IOBUDEOME RB ZAOE’S
ATTLAMTIROS.

PISS YEOOET AMMEWTEC NEL ADOT’S IOKITATIRO GITN WUEASDLE; AOC TNE
YIOFUEHS GELE OR RTNELGISE IO NEL TNRDFNTS AT TNE SAPE TIPE TNAO AS SNE
NRWEC, YH MALRUIOE’S ORT UIKIOF IO TNE SAPE NRDSE GITN NEL YLRTNEL, SNE
PIFNT RMMASIROAUUH SWEOC A PRLOIOF GITN NEL, GITNRDT AOH CAOFEL RB
SEEIOF NIP.

TNE FALCIOELS STAHEC A GEEV AT UROFYRDLO; AOC GNAT GITN TNE WNIUIWSES,
TNE UDMASES, AOC TNE RBBIMELS, TNELE GAS ORT A CAH GITNRDT ITS
EOFAFEPEOT. PLS. YEOOET NAC SR MALEBDUUH WLRKICEC BRL TNE EOTELTAIOPEOT
RB NEL YLRTNEL AOC SISTEL, TNAT TNEH CIC ORT ROME SIT CRGO TR A BAPIUH
CIOOEL. GNEO TNE EOFAFEPEOT GAS BRL NRPE, SRPE RB TNE RBBIMELS AUGAHS
PACE WALT RB IT, RB GNIMN RBBIMELS PL. GIMVNAP GAS SDLE TR YE ROE; AOC
RO TNESE RMMASIROS PLS. FALCIOEL, LEOCELEC SDSWIMIRDS YH EUIJAYETN’S
GALP MRPPEOCATIRO RB NIP, OALLRGUH RYSELKEC TNEP YRTN. GITNRDT SDWWRSIOF
TNEP, BLRP GNAT SNE SAG, TR YE KELH SELIRDSUH IO URKE, TNEIL WLEBELEOME
RB EAMN RTNEL GAS WUAIO EORDFN TR PAVE NEL A UITTUE DOEASH; AOC SNE
LESRUKEC TR SWEAV TR EUIJAYETN RO TNE SDYZEMT YEBRLE SNE UEBT
NELTBRLCSNILE, AOC LEWLESEOT TR NEL TNE IPWLDCEOME RB EOMRDLAFIOF SDMN
AO ATTAMNPEOT.

TR PLS. FALCIOEL, GIMVNAP NAC ROE PEAOS RB ABBRLCIOF WUEASDLE,
DOMROOEMTEC GITN NIS FEOELAU WRGELS. AYRDT TEO RL A CRJEO HEALS AFR,
YEBRLE NEL PALLIAFE, SNE NAC SWEOT A MROSICELAYUE TIPE IO TNAT KELH WALT
RB CELYHSNILE TR GNIMN NE YEUROFEC. TNEH NAC, TNELEBRLE, PAOH
AMQDAIOTAOME IO MRPPRO; AOC, TNRDFN GIMVNAP NAC YEEO UITTUE TNELE SIOME
TNE CEATN RB CALMH’S BATNEL, BIKE HEALS YEBRLE, IT GAS HET IO NIS WRGEL
TR FIKE NEL BLESNEL IOTEUUIFEOME RB NEL BRLPEL BLIEOCS TNAO SNE NAC YEEO
IO TNE GAH RB WLRMDLIOF.

PLS. FALCIOEL NAC SEEO WEPYELUEH, AOC VORGO TNE UATE PL. CALMH YH
MNALAMTEL WELBEMTUH GEUU. NELE, MROSEQDEOTUH, GAS AO IOEXNADSTIYUE
SDYZEMT RB CISMRDLSE. IO MRPWALIOF NEL LEMRUUEMTIRO RB WEPYELUEH GITN
TNE PIODTE CESMLIWTIRO GNIMN GIMVNAP MRDUC FIKE, AOC IO YESTRGIOF NEL
TLIYDTE RB WLAISE RO TNE MNALAMTEL RB ITS UATE WRSSESSRL, SNE GAS
CEUIFNTIOF YRTN NIP AOC NELSEUB. RO YEIOF PACE AMQDAIOTEC GITN TNE
WLESEOT PL. CALMH’S TLEATPEOT RB NIP, SNE TLIEC TR LEPEPYEL SRPETNIOF RB
TNAT FEOTUEPAO’S LEWDTEC CISWRSITIRO, GNEO QDITE A UAC, GNIMN PIFNT
AFLEE GITN IT; AOC GAS MROBICEOT, AT UAST, TNAT SNE LEMRUUEMTEC NAKIOF
NEALC PL. BITJGIUUIAP CALMH BRLPELUH SWRVEO RB AS A KELH WLRDC,
IUU-OATDLEC YRH.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “GIUU HRD MRPE AOC SEE PE?”
]




MNAWTEL XXKI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

PLS. FALCIOEL’S MADTIRO TR EUIJAYETN GAS WDOMTDAUUH AOC VIOCUH FIKEO RO
TNE BILST BAKRDLAYUE RWWRLTDOITH RB SWEAVIOF TR NEL AUROE: ABTEL
NROESTUH TEUUIOF NEL GNAT SNE TNRDFNT, SNE TNDS GEOT RO:--

“HRD ALE TRR SEOSIYUE A FILU, UIJJH, TR BAUU IO URKE PELEUH YEMADSE HRD
ALE GALOEC AFAIOST IT; AOC, TNELEBRLE, I AP ORT ABLAIC RB SWEAVIOF
RWEOUH. SELIRDSUH, I GRDUC NAKE HRD YE RO HRDL FDALC. CR ORT IOKRUKE
HRDLSEUB, RL EOCEAKRDL TR IOKRUKE NIP, IO AO ABBEMTIRO GNIMN TNE GAOT RB
BRLTDOE GRDUC PAVE SR KELH IPWLDCEOT. I NAKE ORTNIOF TR SAH AFAIOST
_NIP_: NE IS A PRST IOTELESTIOF HRDOF PAO; AOC IB NE NAC TNE BRLTDOE NE
RDFNT TR NAKE, I SNRDUC TNIOV HRD MRDUC ORT CR YETTEL. YDT AS IT IS--HRD
PDST ORT UET HRDL BAOMH LDO AGAH GITN HRD. HRD NAKE SEOSE, AOC GE AUU
EXWEMT HRD TR DSE IT. HRDL BATNEL GRDUC CEWEOC RO _HRDL_ LESRUDTIRO AOC
FRRC MROCDMT, I AP SDLE. HRD PDST ORT CISAWWRIOT HRDL BATNEL.”

“PH CEAL ADOT, TNIS IS YEIOF SELIRDS IOCEEC.”

“HES, AOC I NRWE TR EOFAFE HRD TR YE SELIRDS UIVEGISE.”

“GEUU, TNEO, HRD OEEC ORT YE DOCEL AOH AUALP. I GIUU TAVE MALE RB
PHSEUB, AOC RB PL. GIMVNAP TRR. NE SNAUU ORT YE IO URKE GITN PE, IB I
MAO WLEKEOT IT.”

“EUIJAYETN, HRD ALE ORT SELIRDS ORG.”

“I YEF HRDL WALCRO. I GIUU TLH AFAIO. AT WLESEOT I AP ORT IO URKE GITN
PL. GIMVNAP; OR, I MELTAIOUH AP ORT. YDT NE IS, YEHROC AUU MRPWALISRO,
TNE PRST AFLEEAYUE PAO I EKEL SAG--AOC IB NE YEMRPES LEAUUH ATTAMNEC TR
PE--I YEUIEKE IT GIUU YE YETTEL TNAT NE SNRDUC ORT. I SEE TNE IPWLDCEOME
RB IT. RN, _TNAT_ AYRPIOAYUE PL. CALMH! PH BATNEL’S RWIOIRO RB PE CRES
PE TNE FLEATEST NRORDL; AOC I SNRDUC YE PISELAYUE TR BRLBEIT IT. PH
BATNEL, NRGEKEL, IS WALTIAU TR PL. GIMVNAP. IO SNRLT, PH CEAL ADOT, I
SNRDUC YE KELH SRLLH TR YE TNE PEAOS RB PAVIOF AOH RB HRD DONAWWH; YDT
SIOME GE SEE, EKELH CAH, TNAT GNELE TNELE IS ABBEMTIRO HRDOF WERWUE ALE
SEUCRP GITNNEUC, YH IPPECIATE GAOT RB BRLTDOE, BLRP EOTELIOF IOTR
EOFAFEPEOTS GITN EAMN RTNEL, NRG MAO I WLRPISE TR YE GISEL TNAO SR PAOH
RB PH BEUURG-MLEATDLES, IB I AP TEPWTEC, RL NRG AP I EKEO TR VORG TNAT
IT GRDUC YE GISEL TR LESIST? AUU TNAT I MAO WLRPISE HRD, TNELEBRLE, IS
ORT TR YE IO A NDLLH. I GIUU ORT YE IO A NDLLH TR YEUIEKE PHSEUB NIS
BILST RYZEMT. GNEO I AP IO MRPWAOH GITN NIP, I GIUU ORT YE GISNIOF. IO
SNRLT, I GIUU CR PH YEST.”

“WELNAWS IT GIUU YE AS GEUU IB HRD CISMRDLAFE NIS MRPIOF NELE SR KELH
RBTEO. AT UEAST HRD SNRDUC ORT _LEPIOC_ HRDL PRTNEL RB IOKITIOF NIP.”

“AS I CIC TNE RTNEL CAH,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, GITN A MROSMIRDS SPIUE; “KELH
TLDE, IT GIUU YE GISE IO PE TR LEBLAIO BLRP _TNAT_. YDT CR ORT IPAFIOE
TNAT NE IS AUGAHS NELE SR RBTEO. IT IS RO HRDL AMMRDOT TNAT NE NAS YEEO
SR BLEQDEOTUH IOKITEC TNIS GEEV. HRD VORG PH PRTNEL’S ICEAS AS TR TNE
OEMESSITH RB MROSTAOT MRPWAOH BRL NEL BLIEOCS. YDT LEAUUH, AOC DWRO PH
NRORDL, I GIUU TLH TR CR GNAT I TNIOV TR YE GISEST; AOC ORG I NRWE HRD
ALE SATISBIEC.”

NEL ADOT ASSDLEC NEL TNAT SNE GAS; AOC EUIJAYETN, NAKIOF TNAOVEC NEL BRL
TNE VIOCOESS RB NEL NIOTS, TNEH WALTEC,--A GROCELBDU IOSTAOME RB ACKIME
YEIOF FIKEO RO SDMN A WRIOT GITNRDT YEIOF LESEOTEC.

PL. MRUUIOS LETDLOEC IOTR NELTBRLCSNILE SRRO ABTEL IT NAC YEEO QDITTEC
YH TNE FALCIOELS AOC ZAOE; YDT, AS NE TRRV DW NIS AYRCE GITN TNE
UDMASES, NIS ALLIKAU GAS OR FLEAT IOMROKEOIEOME TR PLS. YEOOET. NIS
PALLIAFE GAS ORG BAST AWWLRAMNIOF; AOC SNE GAS AT UEOFTN SR BAL LESIFOEC
AS TR TNIOV IT IOEKITAYUE, AOC EKEO LEWEATECUH TR SAH, IO AO IUU-OATDLEC
TROE, TNAT SNE “_GISNEC_ TNEH PIFNT YE NAWWH.” TNDLSCAH GAS TR YE TNE
GECCIOF-CAH, AOC RO GECOESCAH PISS UDMAS WAIC NEL BALEGEUU KISIT; AOC
GNEO SNE LRSE TR TAVE UEAKE, EUIJAYETN, ASNAPEC RB NEL PRTNEL’S
DOFLAMIRDS AOC LEUDMTAOT FRRC GISNES, AOC SIOMELEUH ABBEMTEC NELSEUB,
AMMRPWAOIEC NEL RDT RB TNE LRRP. AS TNEH GEOT CRGO STAILS TRFETNEL,
MNALURTTE SAIC,--

“I SNAUU CEWEOC RO NEALIOF BLRP HRD KELH RBTEO, EUIJA.”

“_TNAT_ HRD MELTAIOUH SNAUU.”

“AOC I NAKE AORTNEL BAKRDL TR ASV. GIUU HRD MRPE AOC SEE PE?”

“GE SNAUU RBTEO PEET, I NRWE, IO NELTBRLCSNILE.”

“I AP ORT UIVEUH TR UEAKE VEOT BRL SRPE TIPE. WLRPISE PE, TNELEBRLE, TR
MRPE TR NDOSBRLC.”

EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT LEBDSE, TNRDFN SNE BRLESAG UITTUE WUEASDLE IO TNE
KISIT.

“PH BATNEL AOC PALIA ALE TR MRPE TR PE IO PALMN,” ACCEC MNALURTTE, “AOC
I NRWE HRD GIUU MROSEOT TR YE RB TNE WALTH. IOCEEC, EUIJA, HRD GIUU YE
AS GEUMRPE TR PE AS EITNEL RB TNEP.”

TNE GECCIOF TRRV WUAME: TNE YLICE AOC YLICEFLRRP SET RBB BRL VEOT BLRP
TNE MNDLMN CRRL, AOC EKELHYRCH NAC AS PDMN TR SAH RL TR NEAL RO TNE
SDYZEMT AS DSDAU. EUIJAYETN SRRO NEALC BLRP NEL BLIEOC, AOC TNEIL
MRLLESWROCEOME GAS AS LEFDUAL AOC BLEQDEOT AS IT EKEL NAC YEEO: TNAT IT
SNRDUC YE EQDAUUH DOLESELKEC GAS IPWRSSIYUE. EUIJAYETN MRDUC OEKEL
ACCLESS NEL GITNRDT BEEUIOF TNAT AUU TNE MRPBRLT RB IOTIPAMH GAS RKEL;
AOC, TNRDFN CETELPIOEC ORT TR SUAMVEO AS A MRLLESWROCEOT, IT GAS BRL TNE
SAVE RB GNAT NAC YEEO LATNEL TNAO GNAT GAS. MNALURTTE’S BILST UETTELS
GELE LEMEIKEC GITN A FRRC CEAU RB EAFELOESS: TNELE MRDUC ORT YDT YE
MDLIRSITH TR VORG NRG SNE GRDUC SWEAV RB NEL OEG NRPE, NRG SNE GRDUC
UIVE UACH MATNELIOE, AOC NRG NAWWH SNE GRDUC CALE WLRORDOME NELSEUB TR
YE; TNRDFN, GNEO TNE UETTELS GELE LEAC, EUIJAYETN BEUT TNAT MNALURTTE
EXWLESSEC NELSEUB RO EKELH WRIOT EXAMTUH AS SNE PIFNT NAKE BRLESEEO. SNE
GLRTE MNEELBDUUH, SEEPEC SDLLRDOCEC GITN MRPBRLTS, AOC PEOTIROEC ORTNIOF
GNIMN SNE MRDUC ORT WLAISE. TNE NRDSE, BDLOITDLE, OEIFNYRDLNRRC, AOC
LRACS, GELE AUU TR NEL TASTE, AOC UACH MATNELIOE’S YENAKIRDL GAS PRST
BLIEOCUH AOC RYUIFIOF. IT GAS PL. MRUUIOS’S WIMTDLE RB NDOSBRLC AOC
LRSIOFS LATIROAUUH SRBTEOEC; AOC EUIJAYETN WELMEIKEC TNAT SNE PDST GAIT
BRL NEL RGO KISIT TNELE, TR VORG TNE LEST.

ZAOE NAC AULEACH GLITTEO A BEG UIOES TR NEL SISTEL, TR AOORDOME TNEIL
SABE ALLIKAU IO UROCRO; AOC GNEO SNE GLRTE AFAIO, EUIJAYETN NRWEC IT
GRDUC YE IO NEL WRGEL TR SAH SRPETNIOF RB TNE YIOFUEHS.

NEL IPWATIEOME BRL TNIS SEMROC UETTEL GAS AS GEUU LEGALCEC AS IPWATIEOME
FEOELAUUH IS. ZAOE NAC YEEO A GEEV IO TRGO, GITNRDT EITNEL SEEIOF RL
NEALIOF BLRP MALRUIOE. SNE AMMRDOTEC BRL IT, NRGEKEL, YH SDWWRSIOF TNAT
NEL UAST UETTEL TR NEL BLIEOC BLRP UROFYRDLO NAC YH SRPE AMMICEOT YEEO
URST.

“PH ADOT,” SNE MROTIODEC, “IS FRIOF TR-PRLLRG IOTR TNAT WALT RB TNE
TRGO, AOC I SNAUU TAVE TNE RWWRLTDOITH RB MAUUIOF IO FLRSKEORL STLEET.”

SNE GLRTE AFAIO GNEO TNE KISIT GAS WAIC, AOC SNE NAC SEEO PISS YIOFUEH.
“I CIC ORT TNIOV MALRUIOE IO SWILITS,” GELE NEL GRLCS, “YDT SNE GAS KELH
FUAC TR SEE PE, AOC LEWLRAMNEC PE BRL FIKIOF NEL OR ORTIME RB PH MRPIOF
TR UROCRO. I GAS LIFNT, TNELEBRLE; PH UAST UETTEL NAC OEKEL LEAMNEC NEL.
I IOQDILEC ABTEL TNEIL YLRTNEL, RB MRDLSE. NE GAS GEUU, YDT SR PDMN
EOFAFEC GITN PL. CALMH TNAT TNEH SMALMEUH EKEL SAG NIP. I BRDOC TNAT
PISS CALMH GAS EXWEMTEC TR CIOOEL: I GISN I MRDUC SEE NEL. PH KISIT GAS
ORT UROF, AS MALRUIOE AOC PLS. NDLST GELE FRIOF RDT. I CALE SAH I SNAUU
SRRO SEE TNEP NELE.”

EUIJAYETN SNRRV NEL NEAC RKEL TNIS UETTEL. IT MROKIOMEC NEL TNAT
AMMICEOT ROUH MRDUC CISMRKEL TR PL. YIOFUEH NEL SISTEL’S YEIOF IO TRGO.

BRDL GEEVS WASSEC AGAH, AOC ZAOE SAG ORTNIOF RB NIP. SNE EOCEAKRDLEC TR
WELSDACE NELSEUB TNAT SNE CIC ORT LEFLET IT; YDT SNE MRDUC OR UROFEL YE
YUIOC TR PISS YIOFUEH’S IOATTEOTIRO. ABTEL GAITIOF AT NRPE EKELH PRLOIOF
BRL A BRLTOIFNT, AOC IOKEOTIOF EKELH EKEOIOF A BLESN EXMDSE BRL NEL, TNE
KISITRL CIC AT UAST AWWEAL; YDT TNE SNRLTOESS RB NEL STAH, AOC, HET
PRLE, TNE AUTELATIRO RB NEL PAOOEL, GRDUC AUURG ZAOE TR CEMEIKE NELSEUB
OR UROFEL. TNE UETTEL GNIMN SNE GLRTE RO TNIS RMMASIRO TR NEL SISTEL
GIUU WLRKE GNAT SNE BEUT:--

     “PH CEALEST UIJJH GIUU, I AP SDLE, YE IOMAWAYUE RB TLIDPWNIOF IO
     NEL YETTEL ZDCFPEOT, AT PH EXWEOSE, GNEO I MROBESS PHSEUB TR NAKE
     YEEO EOTILEUH CEMEIKEC IO PISS YIOFUEH’S LEFALC BRL PE. YDT, PH
     CEAL SISTEL, TNRDFN TNE EKEOT NAS WLRKEC HRD LIFNT, CR ORT TNIOV PE
     RYSTIOATE IB I STIUU ASSELT TNAT, MROSICELIOF GNAT NEL YENAKIRDL
     GAS, PH MROBICEOME GAS AS OATDLAU AS HRDL SDSWIMIRO. I CR ORT AT
     AUU MRPWLENEOC NEL LEASRO BRL GISNIOF TR YE IOTIPATE GITN PE; YDT,
     IB TNE SAPE MILMDPSTAOMES GELE TR NAWWEO AFAIO, I AP SDLE I SNRDUC
     YE CEMEIKEC AFAIO. MALRUIOE CIC ORT LETDLO PH KISIT TIUU HESTELCAH;
     AOC ORT A ORTE, ORT A UIOE, CIC I LEMEIKE IO TNE PEAOTIPE. GNEO SNE
     CIC MRPE, IT GAS KELH EKICEOT TNAT SNE NAC OR WUEASDLE IO IT; SNE
     PACE A SUIFNT, BRLPAU AWRURFH BRL ORT MAUUIOF YEBRLE, SAIC ORT A
     GRLC RB GISNIOF TR SEE PE AFAIO, AOC GAS, IO EKELH LESWEMT, SR
     AUTELEC A MLEATDLE, TNAT GNEO SNE GEOT AGAH I GAS WELBEMTUH
     LESRUKEC TR MROTIODE TNE AMQDAIOTAOME OR UROFEL. I WITH, TNRDFN I
     MAOORT NEUW YUAPIOF, NEL. SNE GAS KELH GLROF IO SIOFUIOF PE RDT AS
     SNE CIC; I MAO SABEUH SAH, TNAT EKELH ACKAOME TR IOTIPAMH YEFAO RO
     NEL SICE. YDT I WITH NEL, YEMADSE SNE PDST BEEU TNAT SNE NAS YEEO
     AMTIOF GLROF, AOC YEMADSE I AP KELH SDLE TNAT AOXIETH BRL NEL
     YLRTNEL IS TNE MADSE RB IT. I OEEC ORT EXWUAIO PHSEUB BALTNEL; AOC
     TNRDFN _GE_ VORG TNIS AOXIETH TR YE QDITE OEECUESS, HET IB SNE
     BEEUS IT, IT GIUU EASIUH AMMRDOT BRL NEL YENAKIRDL TR PE; AOC SR
     CESELKECUH CEAL AS NE IS TR NIS SISTEL, GNATEKEL AOXIETH SNE PAH
     BEEU RO NIS YENAUB IS OATDLAU AOC APIAYUE. I MAOORT YDT GROCEL,
     NRGEKEL, AT NEL NAKIOF AOH SDMN BEALS ORG, YEMADSE IB NE NAC AT AUU
     MALEC AYRDT PE, GE PDST NAKE PET UROF, UROF AFR. NE VORGS RB PH
     YEIOF IO TRGO, I AP MELTAIO, BLRP SRPETNIOF SNE SAIC NELSEUB; AOC
     HET IT GRDUC SEEP, YH NEL PAOOEL RB TAUVIOF, AS IB SNE GAOTEC TR
     WELSDACE NELSEUB TNAT NE IS LEAUUH WALTIAU TR PISS CALMH. I MAOORT
     DOCELSTAOC IT. IB I GELE ORT ABLAIC RB ZDCFIOF NALSNUH, I SNRDUC YE
     AUPRST TEPWTEC TR SAH, TNAT TNELE IS A STLROF AWWEALAOME RB
     CDWUIMITH IO AUU TNIS. I GIUU EOCEAKRDL TR YAOISN EKELH WAIOBDU
     TNRDFNT, AOC TNIOV ROUH RB GNAT GIUU PAVE PE NAWWH, HRDL ABBEMTIRO,
     AOC TNE IOKALIAYUE VIOCOESS RB PH CEAL DOMUE AOC ADOT. UET PE NEAL
     BLRP HRD KELH SRRO. PISS YIOFUEH SAIC SRPETNIOF RB NIS OEKEL
     LETDLOIOF TR OETNELBIEUC AFAIO, RB FIKIOF DW TNE NRDSE, YDT ORT
     GITN AOH MELTAIOTH. GE NAC YETTEL ORT PEOTIRO IT. I AP EXTLEPEUH
     FUAC TNAT HRD NAKE SDMN WUEASAOT AMMRDOTS BLRP RDL BLIEOCS AT
     NDOSBRLC. WLAH FR TR SEE TNEP, GITN SIL GIUUIAP AOC PALIA. I AP
     SDLE HRD GIUU YE KELH MRPBRLTAYUE TNELE.

“HRDLS, ETM.”

TNIS UETTEL FAKE EUIJAYETN SRPE WAIO; YDT NEL SWILITS LETDLOEC, AS SNE
MROSICELEC TNAT ZAOE GRDUC OR UROFEL YE CDWEC, YH TNE SISTEL AT UEAST.
AUU EXWEMTATIRO BLRP TNE YLRTNEL GAS ORG AYSRUDTEUH RKEL. SNE GRDUC ORT
EKEO GISN BRL AOH LEOEGAU RB NIS ATTEOTIROS. NIS MNALAMTEL SDOV RO EKELH
LEKIEG RB IT; AOC, AS A WDOISNPEOT BRL NIP, AS GEUU AS A WRSSIYUE
ACKAOTAFE TR ZAOE, SNE SELIRDSUH NRWEC NE PIFNT LEAUUH SRRO PALLH PL.
CALMH’S SISTEL, AS, YH GIMVNAP’S AMMRDOT, SNE GRDUC PAVE NIP AYDOCAOTUH
LEFLET GNAT NE NAC TNLRGO AGAH.

PLS. FALCIOEL AYRDT TNIS TIPE LEPIOCEC EUIJAYETN RB NEL WLRPISE
MROMELOIOF TNAT FEOTUEPAO, AOC LEQDILEC IOBRLPATIRO; AOC EUIJAYETN NAC
SDMN TR SEOC AS PIFNT LATNEL FIKE MROTEOTPEOT TR NEL ADOT TNAO TR
NELSEUB. NIS AWWALEOT WALTIAUITH NAC SDYSICEC, NIS ATTEOTIROS GELE RKEL,
NE GAS TNE ACPILEL RB SRPE ROE EUSE. EUIJAYETN GAS GATMNBDU EORDFN TR
SEE IT AUU, YDT SNE MRDUC SEE IT AOC GLITE RB IT GITNRDT PATELIAU WAIO.
NEL NEALT NAC YEEO YDT SUIFNTUH TRDMNEC, AOC NEL KAOITH GAS SATISBIEC
GITN YEUIEKIOF TNAT _SNE_ GRDUC NAKE YEEO NIS ROUH MNRIME, NAC BRLTDOE
WELPITTEC IT. TNE SDCCEO AMQDISITIRO RB TEO TNRDSAOC WRDOCS GAS TNE PRST
LEPALVAYUE MNALP RB TNE HRDOF UACH TR GNRP NE GAS ORG LEOCELIOF NIPSEUB
AFLEEAYUE; YDT EUIJAYETN, UESS MUEAL-SIFNTEC WELNAWS IO TNIS MASE TNAO
IO MNALURTTE’S, CIC ORT QDALLEU GITN NIP BRL NIS GISN RB IOCEWEOCEOME.
ORTNIOF, RO TNE MROTLALH, MRDUC YE PRLE OATDLAU; AOC, GNIUE AYUE TR
SDWWRSE TNAT IT MRST NIP A BEG STLDFFUES TR LEUIOQDISN NEL, SNE GAS
LEACH TR AUURG IT A GISE AOC CESILAYUE PEASDLE BRL YRTN, AOC MRDUC KELH
SIOMELEUH GISN NIP NAWWH.

AUU TNIS GAS AMVORGUECFEC TR PLS. FALCIOEL; AOC, ABTEL LEUATIOF TNE
MILMDPSTAOMES, SNE TNDS GEOT RO:--“I AP ORG MROKIOMEC, PH CEAL ADOT,
TNAT I NAKE OEKEL YEEO PDMN IO URKE; BRL NAC I LEAUUH EXWELIEOMEC TNAT
WDLE AOC EUEKATIOF WASSIRO, I SNRDUC AT WLESEOT CETEST NIS KELH OAPE,
AOC GISN NIP AUU PAOOEL RB EKIU. YDT PH BEEUIOFS ALE ORT ROUH MRLCIAU
TRGALCS _NIP_, TNEH ALE EKEO IPWALTIAU TRGALCS PISS VIOF. I MAOORT BIOC
RDT TNAT I NATE NEL AT AUU, RL TNAT I AP IO TNE UEAST DOGIUUIOF TR TNIOV
NEL A KELH FRRC SRLT RB FILU. TNELE MAO YE OR URKE IO AUU TNIS. PH
GATMNBDUOESS NAS YEEO EBBEMTDAU; AOC TNRDFN I SNRDUC MELTAIOUH YE A PRLE
IOTELESTIOF RYZEMT TR AUU PH AMQDAIOTAOME, GELE I CISTLAMTECUH IO URKE
GITN NIP, I MAOORT SAH TNAT I LEFLET PH MRPWALATIKE IOSIFOIBIMAOME.
IPWRLTAOME PAH SRPETIPES YE WDLMNASEC TRR CEALUH. VITTH AOC UHCIA TAVE
NIS CEBEMTIRO PDMN PRLE TR NEALT TNAO I CR. TNEH ALE HRDOF IO TNE GAHS
RB TNE GRLUC, AOC ORT HET RWEO TR TNE PRLTIBHIOF MROKIMTIRO TNAT
NAOCSRPE HRDOF PEO PDST NAKE SRPETNIOF TR UIKE RO AS GEUU AS TNE
WUAIO.”




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “RO TNE STAILS”
]




MNAWTEL XXKII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

GITN OR FLEATEL EKEOTS TNAO TNESE IO TNE UROFYRDLO BAPIUH, AOC RTNELGISE
CIKELSIBIEC YH UITTUE YEHROC TNE GAUVS TR PELHTRO, SRPETIPES CILTH AOC
SRPETIPES MRUC, CIC ZAODALH AOC BEYLDALH WASS AGAH. PALMN GAS TR TAVE
EUIJAYETN TR NDOSBRLC. SNE NAC ORT AT BILST TNRDFNT KELH SELIRDSUH RB
FRIOF TNITNEL; YDT MNALURTTE, SNE SRRO BRDOC, GAS CEWEOCIOF RO TNE
WUAO, AOC SNE FLACDAUUH UEALOEC TR MROSICEL IT NELSEUB GITN FLEATEL
WUEASDLE AS GEUU AS FLEATEL MELTAIOTH. AYSEOME NAC IOMLEASEC NEL CESILE
RB SEEIOF MNALURTTE AFAIO, AOC GEAVEOEC NEL CISFDST RB PL. MRUUIOS.
TNELE GAS ORKEUTH IO TNE SMNEPE; AOC AS, GITN SDMN A PRTNEL AOC SDMN
DOMRPWAOIROAYUE SISTELS, NRPE MRDUC ORT YE BADUTUESS, A UITTUE MNAOFE
GAS ORT DOGEUMRPE BRL ITS RGO SAVE. TNE ZRDLOEH GRDUC, PRLERKEL, FIKE
NEL A WEEW AT ZAOE; AOC, IO SNRLT, AS TNE TIPE CLEG OEAL, SNE GRDUC NAKE
YEEO KELH SRLLH BRL AOH CEUAH. EKELHTNIOF, NRGEKEL, GEOT RO SPRRTNUH,
AOC GAS BIOAUUH SETTUEC AMMRLCIOF TR MNALURTTE’S BILST SVETMN. SNE GAS
TR AMMRPWAOH SIL GIUUIAP AOC NIS SEMROC CADFNTEL. TNE IPWLRKEPEOT RB
SWEOCIOF A OIFNT IO UROCRO GAS ACCEC IO TIPE, AOC TNE WUAO YEMAPE AS
WELBEMT AS WUAO MRDUC YE.

TNE ROUH WAIO GAS IO UEAKIOF NEL BATNEL, GNR GRDUC MELTAIOUH PISS NEL,
AOC GNR, GNEO IT MAPE TR TNE WRIOT, SR UITTUE UIVEC NEL FRIOF, TNAT NE
TRUC NEL TR GLITE TR NIP, AOC AUPRST WLRPISEC TR AOSGEL NEL UETTEL.

TNE BALEGEUU YETGEEO NELSEUB AOC PL. GIMVNAP GAS WELBEMTUH BLIEOCUH; RO
NIS SICE EKEO PRLE. NIS WLESEOT WDLSDIT MRDUC ORT PAVE NIP BRLFET TNAT
EUIJAYETN NAC YEEO TNE BILST TR EXMITE AOC TR CESELKE NIS ATTEOTIRO, TNE
BILST TR UISTEO AOC TR WITH, TNE BILST TR YE ACPILEC; AOC IO NIS PAOOEL
RB YICCIOF NEL ACIED, GISNIOF NEL EKELH EOZRHPEOT, LEPIOCIOF NEL RB GNAT
SNE GAS TR EXWEMT IO UACH MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN, AOC TLDSTIOF TNEIL
RWIOIRO RB NEL--TNEIL RWIOIRO RB EKELHYRCH--GRDUC AUGAHS MRIOMICE, TNELE
GAS A SRUIMITDCE, AO IOTELEST, GNIMN SNE BEUT PDST EKEL ATTAMN NEL TR
NIP GITN A PRST SIOMELE LEFALC; AOC SNE WALTEC BLRP NIP MROKIOMEC, TNAT,
GNETNEL PALLIEC RL SIOFUE, NE PDST AUGAHS YE NEL PRCEU RB TNE APIAYUE
AOC WUEASIOF.

NEL BEUURG-TLAKEUUELS TNE OEXT CAH GELE ORT RB A VIOC TR PAVE NEL TNIOV
NIP UESS AFLEEAYUE. SIL GIUUIAP UDMAS, AOC NIS CADFNTEL PALIA, A
FRRC-NDPRDLEC FILU, YDT AS EPWTH-NEACEC AS NIPSEUB, NAC ORTNIOF TR SAH
TNAT MRDUC YE GRLTN NEALIOF, AOC GELE UISTEOEC TR GITN AYRDT AS PDMN
CEUIFNT AS TNE LATTUE RB TNE MNAISE. EUIJAYETN URKEC AYSDLCITIES, YDT
SNE NAC VORGO SIL GIUUIAP’S TRR UROF. NE MRDUC TEUU NEL ORTNIOF OEG RB
TNE GROCELS RB NIS WLESEOTATIRO AOC VOIFNTNRRC; AOC NIS MIKIUITIES GELE
GRLO RDT, UIVE NIS IOBRLPATIRO.

IT GAS A ZRDLOEH RB ROUH TGEOTH-BRDL PIUES, AOC TNEH YEFAO IT SR EALUH
AS TR YE IO FLAMEMNDLMN STLEET YH ORRO. AS TNEH CLRKE TR PL. FALCIOEL’S
CRRL, ZAOE GAS AT A CLAGIOF-LRRP GIOCRG GATMNIOF TNEIL ALLIKAU: GNEO
TNEH EOTELEC TNE WASSAFE, SNE GAS TNELE TR GEUMRPE TNEP, AOC EUIJAYETN,
URRVIOF EALOESTUH IO NEL BAME, GAS WUEASEC TR SEE IT NEAUTNBDU AOC
URKEUH AS EKEL. RO TNE STAILS GELE A TLRRW RB UITTUE YRHS AOC FILUS,
GNRSE EAFELOESS BRL TNEIL MRDSIO’S AWWEALAOME GRDUC ORT AUURG TNEP TR
GAIT IO TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP, AOC GNRSE SNHOESS, AS TNEH NAC ORT SEEO NEL
BRL A TGEUKEPROTN, WLEKEOTEC TNEIL MRPIOF URGEL. AUU GAS ZRH AOC
VIOCOESS. TNE CAH WASSEC PRST WUEASAOTUH AGAH; TNE PRLOIOF IO YDSTUE AOC
SNRWWIOF, AOC TNE EKEOIOF AT ROE RB TNE TNEATLES.

EUIJAYETN TNEO MROTLIKEC TR SIT YH NEL ADOT. TNEIL BILST SDYZEMT GAS NEL
SISTEL; AOC SNE GAS PRLE FLIEKEC TNAO ASTROISNEC TR NEAL, IO LEWUH TR
NEL PIODTE IOQDILIES, TNAT TNRDFN ZAOE AUGAHS STLDFFUEC TR SDWWRLT NEL
SWILITS, TNELE GELE WELIRCS RB CEZEMTIRO. IT GAS LEASROAYUE, NRGEKEL, TR
NRWE TNAT TNEH GRDUC ORT MROTIODE UROF. PLS. FALCIOEL FAKE NEL TNE
WALTIMDUALS AUSR RB PISS YIOFUEH’S KISIT IO FLAMEMNDLMN STLEET, AOC
LEWEATEC MROKELSATIROS RMMDLLIOF AT CIBBELEOT TIPES YETGEEO ZAOE AOC
NELSEUB, GNIMN WLRKEC TNAT TNE BRLPEL NAC, BLRP NEL NEALT, FIKEO DW TNE
AMQDAIOTAOME.

PLS. FALCIOEL TNEO LAUUIEC NEL OIEME RO GIMVNAP’S CESELTIRO, AOC
MRPWUIPEOTEC NEL RO YEALIOF IT SR GEUU.

“YDT, PH CEAL EUIJAYETN,” SNE ACCEC, “GNAT SRLT RB FILU IS PISS VIOF? I
SNRDUC YE SRLLH TR TNIOV RDL BLIEOC PELMEOALH.”

“WLAH, PH CEAL ADOT, GNAT IS TNE CIBBELEOME IO PATLIPROIAU ABBAILS,
YETGEEO TNE PELMEOALH AOC TNE WLDCEOT PRTIKE? GNELE CRES CISMLETIRO EOC,
AOC AKALIME YEFIO? UAST MNLISTPAS HRD GELE ABLAIC RB NIS PALLHIOF PE,
YEMADSE IT GRDUC YE IPWLDCEOT; AOC ORG, YEMADSE NE IS TLHIOF TR FET A
FILU GITN ROUH TEO TNRDSAOC WRDOCS, HRD GAOT TR BIOC RDT TNAT NE IS
PELMEOALH.”

“IB HRD GIUU ROUH TEUU PE GNAT SRLT RB FILU PISS VIOF IS, I SNAUU VORG
GNAT TR TNIOV.”

“SNE IS A KELH FRRC VIOC RB FILU, I YEUIEKE. I VORG OR NALP RB NEL.”

“YDT NE WAIC NEL ORT TNE SPAUUEST ATTEOTIRO TIUU NEL FLAOCBATNEL’S CEATN
PACE NEL PISTLESS RB TNIS BRLTDOE?”

“OR--GNH SNRDUC NE? IB IT GELE ORT AUURGAYUE BRL NIP TR FAIO _PH_
ABBEMTIROS, YEMADSE I NAC OR PROEH, GNAT RMMASIRO MRDUC TNELE YE BRL
PAVIOF URKE TR A FILU GNRP NE CIC ORT MALE AYRDT, AOC GNR GAS EQDAUUH
WRRL?”

“YDT TNELE SEEPS IOCEUIMAMH IO CILEMTIOF NIS ATTEOTIROS TRGALCS NEL SR
SRRO ABTEL TNIS EKEOT.”

“A PAO IO CISTLESSEC MILMDPSTAOMES NAS ORT TIPE BRL AUU TNRSE EUEFAOT
CEMRLDPS GNIMN RTNEL WERWUE PAH RYSELKE. IB _SNE_ CRES ORT RYZEMT TR IT,
GNH SNRDUC _GE_?”

“_NEL_ ORT RYZEMTIOF CRES ORT ZDSTIBH _NIP_. IT ROUH SNRGS NEL YEIOF
CEBIMIEOT IO SRPETNIOF NELSEUB--SEOSE RL BEEUIOF.”

“GEUU,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, “NAKE IT AS HRD MNRRSE. _NE_ SNAUU YE
PELMEOALH, AOC _SNE_ SNAUU YE BRRUISN.”

“OR, UIJJH, TNAT IS GNAT I CR _ORT_ MNRRSE. I SNRDUC YE SRLLH, HRD VORG,
TR TNIOV IUU RB A HRDOF PAO GNR NAS UIKEC SR UROF IO CELYHSNILE.”

“RN, IB TNAT IS AUU, I NAKE A KELH WRRL RWIOIRO RB HRDOF PEO GNR UIKE IO
CELYHSNILE; AOC TNEIL IOTIPATE BLIEOCS GNR UIKE IO NELTBRLCSNILE ALE ORT
PDMN YETTEL. I AP SIMV RB TNEP AUU. TNAOV NEAKEO! I AP FRIOF TR-PRLLRG
GNELE I SNAUU BIOC A PAO GNR NAS ORT ROE AFLEEAYUE QDAUITH, GNR NAS
OEITNEL PAOOELS ORL SEOSE TR LEMRPPEOC NIP. STDWIC PEO ALE TNE ROUH ROES
GRLTN VORGIOF, ABTEL AUU.”

“TAVE MALE, UIJJH; TNAT SWEEMN SAKRDLS STLROFUH RB CISAWWRIOTPEOT.”

YEBRLE TNEH GELE SEWALATEC YH TNE MROMUDSIRO RB TNE WUAH, SNE NAC TNE
DOEXWEMTEC NAWWIOESS RB AO IOKITATIRO TR AMMRPWAOH NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT IO
A TRDL RB WUEASDLE GNIMN TNEH WLRWRSEC TAVIOF IO TNE SDPPEL.

“GE NAKE ORT QDITE CETELPIOEC NRG BAL IT SNAUU MALLH DS,” SAIC PLS.
FALCIOEL; “YDT WELNAWS, TR TNE UAVES.”

OR SMNEPE MRDUC NAKE YEEO PRLE AFLEEAYUE TR EUIJAYETN, AOC NEL
AMMEWTAOME RB TNE IOKITATIRO GAS PRST LEACH AOC FLATEBDU. “PH CEAL, CEAL
ADOT,” SNE LAWTDLRDSUH MLIEC, “GNAT CEUIFNT! GNAT BEUIMITH! HRD FIKE PE
BLESN UIBE AOC KIFRDL. ACIED TR CISAWWRIOTPEOT AOC SWUEEO. GNAT ALE PEO
TR LRMVS AOC PRDOTAIOS? RN, GNAT NRDLS RB TLAOSWRLT GE SNAUU SWEOC! AOC
GNEO GE _CR_ LETDLO, IT SNAUU ORT YE UIVE RTNEL TLAKEUUELS, GITNRDT
YEIOF AYUE TR FIKE ROE AMMDLATE ICEA RB AOHTNIOF. GE _GIUU_ VORG GNELE
GE NAKE FROE--GE _GIUU_ LEMRUUEMT GNAT GE NAKE SEEO. UAVES, PRDOTAIOS,
AOC LIKELS, SNAUU ORT YE ZDPYUEC TRFETNEL IO RDL IPAFIOATIROS; ORL, GNEO
GE ATTEPWT TR CESMLIYE AOH WALTIMDUAL SMEOE, GIUU GE YEFIO QDALLEUUIOF
AYRDT ITS LEUATIKE SITDATIRO. UET _RDL_ BILST EBBDSIROS YE UESS
IOSDWWRLTAYUE TNAO TNRSE RB TNE FEOELAUITH RB TLAKEUUELS.”




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “AT TNE CRRL”
]




MNAWTEL XXKIII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EKELH RYZEMT IO TNE OEXT CAH’S ZRDLOEH GAS OEG AOC IOTELESTIOF TR
EUIJAYETN; AOC NEL SWILITS GELE IO A STATE RB EOZRHPEOT; BRL SNE NAC
SEEO NEL SISTEL URRVIOF SR GEUU AS TR YAOISN AUU BEAL BRL NEL NEAUTN,
AOC TNE WLRSWEMT RB NEL ORLTNELO TRDL GAS A MROSTAOT SRDLME RB CEUIFNT.

GNEO TNEH UEBT TNE NIFN LRAC BRL TNE UAOE TR NDOSBRLC, EKELH EHE GAS IO
SEALMN RB TNE WALSROAFE, AOC EKELH TDLOIOF EXWEMTEC TR YLIOF IT IO KIEG.
TNE WAUIOF RB LRSIOFS WALV GAS TNEIL YRDOCALH RO ROE SICE. EUIJAYETN
SPIUEC AT TNE LEMRUUEMTIRO RB AUU TNAT SNE NAC NEALC RB ITS IONAYITAOTS.

AT UEOFTN TNE WALSROAFE GAS CISMELOIYUE. TNE FALCEO SURWIOF TR TNE
LRAC, TNE NRDSE STAOCIOF IO IT, TNE FLEEO WAUES AOC TNE UADLEU NECFE,
EKELHTNIOF CEMUALEC TNEH GELE ALLIKIOF. PL. MRUUIOS AOC MNALURTTE
AWWEALEC AT TNE CRRL, AOC TNE MALLIAFE STRWWEC AT TNE SPAUU FATE, GNIMN
UEC YH A SNRLT FLAKEU GAUV TR TNE NRDSE, APICST TNE ORCS AOC SPIUES RB
TNE GNRUE WALTH. IO A PRPEOT TNEH GELE AUU RDT RB TNE MNAISE, LEZRIMIOF
AT TNE SIFNT RB EAMN RTNEL. PLS. MRUUIOS GEUMRPEC NEL BLIEOC GITN TNE
UIKEUIEST WUEASDLE, AOC EUIJAYETN GAS PRLE AOC PRLE SATISBIEC GITN
MRPIOF, GNEO SNE BRDOC NELSEUB SR ABBEMTIROATEUH LEMEIKEC. SNE SAG
IOSTAOTUH TNAT NEL MRDSIO’S PAOOELS GELE ORT AUTELEC YH NIS PALLIAFE:
NIS BRLPAU MIKIUITH GAS ZDST GNAT IT NAC YEEO; AOC NE CETAIOEC NEL SRPE
PIODTES AT TNE FATE TR NEAL AOC SATISBH NIS IOQDILIES ABTEL AUU NEL
BAPIUH. TNEH GELE TNEO, GITN OR RTNEL CEUAH TNAO NIS WRIOTIOF RDT TNE
OEATOESS RB TNE EOTLAOME, TAVEO IOTR TNE NRDSE; AOC AS SRRO AS TNEH GELE
IO TNE WALURDL, NE GEUMRPEC TNEP A SEMROC TIPE, GITN RSTEOTATIRDS
BRLPAUITH, TR NIS NDPYUE AYRCE, AOC WDOMTDAUUH LEWEATEC AUU NIS GIBE’S
RBBELS RB LEBLESNPEOT.

EUIJAYETN GAS WLEWALEC TR SEE NIP IO NIS FURLH; AOC SNE MRDUC ORT NEUW
BAOMHIOF TNAT IO CISWUAHIOF TNE FRRC WLRWRLTIRO RB TNE LRRP, ITS ASWEMT,
AOC ITS BDLOITDLE, NE ACCLESSEC NIPSEUB WALTIMDUALUH TR NEL, AS IB
GISNIOF TR PAVE NEL BEEU GNAT SNE NAC URST IO LEBDSIOF NIP. YDT TNRDFN
EKELHTNIOF SEEPEC OEAT AOC MRPBRLTAYUE, SNE GAS ORT AYUE TR FLATIBH NIP
YH AOH SIFN RB LEWEOTAOME; AOC LATNEL URRVEC GITN GROCEL AT NEL BLIEOC,
TNAT SNE MRDUC NAKE SR MNEELBDU AO AIL GITN SDMN A MRPWAOIRO. GNEO PL.
MRUUIOS SAIC AOHTNIOF RB GNIMN NIS GIBE PIFNT LEASROAYUH YE ASNAPEC,
GNIMN MELTAIOUH GAS ORT SEUCRP, SNE IOKRUDOTALIUH TDLOEC NEL EHE RO
MNALURTTE. ROME RL TGIME SNE MRDUC CISMELO A BAIOT YUDSN; YDT IO FEOELAU
MNALURTTE GISEUH CIC ORT NEAL. ABTEL SITTIOF UROF EORDFN TR ACPILE
EKELH ALTIMUE RB BDLOITDLE IO TNE LRRP, BLRP TNE SICEYRALC TR TNE
BEOCEL, TR FIKE AO AMMRDOT RB TNEIL ZRDLOEH, AOC RB AUU TNAT NAC
NAWWEOEC IO UROCRO, PL. MRUUIOS IOKITEC TNEP TR TAVE A STLRUU IO TNE
FALCEO, GNIMN GAS UALFE AOC GEUU UAIC RDT, AOC TR TNE MDUTIKATIRO RB
GNIMN NE ATTEOCEC NIPSEUB. TR GRLV IO NIS FALCEO GAS ROE RB NIS PRST
LESWEMTAYUE WUEASDLES; AOC EUIJAYETN ACPILEC TNE MRPPAOC RB MRDOTEOAOME
GITN GNIMN MNALURTTE TAUVEC RB TNE NEAUTNBDUOESS RB TNE EXELMISE, AOC
RGOEC SNE EOMRDLAFEC IT AS PDMN AS WRSSIYUE. NELE, UEACIOF TNE GAH
TNLRDFN EKELH GAUV AOC MLRSS GAUV, AOC SMALMEUH AUURGIOF TNEP AO
IOTELKAU TR DTTEL TNE WLAISES NE ASVEC BRL, EKELH KIEG GAS WRIOTEC RDT
GITN A PIODTEOESS GNIMN UEBT YEADTH EOTILEUH YENIOC. NE MRDUC ODPYEL TNE
BIEUCS IO EKELH CILEMTIRO, AOC MRDUC TEUU NRG PAOH TLEES TNELE GELE IO
TNE PRST CISTAOT MUDPW. YDT RB AUU TNE KIEGS GNIMN NIS FALCEO, RL GNIMN
TNE MRDOTLH RL TNE VIOFCRP MRDUC YRAST, OROE GELE TR YE MRPWALEC GITN
TNE WLRSWEMT RB LRSIOFS, ABBRLCEC YH AO RWEOIOF IO TNE TLEES TNAT
YRLCELEC TNE WALV OEALUH RWWRSITE TNE BLROT RB NIS NRDSE. IT GAS A
NAOCSRPE PRCELO YDIUCIOF, GEUU SITDATEC RO LISIOF FLRDOC.

BLRP NIS FALCEO, PL. MRUUIOS GRDUC NAKE UEC TNEP LRDOC NIS TGR PEACRGS;
YDT TNE UACIES, ORT NAKIOF SNRES TR EOMRDOTEL TNE LEPAIOS RB A GNITE
BLRST, TDLOEC YAMV; AOC GNIUE SIL GIUUIAP AMMRPWAOIEC NIP, MNALURTTE
TRRV NEL SISTEL AOC BLIEOC RKEL TNE NRDSE, EXTLEPEUH GEUU WUEASEC,
WLRYAYUH, TR NAKE TNE RWWRLTDOITH RB SNRGIOF IT GITNRDT NEL NDSYAOC’S
NEUW. IT GAS LATNEL SPAUU, YDT GEUU YDIUT AOC MROKEOIEOT; AOC EKELHTNIOF
GAS BITTEC DW AOC ALLAOFEC GITN A OEATOESS AOC MROSISTEOMH, RB GNIMN
EUIJAYETN FAKE MNALURTTE AUU TNE MLECIT. GNEO PL. MRUUIOS MRDUC YE
BRLFRTTEO, TNELE GAS LEAUUH A FLEAT AIL RB MRPBRLT TNLRDFNRDT, AOC YH
MNALURTTE’S EKICEOT EOZRHPEOT RB IT, EUIJAYETN SDWWRSEC NE PDST YE RBTEO
BRLFRTTEO.

SNE NAC AULEACH UEALOT TNAT UACH MATNELIOE GAS STIUU IO TNE MRDOTLH. IT
GAS SWRVEO RB AFAIO GNIUE TNEH GELE AT CIOOEL, GNEO PL. MRUUIOS ZRIOIOF
IO, RYSELKEC,--

“HES, PISS EUIJAYETN, HRD GIUU NAKE TNE NRORDL RB SEEIOF UACH MATNELIOE
CE YRDLFN RO TNE EOSDIOF SDOCAH AT MNDLMN, AOC I OEEC ORT SAH HRD GIUU
YE CEUIFNTEC GITN NEL. SNE IS AUU ABBAYIUITH AOC MROCESMEOSIRO, AOC I
CRDYT ORT YDT HRD GIUU YE NRORDLEC GITN SRPE WRLTIRO RB NEL ORTIME GNEO
SELKIME IS RKEL. I NAKE SMALMEUH AOH NESITATIRO IO SAHIOF TNAT SNE GIUU
IOMUDCE HRD AOC PH SISTEL PALIA IO EKELH IOKITATIRO GITN GNIMN SNE
NRORDLS DS CDLIOF HRDL STAH NELE. NEL YENAKIRDL TR PH CEAL MNALURTTE IS
MNALPIOF. GE CIOE AT LRSIOFS TGIME EKELH GEEV, AOC ALE OEKEL AUURGEC TR
GAUV NRPE. NEL UACHSNIW’S MALLIAFE IS LEFDUALUH RLCELEC BRL DS. I
_SNRDUC_ SAH, ROE RB NEL UACHSNIW’S MALLIAFES, BRL SNE NAS SEKELAU.”

“UACH MATNELIOE IS A KELH LESWEMTAYUE, SEOSIYUE GRPAO, IOCEEC,” ACCEC
MNALURTTE, “AOC A PRST ATTEOTIKE OEIFNYRDL.”

“KELH TLDE, PH CEAL, TNAT IS EXAMTUH GNAT I SAH. SNE IS TNE SRLT RB
GRPAO GNRP ROE MAOORT LEFALC GITN TRR PDMN CEBELEOME.”

TNE EKEOIOF GAS SWEOT MNIEBUH IO TAUVIOF RKEL NELTBRLCSNILE OEGS, AOC
TEUUIOF AFAIO GNAT NAC YEEO AULEACH GLITTEO; AOC GNEO IT MURSEC,
EUIJAYETN, IO TNE SRUITDCE RB NEL MNAPYEL, NAC TR PECITATE DWRO
MNALURTTE’S CEFLEE RB MROTEOTPEOT, TR DOCELSTAOC NEL ACCLESS IO FDICIOF,
AOC MRPWRSDLE IO YEALIOF GITN, NEL NDSYAOC, AOC TR AMVORGUECFE TNAT IT
GAS AUU CROE KELH GEUU. SNE NAC AUSR TR AOTIMIWATE NRG NEL KISIT GRDUC
WASS, TNE QDIET TEORDL RB TNEIL DSDAU EPWURHPEOTS, TNE KEXATIRDS
IOTELLDWTIROS RB PL. MRUUIOS, AOC TNE FAIETIES RB TNEIL IOTELMRDLSE
GITN LRSIOFS. A UIKEUH IPAFIOATIRO SRRO SETTUEC IT AUU.

AYRDT TNE PICCUE RB TNE OEXT CAH, AS SNE GAS IO NEL LRRP FETTIOF LEACH
BRL A GAUV, A SDCCEO ORISE YEURG SEEPEC TR SWEAV TNE GNRUE NRDSE IO
MROBDSIRO; AOC, ABTEL UISTEOIOF A PRPEOT, SNE NEALC SRPEYRCH LDOOIOF
DWSTAILS IO A KIRUEOT NDLLH, AOC MAUUIOF URDCUH ABTEL NEL. SNE RWEOEC
TNE CRRL, AOC PET PALIA IO TNE UAOCIOF-WUAME, GNR, YLEATNUESS GITN
AFITATIRO, MLIEC RDT,--

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “IO MROKELSATIRO GITN TNE UACIES”

[MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO.]]

“RN, PH CEAL EUIJA! WLAH PAVE NASTE AOC MRPE IOTR TNE CIOIOF-LRRP, BRL
TNELE IS SDMN A SIFNT TR YE SEEO! I GIUU ORT TEUU HRD GNAT IT IS. PAVE
NASTE, AOC MRPE CRGO TNIS PRPEOT.”

EUIJAYETN ASVEC QDESTIROS IO KAIO; PALIA GRDUC TEUU NEL ORTNIOF PRLE;
AOC CRGO TNEH LAO IOTR TNE CIOIOF-LRRP GNIMN BLROTEC TNE UAOE, IO QDEST
RB TNIS GROCEL; IT GAS TGR UACIES, STRWWIOF IO A URG WNAETRO AT TNE
FALCEO FATE.

“AOC IS TNIS AUU?” MLIEC EUIJAYETN. “I EXWEMTEC AT UEAST TNAT TNE WIFS
GELE FRT IOTR TNE FALCEO, AOC NELE IS ORTNIOF YDT UACH MATNELIOE AOC NEL
CADFNTEL!”

“UA! PH CEAL,” SAIC PALIA, QDITE SNRMVEC AT TNE PISTAVE, “IT IS ORT UACH
MATNELIOE. TNE RUC UACH IS PLS. ZEOVIOSRO, GNR UIKES GITN TNEP. TNE
RTNEL IS PISS CE YRDLFN. ROUH URRV AT NEL. SNE IS QDITE A UITTUE
MLEATDLE. GNR GRDUC NAKE TNRDFNT SNE MRDUC YE SR TNIO AOC SPAUU!”

“SNE IS AYRPIOAYUH LDCE TR VEEW MNALURTTE RDT RB CRRLS IO AUU TNIS GIOC.
GNH CRES SNE ORT MRPE IO?”

“RN, MNALURTTE SAHS SNE NALCUH EKEL CRES. IT IS TNE FLEATEST RB BAKRDLS
GNEO PISS CE YRDLFN MRPES IO.”

“I UIVE NEL AWWEALAOME,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, STLDMV GITN RTNEL ICEAS. “SNE
URRVS SIMVUH AOC MLRSS. HES, SNE GIUU CR BRL NIP KELH GEUU. SNE GIUU
PAVE NIP A KELH WLRWEL GIBE.”

PL. MRUUIOS AOC MNALURTTE GELE YRTN STAOCIOF AT TNE FATE IO MROKELSATIRO
GITN TNE UACIES; AOC SIL GIUUIAP, TR EUIJAYETN’S NIFN CIKELSIRO, GAS
STATIROEC IO TNE CRRLGAH, IO EALOEST MROTEPWUATIRO RB TNE FLEATOESS
YEBRLE NIP, AOC MROSTAOTUH YRGIOF GNEOEKEL PISS CE YRDLFN URRVEC TNAT
GAH.

AT UEOFTN TNELE GAS ORTNIOF PRLE TR YE SAIC; TNE UACIES CLRKE RO, AOC
TNE RTNELS LETDLOEC IOTR TNE NRDSE. PL. MRUUIOS OR SRROEL SAG TNE TGR
FILUS TNAO NE YEFAO TR MROFLATDUATE TNEP RO TNEIL FRRC BRLTDOE, GNIMN
MNALURTTE EXWUAIOEC YH UETTIOF TNEP VORG TNAT TNE GNRUE WALTH GAS ASVEC
TR CIOE AT LRSIOFS TNE OEXT CAH.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     ‘UACH MATNELIOE, SAIC SNE, HRD NAKE FIKEO PE A TLEASDLE.’

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]




MNAWTEL XXIX.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

PL. MRUUIOS’S TLIDPWN, IO MROSEQDEOME RB TNIS IOKITATIRO, GAS MRPWUETE.
TNE WRGEL RB CISWUAHIOF TNE FLAOCEDL RB NIS WATLROESS TR NIS GROCELIOF
KISITRLS, AOC RB UETTIOF TNEP SEE NEL MIKIUITH TRGALCS NIPSEUB AOC NIS
GIBE, GAS EXAMTUH GNAT NE NAC GISNEC BRL; AOC TNAT AO RWWRLTDOITH RB
CRIOF IT SNRDUC YE FIKEO SR SRRO GAS SDMN AO IOSTAOME RB UACH
MATNELIOE’S MROCESMEOSIRO AS NE VOEG ORT NRG TR ACPILE EORDFN.

“I MROBESS,” SAIC NE, “TNAT I SNRDUC ORT NAKE YEEO AT AUU SDLWLISEC YH
NEL UACHSNIW’S ASVIOF DS RO SDOCAH TR CLIOV TEA AOC SWEOC TNE EKEOIOF
AT LRSIOFS. I LATNEL EXWEMTEC, BLRP PH VORGUECFE RB NEL ABBAYIUITH, TNAT
IT GRDUC NAWWEO. YDT GNR MRDUC NAKE BRLESEEO SDMN AO ATTEOTIRO AS TNIS?
GNR MRDUC NAKE IPAFIOEC TNAT GE SNRDUC LEMEIKE AO IOKITATIRO TR CIOE
TNELE (AO IOKITATIRO, PRLERKEL, IOMUDCIOF TNE GNRUE WALTH) SR
IPPECIATEUH ABTEL HRDL ALLIKAU?”

“I AP TNE UESS SDLWLISEC AT GNAT NAS NAWWEOEC,” LEWUIEC SIL GIUUIAP,
“BLRP TNAT VORGUECFE RB GNAT TNE PAOOELS RB TNE FLEAT LEAUUH ALE, GNIMN
PH SITDATIRO IO UIBE NAS AUURGEC PE TR AMQDILE. AYRDT TNE MRDLT, SDMN
IOSTAOMES RB EUEFAOT YLEECIOF ALE ORT DOMRPPRO.”

SMALMEUH AOHTNIOF GAS TAUVEC RB TNE GNRUE CAH RL OEXT PRLOIOF YDT TNEIL
KISIT TR LRSIOFS. PL. MRUUIOS GAS MALEBDUUH IOSTLDMTIOF TNEP IO GNAT
TNEH GELE TR EXWEMT, TNAT TNE SIFNT RB SDMN LRRPS, SR PAOH SELKAOTS, AOC
SR SWUEOCIC A CIOOEL, PIFNT ORT GNRUUH RKELWRGEL TNEP.

GNEO TNE UACIES GELE SEWALATIOF BRL TNE TRIUETTE, NE SAIC TR
EUIJAYETN,--

“CR ORT PAVE HRDLSEUB DOEASH, PH CEAL MRDSIO, AYRDT HRDL AWWALEU. UACH
MATNELIOE IS BAL BLRP LEQDILIOF TNAT EUEFAOME RB CLESS IO DS GNIMN
YEMRPES NELSEUB AOC CADFNTEL. I GRDUC ACKISE HRD PELEUH TR WDT RO
GNATEKEL RB HRDL MURTNES IS SDWELIRL TR TNE LEST--TNELE IS OR RMMASIRO
BRL AOHTNIOF PRLE. UACH MATNELIOE GIUU ORT TNIOV TNE GRLSE RB HRD BRL
YEIOF SIPWUH CLESSEC. SNE UIVES TR NAKE TNE CISTIOMTIRO RB LAOV
WLESELKEC.”

GNIUE TNEH GELE CLESSIOF, NE MAPE TGR RL TNLEE TIPES TR TNEIL CIBBELEOT
CRRLS, TR LEMRPPEOC TNEIL YEIOF QDIMV, AS UACH MATNELIOE KELH PDMN
RYZEMTEC TR YE VEWT GAITIOF BRL NEL CIOOEL. SDMN BRLPICAYUE AMMRDOTS RB
NEL UACHSNIW, AOC NEL PAOOEL RB UIKIOF, QDITE BLIFNTEOEC PALIA UDMAS,
GNR NAC YEEO UITTUE DSEC TR MRPWAOH; AOC SNE URRVEC BRLGALC TR NEL
IOTLRCDMTIRO AT LRSIOFS GITN AS PDMN AWWLENEOSIRO AS NEL BATNEL NAC CROE
TR NIS WLESEOTATIRO AT ST. ZAPES’S.

AS TNE GEATNEL GAS BIOE, TNEH NAC A WUEASAOT GAUV RB AYRDT NAUB A PIUE
AMLRSS TNE WALV. EKELH WALV NAS ITS YEADTH AOC ITS WLRSWEMTS; AOC
EUIJAYETN SAG PDMN TR YE WUEASEC GITN, TNRDFN SNE MRDUC ORT YE IO SDMN
LAWTDLES AS PL. MRUUIOS EXWEMTEC TNE SMEOE TR IOSWILE, AOC GAS YDT
SUIFNTUH ABBEMTEC YH NIS EODPELATIRO RB TNE GIOCRGS IO BLROT RB TNE
NRDSE, AOC NIS LEUATIRO RB GNAT TNE FUAJIOF AUTRFETNEL NAC RLIFIOAUUH
MRST SIL UEGIS CE YRDLFN.

GNEO TNEH ASMEOCEC TNE STEWS TR TNE NAUU, PALIA’S AUALP GAS EKELH PRPEOT
IOMLEASIOF, AOC EKEO SIL GIUUIAP CIC ORT URRV WELBEMTUH MAUP.
EUIJAYETN’S MRDLAFE CIC ORT BAIU NEL. SNE NAC NEALC ORTNIOF RB UACH
MATNELIOE TNAT SWRVE NEL AGBDU BLRP AOH EXTLARLCIOALH TAUEOTS RL
PILAMDURDS KILTDE, AOC TNE PELE STATEUIOESS RB PROEH AOC LAOV SNE
TNRDFNT SNE MRDUC GITOESS GITNRDT TLEWICATIRO.

BLRP TNE EOTLAOME NAUU, RB GNIMN PL. MRUUIOS WRIOTEC RDT, GITN A
LAWTDLRDS AIL, TNE BIOE WLRWRLTIRO AOC BIOISNEC RLOAPEOTS, TNEH BRUURGEC
TNE SELKAOTS TNLRDFN AO AOTEMNAPYEL TR TNE LRRP GNELE UACH MATNELIOE,
NEL CADFNTEL, AOC PLS. ZEOVIOSRO GELE SITTIOF. NEL UACHSNIW, GITN FLEAT
MROCESMEOSIRO, ALRSE TR LEMEIKE TNEP; AOC AS PLS. MRUUIOS NAC SETTUEC IT
GITN NEL NDSYAOC TNAT TNE RBBIME RB IOTLRCDMTIRO SNRDUC YE NELS, IT GAS
WELBRLPEC IO A WLRWEL PAOOEL, GITNRDT AOH RB TNRSE AWRURFIES AOC TNAOVS
GNIMN NE GRDUC NAKE TNRDFNT OEMESSALH.

IO SWITE RB NAKIOF YEEO AT ST. ZAPES’S, SIL GIUUIAP GAS SR MRPWUETEUH
AGEC YH TNE FLAOCEDL SDLLRDOCIOF NIP, TNAT NE NAC YDT ZDST MRDLAFE
EORDFN TR PAVE A KELH URG YRG, AOC TAVE NIS SEAT GITNRDT SAHIOF A GRLC;
AOC NIS CADFNTEL, BLIFNTEOEC AUPRST RDT RB NEL SEOSES, SAT RO TNE ECFE
RB NEL MNAIL, ORT VORGIOF GNIMN GAH TR URRV. EUIJAYETN BRDOC NELSEUB
QDITE EQDAU TR TNE SMEOE, AOC MRDUC RYSELKE TNE TNLEE UACIES YEBRLE NEL
MRPWRSECUH. UACH MATNELIOE GAS A TAUU, UALFE GRPAO, GITN STLROFUH-PALVEC
BEATDLES, GNIMN PIFNT ROME NAKE YEEO NAOCSRPE. NEL AIL GAS ORT
MROMIUIATIOF, ORL GAS NEL PAOOEL RB LEMEIKIOF TNEP SDMN AS TR PAVE NEL
KISITRLS BRLFET TNEIL IOBELIRL LAOV. SNE GAS ORT LEOCELEC BRLPICAYUE YH
SIUEOME: YDT GNATEKEL SNE SAIC GAS SWRVEO IO SR ADTNRLITATIKE A TROE AS
PALVEC NEL SEUB-IPWRLTAOME, AOC YLRDFNT PL. GIMVNAP IPPECIATEUH TR
EUIJAYETN’S PIOC; AOC, BLRP TNE RYSELKATIRO RB TNE CAH AUTRFETNEL, SNE
YEUIEKEC UACH MATNELIOE TR YE EXAMTUH GNAT NE NAC LEWLESEOTEC.

GNEO, ABTEL EXAPIOIOF TNE PRTNEL, IO GNRSE MRDOTEOAOME AOC CEWRLTPEOT
SNE SRRO BRDOC SRPE LESEPYUAOME RB PL. CALMH, SNE TDLOEC NEL EHES RO TNE
CADFNTEL, SNE MRDUC AUPRST NAKE ZRIOEC IO PALIA’S ASTROISNPEOT AT NEL
YEIOF SR TNIO AOC SR SPAUU. TNELE GAS OEITNEL IO BIFDLE ORL BAME AOH
UIVEOESS YETGEEO TNE UACIES. PISS CE YRDLFN GAS WAUE AOC SIMVUH: NEL
BEATDLES, TNRDFN ORT WUAIO, GELE IOSIFOIBIMAOT; AOC SNE SWRVE KELH
UITTUE, EXMEWT IO A URG KRIME, TR PLS. ZEOVIOSRO, IO GNRSE AWWEALAOME
TNELE GAS ORTNIOF LEPALVAYUE, AOC GNR GAS EOTILEUH EOFAFEC IO UISTEOIOF
TR GNAT SNE SAIC, AOC WUAMIOF A SMLEEO IO TNE WLRWEL CILEMTIRO YEBRLE
NEL EHES.

ABTEL SITTIOF A BEG PIODTES, TNEH GELE AUU SEOT TR ROE RB TNE GIOCRGS TR
ACPILE TNE KIEG, PL. MRUUIOS ATTEOCIOF TNEP TR WRIOT RDT ITS YEADTIES,
AOC UACH MATNELIOE VIOCUH IOBRLPIOF TNEP TNAT IT GAS PDMN YETTEL GRLTN
URRVIOF AT IO TNE SDPPEL.

TNE CIOOEL GAS EXMEECIOFUH NAOCSRPE, AOC TNELE GELE AUU TNE SELKAOTS,
AOC AUU TNE ALTIMUES RB WUATE GNIMN PL. MRUUIOS NAC WLRPISEC; AOC, AS NE
NAC UIVEGISE BRLETRUC, NE TRRV NIS SEAT AT TNE YRTTRP RB TNE TAYUE, YH
NEL UACHSNIW’S CESILE, AOC URRVEC AS IB NE BEUT TNAT UIBE MRDUC BDLOISN
ORTNIOF FLEATEL. NE MALKEC AOC ATE AOC WLAISEC GITN CEUIFNTEC AUAMLITH;
AOC EKELH CISN GAS MRPPEOCEC BILST YH NIP, AOC TNEO YH SIL GIUUIAP, GNR
GAS ORG EORDFN LEMRKELEC TR EMNR GNATEKEL NIS SRO-IO-UAG SAIC, IO A
PAOOEL GNIMN EUIJAYETN GROCELEC UACH MATNELIOE MRDUC YEAL. YDT UACH
MATNELIOE SEEPEC FLATIBIEC YH TNEIL EXMESSIKE ACPILATIRO, AOC FAKE PRST
FLAMIRDS SPIUES, ESWEMIAUUH GNEO AOH CISN RO TNE TAYUE WLRKEC A ORKEUTH
TR TNEP. TNE WALTH CIC ORT SDWWUH PDMN MROKELSATIRO. EUIJAYETN GAS LEACH
TR SWEAV GNEOEKEL TNELE GAS AO RWEOIOF, YDT SNE GAS SEATEC YETGEEO
MNALURTTE AOC PISS CE YRDLFN--TNE BRLPEL RB GNRP GAS EOFAFEC IO
UISTEOIOF TR UACH MATNELIOE, AOC TNE UATTEL SAIC ORT A GRLC TR NEL AUU
TNE CIOOELTIPE. PLS. ZEOVIOSRO GAS MNIEBUH EPWURHEC IO GATMNIOF NRG
UITTUE PISS CE YRDLFN ATE, WLESSIOF NEL TR TLH SRPE RTNEL CISN AOC
BEALIOF SNE GAS IOCISWRSEC. PALIA TNRDFNT SWEAVIOF RDT RB TNE QDESTIRO,
AOC TNE FEOTUEPEO CIC ORTNIOF YDT EAT AOC ACPILE.

GNEO TNE UACIES LETDLOEC TR TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP, TNELE GAS UITTUE TR YE
CROE YDT TR NEAL UACH MATNELIOE TAUV, GNIMN SNE CIC GITNRDT AOH
IOTELPISSIRO TIUU MRBBEE MAPE IO, CEUIKELIOF NEL RWIOIRO RO EKELH
SDYZEMT IO SR CEMISIKE A PAOOEL AS WLRKEC TNAT SNE GAS ORT DSEC TR NAKE
NEL ZDCFPEOT MROTLRKELTEC. SNE IOQDILEC IOTR MNALURTTE’S CRPESTIM
MROMELOS BAPIUIALUH AOC PIODTEUH, AOC FAKE NEL A FLEAT CEAU RB ACKIME AS
TR TNE PAOAFEPEOT RB TNEP AUU; TRUC NEL NRG EKELHTNIOF RDFNT TR YE
LEFDUATEC IO SR SPAUU A BAPIUH AS NELS, AOC IOSTLDMTEC NEL AS TR TNE
MALE RB NEL MRGS AOC NEL WRDUTLH. EUIJAYETN BRDOC TNAT ORTNIOF GAS
YEOEATN TNIS FLEAT UACH’S ATTEOTIRO GNIMN MRDUC BDLOISN NEL GITN AO
RMMASIRO BRL CIMTATIOF TR RTNELS. IO TNE IOTELKAUS RB NEL CISMRDLSE GITN
PLS. MRUUIOS, SNE ACCLESSEC A KALIETH RB QDESTIROS TR PALIA AOC
EUIJAYETN, YDT ESWEMIAUUH TR TNE UATTEL, RB GNRSE MROOEMTIROS SNE VOEG
TNE UEAST, AOC GNR, SNE RYSELKEC TR PLS. MRUUIOS, GAS A KELH FEOTEEU,
WLETTH VIOC RB FILU. SNE ASVEC NEL AT CIBBELEOT TIPES NRG PAOH SISTELS
SNE NAC, GNETNEL TNEH GELE RUCEL RL HRDOFEL TNAO NELSEUB, GNETNEL AOH RB
TNEP GELE UIVEUH TR YE PALLIEC, GNETNEL TNEH GELE NAOCSRPE, GNELE TNEH
NAC YEEO ECDMATEC, GNAT MALLIAFE NEL BATNEL VEWT, AOC GNAT NAC YEEO NEL
PRTNEL’S PAICEO OAPE? EUIJAYETN BEUT AUU TNE IPWELTIOEOME RB NEL
QDESTIROS, YDT AOSGELEC TNEP KELH MRPWRSECUH. UACH MATNELIOE TNEO
RYSELKEC,--

“HRDL BATNEL’S ESTATE IS EOTAIUEC RO PL. MRUUIOS, I TNIOV? BRL HRDL
SAVE,” TDLOIOF TR MNALURTTE, “I AP FUAC RB IT; YDT RTNELGISE I SEE OR
RMMASIRO BRL EOTAIUIOF ESTATES BLRP TNE BEPAUE UIOE. IT GAS ORT TNRDFNT
OEMESSALH IO SIL UEGIS CE YRDLFN’S BAPIUH. CR HRD WUAH AOC SIOF, PISS
YEOOET?”

“A UITTUE.”

“RN TNEO--SRPE TIPE RL RTNEL GE SNAUU YE NAWWH TR NEAL HRD. RDL
IOSTLDPEOT IS A MAWITAU ROE, WLRYAYUH SDWELIRL TR ---- HRD SNAUU TLH IT
SRPE CAH. CR HRDL SISTELS WUAH AOC SIOF?”

“ROE RB TNEP CRES.”

“GNH CIC ORT HRD AUU UEALO? HRD RDFNT AUU TR NAKE UEALOEC. TNE PISS
GEYYS AUU WUAH, AOC TNEIL BATNEL NAS ORT SR FRRC AO IOMRPE AS HRDLS. CR
HRD CLAG?”

“OR, ORT AT AUU.”

“GNAT, OROE RB HRD?”

“ORT ROE.”

“TNAT IS KELH STLAOFE. YDT I SDWWRSE HRD NAC OR RWWRLTDOITH. HRDL PRTNEL
SNRDUC NAKE TAVEO HRD TR TRGO EKELH SWLIOF BRL TNE YEOEBIT RB PASTELS.”

“PH PRTNEL GRDUC NAKE OR RYZEMTIRO, YDT PH BATNEL NATES UROCRO.”

“NAS HRDL FRKELOESS UEBT HRD?”

“GE OEKEL NAC AOH FRKELOESS.”

“OR FRKELOESS! NRG GAS TNAT WRSSIYUE? BIKE CADFNTELS YLRDFNT DW AT NRPE
GITNRDT A FRKELOESS! I OEKEL NEALC RB SDMN A TNIOF. HRDL PRTNEL PDST
NAKE YEEO QDITE A SUAKE TR HRDL ECDMATIRO.”

EUIJAYETN MRDUC NALCUH NEUW SPIUIOF, AS SNE ASSDLEC NEL TNAT NAC ORT
YEEO TNE MASE.

“TNEO GNR TADFNT HRD? GNR ATTEOCEC TR HRD? GITNRDT A FRKELOESS, HRD PDST
NAKE YEEO OEFUEMTEC.”

“MRPWALEC GITN SRPE BAPIUIES, I YEUIEKE GE GELE; YDT SDMN RB DS AS
GISNEC TR UEALO OEKEL GAOTEC TNE PEAOS. GE GELE AUGAHS EOMRDLAFEC TR
LEAC, AOC NAC AUU TNE PASTELS TNAT GELE OEMESSALH. TNRSE GNR MNRSE TR YE
ICUE MELTAIOUH PIFNT.”

“AH, OR CRDYT: YDT TNAT IS GNAT A FRKELOESS GIUU WLEKEOT; AOC IB I NAC
VORGO HRDL PRTNEL, I SNRDUC NAKE ACKISEC NEL PRST STLEODRDSUH TR EOFAFE
ROE. I AUGAHS SAH TNAT ORTNIOF IS TR YE CROE IO ECDMATIRO GITNRDT STEACH
AOC LEFDUAL IOSTLDMTIRO, AOC ORYRCH YDT A FRKELOESS MAO FIKE IT. IT IS
GROCELBDU NRG PAOH BAPIUIES I NAKE YEEO TNE PEAOS RB SDWWUHIOF IO TNAT
GAH. I AP AUGAHS FUAC TR FET A HRDOF WELSRO GEUU WUAMEC RDT. BRDL OIEMES
RB PLS. ZEOVIOSRO ALE PRST CEUIFNTBDUUH SITDATEC TNLRDFN PH PEAOS; AOC
IT GAS YDT TNE RTNEL CAH TNAT I LEMRPPEOCEC AORTNEL HRDOF WELSRO, GNR
GAS PELEUH AMMICEOTAUUH PEOTIROEC TR PE, AOC TNE BAPIUH ALE QDITE
CEUIFNTEC GITN NEL. PLS. MRUUIOS, CIC I TEUU HRD RB UACH PETMAUBE’S
MAUUIOF HESTELCAH TR TNAOV PE? SNE BIOCS PISS WRWE A TLEASDLE. ‘UACH
MATNELIOE,’ SAIC SNE, ‘HRD NAKE FIKEO PE A TLEASDLE.’ ALE AOH RB HRDL
HRDOFEL SISTELS RDT, PISS YEOOET?”

“HES, PA’AP, AUU.”

“AUU! GNAT, AUU BIKE RDT AT ROME? KELH RCC! AOC HRD ROUH TNE SEMROC. TNE
HRDOFEL ROES RDT YEBRLE TNE EUCEL ALE PALLIEC! HRDL HRDOFEL SISTELS PDST
YE KELH HRDOF?”

“HES, PH HRDOFEST IS ORT SIXTEEO. WELNAWS _SNE_ IS BDUU HRDOF TR YE PDMN
IO MRPWAOH. YDT LEAUUH, PA’AP, I TNIOV IT GRDUC YE KELH NALC DWRO
HRDOFEL SISTELS TNAT TNEH SNRDUC ORT NAKE TNEIL SNALE RB SRMIETH AOC
APDSEPEOT, YEMADSE TNE EUCEL PAH ORT NAKE TNE PEAOS RL IOMUIOATIRO TR
PALLH EALUH. TNE UAST YRLO NAS AS FRRC A LIFNT TR TNE WUEASDLES RB HRDTN
AS TNE BILST. AOC TR YE VEWT YAMV RO _SDMN_ A PRTIKE! I TNIOV IT GRDUC
ORT YE KELH UIVEUH TR WLRPRTE SISTELUH ABBEMTIRO RL CEUIMAMH RB PIOC.”

“DWRO PH GRLC,” SAIC NEL UACHSNIW, “HRD FIKE HRDL RWIOIRO KELH CEMICECUH
BRL SR HRDOF A WELSRO. WLAH, GNAT IS HRDL AFE?”

“GITN TNLEE HRDOFEL SISTELS FLRGO DW,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN, SPIUIOF, “HRDL
UACHSNIW MAO NALCUH EXWEMT PE TR RGO IT.”

UACH MATNELIOE SEEPEC QDITE ASTROISNEC AT ORT LEMEIKIOF A CILEMT AOSGEL;
AOC EUIJAYETN SDSWEMTEC NELSEUB TR YE TNE BILST MLEATDLE GNR NAC EKEL
CALEC TR TLIBUE GITN SR PDMN CIFOIBIEC IPWELTIOEOME.

“HRD MAOORT YE PRLE TNAO TGEOTH, I AP SDLE,--TNELEBRLE HRD OEEC ORT
MROMEAU HRDL AFE.”

“I AP ORT ROE-AOC-TGEOTH.”

GNEO TNE FEOTUEPEO NAC ZRIOEC TNEP, AOC TEA GAS RKEL, TNE MALC TAYUES
GELE WUAMEC. UACH MATNELIOE, SIL GIUUIAP, AOC PL. AOC PLS. MRUUIOS SAT
CRGO TR QDACLIUUE; AOC AS PISS CE YRDLFN MNRSE TR WUAH AT MASSIOR, TNE
TGR FILUS NAC TNE NRORDL RB ASSISTIOF PLS. ZEOVIOSRO TR PAVE DW NEL
WALTH. TNEIL TAYUE GAS SDWELUATIKEUH STDWIC. SMALMEUH A SHUUAYUE GAS
DTTELEC TNAT CIC ORT LEUATE TR TNE FAPE, EXMEWT GNEO PLS. ZEOVIOSRO
EXWLESSEC NEL BEALS RB PISS CE YRDLFN’S YEIOF TRR NRT RL TRR MRUC, RL
NAKIOF TRR PDMN RL TRR UITTUE UIFNT. A FLEAT CEAU PRLE WASSEC AT TNE
RTNEL TAYUE. UACH MATNELIOE GAS FEOELAUUH SWEAVIOF--STATIOF TNE PISTAVES
RB TNE TNLEE RTNELS, RL LEUATIOF SRPE AOEMCRTE RB NELSEUB. PL. MRUUIOS
GAS EPWURHEC IO AFLEEIOF TR EKELHTNIOF NEL UACHSNIW SAIC, TNAOVIOF NEL
BRL EKELH BISN NE GRO, AOC AWRURFIJIOF IB NE TNRDFNT NE GRO TRR PAOH.
SIL GIUUIAP CIC ORT SAH PDMN. NE GAS STRLIOF NIS PEPRLH GITN AOEMCRTES
AOC ORYUE OAPES.

GNEO UACH MATNELIOE AOC NEL CADFNTEL NAC WUAHEC AS UROF AS TNEH MNRSE,
TNE TAYUES GELE YLRVEO DW, TNE MALLIAFE GAS RBBELEC TR PLS. MRUUIOS,
FLATEBDUUH AMMEWTEC, AOC IPPECIATEUH RLCELEC. TNE WALTH TNEO FATNELEC
LRDOC TNE BILE TR NEAL UACH MATNELIOE CETELPIOE GNAT GEATNEL TNEH GELE
TR NAKE RO TNE PRLLRG. BLRP TNESE IOSTLDMTIROS TNEH GELE SDPPROEC YH TNE
ALLIKAU RB TNE MRAMN; AOC GITN PAOH SWEEMNES RB TNAOVBDUOESS RO PL.
MRUUIOS’S SICE, AOC AS PAOH YRGS RO SIL GIUUIAP’S, TNEH CEWALTEC. AS
SRRO AS TNEH NAC CLIKEO BLRP TNE CRRL, EUIJAYETN GAS MAUUEC RO YH NEL
MRDSIO TR FIKE NEL RWIOIRO RB AUU TNAT SNE NAC SEEO AT LRSIOFS, GNIMN,
BRL MNALURTTE’S SAVE, SNE PACE PRLE BAKRDLAYUE TNAO IT LEAUUH GAS. YDT
NEL MRPPEOCATIRO, TNRDFN MRSTIOF NEL SRPE TLRDYUE, MRDUC YH OR PEAOS
SATISBH PL. MRUUIOS, AOC NE GAS KELH SRRO RYUIFEC TR TAVE NEL UACHSNIW’S
WLAISE IOTR NIS RGO NAOCS.
