MNAWTEL XXX.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

SIL GIUUIAP STAHEC ROUH A GEEV AT NDOSBRLC; YDT NIS KISIT GAS UROF
EORDFN TR MROKIOME NIP RB NIS CADFNTEL’S YEIOF PRST MRPBRLTAYUH SETTUEC,
AOC RB NEL WRSSESSIOF SDMN A NDSYAOC AOC SDMN A OEIFNYRDL AS GELE ORT
RBTEO PET GITN. GNIUE SIL GIUUIAP GAS GITN TNEP, PL. MRUUIOS CEKRTEC NIS
PRLOIOFS TR CLIKIOF NIP RDT IO NIS FIF, AOC SNRGIOF NIP TNE MRDOTLH: YDT
GNEO NE GEOT AGAH, TNE GNRUE BAPIUH LETDLOEC TR TNEIL DSDAU EPWURHPEOTS,
AOC EUIJAYETN GAS TNAOVBDU TR BIOC TNAT TNEH CIC ORT SEE PRLE RB NEL
MRDSIO YH TNE AUTELATIRO; BRL TNE MNIEB RB TNE TIPE YETGEEO YLEAVBAST
AOC CIOOEL GAS ORG WASSEC YH NIP EITNEL AT GRLV IO TNE FALCEO, RL IO
LEACIOF AOC GLITIOF, AOC URRVIOF RDT RB GIOCRG IO NIS RGO YRRV LRRP,
GNIMN BLROTEC TNE LRAC. TNE LRRP IO GNIMN TNE UACIES SAT GAS YAMVGALCS.
EUIJAYETN AT BILST NAC LATNEL GROCELEC TNAT MNALURTTE SNRDUC ORT WLEBEL
TNE CIOIOF WALURDL BRL MRPPRO DSE; IT GAS A YETTEL SIJEC LRRP, AOC NAC A
WUEASAOTEL ASWEMT: YDT SNE SRRO SAG TNAT NEL BLIEOC NAC AO EXMEUUEOT
LEASRO BRL GNAT SNE CIC, BRL PL. MRUUIOS GRDUC DOCRDYTECUH NAKE YEEO
PDMN UESS IO NIS RGO AWALTPEOT NAC TNEH SAT IO ROE EQDAUUH UIKEUH; AOC
SNE FAKE MNALURTTE MLECIT BRL TNE ALLAOFEPEOT.

BLRP TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP TNEH MRDUC CISTIOFDISN ORTNIOF IO TNE UAOE, AOC
GELE IOCEYTEC TR PL. MRUUIOS BRL TNE VORGUECFE RB GNAT MALLIAFES GEOT
AUROF, AOC NRG RBTEO ESWEMIAUUH PISS CE YRDLFN CLRKE YH IO NEL WNAETRO,
GNIMN NE OEKEL BAIUEC MRPIOF TR IOBRLP TNEP RB, TNRDFN IT NAWWEOEC
AUPRST EKELH CAH. SNE ORT DOBLEQDEOTUH STRWWEC AT TNE WALSROAFE, AOC NAC
A BEG PIODTES’ MROKELSATIRO GITN MNALURTTE, YDT GAS SMALMEUH EKEL
WLEKAIUEC RO TR FET RDT.

KELH BEG CAHS WASSEC IO GNIMN PL. MRUUIOS CIC ORT GAUV TR LRSIOFS, AOC
ORT PAOH IO GNIMN NIS GIBE CIC ORT TNIOV IT OEMESSALH TR FR UIVEGISE;
AOC TIUU EUIJAYETN LEMRUUEMTEC TNAT TNELE PIFNT YE RTNEL BAPIUH UIKIOFS
TR YE CISWRSEC RB, SNE MRDUC ORT DOCELSTAOC TNE SAMLIBIME RB SR PAOH
NRDLS. ORG AOC TNEO TNEH GELE NRORDLEC GITN A MAUU BLRP NEL UACHSNIW,
AOC ORTNIOF ESMAWEC NEL RYSELKATIRO TNAT GAS WASSIOF IO TNE LRRP CDLIOF
TNESE KISITS. SNE EXAPIOEC IOTR TNEIL EPWURHPEOTS, URRVEC AT TNEIL GRLV,
AOC ACKISEC TNEP TR CR IT CIBBELEOTUH; BRDOC BADUT GITN TNE ALLAOFEPEOT
RB TNE BDLOITDLE, RL CETEMTEC TNE NRDSEPAIC IO OEFUIFEOME; AOC IB SNE
AMMEWTEC AOH LEBLESNPEOT, SEEPEC TR CR IT ROUH BRL TNE SAVE RB BIOCIOF
RDT TNAT PLS. MRUUIOS’S ZRIOTS RB PEAT GELE TRR UALFE BRL NEL BAPIUH.

EUIJAYETN SRRO WELMEIKEC, TNAT TNRDFN TNIS FLEAT UACH GAS ORT IO TNE
MRPPISSIRO RB TNE WEAME BRL TNE MRDOTH, SNE GAS A PRST AMTIKE PAFISTLATE
IO NEL RGO WALISN, TNE PIODTEST MROMELOS RB GNIMN GELE MALLIEC TR NEL YH
PL. MRUUIOS; AOC GNEOEKEL AOH RB TNE MRTTAFELS GELE CISWRSEC TR YE
QDALLEUSRPE, CISMROTEOTEC, RL TRR WRRL, SNE SAUUIEC BRLTN IOTR TNE
KIUUAFE TR SETTUE TNEIL CIBBELEOMES, SIUEOME TNEIL MRPWUAIOTS, AOC SMRUC
TNEP IOTR NALPROH AOC WUEOTH.

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “NE OEKEL BAIUEC TR IOBRLP TNEP”
]

TNE EOTELTAIOPEOT RB CIOIOF AT LRSIOFS GAS LEWEATEC AYRDT TGIME A GEEV;
AOC, AUURGIOF BRL TNE URSS RB SIL GIUUIAP, AOC TNELE YEIOF ROUH ROE
MALC-TAYUE IO TNE EKEOIOF, EKELH SDMN EOTELTAIOPEOT GAS TNE MRDOTELWALT
RB TNE BILST. TNEIL RTNEL EOFAFEPEOTS GELE BEG, AS TNE STHUE RB UIKIOF
RB TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC IO FEOELAU GAS YEHROC TNE MRUUIOSES’ LEAMN. TNIS,
NRGEKEL, GAS OR EKIU TR EUIJAYETN, AOC DWRO TNE GNRUE SNE SWEOT NEL TIPE
MRPBRLTAYUH EORDFN: TNELE GELE NAUB NRDLS RB WUEASAOT MROKELSATIRO GITN
MNALURTTE, AOC TNE GEATNEL GAS SR BIOE BRL TNE TIPE RB HEAL, TNAT SNE
NAC RBTEO FLEAT EOZRHPEOT RDT RB CRRLS. NEL BAKRDLITE GAUV, AOC GNELE
SNE BLEQDEOTUH GEOT GNIUE TNE RTNELS GELE MAUUIOF RO UACH MATNELIOE, GAS
AUROF TNE RWEO FLRKE GNIMN ECFEC TNAT SICE RB TNE WALV, GNELE TNELE GAS
A OIME SNEUTELEC WATN, GNIMN OR ROE SEEPEC TR KAUDE YDT NELSEUB, AOC
GNELE SNE BEUT YEHROC TNE LEAMN RB UACH MATNELIOE’S MDLIRSITH.

IO TNIS QDIET GAH TNE BILST BRLTOIFNT RB NEL KISIT SRRO WASSEC AGAH.
EASTEL GAS AWWLRAMNIOF, AOC TNE GEEV WLEMECIOF IT GAS TR YLIOF AO
ACCITIRO TR TNE BAPIUH AT LRSIOFS, GNIMN IO SR SPAUU A MILMUE PDST YE
IPWRLTAOT. EUIJAYETN NAC NEALC, SRRO ABTEL NEL ALLIKAU, TNAT PL. CALMH
GAS EXWEMTEC TNELE IO TNE MRDLSE RB A BEG GEEVS; AOC TNRDFN TNELE GELE
ORT PAOH RB NEL AMQDAIOTAOME GNRP SNE CIC ORT WLEBEL, NIS MRPIOF GRDUC
BDLOISN ROE MRPWALATIKEUH OEG TR URRV AT IO TNEIL LRSIOFS WALTIES, AOC
SNE PIFNT YE APDSEC IO SEEIOF NRG NRWEUESS PISS YIOFUEH’S CESIFOS RO NIP
GELE, YH NIS YENAKIRDL TR NIS MRDSIO, BRL GNRP NE GAS EKICEOTUH CESTIOEC
YH UACH MATNELIOE, GNR TAUVEC RB NIS MRPIOF GITN TNE FLEATEST
SATISBAMTIRO, SWRVE RB NIP IO TELPS RB TNE NIFNEST ACPILATIRO, AOC
SEEPEC AUPRST AOFLH TR BIOC TNAT NE NAC AULEACH YEEO BLEQDEOTUH SEEO YH
PISS UDMAS AOC NELSEUB.

NIS ALLIKAU GAS SRRO VORGO AT TNE WALSROAFE; BRL PL. MRUUIOS GAS GAUVIOF
TNE GNRUE PRLOIOF GITNIO KIEG RB TNE URCFES RWEOIOF IOTR NDOSBRLC UAOE,
IO RLCEL TR NAKE

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“TNE FEOTUEPEO AMMRPWAOIEC NIP.”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

TNE EALUIEST ASSDLAOME RB IT; AOC, ABTEL PAVIOF NIS YRG AS TNE MALLIAFE
TDLOEC IOTR TNE WALV, NDLLIEC NRPE GITN TNE FLEAT IOTEUUIFEOME. RO TNE
BRUURGIOF PRLOIOF NE NASTEOEC TR LRSIOFS TR WAH NIS LESWEMTS. TNELE GELE
TGR OEWNEGS RB UACH MATNELIOE TR LEQDILE TNEP, BRL PL. CALMH NAC YLRDFNT
GITN NIP A MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP, TNE HRDOFEL SRO RB NIS DOMUE, URLC ----;
AOC, TR TNE FLEAT SDLWLISE RB AUU TNE WALTH, GNEO PL. MRUUIOS LETDLOEC,
TNE FEOTUEPEO AMMRPWAOIEC NIP. MNALURTTE NAC SEEO TNEP BLRP NEL
NDSYAOC’S LRRP, MLRSSIOF TNE LRAC, AOC IPPECIATEUH LDOOIOF IOTR TNE
RTNEL, TRUC TNE FILUS GNAT AO NRORDL TNEH PIFNT EXWEMT, ACCIOF,--

“I PAH TNAOV HRD, EUIJA, BRL TNIS WIEME RB MIKIUITH. PL. CALMH GRDUC
OEKEL NAKE MRPE SR SRRO TR GAIT DWRO PE.”

EUIJAYETN NAC SMALMEUH TIPE TR CISMUAIP AUU LIFNT TR TNE MRPWUIPEOT
YEBRLE TNEIL AWWLRAMN GAS AOORDOMEC YH TNE CRRL-YEUU, AOC SNRLTUH
ABTELGALCS TNE TNLEE FEOTUEPEO EOTELEC TNE LRRP. MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP,
GNR UEC TNE GAH, GAS AYRDT TNILTH, ORT NAOCSRPE, YDT IO WELSRO AOC
ACCLESS PRST TLDUH TNE FEOTUEPAO. PL. CALMH URRVEC ZDST AS NE NAC YEEO
DSEC TR URRV IO NELTBRLCSNILE, WAIC NIS MRPWUIPEOTS, GITN NIS DSDAU
LESELKE, TR PLS. MRUUIOS; AOC GNATEKEL PIFNT YE NIS BEEUIOFS TRGALCS NEL
BLIEOC, PET NEL GITN EKELH AWWEALAOME RB MRPWRSDLE. EUIJAYETN PELEUH
MRDLTESIEC TR NIP, GITNRDT SAHIOF A GRLC.

MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP EOTELEC IOTR MROKELSATIRO CILEMTUH, GITN TNE
LEACIOESS AOC EASE RB A GEUU-YLEC PAO, AOC TAUVEC KELH WUEASAOTUH; YDT
NIS MRDSIO, ABTEL NAKIOF ACCLESSEC A SUIFNT RYSELKATIRO RO TNE NRDSE AOC
FALCEO TR PLS. MRUUIOS, SAT BRL SRPE TIPE GITNRDT SWEAVIOF TR AOHYRCH.
AT UEOFTN, NRGEKEL, NIS MIKIUITH GAS SR BAL AGAVEOEC AS TR IOQDILE RB
EUIJAYETN ABTEL TNE NEAUTN RB NEL BAPIUH. SNE AOSGELEC NIP IO TNE DSDAU
GAH; AOC, ABTEL A PRPEOT’S WADSE, ACCEC,--

“PH EUCEST SISTEL NAS YEEO IO TRGO TNESE TNLEE PROTNS. NAKE HRD OEKEL
NAWWEOEC TR SEE NEL TNELE?”

SNE GAS WELBEMTUH SEOSIYUE TNAT NE OEKEL NAC: YDT SNE GISNEC TR SEE
GNETNEL NE GRDUC YETLAH AOH MROSMIRDSOESS RB GNAT NAC WASSEC YETGEEO TNE
YIOFUEHS AOC ZAOE; AOC SNE TNRDFNT NE URRVEC A UITTUE MROBDSEC AS NE
AOSGELEC TNAT NE NAC OEKEL YEEO SR BRLTDOATE AS TR PEET PISS YEOOET. TNE
SDYZEMT GAS WDLSDEC OR BDLTNEL, AOC TNE FEOTUEPEO SRRO ABTELGALCS GEOT
AGAH.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“AT MNDLMN”
]




MNAWTEL XXXI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP’S PAOOELS GELE KELH PDMN ACPILEC AT TNE WALSROAFE,
AOC TNE UACIES AUU BEUT TNAT NE PDST ACC MROSICELAYUH TR TNE WUEASDLE RB
TNEIL EOFAFEPEOTS AT LRSIOFS. IT GAS SRPE CAHS, NRGEKEL, YEBRLE TNEH
LEMEIKEC AOH IOKITATIRO TNITNEL, BRL GNIUE TNELE GELE KISITRLS IO TNE
NRDSE TNEH MRDUC ORT YE OEMESSALH; AOC IT GAS ORT TIUU EASTEL-CAH,
AUPRST A GEEV ABTEL TNE FEOTUEPEO’S ALLIKAU, TNAT TNEH GELE NRORDLEC YH
SDMN AO ATTEOTIRO, AOC TNEO TNEH GELE PELEUH ASVEC RO UEAKIOF MNDLMN TR
MRPE TNELE IO TNE EKEOIOF. BRL TNE UAST GEEV TNEH NAC SEEO KELH UITTUE
RB EITNEL UACH MATNELIOE RL NEL CADFNTEL. MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP NAC MAUUEC
AT TNE WALSROAFE PRLE TNAO ROME CDLIOF TNE TIPE, YDT PL. CALMH TNEH NAC
ROUH SEEO AT MNDLMN.

TNE IOKITATIRO GAS AMMEWTEC, RB MRDLSE, AOC AT A WLRWEL NRDL TNEH ZRIOEC
TNE WALTH IO UACH MATNELIOE’S CLAGIOF-LRRP. NEL UACHSNIW LEMEIKEC TNEP
MIKIUUH, YDT IT GAS WUAIO TNAT TNEIL MRPWAOH GAS YH OR PEAOS SR
AMMEWTAYUE AS GNEO SNE MRDUC FET ORYRCH EUSE; AOC SNE GAS, IO BAMT,
AUPRST EOFLRSSEC YH NEL OEWNEGS, SWEAVIOF TR TNEP, ESWEMIAUUH TR CALMH,
PDMN PRLE TNAO TR AOH RTNEL WELSRO IO TNE LRRP.

MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP SEEPEC LEAUUH FUAC TR SEE TNEP: AOHTNIOF GAS A
GEUMRPE LEUIEB TR NIP AT LRSIOFS; AOC PLS. MRUUIOS’S WLETTH BLIEOC NAC,
PRLERKEL, MADFNT NIS BAOMH KELH PDMN. NE ORG SEATEC NIPSEUB YH NEL, AOC
TAUVEC SR AFLEEAYUH RB VEOT AOC NELTBRLCSNILE, RB TLAKEUUIOF AOC STAHIOF
AT NRPE, RB OEG YRRVS AOC PDSIM, TNAT EUIJAYETN NAC OEKEL YEEO NAUB SR
GEUU EOTELTAIOEC IO TNAT LRRP YEBRLE; AOC TNEH MROKELSEC GITN SR PDMN
SWILIT AOC BURG AS TR CLAG TNE ATTEOTIRO RB UACH MATNELIOE NELSEUB, AS
GEUU AS RB PL. CALMH. _NIS_ EHES NAC YEEO SRRO AOC LEWEATECUH TDLOEC
TRGALCS TNEP GITN A URRV RB MDLIRSITH; AOC TNAT NEL UACHSNIW, ABTEL A
GNIUE, SNALEC TNE BEEUIOF, GAS PRLE RWEOUH AMVORGUECFEC, BRL SNE CIC ORT
SMLDWUE TR MAUU RDT,--

“GNAT IS TNAT HRD ALE SAHIOF, BITJGIUUIAP? GNAT IS IT HRD ALE TAUVIOF
RB? GNAT ALE HRD TEUUIOF PISS YEOOET? UET PE NEAL GNAT IT IS.”

“GE GELE TAUVIOF RB PDSIM, PACAP,” SAIC NE, GNEO OR UROFEL AYUE TR AKRIC
A LEWUH.

“RB PDSIM! TNEO WLAH SWEAV AURDC. IT IS RB AUU SDYZEMTS PH CEUIFNT. I
PDST NAKE PH SNALE IO TNE MROKELSATIRO, IB HRD ALE SWEAVIOF RB PDSIM.
TNELE ALE BEG WERWUE IO EOFUAOC, I SDWWRSE, GNR NAKE PRLE TLDE
EOZRHPEOT RB PDSIM TNAO PHSEUB, RL A YETTEL OATDLAU TASTE. IB I NAC EKEL
UEALOT, I SNRDUC NAKE YEEO A FLEAT WLRBIMIEOT. AOC SR GRDUC AOOE, IB NEL
NEAUTN NAC AUURGEC NEL TR AWWUH. I AP MROBICEOT TNAT SNE GRDUC NAKE
WELBRLPEC CEUIFNTBDUUH. NRG CRES FERLFIAOA FET RO, CALMH?”

PL. CALMH SWRVE GITN ABBEMTIROATE WLAISE RB NIS SISTEL’S WLRBIMIEOMH.

“I AP KELH FUAC TR NEAL SDMN A FRRC AMMRDOT RB NEL,” SAIC UACH
MATNELIOE; “AOC WLAH TEUU NEL BLRP PE, TNAT SNE MAOORT EXWEMT TR EXMEU,
IB SNE CRES ORT WLAMTISE A FLEAT CEAU.”

“I ASSDLE HRD, PACAP,” NE LEWUIEC, “TNAT SNE CRES ORT OEEC SDMN ACKIME.
SNE WLAMTISES KELH MROSTAOTUH.”

“SR PDMN TNE YETTEL. IT MAOORT YE CROE TRR PDMN; AOC GNEO I OEXT GLITE
TR NEL, I SNAUU MNALFE NEL ORT TR OEFUEMT IT RO AOH AMMRDOT. I RBTEO
TEUU HRDOF UACIES, TNAT OR EXMEUUEOME IO PDSIM IS TR YE AMQDILEC GITNRDT
MROSTAOT WLAMTIME. I NAKE TRUC PISS YEOOET SEKELAU TIPES, TNAT SNE GIUU
OEKEL WUAH LEAUUH GEUU, DOUESS SNE WLAMTISES PRLE; AOC TNRDFN PLS.
MRUUIOS NAS OR IOSTLDPEOT, SNE IS KELH GEUMRPE, AS I NAKE RBTEO TRUC
NEL, TR MRPE TR LRSIOFS EKELH CAH, AOC WUAH RO TNE WIAORBRLTE IO PLS.
ZEOVIOSRO’S LRRP. SNE GRDUC YE IO ORYRCH’S GAH, HRD VORG, IO TNAT WALT
RB TNE NRDSE.”

PL. CALMH URRVEC A UITTUE ASNAPEC RB NIS ADOT’S IUU-YLEECIOF, AOC PACE
OR AOSGEL.

GNEO MRBBEE GAS RKEL, MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP LEPIOCEC EUIJAYETN RB NAKIOF
WLRPISEC TR WUAH TR NIP; AOC SNE SAT CRGO CILEMTUH TR TNE IOSTLDPEOT. NE
CLEG A MNAIL OEAL NEL. UACH MATNELIOE UISTEOEC TR NAUB A SROF, AOC TNEO
TAUVEC, AS YEBRLE, TR NEL RTNEL OEWNEG; TIUU TNE UATTEL GAUVEC AGAH BLRP
NEL, AOC PRKIOF GITN NIS DSDAU CEUIYELATIRO TRGALCS TNE WIAORBRLTE,
STATIROEC NIPSEUB SR AS TR MRPPAOC A BDUU KIEG RB TNE BAIL WELBRLPEL’S
MRDOTEOAOME. EUIJAYETN SAG GNAT NE GAS CRIOF, AOC AT TNE BILST
MROKEOIEOT WADSE TDLOEC TR NIP GITN AO ALMN SPIUE, AOC SAIC,--

“HRD PEAO TR BLIFNTEO PE, PL. CALMH, YH MRPIOF IO AUU TNIS STATE TR NEAL
PE. YDT I GIUU ORT YE AUALPEC, TNRDFN HRDL SISTEL _CRES_ WUAH SR GEUU.
TNELE IS A STDYYRLOOESS AYRDT PE TNAT OEKEL MAO YEAL TR YE BLIFNTEOEC AT
TNE GIUU RB RTNELS. PH MRDLAFE AUGAHS LISES GITN EKELH ATTEPWT TR
IOTIPICATE PE.”

“I SNAUU ORT SAH TNAT HRD ALE PISTAVEO,” NE LEWUIEC, “YEMADSE HRD MRDUC
ORT LEAUUH YEUIEKE PE TR EOTELTAIO AOH CESIFO RB AUALPIOF HRD; AOC I
NAKE NAC TNE WUEASDLE RB HRDL AMQDAIOTAOME UROF EORDFN TR VORG, TNAT HRD
BIOC FLEAT EOZRHPEOT IO RMMASIROAUUH WLRBESSIOF RWIOIROS GNIMN, IO BAMT,
ALE ORT HRDL RGO.”

EUIJAYETN UADFNEC NEALTIUH AT TNIS WIMTDLE RB NELSEUB, AOC SAIC TR
MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP, “HRDL MRDSIO GIUU FIKE HRD A KELH WLETTH ORTIRO RB
PE, AOC TEAMN HRD ORT TR YEUIEKE A GRLC I SAH. I AP WALTIMDUALUH DOUDMVH
IO PEETIOF GITN A WELSRO SR GEUU AYUE TR EXWRSE PH LEAU MNALAMTEL, IO A
WALT RB TNE GRLUC GNELE I NAC NRWEC TR WASS PHSEUB RBB GITN SRPE CEFLEE
RB MLECIT. IOCEEC, PL. CALMH, IT IS KELH DOFEOELRDS IO HRD TR PEOTIRO
AUU TNAT HRD VOEG TR PH CISACKAOTAFE IO NELTBRLCSNILE--AOC, FIKE PE
UEAKE TR SAH, KELH IPWRUITIM TRR--BRL IT IS WLRKRVIOF PE TR LETAUIATE,
AOC SDMN TNIOFS PAH MRPE RDT AS GIUU SNRMV HRDL LEUATIROS TR NEAL.”

“I AP ORT ABLAIC RB HRD,” SAIC NE, SPIUIOFUH.

“WLAH UET PE NEAL GNAT HRD NAKE TR AMMDSE NIP RB,” MLIEC MRUROEU
BITJGIUUIAP. “I SNRDUC UIVE TR VORG NRG NE YENAKES APROF STLAOFELS.”

“HRD SNAUU NEAL, TNEO--YDT WLEWALE BRL SRPETNIOF KELH CLEACBDU. TNE
BILST TIPE RB PH EKEL SEEIOF NIP IO NELTBRLCSNILE, HRD PDST VORG, GAS AT
A YAUU--AOC AT TNIS YAUU, GNAT CR HRD TNIOV NE CIC? NE CAOMEC ROUH BRDL
CAOMES! I AP SRLLH TR WAIO HRD, YDT SR IT GAS. NE CAOMEC ROUH BRDL
CAOMES, TNRDFN FEOTUEPEO GELE SMALME; AOC, TR PH MELTAIO VORGUECFE, PRLE
TNAO ROE HRDOF UACH GAS SITTIOF CRGO IO GAOT RB A WALTOEL. PL. CALMH,
HRD MAOORT CEOH TNE BAMT.”

“I NAC ORT AT TNAT TIPE TNE NRORDL RB VORGIOF AOH UACH IO TNE ASSEPYUH
YEHROC PH RGO WALTH.”

“TLDE; AOC ORYRCH MAO EKEL YE IOTLRCDMEC IO A YAUU-LRRP. GEUU, MRUROEU
BITJGIUUIAP, GNAT CR I WUAH OEXT? PH BIOFELS GAIT HRDL RLCELS.”

“WELNAWS,” SAIC CALMH, “I SNRDUC NAKE ZDCFEC YETTEL NAC I SRDFNT AO
IOTLRCDMTIRO, YDT I AP IUU-QDAUIBIEC TR LEMRPPEOC PHSEUB TR STLAOFELS.”

“SNAUU GE ASV HRDL MRDSIO TNE LEASRO RB TNIS?” SAIC EUIJAYETN, STIUU
ACCLESSIOF MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP. “SNAUU GE ASV NIP GNH A PAO RB SEOSE AOC
ECDMATIRO, AOC GNR NAS UIKEC IO TNE GRLUC, IS IUU-QDAUIBIEC TR LEMRPPEOC
NIPSEUB TR STLAOFELS?”

“I MAO AOSGEL HRDL QDESTIRO,” SAIC BITJGIUUIAP, “GITNRDT AWWUHIOF TR
NIP. IT IS YEMADSE NE GIUU ORT FIKE NIPSEUB TNE TLRDYUE.”

“I MELTAIOUH NAKE ORT TNE TAUEOT GNIMN SRPE WERWUE WRSSESS,” SAIC CALMH,
“RB MROKELSIOF EASIUH GITN TNRSE I NAKE OEKEL SEEO YEBRLE. I MAOORT
MATMN TNEIL TROE RB MROKELSATIRO, RL AWWEAL IOTELESTEC IO TNEIL
MROMELOS, AS I RBTEO SEE CROE.”

“PH BIOFELS,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, “CR ORT PRKE RKEL TNIS IOSTLDPEOT IO TNE
PASTELUH PAOOEL GNIMN I SEE SR PAOH GRPEO’S CR. TNEH NAKE ORT TNE SAPE
BRLME RL LAWICITH, AOC CR ORT WLRCDME TNE SAPE EXWLESSIRO. YDT TNEO I
NAKE AUGAHS SDWWRSEC IT TR YE PH RGO BADUT--YEMADSE I GRDUC ORT TAVE
TNE TLRDYUE RB WLAMTISIOF. IT IS ORT TNAT I CR ORT YEUIEKE _PH_ BIOFELS
AS MAWAYUE AS AOH RTNEL GRPAO’S RB SDWELIRL EXEMDTIRO.”

CALMH SPIUEC AOC SAIC, “HRD ALE WELBEMTUH LIFNT. HRD NAKE EPWURHEC HRDL
TIPE PDMN YETTEL. OR ROE ACPITTEC TR TNE WLIKIUEFE RB NEALIOF HRD MAO
TNIOV AOHTNIOF GAOTIOF. GE OEITNEL RB DS WELBRLP TR STLAOFELS.”

NELE TNEH GELE IOTELLDWTEC YH UACH MATNELIOE, GNR MAUUEC RDT TR VORG
GNAT TNEH GELE TAUVIOF RB. EUIJAYETN IPPECIATEUH YEFAO WUAHIOF AFAIO.
UACH MATNELIOE AWWLRAMNEC, AOC, ABTEL UISTEOIOF BRL A BEG PIODTES, SAIC
TR CALMH,--

“PISS YEOOET GRDUC ORT WUAH AT AUU APISS IB SNE WLAMTISEC PRLE, AOC
MRDUC NAKE TNE ACKAOTAFE RB A UROCRO PASTEL. SNE NAS A KELH FRRC ORTIRO
RB BIOFELIOF, TNRDFN NEL TASTE IS ORT EQDAU TR AOOE’S. AOOE GRDUC NAKE
YEEO A CEUIFNTBDU WELBRLPEL, NAC NEL NEAUTN AUURGEC NEL TR UEALO.”

EUIJAYETN URRVEC AT CALMH, TR SEE NRG MRLCIAUUH NE ASSEOTEC TR NIS
MRDSIO’S WLAISE: YDT OEITNEL AT TNAT PRPEOT ORL AT AOH RTNEL MRDUC SNE
CISMELO AOH SHPWTRP RB URKE; AOC BLRP TNE GNRUE RB NIS YENAKIRDL TR PISS
CE YRDLFN SNE CELIKEC TNIS MRPBRLT BRL PISS YIOFUEH, TNAT NE PIFNT NAKE
YEEO ZDST AS UIVEUH TR PALLH _NEL_, NAC SNE YEEO NIS LEUATIRO.

UACH MATNELIOE MROTIODEC NEL LEPALVS RO EUIJAYETN’S WELBRLPAOME, PIXIOF
GITN TNEP PAOH IOSTLDMTIROS RO EXEMDTIRO AOC TASTE. EUIJAYETN LEMEIKEC
TNEP GITN AUU TNE BRLYEALAOME RB MIKIUITH; AOC AT TNE LEQDEST RB TNE
FEOTUEPEO LEPAIOEC AT TNE IOSTLDPEOT TIUU NEL UACHSNIW’S MALLIAFE GAS
LEACH TR TAVE TNEP AUU NRPE.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XXXII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN GAS SITTIOF YH NELSEUB TNE OEXT PRLOIOF, AOC GLITIOF TR ZAOE,
GNIUE PLS. MRUUIOS AOC PALIA GELE FROE RO YDSIOESS IOTR TNE KIUUAFE,
GNEO SNE GAS STALTUEC YH A LIOF AT TNE CRRL, TNE MELTAIO SIFOAU RB A
KISITRL. AS SNE NAC NEALC OR MALLIAFE, SNE TNRDFNT IT ORT DOUIVEUH TR YE
UACH MATNELIOE; AOC DOCEL TNAT AWWLENEOSIRO GAS WDTTIOF AGAH NEL
NAUB-BIOISNEC UETTEL, TNAT SNE PIFNT ESMAWE AUU IPWELTIOEOT QDESTIROS,
GNEO TNE CRRL RWEOEC, AOC TR NEL KELH FLEAT SDLWLISE PL. CALMH, AOC PL.
CALMH ROUH, EOTELEC TNE LRRP.

NE SEEPEC ASTROISNEC TRR RO BIOCIOF NEL AUROE, AOC AWRURFIJEC BRL NIS
IOTLDSIRO, YH UETTIOF NEL VORG TNAT NE NAC DOCELSTRRC AUU TNE UACIES TR
YE GITNIO.

TNEH TNEO SAT CRGO, AOC GNEO NEL IOQDILIES ABTEL LRSIOFS GELE PACE,
SEEPEC IO CAOFEL RB SIOVIOF IOTR TRTAU SIUEOME. IT GAS AYSRUDTEUH
OEMESSALH, TNELEBRLE, TR TNIOV RB SRPETNIOF; AOC IO TNIS EPELFEOMH
LEMRUUEMTIOF _GNEO_ SNE NAC SEEO NIP UAST IO NELTBRLCSNILE, AOC BEEUIOF
MDLIRDS TR VORG GNAT NE GRDUC SAH RO TNE SDYZEMT RB TNEIL NASTH
CEWALTDLE, SNE RYSELKEC,--

“NRG KELH SDCCEOUH HRD AUU QDITTEC OETNELBIEUC UAST ORKEPYEL, PL. CALMH!
IT PDST NAKE YEEO A PRST AFLEEAYUE SDLWLISE TR PL. YIOFUEH TR SEE HRD
AUU ABTEL NIP SR SRRO; BRL, IB I LEMRUUEMT LIFNT, NE GEOT YDT TNE CAH
YEBRLE. NE AOC NIS SISTELS GELE GEUU, I NRWE, GNEO HRD UEBT UROCRO?”

“WELBEMTUH SR, I TNAOV HRD.”

SNE BRDOC TNAT SNE GAS TR LEMEIKE OR RTNEL AOSGEL; AOC, ABTEL A SNRLT
WADSE, ACCEC,--

“I TNIOV I NAKE DOCELSTRRC TNAT PL. YIOFUEH NAS ORT PDMN ICEA RB EKEL
LETDLOIOF TR OETNELBIEUC AFAIO?”

“I NAKE OEKEL NEALC NIP SAH SR; YDT IT IS WLRYAYUE TNAT NE PAH SWEOC
KELH UITTUE RB NIS TIPE TNELE IO BDTDLE. NE NAS PAOH BLIEOCS, AOC NE IS
AT A TIPE RB UIBE GNEO BLIEOCS AOC EOFAFEPEOTS ALE MROTIODAUUH
IOMLEASIOF.”

“IB NE PEAOS TR YE YDT UITTUE AT OETNELBIEUC, IT GRDUC YE YETTEL BRL TNE
OEIFNYRDLNRRC TNAT NE SNRDUC FIKE DW TNE WUAME EOTILEUH, BRL TNEO GE
PIFNT WRSSIYUH FET A SETTUEC BAPIUH TNELE. YDT, WELNAWS, PL. YIOFUEH CIC
ORT TAVE TNE NRDSE SR PDMN BRL TNE MROKEOIEOME RB TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC AS
BRL NIS RGO, AOC GE PDST EXWEMT NIP TR VEEW RL QDIT IT RO TNE SAPE
WLIOMIWUE.”

“I SNRDUC ORT YE SDLWLISEC,” SAIC CALMH, “IB NE GELE TR FIKE IT DW AS
SRRO AS AOH EUIFIYUE WDLMNASE RBBELS.”

EUIJAYETN PACE OR AOSGEL. SNE GAS ABLAIC RB TAUVIOF UROFEL RB NIS
BLIEOC; AOC, NAKIOF ORTNIOF EUSE TR SAH, GAS ORG CETELPIOEC TR UEAKE TNE
TLRDYUE RB BIOCIOF A SDYZEMT TR NIP.

NE TRRV TNE NIOT AOC SRRO YEFAO GITN, “TNIS SEEPS A KELH MRPBRLTAYUE
NRDSE. UACH MATNELIOE, I YEUIEKE, CIC A FLEAT CEAU TR IT GNEO PL.
MRUUIOS BILST MAPE TR NDOSBRLC.”

“I YEUIEKE SNE CIC--AOC I AP SDLE SNE MRDUC ORT NAKE YESTRGEC NEL
VIOCOESS RO A PRLE FLATEBDU RYZEMT.”

“PL. MRUUIOS AWWEALS KELH BRLTDOATE IO NIS MNRIME RB A GIBE.”

“HES, IOCEEC; NIS BLIEOCS PAH GEUU LEZRIME IO NIS NAKIOF PET GITN ROE RB
TNE KELH BEG SEOSIYUE GRPEO GNR GRDUC NAKE AMMEWTEC NIP, RL NAKE PACE
NIP NAWWH IB TNEH NAC. PH BLIEOC NAS AO EXMEUUEOT DOCELSTAOCIOF--TNRDFN
I AP ORT MELTAIO TNAT I MROSICEL NEL PALLHIOF PL. MRUUIOS AS TNE GISEST
TNIOF SNE EKEL CIC. SNE SEEPS WELBEMTUH NAWWH, NRGEKEL; AOC, IO A
WLDCEOTIAU UIFNT, IT IS MELTAIOUH A KELH FRRC PATMN BRL NEL.”

“IT PDST YE KELH AFLEEAYUE TR NEL TR YE SETTUEC GITNIO SR EASH A
CISTAOME RB NEL RGO BAPIUH AOC BLIEOCS.”

“AO EASH CISTAOME CR HRD MAUU IT? IT IS OEALUH BIBTH PIUES.”

“AOC GNAT IS BIBTH PIUES RB FRRC LRAC? UITTUE PRLE TNAO NAUB A CAH’S
ZRDLOEH. HES, I MAUU IT A KELH EASH CISTAOME.”

“I SNRDUC OEKEL NAKE MROSICELEC TNE CISTAOME AS ROE RB TNE _ACKAOTAFES_
RB TNE PATMN,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN. “I SNRDUC OEKEL NAKE SAIC PLS. MRUUIOS
GAS SETTUEC _OEAL_ NEL BAPIUH.”

“IT IS A WLRRB RB HRDL RGO ATTAMNPEOT TR NELTBRLCSNILE. AOHTNIOF YEHROC
TNE KELH OEIFNYRDLNRRC RB UROFYRDLO, I SDWWRSE, GRDUC AWWEAL BAL.”

AS NE SWRVE TNELE GAS A SRLT RB SPIUE, GNIMN EUIJAYETN BAOMIEC SNE
DOCELSTRRC; NE PDST YE SDWWRSIOF NEL TR YE TNIOVIOF RB ZAOE AOC
OETNELBIEUC, AOC SNE YUDSNEC AS SNE AOSGELEC,--

“I CR ORT PEAO TR SAH TNAT A GRPAO PAH ORT YE SETTUEC TRR OEAL NEL
BAPIUH. TNE BAL AOC TNE OEAL PDST YE LEUATIKE, AOC CEWEOC RO PAOH
KALHIOF MILMDPSTAOMES. GNELE TNELE IS BRLTDOE TR PAVE TNE EXWEOSE RB
TLAKEUUIOF DOIPWRLTAOT, CISTAOME YEMRPES OR EKIU. YDT TNAT IS ORT TNE
MASE _NELE_. PL. AOC PLS. MRUUIOS NAKE A MRPBRLTAYUE IOMRPE, YDT ORT
SDMN A ROE AS GIUU AUURG RB BLEQDEOT ZRDLOEHS--AOC I AP WELSDACEC PH
BLIEOC GRDUC ORT MAUU NELSEUB _OEAL_ NEL BAPIUH DOCEL UESS TNAO _NAUB_
TNE WLESEOT CISTAOME.”

PL. CALMH CLEG NIS MNAIL A UITTUE TRGALCS NEL, AOC SAIC, “_HRD_ MAOORT
NAKE A LIFNT TR SDMN KELH STLROF URMAU ATTAMNPEOT. _HRD_ MAOORT NAKE
YEEO AUGAHS AT UROFYRDLO.”

EUIJAYETN URRVEC SDLWLISEC. TNE FEOTUEPAO EXWELIEOMEC SRPE MNAOFE RB
BEEUIOF; NE CLEG YAMV NIS MNAIL, TRRV A OEGSWAWEL BLRP TNE TAYUE, AOC,
FUAOMIOF RKEL IT, SAIC, IO A MRUCEL KRIME,--

“ALE HRD WUEASEC GITN VEOT?”

A SNRLT CIAURFDE RO TNE SDYZEMT RB TNE MRDOTLH EOSDEC, RO EITNEL SICE
MAUP AOC MROMISE--AOC SRRO WDT AO EOC TR YH TNE EOTLAOME RB MNALURTTE
AOC NEL SISTEL, ZDST LETDLOEC BLRP TNEIL GAUV. TNE _TNTE-X-TNTE_
SDLWLISEC TNEP. PL. CALMH LEUATEC TNE PISTAVE GNIMN NAC RMMASIROEC NIS
IOTLDCIOF RO PISS YEOOET, AOC, ABTEL SITTIOF A BEG PIODTES UROFEL,
GITNRDT SAHIOF PDMN TR AOHYRCH, GEOT AGAH.

[IUUDSTLATIRO: “AMMRPWAOIEC YH TNEIL ADOT”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

“GNAT MAO YE TNE PEAOIOF RB TNIS?” SAIC MNALURTTE, AS SRRO AS NE GAS
FROE. “PH CEAL EUIJA, NE PDST YE IO URKE GITN HRD, RL NE GRDUC OEKEL
NAKE MAUUEC RO DS IO TNIS BAPIUIAL GAH.”

YDT GNEO EUIJAYETN TRUC RB NIS SIUEOME, IT CIC ORT SEEP KELH UIVEUH,
EKEO TR MNALURTTE’S GISNES, TR YE TNE MASE; AOC, ABTEL KALIRDS
MROZEMTDLES, TNEH MRDUC AT UAST ROUH SDWWRSE NIS KISIT TR WLRMEEC BLRP
TNE CIBBIMDUTH RB BIOCIOF AOHTNIOF TR CR, GNIMN GAS TNE PRLE WLRYAYUE
BLRP TNE TIPE RB HEAL. AUU BIEUC SWRLTS GELE RKEL. GITNIO CRRLS TNELE
GAS UACH MATNELIOE, YRRVS, AOC A YIUUIALC TAYUE, YDT FEOTUEPEO MAOORT YE
AUGAHS GITNIO CRRLS; AOC IO TNE OEALOESS RB TNE WALSROAFE, RL TNE
WUEASAOTOESS RB TNE GAUV TR IT, RL RB TNE WERWUE GNR UIKEC IO IT, TNE
TGR MRDSIOS BRDOC A TEPWTATIRO BLRP TNIS WELIRC RB GAUVIOF TNITNEL
AUPRST EKELH CAH. TNEH MAUUEC AT KALIRDS TIPES RB TNE PRLOIOF, SRPETIPES
SEWALATEUH, SRPETIPES TRFETNEL, AOC ORG AOC TNEO AMMRPWAOIEC YH TNEIL
ADOT. IT GAS WUAIO TR TNEP AUU TNAT MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP MAPE YEMADSE NE
NAC WUEASDLE IO TNEIL SRMIETH, A WELSDASIRO GNIMN RB MRDLSE LEMRPPEOCEC
NIP STIUU PRLE; AOC EUIJAYETN GAS LEPIOCEC YH NEL RGO SATISBAMTIRO IO
YEIOF GITN NIP, AS GEUU AS YH NIS EKICEOT ACPILATIRO, RB NEL BRLPEL
BAKRDLITE, FERLFE GIMVNAP; AOC TNRDFN, IO MRPWALIOF TNEP, SNE SAG TNELE
GAS UESS MAWTIKATIOF SRBTOESS IO MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP’S PAOOELS, SNE
YEUIEKEC NE PIFNT NAKE TNE YEST IOBRLPEC PIOC.

YDT GNH PL. CALMH MAPE SR RBTEO TR TNE WALSROAFE IT GAS PRLE CIBBIMDUT
TR DOCELSTAOC. IT MRDUC ORT YE BRL SRMIETH, AS NE BLEQDEOTUH SAT TNELE
TEO PIODTES TRFETNEL GITNRDT RWEOIOF NIS UIWS; AOC GNEO NE CIC SWEAV, IT
SEEPEC TNE EBBEMT RB OEMESSITH LATNEL TNAO RB MNRIME--A SAMLIBIME TR
WLRWLIETH, ORT A WUEASDLE TR NIPSEUB. NE SEUCRP AWWEALEC LEAUUH
AOIPATEC. PLS. MRUUIOS VOEG ORT GNAT TR PAVE RB NIP. MRUROEU
BITJGIUUIAP’S RMMASIROAUUH UADFNIOF AT NIS STDWICITH WLRKEC TNAT NE GAS
FEOELAUUH CIBBELEOT, GNIMN NEL RGO VORGUECFE RB NIP MRDUC ORT NAKE TRUC
NEL; AOC AS SNE GRDUC NAKE UIVEC TR YEUIEKE TNIS MNAOFE TNE EBBEMT RB
URKE, AOC TNE RYZEMT RB TNAT URKE NEL BLIEOC EUIJA, SNE SET NELSEUB
SELIRDSUH TR GRLV TR BIOC IT RDT: SNE GATMNEC NIP GNEOEKEL TNEH GELE AT
LRSIOFS, AOC GNEOEKEL NE MAPE TR NDOSBRLC; YDT GITNRDT PDMN SDMMESS. NE
MELTAIOUH URRVEC AT NEL BLIEOC A FLEAT CEAU, YDT TNE EXWLESSIRO RB TNAT
URRV GAS CISWDTAYUE. IT GAS AO EALOEST, STEACBAST FAJE, YDT SNE RBTEO
CRDYTEC GNETNEL TNELE GELE PDMN ACPILATIRO IO IT, AOC SRPETIPES IT
SEEPEC ORTNIOF YDT AYSEOME RB PIOC.

SNE NAC ROME RL TGIME SDFFESTEC TR EUIJAYETN TNE WRSSIYIUITH RB NIS
YEIOF WALTIAU TR NEL, YDT EUIJAYETN AUGAHS UADFNEC AT TNE ICEA; AOC PLS.
MRUUIOS CIC ORT TNIOV IT LIFNT TR WLESS TNE SDYZEMT, BLRP TNE CAOFEL RB
LAISIOF EXWEMTATIROS GNIMN PIFNT ROUH EOC IO CISAWWRIOTPEOT; BRL IO NEL
RWIOIRO IT ACPITTEC ORT RB A CRDYT, TNAT AUU NEL BLIEOC’S CISUIVE GRDUC
KAOISN, IB SNE MRDUC SDWWRSE NIP TR YE IO NEL WRGEL.

IO NEL VIOC SMNEPES BRL EUIJAYETN, SNE SRPETIPES WUAOOEC NEL PALLHIOF
MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP. NE GAS, YEHROC MRPWALISRO, TNE WUEASAOTEST PAO: NE
MELTAIOUH ACPILEC NEL, AOC NIS SITDATIRO IO UIBE GAS PRST EUIFIYUE; YDT,
TR MRDOTELYAUAOME TNESE ACKAOTAFES, PL. CALMH NAC MROSICELAYUE WATLROAFE
IO TNE MNDLMN, AOC NIS MRDSIO MRDUC NAKE OROE AT AUU.




[IUUDSTLATIRO: “RO URRVIOF DW”]




MNAWTEL XXXIII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

PRLE TNAO ROME CIC EUIJAYETN, IO NEL LAPYUE GITNIO TNE WALV,
DOEXWEMTECUH PEET PL. CALMH. SNE BEUT AUU TNE WELKELSEOESS RB TNE
PISMNAOME TNAT SNRDUC YLIOF NIP GNELE OR ROE EUSE GAS YLRDFNT; AOC, TR
WLEKEOT ITS EKEL NAWWEOIOF AFAIO, TRRV MALE TR IOBRLP NIP, AT BILST,
TNAT IT GAS A BAKRDLITE NADOT RB NELS. NRG IT MRDUC RMMDL A SEMROC TIPE,
TNELEBRLE, GAS KELH RCC! HET IT CIC, AOC EKEO TNE TNILC. IT SEEPEC UIVE
GIUBDU IUU-OATDLE, RL A KRUDOTALH WEOAOME; BRL RO TNESE RMMASIROS IT GAS
ORT PELEUH A BEG BRLPAU IOQDILIES AOC AO AGVGALC WADSE AOC TNEO AGAH,
YDT NE AMTDAUUH TNRDFNT IT OEMESSALH TR TDLO YAMV AOC GAUV GITN NEL. NE
OEKEL SAIC A FLEAT CEAU, ORL CIC SNE FIKE NELSEUB TNE TLRDYUE RB TAUVIOF
RL RB UISTEOIOF PDMN; YDT IT STLDMV NEL IO TNE MRDLSE RB TNEIL TNILC
LEOMRDOTEL TNAT NE GAS ASVIOF SRPE RCC DOMROOEMTEC QDESTIROS--AYRDT NEL
WUEASDLE IO YEIOF AT NDOSBRLC, NEL URKE RB SRUITALH GAUVS, AOC NEL
RWIOIRO RB PL. AOC PLS. MRUUIOS’S NAWWIOESS; AOC TNAT IO SWEAVIOF RB
LRSIOFS, AOC NEL ORT WELBEMTUH DOCELSTAOCIOF TNE NRDSE, NE SEEPEC TR
EXWEMT TNAT GNEOEKEL SNE MAPE IOTR VEOT AFAIO SNE GRDUC YE STAHIOF
_TNELE_ TRR. NIS GRLCS SEEPEC TR IPWUH IT. MRDUC NE NAKE MRUROEU
BITJGIUUIAP IO NIS TNRDFNTS? SNE SDWWRSEC, IB NE PEAOT AOHTNIOF, NE PDST
PEAO AO AUUDSIRO TR GNAT PIFNT ALISE IO TNAT QDALTEL. IT CISTLESSEC NEL
A UITTUE, AOC SNE GAS QDITE FUAC TR BIOC NELSEUB AT TNE FATE IO TNE
WAUES RWWRSITE TNE WALSROAFE.

SNE GAS EOFAFEC ROE CAH, AS SNE GAUVEC, IO LE-WELDSIOF ZAOE’S UAST
UETTEL, AOC CGEUUIOF RO SRPE WASSAFES GNIMN WLRKEC TNAT ZAOE NAC ORT
GLITTEO IO SWILITS, GNEO, IOSTEAC RB YEIOF AFAIO SDLWLISEC YH PL. CALMH,
SNE SAG, RO URRVIOF DW, TNAT MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP GAS PEETIOF NEL.
WDTTIOF AGAH TNE UETTEL IPPECIATEUH, AOC BRLMIOF A SPIUE, SNE SAIC,--

“I CIC ORT VORG YEBRLE TNAT HRD EKEL GAUVEC TNIS GAH.”

“I NAKE YEEO PAVIOF TNE TRDL RB TNE WALV,” NE LEWUIEC, “AS I FEOELAUUH
CR EKELH HEAL, AOC IOTEOCEC TR MURSE IT GITN A MAUU AT TNE WALSROAFE.
ALE HRD FRIOF PDMN BALTNEL?”

“OR, I SNRDUC NAKE TDLOEC IO A PRPEOT.”

AOC AMMRLCIOFUH SNE CIC TDLO, AOC TNEH GAUVEC TRGALCS TNE WALSROAFE
TRFETNEL.

“CR HRD MELTAIOUH UEAKE VEOT RO SATDLCAH?” SAIC SNE.

“HES--IB CALMH CRES ORT WDT IT RBB AFAIO. YDT I AP AT NIS CISWRSAU. NE
ALLAOFES TNE YDSIOESS ZDST AS NE WUEASES.”

“AOC IB ORT AYUE TR WUEASE NIPSEUB IO TNE ALLAOFEPEOT, NE NAS AT UEAST
FLEAT WUEASDLE IO TNE WRGEL RB MNRIME. I CR ORT VORG AOHYRCH GNR SEEPS
PRLE TR EOZRH TNE WRGEL RB CRIOF GNAT NE UIVES TNAO PL. CALMH.”

“NE UIVES TR NAKE NIS RGO GAH KELH GEUU,” LEWUIEC MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP.
“YDT SR GE AUU CR. IT IS ROUH TNAT NE NAS YETTEL PEAOS RB NAKIOF IT TNAO
PAOH RTNELS, YEMADSE NE IS LIMN, AOC PAOH RTNELS ALE WRRL. I SWEAV
BEEUIOFUH. A HRDOFEL SRO, HRD VORG, PDST YE IODLEC TR SEUB-CEOIAU AOC
CEWEOCEOME.”

“IO PH RWIOIRO, TNE HRDOFEL SRO RB AO EALU MAO VORG KELH UITTUE RB
EITNEL. ORG, SELIRDSUH, GNAT NAKE HRD EKEL VORGO RB SEUB-CEOIAU AOC
CEWEOCEOME? GNEO NAKE HRD YEEO WLEKEOTEC YH GAOT RB PROEH BLRP FRIOF
GNELEKEL HRD MNRSE RL WLRMDLIOF AOHTNIOF HRD NAC A BAOMH BRL?”

“TNESE ALE NRPE QDESTIROS--AOC WELNAWS I MAOORT SAH TNAT I NAKE
EXWELIEOMEC PAOH NALCSNIWS RB TNAT OATDLE. YDT IO PATTELS RB FLEATEL
GEIFNT, I PAH SDBBEL BLRP TNE GAOT RB PROEH. HRDOFEL SROS MAOORT PALLH
GNELE TNEH UIVE.”

“DOUESS GNELE TNEH UIVE GRPEO RB BRLTDOE, GNIMN I TNIOV TNEH KELH RBTEO
CR.”

“RDL NAYITS RB EXWEOSE PAVE DS TRR CEWEOCEOT, AOC TNELE ALE ORT PAOH IO
PH LAOV RB UIBE GNR MAO ABBRLC TR PALLH GITNRDT SRPE ATTEOTIRO TR
PROEH.”

“IS TNIS,” TNRDFNT EUIJAYETN, “PEAOT BRL PE?” AOC SNE MRURDLEC AT TNE
ICEA; YDT, LEMRKELIOF NELSEUB, SAIC IO A UIKEUH TROE, “AOC WLAH, GNAT IS
TNE DSDAU WLIME RB AO EALU’S HRDOFEL SRO? DOUESS TNE EUCEL YLRTNEL IS
KELH SIMVUH, I SDWWRSE HRD GRDUC ORT ASV AYRKE BIBTH TNRDSAOC WRDOCS.”

NE AOSGELEC NEL IO TNE SAPE STHUE, AOC TNE SDYZEMT CLRWWEC. TR IOTELLDWT
A SIUEOME GNIMN PIFNT PAVE NIP BAOMH NEL ABBEMTEC GITN GNAT NAC WASSEC,
SNE SRRO ABTELGALCS SAIC,--

“I IPAFIOE HRDL MRDSIO YLRDFNT HRD CRGO GITN NIP MNIEBUH BRL TNE SAVE RB
NAKIOF SRPEYRCH AT NIS CISWRSAU. I GROCEL NE CRES ORT PALLH, TR SEMDLE A
UASTIOF MROKEOIEOME RB TNAT VIOC. YDT, WELNAWS, NIS SISTEL CRES AS GEUU
BRL TNE WLESEOT; AOC, AS SNE IS DOCEL NIS SRUE MALE, NE PAH CR GNAT NE
UIVES GITN NEL.”

“OR,” SAIC MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP, “TNAT IS AO ACKAOTAFE GNIMN NE PDST
CIKICE GITN PE. I AP ZRIOEC GITN NIP IO TNE FDALCIAOSNIW RB PISS CALMH.”

“ALE HRD, IOCEEC? AOC WLAH GNAT SRLT RB A FDALCIAO CR HRD PAVE? CRES
HRDL MNALFE FIKE HRD PDMN TLRDYUE? HRDOF UACIES RB NEL AFE ALE SRPETIPES
A UITTUE CIBBIMDUT TR PAOAFE; AOC IB SNE NAS TNE TLDE CALMH SWILIT, SNE
PAH UIVE TR NAKE NEL RGO GAH.”

AS SNE SWRVE, SNE RYSELKEC NIP URRVIOF AT NEL EALOESTUH; AOC TNE PAOOEL
IO GNIMN NE IPPECIATEUH ASVEC NEL GNH SNE SDWWRSEC PISS CALMH UIVEUH TR
FIKE TNEP AOH DOEASIOESS, MROKIOMEC NEL TNAT SNE NAC SRPENRG RL RTNEL
FRT WLETTH OEAL TNE TLDTN. SNE CILEMTUH LEWUIEC,--

“HRD OEEC ORT YE BLIFNTEOEC. I OEKEL NEALC AOH NALP RB NEL; AOC I CALE
SAH SNE IS ROE RB TNE PRST TLAMTAYUE MLEATDLES IO TNE GRLUC. SNE IS A
KELH FLEAT BAKRDLITE GITN SRPE UACIES RB PH AMQDAIOTAOME, PLS. NDLST AOC
PISS YIOFUEH. I TNIOV I NAKE NEALC HRD SAH TNAT HRD VORG TNEP.”

“I VORG TNEP A UITTUE. TNEIL YLRTNEL IS A WUEASAOT, FEOTUEPAOUIVE
PAO--NE IS A FLEAT BLIEOC RB CALMH’S.”

“RN HES,” SAIC EUIJAYETN CLIUH--“PL. CALMH IS DOMRPPROUH VIOC TR PL.
YIOFUEH, AOC TAVES A WLRCIFIRDS CEAU RB MALE RB NIP.”

“MALE RB NIP! HES, I LEAUUH YEUIEKE CALMH _CRES_ TAVE MALE RB NIP IO
TNRSE WRIOTS GNELE NE PRST GAOTS MALE. BLRP SRPETNIOF TNAT NE TRUC PE
IO RDL ZRDLOEH NITNEL, I NAKE LEASRO TR TNIOV YIOFUEH KELH PDMN IOCEYTEC
TR NIP. YDT I RDFNT TR YEF NIS WALCRO, BRL I NAKE OR LIFNT TR SDWWRSE
TNAT YIOFUEH GAS TNE WELSRO PEAOT. IT GAS AUU MROZEMTDLE.”

“GNAT IS IT HRD PEAO?”

“IT IS A MILMDPSTAOME GNIMN CALMH RB MRDLSE MRDUC ORT GISN TR YE
FEOELAUUH VORGO, YEMADSE IB IT GELE TR FET LRDOC TR TNE UACH’S BAPIUH IT
GRDUC YE AO DOWUEASAOT TNIOF.”

“HRD PAH CEWEOC DWRO PH ORT PEOTIROIOF IT.”

“AOC LEPEPYEL TNAT I NAKE ORT PDMN LEASRO BRL SDWWRSIOF IT TR YE
YIOFUEH. GNAT NE TRUC PE GAS PELEUH TNIS: TNAT NE MROFLATDUATEC NIPSEUB
RO NAKIOF UATEUH SAKEC A BLIEOC BLRP TNE IOMROKEOIEOMES RB A PRST
IPWLDCEOT PALLIAFE, YDT GITNRDT PEOTIROIOF OAPES RL AOH RTNEL
WALTIMDUALS; AOC I ROUH SDSWEMTEC IT TR YE YIOFUEH BLRP YEUIEKIOF NIP
TNE VIOC RB HRDOF PAO TR FET IOTR A SMLAWE RB TNAT SRLT, AOC BLRP
VORGIOF TNEP TR NAKE YEEO TRFETNEL TNE GNRUE RB UAST SDPPEL.”

“CIC PL. CALMH FIKE HRD NIS LEASROS BRL TNIS IOTELBELEOME?”

“I DOCELSTRRC TNAT TNELE GELE SRPE KELH STLROF RYZEMTIROS AFAIOST TNE
UACH.”

“AOC GNAT ALTS CIC NE DSE TR SEWALATE TNEP?”

“NE CIC ORT TAUV TR PE RB NIS RGO ALTS,” SAIC BITJGIUUIAP, SPIUIOF. “NE
ROUH TRUC PE GNAT I NAKE ORG TRUC HRD.”

EUIJAYETN PACE OR AOSGEL, AOC GAUVEC RO, NEL NEALT SGEUUIOF GITN
IOCIFOATIRO. ABTEL GATMNIOF NEL A UITTUE, BITJGIUUIAP ASVEC NEL GNH SNE
GAS SR TNRDFNTBDU.

“I AP TNIOVIOF RB GNAT HRD NAKE YEEO TEUUIOF PE,” SAIC SNE. “HRDL
MRDSIO’S MROCDMT CRES ORT SDIT PH BEEUIOFS. GNH GAS NE TR YE TNE
ZDCFE?”

“HRD ALE LATNEL CISWRSEC TR MAUU NIS IOTELBELEOME RBBIMIRDS?”

“I CR ORT SEE GNAT LIFNT PL. CALMH NAC TR CEMICE RO TNE WLRWLIETH RB NIS
BLIEOC’S IOMUIOATIRO; RL GNH, DWRO NIS RGO ZDCFPEOT AUROE, NE GAS TR
CETELPIOE AOC CILEMT IO GNAT PAOOEL TNAT BLIEOC GAS TR YE NAWWH. YDT,”
SNE MROTIODEC, LEMRUUEMTIOF NELSEUB, “AS GE VORG OROE RB TNE
WALTIMDUALS, IT IS ORT BAIL TR MROCEPO NIP. IT IS ORT TR YE SDWWRSEC
TNAT TNELE GAS PDMN ABBEMTIRO IO TNE MASE.”

“TNAT IS ORT AO DOOATDLAU SDLPISE,” SAIC BITJGIUUIAP; “YDT IT IS
UESSEOIOF TNE NRORDL RB PH MRDSIO’S TLIDPWN KELH SACUH.”

TNIS GAS SWRVEO ZESTIOFUH, YDT IT AWWEALEC TR NEL SR ZDST A WIMTDLE RB
PL. CALMH, TNAT SNE GRDUC ORT TLDST NELSEUB GITN AO AOSGEL; AOC,
TNELEBRLE, AYLDWTUH MNAOFIOF TNE MROKELSATIRO, TAUVEC RO IOCIBBELEOT
PATTELS TIUU TNEH LEAMNEC TNE WALSROAFE. TNELE, SNDT IOTR NEL RGO LRRP,
AS SRRO AS TNEIL KISITRL UEBT TNEP, SNE MRDUC TNIOV GITNRDT IOTELLDWTIRO
RB AUU TNAT SNE NAC NEALC. IT GAS ORT TR YE SDWWRSEC TNAT AOH RTNEL
WERWUE MRDUC YE PEAOT TNAO TNRSE GITN GNRP SNE GAS MROOEMTEC. TNELE
MRDUC ORT EXIST IO TNE GRLUC _TGR_ PEO RKEL GNRP PL. CALMH MRDUC NAKE
SDMN YRDOCUESS IOBUDEOME. TNAT NE NAC YEEO MROMELOEC IO TNE PEASDLES
TAVEO TR SEWALATE PL. YIOFUEH AOC ZAOE, SNE NAC OEKEL CRDYTEC; YDT SNE
NAC AUGAHS ATTLIYDTEC TR PISS YIOFUEH TNE WLIOMIWAU CESIFO AOC
ALLAOFEPEOT RB TNEP. IB NIS RGO KAOITH, NRGEKEL, CIC ORT PISUEAC NIP,
_NE_ GAS TNE MADSE--NIS WLICE AOC MAWLIME GELE TNE MADSE--RB AUU TNAT
ZAOE NAC SDBBELEC, AOC STIUU MROTIODEC TR SDBBEL. NE NAC LDIOEC BRL A
GNIUE EKELH NRWE RB NAWWIOESS BRL TNE PRST ABBEMTIROATE, FEOELRDS NEALT
IO TNE GRLUC; AOC OR ROE MRDUC SAH NRG UASTIOF AO EKIU NE PIFNT NAKE
IOBUIMTEC.

“TNELE GELE SRPE KELH STLROF RYZEMTIROS AFAIOST TNE UACH,” GELE MRUROEU
BITJGIUUIAP’S GRLCS; AOC TNESE STLROF RYZEMTIROS WLRYAYUH GELE, NEL
NAKIOF ROE DOMUE GNR GAS A MRDOTLH ATTRLOEH, AOC AORTNEL GNR GAS IO
YDSIOESS IO UROCRO.

“TR ZAOE NELSEUB,” SNE EXMUAIPEC, “TNELE MRDUC YE OR WRSSIYIUITH RB
RYZEMTIRO,--AUU URKEUIOESS AOC FRRCOESS AS SNE IS! NEL DOCELSTAOCIOF
EXMEUUEOT, NEL PIOC IPWLRKEC, AOC NEL PAOOELS MAWTIKATIOF. OEITNEL MRDUC
AOHTNIOF YE DLFEC AFAIOST PH BATNEL, GNR, TNRDFN GITN SRPE
WEMDUIALITIES, NAS AYIUITIES GNIMN PL. CALMH NIPSEUB OEEC ORT CISCAIO,
AOC LESWEMTAYIUITH GNIMN NE GIUU WLRYAYUH OEKEL LEAMN.” GNEO SNE TNRDFNT
RB NEL PRTNEL, IOCEEC, NEL MROBICEOME FAKE GAH A UITTUE; YDT SNE GRDUC
ORT AUURG TNAT AOH RYZEMTIROS _TNELE_ NAC PATELIAU GEIFNT GITN PL.
CALMH, GNRSE WLICE, SNE GAS MROKIOMEC, GRDUC LEMEIKE A CEEWEL GRDOC BLRP
TNE GAOT RB IPWRLTAOME IO NIS BLIEOC’S MROOEMTIROS TNAO BLRP TNEIL GAOT
RB SEOSE; AOC SNE GAS QDITE CEMICEC, AT UAST, TNAT NE NAC YEEO WALTUH
FRKELOEC YH TNIS GRLST VIOC RB WLICE, AOC WALTUH YH TNE GISN RB
LETAIOIOF PL. YIOFUEH BRL NIS SISTEL.

TNE AFITATIRO AOC TEALS GNIMN TNE SDYZEMT RMMASIROEC YLRDFNT RO A
NEACAMNE; AOC IT FLEG SR PDMN GRLSE TRGALCS TNE EKEOIOF TNAT, ACCEC TR
NEL DOGIUUIOFOESS TR SEE PL. CALMH, IT CETELPIOEC NEL ORT TR ATTEOC NEL
MRDSIOS TR LRSIOFS, GNELE TNEH GELE EOFAFEC TR CLIOV TEA. PLS. MRUUIOS,
SEEIOF TNAT SNE GAS LEAUUH DOGEUU, CIC ORT WLESS NEL TR FR, AOC AS PDMN
AS WRSSIYUE WLEKEOTEC NEL NDSYAOC BLRP WLESSIOF NEL; YDT PL. MRUUIOS
MRDUC ORT MROMEAU NIS AWWLENEOSIRO RB UACH MATNELIOE’S YEIOF LATNEL
CISWUEASEC YH NEL STAHIOF AT NRPE.

MNAWTEL XXXIK.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

GNEO TNEH GELE FROE, EUIJAYETN, AS IB IOTEOCIOF TR EXASWELATE NELSEUB AS
PDMN AS WRSSIYUE AFAIOST PL. CALMH, MNRSE BRL NEL EPWURHPEOT TNE
EXAPIOATIRO RB AUU TNE UETTELS GNIMN ZAOE NAC GLITTEO TR NEL SIOME NEL
YEIOF IO VEOT. TNEH MROTAIOEC OR AMTDAU MRPWUAIOT, ORL GAS TNELE AOH
LEKIKAU RB WAST RMMDLLEOMES, RL AOH MRPPDOIMATIRO RB WLESEOT SDBBELIOF.
YDT IO AUU, AOC IO AUPRST EKELH UIOE RB EAMN, TNELE GAS A GAOT RB TNAT
MNEELBDUOESS GNIMN NAC YEEO DSEC TR MNALAMTELIJE NEL STHUE, AOC GNIMN,
WLRMEECIOF BLRP TNE SELEOITH RB A PIOC AT EASE GITN ITSEUB, AOC VIOCUH
CISWRSEC TRGALCS EKELHROE, NAC YEEO SMALMEUH EKEL MURDCEC. EUIJAYETN
ORTIMEC EKELH SEOTEOME MROKEHIOF TNE ICEA RB DOEASIOESS, GITN AO
ATTEOTIRO GNIMN IT NAC NALCUH LEMEIKEC RO TNE BILST WELDSAU. PL. CALMH’S
SNAPEBDU YRAST RB GNAT PISELH NE NAC YEEO AYUE TR IOBUIMT FAKE NEL A
VEEOEL SEOSE RB NEL SISTEL’S SDBBELIOFS. IT GAS SRPE MROSRUATIRO TR
TNIOV TNAT NIS KISIT TR LRSIOFS GAS TR EOC RO TNE CAH ABTEL TNE OEXT,
AOC A STIUU FLEATEL TNAT IO UESS TNAO A BRLTOIFNT SNE SNRDUC NELSEUB YE
GITN ZAOE AFAIO, AOC EOAYUEC TR MROTLIYDTE TR TNE LEMRKELH RB NEL
SWILITS, YH AUU TNAT ABBEMTIRO MRDUC CR.

SNE MRDUC ORT TNIOV RB CALMH’S UEAKIOF VEOT GITNRDT LEPEPYELIOF TNAT NIS
MRDSIO GAS TR FR GITN NIP; YDT MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP NAC PACE IT MUEAL
TNAT NE NAC OR IOTEOTIROS AT AUU, AOC, AFLEEAYUE AS NE GAS, SNE CIC ORT
PEAO TR YE DONAWWH AYRDT NIP.

GNIUE SETTUIOF TNIS WRIOT, SNE GAS SDCCEOUH LRDSEC YH TNE SRDOC RB TNE
CRRL-YEUU; AOC NEL SWILITS GELE A UITTUE BUDTTELEC YH TNE ICEA RB ITS
YEIOF MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP NIPSEUB, GNR NAC ROME YEBRLE MAUUEC UATE IO
TNE EKEOIOF, AOC PIFNT ORG MRPE TR IOQDILE WALTIMDUALUH ABTEL NEL. YDT
TNIS ICEA GAS SRRO YAOISNEC, AOC NEL SWILITS GELE KELH CIBBELEOTUH
ABBEMTEC, GNEO, TR NEL DTTEL APAJEPEOT, SNE SAG PL. CALMH GAUV IOTR TNE
LRRP. IO A NDLLIEC PAOOEL NE IPPECIATEUH YEFAO AO IOQDILH ABTEL NEL
NEAUTN, IPWDTIOF NIS KISIT TR A GISN RB NEALIOF TNAT SNE GELE YETTEL.
SNE AOSGELEC NIP GITN MRUC MIKIUITH. NE SAT CRGO BRL A BEG PRPEOTS, AOC
TNEO FETTIOF DW GAUVEC AYRDT TNE LRRP. EUIJAYETN GAS SDLWLISEC, YDT
SAIC ORT A GRLC. ABTEL A SIUEOME RB SEKELAU PIODTES, NE MAPE TRGALCS NEL
IO AO AFITATEC PAOOEL, AOC TNDS YEFAO:--

“IO KAIO NAKE I STLDFFUEC. IT GIUU ORT CR. PH BEEUIOFS GIUU ORT YE
LEWLESSEC. HRD PDST AUURG PE TR TEUU HRD NRG ALCEOTUH I ACPILE AOC URKE
HRD.”

EUIJAYETN’S ASTROISNPEOT GAS YEHROC EXWLESSIRO. SNE STALEC, MRURDLEC,
CRDYTEC, AOC GAS SIUEOT. TNIS NE MROSICELEC SDBBIMIEOT EOMRDLAFEPEOT,
AOC TNE AKRGAU RB AUU TNAT NE BEUT AOC NAC UROF BEUT BRL NEL IPPECIATEUH
BRUURGEC. NE SWRVE GEUU; YDT TNELE GELE BEEUIOFS YESICES TNRSE RB TNE
NEALT TR YE CETAIUEC, AOC NE GAS ORT PRLE EURQDEOT RO TNE SDYZEMT RB
TEOCELOESS TNAO RB WLICE. NIS SEOSE RB NEL IOBELIRLITH, RB ITS YEIOF A
CEFLACATIRO, RB TNE BAPIUH RYSTAMUES GNIMN ZDCFPEOT NAC AUGAHS RWWRSEC
TR IOMUIOATIRO, GELE CGEUT RO GITN A GALPTN GNIMN SEEPEC CDE TR TNE
MROSEQDEOME NE GAS GRDOCIOF, YDT GAS KELH DOUIVEUH TR LEMRPPEOC NIS
SDIT.

IO SWITE RB NEL CEEWUH-LRRTEC CISUIVE, SNE MRDUC ORT YE IOSEOSIYUE TR
TNE MRPWUIPEOT RB SDMN A PAO’S ABBEMTIRO, AOC TNRDFN NEL IOTEOTIROS CIC
ORT KALH BRL AO IOSTAOT, SNE GAS AT BILST SRLLH BRL TNE WAIO NE GAS TR
LEMEIKE; TIUU LRDSEC TR LESEOTPEOT YH NIS SDYSEQDEOT UAOFDAFE, SNE URST
AUU MRPWASSIRO IO AOFEL. SNE TLIEC, NRGEKEL, TR MRPWRSE NELSEUB TR
AOSGEL NIP GITN WATIEOME, GNEO NE SNRDUC NAKE CROE. NE MROMUDCEC GITN
LEWLESEOTIOF TR NEL TNE STLEOFTN RB TNAT ATTAMNPEOT GNIMN IO SWITE RB
AUU NIS EOCEAKRDLS NE NAC BRDOC IPWRSSIYUE TR MROQDEL; AOC GITN
EXWLESSIOF NIS NRWE TNAT IT GRDUC ORG YE LEGALCEC YH NEL AMMEWTAOME RB
NIS NAOC. AS NE SAIC TNIS SNE MRDUC EASIUH SEE TNAT NE NAC OR CRDYT RB A
BAKRDLAYUE AOSGEL. NE _SWRVE_ RB AWWLENEOSIRO AOC AOXIETH, YDT NIS
MRDOTEOAOME EXWLESSEC LEAU SEMDLITH. SDMN A MILMDPSTAOME MRDUC ROUH
EXASWELATE BALTNEL; AOC GNEO NE MEASEC TNE MRURDL LRSE IOTR NEL MNEEVS
AOC SNE SAIC,--

“IO SDMN MASES AS TNIS, IT IS, I YEUIEKE, TNE ESTAYUISNEC PRCE TR
EXWLESS A SEOSE RB RYUIFATIRO BRL TNE SEOTIPEOTS AKRGEC, NRGEKEL
DOEQDAUUH TNEH PAH YE LETDLOEC. IT IS OATDLAU TNAT RYUIFATIRO SNRDUC YE
BEUT, AOC IB I MRDUC _BEEU_ FLATITDCE, I GRDUC ORG TNAOV HRD. YDT I
MAOORT--I NAKE OEKEL CESILEC HRDL FRRC RWIOIRO, AOC HRD NAKE MELTAIOUH
YESTRGEC IT PRST DOGIUUIOFUH. I AP SRLLH TR NAKE RMMASIROEC WAIO TR
AOHROE. IT NAS YEEO PRST DOMROSMIRDSUH CROE, NRGEKEL, AOC I NRWE GIUU YE
RB SNRLT CDLATIRO. TNE BEEUIOFS GNIMN HRD TEUU PE NAKE UROF WLEKEOTEC
TNE AMVORGUECFPEOT RB HRDL LEFALC MAO NAKE UITTUE CIBBIMDUTH IO
RKELMRPIOF IT ABTEL TNIS EXWUAOATIRO.”

PL. CALMH, GNR GAS UEAOIOF AFAIOST TNE PAOTEU-WIEME GITN NIS EHES BIXEC
RO NEL BAME, SEEPEC TR MATMN NEL GRLCS GITN OR UESS LESEOTPEOT TNAO
SDLWLISE. NIS MRPWUEXIRO YEMAPE WAUE GITN AOFEL, AOC TNE CISTDLYAOME RB
NIS PIOC GAS KISIYUE IO EKELH BEATDLE. NE GAS STLDFFUIOF BRL TNE
AWWEALAOME RB MRPWRSDLE, AOC GRDUC ORT RWEO NIS UIWS TIUU NE YEUIEKEC
NIPSEUB TR NAKE ATTAIOEC IT. TNE WADSE GAS TR EUIJAYETN’S BEEUIOFS
CLEACBDU. AT UEOFTN, IO A KRIME RB BRLMEC MAUPOESS, NE SAIC,--

“AOC TNIS IS AUU TNE LEWUH GNIMN I AP TR NAKE TNE NRORDL RB EXWEMTIOF! I
PIFNT, WELNAWS, GISN TR YE IOBRLPEC GNH, GITN SR UITTUE _EOCEAKRDL_ AT
MIKIUITH, I AP TNDS LEZEMTEC. YDT IT IS RB SPAUU IPWRLTAOME.”

“I PIFNT AS GEUU IOQDILE,” LEWUIEC SNE, “GNH, GITN SR EKICEOT A CESIFO
RB RBBEOCIOF AOC IOSDUTIOF PE, HRD MNRSE TR TEUU PE TNAT HRD UIVEC PE
AFAIOST HRDL GIUU, AFAIOST HRDL LEASRO, AOC EKEO AFAIOST HRDL MNALAMTEL?
GAS ORT TNIS SRPE EXMDSE BRL IOMIKIUITH, IB I _GAS_ DOMIKIU? YDT I NAKE
RTNEL WLRKRMATIROS. HRD VORG I NAKE. NAC ORT PH RGO BEEUIOFS CEMICEC
AFAIOST HRD, NAC TNEH YEEO IOCIBBELEOT, RL NAC TNEH EKEO YEEO
BAKRDLAYUE, CR HRD TNIOV TNAT AOH MROSICELATIRO GRDUC TEPWT PE TR AMMEWT
TNE PAO GNR NAS YEEO TNE PEAOS RB LDIOIOF, WELNAWS BRL EKEL, TNE
NAWWIOESS RB A PRST YEURKEC SISTEL?”

AS SNE WLRORDOMEC TNESE GRLCS, PL. CALMH MNAOFEC MRURDL; YDT TNE EPRTIRO
GAS SNRLT, AOC NE UISTEOEC GITNRDT ATTEPWTIOF TR IOTELLDWT NEL GNIUE SNE
MROTIODEC,--

“I NAKE EKELH LEASRO IO TNE GRLUC TR TNIOV IUU RB HRD. OR PRTIKE MAO
EXMDSE TNE DOZDST AOC DOFEOELRDS WALT HRD AMTEC _TNELE_. HRD CALE ORT,
HRD MAOORT CEOH TNAT HRD NAKE YEEO TNE WLIOMIWAU, IB ORT TNE ROUH PEAOS
RB CIKICIOF TNEP BLRP EAMN RTNEL, RB EXWRSIOF ROE TR TNE MEOSDLE RB TNE
GRLUC BRL MAWLIME AOC IOSTAYIUITH, TNE RTNEL TR ITS CELISIRO BRL
CISAWWRIOTEC NRWES, AOC IOKRUKIOF TNEP YRTN IO PISELH RB TNE AMDTEST
VIOC.”

SNE WADSEC, AOC SAG GITN OR SUIFNT IOCIFOATIRO TNAT NE GAS UISTEOIOF
GITN AO AIL GNIMN WLRKEC NIP GNRUUH DOPRKEC YH AOH BEEUIOF RB LEPRLSE.
NE EKEO URRVEC AT NEL GITN A SPIUE RB ABBEMTEC IOMLECDUITH.

“MAO HRD CEOH TNAT HRD NAKE CROE IT?” SNE LEWEATEC.

GITN ASSDPEC TLAOQDIUUITH NE TNEO LEWUIEC, “I NAKE OR GISN RB CEOHIOF
TNAT I CIC EKELHTNIOF IO PH WRGEL TR SEWALATE PH BLIEOC BLRP HRDL
SISTEL, RL TNAT I LEZRIME IO PH SDMMESS. TRGALCS _NIP_ I NAKE YEEO
VIOCEL TNAO TRGALCS PHSEUB.”

EUIJAYETN CISCAIOEC TNE AWWEALAOME RB ORTIMIOF TNIS MIKIU LEBUEMTIRO,
YDT ITS PEAOIOF CIC ORT ESMAWE, ORL GAS IT UIVEUH TR MROMIUIATE NEL.

“YDT IT IS ORT PELEUH TNIS ABBAIL,” SNE MROTIODEC, “RO GNIMN PH CISUIVE
IS BRDOCEC. UROF YEBRLE IT NAC TAVEO WUAME, PH RWIOIRO RB HRD GAS
CEMICEC. HRDL MNALAMTEL GAS DOBRUCEC IO TNE LEMITAU GNIMN I LEMEIKEC
PAOH PROTNS AFR BLRP PL. GIMVNAP. RO TNIS SDYZEMT, GNAT MAO HRD NAKE TR
SAH? IO GNAT IPAFIOALH AMT RB BLIEOCSNIW MAO HRD NELE CEBEOC HRDLSEUB?
RL DOCEL GNAT PISLEWLESEOTATIRO MAO HRD NELE IPWRSE DWRO RTNELS?”

“HRD TAVE AO EAFEL IOTELEST IO TNAT FEOTUEPAO’S MROMELOS,” SAIC CALMH,
IO A UESS TLAOQDIU TROE, AOC GITN A NEIFNTEOEC MRURDL.

“GNR TNAT VORGS GNAT NIS PISBRLTDOES NAKE YEEO MAO NEUW BEEUIOF AO
IOTELEST IO NIP?”

“NIS PISBRLTDOES!” LEWEATEC CALMH, MROTEPWTDRDSUH,--“HES, NIS
PISBRLTDOES NAKE YEEO FLEAT IOCEEC.”

“AOC RB HRDL IOBUIMTIRO,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, GITN EOELFH; “HRD NAKE
LECDMEC NIP TR NIS WLESEOT STATE RB WRKELTH--MRPWALATIKE WRKELTH. HRD
NAKE GITNNEUC TNE ACKAOTAFES GNIMN HRD PDST VORG TR NAKE YEEO CESIFOEC
BRL NIP. HRD NAKE CEWLIKEC TNE YEST HEALS RB NIS UIBE RB TNAT
IOCEWEOCEOME GNIMN GAS OR UESS NIS CDE TNAO NIS CESELT. HRD NAKE CROE
AUU TNIS! AOC HET HRD MAO TLEAT TNE PEOTIRO RB NIS PISBRLTDOES GITN
MROTEPWT AOC LICIMDUE.”

“AOC TNIS,” MLIEC CALMH, AS NE GAUVEC GITN QDIMV STEWS AMLRSS TNE LRRP,
“IS HRDL RWIOIRO RB PE! TNIS IS TNE ESTIPATIRO IO GNIMN HRD NRUC PE! I
TNAOV HRD BRL EXWUAIOIOF IT SR BDUUH. PH BADUTS, AMMRLCIOF TR TNIS
MAUMDUATIRO, ALE NEAKH IOCEEC! YDT, WELNAWS,” ACCEC NE, STRWWIOF IO NIS
GAUV, AOC TDLOIOF TRGALCS NEL, “TNESE RBBEOMES PIFNT NAKE YEEO
RKELURRVEC, NAC ORT HRDL WLICE YEEO NDLT YH PH NROEST MROBESSIRO RB TNE
SMLDWUES TNAT NAC UROF WLEKEOTEC PH BRLPIOF AOH SELIRDS CESIFO. TNESE
YITTEL AMMDSATIROS PIFNT NAKE YEEO SDWWLESSEC, NAC I, GITN FLEATEL
WRUIMH, MROMEAUEC PH STLDFFUES, AOC BUATTELEC HRD IOTR TNE YEUIEB RB PH
YEIOF IPWEUUEC YH DOQDAUIBIEC, DOAUURHEC IOMUIOATIRO; YH LEASRO, YH
LEBUEMTIRO, YH EKELHTNIOF. YDT CISFDISE RB EKELH SRLT IS PH AYNRLLEOME.
ORL AP I ASNAPEC RB TNE BEEUIOFS I LEUATEC. TNEH GELE OATDLAU AOC ZDST.
MRDUC HRD EXWEMT PE TR LEZRIME IO TNE IOBELIRLITH RB HRDL
MROOEMTIROS?--TR MROFLATDUATE PHSEUB RO TNE NRWE RB LEUATIROS GNRSE
MROCITIRO IO UIBE IS SR CEMICECUH YEOEATN PH RGO?”

EUIJAYETN BEUT NELSEUB FLRGIOF PRLE AOFLH EKELH PRPEOT; HET SNE TLIEC TR
TNE DTPRST TR SWEAV GITN MRPWRSDLE GNEO SNE SAIC,--

“HRD ALE PISTAVEO, PL. CALMH, IB HRD SDWWRSE TNAT TNE PRCE RB HRDL
CEMUALATIRO ABBEMTEC PE IO AOH RTNEL GAH TNAO AS IT SWALEC PE TNE
MROMELO GNIMN I PIFNT NAKE BEUT IO LEBDSIOF HRD, NAC HRD YENAKEC IO A
PRLE FEOTUEPAOUIVE PAOOEL.”

SNE SAG NIP STALT AT TNIS; YDT NE SAIC ORTNIOF, AOC SNE MROTIODEC,--

“HRD MRDUC ORT NAKE PACE PE TNE RBBEL RB HRDL NAOC IO AOH WRSSIYUE GAH
TNAT GRDUC NAKE TEPWTEC PE TR AMMEWT IT.”

AFAIO NIS ASTROISNPEOT GAS RYKIRDS; AOC NE URRVEC AT NEL GITN AO
EXWLESSIRO RB PIOFUEC IOMLECDUITH AOC PRLTIBIMATIRO. SNE GEOT RO,--

“BLRP TNE KELH YEFIOOIOF, BLRP TNE BILST PRPEOT, I PAH AUPRST SAH, RB PH
AMQDAIOTAOME GITN HRD, HRDL PAOOELS IPWLESSIOF PE GITN TNE BDUUEST
YEUIEB RB HRDL ALLRFAOME, HRDL MROMEIT, AOC HRDL SEUBISN CISCAIO RB TNE
BEEUIOFS RB RTNELS, GELE SDMN AS TR BRLP TNAT FLRDOCGRLV RB
CISAWWLRYATIRO, RO GNIMN SDMMEECIOF EKEOTS NAKE YDIUT SR IPPRKAYUE A
CISUIVE; AOC I NAC ORT VORGO HRD A PROTN YEBRLE I BEUT TNAT HRD GELE TNE
UAST PAO IO TNE GRLUC GNRP I MRDUC EKEL YE WLEKAIUEC RO TR PALLH.”

“HRD NAKE SAIC QDITE EORDFN, PACAP. I WELBEMTUH MRPWLENEOC HRDL
BEEUIOFS, AOC NAKE ORG ROUH TR YE ASNAPEC RB GNAT PH RGO NAKE YEEO.
BRLFIKE PE BRL NAKIOF TAVEO DW SR PDMN RB HRDL TIPE, AOC AMMEWT PH YEST
GISNES BRL HRDL NEAUTN AOC NAWWIOESS.”

AOC GITN TNESE GRLCS NE NASTIUH UEBT TNE LRRP, AOC EUIJAYETN NEALC NIP
TNE OEXT PRPEOT RWEO TNE BLROT CRRL AOC QDIT TNE NRDSE. TNE TDPDUT RB
NEL PIOC GAS ORG WAIOBDUUH FLEAT. SNE VOEG ORT NRG TR SDWWRLT NELSEUB,
AOC, BLRP AMTDAU GEAVOESS, SAT CRGO AOC MLIEC BRL NAUB AO NRDL. NEL
ASTROISNPEOT, AS SNE LEBUEMTEC RO GNAT NAC WASSEC, GAS IOMLEASEC YH
EKELH LEKIEG RB IT. TNAT SNE SNRDUC LEMEIKE AO RBBEL RB PALLIAFE BLRP
PL. CALMH! TNAT NE SNRDUC NAKE YEEO IO URKE GITN NEL BRL SR PAOH PROTNS!
SR PDMN IO URKE AS TR GISN TR PALLH NEL IO SWITE RB AUU TNE RYZEMTIROS
GNIMN NAC PACE NIP WLEKEOT NIS BLIEOC’S PALLHIOF NEL SISTEL, AOC GNIMN
PDST AWWEAL AT UEAST GITN EQDAU BRLME IO NIS RGO MASE, GAS AUPRST
IOMLECIYUE! IT GAS FLATIBHIOF TR NAKE IOSWILEC DOMROSMIRDSUH SR STLROF
AO ABBEMTIRO. YDT NIS WLICE, NIS AYRPIOAYUE WLICE, NIS SNAPEUESS AKRGAU
RB GNAT NE NAC CROE GITN LESWEMT TR ZAOE, NIS DOWALCROAYUE ASSDLAOME IO
AMVORGUECFIOF, TNRDFN NE MRDUC ORT ZDSTIBH IT, AOC TNE DOBEEUIOF PAOOEL
GNIMN NE NAC PEOTIROEC PL. GIMVNAP, NIS MLDEUTH TRGALCS GNRP NE NAC ORT
ATTEPWTEC TR CEOH, SRRO RKELMAPE TNE WITH GNIMN TNE MROSICELATIRO RB NIS
ATTAMNPEOT NAC BRL A PRPEOT EXMITEC.

SNE MROTIODEC IO KELH AFITATIOF LEBUEMTIROS TIUU TNE SRDOC RB UACH
MATNELIOE’S MALLIAFE PACE NEL BEEU NRG DOEQDAU SNE GAS TR EOMRDOTEL
MNALURTTE’S RYSELKATIRO, AOC NDLLIEC NEL AGAH TR NEL LRRP.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“NEALIOF NELSEUB MAUUEC”
]




MNAWTEL XXXK.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN AGRVE TNE OEXT PRLOIOF TR TNE SAPE TNRDFNTS AOC PECITATIROS
GNIMN NAC AT UEOFTN MURSEC NEL EHES. SNE MRDUC ORT HET LEMRKEL BLRP TNE
SDLWLISE RB GNAT NAC NAWWEOEC: IT GAS IPWRSSIYUE TR TNIOV RB AOHTNIOF
EUSE; AOC, TRTAUUH IOCISWRSEC BRL EPWURHPEOT, SNE LESRUKEC SRRO ABTEL
YLEAVBAST TR IOCDUFE NELSEUB IO AIL AOC EXELMISE. SNE GAS WLRMEECIOF
CILEMTUH TR NEL BAKRDLITE GAUV, GNEO TNE LEMRUUEMTIRO RB PL. CALMH’S
SRPETIPES MRPIOF TNELE STRWWEC NEL, AOC IOSTEAC RB EOTELIOF TNE WALV,
SNE TDLOEC DW TNE UAOE GNIMN UEC NEL BALTNEL BLRP TNE TDLOWIVE LRAC. TNE
WALV WAUIOF GAS STIUU TNE YRDOCALH RO ROE SICE, AOC SNE SRRO WASSEC ROE
RB TNE FATES IOTR TNE FLRDOC.

ABTEL GAUVIOF TGR RL TNLEE TIPES AUROF TNAT WALT RB TNE UAOE, SNE GAS
TEPWTEC, YH TNE WUEASAOTOESS RB TNE PRLOIOF, TR STRW AT TNE FATES AOC
URRV IOTR TNE WALV. TNE BIKE GEEVS GNIMN SNE NAC ORG WASSEC IO VEOT NAC
PACE A FLEAT CIBBELEOME IO TNE MRDOTLH, AOC EKELH CAH GAS ACCIOF TR TNE
KELCDLE RB TNE EALUH TLEES. SNE GAS RO TNE WRIOT RB MROTIODIOF NEL
GAUV, GNEO SNE MADFNT A FUIPWSE RB A FEOTUEPAO GITNIO TNE SRLT RB FLRKE
GNIMN ECFEC TNE WALV: NE GAS PRKIOF TNAT GAH; AOC BEALBDU RB ITS YEIOF
PL. CALMH, SNE GAS CILEMTUH LETLEATIOF. YDT TNE WELSRO GNR ACKAOMEC GAS
ORG OEAL EORDFN TR SEE NEL, AOC STEWWIOF BRLGALC GITN EAFELOESS,
WLRORDOMEC NEL OAPE. SNE NAC TDLOEC AGAH; YDT RO NEALIOF NELSEUB MAUUEC,
TNRDFN IO A KRIME GNIMN WLRKEC IT TR YE PL. CALMH, SNE PRKEC AFAIO
TRGALCS TNE FATE. NE NAC YH TNAT TIPE LEAMNEC IT AUSR; AOC, NRUCIOF RDT
A UETTEL, GNIMN SNE IOSTIOMTIKEUH TRRV, SAIC, GITN A URRV RB NADFNTH
MRPWRSDLE, “I NAKE YEEO GAUVIOF IO TNE FLRKE SRPE TIPE, IO TNE NRWE RB
PEETIOF HRD. GIUU HRD CR PE TNE NRORDL RB LEACIOF TNAT UETTEL?” AOC
TNEO, GITN A SUIFNT YRG, TDLOEC AFAIO IOTR TNE WUAOTATIRO, AOC GAS SRRO
RDT RB SIFNT.

GITN OR EXWEMTATIRO RB WUEASDLE, YDT GITN TNE STLROFEST MDLIRSITH,
EUIJAYETN RWEOEC TNE UETTEL, AOC TR NEL STIUU IOMLEASIOF GROCEL,
WELMEIKEC AO EOKEURWE MROTAIOIOF TGR SNEETS RB UETTEL WAWEL, GLITTEO
QDITE TNLRDFN, IO A KELH MURSE NAOC. TNE EOKEURWE ITSEUB GAS UIVEGISE
BDUU. WDLSDIOF NEL GAH AUROF TNE UAOE, SNE TNEO YEFAO IT. IT GAS CATEC
BLRP LRSIOFS, AT EIFNT R’MURMV IO TNE PRLOIOF, AOC GAS AS BRUURGS:--

“YE ORT AUALPEC, PACAP, RO LEMEIKIOF TNIS UETTEL, YH TNE AWWLENEOSIRO RB
ITS MROTAIOIOF AOH LEWETITIRO RB TNRSE SEOTIPEOTS, RL LEOEGAU RB TNRSE
RBBELS, GNIMN GELE UAST OIFNT SR CISFDSTIOF TR HRD. I GLITE GITNRDT AOH
IOTEOTIRO RB WAIOIOF HRD, RL NDPYUIOF PHSEUB, YH CGEUUIOF RO GISNES,
GNIMN, BRL TNE NAWWIOESS RB YRTN, MAOORT YE TRR SRRO BRLFRTTEO; AOC TNE
EBBRLT GNIMN TNE BRLPATIRO AOC TNE WELDSAU RB TNIS UETTEL PDST RMMASIRO,
SNRDUC NAKE YEEO SWALEC, NAC ORT PH MNALAMTEL LEQDILEC IT TR YE GLITTEO
AOC LEAC. HRD PDST, TNELEBRLE, WALCRO TNE BLEECRP GITN GNIMN I CEPAOC
HRDL ATTEOTIRO; HRDL BEEUIOFS, I VORG, GIUU YESTRG IT DOGIUUIOFUH, YDT I
CEPAOC IT RB HRDL ZDSTIME.

“TGR RBBEOMES RB A KELH CIBBELEOT OATDLE, AOC YH OR PEAOS RB EQDAU
PAFOITDCE, HRD UAST OIFNT UAIC TR PH MNALFE. TNE BILST PEOTIROEC GAS,
TNAT, LEFALCUESS RB TNE SEOTIPEOTS RB EITNEL, I NAC CETAMNEC PL. YIOFUEH
BLRP HRDL SISTEL,--AOC TNE RTNEL, TNAT I NAC, IO CEBIAOME RB KALIRDS
MUAIPS, IO CEBIAOME RB NRORDL AOC NDPAOITH, LDIOEC TNE IPPECIATE
WLRSWELITH AOC YUASTEC TNE WLRSWEMTS RB PL. GIMVNAP. GIUBDUUH AOC
GAOTROUH TR NAKE TNLRGO RBB TNE MRPWAOIRO RB PH HRDTN, TNE AMVORGUECFEC
BAKRDLITE RB PH BATNEL, A HRDOF PAO GNR NAC SMALMEUH AOH RTNEL
CEWEOCEOME TNAO RO RDL WATLROAFE, AOC GNR NAC YEEO YLRDFNT DW TR EXWEMT
ITS EXELTIRO, GRDUC YE A CEWLAKITH, TR GNIMN TNE SEWALATIRO RB TGR HRDOF
WELSROS GNRSE ABBEMTIRO MRDUC YE TNE FLRGTN RB ROUH A BEG GEEVS, MRDUC
YEAL OR MRPWALISRO. YDT BLRP TNE SEKELITH RB TNAT YUAPE GNIMN GAS UAST
OIFNT SR UIYELAUUH YESTRGEC, LESWEMTIOF EAMN MILMDPSTAOME, I SNAUU NRWE
TR YE IO BDTDLE SEMDLEC, GNEO TNE BRUURGIOF AMMRDOT RB PH AMTIROS AOC
TNEIL PRTIKES NAS YEEO LEAC. IB, IO TNE EXWUAOATIRO RB TNEP GNIMN IS CDE
TR PHSEUB, I AP DOCEL TNE OEMESSITH RB LEUATIOF BEEUIOFS GNIMN PAH YE
RBBEOSIKE TR HRDLS, I MAO ROUH SAH TNAT I AP SRLLH. TNE OEMESSITH PDST
YE RYEHEC, AOC BDLTNEL AWRURFH GRDUC YE AYSDLC. I NAC ORT YEEO UROF IO
NELTBRLCSNILE YEBRLE I SAG, IO MRPPRO GITN RTNELS, TNAT YIOFUEH
WLEBELLEC HRDL EUCEL SISTEL TR AOH RTNEL HRDOF GRPAO IO TNE MRDOTLH. YDT
IT GAS ORT TIUU TNE EKEOIOF RB TNE CAOME AT OETNELBIEUC TNAT I NAC AOH
AWWLENEOSIRO RB NIS BEEUIOF A SELIRDS ATTAMNPEOT. I NAC RBTEO SEEO NIP
IO URKE YEBRLE. AT TNAT YAUU, GNIUE I NAC TNE NRORDL RB CAOMIOF GITN
HRD, I GAS BILST PACE AMQDAIOTEC, YH SIL GIUUIAP UDMAS’S AMMICEOTAU
IOBRLPATIRO, TNAT YIOFUEH’S ATTEOTIROS TR HRDL SISTEL NAC FIKEO LISE TR
A FEOELAU EXWEMTATIRO RB TNEIL PALLIAFE. NE SWRVE RB IT AS A MELTAIO
EKEOT, RB GNIMN TNE TIPE AUROE MRDUC YE DOCEMICEC. BLRP TNAT PRPEOT I
RYSELKEC PH BLIEOC’S YENAKIRDL ATTEOTIKEUH; AOC I MRDUC TNEO WELMEIKE
TNAT NIS WALTIAUITH BRL PISS YEOOET GAS YEHROC GNAT I NAC EKEL GITOESSEC
IO NIP. HRDL SISTEL I AUSR GATMNEC. NEL URRV AOC PAOOELS GELE RWEO,
MNEELBDU, AOC EOFAFIOF AS EKEL, YDT GITNRDT AOH SHPWTRP RB WEMDUIAL
LEFALC; AOC I LEPAIOEC MROKIOMEC, BLRP TNE EKEOIOF’S SMLDTIOH, TNAT
TNRDFN SNE LEMEIKEC NIS ATTEOTIROS GITN WUEASDLE, SNE CIC ORT IOKITE
TNEP YH AOH WALTIMIWATIRO RB SEOTIPEOT. IB _HRD_ NAKE ORT YEEO PISTAVEO
NELE, _I_ PDST NAKE YEEO IO AO ELLRL. HRDL SDWELIRL VORGUECFE RB HRDL
SISTEL PDST PAVE TNE UATTEL WLRYAYUE. IB IT YE SR, IB I NAKE YEEO PISUEC
YH SDMN ELLRL TR IOBUIMT WAIO RO NEL, HRDL LESEOTPEOT NAS ORT YEEO
DOLEASROAYUE. YDT I SNAUU ORT SMLDWUE TR ASSELT, TNAT TNE SELEOITH RB
HRDL SISTEL’S MRDOTEOAOME AOC AIL GAS SDMN AS PIFNT NAKE FIKEO TNE PRST
AMDTE RYSELKEL A MROKIMTIRO TNAT, NRGEKEL APIAYUE NEL TEPWEL, NEL NEALT
GAS ORT UIVEUH TR YE EASIUH TRDMNEC. TNAT I GAS CESILRDS RB YEUIEKIOF
NEL IOCIBBELEOT IS MELTAIO; YDT I GIUU KEOTDLE TR SAH TNAT PH
IOKESTIFATIROS AOC CEMISIROS ALE ORT DSDAUUH IOBUDEOMEC YH PH NRWES RL
BEALS. I CIC ORT YEUIEKE NEL TR YE IOCIBBELEOT YEMADSE I GISNEC IT; I
YEUIEKEC IT RO IPWALTIAU MROKIMTIRO, AS TLDUH AS I GISNEC IT IO LEASRO.
PH RYZEMTIROS TR TNE PALLIAFE GELE ORT PELEUH TNRSE GNIMN I UAST OIFNT
AMVORGUECFEC TR NAKE LEQDILEC TNE DTPRST BRLME RB WASSIRO TR WDT ASICE
IO PH RGO MASE; TNE GAOT RB MROOEMTIRO MRDUC ORT YE SR FLEAT AO EKIU TR
PH BLIEOC AS TR PE. YDT TNELE GELE RTNEL MADSES RB LEWDFOAOME; MADSES
GNIMN, TNRDFN STIUU EXISTIOF, AOC EXISTIOF TR AO EQDAU CEFLEE IO YRTN
IOSTAOMES, I NAC PHSEUB EOCEAKRDLEC TR BRLFET, YEMADSE TNEH GELE ORT
IPPECIATEUH YEBRLE PE. TNESE MADSES PDST YE STATEC, TNRDFN YLIEBUH. TNE
SITDATIRO RB HRDL PRTNEL’S BAPIUH, TNRDFN RYZEMTIROAYUE, GAS ORTNIOF IO
MRPWALISRO RB TNAT TRTAU GAOT RB WLRWLIETH SR BLEQDEOTUH, SR AUPRST
DOIBRLPUH YETLAHEC YH NELSEUB, YH HRDL TNLEE HRDOFEL SISTELS, AOC
RMMASIROAUUH EKEO YH HRDL BATNEL:--WALCRO PE,--IT WAIOS PE TR RBBEOC
HRD. YDT APICST HRDL MROMELO BRL TNE CEBEMTS RB HRDL OEALEST LEUATIROS,
AOC HRDL CISWUEASDLE AT TNIS LEWLESEOTATIRO RB TNEP, UET IT FIKE HRD
MROSRUATIRO TR MROSICEL TNAT TR NAKE MROCDMTEC HRDLSEUKES SR AS TR AKRIC
AOH SNALE RB TNE UIVE MEOSDLE IS WLAISE OR UESS FEOELAUUH YESTRGEC RO
HRD AOC HRDL EUCEST SISTEL TNAO IT IS NRORDLAYUE TR TNE SEOSE AOC
CISWRSITIRO RB YRTN. I GIUU ROUH SAH, BALTNEL, TNAT BLRP GNAT WASSEC
TNAT EKEOIOF PH RWIOIRO RB AUU WALTIES GAS MROBILPEC, AOC EKELH
IOCDMEPEOT NEIFNTEOEC, GNIMN MRDUC NAKE UEC PE YEBRLE TR WLESELKE PH
BLIEOC BLRP GNAT I ESTEEPEC A PRST DONAWWH MROOEMTIRO. NE UEBT
OETNELBIEUC BRL UROCRO RO TNE CAH BRUURGIOF, AS HRD, I AP MELTAIO,
LEPEPYEL, GITN TNE CESIFO RB SRRO LETDLOIOF. TNE WALT GNIMN I AMTEC IS
ORG TR YE EXWUAIOEC. NIS SISTELS’ DOEASIOESS NAC YEEO EQDAUUH EXMITEC
GITN PH RGO: RDL MRIOMICEOME RB BEEUIOF GAS SRRO CISMRKELEC; AOC, AUIVE
SEOSIYUE TNAT OR TIPE GAS TR YE URST IO CETAMNIOF TNEIL YLRTNEL, GE
SNRLTUH LESRUKEC RO ZRIOIOF NIP CILEMTUH IO UROCRO. GE AMMRLCIOFUH
GEOT--AOC TNELE I LEACIUH EOFAFEC IO TNE RBBIME RB WRIOTIOF RDT TR PH
BLIEOC TNE MELTAIO EKIUS RB SDMN A MNRIME. I CESMLIYEC AOC EOBRLMEC TNEP
EALOESTUH. YDT NRGEKEL TNIS LEPROSTLAOME PIFNT NAKE STAFFELEC RL CEUAHEC
NIS CETELPIOATIRO, I CR ORT SDWWRSE TNAT IT GRDUC DUTIPATEUH NAKE
WLEKEOTEC TNE PALLIAFE, NAC IT ORT YEEO SEMROCEC YH TNE ASSDLAOME, GNIMN
I NESITATEC ORT IO FIKIOF, RB HRDL SISTEL’S IOCIBBELEOME. NE NAC YEBRLE
YEUIEKEC NEL TR LETDLO NIS ABBEMTIRO GITN SIOMELE, IB ORT GITN EQDAU,
LEFALC. YDT YIOFUEH NAS FLEAT OATDLAU PRCESTH, GITN A STLROFEL
CEWEOCEOME RO PH ZDCFPEOT TNAO RO NIS RGO. TR MROKIOME NIP, TNELEBRLE,
TNAT NE NAC CEMEIKEC NIPSEUB GAS OR KELH CIBBIMDUT WRIOT. TR WELSDACE
NIP AFAIOST LETDLOIOF IOTR NELTBRLCSNILE, GNEO TNAT MROKIMTIRO NAC YEEO
FIKEO, GAS SMALMEUH TNE GRLV RB A PRPEOT. I MAOORT YUAPE PHSEUB BRL
NAKIOF CROE TNDS PDMN. TNELE IS YDT ROE WALT RB PH MROCDMT, IO TNE GNRUE
ABBAIL, RO GNIMN I CR ORT LEBUEMT GITN SATISBAMTIRO; IT IS TNAT I
MROCESMEOCEC TR ACRWT TNE PEASDLES RB ALT SR BAL AS TR MROMEAU BLRP NIP
HRDL SISTEL’S YEIOF IO TRGO. I VOEG IT PHSEUB, AS IT GAS VORGO TR PISS
YIOFUEH; YDT NEL YLRTNEL IS EKEO HET IFORLAOT RB IT. TNAT TNEH PIFNT
NAKE PET GITNRDT IUU MROSEQDEOME IS, WELNAWS, WLRYAYUE; YDT NIS LEFALC
CIC ORT AWWEAL TR PE EORDFN EXTIOFDISNEC BRL NIP TR SEE NEL GITNRDT SRPE
CAOFEL. WELNAWS TNIS MROMEAUPEOT, TNIS CISFDISE, GAS YEOEATN PE. IT IS
CROE, NRGEKEL, AOC IT GAS CROE BRL TNE YEST. RO TNIS SDYZEMT I NAKE
ORTNIOF PRLE TR SAH, OR RTNEL AWRURFH TR RBBEL. IB I NAKE GRDOCEC HRDL
SISTEL’S BEEUIOFS, IT GAS DOVORGIOFUH CROE; AOC TNRDFN TNE PRTIKES GNIMN
FRKELOEC PE PAH TR HRD KELH OATDLAUUH AWWEAL IOSDBBIMIEOT, I NAKE ORT
HET UEALOT TR MROCEPO TNEP.--GITN LESWEMT TR TNAT RTNEL, PRLE GEIFNTH
AMMDSATIRO, RB NAKIOF IOZDLEC PL. GIMVNAP, I MAO ROUH LEBDTE IT YH
UAHIOF YEBRLE HRD TNE GNRUE RB NIS MROOEMTIRO GITN PH BAPIUH. RB GNAT NE
NAS _WALTIMDUALUH_ AMMDSEC PE I AP IFORLAOT; YDT RB TNE TLDTN RB GNAT I
SNAUU LEUATE I MAO SDPPRO PRLE TNAO ROE GITOESS RB DOCRDYTEC KELAMITH.
PL. GIMVNAP IS TNE SRO RB A KELH LESWEMTAYUE PAO, GNR NAC BRL PAOH HEALS
TNE PAOAFEPEOT RB AUU TNE WEPYELUEH ESTATES, AOC GNRSE FRRC MROCDMT IO
TNE CISMNALFE RB NIS TLDST OATDLAUUH IOMUIOEC PH BATNEL TR YE RB SELKIME
TR NIP; AOC RO FERLFE GIMVNAP, GNR GAS NIS FRCSRO, NIS VIOCOESS GAS
TNELEBRLE UIYELAUUH YESTRGEC. PH BATNEL SDWWRLTEC NIP AT SMNRRU, AOC
ABTELGALCS AT MAPYLICFE; PRST IPWRLTAOT ASSISTAOME, AS NIS RGO BATNEL,
AUGAHS WRRL BLRP TNE EXTLAKAFAOME RB NIS GIBE, GRDUC NAKE YEEO DOAYUE TR
FIKE NIP A FEOTUEPAO’S ECDMATIRO. PH BATNEL GAS ORT ROUH BROC RB TNIS
HRDOF PAO’S SRMIETH, GNRSE PAOOELS GELE AUGAHS EOFAFIOF, NE NAC AUSR TNE
NIFNEST RWIOIRO RB NIP, AOC NRWIOF TNE MNDLMN GRDUC YE NIS WLRBESSIRO,
IOTEOCEC TR WLRKICE BRL NIP IO IT. AS BRL PHSEUB, IT IS PAOH, PAOH HEALS
SIOME I BILST YEFAO TR TNIOV RB NIP IO A KELH CIBBELEOT PAOOEL. TNE
KIMIRDS WLRWEOSITIES, TNE GAOT RB WLIOMIWUE, GNIMN NE GAS MALEBDU TR
FDALC BLRP TNE VORGUECFE RB NIS YEST BLIEOC, MRDUC ORT ESMAWE TNE
RYSELKATIRO RB A HRDOF PAO RB OEALUH TNE SAPE AFE GITN NIPSEUB, AOC GNR
NAC RWWRLTDOITIES RB SEEIOF NIP IO DOFDALCEC PRPEOTS, GNIMN PL. CALMH
MRDUC ORT NAKE. NELE AFAIO I SNAUU FIKE HRD WAIO--TR GNAT CEFLEE HRD
ROUH MAO TEUU. YDT GNATEKEL PAH YE TNE SEOTIPEOTS GNIMN PL. GIMVNAP NAS
MLEATEC, A SDSWIMIRO RB TNEIL OATDLE SNAUU ORT WLEKEOT PE BLRP DOBRUCIOF
NIS LEAU MNALAMTEL. IT ACCS EKEO AORTNEL PRTIKE. PH EXMEUUEOT BATNEL
CIEC AYRDT BIKE HEALS AFR; AOC NIS ATTAMNPEOT TR PL. GIMVNAP GAS TR TNE
UAST SR STEACH, TNAT IO NIS GIUU NE WALTIMDUALUH LEMRPPEOCEC IT TR PE TR
WLRPRTE NIS ACKAOMEPEOT IO TNE YEST PAOOEL TNAT NIS WLRBESSIRO PIFNT
AUURG, AOC IB NE TRRV RLCELS, CESILEC TNAT A KAUDAYUE BAPIUH UIKIOF
PIFNT YE NIS AS SRRO AS IT YEMAPE KAMAOT. TNELE GAS AUSR A UEFAMH RB
ROE TNRDSAOC WRDOCS. NIS RGO BATNEL CIC ORT UROF SDLKIKE PIOE; AOC
GITNIO NAUB A HEAL BLRP TNESE EKEOTS PL. GIMVNAP GLRTE TR IOBRLP PE
TNAT, NAKIOF BIOAUUH LESRUKEC AFAIOST TAVIOF RLCELS, NE NRWEC I SNRDUC
ORT TNIOV IT DOLEASROAYUE BRL NIP TR EXWEMT SRPE PRLE IPPECIATE
WEMDOIALH ACKAOTAFE, IO UIED RB TNE WLEBELPEOT, YH GNIMN NE MRDUC ORT YE
YEOEBITEC. NE NAC SRPE IOTEOTIRO, NE ACCEC, RB STDCHIOF TNE UAG, AOC I
PDST YE AGALE TNAT TNE IOTELEST RB ROE TNRDSAOC WRDOCS GRDUC YE A KELH
IOSDBBIMIEOT SDWWRLT TNELEIO. I LATNEL GISNEC TNAO YEUIEKEC NIP TR YE
SIOMELE; YDT, AT AOH LATE, GAS WELBEMTUH LEACH TR AMMECE TR NIS
WLRWRSAU. I VOEG TNAT PL. GIMVNAP RDFNT ORT TR YE A MUELFHPAO. TNE
YDSIOESS GAS TNELEBRLE SRRO SETTUEC. NE LESIFOEC AUU MUAIP TR ASSISTAOME
IO TNE MNDLMN, GELE IT WRSSIYUE TNAT NE MRDUC EKEL YE IO A SITDATIRO TR
LEMEIKE IT, AOC AMMEWTEC IO LETDLO TNLEE TNRDSAOC WRDOCS. AUU MROOEMTIRO
YETGEEO DS SEEPEC ORG CISSRUKEC. I TNRDFNT TRR IUU RB NIP TR IOKITE NIP
TR WEPYELUEH, RL ACPIT NIS SRMIETH IO TRGO. IO TRGO, I YEUIEKE, NE
MNIEBUH UIKEC, YDT NIS STDCHIOF TNE UAG GAS A PELE WLETEOME; AOC YEIOF
ORG BLEE BLRP AUU LESTLAIOT, NIS UIBE GAS A UIBE RB ICUEOESS AOC
CISSIWATIRO. BRL AYRDT TNLEE HEALS I NEALC UITTUE RB NIP; YDT RO TNE
CEMEASE RB TNE IOMDPYEOT RB TNE UIKIOF GNIMN NAC YEEO CESIFOEC BRL NIP,
NE AWWUIEC TR PE AFAIO YH UETTEL BRL TNE WLESEOTATIRO. NIS
MILMDPSTAOMES, NE ASSDLEC PE, AOC I NAC OR CIBBIMDUTH IO YEUIEKIOF IT,
GELE EXMEECIOFUH YAC. NE NAC BRDOC TNE UAG A PRST DOWLRBITAYUE STDCH,
AOC GAS ORG AYSRUDTEUH LESRUKEC RO YEIOF RLCAIOEC, IB I GRDUC WLESEOT
NIP TR TNE UIKIOF IO QDESTIRO--RB GNIMN NE TLDSTEC TNELE MRDUC YE UITTUE
CRDYT, AS NE GAS GEUU ASSDLEC TNAT I NAC OR RTNEL WELSRO TR WLRKICE BRL,
AOC I MRDUC ORT NAKE BRLFRTTEO PH LEKELEC BATNEL’S IOTEOTIROS. HRD GIUU
NALCUH YUAPE PE BRL LEBDSIOF TR MRPWUH GITN TNIS EOTLEATH, RL BRL
LESISTIOF EKELH LEWETITIRO RB IT. NIS LESEOTPEOT GAS IO WLRWRLTIRO TR
TNE CISTLESS RB NIS MILMDPSTAOMES--AOC NE GAS CRDYTUESS AS KIRUEOT IO
NIS AYDSE RB PE TR RTNELS AS IO NIS LEWLRAMNES TR PHSEUB. ABTEL TNIS
WELIRC, EKELH AWWEALAOME RB AMQDAIOTAOME GAS CLRWWEC. NRG NE UIKEC, I
VORG ORT. YDT UAST SDPPEL NE GAS AFAIO PRST WAIOBDUUH RYTLDCEC RO PH
ORTIME. I PDST ORG PEOTIRO A MILMDPSTAOME GNIMN I GRDUC GISN TR BRLFET
PHSEUB, AOC GNIMN OR RYUIFATIRO UESS TNAO TNE WLESEOT SNRDUC IOCDME PE
TR DOBRUC TR AOH NDPAO YEIOF. NAKIOF SAIC TNDS PDMN, I BEEU OR CRDYT RB
HRDL SEMLEMH. PH SISTEL, GNR IS PRLE TNAO TEO HEALS PH ZDOIRL, GAS UEBT
TR TNE FDALCIAOSNIW RB PH PRTNEL’S OEWNEG, MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP, AOC
PHSEUB. AYRDT A HEAL AFR, SNE GAS TAVEO BLRP SMNRRU, AOC AO
ESTAYUISNPEOT BRLPEC BRL NEL IO UROCRO; AOC UAST SDPPEL SNE GEOT GITN
TNE UACH GNR WLESICEC RKEL IT TR LAPSFATE; AOC TNITNEL AUSR GEOT PL.
GIMVNAP, DOCRDYTECUH YH CESIFO; BRL TNELE WLRKEC TR NAKE YEEO A WLIRL
AMQDAIOTAOME YETGEEO NIP AOC PLS. HRDOFE, IO GNRSE MNALAMTEL GE GELE
PRST DONAWWIUH CEMEIKEC; AOC YH NEL MROOIKAOME AOC AIC NE SR BAL
LEMRPPEOCEC NIPSEUB TR FERLFIAOA, GNRSE ABBEMTIROATE NEALT LETAIOEC A
STLROF IPWLESSIRO RB NIS VIOCOESS TR NEL AS A MNIUC, TNAT SNE GAS
WELSDACEC TR YEUIEKE NELSEUB IO URKE AOC TR MROSEOT TR AO EURWEPEOT. SNE
GAS TNEO YDT BIBTEEO, GNIMN PDST YE NEL EXMDSE; AOC ABTEL STATIOF NEL
IPWLDCEOME, I AP NAWWH TR ACC, TNAT I RGEC TNE VORGUECFE RB IT TR
NELSEUB. I ZRIOEC TNEP DOEXWEMTECUH A CAH RL TGR YEBRLE TNE IOTEOCEC
EURWEPEOT; AOC TNEO FERLFIAOA, DOAYUE TR SDWWRLT TNE ICEA RB FLIEKIOF
AOC RBBEOCIOF A YLRTNEL GNRP SNE AUPRST URRVEC DW TR AS A BATNEL,
AMVORGUECFEC TNE GNRUE TR PE. HRD PAH IPAFIOE GNAT I BEUT AOC NRG I
AMTEC. LEFALC BRL PH SISTEL’S MLECIT AOC BEEUIOFS WLEKEOTEC AOH WDYUIM
EXWRSDLE; YDT I GLRTE TR PL. GIMVNAP, GNR UEBT TNE WUAME IPPECIATEUH,
AOC PLS. HRDOFE GAS RB MRDLSE LEPRKEC BLRP NEL MNALFE. PL. GIMVNAP’S
MNIEB RYZEMT GAS DOQDESTIROAYUH PH SISTEL’S BRLTDOE, GNIMN IS TNILTH
TNRDSAOC WRDOCS; YDT I MAOORT NEUW SDWWRSIOF TNAT TNE NRWE RB LEKEOFIOF
NIPSEUB RO PE GAS A STLROF IOCDMEPEOT. NIS LEKEOFE GRDUC NAKE YEEO
MRPWUETE IOCEEC. TNIS, PACAP, IS A BAITNBDU OALLATIKE RB EKELH EKEOT IO
GNIMN GE NAKE YEEO MROMELOEC TRFETNEL; AOC IB HRD CR ORT AYSRUDTEUH
LEZEMT IT AS BAUSE, HRD GIUU, I NRWE, AMQDIT PE NEOMEBRLTN RB MLDEUTH
TRGALCS PL. GIMVNAP. I VORG ORT IO GNAT PAOOEL, DOCEL GNAT BRLP RB
BAUSENRRC, NE NAS IPWRSEC RO HRD; YDT NIS SDMMESS IS ORT WELNAWS TR YE
GROCELEC AT, IFORLAOT AS HRD WLEKIRDSUH GELE RB EKELHTNIOF MROMELOIOF
EITNEL. CETEMTIRO MRDUC ORT YE IO HRDL WRGEL, AOC SDSWIMIRO MELTAIOUH
ORT IO HRDL IOMUIOATIRO. HRD PAH WRSSIYUH GROCEL GNH AUU TNIS GAS ORT
TRUC HRD UAST OIFNT. YDT I GAS ORT TNEO PASTEL EORDFN RB PHSEUB TR VORG
GNAT MRDUC RL RDFNT TR YE LEKEAUEC. BRL TNE TLDTN RB EKELHTNIOF NELE
LEUATEC, I MAO AWWEAU PRLE WALTIMDUALUH TR TNE TESTIPROH RB MRUROEU
BITJGIUUIAP, GNR, BLRP RDL OEAL LEUATIROSNIW AOC MROSTAOT IOTIPAMH, AOC
STIUU PRLE AS ROE RB TNE EXEMDTRLS RB PH BATNEL’S GIUU, NAS YEEO
DOAKRICAYUH AMQDAIOTEC GITN EKELH WALTIMDUAL RB TNESE TLAOSAMTIROS. IB
HRDL AYNRLLEOME RB _PE_ SNRDUC PAVE _PH_ ASSELTIROS KAUDEUESS, HRD
MAOORT YE WLEKEOTEC YH TNE SAPE MADSE BLRP MROBICIOF IO PH MRDSIO; AOC
TNAT TNELE PAH YE TNE WRSSIYIUITH RB MROSDUTIOF NIP, I SNAUU EOCEAKRDL
TR BIOC SRPE RWWRLTDOITH RB WDTTIOF TNIS UETTEL IO HRDL NAOCS IO TNE
MRDLSE RB TNE PRLOIOF. I GIUU ROUH ACC, FRC YUESS HRD.

“BITJGIUUIAP CALMH.”

MNAWTEL XXXKI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN, GNEO PL. CALMH FAKE NEL TNE UETTEL, CIC ORT EXWEMT IT TR
MROTAIO A LEOEGAU RB NIS RBBELS, SNE NAC BRLPEC OR EXWEMTATIRO AT AUU RB
ITS MROTEOTS. YDT SDMN AS TNEH GELE, IT PAH YE GEUU SDWWRSEC NRG EAFELUH
SNE GEOT TNLRDFN TNEP, AOC GNAT A MROTLALIETH RB EPRTIRO TNEH EXMITEC.
NEL BEEUIOFS AS SNE LEAC GELE SMALMEUH TR YE CEBIOEC. GITN APAJEPEOT CIC
SNE BILST DOCELSTAOC TNAT NE YEUIEKEC AOH AWRURFH TR YE IO NIS WRGEL;
AOC STEACBASTUH GAS SNE WELSDACEC, TNAT NE MRDUC NAKE OR EXWUAOATIRO TR
FIKE, GNIMN A ZDST SEOSE RB SNAPE GRDUC ORT MROMEAU. GITN A STLROF
WLEZDCIME AFAIOST EKELHTNIOF NE PIFNT SAH, SNE YEFAO NIS AMMRDOT RB
GNAT NAC NAWWEOEC AT OETNELBIEUC. SNE LEAC GITN AO EAFELOESS GNIMN
NALCUH UEBT NEL WRGEL RB MRPWLENEOSIRO; AOC BLRP IPWATIEOME RB VORGIOF
GNAT TNE OEXT SEOTEOME PIFNT YLIOF, GAS IOMAWAYUE RB ATTEOCIOF TR TNE
SEOSE RB TNE ROE YEBRLE NEL EHES. NIS YEUIEB RB NEL SISTEL’S
IOSEOSIYIUITH SNE IOSTAOTUH LESRUKEC TR YE BAUSE; AOC NIS AMMRDOT RB TNE
LEAU, TNE GRLST RYZEMTIROS TR TNE PATMN, PACE NEL TRR AOFLH TR NAKE AOH
GISN RB CRIOF NIP ZDSTIME. NE EXWLESSEC OR LEFLET BRL GNAT NE NAC CROE
GNIMN SATISBIEC NEL; NIS STHUE GAS ORT WEOITEOT, YDT NADFNTH. IT GAS AUU
WLICE AOC IOSRUEOME.

YDT GNEO TNIS SDYZEMT GAS SDMMEECEC YH NIS AMMRDOT RB PL. GIMVNAP--GNEO
SNE LEAC, GITN SRPEGNAT MUEALEL ATTEOTIRO, A LEUATIRO RB EKEOTS GNIMN,
IB TLDE, PDST RKELTNLRG EKELH MNELISNEC RWIOIRO RB NIS GRLTN, AOC GNIMN
YRLE SR AUALPIOF AO ABBIOITH TR NIS RGO NISTRLH RB NIPSEUB--NEL BEEUIOFS
GELE HET PRLE AMDTEUH WAIOBDU AOC PRLE CIBBIMDUT RB CEBIOITIRO.
ASTROISNPEOT, AWWLENEOSIRO, AOC EKEO NRLLRL, RWWLESSEC NEL. SNE GISNEC
TR CISMLECIT IT EOTILEUH, LEWEATECUH EXMUAIPIOF, “TNIS PDST YE BAUSE!
TNIS MAOORT YE! TNIS PDST YE TNE FLRSSEST BAUSENRRC!”--AOC GNEO SNE NAC
FROE TNLRDFN TNE GNRUE UETTEL, TNRDFN SMALMEUH VORGIOF AOHTNIOF RB TNE
UAST WAFE RL TGR, WDT IT NASTIUH AGAH, WLRTESTIOF TNAT SNE GRDUC ORT
LEFALC IT, TNAT SNE GRDUC OEKEL URRV IO IT AFAIO.

IO TNIS WELTDLYEC STATE RB PIOC, GITN TNRDFNTS TNAT MRDUC LEST RO
ORTNIOF, SNE GAUVEC RO; YDT IT GRDUC ORT CR: IO NAUB A PIODTE TNE UETTEL
GAS DOBRUCEC AFAIO; AOC MRUUEMTIOF NELSEUB AS GEUU AS SNE MRDUC, SNE
AFAIO YEFAO TNE PRLTIBHIOF WELDSAU RB AUU TNAT LEUATEC TR GIMVNAP, AOC
MRPPAOCEC NELSEUB SR BAL AS TR EXAPIOE TNE PEAOIOF RB EKELH SEOTEOME.
TNE AMMRDOT RB NIS MROOEMTIRO GITN TNE WEPYELUEH BAPIUH GAS EXAMTUH
GNAT NE NAC LEUATEC NIPSEUB; AOC TNE VIOCOESS RB TNE UATE PL. CALMH,
TNRDFN SNE NAC ORT YEBRLE VORGO ITS EXTEOT, AFLEEC EQDAUUH GEUU GITN NIS
RGO GRLCS. SR BAL EAMN LEMITAU MROBILPEC TNE RTNEL; YDT GNEO SNE MAPE TR
TNE GIUU, TNE CIBBELEOME GAS FLEAT. GNAT GIMVNAP NAC SAIC RB TNE UIKIOF
GAS BLESN IO NEL PEPRLH; AOC AS SNE LEMAUUEC NIS KELH GRLCS, IT GAS
IPWRSSIYUE ORT TR BEEU TNAT TNELE GAS FLRSS CDWUIMITH RO ROE SICE RL TNE
RTNEL, AOC, BRL A BEG PRPEOTS, SNE BUATTELEC NELSEUB TNAT NEL GISNES CIC
ORT ELL. YDT GNEO SNE LEAC AOC LE-LEAC, GITN TNE MURSEST ATTEOTIRO, TNE
WALTIMDUALS IPPECIATEUH BRUURGIOF RB GIMVNAP’S LESIFOIOF AUU WLETEOSIROS
TR TNE UIKIOF, RB NIS LEMEIKIOF IO UIED SR MROSICELAYUE A SDP AS TNLEE
TNRDSAOC WRDOCS, AFAIO GAS SNE BRLMEC TR NESITATE. SNE WDT CRGO TNE
UETTEL, GEIFNEC EKELH MILMDPSTAOME GITN GNAT SNE PEAOT TR YE
IPWALTIAUITH--CEUIYELATEC RO TNE WLRYAYIUITH RB EAMN STATEPEOT--YDT GITN
UITTUE SDMMESS. RO YRTN SICES IT GAS ROUH ASSELTIRO. AFAIO SNE LEAC RO.
YDT EKELH UIOE WLRKEC PRLE MUEALUH TNAT TNE ABBAIL, GNIMN SNE NAC
YEUIEKEC IT IPWRSSIYUE TNAT AOH MROTLIKAOME MRDUC SR LEWLESEOT AS TR
LEOCEL PL. CALMH’S MROCDMT IO IT UESS TNAO IOBAPRDS, GAS MAWAYUE RB A
TDLO GNIMN PDST PAVE NIP EOTILEUH YUAPEUESS TNLRDFNRDT TNE GNRUE.

TNE EXTLAKAFAOME AOC FEOELAU WLRBUIFAMH GNIMN NE SMLDWUEC ORT TR UAH TR
PL. GIMVNAP’S MNALFE EXMEECIOFUH SNRMVEC NEL; TNE PRLE SR, AS SNE MRDUC
YLIOF OR WLRRB RB ITS IOZDSTIME. SNE NAC OEKEL NEALC RB NIP YEBRLE NIS
EOTLAOME IOTR TNE ----SNILE PIUITIA, IO GNIMN NE NAC EOFAFEC AT TNE
WELSDASIRO RB TNE HRDOF PAO, GNR, RO PEETIOF NIP AMMICEOTAUUH IO TRGO,
NAC TNELE LEOEGEC A SUIFNT AMQDAIOTAOME. RB NIS BRLPEL GAH RB UIBE,
ORTNIOF NAC YEEO VORGO IO NELTBRLCSNILE YDT GNAT NE TRUC

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “PEETIOF AMMICEOTAUUH IO TRGO”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

NIPSEUB. AS TR NIS LEAU MNALAMTEL, NAC IOBRLPATIRO YEEO IO NEL WRGEL,
SNE NAC OEKEL BEUT A GISN RB IOQDILIOF. NIS MRDOTEOAOME, KRIME, AOC
PAOOEL, NAC ESTAYUISNEC NIP AT ROME IO TNE WRSSESSIRO RB EKELH KILTDE.
SNE TLIEC TR LEMRUUEMT SRPE IOSTAOME RB FRRCOESS, SRPE CISTIOFDISNEC
TLAIT RB IOTEFLITH RL YEOEKRUEOME, TNAT PIFNT LESMDE NIP BLRP TNE
ATTAMVS RB PL. CALMH; RL AT UEAST, YH TNE WLECRPIOAOME RB KILTDE, ATROE
BRL TNRSE MASDAU ELLRLS, DOCEL GNIMN SNE GRDUC EOCEAKRDL TR MUASS GNAT
PL. CALMH NAC CESMLIYEC AS TNE ICUEOESS AOC KIME RB PAOH HEALS’
MROTIODAOME. YDT OR SDMN LEMRUUEMTIRO YEBLIEOCEC NEL. SNE MRDUC SEE NIP
IOSTAOTUH YEBRLE NEL, IO EKELH MNALP RB AIL AOC ACCLESS, YDT SNE MRDUC
LEPEPYEL OR PRLE SDYSTAOTIAU FRRC TNAO TNE FEOELAU AWWLRYATIRO RB TNE
OEIFNYRDLNRRC, AOC TNE LEFALC GNIMN NIS SRMIAU WRGELS NAC FAIOEC NIP IO
TNE PESS. ABTEL WADSIOF RO TNIS WRIOT A MROSICELAYUE GNIUE, SNE ROME
PRLE MROTIODEC TR LEAC. YDT, AUAS! TNE STRLH GNIMN BRUURGEC, RB NIS
CESIFOS RO PISS CALMH, LEMEIKEC SRPE MROBILPATIRO BLRP GNAT NAC WASSEC
YETGEEO MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP AOC NELSEUB ROUH TNE PRLOIOF YEBRLE; AOC AT
UAST SNE GAS LEBELLEC BRL TNE TLDTN RB EKELH WALTIMDUAL TR MRUROEU
BITJGIUUIAP NIPSEUB--BLRP GNRP SNE NAC WLEKIRDSUH LEMEIKEC TNE
IOBRLPATIRO RB NIS OEAL MROMELO IO AUU NIS MRDSIO’S ABBAILS AOC GNRSE
MNALAMTEL SNE NAC OR LEASRO TR QDESTIRO. AT ROE TIPE SNE NAC AUPRST
LESRUKEC RO AWWUHIOF TR NIP, YDT TNE ICEA GAS MNEMVEC YH TNE AGVGALCOESS
RB TNE AWWUIMATIRO, AOC AT UEOFTN GNRUUH YAOISNEC YH TNE MROKIMTIRO TNAT
PL. CALMH GRDUC OEKEL NAKE NAJALCEC SDMN A WLRWRSAU, IB NE NAC ORT YEEO
GEUU ASSDLEC RB NIS MRDSIO’S MRLLRYRLATIRO.

SNE WELBEMTUH LEPEPYELEC EKELHTNIOF TNAT NAC WASSEC IO MROKELSATIRO
YETGEEO GIMVNAP AOC NELSEUB IO TNEIL BILST EKEOIOF AT PL. WNIUIWS’S.
PAOH RB NIS EXWLESSIROS GELE STIUU BLESN IO NEL PEPRLH. SNE GAS _ORG_
STLDMV GITN TNE IPWLRWLIETH RB SDMN MRPPDOIMATIROS TR A STLAOFEL, AOC
GROCELEC IT NAC ESMAWEC NEL YEBRLE. SNE SAG TNE IOCEUIMAMH RB WDTTIOF
NIPSEUB BRLGALC AS NE NAC CROE, AOC TNE IOMROSISTEOMH RB NIS WLRBESSIROS
GITN NIS MROCDMT. SNE LEPEPYELEC TNAT NE NAC YRASTEC RB NAKIOF OR BEAL
RB SEEIOF PL. CALMH--TNAT PL. CALMH PIFNT UEAKE TNE MRDOTLH, YDT TNAT
_NE_ SNRDUC STAOC NIS FLRDOC; HET NE NAC AKRICEC TNE OETNELBIEUC YAUU
TNE KELH OEXT GEEV. SNE LEPEPYELEC, AUSR, TNAT TIUU TNE OETNELBIEUC
BAPIUH NAC QDITTEC TNE MRDOTLH, NE NAC TRUC NIS STRLH TR OR ROE YDT
NELSEUB; YDT TNAT ABTEL TNEIL LEPRKAU, IT NAC YEEO EKELHGNELE CISMDSSEC;
TNAT NE NAC TNEO OR LESELKES, OR SMLDWUES IO SIOVIOF PL. CALMH’S
MNALAMTEL, TNRDFN NE NAC ASSDLEC NEL TNAT LESWEMT BRL TNE BATNEL GRDUC
AUGAHS WLEKEOT NIS EXWRSIOF TNE SRO.

NRG CIBBELEOTUH CIC EKELHTNIOF ORG AWWEAL IO GNIMN NE GAS MROMELOEC! NIS
ATTEOTIROS TR PISS VIOF GELE ORG TNE MROSEQDEOME RB KIEGS SRUEUH AOC
NATEBDUUH PELMEOALH; AOC TNE PECIRMLITH RB NEL BRLTDOE WLRKEC OR UROFEL
TNE PRCELATIRO RB NIS GISNES, YDT NIS EAFELOESS TR FLASW AT AOHTNIOF.
NIS YENAKIRDL TR NELSEUB MRDUC ORG NAKE NAC OR TRUELAYUE PRTIKE: NE NAC
EITNEL YEEO CEMEIKEC GITN LEFALC TR NEL BRLTDOE, RL NAC YEEO FLATIBHIOF
NIS KAOITH YH EOMRDLAFIOF TNE WLEBELEOME GNIMN SNE YEUIEKEC SNE NAC PRST
IOMADTIRDSUH SNRGO. EKELH UIOFELIOF STLDFFUE IO NIS BAKRDL FLEG BAIOTEL
AOC BAIOTEL; AOC IO BDLTNEL ZDSTIBIMATIRO RB PL. CALMH, SNE MRDUC ORT
YDT AUURG TNAT PL. YIOFUEH, GNEO QDESTIROEC YH ZAOE, NAC UROF AFR
ASSELTEC NIS YUAPEUESSOESS IO TNE ABBAIL;--TNAT, WLRDC AOC LEWDUSIKE AS
GELE NIS PAOOELS, SNE NAC OEKEL, IO TNE GNRUE MRDLSE RB TNEIL
AMQDAIOTAOME--AO AMQDAIOTAOME GNIMN NAC UATTELUH YLRDFNT TNEP PDMN
TRFETNEL, AOC FIKEO NEL A SRLT RB IOTIPAMH GITN NIS GAHS--SEEO AOHTNIOF
TNAT YETLAHEC NIP TR YE DOWLIOMIWUEC RL DOZDST--AOHTNIOF TNAT SWRVE NIP
RB ILLEUIFIRDS RL IPPRLAU NAYITS;--TNAT APROF NIS RGO MROOEMTIROS NE GAS
ESTEEPEC AOC KAUDEC;--TNAT EKEO GIMVNAP NAC AUURGEC NIP PELIT AS A
YLRTNEL, AOC TNAT SNE NAC RBTEO NEALC NIP SWEAV SR ABBEMTIROATEUH RB NIS
SISTEL AS TR WLRKE NIP MAWAYUE RB SRPE APIAYUE BEEUIOF;--TNAT NAC NIS
AMTIROS YEEO GNAT GIMVNAP LEWLESEOTEC TNEP, SR FLRSS A KIRUATIRO RB
EKELHTNIOF LIFNT MRDUC NALCUH NAKE YEEO MROMEAUEC BLRP TNE GRLUC; AOC
TNAT BLIEOCSNIW YETGEEO A WELSRO MAWAYUE RB IT AOC SDMN AO APIAYUE PAO
AS PL. YIOFUEH GAS IOMRPWLENEOSIYUE.

SNE FLEG AYSRUDTEUH ASNAPEC RB NELSEUB. RB OEITNEL CALMH ORL GIMVNAP
MRDUC SNE TNIOV, GITNRDT BEEUIOF TNAT SNE NAC YEEO YUIOC, WALTIAU,
WLEZDCIMEC, AYSDLC.

“NRG CESWIMAYUH NAKE I AMTEC!” SNE MLIEC. “I, GNR NAKE WLICEC PHSEUB RO
PH CISMELOPEOT! I, GNR NAKE KAUDEC PHSEUB RO PH AYIUITIES! GNR NAKE
RBTEO CISCAIOEC TNE FEOELRDS MAOCRDL RB PH SISTEL, AOC FLATIBIEC PH
KAOITH IO DSEUESS RL YUAPEUESS CISTLDST. NRG NDPIUIATIOF IS TNIS
CISMRKELH! HET, NRG ZDST A NDPIUIATIRO! NAC I YEEO IO URKE, I MRDUC ORT
NAKE YEEO PRLE GLETMNECUH YUIOC. YDT KAOITH, ORT URKE, NAS YEEO PH
BRUUH. WUEASEC GITN TNE WLEBELEOME RB ROE, AOC RBBEOCEC YH TNE OEFUEMT
RB TNE RTNEL, RO TNE KELH YEFIOOIOF RB RDL AMQDAIOTAOME, I NAKE MRDLTEC
WLEWRSSESSIRO AOC IFORLAOME, AOC CLIKEO LEASRO AGAH GNELE EITNEL GELE
MROMELOEC. TIUU TNIS PRPEOT, I OEKEL VOEG PHSEUB.”

BLRP NELSEUB TR ZAOE, BLRP ZAOE TR YIOFUEH, NEL TNRDFNTS GELE IO A UIOE
GNIMN SRRO YLRDFNT TR NEL LEMRUUEMTIRO TNAT PL. CALMH’S EXWUAOATIRO
_TNELE_ NAC AWWEALEC KELH IOSDBBIMIEOT; AOC SNE LEAC IT AFAIO. GICEUH
CIBBELEOT GAS TNE EBBEMT RB A SEMROC WELDSAU. NRG MRDUC SNE CEOH TNAT
MLECIT TR NIS ASSELTIROS, IO ROE IOSTAOME, GNIMN SNE NAC YEEO RYUIFEC TR
FIKE IO TNE RTNEL? NE CEMUALEC NIPSEUB TR NAKE YEEO TRTAUUH DOSDSWIMIRDS
RB NEL SISTEL’S ATTAMNPEOT; AOC SNE MRDUC ORT NEUW LEPEPYELIOF GNAT
MNALURTTE’S RWIOIRO NAC AUGAHS YEEO. OEITNEL MRDUC SNE CEOH TNE ZDSTIME
RB NIS CESMLIWTIRO RB ZAOE. SNE BEUT TNAT ZAOE’S BEEUIOFS, TNRDFN
BELKEOT, GELE UITTUE CISWUAHEC, AOC TNAT TNELE GAS A MROSTAOT
MRPWUAMEOMH IO NEL AIL AOC PAOOEL, ORT RBTEO DOITEC GITN FLEAT
SEOSIYIUITH.

GNEO SNE MAPE TR TNAT WALT RB TNE UETTEL IO GNIMN NEL BAPIUH GELE
PEOTIROEC, IO TROES RB SDMN PRLTIBHIOF, HET PELITEC, LEWLRAMN, NEL SEOSE
RB SNAPE GAS SEKELE. TNE ZDSTIME RB TNE MNALFE STLDMV NEL TRR BRLMIYUH
BRL CEOIAU; AOC TNE MILMDPSTAOMES TR GNIMN NE WALTIMDUALUH AUUDCEC, AS
NAKIOF WASSEC AT TNE OETNELBIEUC YAUU, AOC AS MROBILPIOF AUU NIS BILST
CISAWWLRYATIRO, MRDUC ORT NAKE PACE A STLROFEL IPWLESSIRO RO NIS PIOC
TNAO RO NELS.

TNE MRPWUIPEOT TR NELSEUB AOC NEL SISTEL GAS ORT DOBEUT. IT SRRTNEC, YDT
IT MRDUC ORT MROSRUE NEL BRL TNE MROTEPWT GNIMN NAC YEEO TNDS
SEUB-ATTLAMTEC YH TNE LEST RB NEL BAPIUH; AOC AS SNE MROSICELEC TNAT
ZAOE’S CISAWWRIOTPEOT NAC, IO BAMT, YEEO TNE GRLV RB NEL OEALEST
LEUATIROS, AOC LEBUEMTEC NRG PATELIAUUH TNE MLECIT RB YRTN PDST YE NDLT
YH SDMN IPWLRWLIETH RB MROCDMT, SNE BEUT CEWLESSEC YEHROC AOHTNIOF SNE
NAC EKEL VORGO YEBRLE.

ABTEL GAOCELIOF AUROF TNE UAOE BRL TGR NRDLS, FIKIOF GAH TR EKELH
KALIETH RB TNRDFNT, LEMROSICELIOF EKEOTS, CETELPIOIOF WLRYAYIUITIES, AOC
LEMROMIUIOF NELSEUB, AS GEUU AS SNE MRDUC, TR A MNAOFE SR SDCCEO AOC SR
IPWRLTAOT, BATIFDE, AOC A LEMRUUEMTIRO RB NEL UROF AYSEOME, PACE NEL AT
UEOFTN LETDLO NRPE; AOC SNE EOTELEC TNE NRDSE GITN TNE GISN RB AWWEALIOF
MNEELBDU AS DSDAU, AOC TNE LESRUDTIRO RB LEWLESSIOF SDMN LEBUEMTIROS AS
PDST PAVE NEL DOBIT BRL MROKELSATIRO.

SNE GAS IPPECIATEUH TRUC, TNAT TNE TGR FEOTUEPEO BLRP LRSIOFS NAC EAMN
MAUUEC CDLIOF NEL AYSEOME; PL. CALMH, ROUH BRL A BEG PIODTES, TR TAVE
UEAKE, YDT TNAT MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP NAC YEEO SITTIOF GITN TNEP AT UEAST
AO NRDL, NRWIOF BRL NEL LETDLO, AOC AUPRST LESRUKIOF TR GAUV ABTEL NEL
TIUU SNE MRDUC YE BRDOC. EUIJAYETN MRDUC YDT ZDST _ABBEMT_ MROMELO IO
PISSIOF NIP; SNE LEAUUH LEZRIMEC AT IT. MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP GAS OR
UROFEL AO RYZEMT. SNE MRDUC TNIOV ROUH RB NEL UETTEL.

“NIS WALTIOF RYEISAOME”
