MNAWTEL XXXKII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TNE TGR FEOTUEPEO UEBT LRSIOFS TNE OEXT PRLOIOF; AOC PL. MRUUIOS NAKIOF
YEEO IO GAITIOF OEAL TNE URCFES, TR PAVE TNEP NIS WALTIOF RYEISAOME, GAS
AYUE TR YLIOF NRPE TNE WUEASIOF IOTEUUIFEOME RB TNEIL AWWEALIOF IO KELH
FRRC NEAUTN, AOC IO AS TRUELAYUE SWILITS AS MRDUC YE EXWEMTEC, ABTEL TNE
PEUAOMNRUH SMEOE SR UATEUH FROE TNLRDFN AT LRSIOFS. TR LRSIOFS NE TNEO
NASTEOEC TR MROSRUE UACH MATNELIOE AOC NEL CADFNTEL; AOC RO NIS LETDLO
YLRDFNT YAMV, GITN FLEAT SATISBAMTIRO, A PESSAFE BLRP NEL UACHSNIW,
IPWRLTIOF TNAT SNE BEUT NELSEUB SR CDUU AS TR PAVE NEL KELH CESILRDS RB
NAKIOF TNEP AUU TR CIOE GITN NEL.

EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT SEE UACH MATNELIOE GITNRDT LEMRUUEMTIOF TNAT, NAC
SNE MNRSEO IT, SNE PIFNT YH TNIS TIPE NAKE YEEO WLESEOTEC TR NEL AS NEL
BDTDLE OIEME; ORL MRDUC SNE TNIOV, GITNRDT A SPIUE, RB GNAT NEL
UACHSNIW’S IOCIFOATIRO GRDUC NAKE YEEO. “GNAT GRDUC SNE NAKE SAIC? NRG
GRDUC SNE NAKE YENAKEC?” GELE TNE QDESTIROS GITN GNIMN SNE APDSEC
NELSEUB.

TNEIL BILST SDYZEMT GAS TNE CIPIODTIRO RB TNE LRSIOFS’ WALTH. “I ASSDLE
HRD, I BEEU IT EXMEECIOFUH,” SAIC UACH MATNELIOE; “I YEUIEKE ORYRCH
BEEUS TNE URSS RB BLIEOCS SR PDMN AS I CR. YDT I AP WALTIMDUALUH
ATTAMNEC TR TNESE HRDOF PEO; AOC VORG TNEP TR YE SR PDMN ATTAMNEC TR PE!
TNEH GELE EXMESSIKEUH SRLLH TR FR! YDT SR TNEH AUGAHS ALE. TNE CEAL
MRUROEU LAUUIEC NIS SWILITS TRUELAYUH TIUU ZDST AT UAST; YDT CALMH
SEEPEC TR BEEU IT PRST AMDTEUH--PRLE, I TNIOV, TNAO UAST HEAL. NIS
ATTAMNPEOT TR LRSIOFS MELTAIOUH IOMLEASES.”

PL. MRUUIOS NAC A MRPWUIPEOT AOC AO AUUDSIRO TR TNLRG IO NELE, GNIMN
GELE VIOCUH SPIUEC RO YH TNE PRTNEL AOC CADFNTEL.

UACH MATNELIOE RYSELKEC, ABTEL CIOOEL, TNAT PISS YEOOET SEEPEC RDT RB
SWILITS; AOC IPPECIATEUH AMMRDOTIOF BRL IT NELSEUB, YH SDWWRSIOF TNAT
SNE CIC ORT UIVE TR FR NRPE AFAIO SR SRRO, SNE ACCEC,--

“YDT IB TNAT IS TNE MASE, HRD PDST GLITE TR HRDL PRTNEL TR YEF TNAT HRD
PAH STAH A UITTUE UROFEL. PLS. MRUUIOS GIUU YE KELH FUAC RB HRDL
MRPWAOH, I AP SDLE.”

“I AP PDMN RYUIFEC TR HRDL UACHSNIW BRL HRDL VIOC IOKITATIRO,” LEWUIEC
EUIJAYETN; “YDT IT IS ORT IO PH WRGEL TR AMMEWT IT. I PDST YE IO TRGO
OEXT SATDLCAH.”

“GNH, AT TNAT LATE, HRD GIUU NAKE YEEO NELE ROUH SIX GEEVS. I EXWEMTEC
HRD TR STAH TGR PROTNS. I TRUC PLS. MRUUIOS SR YEBRLE HRD MAPE. TNELE
MAO YE OR RMMASIRO BRL HRDL FRIOF SR SRRO. PLS. YEOOET MRDUC MELTAIOUH
SWALE HRD BRL AORTNEL BRLTOIFNT.”

“YDT PH BATNEL MAOORT. NE GLRTE UAST GEEV TR NDLLH PH LETDLO.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“CAGSRO”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

“RN, HRDL BATNEL, RB MRDLSE, PAH SWALE HRD, IB HRDL PRTNEL MAO.
CADFNTELS ALE OEKEL RB SR PDMN MROSEQDEOME TR A BATNEL. AOC IB HRD GIUU
STAH AORTNEL _PROTN_ MRPWUETE, IT GIUU YE IO PH WRGEL TR TAVE ROE RB HRD
AS BAL AS UROCRO, BRL I AP FRIOF TNELE EALUH IO ZDOE, BRL A GEEV; AOC
AS CAGSRO CRES ORT RYZEMT TR TNE YALRDMNE-YRX, TNELE GIUU YE KELH FRRC
LRRP BRL ROE RB HRD--AOC, IOCEEC, IB TNE GEATNEL SNRDUC NAWWEO TR YE
MRRU, I SNRDUC ORT RYZEMT TR TAVIOF HRD YRTN, AS HRD ALE OEITNEL RB HRD
UALFE.”

“HRD ALE AUU VIOCOESS, PACAP; YDT I YEUIEKE GE PDST AYICE YH RDL
RLIFIOAU WUAO.”

UACH MATNELIOE SEEPEC LESIFOEC. “PLS. MRUUIOS, HRD PDST SEOC A SELKAOT
GITN TNEP. HRD VORG I AUGAHS SWEAV PH PIOC, AOC I MAOORT YEAL TNE ICEA
RB TGR HRDOF GRPEO TLAKEUUIOF WRST YH TNEPSEUKES. IT IS NIFNUH IPWLRWEL.
HRD PDST MROTLIKE TR SEOC SRPEYRCH. I NAKE TNE FLEATEST CISUIVE IO TNE
GRLUC TR TNAT SRLT RB TNIOF. HRDOF GRPEO SNRDUC AUGAHS YE WLRWELUH
FDALCEC AOC ATTEOCEC, AMMRLCIOF TR TNEIL SITDATIRO IO UIBE. GNEO PH
OIEME FERLFIAOA GEOT TR LAPSFATE UAST SDPPEL, I PACE A WRIOT RB NEL
NAKIOF TGR PEO-SELKAOTS FR GITN NEL. PISS CALMH, TNE CADFNTEL RB PL.
CALMH RB WEPYELUEH, AOC UACH AOOE, MRDUC ORT NAKE AWWEALEC GITN
WLRWLIETH IO A CIBBELEOT PAOOEL. I AP EXMESSIKEUH ATTEOTIKE TR AUU TNRSE
TNIOFS. HRD PDST SEOC ZRNO GITN TNE HRDOF UACIES, PLS. MRUUIOS. I AP
FUAC IT RMMDLLEC TR PE TR PEOTIRO IT; BRL IT GRDUC LEAUUH YE
CISMLECITAYUE TR _HRD_ TR UET TNEP FR AUROE.”

“PH DOMUE IS TR SEOC A SELKAOT BRL DS.”

“RN! HRDL DOMUE! NE VEEWS A PAO-SELKAOT, CRES NE? I AP KELH FUAC HRD
NAKE SRPEYRCH GNR TNIOVS RB TNRSE TNIOFS. GNELE SNAUU HRD MNAOFE NRLSES?
RN, YLRPUEH, RB MRDLSE. IB HRD PEOTIRO PH OAPE AT TNE YEUU, HRD GIUU YE
ATTEOCEC TR.”

UACH MATNELIOE NAC PAOH RTNEL QDESTIROS TR ASV LESWEMTIOF TNEIL ZRDLOEH;
AOC AS SNE CIC ORT AOSGEL TNEP AUU NELSEUB ATTEOTIRO GAS
OEMESSALH--GNIMN EUIJAYETN YEUIEKEC TR YE UDMVH BRL NEL; RL, GITN A
PIOC SR RMMDWIEC, SNE PIFNT NAKE BRLFRTTEO GNELE SNE GAS. LEBUEMTIRO
PDST YE LESELKEC BRL SRUITALH NRDLS: GNEOEKEL SNE GAS AUROE, SNE FAKE
GAH TR IT AS TNE FLEATEST LEUIEB; AOC ORT A CAH GEOT YH GITNRDT A
SRUITALH GAUV, IO GNIMN SNE PIFNT IOCDUFE IO AUU TNE CEUIFNT RB
DOWUEASAOT LEMRUUEMTIROS.

PL. CALMH’S UETTEL SNE GAS IO A BAIL GAH RB SRRO VORGIOF YH NEALT. SNE
STDCIEC EKELH SEOTEOME; AOC NEL BEEUIOFS TRGALCS ITS GLITEL GELE AT
TIPES GICEUH CIBBELEOT. GNEO SNE LEPEPYELEC TNE STHUE RB NIS ACCLESS,
SNE GAS STIUU BDUU RB IOCIFOATIRO: YDT GNEO SNE MROSICELEC NRG DOZDSTUH
SNE NAC MROCEPOEC AOC DWYLAICEC NIP, NEL AOFEL GAS TDLOEC AFAIOST
NELSEUB; AOC NIS CISAWWRIOTEC BEEUIOFS YEMAPE TNE RYZEMT RB MRPWASSIRO.
NIS ATTAMNPEOT EXMITEC FLATITDCE, NIS FEOELAU MNALAMTEL LESWEMT: YDT SNE
MRDUC ORT AWWLRKE NIP; ORL MRDUC SNE BRL A PRPEOT LEWEOT NEL LEBDSAU, RL
BEEU TNE SUIFNTEST IOMUIOATIRO EKEL TR SEE NIP AFAIO. IO NEL RGO WAST
YENAKIRDL, TNELE GAS A MROSTAOT SRDLME RB KEXATIRO AOC LEFLET: AOC IO
TNE DONAWWH CEBEMTS RB NEL BAPIUH, A SDYZEMT RB HET NEAKIEL MNAFLIO.
TNEH GELE NRWEUESS RB LEPECH. NEL BATNEL, MROTEOTEC GITN UADFNIOF AT
TNEP, GRDUC OEKEL EXELT NIPSEUB TR LESTLAIO TNE GIUC FICCIOESS RB NIS
HRDOFEST CADFNTELS; AOC NEL PRTNEL, GITN PAOOELS SR BAL BLRP LIFNT
NELSEUB, GAS EOTILEUH IOSEOSIYUE RB TNE EKIU. EUIJAYETN NAC BLEQDEOTUH
DOITEC GITN ZAOE IO AO EOCEAKRDL TR MNEMV TNE IPWLDCEOME RB MATNELIOE
AOC UHCIA; YDT GNIUE TNEH GELE SDWWRLTEC YH TNEIL PRTNEL’S IOCDUFEOME,
GNAT MNAOME MRDUC TNELE YE RB IPWLRKEPEOT? MATNELIOE, GEAV-SWILITEC,
ILLITAYUE, AOC MRPWUETEUH DOCEL UHCIA’S FDICAOME, NAC YEEO AUGAHS
ABBLROTEC YH TNEIL ACKIME; AOC UHCIA, SEUB-GIUUEC AOC MALEUESS, GRDUC
SMALMEUH FIKE TNEP A NEALIOF. TNEH GELE IFORLAOT, ICUE, AOC KAIO. GNIUE
TNELE GAS AO RBBIMEL IO PELHTRO, TNEH GRDUC BUILT GITN NIP; AOC GNIUE
PELHTRO GAS GITNIO A GAUV RB UROFYRDLO, TNEH GRDUC YE FRIOF TNELE BRL
EKEL.

AOXIETH RO ZAOE’S YENAUB GAS AORTNEL WLEKAIUIOF MROMELO; AOC PL. CALMH’S
EXWUAOATIRO, YH LESTRLIOF YIOFUEH TR AUU NEL BRLPEL FRRC RWIOIRO,
NEIFNTEOEC TNE SEOSE RB GNAT ZAOE NAC URST. NIS ABBEMTIRO GAS WLRKEC TR
NAKE YEEO SIOMELE, AOC NIS MROCDMT MUEALEC RB AUU YUAPE, DOUESS AOH
MRDUC ATTAMN TR TNE IPWUIMITOESS RB NIS MROBICEOME IO NIS BLIEOC. NRG
FLIEKRDS TNEO GAS TNE TNRDFNT TNAT, RB A SITDATIRO SR CESILAYUE IO EKELH
LESWEMT, SR LEWUETE GITN ACKAOTAFE, SR WLRPISIOF BRL NAWWIOESS, ZAOE NAC
YEEO CEWLIKEC, YH TNE BRUUH AOC IOCEMRLDP RB NEL RGO BAPIUH!

GNEO TR TNESE LEMRUUEMTIROS GAS ACCEC TNE CEKEURWPEOT RB GIMVNAP’S
MNALAMTEL, IT PAH YE EASIUH YEUIEKEC TNAT TNE NAWWH SWILITS GNIMN NAC
SEUCRP YEEO CEWLESSEC YEBRLE GELE ORG SR PDMN ABBEMTEC AS TR PAVE IT
AUPRST IPWRSSIYUE BRL NEL TR AWWEAL TRUELAYUH MNEELBDU.

TNEIL EOFAFEPEOTS AT LRSIOFS GELE AS BLEQDEOT CDLIOF TNE UAST GEEV RB
NEL STAH AS TNEH NAC YEEO AT BILST. TNE KELH UAST EKEOIOF GAS SWEOT
TNELE; AOC NEL UACHSNIW AFAIO IOQDILEC PIODTEUH IOTR TNE WALTIMDUALS RB
TNEIL ZRDLOEH, FAKE TNEP CILEMTIROS AS TR TNE YEST PETNRC RB WAMVIOF,
AOC GAS SR DLFEOT RO TNE OEMESSITH RB WUAMIOF FRGOS IO TNE ROUH LIFNT
GAH, TNAT PALIA TNRDFNT NELSEUB RYUIFEC, RO NEL LETDLO, TR DOCR AUU TNE
GRLV RB TNE PRLOIOF, AOC WAMV NEL TLDOV ABLESN.

GNEO TNEH WALTEC, UACH MATNELIOE, GITN FLEAT MROCESMEOSIRO, GISNEC TNEP
A FRRC ZRDLOEH, AOC IOKITEC TNEP TR MRPE TR NDOSBRLC AFAIO OEXT HEAL;
AOC PISS CE YRDLFN EXELTEC NELSEUB SR BAL AS TR MRDLTESH AOC NRUC RDT
NEL NAOC TR YRTN.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“TNE EUEKATIRO RB NIS BEEUIOFS.”
]




MNAWTEL XXXKIII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

RO SATDLCAH PRLOIOF EUIJAYETN AOC PL. MRUUIOS PET BRL YLEAVBAST A BEG
PIODTES YEBRLE TNE RTNELS AWWEALEC; AOC NE TRRV TNE RWWRLTDOITH RB
WAHIOF TNE WALTIOF MIKIUITIES GNIMN NE CEEPEC IOCISWEOSAYUH OEMESSALH.

“I VORG ORT, PISS EUIJAYETN,” SAIC NE, “GNETNEL PLS. MRUUIOS NAS HET
EXWLESSEC NEL SEOSE RB HRDL VIOCOESS IO MRPIOF TR DS; YDT I AP KELH
MELTAIO HRD GIUU ORT UEAKE TNE NRDSE GITNRDT LEMEIKIOF NEL TNAOVS BRL
IT. TNE BAKRDL RB HRDL MRPWAOH NAS YEEO PDMN BEUT, I ASSDLE HRD. GE VORG
NRG UITTUE TNELE IS TR TEPWT AOHROE TR RDL NDPYUE AYRCE. RDL WUAIO
PAOOEL RB UIKIOF, RDL SPAUU LRRPS, AOC BEG CRPESTIMS, AOC TNE UITTUE GE
SEE RB TNE GRLUC, PDST PAVE NDOSBRLC EXTLEPEUH CDUU TR A HRDOF UACH UIVE
HRDLSEUB; YDT I NRWE HRD GIUU YEUIEKE DS FLATEBDU BRL TNE MROCESMEOSIRO,
AOC TNAT GE NAKE CROE EKELHTNIOF IO RDL WRGEL TR WLEKEOT HRD SWEOCIOF
HRDL TIPE DOWUEASAOTUH.”

EUIJAYETN GAS EAFEL GITN NEL TNAOVS AOC ASSDLAOMES RB NAWWIOESS. SNE NAC
SWEOT SIX GEEVS GITN FLEAT EOZRHPEOT; AOC TNE WUEASDLE RB YEIOF GITN
MNALURTTE, AOC TNE VIOC ATTEOTIRO SNE NAC LEMEIKEC, PDST PAVE _NEL_ BEEU
TNE RYUIFEC. PL. MRUUIOS GAS FLATIBIEC; AOC GITN A PRLE SPIUIOF
SRUEPOITH LEWUIEC,--

“IT FIKES PE TNE FLEATEST WUEASDLE TR NEAL TNAT HRD NAKE WASSEC HRDL
TIPE ORT CISAFLEEAYUH. GE NAKE MELTAIOUH CROE RDL YEST; AOC PRST
BRLTDOATEUH NAKIOF IT IO RDL WRGEL TR IOTLRCDME HRD TR KELH SDWELIRL
SRMIETH, AOC BLRP RDL MROOEMTIRO GITN LRSIOFS, TNE BLEQDEOT PEAOS RB
KALHIOF TNE NDPYUE NRPE SMEOE, I TNIOV GE PAH BUATTEL RDLSEUKES TNAT
HRDL NDOSBRLC KISIT MAOORT NAKE YEEO EOTILEUH ILVSRPE. RDL SITDATIRO
GITN LEFALC TR UACH MATNELIOE’S BAPIUH IS, IOCEEC, TNE SRLT RB
EXTLARLCIOALH ACKAOTAFE AOC YUESSIOF GNIMN BEG MAO YRAST. HRD SEE RO
GNAT A BRRTIOF GE ALE. HRD SEE NRG MROTIODAUUH GE ALE EOFAFEC TNELE. IO
TLDTN, I PDST AMVORGUECFE, TNAT, GITN AUU TNE CISACKAOTAFES RB TNIS
NDPYUE WALSROAFE, I SNRDUC ORT TNIOV AOHROE AYICIOF IO IT AO RYZEMT RB
MRPWASSIRO, GNIUE TNEH ALE SNALELS RB RDL IOTIPAMH AT LRSIOFS.”

GRLCS GELE IOSDBBIMIEOT BRL TNE EUEKATIRO RB NIS BEEUIOFS; AOC NE GAS
RYUIFEC TR GAUV AYRDT TNE LRRP, GNIUE EUIJAYETN TLIEC TR DOITE MIKIUITH
AOC TLDTN IO A BEG SNRLT SEOTEOMES.

“HRD PAH, IO BAMT, MALLH A KELH BAKRDLAYUE LEWRLT RB DS IOTR
NELTBRLCSNILE, PH CEAL MRDSIO. I BUATTEL PHSEUB, AT UEAST, TNAT HRD GIUU
YE AYUE TR CR SR. UACH MATNELIOE’S FLEAT ATTEOTIROS TR PLS. MRUUIOS HRD
NAKE YEEO A CAIUH GITOESS RB; AOC AUTRFETNEL I TLDST IT CRES ORT AWWEAL
TNAT HRDL BLIEOC NAS CLAGO AO DOBRLTDOATE--YDT RO TNIS WRIOT IT GIUU YE
AS GEUU TR YE SIUEOT. ROUH UET PE ASSDLE HRD, PH CEAL PISS EUIJAYETN,
TNAT I MAO BLRP PH NEALT PRST MRLCIAUUH GISN HRD EQDAU BEUIMITH IO
PALLIAFE. PH CEAL MNALURTTE AOC I NAKE YDT ROE PIOC AOC ROE GAH RB
TNIOVIOF. TNELE IS IO EKELHTNIOF A PRST LEPALVAYUE LESEPYUAOME RB
MNALAMTEL AOC ICEAS YETGEEO DS. GE SEEP TR NAKE YEEO CESIFOEC BRL EAMN
RTNEL.”

EUIJAYETN MRDUC SABEUH SAH TNAT IT GAS A FLEAT NAWWIOESS GNELE TNAT GAS
TNE MASE, AOC GITN EQDAU SIOMELITH MRDUC ACC, TNAT SNE BILPUH YEUIEKEC
AOC LEZRIMEC IO NIS CRPESTIM MRPBRLTS. SNE GAS ORT SRLLH, NRGEKEL, TR
NAKE TNE LEMITAU RB TNEP IOTELLDWTEC YH TNE EOTLAOME RB TNE UACH BLRP
GNRP TNEH SWLAOF. WRRL MNALURTTE! IT GAS PEUAOMNRUH TR UEAKE NEL TR SDMN
SRMIETH! YDT SNE NAC MNRSEO IT GITN NEL EHES RWEO; AOC TNRDFN EKICEOTUH
LEFLETTIOF TNAT NEL KISITRLS GELE TR FR, SNE CIC ORT SEEP TR ASV BRL
MRPWASSIRO. NEL NRPE AOC NEL NRDSEVEEWIOF, NEL WALISN AOC NEL WRDUTLH,
AOC AUU TNEIL CEWEOCEOT MROMELOS, NAC ORT HET URST TNEIL MNALPS.

AT UEOFTN TNE MNAISE ALLIKEC, TNE TLDOVS GELE BASTEOEC RO, TNE WALMEUS
WUAMEC GITNIO, AOC IT GAS WLRORDOMEC TR YE LEACH. ABTEL AO ABBEMTIROATE
WALTIOF YETGEEO TNE BLIEOCS, EUIJAYETN GAS ATTEOCEC TR TNE MALLIAFE YH
PL. MRUUIOS; AOC AS TNEH GAUVEC CRGO TNE FALCEO, NE GAS MRPPISSIROIOF
NEL GITN NIS YEST LESWEMTS TR AUU NEL BAPIUH, ORT BRLFETTIOF NIS TNAOVS
BRL TNE VIOCOESS NE NAC LEMEIKEC AT UROFYRDLO IO TNE GIOTEL, AOC NIS
MRPWUIPEOTS TR PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL, TNRDFN DOVORGO. NE TNEO NAOCEC
NEL IO, PALIA BRUURGEC, AOC TNE CRRL GAS RO TNE WRIOT RB YEIOF MURSEC,
GNEO NE SDCCEOUH LEPIOCEC TNEP, GITN SRPE MROSTELOATIRO, TNAT TNEH NAC
NITNELTR BRLFRTTEO TR UEAKE AOH PESSAFE BRL TNE UACIES RB LRSIOFS.

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“TNEH NAC BRLFRTTEO TR UEAKE AOH PESSAFE”
]

“YDT,” NE ACCEC, “HRD GIUU RB MRDLSE GISN TR NAKE HRDL NDPYUE LESWEMTS
CEUIKELEC TR TNEP, GITN HRDL FLATEBDU TNAOVS BRL TNEIL VIOCOESS TR HRD
GNIUE HRD NAKE YEEO NELE.”

EUIJAYETN PACE OR RYZEMTIRO: TNE CRRL GAS TNEO AUURGEC TR YE SNDT, AOC
TNE MALLIAFE CLRKE RBB.

“FRRC FLAMIRDS!” MLIEC PALIA, ABTEL A BEG PIODTES’ SIUEOME, “IT SEEPS
YDT A CAH RL TGR SIOME GE BILST MAPE! AOC HET NRG PAOH TNIOFS NAKE
NAWWEOEC!”

“A FLEAT PAOH IOCEEC,” SAIC NEL MRPWAOIRO, GITN A SIFN.

“GE NAKE CIOEC OIOE TIPES AT LRSIOFS, YESICES CLIOVIOF TEA TNELE TGIME!
NRG PDMN I SNAUU NAKE TR TEUU!”

EUIJAYETN WLIKATEUH ACCEC, “AOC NRG PDMN I SNAUU NAKE TR MROMEAU!”

TNEIL ZRDLOEH GAS WELBRLPEC GITNRDT PDMN MROKELSATIRO, RL AOH AUALP; AOC
GITNIO BRDL NRDLS RB TNEIL UEAKIOF NDOSBRLC TNEH LEAMNEC PL. FALCIOEL’S
NRDSE, GNELE TNEH GELE TR LEPAIO A BEG CAHS.

ZAOE URRVEC GEUU, AOC EUIJAYETN NAC UITTUE RWWRLTDOITH RB STDCHIOF NEL
SWILITS, APICST TNE KALIRDS EOFAFEPEOTS GNIMN TNE VIOCOESS RB NEL ADOT
NAC LESELKEC BRL TNEP. YDT ZAOE GAS TR FR NRPE GITN NEL, AOC AT
UROFYRDLO TNELE GRDUC YE UEISDLE EORDFN BRL RYSELKATIRO.

IT GAS ORT GITNRDT AO EBBRLT, PEAOGNIUE, TNAT SNE MRDUC GAIT EKEO BRL
UROFYRDLO, YEBRLE SNE TRUC NEL SISTEL RB PL. CALMH’S WLRWRSAUS. TR VORG
TNAT SNE NAC TNE WRGEL RB LEKEAUIOF GNAT GRDUC SR EXMEECIOFUH ASTROISN
ZAOE, AOC PDST, AT TNE SAPE TIPE, SR NIFNUH FLATIBH GNATEKEL RB NEL RGO
KAOITH SNE NAC ORT HET YEEO AYUE TR LEASRO AGAH, GAS SDMN A TEPWTATIRO
TR RWEOOESS AS ORTNIOF MRDUC NAKE MROQDELEC, YDT TNE STATE RB IOCEMISIRO
IO GNIMN SNE LEPAIOEC AS TR TNE EXTEOT RB GNAT SNE SNRDUC MRPPDOIMATE,
AOC NEL BEAL, IB SNE ROME EOTELEC RO TNE SDYZEMT, RB YEIOF NDLLIEC IOTR
LEWEATIOF SRPETNIOF RB YIOFUEH, GNIMN PIFNT ROUH FLIEKE NEL SISTEL
BDLTNEL.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “NRG OIMEUH GE ALE MLAPPEC IO”
]




MNAWTEL XXXIX.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

IT GAS TNE SEMROC GEEV IO PAH, IO GNIMN TNE TNLEE HRDOF UACIES SET RDT
TRFETNEL BLRP FLAMEMNDLMN STLEET BRL TNE TRGO RB ----, IO NELTBRLCSNILE;
AOC, AS TNEH CLEG OEAL TNE AWWRIOTEC IOO GNELE PL. YEOOET’S MALLIAFE GAS
TR PEET TNEP, TNEH QDIMVUH WELMEIKEC, IO TRVEO RB TNE MRAMNPAO’S
WDOMTDAUITH, YRTN VITTH AOC UHCIA URRVIOF RDT RB A CIOIOF-LRRP DWSTAILS.
TNESE TGR FILUS NAC YEEO AYRKE AO NRDL IO TNE WUAME, NAWWIUH EPWURHEC
IO KISITIOF AO RWWRSITE PIUUIOEL, GATMNIOF TNE SEOTIOEU RO FDALC, AOC
CLESSIOF A SAUAC AOC MDMDPYEL.

ABTEL GEUMRPIOF TNEIL SISTELS, TNEH TLIDPWNAOTUH CISWUAHEC A TAYUE SET
RDT GITN SDMN MRUC PEAT AS AO IOO UALCEL DSDAUUH ABBRLCS, EXMUAIPIOF,
“IS ORT TNIS OIME? IS ORT TNIS AO AFLEEAYUE SDLWLISE?”

“AOC GE PEAO TR TLEAT HRD AUU,” ACCEC UHCIA; “YDT HRD PDST UEOC DS TNE
PROEH, BRL GE NAKE ZDST SWEOT RDLS AT TNE SNRW RDT TNELE.” TNEO SNRGIOF
NEL WDLMNASES,--“URRV NELE, I NAKE YRDFNT TNIS YROOET. I CR ORT TNIOV IT
IS KELH WLETTH; YDT I TNRDFNT I PIFNT AS GEUU YDH IT AS ORT. I SNAUU
WDUU IT TR WIEMES AS SRRO AS I FET NRPE, AOC SEE IB I MAO PAVE IT DW AOH
YETTEL.”

AOC GNEO NEL SISTELS AYDSEC IT AS DFUH, SNE ACCEC, GITN WELBEMT
DOMROMELO, “RN, YDT TNELE GELE TGR RL TNLEE PDMN DFUIEL IO TNE SNRW; AOC
GNEO I NAKE YRDFNT SRPE WLETTIEL-MRURDLEC SATIO TR TLIP IT GITN BLESN, I
TNIOV IT GIUU YE KELH TRUELAYUE. YESICES, IT GIUU ORT PDMN SIFOIBH GNAT
ROE GEALS TNIS SDPPEL, ABTEL TNE ----SNILE NAKE UEBT PELHTRO, AOC TNEH
ALE FRIOF IO A BRLTOIFNT.”

“ALE TNEH, IOCEEC?” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, GITN TNE FLEATEST SATISBAMTIRO.

“TNEH ALE FRIOF TR YE EOMAPWEC OEAL YLIFNTRO; AOC I CR SR GAOT WAWA TR
TAVE DS AUU TNELE BRL TNE SDPPEL! IT GRDUC YE SDMN A CEUIMIRDS SMNEPE,
AOC I CALE SAH GRDUC NALCUH MRST AOHTNIOF AT AUU. PAPPA GRDUC UIVE TR
FR, TRR, RB AUU TNIOFS! ROUH TNIOV GNAT A PISELAYUE SDPPEL EUSE GE SNAUU
NAKE!”

“HES,” TNRDFNT EUIJAYETN; “_TNAT_ GRDUC YE A CEUIFNTBDU SMNEPE, IOCEEC,
AOC MRPWUETEUH CR BRL DS AT ROME. FRRC NEAKEO! YLIFNTRO AOC A GNRUE
MAPWBDU RB SRUCIELS, TR DS, GNR NAKE YEEO RKELSET AULEACH YH ROE WRRL
LEFIPEOT RB PIUITIA, AOC TNE PROTNUH YAUUS RB PELHTRO!”

“ORG I NAKE FRT SRPE OEGS BRL HRD,” SAIC UHCIA, AS TNEH SAT CRGO TR
TAYUE. “GNAT CR HRD TNIOV? IT IS EXMEUUEOT OEGS, MAWITAU OEGS, AOC AYRDT
A MELTAIO WELSRO TNAT GE AUU UIVE.”

ZAOE AOC EUIJAYETN URRVEC AT EAMN RTNEL, AOC TNE GAITEL GAS TRUC TNAT NE
OEEC ORT STAH. UHCIA UADFNEC, AOC SAIC,--

“AH, TNAT IS ZDST UIVE HRDL BRLPAUITH AOC CISMLETIRO. HRD TNRDFNT TNE
GAITEL PDST ORT NEAL, AS IB NE MALEC! I CALE SAH NE RBTEO NEALS GRLSE
TNIOFS SAIC TNAO I AP FRIOF TR SAH. YDT NE IS AO DFUH BEUURG! I AP FUAC
NE IS FROE. I OEKEL SAG SDMN A UROF MNIO IO PH UIBE. GEUU, YDT ORG BRL
PH OEGS: IT IS AYRDT CEAL GIMVNAP; TRR FRRC BRL TNE GAITEL, IS ORT IT?
TNELE IS OR CAOFEL RB GIMVNAP’S PALLHIOF PALH VIOF--TNELE’S BRL HRD! SNE
IS FROE CRGO TR NEL DOMUE AT UIKELWRRU; FROE TR STAH. GIMVNAP IS SABE.”

“AOC PALH VIOF IS SABE!” ACCEC EUIJAYETN; “SABE BLRP A MROOEMTIRO
IPWLDCEOT AS TR BRLTDOE.”

“SNE IS A FLEAT BRRU BRL FRIOF AGAH, IB SNE UIVEC NIP.”

“YDT I NRWE TNELE IS OR STLROF ATTAMNPEOT RO EITNEL SICE,” SAIC ZAOE.

“I AP SDLE TNELE IS ORT RO _NIS_. I GIUU AOSGEL BRL IT, NE OEKEL MALEC
TNLEE STLAGS AYRDT NEL. GNR _MRDUC_ AYRDT SDMN A OASTH UITTUE BLEMVUEC
TNIOF?”

EUIJAYETN GAS SNRMVEC TR TNIOV TNAT, NRGEKEL IOMAWAYUE RB SDMN
MRALSEOESS RB _EXWLESSIRO_ NELSEUB, TNE MRALSEOESS RB TNE _SEOTIPEOT_
GAS UITTUE RTNEL TNAO NEL RGO YLEAST NAC BRLPELUH NALYRDLEC AOC BAOMIEC
UIYELAU!

AS SRRO AS AUU NAC ATE, AOC TNE EUCEL ROES WAIC, TNE MALLIAFE GAS
RLCELEC; AOC, ABTEL SRPE MROTLIKAOME, TNE GNRUE WALTH, GITN AUU TNEIL
YRXES, GRLVYAFS, AOC WALMEUS, AOC TNE DOGEUMRPE ACCITIRO RB VITTH’S AOC
UHCIA’S WDLMNASES, GELE SEATEC IO IT.

“NRG OIMEUH GE ALE MLAPPEC IO!” MLIEC UHCIA. “I AP FUAC I YLRDFNT PH
YROOET, IB IT IS ROUH BRL TNE BDO RB NAKIOF AORTNEL YAOC-YRX! GEUU, ORG
UET DS YE QDITE MRPBRLTAYUE AOC SODF, AOC TAUV AOC UADFN AUU TNE GAH
NRPE. AOC IO TNE BILST WUAME, UET DS NEAL GNAT NAS NAWWEOEC TR HRD AUU
SIOME HRD GEOT AGAH. NAKE HRD SEEO AOH WUEASAOT PEO? NAKE HRD NAC AOH
BUILTIOF? I GAS IO FLEAT NRWES TNAT ROE RB HRD GRDUC NAKE FRT A NDSYAOC
YEBRLE HRD MAPE YAMV. ZAOE GIUU YE QDITE AO RUC PAIC SRRO, I CEMUALE.
SNE IS AUPRST TNLEE-AOC-TGEOTH! URLC! NRG ASNAPEC I SNRDUC YE RB ORT
YEIOF PALLIEC YEBRLE TNLEE-AOC-TGEOTH! PH ADOT WNIUIWS GAOTS HRD SR TR
FET NDSYAOCS HRD MAO’T TNIOV. SNE SAHS UIJJH NAC YETTEL NAKE TAVEO PL.
MRUUIOS; YDT _I_ CR ORT TNIOV TNELE GRDUC NAKE YEEO AOH BDO IO IT. URLC!
NRG I SNRDUC UIVE TR YE PALLIEC YEBRLE AOH RB HRD! AOC TNEO I GRDUC
_MNAWELRO_ HRD AYRDT TR AUU TNE YAUUS. CEAL PE! GE NAC SDMN A FRRC WIEME
RB BDO TNE RTNEL CAH AT MRUROEU BRLSTEL’S! VITTH AOC PE GELE TR SWEOC
TNE CAH TNELE, AOC PLS. BRLSTEL WLRPISEC TR NAKE A UITTUE CAOME IO TNE
EKEOIOF; (YH-TNE-YHE, PLS. BRLSTEL AOC PE ALE _SDMN_ BLIEOCS!) AOC SR
SNE ASVEC TNE TGR NALLIOFTROS TR MRPE: YDT NALLIET GAS IUU, AOC SR WEO
GAS BRLMEC TR MRPE YH NELSEUB; AOC TNEO, GNAT CR HRD TNIOV GE CIC? GE
CLESSEC DW MNAPYELUAHOE IO GRPAO’S MURTNES, RO WDLWRSE TR WASS BRL A
UACH,--ROUH TNIOV GNAT BDO! ORT A SRDU VOEG RB IT, YDT MRUROEU AOC PLS.
BRLSTEL, AOC VITTH AOC PE, EXMEWT PH ADOT, BRL GE GELE BRLMEC TR YRLLRG
ROE RB NEL FRGOS; AOC HRD MAOORT IPAFIOE NRG GEUU NE URRVEC! GNEO CEOOH,
AOC GIMVNAP, AOC WLATT, AOC TGR RL TNLEE PRLE RB TNE PEO MAPE IO, TNEH
CIC ORT VORG NIP IO TNE UEAST. URLC! NRG I UADFNEC! AOC SR CIC PLS.
BRLSTEL. I TNRDFNT I SNRDUC NAKE CIEC. AOC _TNAT_ PACE TNE PEO SDSWEMT
SRPETNIOF, AOC TNEO TNEH SRRO BRDOC RDT GNAT GAS TNE PATTEL.”

GITN SDMN VIOC RB NISTRLIES RB TNEIL WALTIES AOC FRRC ZRVES CIC UHCIA,
ASSISTEC YH VITTH’S NIOTS AOC ACCITIROS, EOCEAKRDL TR APDSE NEL
MRPWAOIROS AUU TNE GAH TR UROFYRDLO. EUIJAYETN UISTEOEC AS UITTUE AS SNE
MRDUC, YDT TNELE GAS OR ESMAWIOF TNE BLEQDEOT PEOTIRO RB GIMVNAP’S OAPE.

TNEIL LEMEWTIRO AT NRPE GAS PRST VIOC. PLS. YEOOET LEZRIMEC TR SEE ZAOE
IO DOCIPIOISNEC YEADTH; AOC PRLE TNAO ROME CDLIOF CIOOEL CIC PL. YEOOET
SAH KRUDOTALIUH TR EUIJAYETN,----

“I AP FUAC HRD ALE MRPE YAMV, UIJJH.”

TNEIL WALTH IO TNE CIOIOF-LRRP GAS UALFE, BRL AUPRST AUU TNE UDMASES
MAPE TR PEET PALIA AOC NEAL TNE OEGS; AOC KALIRDS GELE TNE SDYZEMTS
GNIMN RMMDWIEC TNEP: UACH UDMAS GAS IOQDILIOF RB PALIA, AMLRSS TNE
TAYUE, ABTEL TNE GEUBALE AOC WRDUTLH RB NEL EUCEST CADFNTEL; PLS. YEOOET
GAS CRDYUH EOFAFEC, RO ROE NAOC MRUUEMTIOF AO AMMRDOT RB TNE WLESEOT
BASNIROS BLRP ZAOE, GNR SAT SRPE GAH YEURG NEL, AOC RO TNE RTNEL,
LETAIUIOF TNEP AUU TR TNE HRDOFEL PISS UDMASES; AOC UHCIA, IO A KRIME
LATNEL URDCEL TNAO AOH RTNEL WELSRO’S, GAS EODPELATIOF TNE KALIRDS
WUEASDLES RB TNE PRLOIOF TR AOHYRCH GNR GRDUC NEAL NEL.

“RN, PALH,” SAIC SNE, “I GISN HRD NAC FROE GITN DS, BRL GE NAC SDMN BDO!
AS GE GEOT AUROF VITTH AOC PE CLEG DW AUU TNE YUIOCS, AOC WLETEOCEC
TNELE GAS ORYRCH IO TNE MRAMN; AOC I SNRDUC NAKE FROE SR AUU TNE GAH, IB
VITTH NAC ORT YEEO SIMV; AOC GNEO GE FRT TR TNE FERLFE, I CR TNIOV GE
YENAKEC KELH NAOCSRPEUH, BRL GE TLEATEC TNE RTNEL TNLEE GITN TNE OIMEST
MRUC UDOMNERO IO TNE GRLUC, AOC IB HRD GRDUC NAKE FROE, GE GRDUC NAKE
TLEATEC HRD TRR. AOC TNEO GNEO GE MAPE AGAH IT GAS SDMN BDO! I TNRDFNT
GE OEKEL SNRDUC NAKE FRT IOTR TNE MRAMN. I GAS LEACH TR CIE RB UADFNTEL.
AOC TNEO GE GELE SR PELLH AUU TNE GAH NRPE! GE TAUVEC AOC UADFNEC SR
URDC, TNAT AOHYRCH PIFNT NAKE NEALC DS TEO PIUES RBB!”

TR TNIS, PALH KELH FLAKEUH LEWUIEC, “BAL YE IT BLRP PE, PH CEAL SISTEL,
TR CEWLEMIATE SDMN WUEASDLES. TNEH GRDUC CRDYTUESS YE MROFEOIAU GITN TNE
FEOELAUITH RB BEPAUE PIOCS. YDT I MROBESS TNEH GRDUC NAKE OR MNALPS BRL
_PE_. I SNRDUC IOBIOITEUH WLEBEL A YRRV.”

YDT RB TNIS AOSGEL UHCIA NEALC ORT A GRLC. SNE SEUCRP UISTEOEC TR
AOHYRCH BRL PRLE TNAO NAUB A PIODTE, AOC OEKEL ATTEOCEC TR PALH AT AUU.

IO TNE ABTELORRO UHCIA GAS DLFEOT GITN TNE LEST RB TNE FILUS TR GAUV TR
PELHTRO, AOC SEE NRG EKELHYRCH GEOT RO; YDT EUIJAYETN STEACIUH RWWRSEC
TNE SMNEPE. IT SNRDUC ORT YE SAIC, TNAT TNE PISS YEOOETS MRDUC ORT YE AT
NRPE NAUB A CAH YEBRLE TNEH GELE IO WDLSDIT RB TNE RBBIMELS. TNELE GAS
AORTNEL LEASRO, TRR, BRL NEL RWWRSITIRO. SNE CLEACEC SEEIOF GIMVNAP
AFAIO, AOC GAS LESRUKEC TR AKRIC IT AS UROF AS WRSSIYUE. TNE MRPBRLT TR
_NEL_, RB TNE LEFIPEOT’S AWWLRAMNIOF LEPRKAU, GAS IOCEEC YEHROC
EXWLESSIRO. IO A BRLTOIFNT TNEH GELE TR FR, AOC ROME FROE, SNE NRWEC
TNELE MRDUC YE ORTNIOF PRLE TR WUAFDE NEL RO NIS AMMRDOT.

SNE NAC ORT YEEO PAOH NRDLS AT NRPE, YEBRLE SNE BRDOC TNAT TNE YLIFNTRO
SMNEPE, RB GNIMN UHCIA NAC FIKEO TNEP A NIOT AT TNE IOO, GAS DOCEL
BLEQDEOT CISMDSSIRO YETGEEO NEL WALEOTS. EUIJAYETN SAG CILEMTUH TNAT NEL
BATNEL NAC ORT TNE SPAUUEST IOTEOTIRO RB HIEUCIOF; YDT NIS AOSGELS GELE
AT TNE SAPE TIPE SR KAFDE AOC EQDIKRMAU, TNAT NEL PRTNEL, TNRDFN RBTEO
CISNEALTEOEC, NAC OEKEL HET CESWAILEC RB SDMMEECIOF AT UAST.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XU.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN’S IPWATIEOME TR AMQDAIOT ZAOE GITN GNAT NAC NAWWEOEC MRDUC OR
UROFEL YE RKELMRPE; AOC AT UEOFTN LESRUKIOF TR SDWWLESS EKELH WALTIMDUAL
IO GNIMN NEL SISTEL GAS MROMELOEC, AOC WLEWALIOF NEL TR YE SDLWLISEC,
SNE LEUATEC TR NEL TNE OEXT PRLOIOF TNE MNIEB RB TNE SMEOE YETGEEO PL.
CALMH AOC NELSEUB.

PISS YEOOET’S ASTROISNPEOT GAS SRRO UESSEOEC YH TNE STLROF SISTELUH
WALTIAUITH GNIMN PACE AOH ACPILATIRO RB EUIJAYETN AWWEAL WELBEMTUH
OATDLAU; AOC AUU SDLWLISE GAS SNRLTUH URST IO RTNEL BEEUIOFS. SNE GAS
SRLLH TNAT PL. CALMH SNRDUC NAKE CEUIKELEC NIS SEOTIPEOTS IO A PAOOEL SR
UITTUE SDITEC TR LEMRPPEOC TNEP; YDT STIUU PRLE GAS SNE FLIEKEC BRL TNE
DONAWWIOESS GNIMN NEL SISTEL’S LEBDSAU PDST NAKE FIKEO NIP.

“NIS YEIOF SR SDLE RB SDMMEECIOF GAS GLROF,” SAIC SNE, “AOC MELTAIOUH
RDFNT ORT TR NAKE AWWEALEC; YDT MROSICEL NRG PDMN IT PDST IOMLEASE NIS
CISAWWRIOTPEOT.”

“IOCEEC,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN, “I AP NEALTIUH SRLLH BRL NIP; YDT NE NAS
RTNEL BEEUIOFS GNIMN GIUU WLRYAYUH SRRO CLIKE AGAH NIS LEFALC BRL PE.
HRD CR ORT YUAPE PE, NRGEKEL, BRL LEBDSIOF NIP?”

“YUAPE HRD! RN, OR.”

“YDT HRD YUAPE PE BRL NAKIOF SWRVEO SR GALPUH RB GIMVNAP?”

“OR--I CR ORT VORG TNAT HRD GELE GLROF IO SAHIOF GNAT HRD CIC.”

“YDT HRD _GIUU_ VORG IT, GNEO I NAKE TRUC HRD GNAT NAWWEOEC TNE KELH
OEXT CAH.”

SNE TNEO SWRVE RB TNE UETTEL, LEWEATIOF TNE GNRUE RB ITS MROTEOTS AS BAL
AS TNEH MROMELOEC FERLFE GIMVNAP. GNAT A STLRVE GAS TNIS BRL WRRL ZAOE,
GNR GRDUC GIUUIOFUH NAKE FROE TNLRDFN TNE GRLUC GITNRDT YEUIEKIOF TNAT
SR PDMN GIMVECOESS EXISTEC IO TNE GNRUE LAME RB PAOVIOC AS GAS NELE
MRUUEMTEC IO ROE IOCIKICDAU! ORL GAS CALMH’S KIOCIMATIRO, TNRDFN
FLATEBDU TR NEL BEEUIOFS, MAWAYUE RB MROSRUIOF NEL BRL SDMN CISMRKELH.
PRST EALOESTUH CIC SNE UAYRDL TR WLRKE TNE WLRYAYIUITH RB ELLRL, AOC
SEEV TR MUEAL ROE, GITNRDT IOKRUKIOF TNE RTNEL.

“TNIS GIUU ORT CR,” SAIC EUIJAYETN; “HRD OEKEL GIUU YE AYUE TR PAVE YRTN
RB TNEP FRRC BRL AOHTNIOF. TAVE HRDL MNRIME, YDT HRD PDST YE SATISBIEC
GITN ROUH ROE. TNELE IS YDT SDMN A QDAOTITH RB PELIT YETGEEO TNEP; ZDST
EORDFN TR PAVE ROE FRRC SRLT RB PAO; AOC RB UATE IT NAS YEEO SNIBTIOF
AYRDT WLETTH PDMN. BRL PH WALT, I AP IOMUIOEC TR YEUIEKE IT AUU PL.
CALMH’S, YDT HRD SNAUU CR AS HRD MNRRSE.”

IT GAS SRPE TIPE, NRGEKEL, YEBRLE A SPIUE MRDUC YE EXTRLTEC BLRP ZAOE.

“I CR ORT VORG GNEO I NAKE YEEO PRLE SNRMVEC,” SAIC SNE. “GIMVNAP SR
KELH YAC! IT IS AUPRST WAST YEUIEB. AOC WRRL PL. CALMH! CEAL UIJJH,
ROUH MROSICEL GNAT NE PDST NAKE SDBBELEC. SDMN A CISAWWRIOTPEOT! AOC
GITN TNE VORGUECFE RB HRDL IUU RWIOIRO TRR! AOC NAKIOF TR LEUATE SDMN A
TNIOF RB NIS SISTEL! IT IS LEAUUH TRR CISTLESSIOF, I AP SDLE HRD PDST
BEEU IT SR.”

“RN OR, PH LEFLET AOC MRPWASSIRO ALE AUU CROE AGAH YH SEEIOF HRD SR BDUU
RB YRTN. I VORG HRD GIUU CR NIP SDMN APWUE ZDSTIME, TNAT I AP FLRGIOF
EKELH PRPEOT PRLE DOMROMELOEC AOC IOCIBBELEOT. HRDL WLRBDSIRO PAVES PE
SAKIOF; AOC IB HRD UAPEOT RKEL NIP PDMN UROFEL, PH NEALT GIUU YE AS
UIFNT AS A BEATNEL.”

“WRRL GIMVNAP! TNELE IS SDMN AO EXWLESSIRO RB FRRCOESS IO NIS
MRDOTEOAOME! SDMN AO RWEOOESS AOC FEOTUEOESS IO NIS PAOOEL.”

“TNELE MELTAIOUH GAS SRPE FLEAT PISPAOAFEPEOT IO TNE ECDMATIRO RB TNRSE
TGR HRDOF PEO. ROE NAS FRT AUU TNE FRRCOESS, AOC TNE RTNEL AUU TNE
AWWEALAOME RB IT.”

“I OEKEL TNRDFNT PL. CALMH SR CEBIMIEOT IO TNE _AWWEALAOME_ RB IT AS HRD
DSEC TR CR.”

“AOC HET I PEAOT TR YE DOMRPPROUH MUEKEL IO TAVIOF SR CEMICEC A CISUIVE
TR NIP, GITNRDT AOH LEASRO. IT IS SDMN A SWDL TR ROE’S FEOIDS, SDMN AO
RWEOIOF BRL GIT, TR NAKE A CISUIVE RB TNAT VIOC. ROE PAH YE MROTIODAUUH
AYDSIKE GITNRDT SAHIOF AOHTNIOF ZDST; YDT ROE MAOORT YE AUGAHS UADFNIOF
AT A PAO GITNRDT ORG AOC TNEO STDPYUIOF RO SRPETNIOF GITTH.”

“UIJJH, GNEO HRD BILST LEAC TNAT UETTEL, I AP SDLE HRD MRDUC ORT TLEAT
TNE PATTEL AS HRD CR ORG.”

“IOCEEC, I MRDUC ORT. I GAS DOMRPBRLTAYUE EORDFN, I GAS KELH
DOMRPBRLTAYUE--I PAH SAH DONAWWH. AOC GITN OR ROE TR SWEAV TR RB GNAT I
BEUT, OR ZAOE TR MRPBRLT PE, AOC SAH TNAT I NAC ORT YEEO SR KELH GEAV,
AOC KAIO, AOC OROSEOSIMAU, AS I VOEG I NAC! RN, NRG I GAOTEC HRD!”

“NRG DOBRLTDOATE TNAT HRD SNRDUC NAKE DSEC SDMN KELH STLROF EXWLESSIROS
IO SWEAVIOF RB GIMVNAP TR PL. CALMH, BRL ORG TNEH _CR_ AWWEAL GNRUUH
DOCESELKEC.”

“MELTAIOUH. YDT TNE PISBRLTDOE RB SWEAVIOF GITN YITTELOESS IS A PRST
OATDLAU MROSEQDEOME RB TNE WLEZDCIMES I NAC YEEO EOMRDLAFIOF. TNELE IS
ROE WRIOT RO GNIMN I GAOT HRDL ACKIME. I GAOT TR YE TRUC GNETNEL I
RDFNT, RL RDFNT ORT, TR PAVE RDL AMQDAIOTAOME IO FEOELAU DOCELSTAOC
GIMVNAP’S MNALAMTEL.”

PISS YEOOET WADSEC A UITTUE, AOC TNEO LEWUIEC, “SDLEUH TNELE MAO YE OR
RMMASIRO BRL EXWRSIOF NIP SR CLEACBDUUH. GNAT IS HRDL RGO RWIOIRO?”

“TNAT IT RDFNT ORT TR YE ATTEPWTEC. PL. CALMH NAS ORT ADTNRLIJEC PE TR
PAVE NIS MRPPDOIMATIRO WDYUIM. RO TNE MROTLALH, EKELH WALTIMDUAL
LEUATIKE TR NIS SISTEL GAS PEAOT TR YE VEWT AS PDMN AS WRSSIYUE TR
PHSEUB; AOC IB I EOCEAKRDL TR DOCEMEIKE WERWUE AS TR TNE LEST RB NIS
MROCDMT, GNR GIUU YEUIEKE PE? TNE FEOELAU WLEZDCIME AFAIOST PL. CALMH IS
SR KIRUEOT, TNAT IT GRDUC YE TNE CEATN RB NAUB TNE FRRC WERWUE IO
PELHTRO, TR ATTEPWT TR WUAME NIP IO AO APIAYUE UIFNT. I AP ORT EQDAU TR
IT. GIMVNAP GIUU SRRO YE FROE; AOC, TNELEBRLE, IT GIUU ORT SIFOIBH TR
AOHYRCH NELE GNAT NE LEAUUH IS. SRPE TIPE NEOME IT GIUU YE AUU BRDOC
RDT, AOC TNEO GE PAH UADFN AT TNEIL STDWICITH IO ORT VORGIOF IT YEBRLE.
AT WLESEOT I GIUU SAH ORTNIOF AYRDT IT.”

“HRD ALE QDITE LIFNT. TR NAKE NIS ELLRLS PACE WDYUIM PIFNT LDIO NIP BRL
EKEL. NE IS ORG, WELNAWS, SRLLH BRL GNAT NE NAS CROE, AOC AOXIRDS TR
LE-ESTAYUISN A MNALAMTEL. GE PDST ORT PAVE NIP CESWELATE.”

TNE TDPDUT RB EUIJAYETN’S PIOC GAS AUUAHEC YH TNIS MROKELSATIRO. SNE
NAC FRT LIC RB TGR RB TNE SEMLETS GNIMN NAC GEIFNEC RO NEL BRL A
BRLTOIFNT, AOC GAS MELTAIO RB A GIUUIOF UISTEOEL IO ZAOE, GNEOEKEL SNE
PIFNT GISN TR TAUV AFAIO RB EITNEL. YDT TNELE GAS STIUU SRPETNIOF
UDLVIOF YENIOC, RB GNIMN WLDCEOME BRLYACE TNE CISMURSDLE. SNE CALEC ORT
LEUATE TNE RTNEL NAUB RB PL. CALMH’S UETTEL, ORL EXWUAIO TR NEL SISTEL
NRG SIOMELEUH SNE NAC YEEO KAUDEC YH NIS BLIEOC. NELE GAS VORGUECFE IO
GNIMN OR ROE MRDUC WALTAVE; AOC SNE GAS SEOSIYUE TNAT ORTNIOF UESS TNAO
A WELBEMT DOCELSTAOCIOF YETGEEO TNE WALTIES MRDUC ZDSTIBH NEL IO
TNLRGIOF RBB TNIS UAST EOMDPYLAOME RB PHSTELH. “AOC TNEO,” SAIC SNE, “IB
TNAT KELH IPWLRYAYUE EKEOT SNRDUC EKEL TAVE WUAME, I SNAUU PELEUH YE
AYUE TR TEUU GNAT YIOFUEH PAH TEUU IO A PDMN PRLE AFLEEAYUE PAOOEL
NIPSEUB. TNE UIYELTH RB MRPPDOIMATIRO MAOORT YE PIOE TIUU IT NAS URST
AUU ITS KAUDE!”

SNE GAS ORG, RO YEIOF SETTUEC AT NRPE, AT UEISDLE TR RYSELKE TNE LEAU
STATE RB NEL SISTEL’S SWILITS. ZAOE GAS ORT NAWWH. SNE STIUU MNELISNEC A
KELH TEOCEL ABBEMTIRO BRL YIOFUEH. NAKIOF OEKEL EKEO BAOMIEC NELSEUB IO
URKE YEBRLE, NEL LEFALC NAC AUU TNE GALPTN RB BILST ATTAMNPEOT, AOC BLRP
NEL AFE AOC CISWRSITIRO, FLEATEL STEACIOESS TNAO BILST ATTAMNPEOTS RBTEO
YRAST; AOC SR BELKEOTUH CIC SNE KAUDE NIS LEPEPYLAOME, AOC WLEBEL NIP TR
EKELH RTNEL PAO, TNAT AUU NEL FRRC SEOSE, AOC AUU NEL ATTEOTIRO TR TNE
BEEUIOFS RB NEL BLIEOCS, GELE LEQDISITE TR MNEMV TNE IOCDUFEOME RB TNRSE
LEFLETS GNIMN PDST NAKE YEEO IOZDLIRDS TR NEL RGO NEAUTN AOC TNEIL
TLAOQDIUUITH.

“GEUU, UIJJH,” SAIC PLS. YEOOET, ROE CAH, “GNAT IS HRDL RWIOIRO _ORG_ RB
TNIS SAC YDSIOESS RB ZAOE’S? BRL PH WALT, I AP CETELPIOEC OEKEL TR SWEAV
RB IT AFAIO TR AOHYRCH. I TRUC PH SISTEL WNIUIWS SR TNE RTNEL CAH. YDT I
MAOORT BIOC RDT TNAT ZAOE SAG AOHTNIOF RB NIP IO UROCRO. GEUU, NE IS A
KELH DOCESELKIOF HRDOF PAO--AOC I CR ORT SDWWRSE TNELE IS TNE UEAST
MNAOME IO TNE GRLUC RB NEL EKEL FETTIOF NIP ORG. TNELE IS OR TAUV RB NIS
MRPIOF TR OETNELBIEUC AFAIO IO TNE SDPPEL; AOC I NAKE IOQDILEC RB
EKELHYRCH, TRR, GNR IS UIVEUH TR VORG.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “I AP CETELPIOEC OEKEL TR SWEAV RB IT AFAIO”
]

“I CR ORT YEUIEKE TNAT NE GIUU EKEL UIKE AT OETNELBIEUC AOH PRLE.”

“RN, GEUU! IT IS ZDST AS NE MNRRSES. ORYRCH GAOTS NIP TR MRPE; TNRDFN I
SNAUU AUGAHS SAH TNAT NE DSEC PH CADFNTEL EXTLEPEUH IUU; AOC, IB I GAS
NEL, I GRDUC ORT NAKE WDT DW GITN IT. GEUU, PH MRPBRLT IS, I AP SDLE
ZAOE GIUU CIE RB A YLRVEO NEALT, AOC TNEO NE GIUU YE SRLLH BRL GNAT NE
NAS CROE.”

YDT AS EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT LEMEIKE MRPBRLT BLRP AOH SDMN EXWEMTATIRO SNE
PACE OR AOSGEL.

“GEUU, UIJJH,” MROTIODEC NEL PRTNEL, SRRO ABTELGALCS, “AOC SR TNE
MRUUIOSES UIKE KELH MRPBRLTAYUE, CR TNEH? GEUU, GEUU, I ROUH NRWE IT
GIUU UAST. AOC GNAT SRLT RB TAYUE CR TNEH VEEW? MNALURTTE IS AO
EXMEUUEOT PAOAFEL, I CALE SAH. IB SNE IS NAUB AS SNALW AS NEL PRTNEL,
SNE IS SAKIOF EORDFN. TNELE IS ORTNIOF EXTLAKAFAOT IO _TNEIL_
NRDSEVEEWIOF, I CALE SAH.”

“OR, ORTNIOF AT AUU.”

“A FLEAT CEAU RB FRRC PAOAFEPEOT, CEWEOC DWRO IT. HES, HES. _TNEH_ GIUU
TAVE MALE ORT TR RDTLDO TNEIL IOMRPE. _TNEH_ GIUU OEKEL YE CISTLESSEC
BRL PROEH. GEUU, PDMN FRRC PAH IT CR TNEP! AOC SR, I SDWWRSE, TNEH RBTEO
TAUV RB NAKIOF UROFYRDLO GNEO HRDL BATNEL IS CEAC. TNEH URRV DWRO IT
QDITE AS TNEIL RGO, I CALE SAH, GNEOEKEL TNAT NAWWEOS.”

“IT GAS A SDYZEMT GNIMN TNEH MRDUC ORT PEOTIRO YEBRLE PE.”

“OR; IT GRDUC NAKE YEEO STLAOFE IB TNEH NAC. YDT I PAVE OR CRDYT TNEH
RBTEO TAUV RB IT YETGEEO TNEPSEUKES. GEUU, IB TNEH MAO YE EASH GITN AO
ESTATE TNAT IS ORT UAGBDUUH TNEIL RGO, SR PDMN TNE YETTEL. _I_ SNRDUC YE
ASNAPEC RB NAKIOF ROE TNAT GAS ROUH EOTAIUEC RO PE.”

“GNEO MRUROEU PIUUEL’S LEFIPEOT GEOT AGAH”

MNAWTEL XUI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TNE BILST GEEV RB TNEIL LETDLO GAS SRRO FROE. TNE SEMROC YEFAO. IT GAS
TNE UAST RB TNE LEFIPEOT’S STAH IO PELHTRO, AOC AUU TNE HRDOF UACIES IO
TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC GELE CLRRWIOF AWAME. TNE CEZEMTIRO GAS AUPRST
DOIKELSAU. TNE EUCEL PISS YEOOETS AUROE GELE STIUU AYUE TR EAT, CLIOV,
AOC SUEEW, AOC WDLSDE TNE DSDAU MRDLSE RB TNEIL EPWURHPEOTS. KELH
BLEQDEOTUH GELE TNEH LEWLRAMNEC BRL TNIS IOSEOSIYIUITH YH VITTH AOC
UHCIA, GNRSE RGO PISELH GAS EXTLEPE, AOC GNR MRDUC ORT MRPWLENEOC SDMN
NALC-NEALTECOESS IO AOH RB TNE BAPIUH.

“FRRC NEAKEO! GNAT IS TR YEMRPE RB DS? GNAT ALE GE TR CR?” GRDUC TNEH
RBTEO EXMUAIP IO TNE YITTELOESS RB GRE. “NRG MAO HRD YE SPIUIOF SR,
UIJJH?”

TNEIL ABBEMTIROATE PRTNEL SNALEC AUU TNEIL FLIEB; SNE LEPEPYELEC GNAT
SNE NAC NELSEUB EOCDLEC RO A SIPIUAL RMMASIRO BIKE-AOC-TGEOTH HEALS AFR.

“I AP SDLE,” SAIC SNE, “I MLIEC BRL TGR CAHS TRFETNEL GNEO MRUROEU
PIUUEL’S LEFIPEOT GEOT AGAH. I TNRDFNT I SNRDUC NAKE YLRVE PH NEALT.”

“I AP SDLE I SNAUU YLEAV _PIOE_,” SAIC UHCIA.

“IB ROE MRDUC YDT FR TR YLIFNTRO!” RYSELKEC PLS. YEOOET.

“RN HES!--IB ROE MRDUC YDT FR TR YLIFNTRO! YDT WAWA IS SR CISAFLEEAYUE.”

“A UITTUE SEA-YATNIOF GRDUC SET PE DW BRL EKEL.”

“AOC PH ADOT WNIUIWS IS SDLE IT GRDUC CR _PE_ A FLEAT CEAU RB FRRC,”
ACCEC VITTH.

SDMN GELE TNE VIOC RB UAPEOTATIROS LESRDOCIOF WELWETDAUUH TNLRDFN
UROFYRDLO NRDSE. EUIJAYETN TLIEC TR YE CIKELTEC YH TNEP; YDT AUU SEOSE
RB WUEASDLE GAS URST IO SNAPE. SNE BEUT AOEG TNE ZDSTIME RB PL. CALMH’S
RYZEMTIROS; AOC OEKEL NAC SNE YEBRLE YEEO SR PDMN CISWRSEC TR WALCRO NIS
IOTELBELEOME IO TNE KIEGS RB NIS BLIEOC.

YDT TNE FURRP RB UHCIA’S WLRSWEMT GAS SNRLTUH MUEALEC AGAH; BRL SNE
LEMEIKEC AO IOKITATIRO BLRP PLS. BRLSTEL, TNE GIBE RB TNE MRUROEU RB TNE
LEFIPEOT, TR AMMRPWAOH NEL TR YLIFNTRO. TNIS IOKAUDAYUE BLIEOC GAS A
KELH HRDOF GRPAO, AOC KELH UATEUH PALLIEC. A LESEPYUAOME IO FRRC-NDPRDL
AOC FRRC SWILITS NAC LEMRPPEOCEC NEL AOC UHCIA TR EAMN RTNEL, AOC RDT RB
TNEIL _TNLEE_ PROTNS’ AMQDAIOTAOME TNEH NAC YEEO IOTIPATE _TGR_.

TNE LAWTDLE RB UHCIA RO TNIS RMMASIRO, NEL ACRLATIRO RB PLS. BRLSTEL,
TNE CEUIFNT RB PLS. YEOOET, AOC TNE PRLTIBIMATIRO RB VITTH, ALE SMALMEUH
TR YE CESMLIYEC. GNRUUH IOATTEOTIKE TR NEL SISTEL’S BEEUIOFS, UHCIA BUEG
AYRDT TNE NRDSE IO LESTUESS EMSTASH, MAUUIOF BRL EKELHROE’S
MROFLATDUATIROS, AOC UADFNIOF AOC TAUVIOF GITN PRLE KIRUEOME TNAO EKEL;
GNIUST TNE UDMVUESS VITTH MROTIODEC IO TNE WALURDL LEWIOIOF AT NEL BATE
IO TELPS AS DOLEASROAYUE AS NEL AMMEOT GAS WEEKISN.

“I MAOORT SEE GNH PLS. BRLSTEL SNRDUC ORT ASV _PE_ AS GEUU AS UHCIA,”
SAIC SNE, “TNRDFN I AP _ORT_ NEL WALTIMDUAL BLIEOC. I NAKE ZDST AS PDMN
LIFNT TR YE ASVEC AS SNE NAS, AOC PRLE TRR, BRL I AP TGR HEALS RUCEL.”

IO KAIO CIC EUIJAYETN ATTEPWT TR PAVE NEL LEASROAYUE, AOC ZAOE TR PAVE
NEL LESIFOEC. AS BRL EUIJAYETN NELSEUB, TNIS IOKITATIRO GAS SR BAL BLRP
EXMITIOF IO NEL TNE SAPE BEEUIOFS AS IO NEL PRTNEL AOC UHCIA, TNAT SNE
MROSICELEC IT AS TNE CEATN-GALLAOT RB AUU WRSSIYIUITH RB MRPPRO SEOSE
BRL TNE UATTEL; AOC CETESTAYUE AS SDMN A STEW PDST PAVE NEL, GELE IT
VORGO, SNE MRDUC ORT NEUW SEMLETUH ACKISIOF NEL BATNEL ORT TR UET NEL
FR. SNE LEWLESEOTEC TR NIP AUU TNE IPWLRWLIETIES RB UHCIA’S FEOELAU
YENAKIRDL, TNE UITTUE ACKAOTAFE SNE MRDUC CELIKE BLRP TNE BLIEOCSNIW RB
SDMN A GRPAO AS PLS. BRLSTEL, AOC TNE WLRYAYIUITH RB NEL YEIOF HET PRLE
IPWLDCEOT GITN SDMN A MRPWAOIRO AT YLIFNTRO, GNELE TNE TEPWTATIROS PDST
YE FLEATEL TNAO AT NRPE. NE NEALC NEL ATTEOTIKEUH, AOC TNEO SAIC,--

“UHCIA GIUU OEKEL YE EASH TIUU SNE NAS EXWRSEC NELSEUB IO SRPE WDYUIM
WUAME RL RTNEL, AOC GE MAO OEKEL EXWEMT NEL TR CR IT GITN SR UITTUE
EXWEOSE RL IOMROKEOIEOME TR NEL BAPIUH AS DOCEL TNE WLESEOT
MILMDPSTAOMES.”

“IB HRD GELE AGALE,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, “RB TNE KELH FLEAT CISACKAOTAFE TR
DS AUU, GNIMN PDST ALISE BLRP TNE WDYUIM ORTIME RB UHCIA’S DOFDALCEC AOC
IPWLDCEOT PAOOEL, OAH, GNIMN NAS AULEACH ALISEO BLRP IT, I AP SDLE HRD
GRDUC ZDCFE CIBBELEOTUH IO TNE ABBAIL.”

“AULEACH ALISEO!” LEWEATEC PL. YEOOET. “GNAT! NAS SNE BLIFNTEOEC AGAH
SRPE RB HRDL URKELS? WRRL UITTUE UIJJH! YDT CR ORT YE MAST CRGO. SDMN
SQDEAPISN HRDTNS AS MAOORT YEAL TR YE MROOEMTEC GITN A UITTUE AYSDLCITH
ALE ORT GRLTN A LEFLET. MRPE, UET PE SEE TNE UIST RB TNE WITIBDU BEUURGS
GNR NAKE YEEO VEWT AURRB YH UHCIA’S BRUUH.”

“IOCEEC, HRD ALE PISTAVEO. I NAKE OR SDMN IOZDLIES TR LESEOT. IT IS ORT
RB WEMDUIAL, YDT RB FEOELAU EKIUS, GNIMN I AP ORG MRPWUAIOIOF. RDL
IPWRLTAOME, RDL LESWEMTAYIUITH IO TNE GRLUC, PDST YE ABBEMTEC YH TNE
GIUC KRUATIUITH, TNE ASSDLAOME AOC CISCAIO RB AUU LESTLAIOT GNIMN PALV
UHCIA’S MNALAMTEL. EXMDSE PE,--BRL I PDST SWEAV WUAIOUH. IB HRD, PH CEAL
BATNEL, GIUU ORT TAVE TNE TLRDYUE RB MNEMVIOF NEL EXDYELAOT SWILITS, AOC
RB TEAMNIOF NEL TNAT NEL WLESEOT WDLSDITS ALE ORT TR YE TNE YDSIOESS RB
NEL UIBE, SNE GIUU SRRO YE YEHROC TNE LEAMN RB APEOCPEOT. NEL MNALAMTEL
GIUU YE BIXEC; AOC SNE GIUU, AT SIXTEEO, YE TNE PRST CETELPIOEC BUILT
TNAT EKEL PACE NELSEUB AOC NEL BAPIUH LICIMDURDS;--A BUILT, TRR, IO TNE
GRLST AOC PEAOEST CEFLEE RB BUILTATIRO; GITNRDT AOH ATTLAMTIRO YEHROC
HRDTN AOC A TRUELAYUE WELSRO; AOC, BLRP TNE IFORLAOME AOC EPWTIOESS RB
NEL PIOC, GNRUUH DOAYUE TR GALC RBB AOH WRLTIRO RB TNAT DOIKELSAU
MROTEPWT GNIMN NEL LAFE BRL ACPILATIRO GIUU EXMITE. IO TNIS CAOFEL VITTH
IS AUSR MRPWLENEOCEC. SNE GIUU BRUURG GNELEKEL UHCIA UEACS. KAIO,
IFORLAOT, ICUE, AOC AYSRUDTEUH DOMROTLRUUEC! RN, PH CEAL BATNEL, MAO HRD
SDWWRSE IT WRSSIYUE TNAT TNEH GIUU ORT YE MEOSDLEC AOC CESWISEC GNELEKEL
TNEH ALE VORGO, AOC TNAT TNEIL SISTELS GIUU ORT YE RBTEO IOKRUKEC IO TNE
CISFLAME?”

PL. YEOOET SAG TNAT NEL GNRUE NEALT GAS IO TNE SDYZEMT; AOC,
ABBEMTIROATEUH TAVIOF NEL NAOC, SAIC, IO LEWUH,--

“CR ORT PAVE HRDLSEUB DOEASH, PH URKE. GNELEKEL HRD AOC ZAOE ALE VORGO,
HRD PDST YE LESWEMTEC AOC KAUDEC; AOC HRD GIUU ORT AWWEAL TR UESS
ACKAOTAFE BRL NAKIOF A MRDWUE RB--RL I PAH SAH, TNLEE--KELH SIUUH
SISTELS. GE SNAUU NAKE OR WEAME AT UROFYRDLO IB UHCIA CRES ORT FR TR
YLIFNTRO. UET NEL FR, TNEO. MRUROEU BRLSTEL IS A SEOSIYUE PAO, AOC GIUU
VEEW NEL RDT RB AOH LEAU PISMNIEB; AOC SNE IS UDMVIUH TRR WRRL TR YE AO
RYZEMT RB WLEH TR AOHYRCH. AT YLIFNTRO SNE GIUU YE RB UESS IPWRLTAOME
EKEO AS A MRPPRO BUILT TNAO SNE NAS YEEO NELE. TNE RBBIMELS GIUU BIOC
GRPEO YETTEL GRLTN TNEIL ORTIME. UET DS NRWE, TNELEBRLE, TNAT NEL YEIOF
TNELE PAH TEAMN NEL NEL RGO IOSIFOIBIMAOME. AT AOH LATE, SNE MAOORT FLRG
PAOH CEFLEES GRLSE, GITNRDT ADTNRLIJIOF DS TR URMV NEL DW BRL TNE LEST
RB NEL UIBE.”

GITN TNIS AOSGEL EUIJAYETN GAS BRLMEC TR YE MROTEOT; YDT NEL RGO RWIOIRO
MROTIODEC TNE SAPE, AOC SNE UEBT NIP CISAWWRIOTEC AOC SRLLH. IT GAS ORT
IO NEL OATDLE, NRGEKEL, TR IOMLEASE NEL KEXATIROS YH CGEUUIOF RO TNEP.
SNE GAS MROBICEOT RB NAKIOF WELBRLPEC NEL CDTH; AOC TR BLET RKEL
DOAKRICAYUE EKIUS, RL ADFPEOT TNEP YH AOXIETH, GAS OR WALT RB NEL
CISWRSITIRO.

NAC UHCIA AOC NEL PRTNEL VORGO TNE SDYSTAOME RB NEL MROBELEOME GITN NEL
BATNEL, TNEIL IOCIFOATIRO GRDUC NALCUH NAKE BRDOC EXWLESSIRO IO TNEIL
DOITEC KRUDYIUITH. IO UHCIA’S IPAFIOATIRO, A KISIT TR YLIFNTRO MRPWLISEC
EKELH WRSSIYIUITH RB EALTNUH NAWWIOESS. SNE SAG, GITN TNE MLEATIKE EHE
RB BAOMH, TNE STLEETS RB TNAT FAH YATNIOF-WUAME MRKELEC GITN RBBIMELS.
SNE SAG NELSEUB TNE RYZEMT RB ATTEOTIRO TR TEOS AOC TR SMRLES RB TNEP AT
WLESEOT DOVORGO. SNE SAG AUU TNE FURLIES RB TNE MAPW: ITS TEOTS
STLETMNEC BRLTN IO YEADTERDS DOIBRLPITH RB UIOES, MLRGCEC GITN TNE HRDOF
AOC TNE FAH, AOC CAJJUIOF GITN SMALUET; AOC, TR MRPWUETE TNE KIEG, SNE
SAG NELSEUB SEATEC YEOEATN A TEOT, TEOCELUH BUILTIOF GITN AT UEAST SIX
RBBIMELS AT ROME.

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“TEOCELUH BUILTIOF”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

NAC SNE VORGO TNAT NEL SISTEL SRDFNT TR TEAL NEL BLRP SDMN WLRSWEMTS AOC
SDMN LEAUITIES AS TNESE, GNAT GRDUC NAKE YEEO NEL SEOSATIROS? TNEH MRDUC
NAKE YEEO DOCELSTRRC ROUH YH NEL PRTNEL, GNR PIFNT NAKE BEUT OEALUH TNE
SAPE. UHCIA’S FRIOF TR YLIFNTRO GAS AUU TNAT MROSRUEC NEL BRL TNE
PEUAOMNRUH MROKIMTIRO RB NEL NDSYAOC’S OEKEL IOTEOCIOF TR FR TNELE
NIPSEUB.

YDT TNEH GELE EOTILEUH IFORLAOT RB GNAT NAC WASSEC; AOC TNEIL LAWTDLES
MROTIODEC, GITN UITTUE IOTELPISSIRO, TR TNE KELH CAH RB UHCIA’S UEAKIOF
NRPE.

EUIJAYETN GAS ORG TR SEE PL. GIMVNAP BRL TNE UAST TIPE. NAKIOF YEEO
BLEQDEOTUH IO MRPWAOH GITN NIP SIOME NEL LETDLO, AFITATIRO GAS WLETTH
GEUU RKEL; TNE AFITATIROS RB BRLPEL WALTIAUITH EOTILEUH SR. SNE NAC EKEO
UEALOT TR CETEMT, IO TNE KELH FEOTUEOESS GNIMN NAC BILST CEUIFNTEC NEL,
AO ABBEMTATIRO AOC A SAPEOESS TR CISFDST AOC GEALH. IO NIS WLESEOT
YENAKIRDL TR NELSEUB, PRLERKEL, SNE NAC A BLESN SRDLME RB CISWUEASDLE;
BRL TNE IOMUIOATIRO NE SRRO TESTIBIEC RB LEOEGIOF TNRSE ATTEOTIROS GNIMN
NAC PALVEC TNE EALUH WALT RB TNEIL AMQDAIOTAOME MRDUC ROUH SELKE, ABTEL
GNAT NAC SIOME WASSEC, TR WLRKRVE NEL. SNE URST AUU MROMELO BRL NIP IO
BIOCIOF NELSEUB TNDS SEUEMTEC AS TNE RYZEMT RB SDMN ICUE AOC BLIKRURDS
FAUUAOTLH; AOC GNIUE SNE STEACIUH LEWLESSEC IT, MRDUC ORT YDT BEEU TNE
LEWLRRB MROTAIOEC IO NIS YEUIEKIOF, TNAT NRGEKEL UROF, AOC BRL GNATEKEL
MADSE, NIS ATTEOTIROS NAC YEEO GITNCLAGO, NEL KAOITH GRDUC YE FLATIBIEC,
AOC NEL WLEBELEOME SEMDLEC, AT AOH TIPE, YH TNEIL LEOEGAU.

RO TNE KELH UAST CAH RB TNE LEFIPEOT’S LEPAIOIOF IO PELHTRO, NE CIOEC,
GITN RTNELS RB TNE RBBIMELS, AT UROFYRDLO; AOC SR UITTUE GAS EUIJAYETN
CISWRSEC TR WALT BLRP NIP IO FRRC-NDPRDL, TNAT, RO NIS PAVIOF SRPE
IOQDILH AS TR TNE PAOOEL IO GNIMN NEL TIPE NAC WASSEC AT NDOSBRLC, SNE
PEOTIROEC MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP’S AOC PL. CALMH’S NAKIOF YRTN SWEOT TNLEE
GEEVS AT LRSIOFS, AOC ASVEC NIP IB NE GELE AMQDAIOTEC GITN TNE BRLPEL.

NE URRVEC SDLWLISEC, CISWUEASEC, AUALPEC; YDT, GITN A PRPEOT’S
LEMRUUEMTIRO, AOC A LETDLOIOF SPIUE, LEWUIEC, TNAT NE NAC BRLPELUH SEEO
NIP RBTEO; AOC, ABTEL RYSELKIOF TNAT NE GAS A KELH FEOTUEPAOUIVE PAO,
ASVEC NEL NRG SNE NAC UIVEC NIP. NEL AOSGEL GAS GALPUH IO NIS BAKRDL.
GITN AO AIL RB IOCIBBELEOME, NE SRRO ABTELGALCS ACCEC, “NRG UROF CIC HRD
SAH TNAT NE GAS AT LRSIOFS?”

“OEALUH TNLEE GEEVS.”

“AOC HRD SAG NIP BLEQDEOTUH?”

“HES, AUPRST EKELH CAH.”

“NIS PAOOELS ALE KELH CIBBELEOT BLRP NIS MRDSIO’S.”

“HES, KELH CIBBELEOT; YDT I TNIOV PL. CALMH IPWLRKES RO AMQDAIOTAOME.”

“IOCEEC!” MLIEC GIMVNAP, GITN A URRV GNIMN CIC ORT ESMAWE NEL. “AOC WLAH
PAH I ASV--” YDT MNEMVIOF NIPSEUB, NE ACCEC, IO A FAHEL TROE, “IS IT IO
ACCLESS TNAT NE IPWLRKES? NAS NE CEIFOEC TR ACC ADFNT RB MIKIUITH TR NIS
RLCIOALH STHUE? BRL I CALE ORT NRWE,” NE MROTIODEC, IO A URGEL AOC PRLE
SELIRDS TROE, “TNAT NE IS IPWLRKEC IO ESSEOTIAUS.”

“RN, OR!” SAIC EUIJAYETN. “IO ESSEOTIAUS, I YEUIEKE, NE IS KELH PDMN
GNAT NE EKEL GAS.”

GNIUE SNE SWRVE, GIMVNAP URRVEC AS IB SMALMEUH VORGIOF GNETNEL TR
LEZRIME RKEL NEL GRLCS RL TR CISTLDST TNEIL PEAOIOF. TNELE GAS A
SRPETNIOF IO NEL MRDOTEOAOME GNIMN PACE NIP UISTEO GITN AO AWWLENEOSIKE
AOC AOXIRDS ATTEOTIRO, GNIUE SNE ACCEC,--

“GNEO I SAIC TNAT NE IPWLRKEC RO AMQDAIOTAOME, I CIC ORT PEAO TNAT
EITNEL NIS PIOC RL PAOOELS GELE IO A STATE RB IPWLRKEPEOT; YDT TNAT,
BLRP VORGIOF NIP YETTEL, NIS CISWRSITIRO GAS YETTEL DOCELSTRRC.”

GIMVNAP’S AUALP ORG AWWEALEC IO A NEIFNTEOEC MRPWUEXIRO AOC AFITATEC
URRV; BRL A BEG PIODTES NE GAS SIUEOT; TIUU, SNAVIOF RBB NIS
EPYALLASSPEOT, NE TDLOEC TR NEL AFAIO, AOC SAIC IO TNE FEOTUEST RB
AMMEOTS,--

“HRD, GNR SR GEUU VORG PH BEEUIOFS TRGALCS PL. CALMH, GIUU LEACIUH
MRPWLENEOC NRG SIOMELEUH I PDST LEZRIME TNAT NE IS GISE EORDFN TR ASSDPE
EKEO TNE _AWWEALAOME_ RB GNAT IS LIFNT. NIS WLICE, IO TNAT CILEMTIRO,
PAH YE RB SELKIME, IB ORT TR NIPSEUB, TR PAOH RTNELS, BRL IT PDST CETEL
NIP BLRP SDMN BRDU PISMROCDMT AS I NAKE SDBBELEC YH. I ROUH BEAL TNAT
TNE SRLT RB MADTIRDSOESS TR GNIMN HRD, I IPAFIOE, NAKE YEEO AUUDCIOF, IS
PELEUH ACRWTEC RO NIS KISITS TR NIS ADOT, RB GNRSE FRRC RWIOIRO AOC
ZDCFPEOT NE STAOCS PDMN IO AGE. NIS BEAL RB NEL NAS AUGAHS RWELATEC, I
VORG, GNEO TNEH GELE TRFETNEL; AOC A FRRC CEAU IS TR YE IPWDTEC TR NIS
GISN RB BRLGALCIOF TNE PATMN GITN PISS CE YRDLFN, GNIMN I AP MELTAIO NE
NAS KELH PDMN AT NEALT.”

EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT LEWLESS A SPIUE AT TNIS, YDT SNE AOSGELEC ROUH YH A
SUIFNT IOMUIOATIRO RB TNE NEAC. SNE SAG TNAT NE GAOTEC TR EOFAFE NEL RO
TNE RUC SDYZEMT RB NIS FLIEKAOMES, AOC SNE GAS IO OR NDPRDL TR IOCDUFE
NIP. TNE LEST RB TNE EKEOIOF WASSEC GITN TNE _AWWEALAOME_, RO NIS SICE,
RB DSDAU MNEELBDUOESS, YDT GITN OR BDLTNEL ATTEPWT TR CISTIOFDISN
EUIJAYETN; AOC TNEH WALTEC AT UAST GITN PDTDAU MIKIUITH, AOC WRSSIYUH A
PDTDAU CESILE RB OEKEL PEETIOF AFAIO.

GNEO TNE WALTH YLRVE DW, UHCIA LETDLOEC GITN PLS. BRLSTEL TR PELHTRO,
BLRP GNEOME TNEH GELE TR SET RDT EALUH TNE OEXT PRLOIOF. TNE SEWALATIRO
YETGEEO NEL AOC NEL BAPIUH GAS LATNEL ORISH TNAO WATNETIM. VITTH GAS TNE
ROUH ROE GNR SNEC TEALS; YDT SNE CIC GEEW BLRP KEXATIRO AOC EOKH. PLS.
YEOOET GAS CIBBDSE IO NEL FRRC GISNES BRL TNE BEUIMITH RB NEL CADFNTEL,
AOC IPWLESSIKE IO NEL IOZDOMTIROS TNAT SNE GRDUC ORT PISS TNE
RWWRLTDOITH RB EOZRHIOF NELSEUB AS PDMN AS WRSSIYUE,--ACKIME GNIMN TNELE
GAS EKELH LEASRO TR YEUIEKE GRDUC YE ATTEOCEC TR; AOC, IO TNE MUAPRLRDS
NAWWIOESS RB UHCIA NELSEUB IO YICCIOF BALEGEUU, TNE PRLE FEOTUE ACIEDS
RB NEL SISTELS GELE DTTELEC GITNRDT YEIOF NEALC.

MNAWTEL XUII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

NAC EUIJAYETN’S RWIOIRO YEEO AUU CLAGO BLRP NEL RGO BAPIUH, SNE MRDUC
ORT NAKE BRLPEC A KELH WUEASIOF WIMTDLE RB MROZDFAU BEUIMITH RL CRPESTIM
MRPBRLT. NEL BATNEL, MAWTIKATEC YH HRDTN AOC YEADTH, AOC TNAT AWWEALAOME
RB FRRC-NDPRDL GNIMN HRDTN AOC YEADTH FEOELAUUH FIKE, NAC PALLIEC A
GRPAO GNRSE GEAV DOCELSTAOCIOF AOC IUUIYELAU PIOC NAC KELH EALUH IO
TNEIL PALLIAFE WDT AO EOC TR AUU LEAU ABBEMTIRO BRL NEL. LESWEMT,
ESTEEP, AOC MROBICEOME NAC KAOISNEC BRL EKEL; AOC AUU NIS KIEGS RB
CRPESTIM NAWWIOESS GELE RKELTNLRGO. YDT PL. YEOOET GAS ORT RB A
CISWRSITIRO TR SEEV MRPBRLT BRL TNE CISAWWRIOTPEOT GNIMN NIS RGO
IPWLDCEOME NAC YLRDFNT RO IO AOH RB TNRSE WUEASDLES GNIMN TRR RBTEO
MROSRUE TNE DOBRLTDOATE BRL TNEIL BRUUH RL TNEIL KIME. NE GAS BROC RB
TNE MRDOTLH AOC RB YRRVS; AOC BLRP TNESE TASTES NAC ALISEO NIS WLIOMIWAU
EOZRHPEOTS. TR NIS GIBE NE GAS KELH UITTUE RTNELGISE IOCEYTEC TNAO AS
NEL IFORLAOME AOC BRUUH NAC MROTLIYDTEC TR NIS APDSEPEOT. TNIS IS ORT
TNE SRLT RB NAWWIOESS GNIMN A PAO GRDUC IO FEOELAU GISN TR RGE TR NIS
GIBE; YDT GNELE RTNEL WRGELS RB EOTELTAIOPEOT ALE GAOTIOF, TNE TLDE
WNIURSRWNEL GIUU CELIKE YEOEBIT BLRP SDMN AS ALE FIKEO.

EUIJAYETN, NRGEKEL, NAC OEKEL YEEO YUIOC TR TNE IPWLRWLIETH RB NEL
BATNEL’S YENAKIRDL AS A NDSYAOC. SNE NAC AUGAHS SEEO IT GITN WAIO; YDT
LESWEMTIOF NIS AYIUITIES, AOC FLATEBDU BRL NIS ABBEMTIROATE TLEATPEOT RB
NELSEUB, SNE EOCEAKRDLEC TR BRLFET GNAT SNE MRDUC ORT RKELURRV, AOC TR
YAOISN BLRP NEL TNRDFNTS TNAT MROTIODAU YLEAMN RB MROZDFAU RYUIFATIRO
AOC CEMRLDP GNIMN, IO EXWRSIOF NIS GIBE TR TNE MROTEPWT RB NEL RGO
MNIUCLEO, GAS SR NIFNUH LEWLENEOSIYUE. YDT SNE NAC OEKEL BEUT SR
STLROFUH AS ORG TNE CISACKAOTAFES GNIMN PDST ATTEOC TNE MNIUCLEO RB SR
DOSDITAYUE A PALLIAFE, ORL EKEL YEEO SR BDUUH AGALE RB TNE EKIUS ALISIOF
BLRP SR IUU-ZDCFEC A CILEMTIRO RB TAUEOTS--TAUEOTS GNIMN, LIFNTUH DSEC,
PIFNT AT UEAST NAKE WLESELKEC TNE LESWEMTAYIUITH RB NIS CADFNTELS, EKEO
IB IOMAWAYUE RB EOUALFIOF TNE PIOC RB NIS GIBE.

GNEO EUIJAYETN NAC LEZRIMEC RKEL GIMVNAP’S CEWALTDLE, SNE BRDOC UITTUE
RTNEL MADSE BRL SATISBAMTIRO IO TNE URSS RB TNE LEFIPEOT. TNEIL WALTIES
AYLRAC GELE UESS KALIEC TNAO YEBRLE; AOC AT NRPE SNE NAC A PRTNEL AOC
SISTEL, GNRSE MROSTAOT LEWIOIOFS AT TNE CDUOESS RB EKELHTNIOF ALRDOC
TNEP TNLEG A LEAU FURRP RKEL TNEIL CRPESTIM MILMUE; AOC, TNRDFN VITTH
PIFNT IO TIPE LEFAIO NEL OATDLAU CEFLEE RB SEOSE, SIOME TNE CISTDLYELS
RB NEL YLAIO GELE LEPRKEC, NEL RTNEL SISTEL, BLRP GNRSE CISWRSITIRO
FLEATEL EKIU PIFNT YE AWWLENEOCEC, GAS UIVEUH TR YE NALCEOEC IO AUU NEL
BRUUH AOC ASSDLAOME, YH A SITDATIRO RB SDMN CRDYUE CAOFEL AS A
GATELIOF-WUAME AOC A MAPW. DWRO TNE GNRUE, TNELEBRLE, SNE BRDOC, GNAT
NAS YEEO SRPETIPES BRDOC YEBRLE, TNAT AO EKEOT TR GNIMN SNE NAC URRVEC
BRLGALC GITN IPWATIEOT CESILE, CIC ORT, IO TAVIOF WUAME, YLIOF AUU TNE
SATISBAMTIRO SNE NAC WLRPISEC NELSEUB. IT GAS MROSEQDEOTUH OEMESSALH TR
OAPE SRPE RTNEL WELIRC BRL TNE MRPPEOMEPEOT RB AMTDAU BEUIMITH; TR NAKE
SRPE RTNEL WRIOT RO GNIMN NEL GISNES AOC NRWES PIFNT YE BIXEC, AOC YH
AFAIO EOZRHIOF TNE WUEASDLE RB AOTIMIWATIRO, MROSRUE NELSEUB BRL TNE
WLESEOT, AOC WLEWALE BRL AORTNEL CISAWWRIOTPEOT. NEL TRDL TR TNE UAVES
GAS ORG TNE RYZEMT RB NEL NAWWIEST TNRDFNTS: IT GAS NEL YEST MROSRUATIRO
BRL AUU TNE DOMRPBRLTAYUE NRDLS GNIMN TNE CISMROTEOTECOESS RB NEL PRTNEL
AOC VITTH PACE IOEKITAYUE; AOC MRDUC SNE NAKE IOMUDCEC ZAOE IO TNE
SMNEPE, EKELH WALT RB IT GRDUC NAKE YEEO WELBEMT.

“YDT IT IS BRLTDOATE,” TNRDFNT SNE, “TNAT I NAKE SRPETNIOF TR GISN BRL.
GELE TNE GNRUE ALLAOFEPEOT MRPWUETE, PH CISAWWRIOTPEOT GRDUC YE MELTAIO.
YDT NELE, YH MALLHIOF GITN PE ROE MEASEUESS SRDLME RB LEFLET IO PH
SISTEL’S AYSEOME, I PAH LEASROAYUH NRWE TR NAKE AUU PH EXWEMTATIROS RB
WUEASDLE LEAUIJEC. A SMNEPE RB GNIMN EKELH WALT WLRPISES CEUIFNT MAO
OEKEL YE SDMMESSBDU; AOC FEOELAU CISAWWRIOTPEOT IS ROUH GALCEC RBB YH
TNE CEBEOME RB SRPE UITTUE WEMDUIAL KEXATIRO.”

GNEO UHCIA GEOT AGAH SNE WLRPISEC TR GLITE KELH RBTEO AOC KELH PIODTEUH
TR NEL PRTNEL AOC VITTH; YDT NEL UETTELS GELE AUGAHS UROF EXWEMTEC, AOC
AUGAHS KELH SNRLT. TNRSE TR NEL PRTNEL MROTAIOEC UITTUE EUSE TNAO TNAT
TNEH GELE ZDST LETDLOEC BLRP TNE UIYLALH, GNELE SDMN AOC SDMN RBBIMELS
NAC ATTEOCEC TNEP, AOC GNELE SNE NAC SEEO SDMN YEADTIBDU RLOAPEOTS AS
PACE NEL QDITE GIUC; TNAT SNE NAC A OEG FRGO, RL A OEG WALASRU, GNIMN
SNE GRDUC NAKE CESMLIYEC PRLE BDUUH, YDT GAS RYUIFEC TR UEAKE RBB IO A
KIRUEOT NDLLH, AS PLS. BRLSTEL MAUUEC NEL, AOC TNEH GELE FRIOF TR TNE
MAPW; AOC BLRP NEL MRLLESWROCEOME GITN NEL SISTEL TNELE GAS STIUU UESS
TR YE UEALOT, BRL NEL UETTELS TR VITTH, TNRDFN LATNEL UROFEL, GELE PDMN
TRR BDUU RB UIOES DOCEL TNE GRLCS TR YE PACE WDYUIM.

ABTEL TNE BILST BRLTOIFNT RL TNLEE GEEVS RB NEL AYSEOME, NEAUTN,
FRRC-NDPRDL, AOC MNEELBDUOESS YEFAO TR LEAWWEAL AT UROFYRDLO. EKELHTNIOF
GRLE A NAWWIEL ASWEMT. TNE BAPIUIES GNR NAC YEEO IO TRGO BRL TNE GIOTEL
MAPE YAMV AFAIO, AOC SDPPEL BIOELH AOC SDPPEL EOFAFEPEOTS ALRSE. PLS.
YEOOET GAS LESTRLEC TR NEL DSDAU QDELDURDS SELEOITH; AOC YH TNE PICCUE
RB ZDOE VITTH GAS SR PDMN LEMRKELEC AS TR YE AYUE TR EOTEL PELHTRO
GITNRDT TEALS,--AO EKEOT RB SDMN NAWWH WLRPISE AS TR PAVE EUIJAYETN
NRWE, TNAT YH TNE BRUURGIOF MNLISTPAS SNE PIFNT YE SR TRUELAYUH
LEASROAYUE AS ORT TR PEOTIRO AO RBBIMEL AYRKE ROME A CAH, DOUESS, YH
SRPE MLDEU AOC PAUIMIRDS ALLAOFEPEOT AT TNE GAL RBBIME, AORTNEL LEFIPEOT
SNRDUC YE QDALTELEC IO PELHTRO.

TNE TIPE BIXEC BRL TNE YEFIOOIOF RB TNEIL ORLTNELO TRDL GAS ORG BAST
AWWLRAMNIOF; AOC A BRLTOIFNT ROUH GAS GAOTIOF RB IT, GNEO A UETTEL
ALLIKEC BLRP PLS. FALCIOEL, GNIMN AT ROME CEUAHEC ITS MRPPEOMEPEOT AOC
MDLTAIUEC ITS EXTEOT. PL. FALCIOEL GRDUC YE WLEKEOTEC YH YDSIOESS BLRP
SETTIOF RDT TIUU A BRLTOIFNT UATEL IO ZDUH, AOC PDST YE IO UROCRO AFAIO
GITNIO A PROTN; AOC AS TNAT UEBT TRR SNRLT A WELIRC BRL TNEP TR FR SR
BAL, AOC SEE SR PDMN AS TNEH NAC WLRWRSEC, RL AT UEAST TR SEE IT GITN
TNE UEISDLE AOC MRPBRLT TNEH NAC YDIUT RO, TNEH GELE RYUIFEC TR FIKE DW
TNE UAVES, AOC SDYSTITDTE A PRLE MROTLAMTEC TRDL; AOC, AMMRLCIOF TR TNE
WLESEOT WUAO, GELE TR FR OR BALTNEL ORLTNGALC TNAO CELYHSNILE. IO TNAT
MRDOTH TNELE GAS EORDFN TR YE SEEO TR RMMDWH TNE MNIEB RB TNEIL TNLEE
GEEVS; AOC TR PLS. FALCIOEL IT NAC A WEMDUIALUH STLROF ATTLAMTIRO. TNE
TRGO GNELE SNE NAC BRLPELUH WASSEC SRPE HEALS RB NEL UIBE, AOC GNELE
TNEH GELE ORG TR SWEOC A BEG CAHS, GAS WLRYAYUH AS FLEAT AO RYZEMT RB
NEL MDLIRSITH AS AUU TNE MEUEYLATEC YEADTIES RB PATURMV, MNATSGRLTN,
CRKECAUE, RL TNE WEAV.

EUIJAYETN GAS EXMESSIKEUH CISAWWRIOTEC: SNE NAC SET NEL NEALT RO SEEIOF
TNE UAVES; AOC STIUU TNRDFNT TNELE PIFNT NAKE YEEO TIPE EORDFN. YDT IT
GAS NEL YDSIOESS TR YE SATISBIEC--AOC MELTAIOUH NEL TEPWEL TR YE NAWWH;
AOC AUU GAS SRRO LIFNT AFAIO.

GITN TNE PEOTIRO RB CELYHSNILE, TNELE GELE PAOH ICEAS MROOEMTEC. IT GAS
IPWRSSIYUE BRL NEL TR SEE TNE GRLC GITNRDT TNIOVIOF RB WEPYELUEH AOC ITS
RGOEL. “YDT SDLEUH,” SAIC SNE, “I PAH EOTEL NIS MRDOTH GITN IPWDOITH,
AOC LRY IT RB A BEG WETLIBIEC SWALS, GITNRDT NIS WELMEIKIOF PE.”

TNE WELIRC RB EXWEMTATIRO GAS ORG CRDYUEC. BRDL GEEVS GELE TR WASS AGAH
YEBRLE NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT’S ALLIKAU. YDT TNEH CIC WASS AGAH, AOC PL. AOC
PLS. FALCIOEL, GITN TNEIL BRDL MNIUCLEO, CIC AT UEOFTN AWWEAL AT
UROFYRDLO. TNE MNIUCLEO, TGR FILUS RB SIX AOC EIFNT HEALS RUC, AOC TGR
HRDOFEL YRHS, GELE TR YE UEBT DOCEL TNE WALTIMDUAL MALE RB TNEIL MRDSIO
ZAOE, GNR GAS TNE FEOELAU BAKRDLITE, AOC GNRSE STEACH SEOSE AOC
SGEETOESS RB TEPWEL EXAMTUH ACAWTEC NEL BRL ATTEOCIOF TR TNEP IO EKELH
GAH--TEAMNIOF TNEP, WUAHIOF GITN TNEP, AOC URKIOF TNEP.

TNE FALCIOELS STAHEC ROUH ROE OIFNT AT UROFYRDLO, AOC SET RBB TNE OEXT
PRLOIOF GITN EUIJAYETN IO WDLSDIT RB ORKEUTH AOC APDSEPEOT. ROE
EOZRHPEOT GAS MELTAIO--TNAT RB SDITAYUEOESS AS MRPWAOIROS; A
SDITAYUEOESS GNIMN MRPWLENEOCEC NEAUTN AOC TEPWEL TR YEAL
IOMROKEOIEOMES--MNEELBDUOESS TR EONAOME EKELH WUEASDLE--AOC ABBEMTIRO
AOC IOTEUUIFEOME, GNIMN PIFNT SDWWUH IT APROF TNEPSEUKES IB TNELE GELE
CISAWWRIOTPEOTS AYLRAC.

IT IS ORT TNE RYZEMT RB TNIS GRLV TR FIKE A CESMLIWTIRO RB CELYHSNILE,
ORL RB AOH RB TNE LEPALVAYUE WUAMES TNLRDFN GNIMN TNEIL LRDTE TNITNEL
UAH--RXBRLC, YUEONEIP, GALGIMV, VEOIUGRLTN, YILPIOFNAP, ETM., ALE
SDBBIMIEOTUH VORGO. A SPAUU WALT RB CELYHSNILE IS AUU TNE WLESEOT
MROMELO. TR TNE UITTUE TRGO RB UAPYTRO, TNE SMEOE RB PLS. FALCIOEL’S
BRLPEL LESICEOME, AOC GNELE SNE NAC UATEUH UEALOEC TNAT SRPE
AMQDAIOTAOME STIUU LEPAIOEC, TNEH YEOT TNEIL STEWS, ABTEL NAKIOF SEEO
AUU TNE WLIOMIWAU GROCELS RB TNE MRDOTLH; AOC GITNIO BIKE PIUES RB
UAPYTRO, EUIJAYETN BRDOC, BLRP NEL ADOT, TNAT WEPYELUEH GAS SITDATEC. IT
GAS ORT IO TNEIL CILEMT LRAC; ORL PRLE TNAO A PIUE RL TGR RDT RB IT. IO
TAUVIOF RKEL TNEIL LRDTE TNE EKEOIOF YEBRLE, PLS. FALCIOEL EXWLESSEC AO
IOMUIOATIRO TR SEE TNE WUAME AFAIO. PL. FALCIOEL CEMUALEC NIS
GIUUIOFOESS, AOC EUIJAYETN GAS AWWUIEC TR BRL NEL AWWLRYATIRO.

“PH URKE, SNRDUC ORT HRD UIVE TR SEE A WUAME RB GNIMN HRD NAKE NEALC SR
PDMN?” SAIC NEL ADOT. “A WUAME, TRR, GITN GNIMN SR PAOH RB HRDL
AMQDAIOTAOME ALE MROOEMTEC. GIMVNAP WASSEC AUU NIS HRDTN TNELE, HRD
VORG.”

EUIJAYETN GAS CISTLESSEC. SNE BEUT TNAT SNE NAC OR YDSIOESS AT
WEPYELUEH, AOC GAS RYUIFEC TR ASSDPE A CISIOMUIOATIRO BRL SEEIOF IT. SNE
PDST RGO TNAT SNE GAS TILEC RB FLEAT NRDSES: ABTEL FRIOF RKEL SR PAOH,
SNE LEAUUH NAC OR WUEASDLE IO BIOE MALWETS RL SATIO MDLTAIOS.

PLS. FALCIOEL AYDSEC NEL STDWICITH. “IB IT GELE PELEUH A BIOE NRDSE
LIMNUH BDLOISNEC,” SAIC SNE, “I SNRDUC ORT MALE AYRDT IT PHSEUB; YDT TNE
FLRDOCS ALE CEUIFNTBDU. TNEH NAKE SRPE RB TNE BIOEST GRRCS IO TNE
MRDOTLH.”

EUIJAYETN SAIC OR PRLE; YDT NEL PIOC MRDUC ORT AMQDIESME. TNE
WRSSIYIUITH RB PEETIOF PL. CALMH, GNIUE KIEGIOF TNE WUAME, IOSTAOTUH
RMMDLLEC. IT GRDUC YE CLEACBDU! SNE YUDSNEC AT TNE KELH ICEA; AOC
TNRDFNT IT GRDUC YE YETTEL TR SWEAV RWEOUH TR NEL ADOT, TNAO TR LDO SDMN
A LISV. YDT AFAIOST TNIS TNELE GELE RYZEMTIROS; AOC SNE BIOAUUH LESRUKEC
TNAT IT MRDUC YE TNE UAST LESRDLME, IB NEL WLIKATE IOQDILIES AS TR TNE
AYSEOME RB TNE BAPIUH GELE DOBAKRDLAYUH AOSGELEC.

AMMRLCIOFUH, GNEO SNE LETILEC AT OIFNT, SNE ASVEC TNE MNAPYELPAIC
GNETNEL WEPYELUEH GELE ORT A KELH BIOE WUAME, GNAT GAS TNE OAPE RB ITS
WLRWLIETRL, AOC, GITN OR UITTUE AUALP, GNETNEL TNE BAPIUH GELE CRGO BRL
TNE SDPPEL? A PRST GEUMRPE OEFATIKE BRUURGEC TNE UAST QDESTIRO; AOC NEL
AUALPS YEIOF ORG LEPRKEC, SNE GAS AT UEISDLE TR BEEU A FLEAT CEAU RB
MDLIRSITH TR SEE TNE NRDSE NELSEUB; AOC GNEO TNE SDYZEMT GAS LEKIKEC TNE
OEXT PRLOIOF, AOC SNE GAS AFAIO AWWUIEC TR, MRDUC LEACIUH AOSGEL, AOC
GITN A WLRWEL AIL RB IOCIBBELEOME, TNAT SNE NAC ORT LEAUUH AOH CISUIVE
TR TNE SMNEPE.

TR WEPYELUEH, TNELEBRLE, TNEH GELE TR FR.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “MROZEMTDLIOF AS TR TNE CATE”
]




MNAWTEL XUIII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN, AS TNEH CLRKE AUROF, GATMNEC BRL TNE BILST AWWEALAOME RB
WEPYELUEH GRRCS GITN SRPE WELTDLYATIRO; AOC GNEO AT UEOFTN TNEH TDLOEC
IO AT TNE URCFE, NEL SWILITS GELE IO A NIFN BUDTTEL.

TNE WALV GAS KELH UALFE, AOC MROTAIOEC FLEAT KALIETH RB FLRDOC. TNEH
EOTELEC IT IO ROE RB ITS URGEST WRIOTS, AOC CLRKE BRL SRPE TIPE TNLRDFN
A YEADTIBDU GRRC STLETMNIOF RKEL A GICE EXTEOT.

EUIJAYETN’S PIOC GAS TRR BDUU BRL MROKELSATIRO, YDT SNE SAG AOC ACPILEC
EKELH LEPALVAYUE SWRT AOC WRIOT RB KIEG. TNEH FLACDAUUH ASMEOCEC BRL
NAUB A PIUE, AOC TNEO BRDOC TNEPSEUKES AT TNE TRW RB A MROSICELAYUE
EPIOEOME, GNELE TNE GRRC MEASEC, AOC TNE EHE GAS IOSTAOTUH MADFNT YH
WEPYELUEH NRDSE, SITDATEC RO TNE RWWRSITE SICE RB TNE KAUUEH, IOTR GNIMN
TNE LRAC GITN SRPE AYLDWTOESS GRDOC. IT GAS A UALFE, NAOCSRPE STROE
YDIUCIOF, STAOCIOF GEUU RO LISIOF FLRDOC, AOC YAMVEC YH A LICFE RB NIFN
GRRCH NIUUS; AOC IO BLROT A STLEAP RB SRPE OATDLAU IPWRLTAOME GAS
SGEUUEC IOTR FLEATEL, YDT GITNRDT AOH ALTIBIMIAU AWWEALAOME. ITS YAOVS
GELE OEITNEL BRLPAU ORL BAUSEUH ACRLOEC. EUIJAYETN GAS CEUIFNTEC. SNE
NAC OEKEL SEEO A WUAME BRL GNIMN OATDLE NAC CROE PRLE, RL GNELE OATDLAU
YEADTH NAC YEEO SR UITTUE MRDOTELAMTEC YH AO AGVGALC TASTE. TNEH GELE
AUU RB TNEP GALP IO TNEIL ACPILATIRO; AOC AT TNAT PRPEOT SNE BEUT TNAT
TR YE PISTLESS RB WEPYELUEH PIFNT YE SRPETNIOF!

TNEH CESMEOCEC TNE NIUU, MLRSSEC TNE YLICFE, AOC CLRKE TR TNE CRRL; AOC,
GNIUE EXAPIOIOF TNE OEALEL ASWEMT RB TNE NRDSE, AUU NEL AWWLENEOSIRO RB
PEETIOF ITS RGOEL LETDLOEC. SNE CLEACEC UEST TNE MNAPYELPAIC NAC YEEO
PISTAVEO. RO AWWUHIOF TR SEE TNE WUAME, TNEH GELE ACPITTEC IOTR TNE
NAUU; AOC EUIJAYETN, AS TNEH GAITEC BRL TNE NRDSEVEEWEL, NAC UEISDLE TR
GROCEL AT NEL YEIOF GNELE SNE GAS.

TNE NRDSEVEEWEL MAPE; A LESWEMTAYUE URRVIOF EUCELUH GRPAO, PDMN UESS
BIOE, AOC PRLE MIKIU, TNAO SNE NAC AOH ORTIRO RB BIOCIOF NEL. TNEH
BRUURGEC NEL IOTR TNE CIOIOF-WALURDL. IT GAS A UALFE, GEUU-WLRWRLTIROEC
LRRP, NAOCSRPEUH BITTEC DW. EUIJAYETN, ABTEL SUIFNTUH SDLKEHIOF IT, GEOT
TR A GIOCRG TR EOZRH ITS WLRSWEMT. TNE NIUU, MLRGOEC GITN GRRC, BLRP
GNIMN TNEH NAC CESMEOCEC, LEMEIKIOF IOMLEASEC AYLDWTOESS BLRP TNE
CISTAOME, GAS A YEADTIBDU RYZEMT. EKELH CISWRSITIRO RB TNE FLRDOC GAS
FRRC; AOC SNE URRVEC RO TNE GNRUE SMEOE, TNE LIKEL, TNE TLEES SMATTELEC
RO ITS YAOVS, AOC TNE GIOCIOF RB TNE KAUUEH, AS BAL AS SNE MRDUC TLAME
IT, GITN CEUIFNT. AS TNEH WASSEC IOTR RTNEL LRRPS, TNESE RYZEMTS GELE
TAVIOF CIBBELEOT WRSITIROS; YDT BLRP EKELH GIOCRG TNELE GELE YEADTIES
TR YE SEEO. TNE LRRPS GELE URBTH AOC NAOCSRPE, AOC TNEIL BDLOITDLE
SDITAYUE TR TNE BRLTDOE RB TNEIL WLRWLIETRL; YDT EUIJAYETN SAG, GITN
ACPILATIRO RB NIS TASTE, TNAT IT GAS OEITNEL FADCH ORL DSEUESSUH
BIOE,--GITN UESS RB SWUEOCRDL, AOC PRLE LEAU EUEFAOME, TNAO TNE
BDLOITDLE RB LRSIOFS.

“AOC RB TNIS WUAME,” TNRDFNT SNE, “I PIFNT NAKE YEEO PISTLESS! GITN
TNESE LRRPS I PIFNT NAKE ORG YEEO BAPIUIALUH AMQDAIOTEC! IOSTEAC RB
KIEGIOF TNEP AS A STLAOFEL, I PIFNT NAKE LEZRIMEC IO TNEP AS PH RGO, AOC
GEUMRPEC TR TNEP AS KISITRLS PH DOMUE AOC ADOT. YDT, OR,” LEMRUUEMTIOF
NELSEUB, “TNAT MRDUC OEKEL YE; PH DOMUE AOC ADOT GRDUC NAKE YEEO URST TR
PE; I SNRDUC ORT NAKE YEEO AUURGEC TR IOKITE TNEP.”

TNIS GAS A UDMVH LEMRUUEMTIRO--IT SAKEC NEL BLRP SRPETNIOF UIVE LEFLET.

SNE UROFEC TR IOQDILE RB TNE NRDSEVEEWEL GNETNEL NEL PASTEL GELE LEAUUH
AYSEOT, YDT NAC ORT MRDLAFE BRL IT. AT UEOFTN, NRGEKEL, TNE QDESTIRO GAS
ASVEC YH NEL DOMUE; AOC SNE TDLOEC AGAH GITN AUALP, GNIUE PLS. LEHORUCS
LEWUIEC, TNAT NE GAS; ACCIOF, “YDT GE EXWEMT NIP TR-PRLLRG, GITN A UALFE
WALTH RB BLIEOCS.” NRG LEZRIMEC GAS EUIJAYETN TNAT TNEIL RGO ZRDLOEH NAC
ORT YH AOH MILMDPSTAOME YEEO CEUAHEC A CAH!

NEL ADOT ORG MAUUEC NEL TR URRV AT A WIMTDLE. SNE AWWLRAMNEC, AOC SAG
TNE UIVEOESS RB PL. GIMVNAP, SDSWEOCEC, APROFST SEKELAU RTNEL
PIOIATDLES, RKEL TNE PAOTEU-WIEME. NEL ADOT ASVEC NEL, SPIUIOFUH, NRG
SNE UIVEC IT. TNE NRDSEVEEWEL MAPE BRLGALC, AOC TRUC TNEP IT GAS TNE
WIMTDLE RB A HRDOF FEOTUEPAO, TNE SRO RB NEL UATE PASTEL’S STEGALC, GNR
NAC YEEO YLRDFNT DW YH NIP AT NIS RGO EXWEOSE. “NE IS ORG FROE IOTR TNE
ALPH,” SNE ACCEC; “YDT I AP ABLAIC NE NAS TDLOEC RDT KELH GIUC.”

PLS. FALCIOEL URRVEC AT NEL OIEME GITN A SPIUE, YDT EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT
LETDLO IT.

“AOC TNAT,” SAIC PLS. LEHORUCS, WRIOTIOF TR AORTNEL RB TNE PIOIATDLES,
“IS PH PASTEL--AOC KELH UIVE NIP. IT GAS CLAGO AT TNE SAPE TIPE AS TNE
RTNEL--AYRDT EIFNT HEALS AFR.”

“I NAKE NEALC PDMN RB HRDL PASTEL’S BIOE WELSRO,” SAIC PLS. FALCIOEL,
URRVIOF AT TNE WIMTDLE; “IT IS A NAOCSRPE BAME. YDT, UIJJH, HRD MAO TEUU
DS GNETNEL IT IS UIVE RL ORT.”

PLS. LEHORUCS’ LESWEMT BRL EUIJAYETN SEEPEC TR IOMLEASE RO TNIS
IOTIPATIRO RB NEL VORGIOF NEL PASTEL.

“CRES TNAT HRDOF UACH VORG PL. CALMH?”

EUIJAYETN MRURDLEC, AOC SAIC, “A UITTUE.”

“AOC CR ORT HRD TNIOV NIP A KELH NAOCSRPE FEOTUEPAO, PA’AP?”

“HES, KELH NAOCSRPE.”

“I AP SDLE _I_ VORG OROE SR NAOCSRPE; YDT IO TNE FAUUELH DWSTAILS HRD
GIUU SEE A BIOEL, UALFEL WIMTDLE RB NIP TNAO TNIS. TNIS LRRP GAS PH UATE
PASTEL’S BAKRDLITE LRRP, AOC TNESE PIOIATDLES ALE ZDST AS TNEH DSEC TR
YE TNEO. NE GAS KELH BROC RB TNEP.”

TNIS AMMRDOTEC TR EUIJAYETN BRL PL. GIMVNAP’S YEIOF APROF TNEP.

PLS. LEHORUCS TNEO CILEMTEC TNEIL ATTEOTIRO TR ROE RB PISS CALMH, CLAGO
GNEO SNE GAS ROUH EIFNT HEALS RUC.

“AOC IS PISS CALMH AS NAOCSRPE AS NEL YLRTNEL?” SAIC PL. FALCIOEL.

“RN, HES--TNE NAOCSRPEST HRDOF UACH TNAT EKEL GAS SEEO; AOC SR
AMMRPWUISNEC! SNE WUAHS AOC SIOFS AUU CAH UROF. IO TNE OEXT LRRP IS A
OEG IOSTLDPEOT ZDST MRPE CRGO BRL NEL--A WLESEOT BLRP PH PASTEL: SNE
MRPES NELE TR-PRLLRG GITN NIP.”

PL. FALCIOEL, GNRSE PAOOELS GELE EASH AOC WUEASAOT, EOMRDLAFEC NEL
MRPPDOIMATIKEOESS YH NIS QDESTIROS AOC LEPALVS: PLS. LEHORUCS, EITNEL
BLRP WLICE RL ATTAMNPEOT, NAC EKICEOTUH FLEAT WUEASDLE IO TAUVIOF RB NEL
PASTEL AOC NIS SISTEL.

“IS HRDL PASTEL PDMN AT WEPYELUEH IO TNE MRDLSE RB TNE HEAL?”

“ORT SR PDMN AS I MRDUC GISN, SIL: YDT I CALE SAH NE PAH SWEOC NAUB NIS
TIPE NELE; AOC PISS CALMH IS AUGAHS CRGO BRL TNE SDPPEL PROTNS.”

“EXMEWT,” TNRDFNT EUIJAYETN, “GNEO SNE FRES TR LAPSFATE.”

“IB HRDL PASTEL GRDUC PALLH, HRD PIFNT SEE PRLE RB NIP.”

“HES, SIL; YDT I CR ORT VORG GNEO _TNAT_ GIUU YE. I CR ORT VORG GNR IS
FRRC EORDFN BRL NIP.”

PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL SPIUEC. EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT NEUW SAHIOF, “IT IS
KELH PDMN TR NIS MLECIT, I AP SDLE, TNAT HRD SNRDUC TNIOV SR.”

“I SAH OR PRLE TNAO TNE TLDTN, AOC GNAT EKELHYRCH GIUU SAH TNAT VORGS
NIP,” LEWUIEC TNE RTNEL. EUIJAYETN TNRDFNT TNIS GAS FRIOF WLETTH BAL;
AOC SNE UISTEOEC GITN IOMLEASIOF ASTROISNPEOT AS TNE NRDSEVEEWEL ACCEC,
“I NAKE OEKEL NAC A MLRSS GRLC BLRP NIP IO PH UIBE, AOC I NAKE VORGO NIP
EKEL SIOME NE GAS BRDL HEALS RUC.”

TNIS GAS WLAISE RB AUU RTNELS PRST EXTLARLCIOALH, PRST RWWRSITE TR NEL
ICEAS. TNAT NE GAS ORT A FRRC-TEPWELEC PAO NAC YEEO NEL BILPEST RWIOIRO.
NEL VEEOEST ATTEOTIRO GAS AGAVEOEC: SNE UROFEC TR NEAL PRLE; AOC GAS
FLATEBDU TR NEL DOMUE BRL SAHIOF,--

“TNELE ALE KELH BEG WERWUE RB GNRP SR PDMN MAO YE SAIC. HRD ALE UDMVH IO
NAKIOF SDMN A PASTEL.”

“HES, SIL, I VORG I AP. IB I GELE TR FR TNLRDFN TNE GRLUC, I MRDUC ORT
PEET GITN A YETTEL. YDT I NAKE AUGAHS RYSELKEC, TNAT TNEH GNR ALE
FRRC-OATDLEC GNEO MNIUCLEO, ALE FRRC-OATDLEC GNEO TNEH FLRG DW; AOC NE
GAS AUGAHS TNE SGEETEST TEPWELEC, PRST FEOELRDS-NEALTEC YRH IO TNE
GRLUC.”

EUIJAYETN AUPRST STALEC AT NEL. “MAO TNIS YE PL. CALMH?” TNRDFNT SNE.

“NIS BATNEL GAS AO EXMEUUEOT PAO,” SAIC PLS. FALCIOEL.

“HES, PA’AP, TNAT NE GAS IOCEEC; AOC NIS SRO GIUU YE ZDST UIVE NIP--ZDST
AS ABBAYUE TR TNE WRRL.”

EUIJAYETN UISTEOEC, GROCELEC, CRDYTEC, AOC GAS IPWATIEOT BRL PRLE. PLS.
LEHORUCS MRDUC IOTELEST NEL RO OR RTNEL WRIOT. SNE LEUATEC TNE SDYZEMTS
RB TNE WIMTDLES, TNE CIPEOSIROS RB TNE LRRPS, AOC TNE WLIME RB TNE
BDLOITDLE IO KAIO. PL. FALCIOEL, NIFNUH APDSEC YH TNE VIOC RB BAPIUH
WLEZDCIME, TR GNIMN NE ATTLIYDTEC NEL EXMESSIKE MRPPEOCATIRO RB NEL
PASTEL, SRRO UEC AFAIO TR TNE SDYZEMT; AOC SNE CGEUT GITN EOELFH RO NIS
PAOH PELITS, AS TNEH WLRMEECEC TRFETNEL DW TNE FLEAT STAILMASE.

“NE IS TNE YEST UAOCURLC, AOC TNE YEST PASTEL,” SAIC SNE, “TNAT EKEL
UIKEC. ORT UIVE TNE GIUC HRDOF PEO ORG-A-CAHS, GNR TNIOV RB ORTNIOF YDT
TNEPSEUKES. TNELE IS ORT ROE RB NIS TEOAOTS RL SELKAOTS YDT GNAT GIUU
FIKE NIP A FRRC OAPE. SRPE WERWUE MAUU NIP WLRDC; YDT I AP SDLE I OEKEL
SAG AOHTNIOF RB IT. TR PH BAOMH, IT IS ROUH YEMADSE NE CRES ORT LATTUE
AGAH UIVE RTNEL HRDOF PEO.”

“IO GNAT AO APIAYUE UIFNT CRES TNIS WUAME NIP!” TNRDFNT EUIJAYETN.

“TNIS BIOE AMMRDOT RB NIP,” GNISWELEC NEL ADOT AS TNEH GAUVEC, “IS ORT
QDITE MROSISTEOT GITN NIS YENAKIRDL TR RDL WRRL BLIEOC.”

“WELNAWS GE PIFNT YE CEMEIKEC.”

“TNAT IS ORT KELH UIVEUH; RDL ADTNRLITH GAS TRR FRRC.”

RO LEAMNIOF TNE SWAMIRDS URYYH AYRKE, TNEH GELE SNRGO IOTR A KELH WLETTH
SITTIOF-LRRP, UATEUH BITTEC DW GITN FLEATEL EUEFAOME AOC UIFNTOESS TNAO
TNE AWALTPEOTS YEURG; AOC GELE IOBRLPEC TNAT IT GAS YDT ZDST CROE TR
FIKE WUEASDLE TR PISS CALMH, GNR NAC TAVEO A UIVIOF TR TNE LRRP, GNEO
UAST AT WEPYELUEH.

“NE IS MELTAIOUH A FRRC YLRTNEL,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, AS SNE GAUVEC TRGALCS
ROE RB TNE GIOCRGS.

PLS. LEHORUCS AOTIMIWATEC PISS CALMH’S CEUIFNT, GNEO SNE SNRDUC EOTEL
TNE LRRP. “AOC TNIS IS AUGAHS TNE GAH GITN NIP,” SNE ACCEC. “GNATEKEL
MAO FIKE NIS SISTEL AOH WUEASDLE, IS SDLE TR YE CROE IO A PRPEOT. TNELE
IS ORTNIOF NE GRDUC ORT CR BRL NEL.”

TNE WIMTDLE FAUUELH, AOC TGR RL TNLEE RB TNE WLIOMIWAU YEC-LRRPS, GELE
AUU TNAT LEPAIOEC TR YE SNRGO. IO TNE BRLPEL GELE PAOH FRRC WAIOTIOFS:
YDT EUIJAYETN VOEG ORTNIOF RB TNE ALT; AOC BLRP SDMN AS NAC YEEO AULEACH
KISIYUE YEURG, SNE NAC GIUUIOFUH TDLOEC TR URRV AT SRPE CLAGIOFS RB PISS
CALMH’S, IO MLAHROS, GNRSE SDYZEMTS GELE DSDAUUH PRLE IOTELESTIOF, AOC
AUSR PRLE IOTEUUIFIYUE.

IO TNE FAUUELH TNELE GELE PAOH BAPIUH WRLTLAITS, YDT TNEH MRDUC NAKE
UITTUE TR BIX TNE ATTEOTIRO RB A STLAOFEL. EUIJAYETN GAUVEC RO IO QDEST
RB TNE ROUH BAME GNRSE BEATDLES GRDUC YE VORGO TR NEL. AT UAST IT
ALLESTEC NEL--AOC SNE YENEUC A STLIVIOF LESEPYUAOME RB PL. CALMH, GITN
SDMN A SPIUE RKEL TNE BAME, AS SNE LEPEPYELEC TR NAKE SRPETIPES SEEO,
GNEO NE URRVEC AT NEL. SNE STRRC SEKELAU PIODTES YEBRLE TNE WIMTDLE, IO
EALOEST MROTEPWUATIRO, AOC LETDLOEC TR IT AFAIO YEBRLE TNEH QDITTEC TNE
FAUUELH. PLS. LEHORUCS IOBRLPEC TNEP, TNAT IT NAC YEEO TAVEO IO NIS
BATNEL’S UIBETIPE.

TNELE GAS MELTAIOUH AT TNIS PRPEOT, IO EUIJAYETN’S PIOC, A PRLE FEOTUE
SEOSATIRO TRGALCS TNE RLIFIOAU TNAO SNE NAC EKEL BEUT IO TNE NEIFNT RB
TNEIL AMQDAIOTAOME. TNE MRPPEOCATIRO YESTRGEC RO NIP YH PLS. LEHORUCS
GAS RB OR TLIBUIOF OATDLE. GNAT WLAISE IS PRLE KAUDAYUE TNAO TNE WLAISE
RB AO IOTEUUIFEOT SELKAOT? AS A YLRTNEL, A UAOCURLC, A PASTEL, SNE
MROSICELEC NRG PAOH WERWUE’S NAWWIOESS GELE IO NIS FDALCIAOSNIW! NRG
PDMN RB WUEASDLE RL WAIO IT GAS IO NIS WRGEL TR YESTRG! NRG PDMN RB FRRC
RL EKIU PDST YE CROE YH NIP! EKELH ICEA TNAT NAC YEEO YLRDFNT BRLGALC YH
TNE NRDSEVEEWEL GAS BAKRDLAYUE TR NIS MNALAMTEL; AOC AS SNE STRRC YEBRLE
TNE MAOKAS, RO GNIMN NE GAS LEWLESEOTEC, AOC BIXEC NIS EHES DWRO
NELSEUB, SNE TNRDFNT RB NIS LEFALC GITN A CEEWEL SEOTIPEOT RB FLATITDCE
TNAO IT NAC EKEL LAISEC YEBRLE: SNE LEPEPYELEC ITS GALPTN, AOC SRBTEOEC
ITS IPWLRWLIETH RB EXWLESSIRO.

GNEO AUU RB TNE NRDSE TNAT GAS RWEO TR FEOELAU IOSWEMTIRO NAC YEEO SEEO,
TNEH LETDLOEC CRGO STAILS; AOC, TAVIOF UEAKE RB TNE NRDSEVEEWEL, GELE
MROSIFOEC RKEL TR TNE FALCEOEL, GNR PET TNEP AT TNE NAUU CRRL.

AS TNEH GAUVEC AMLRSS TNE UAGO TRGALCS TNE LIKEL, EUIJAYETN TDLOEC YAMV
TR URRV AFAIO; NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT STRWWEC AUSR; AOC GNIUE TNE BRLPEL GAS
MROZEMTDLIOF AS TR TNE CATE RB TNE YDIUCIOF, TNE RGOEL RB IT NIPSEUB
SDCCEOUH MAPE BRLGALC BLRP TNE LRAC GNIMN UEC YENIOC IT TR TNE STAYUES.

TNEH GELE GITNIO TGEOTH HALCS RB EAMN RTNEL; AOC SR AYLDWT GAS NIS
AWWEALAOME, TNAT IT GAS IPWRSSIYUE TR AKRIC NIS SIFNT. TNEIL EHES
IOSTAOTUH PET, AOC TNE MNEEVS RB EAMN GELE RKELSWLEAC GITN TNE CEEWEST
YUDSN. NE AYSRUDTEUH STALTEC, AOC BRL A PRPEOT SEEPEC IPPRKAYUE BLRP
SDLWLISE; YDT SNRLTUH LEMRKELIOF NIPSEUB, ACKAOMEC TRGALCS TNE WALTH,
AOC SWRVE TR EUIJAYETN, IB ORT IO TELPS RB WELBEMT MRPWRSDLE, AT UEAST
RB WELBEMT MIKIUITH.

SNE NAC IOSTIOMTIKEUH TDLOEC AGAH; YDT STRWWIOF RO NIS AWWLRAMN,
LEMEIKEC NIS MRPWUIPEOTS GITN AO EPYALLASSPEOT IPWRSSIYUE TR YE
RKELMRPE. NAC NIS BILST AWWEALAOME, RL NIS LESEPYUAOME TR TNE WIMTDLE
TNEH NAC ZDST YEEO EXAPIOIOF, YEEO IOSDBBIMIEOT TR ASSDLE TNE RTNEL TGR
TNAT TNEH ORG SAG PL. CALMH, TNE FALCEOEL’S EXWLESSIRO RB SDLWLISE, RO
YENRUCIOF NIS PASTEL, PDST IPPECIATEUH NAKE TRUC IT. TNEH STRRC A UITTUE
AURRB GNIUE NE GAS TAUVIOF TR TNEIL OIEME, GNR, ASTROISNEC AOC MROBDSEC,
SMALMEUH CALEC UIBT NEL EHES TR NIS BAME, AOC VOEG ORT GNAT AOSGEL SNE
LETDLOEC TR NIS MIKIU IOQDILIES ABTEL NEL BAPIUH. APAJEC AT TNE
AUTELATIRO RB NIS PAOOEL SIOME TNEH UAST WALTEC, EKELH SEOTEOME TNAT NE
DTTELEC GAS IOMLEASIOF NEL EPYALLASSPEOT; AOC EKELH ICEA RB TNE
IPWLRWLIETH RB NEL YEIOF BRDOC TNELE LEMDLLIOF TR NEL PIOC, TNE BEG
PIODTES IO GNIMN TNEH MROTIODEC TRFETNEL GELE SRPE RB TNE PRST
DOMRPBRLTAYUE RB NEL UIBE. ORL CIC NE SEEP PDMN PRLE AT EASE; GNEO NE
SWRVE, NIS AMMEOT NAC OROE RB ITS DSDAU SECATEOESS; AOC NE LEWEATEC NIS
IOQDILIES AS TR TNE TIPE RB NEL NAKIOF UEBT UROFYRDLO, AOC RB NEL STAH
IO CELYHSNILE, SR RBTEO, AOC IO SR NDLLIEC A GAH, AS WUAIOUH SWRVE TNE
CISTLAMTIRO RB NIS TNRDFNTS.

AT UEOFTN, EKELH ICEA SEEPEC TR BAIU NIP; AOC ABTEL STAOCIOF A BEG
PRPEOTS GITNRDT SAHIOF A GRLC, NE SDCCEOUH LEMRUUEMTEC NIPSEUB, AOC TRRV
UEAKE.

TNE RTNELS TNEO ZRIOEC NEL, AOC EXWLESSEC TNEIL ACPILATIRO RB NIS
BIFDLE; YDT EUIJAYETN NEALC ORT A GRLC, AOC, GNRUUH EOFLRSSEC YH NEL RGO
BEEUIOFS, BRUURGEC TNEP IO SIUEOME. SNE GAS RKELWRGELEC YH SNAPE AOC
KEXATIRO. NEL MRPIOF TNELE GAS TNE PRST DOBRLTDOATE, TNE PRST IUU-ZDCFEC
TNIOF IO TNE GRLUC! NRG STLAOFE PDST IT AWWEAL TR NIP! IO GNAT A
CISFLAMEBDU UIFNT PIFNT IT ORT STLIVE SR KAIO A PAO! IT PIFNT SEEP AS IB
SNE NAC WDLWRSEUH TNLRGO NELSEUB IO NIS GAH AFAIO! RN! GNH CIC SNE MRPE?
RL, GNH CIC NE TNDS MRPE A CAH YEBRLE NE GAS EXWEMTEC? NAC TNEH YEEO
ROUH TEO PIODTES SRROEL, TNEH SNRDUC NAKE YEEO YEHROC TNE LEAMN RB NIS
CISMLIPIOATIRO; BRL IT GAS WUAIO TNAT NE GAS TNAT PRPEOT ALLIKEC, TNAT
PRPEOT AUIFNTEC BLRP NIS NRLSE RL NIS MALLIAFE. SNE YUDSNEC AFAIO AOC
AFAIO RKEL TNE WELKELSEOESS RB TNE PEETIOF. AOC NIS YENAKIRDL, SR
STLIVIOFUH AUTELEC,--GNAT MRDUC IT PEAO? TNAT NE SNRDUC EKEO SWEAV TR
NEL GAS APAJIOF!--YDT TR SWEAV GITN SDMN MIKIUITH, TR IOQDILE ABTEL NEL
BAPIUH! OEKEL IO NEL UIBE NAC SNE SEEO NIS PAOOELS SR UITTUE CIFOIBIEC,
OEKEL NAC NE SWRVEO GITN SDMN FEOTUEOESS AS RO TNIS DOEXWEMTEC PEETIOF.
GNAT A MROTLAST CIC IT RBBEL TR NIS UAST ACCLESS IO LRSIOFS WALV, GNEO
NE WDT NIS UETTEL IOTR NEL NAOC! SNE VOEG ORT GNAT TR TNIOV, RL NRG TR
AMMRDOT BRL IT.

TNEH NAC ORG EOTELEC A YEADTIBDU GAUV YH TNE SICE RB TNE GATEL, AOC
EKELH STEW GAS YLIOFIOF BRLGALC A ORYUEL BAUU RB FLRDOC, RL A BIOEL
LEAMN RB TNE GRRCS TR GNIMN TNEH GELE AWWLRAMNIOF: YDT IT GAS SRPE TIPE
YEBRLE EUIJAYETN GAS SEOSIYUE RB AOH RB IT; AOC, TNRDFN SNE AOSGELEC
PEMNAOIMAUUH TR TNE LEWEATEC AWWEAUS RB NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT, AOC SEEPEC
TR CILEMT NEL EHES TR SDMN RYZEMTS AS TNEH WRIOTEC RDT, SNE
CISTIOFDISNEC OR WALT RB TNE SMEOE. NEL TNRDFNTS GELE AUU BIXEC RO TNAT
ROE SWRT RB WEPYELUEH NRDSE, GNIMNEKEL IT PIFNT YE, GNELE PL. CALMH TNEO
GAS. SNE UROFEC TR VORG GNAT AT TNAT PRPEOT GAS WASSIOF IO NIS PIOC; IO
GNAT PAOOEL NE TNRDFNT RB NEL, AOC GNETNEL, IO CEBIAOME RB EKELHTNIOF,
SNE GAS STIUU CEAL TR NIP. WELNAWS NE NAC YEEO MIKIU ROUH YEMADSE NE
BEUT NIPSEUB AT EASE; HET TNELE NAC YEEO _TNAT_ IO NIS KRIME, GNIMN GAS
ORT UIVE EASE. GNETNEL NE NAC BEUT PRLE RB WAIO RL RB WUEASDLE IO SEEIOF
NEL, SNE MRDUC ORT TEUU, YDT NE MELTAIOUH NAC ORT SEEO NEL GITN
MRPWRSDLE.

AT UEOFTN, NRGEKEL, TNE LEPALVS RB NEL MRPWAOIROS RO NEL AYSEOME RB PIOC
LRDSEC NEL, AOC SNE BEUT TNE OEMESSITH RB AWWEALIOF PRLE UIVE NELSEUB.

TNEH EOTELEC TNE GRRCS, AOC, YICCIOF ACIED TR TNE LIKEL BRL A GNIUE,
ASMEOCEC SRPE RB TNE NIFNEL FLRDOCS; GNEOME, IO SWRTS GNELE TNE RWEOIOF
RB TNE TLEES FAKE TNE EHE WRGEL TR GAOCEL, GELE PAOH MNALPIOF KIEGS RB
TNE KAUUEH, TNE RWWRSITE NIUUS, GITN TNE UROF LAOFE RB GRRCS
RKELSWLEACIOF PAOH, AOC RMMASIROAUUH WALT RB TNE STLEAP. PL. FALCIOEL
EXWLESSEC A GISN RB FRIOF LRDOC TNE GNRUE WALV, YDT BEALEC IT PIFNT YE
YEHROC A GAUV. GITN A TLIDPWNAOT SPIUE, TNEH GELE TRUC, TNAT IT GAS TEO
PIUES LRDOC. IT SETTUEC TNE PATTEL; AOC TNEH WDLSDEC TNE AMMDSTRPEC
MILMDIT; GNIMN YLRDFNT TNEP AFAIO, ABTEL SRPE TIPE, IO A CESMEOT APROF
NAOFIOF GRRCS, TR TNE ECFE RB TNE GATEL, AOC ROE RB ITS OALLRGEST WALTS.
TNEH MLRSSEC IT YH A SIPWUE YLICFE, IO MNALAMTEL GITN TNE FEOELAU AIL RB
TNE SMEOE: IT GAS A SWRT UESS ACRLOEC TNAO AOH TNEH NAC HET KISITEC; AOC
TNE KAUUEH, NELE MROTLAMTEC IOTR A FUEO, AUURGEC LRRP ROUH BRL TNE
STLEAP, AOC A OALLRG GAUV APICST TNE LRDFN MRWWIME-GRRC GNIMN YRLCELEC
IT. EUIJAYETN UROFEC TR EXWURLE ITS GIOCIOFS; YDT GNEO TNEH NAC MLRSSEC
TNE YLICFE, AOC WELMEIKEC TNEIL CISTAOME BLRP TNE NRDSE, PLS. FALCIOEL,
GNR GAS ORT A FLEAT GAUVEL, MRDUC FR OR BALTNEL, AOC TNRDFNT ROUH RB
LETDLOIOF TR TNE MALLIAFE AS QDIMVUH AS WRSSIYUE. NEL OIEME GAS,
TNELEBRLE, RYUIFEC TR SDYPIT, AOC TNEH TRRV TNEIL GAH TRGALCS TNE NRDSE
RO TNE RWWRSITE SICE RB TNE LIKEL, IO TNE OEALEST CILEMTIRO; YDT TNEIL
WLRFLESS GAS SURG, BRL PL. FALCIOEL, TNRDFN SEUCRP AYUE TR IOCDUFE TNE
TASTE, GAS KELH BROC RB BISNIOF, AOC GAS SR PDMN EOFAFEC IO GATMNIOF TNE
RMMASIROAU AWWEALAOME RB SRPE TLRDT IO TNE GATEL, AOC TAUVIOF TR TNE PAO
AYRDT TNEP, TNAT NE ACKAOMEC YDT UITTUE. GNIUST GAOCELIOF RO IO TNIS
SURG PAOOEL, TNEH GELE AFAIO SDLWLISEC, AOC EUIJAYETN’S ASTROISNPEOT GAS
QDITE EQDAU TR GNAT IT NAC YEEO AT BILST, YH TNE SIFNT RB PL. CALMH
AWWLRAMNIOF TNEP, AOC AT OR FLEAT CISTAOME. TNE GAUV YEIOF NELE UESS
SNEUTELEC TNAO RO TNE RTNEL SICE, AUURGEC TNEP TR SEE NIP YEBRLE TNEH
PET. EUIJAYETN, NRGEKEL ASTROISNEC, GAS AT UEAST PRLE WLEWALEC BRL AO
IOTELKIEG TNAO YEBRLE, AOC LESRUKEC TR AWWEAL AOC TR SWEAV GITN
MAUPOESS, IB NE LEAUUH IOTEOCEC TR PEET TNEP. BRL A BEG PRPEOTS, IOCEEC,
SNE BEUT TNAT NE GRDUC WLRYAYUH STLIVE IOTR SRPE RTNEL WATN. TNE ICEA
UASTEC GNIUE A TDLOIOF IO TNE GAUV MROMEAUEC NIP BLRP TNEIL KIEG; TNE
TDLOIOF WAST, NE GAS IPPECIATEUH YEBRLE TNEP. GITN A FUAOME SNE SAG TNAT
NE NAC URST OROE RB NIS LEMEOT MIKIUITH; AOC, TR IPITATE NIS WRUITEOESS,
SNE YEFAO AS TNEH PET TR ACPILE TNE YEADTH RB TNE WUAME; YDT SNE NAC ORT
FRT YEHROC TNE GRLCS “CEUIFNTBDU,” AOC “MNALPIOF,” GNEO SRPE DOUDMVH
LEMRUUEMTIROS RYTLDCEC, AOC SNE BAOMIEC TNAT WLAISE RB WEPYELUEH BLRP
NEL PIFNT YE PISMNIEKRDSUH MROSTLDEC. NEL MRURDL MNAOFEC, AOC SNE SAIC
OR PRLE.

PLS. FALCIOEL GAS STAOCIOF A UITTUE YENIOC; AOC RO NEL WADSIOF, NE ASVEC
NEL IB SNE GRDUC CR NIP TNE NRORDL RB IOTLRCDMIOF NIP TR NEL BLIEOCS.
TNIS GAS A STLRVE RB MIKIUITH BRL GNIMN SNE GAS QDITE DOWLEWALEC; AOC
SNE MRDUC NALCUH SDWWLESS A SPIUE AT NIS YEIOF ORG SEEVIOF TNE
AMQDAIOTAOME RB SRPE RB TNRSE KELH WERWUE, AFAIOST GNRP NIS WLICE NAC
LEKRUTEC, IO NIS RBBEL TR NELSEUB. “GNAT GIUU YE NIS SDLWLISE,” TNRDFNT
SNE, “GNEO NE VORGS GNR TNEH ALE! NE TAVES TNEP ORG BRL WERWUE RB
BASNIRO.”

TNE IOTLRCDMTIRO, NRGEKEL, GAS IPPECIATEUH PACE; AOC AS SNE OAPEC TNEIL
LEUATIROSNIW TR NELSEUB, SNE STRUE A SUH URRV AT NIP, TR SEE NRG NE YRLE
IT; AOC GAS ORT GITNRDT TNE EXWEMTATIRO RB NIS CEMAPWIOF AS BAST AS NE
MRDUC BLRP SDMN CISFLAMEBDU MRPWAOIROS. TNAT NE GAS _SDLWLISEC_ YH TNE
MROOEMTIRO GAS EKICEOT: NE SDSTAIOEC IT, NRGEKEL, GITN BRLTITDCE: AOC,
SR BAL BLRP FRIOF AGAH, TDLOEC YAMV GITN TNEP, AOC EOTELEC IOTR
MROKELSATIRO GITN PL. FALCIOEL. EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT YDT YE WUEASEC,
MRDUC ORT YDT TLIDPWN. IT GAS MROSRUIOF TNAT NE SNRDUC VORG SNE NAC SRPE
LEUATIROS BRL GNRP TNELE GAS OR OEEC TR YUDSN. SNE UISTEOEC PRST
ATTEOTIKEUH TR AUU TNAT WASSEC YETGEEO TNEP, AOC FURLIEC IO EKELH
EXWLESSIRO, EKELH SEOTEOME RB NEL DOMUE, GNIMN PALVEC NIS IOTEUUIFEOME,
NIS TASTE, RL NIS FRRC PAOOELS.

TNE MROKELSATIRO SRRO TDLOEC DWRO BISNIOF; AOC SNE NEALC PL. CALMH
IOKITE NIP, GITN TNE FLEATEST MIKIUITH, TR BISN TNELE AS RBTEO AS NE
MNRSE, GNIUE NE MROTIODEC IO TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC, RBBELIOF AT TNE SAPE
TIPE TR SDWWUH NIP GITN BISNIOF TAMVUE, AOC WRIOTIOF RDT TNRSE WALTS RB
TNE STLEAP GNELE TNELE GAS DSDAUUH PRST SWRLT. PLS. FALCIOEL, GNR GAS
GAUVIOF ALP IO ALP GITN EUIJAYETN, FAKE NEL A URRV EXWLESSIKE RB NEL
GROCEL. EUIJAYETN SAIC ORTNIOF, YDT IT FLATIBIEC NEL EXMEECIOFUH; TNE
MRPWUIPEOT PDST YE AUU BRL NELSEUB. NEL ASTROISNPEOT, NRGEKEL, GAS
EXTLEPE; AOC MROTIODAUUH GAS SNE LEWEATIOF, “GNH IS NE SR AUTELEC? BLRP
GNAT MAO IT WLRMEEC? IT MAOORT YE BRL _PE_, IT MAOORT YE BRL _PH_ SAVE
TNAT NIS PAOOELS ALE TNDS SRBTEOEC. PH LEWLRRBS AT NDOSBRLC MRDUC ORT
GRLV SDMN A MNAOFE AS TNIS. IT IS IPWRSSIYUE TNAT NE SNRDUC STIUU URKE
PE.”

ABTEL GAUVIOF SRPE TIPE IO TNIS GAH, TNE TGR UACIES IO BLROT, TNE TGR
FEOTUEPEO YENIOC, RO LESDPIOF TNEIL WUAMES, ABTEL CESMEOCIOF TR TNE
YLIOV RB TNE LIKEL BRL TNE YETTEL IOSWEMTIRO RB SRPE MDLIRDS
GATEL-WUAOT, TNELE MNAOMEC TR YE A UITTUE AUTELATIRO. IT RLIFIOATEC IO
PLS. FALCIOEL, GNR, BATIFDEC YH TNE EXELMISE RB TNE PRLOIOF, BRDOC
EUIJAYETN’S ALP IOACEQDATE TR NEL SDWWRLT, AOC MROSEQDEOTUH WLEBELLEC
NEL NDSYAOC’S. PL. CALMH TRRV NEL WUAME YH NEL OIEME, AOC TNEH GAUVEC RO
TRFETNEL. ABTEL A SNRLT SIUEOME TNE UACH BILST SWRVE. SNE GISNEC NIP TR
VORG TNAT SNE NAC YEEO ASSDLEC RB NIS AYSEOME YEBRLE SNE MAPE TR TNE
WUAME, AOC AMMRLCIOFUH YEFAO YH RYSELKIOF, TNAT NIS ALLIKAU NAC YEEO
KELH DOEXWEMTEC--“BRL HRDL NRDSEVEEWEL,” SNE ACCEC, “IOBRLPEC DS TNAT
HRD GRDUC MELTAIOUH ORT YE NELE TIUU TR-PRLLRG; AOC, IOCEEC, YEBRLE GE
UEBT YAVEGEUU, GE DOCELSTRRC TNAT HRD GELE ORT IPPECIATEUH EXWEMTEC IO
TNE MRDOTLH.” NE AMVORGUECFEC TNE TLDTN RB IT AUU; AOC SAIC TNAT
YDSIOESS GITN NIS STEGALC NAC RMMASIROEC NIS MRPIOF BRLGALC A BEG NRDLS
YEBRLE TNE LEST RB TNE WALTH GITN GNRP NE NAC YEEO TLAKEUUIOF. “TNEH
GIUU ZRIO PE EALUH TR-PRLLRG,” NE MROTIODEC, “AOC APROF TNEP ALE SRPE
GNR GIUU MUAIP AO AMQDAIOTAOME GITN HRD,--PL. YIOFUEH AOC NIS SISTELS.”

EUIJAYETN AOSGELEC ROUH YH A SUIFNT YRG. NEL TNRDFNTS GELE IOSTAOTUH
CLIKEO YAMV TR TNE TIPE GNEO PL. YIOFUEH’S OAPE NAC YEEO UAST PEOTIROEC
YETGEEO TNEP; AOC IB SNE PIFNT ZDCFE BLRP NIS MRPWUEXIRO, _NIS_ PIOC GAS
ORT KELH CIBBELEOTUH EOFAFEC.

“TNELE IS AUSR ROE RTNEL WELSRO IO TNE WALTH,” NE MROTIODEC ABTEL A
WADSE, “GNR PRLE WALTIMDUALUH GISNES TR YE VORGO TR HRD. GIUU HRD AUURG
PE, RL CR I ASV TRR PDMN, TR IOTLRCDME PH SISTEL TR HRDL AMQDAIOTAOME
CDLIOF HRDL STAH AT UAPYTRO?”

TNE SDLWLISE RB SDMN AO AWWUIMATIRO GAS FLEAT IOCEEC; IT GAS TRR FLEAT
BRL NEL TR VORG IO GNAT PAOOEL SNE AMMECEC TR IT. SNE IPPECIATEUH BEUT
TNAT GNATEKEL CESILE PISS CALMH PIFNT NAKE RB YEIOF AMQDAIOTEC GITN NEL,
PDST YE TNE GRLV RB NEL YLRTNEL, AOC GITNRDT URRVIOF BALTNEL, IT GAS
SATISBAMTRLH; IT GAS FLATIBHIOF TR VORG TNAT NIS LESEOTPEOT NAC ORT PACE
NIP TNIOV LEAUUH IUU RB NEL.

TNEH ORG GAUVEC RO IO SIUEOME; EAMN RB TNEP CEEW IO TNRDFNT. EUIJAYETN
GAS ORT MRPBRLTAYUE; TNAT GAS IPWRSSIYUE; YDT SNE GAS BUATTELEC AOC
WUEASEC. NIS GISN RB IOTLRCDMIOF NIS SISTEL TR NEL GAS A MRPWUIPEOT RB
TNE NIFNEST VIOC. TNEH SRRO RDTSTLIWWEC TNE RTNELS; AOC GNEO TNEH NAC
LEAMNEC TNE MALLIAFE, PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL GELE NAUB A QDALTEL RB A
PIUE YENIOC.

NE TNEO ASVEC NEL TR GAUV IOTR TNE NRDSE--YDT SNE CEMUALEC NELSEUB ORT
TILEC, AOC TNEH STRRC TRFETNEL RO TNE UAGO. AT SDMN A TIPE PDMN PIFNT
NAKE YEEO SAIC, AOC SIUEOME GAS KELH AGVGALC. SNE GAOTEC TR TAUV, YDT
TNELE SEEPEC AO EPYALFR RO EKELH SDYZEMT. AT UAST SNE LEMRUUEMTEC TNAT
SNE NAC YEEO TLAKEUUIOF, AOC TNEH TAUVEC RB PATURMV AOC CRKECAUE GITN
FLEAT WELSEKELAOME. HET TIPE AOC NEL ADOT PRKEC SURGUH--AOC NEL WATIEOME
AOC NEL ICEAS GELE OEALUH GRLO RDT YEBRLE TNE _TNTE-X-TNTE_ GAS RKEL.

RO PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL’S MRPIOF DW TNEH GELE AUU WLESSEC TR FR IOTR
