TNE NRDSE AOC TAVE SRPE LEBLESNPEOT; YDT TNIS GAS CEMUIOEC, AOC TNEH
WALTEC RO EAMN SICE GITN TNE DTPRST WRUITEOESS. PL. CALMH NAOCEC TNE
UACIES IOTR TNE MALLIAFE; AOC GNEO IT CLRKE RBB, EUIJAYETN SAG NIP
GAUVIOF SURGUH TRGALCS TNE NRDSE.

TNE RYSELKATIROS RB NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT ORG YEFAO; AOC EAMN RB TNEP
WLRORDOMEC NIP TR YE IOBIOITEUH SDWELIRL TR AOHTNIOF TNEH NAC EXWEMTEC.

“NE IS WELBEMTUH GEUU-YENAKEC, WRUITE, AOC DOASSDPIOF,” SAIC NEL DOMUE.

“TNELE _IS_ SRPETNIOF A UITTUE STATEUH IO NIP, TR YE SDLE,” LEWUIEC NEL
ADOT; “YDT IT IS MROBIOEC TR NIS AIL, AOC IS ORT DOYEMRPIOF. I MAO ORG
SAH GITN TNE NRDSEVEEWEL, TNAT TNRDFN SRPE WERWUE PAH MAUU NIP WLRDC,
_I_ NAKE SEEO ORTNIOF RB IT.”

“I GAS OEKEL PRLE SDLWLISEC TNAO YH NIS YENAKIRDL TR DS. IT GAS PRLE
TNAO MIKIU; IT GAS LEAUUH ATTEOTIKE; AOC TNELE GAS OR OEMESSITH BRL SDMN
ATTEOTIRO. NIS AMQDAIOTAOME GITN EUIJAYETN GAS KELH TLIBUIOF.”

“TR YE SDLE, UIJJH,” SAIC NEL ADOT, “NE IS ORT SR NAOCSRPE AS GIMVNAP;
RL LATNEL NE NAS ORT GIMVNAP’S MRDOTEOAOME, BRL NIS BEATDLES ALE
WELBEMTUH FRRC. YDT NRG MAPE HRD TR TEUU DS TNAT NE GAS SR
CISAFLEEAYUE?”

EUIJAYETN EXMDSEC NELSEUB AS GEUU AS SNE MRDUC: SAIC TNAT SNE NAC UIVEC
NIP YETTEL GNEO TNEH PET IO VEOT TNAO YEBRLE, AOC TNAT SNE NAC OEKEL
SEEO NIP SR WUEASAOT AS TNIS PRLOIOF.

“YDT WELNAWS NE PAH YE A UITTUE GNIPSIMAU IO NIS MIKIUITIES,” LEWUIEC
NEL DOMUE. “HRDL FLEAT PEO RBTEO ALE; AOC TNELEBRLE I SNAUU ORT TAVE NIP
AT NIS GRLC AYRDT BISNIOF, AS NE PIFNT MNAOFE NIS PIOC AORTNEL CAH, AOC
GALO PE RBB NIS FLRDOCS.”

EUIJAYETN BEUT TNAT TNEH NAC EOTILEUH PISTAVEO NIS MNALAMTEL, YDT SAIC
ORTNIOF.

“BLRP GNAT GE NAKE SEEO RB NIP,” MROTIODEC PLS. FALCIOEL, “I LEAUUH
SNRDUC ORT NAKE TNRDFNT TNAT NE MRDUC NAKE YENAKEC IO SR MLDEU A GAH YH
AOHYRCH AS NE NAS CROE YH WRRL GIMVNAP. NE NAS ORT AO IUU-OATDLEC URRV.
RO TNE MROTLALH, TNELE IS SRPETNIOF WUEASIOF AYRDT NIS PRDTN GNEO NE
SWEAVS. AOC TNELE IS SRPETNIOF RB CIFOITH IO NIS MRDOTEOAOME, TNAT GRDUC
ORT FIKE ROE AO DOBAKRDLAYUE ICEA RB NIS NEALT. YDT, TR YE SDLE, TNE
FRRC UACH GNR SNRGEC DS TNE NRDSE CIC FIKE NIP A PRST BUAPIOF MNALAMTEL!
I MRDUC NALCUH NEUW UADFNIOF AURDC SRPETIPES. YDT NE IS A UIYELAU
PASTEL, I SDWWRSE, AOC _TNAT_, IO TNE EHE RB A SELKAOT, MRPWLENEOCS
EKELH KILTDE.”

EUIJAYETN NELE BEUT NELSEUB MAUUEC RO TR SAH SRPETNIOF IO KIOCIMATIRO RB
NIS YENAKIRDL TR GIMVNAP; AOC, TNELEBRLE, FAKE TNEP TR DOCELSTAOC, IO AS
FDALCEC A PAOOEL AS SNE MRDUC, TNAT YH GNAT SNE NAC NEALC BLRP NIS
LEUATIROS IO VEOT, NIS AMTIROS GELE MAWAYUE RB A KELH CIBBELEOT
MROSTLDMTIRO; AOC TNAT NIS MNALAMTEL GAS YH OR PEAOS SR BADUTH, ORL
GIMVNAP’S SR APIAYUE, AS TNEH NAC YEEO MROSICELEC IO NELTBRLCSNILE. IO
MROBILPATIRO RB TNIS, SNE LEUATEC TNE WALTIMDUALS RB AUU TNE WEMDOIALH
TLAOSAMTIROS IO GNIMN TNEH NAC YEEO MROOEMTEC, GITNRDT AMTDAUUH OAPIOF
NEL ADTNRLITH, YDT STATIOF IT TR YE SDMN AS PIFNT YE LEUIEC RO.

PLS. FALCIOEL GAS SDLWLISEC AOC MROMELOEC: YDT AS TNEH GELE ORG
AWWLRAMNIOF TNE SMEOE RB NEL BRLPEL WUEASDLES, EKELH ICEA FAKE GAH TR
TNE MNALP RB LEMRUUEMTIRO; AOC SNE GAS TRR PDMN EOFAFEC IO WRIOTIOF RDT
TR NEL NDSYAOC AUU TNE IOTELESTIOF SWRTS IO ITS EOKILROS, TR TNIOV RB
AOHTNIOF EUSE. BATIFDEC AS SNE NAC YEEO YH TNE PRLOIOF’S GAUV, TNEH NAC
OR SRROEL CIOEC TNAO SNE SET RBB AFAIO IO QDEST RB NEL BRLPEL
AMQDAIOTAOME, AOC TNE EKEOIOF GAS SWEOT IO TNE SATISBAMTIROS RB AO
IOTELMRDLSE LEOEGEC ABTEL PAOH HEALS’ CISMROTIODAOME.

TNE RMMDLLEOMES RB TNE CAH GELE TRR BDUU RB IOTELEST TR UEAKE EUIJAYETN
PDMN ATTEOTIRO BRL AOH RB TNESE OEG BLIEOCS; AOC SNE MRDUC CR ORTNIOF
YDT TNIOV, AOC TNIOV GITN GROCEL, RB PL. CALMH’S MIKIUITH, AOC, AYRKE
AUU, RB NIS GISNIOF NEL TR YE AMQDAIOTEC GITN NIS SISTEL.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XUIK.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN NAC SETTUEC IT TNAT PL. CALMH GRDUC YLIOF NIS SISTEL TR KISIT
NEL TNE KELH CAH ABTEL NEL LEAMNIOF WEPYELUEH; AOC GAS, MROSEQDEOTUH,
LESRUKEC ORT TR YE RDT RB SIFNT RB TNE IOO TNE GNRUE RB TNAT PRLOIOF.
YDT NEL MROMUDSIRO GAS BAUSE; BRL RO TNE KELH PRLOIOF ABTEL TNEIL RGO
ALLIKAU AT UAPYTRO TNESE KISITRLS MAPE. TNEH NAC YEEO GAUVIOF AYRDT TNE
WUAME GITN SRPE RB TNEIL OEG BLIEOCS, AOC GELE ZDST LETDLOEC TR TNE IOO
TR CLESS TNEPSEUKES BRL CIOIOF GITN TNE SAPE BAPIUH, GNEO TNE SRDOC RB A
MALLIAFE CLEG TNEP TR A GIOCRG, AOC TNEH SAG A FEOTUEPAO AOC UACH IO A
MDLLIMUE CLIKIOF DW TNE STLEET. EUIJAYETN, IPPECIATEUH LEMRFOIJIOF TNE
UIKELH, FDESSEC GNAT IT PEAOT, AOC IPWALTEC OR SPAUU CEFLEE RB SDLWLISE
TR NEL LEUATIROS, YH AMQDAIOTIOF TNEP GITN TNE NRORDL GNIMN SNE
EXWEMTEC. NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT GELE AUU APAJEPEOT; AOC TNE EPYALLASSPEOT
RB NEL PAOOEL AS SNE SWRVE, ZRIOEC TR TNE MILMDPSTAOME ITSEUB, AOC PAOH
RB TNE MILMDPSTAOMES RB TNE WLEMECIOF CAH, RWEOEC TR TNEP A OEG ICEA RO
TNE YDSIOESS. ORTNIOF NAC EKEL SDFFESTEC IT YEBRLE, YDT TNEH ORG BEUT
TNAT TNELE GAS OR RTNEL GAH RB AMMRDOTIOF BRL SDMN ATTEOTIROS BLRP SDMN
A QDALTEL TNAO YH SDWWRSIOF A WALTIAUITH BRL TNEIL OIEME. GNIUE TNESE
OEGUH-YRLO ORTIROS GELE WASSIOF IO TNEIL NEACS, TNE WELTDLYATIRO RB
EUIJAYETN’S BEEUIOFS GAS EKELH PRPEOT IOMLEASIOF. SNE GAS QDITE APAJEC
AT NEL RGO CISMRPWRSDLE; YDT, APROFST RTNEL MADSES RB CISQDIET, SNE
CLEACEC UEST TNE WALTIAUITH RB TNE YLRTNEL SNRDUC NAKE SAIC TRR PDMN IO
NEL BAKRDL; AOC, PRLE TNAO MRPPROUH AOXIRDS TR WUEASE, SNE OATDLAUUH
SDSWEMTEC TNAT EKELH WRGEL RB WUEASIOF GRDUC BAIU NEL.

SNE LETLEATEC BLRP TNE GIOCRG, BEALBDU RB YEIOF SEEO; AOC AS SNE GAUVEC
DW AOC CRGO TNE LRRP, EOCEAKRDLIOF TR MRPWRSE NELSEUB, SAG SDMN URRVS RB
IOQDILIOF SDLWLISE IO NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT AS PACE EKELHTNIOF GRLSE.

PISS CALMH AOC NEL YLRTNEL AWWEALEC, AOC TNIS BRLPICAYUE IOTLRCDMTIRO
TRRV WUAME. GITN ASTROISNPEOT CIC EUIJAYETN SEE TNAT NEL OEG
AMQDAIOTAOME GAS AT UEAST AS PDMN EPYALLASSEC AS NELSEUB. SIOME NEL
YEIOF AT UAPYTRO, SNE NAC NEALC TNAT PISS CALMH GAS EXMEECIOFUH WLRDC;
YDT TNE RYSELKATIRO RB A KELH BEG PIODTES MROKIOMEC NEL TNAT SNE GAS
ROUH EXMEECIOFUH SNH. SNE BRDOC IT CIBBIMDUT TR RYTAIO EKEO A GRLC BLRP
NEL YEHROC A PRORSHUUAYUE.

PISS CALMH GAS TAUU, AOC RO A UALFEL SMAUE TNAO EUIJAYETN; AOC, TNRDFN
UITTUE PRLE TNAO SIXTEEO, NEL BIFDLE GAS BRLPEC, AOC NEL AWWEALAOME
GRPAOUH AOC FLAMEBDU. SNE GAS UESS NAOCSRPE TNAO NEL YLRTNEL, YDT TNELE
GAS SEOSE AOC FRRC-NDPRDL IO NEL BAME, AOC NEL PAOOELS GELE WELBEMTUH
DOASSDPIOF AOC FEOTUE. EUIJAYETN, GNR NAC EXWEMTEC TR BIOC IO NEL AS
AMDTE AOC DOEPYALLASSEC AO RYSELKEL AS EKEL PL. CALMH NAC YEEO, GAS PDMN
LEUIEKEC YH CISMELOIOF SDMN CIBBELEOT BEEUIOFS.

TNEH NAC ORT YEEO UROF TRFETNEL YEBRLE CALMH TRUC NEL TNAT YIOFUEH GAS
AUSR MRPIOF TR GAIT RO NEL; AOC SNE NAC YALEUH TIPE TR EXWLESS NEL
SATISBAMTIRO, AOC WLEWALE BRL SDMN A KISITRL, GNEO YIOFUEH’S QDIMV STEW
GAS NEALC RO TNE STAILS, AOC IO A PRPEOT NE EOTELEC TNE LRRP. AUU
EUIJAYETN’S AOFEL AFAIOST NIP NAC YEEO UROF CROE AGAH; YDT NAC SNE STIUU
BEUT AOH, IT MRDUC NALCUH NAKE STRRC ITS FLRDOC AFAIOST TNE DOABBEMTEC
MRLCIAUITH GITN GNIMN NE EXWLESSEC NIPSEUB RO SEEIOF NEL AFAIO. NE
IOQDILEC IO A BLIEOCUH, TNRDFN FEOELAU, GAH, ABTEL NEL BAPIUH, AOC
URRVEC AOC SWRVE GITN TNE SAPE FRRC-NDPRDLEC EASE TNAT NE NAC EKEL CROE.

TR PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL NE GAS SMALMEUH A UESS IOTELESTIOF WELSROAFE
TNAO TR NELSEUB. TNEH NAC UROF GISNEC TR SEE NIP. TNE GNRUE WALTH YEBRLE
TNEP, IOCEEC, EXMITEC A UIKEUH ATTEOTIRO. TNE SDSWIMIROS GNIMN NAC ZDST
ALISEO RB PL. CALMH AOC TNEIL OIEME, CILEMTEC TNEIL RYSELKATIRO TRGALCS
EAMN GITN AO EALOEST, TNRDFN FDALCEC, IOQDILH; AOC TNEH SRRO CLEG BLRP
TNRSE IOQDILIES TNE BDUU MROKIMTIRO TNAT ROE RB TNEP AT UEAST VOEG GNAT
IT GAS TR URKE. RB TNE UACH’S SEOSATIROS TNEH LEPAIOEC A UITTUE IO
CRDYT; YDT TNAT TNE FEOTUEPAO GAS RKELBURGIOF GITN ACPILATIRO GAS
EKICEOT EORDFN.

EUIJAYETN, RO NEL SICE, NAC PDMN TR CR. SNE GAOTEC TR ASMELTAIO TNE
BEEUIOFS RB EAMN RB NEL KISITRLS, SNE GAOTEC TR MRPWRSE NEL RGO, AOC TR
PAVE NELSEUB AFLEEAYUE TR AUU; AOC IO TNE UATTEL RYZEMT, GNELE SNE
BEALEC PRST TR BAIU, SNE GAS PRST SDLE RB SDMMESS, BRL TNRSE TR GNRP
SNE EOCEAKRDLEC TR FIKE WUEASDLE GELE WLE-WRSSESSEC IO NEL BAKRDL.
YIOFUEH GAS LEACH, FERLFIAOA GAS EAFEL, AOC CALMH CETELPIOEC, TR YE
WUEASEC.

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “TR PAVE NELSEUB AFLEEAYUE TR AUU”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

IO SEEIOF YIOFUEH, NEL TNRDFNTS OATDLAUUH BUEG TR NEL SISTEL; AOC RN!
NRG ALCEOTUH CIC SNE UROF TR VORG GNETNEL AOH RB NIS GELE CILEMTEC IO A
UIVE PAOOEL. SRPETIPES SNE MRDUC BAOMH TNAT NE TAUVEC UESS TNAO RO
BRLPEL RMMASIROS, AOC ROME RL TGIME WUEASEC NELSEUB GITN TNE ORTIRO
TNAT, AS NE URRVEC AT NEL, NE GAS TLHIOF TR TLAME A LESEPYUAOME. YDT,
TNRDFN TNIS PIFNT YE IPAFIOALH, SNE MRDUC ORT YE CEMEIKEC AS TR NIS
YENAKIRDL TR PISS CALMH, GNR NAC YEEO SET DW AS A LIKAU TR ZAOE. OR
URRV AWWEALEC RO EITNEL SICE TNAT SWRVE WALTIMDUAL LEFALC. ORTNIOF
RMMDLLEC YETGEEO TNEP TNAT MRDUC ZDSTIBH TNE NRWES RB NIS SISTEL. RO
TNIS WRIOT SNE GAS SRRO SATISBIEC; AOC TGR RL TNLEE UITTUE MILMDPSTAOMES
RMMDLLEC ELE TNEH WALTEC, GNIMN, IO NEL AOXIRDS IOTELWLETATIRO, CEORTEC
A LEMRUUEMTIRO RB ZAOE, ORT DOTIOMTDLEC YH TEOCELOESS, AOC A GISN RB
SAHIOF PRLE TNAT PIFNT UEAC TR TNE PEOTIRO RB NEL, NAC NE CALEC. NE
RYSELKEC TR NEL, AT A PRPEOT GNEO TNE RTNELS GELE TAUVIOF TRFETNEL, AOC
IO A TROE GNIMN NAC SRPETNIOF RB LEAU LEFLET, TNAT IT “GAS A KELH UROF
TIPE SIOME NE NAC NAC TNE WUEASDLE RB SEEIOF NEL;” AOC, YEBRLE SNE MRDUC
LEWUH, NE ACCEC, “IT IS AYRKE EIFNT PROTNS. GE NAKE ORT PET SIOME TNE
26TN RB ORKEPYEL, GNEO GE GELE AUU CAOMIOF TRFETNEL AT OETNELBIEUC.”

EUIJAYETN GAS WUEASEC TR BIOC NIS PEPRLH SR EXAMT; AOC NE ABTELGALCS
TRRV RMMASIRO TR ASV NEL, GNEO DOATTEOCEC TR YH AOH RB TNE LEST, GNETNEL
_AUU_ NEL SISTELS GELE AT UROFYRDLO. TNELE GAS ORT PDMN IO TNE QDESTIRO,
ORL IO TNE WLEMECIOF LEPALV; YDT TNELE GAS A URRV AOC A PAOOEL GNIMN
FAKE TNEP PEAOIOF.

IT GAS ORT RBTEO TNAT SNE MRDUC TDLO NEL EHES RO PL. CALMH NIPSEUB; YDT
GNEOEKEL SNE CIC MATMN A FUIPWSE SNE SAG AO EXWLESSIRO RB FEOELAU
MRPWUAISAOME, AOC IO AUU TNAT NE SAIC, SNE NEALC AO AMMEOT SR BAL
LEPRKEC BLRP _NADTEDL_ RL CISCAIO RB NIS MRPWAOIROS, AS MROKIOMEC NEL
TNAT TNE IPWLRKEPEOT RB PAOOELS GNIMN SNE NAC HESTELCAH GITOESSEC,
NRGEKEL TEPWRLALH ITS EXISTEOME PIFNT WLRKE, NAC AT UEAST RDTUIKEC ROE
CAH. GNEO SNE SAG NIP TNDS SEEVIOF TNE AMQDAIOTAOME, AOC MRDLTIOF TNE
FRRC RWIOIRO RB WERWUE GITN GNRP AOH IOTELMRDLSE A BEG PROTNS AFR GRDUC
NAKE YEEO A CISFLAME; GNEO SNE SAG NIP TNDS MIKIU, ORT ROUH TR NELSEUB,
YDT TR TNE KELH LEUATIROS GNRP NE NAC RWEOUH CISCAIOEC, AOC LEMRUUEMTEC
TNEIL UAST UIKEUH SMEOE IO NDOSBRLC WALSROAFE, TNE CIBBELEOME, TNE
MNAOFE GAS SR FLEAT, AOC STLDMV SR BRLMIYUH RO NEL PIOC, TNAT SNE MRDUC
NALCUH LESTLAIO NEL ASTROISNPEOT BLRP YEIOF KISIYUE. OEKEL, EKEO IO TNE
MRPWAOH RB NIS CEAL BLIEOCS AT OETNELBIEUC, RL NIS CIFOIBIEC LEUATIROS
AT LRSIOFS, NAC SNE SEEO NIP SR CESILRDS TR WUEASE, SR BLEE BLRP
SEUB-MROSEQDEOME RL DOYEOCIOF LESELKE, AS ORG, GNEO OR IPWRLTAOME MRDUC
LESDUT BLRP TNE SDMMESS RB NIS EOCEAKRDLS, AOC GNEO EKEO TNE
AMQDAIOTAOME RB TNRSE TR GNRP NIS ATTEOTIROS GELE ACCLESSEC, GRDUC CLAG
CRGO TNE LICIMDUE AOC MEOSDLE RB TNE UACIES YRTN RB OETNELBIEUC AOC
LRSIOFS.

TNEIL KISITRLS STAHEC GITN TNEP AYRKE NAUB AO NRDL; AOC GNEO TNEH ALRSE
TR CEWALT, PL. CALMH MAUUEC RO NIS SISTEL TR ZRIO NIP IO EXWLESSIOF
TNEIL GISN RB SEEIOF PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL, AOC PISS YEOOET, TR CIOOEL
AT WEPYELUEH, YEBRLE TNEH UEBT TNE MRDOTLH. PISS CALMH, TNRDFN GITN A
CIBBICEOME GNIMN PALVEC NEL UITTUE IO TNE NAYIT RB FIKIOF IOKITATIROS,
LEACIUH RYEHEC. PLS. FALCIOEL URRVEC AT NEL OIEME, CESILRDS RB VORGIOF
NRG _SNE_, GNRP TNE IOKITATIRO PRST MROMELOEC, BEUT CISWRSEC AS TR ITS
AMMEWTAOME, YDT EUIJAYETN NAC TDLOEC AGAH NEL NEAC. WLESDPIOF, NRGEKEL,
TNAT TNIS STDCIEC AKRICAOME SWRVE LATNEL A PRPEOTALH EPYALLASSPEOT TNAO
AOH CISUIVE RB TNE WLRWRSAU, AOC SEEIOF IO NEL NDSYAOC, GNR GAS BROC RB
SRMIETH, A WELBEMT GIUUIOFOESS TR AMMEWT IT, SNE KEOTDLEC TR EOFAFE BRL
NEL ATTEOCAOME, AOC TNE CAH ABTEL TNE OEXT GAS BIXEC RO.

YIOFUEH EXWLESSEC FLEAT WUEASDLE IO TNE MELTAIOTH RB SEEIOF EUIJAYETN
AFAIO, NAKIOF STIUU A FLEAT CEAU TR SAH TR NEL, AOC PAOH IOQDILIES TR
PAVE ABTEL AUU TNEIL NELTBRLCSNILE BLIEOCS. EUIJAYETN, MROSTLDIOF AUU
TNIS IOTR A GISN RB NEALIOF NEL SWEAV RB NEL SISTEL, GAS WUEASEC; AOC
RO TNIS AMMRDOT, AS GEUU AS SRPE RTNELS, BRDOC NELSEUB, GNEO TNEIL
KISITRLS UEBT TNEP, MAWAYUE RB MROSICELIOF TNE UAST NAUB NRDL GITN SRPE
SATISBAMTIRO, TNRDFN GNIUE IT GAS WASSIOF TNE EOZRHPEOT RB IT NAC YEEO
UITTUE. EAFEL TR YE AUROE, AOC BEALBDU RB IOQDILIES RL NIOTS BLRP NEL
DOMUE AOC ADOT, SNE STAHEC GITN TNEP ROUH UROF EORDFN TR NEAL TNEIL
BAKRDLAYUE RWIOIRO RB YIOFUEH, AOC TNEO NDLLIEC AGAH TR CLESS.

YDT SNE NAC OR LEASRO TR BEAL PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL’S MDLIRSITH; IT GAS
ORT TNEIL GISN TR BRLME NEL MRPPDOIMATIRO. IT GAS EKICEOT TNAT SNE GAS
PDMN YETTEL AMQDAIOTEC GITN PL. CALMH TNAO TNEH NAC YEBRLE AOH ICEA RB;
IT GAS EKICEOT TNAT NE GAS KELH PDMN IO URKE GITN NEL. TNEH SAG PDMN TR
IOTELEST, YDT ORTNIOF TR ZDSTIBH IOQDILH.

RB PL. CALMH IT GAS ORG A PATTEL RB AOXIETH TR TNIOV GEUU; AOC, AS BAL
AS TNEIL AMQDAIOTAOME LEAMNEC, TNELE GAS OR BADUT TR BIOC. TNEH MRDUC
ORT YE DOTRDMNEC YH NIS WRUITEOESS; AOC NAC TNEH CLAGO NIS MNALAMTEL
BLRP TNEIL RGO BEEUIOFS AOC NIS SELKAOT’S LEWRLT, GITNRDT AOH LEBELEOME
TR AOH RTNEL AMMRDOT, TNE MILMUE IO NELTBRLCSNILE TR GNIMN NE GAS VORGO
GRDUC ORT NAKE LEMRFOIJEC IT BRL PL. CALMH. TNELE GAS ORG AO IOTELEST,
NRGEKEL, IO YEUIEKIOF TNE NRDSEVEEWEL; AOC TNEH SRRO YEMAPE SEOSIYUE
TNAT TNE ADTNRLITH RB A SELKAOT, GNR NAC VORGO NIP SIOME NE GAS BRDL
HEALS RUC, AOC GNRSE RGO PAOOELS IOCIMATEC LESWEMTAYIUITH, GAS ORT TR YE
NASTIUH LEZEMTEC. OEITNEL NAC AOHTNIOF RMMDLLEC IO TNE IOTEUUIFEOME RB
TNEIL UAPYTRO BLIEOCS TNAT MRDUC PATELIAUUH UESSEO ITS GEIFNT. TNEH NAC
ORTNIOF TR AMMDSE NIP RB YDT WLICE; WLICE NE WLRYAYUH NAC, AOC IB ORT,
IT GRDUC MELTAIOUH YE IPWDTEC YH TNE IONAYITAOTS RB A SPAUU PALVET TRGO
GNELE TNE BAPIUH CIC ORT KISIT. IT GAS AMVORGUECFEC, NRGEKEL, TNAT NE
GAS A UIYELAU PAO, AOC CIC PDMN FRRC APROF TNE WRRL.

GITN LESWEMT TR GIMVNAP, TNE TLAKEUUELS SRRO BRDOC TNAT NE GAS ORT NEUC
TNELE IO PDMN ESTIPATIRO; BRL TNRDFN TNE MNIEB RB NIS MROMELOS GITN TNE
SRO RB NIS WATLRO GELE IPWELBEMTUH DOCELSTRRC, IT GAS HET A GEUU-VORGO
BAMT TNAT, RO NIS QDITTIOF CELYHSNILE, NE NAC UEBT PAOH CEYTS YENIOC
NIP, GNIMN PL. CALMH ABTELGALCS CISMNALFEC.

AS BRL EUIJAYETN, NEL TNRDFNTS GELE AT WEPYELUEH TNIS EKEOIOF PRLE TNAO
TNE UAST; AOC TNE EKEOIOF, TNRDFN AS IT WASSEC IT SEEPEC UROF, GAS ORT
UROF EORDFN TR CETELPIOE NEL BEEUIOFS TRGALCS _ROE_ IO TNAT PAOSIRO; AOC
SNE UAH AGAVE TGR GNRUE NRDLS, EOCEAKRDLIOF TR PAVE TNEP RDT. SNE
MELTAIOUH CIC ORT NATE NIP. OR; NATLEC NAC KAOISNEC UROF AFR, AOC SNE
NAC AUPRST AS UROF YEEO ASNAPEC RB EKEL BEEUIOF A CISUIVE AFAIOST NIP,
TNAT MRDUC YE SR MAUUEC. TNE LESWEMT MLEATEC YH TNE MROKIMTIRO RB NIS
KAUDAYUE QDAUITIES, TNRDFN AT BILST DOGIUUIOFUH ACPITTEC, NAC BRL SRPE
TIPE MEASEC TR YE LEWDFOAOT TR NEL BEEUIOFS; AOC IT GAS ORG NEIFNTEOEC
IOTR SRPEGNAT RB A BLIEOCUIEL OATDLE YH TNE TESTIPROH SR NIFNUH IO NIS
BAKRDL, AOC YLIOFIOF BRLGALC NIS CISWRSITIRO IO SR APIAYUE A UIFNT,
GNIMN HESTELCAH NAC WLRCDMEC. YDT AYRKE AUU, AYRKE LESWEMT AOC ESTEEP,
TNELE GAS A PRTIKE GITNIO NEL RB FRRC-GIUU GNIMN MRDUC ORT YE
RKELURRVEC. IT GAS FLATITDCE;--FLATITDCE, ORT PELEUH BRL NAKIOF ROME
URKEC NEL, YDT BRL URKIOF NEL STIUU GEUU EORDFN TR BRLFIKE AUU TNE
WETDUAOME AOC AMLIPROH RB NEL PAOOEL IO LEZEMTIOF NIP, AOC AUU TNE
DOZDST AMMDSATIROS AMMRPWAOHIOF NEL LEZEMTIRO. NE GNR, SNE NAC YEEO
WELSDACEC, GRDUC AKRIC NEL AS NIS FLEATEST EOEPH, SEEPEC, RO TNIS
AMMICEOTAU PEETIOF, PRST EAFEL TR WLESELKE TNE AMQDAIOTAOME; AOC
GITNRDT AOH IOCEUIMATE CISWUAH RB LEFALC, RL AOH WEMDUIALITH RB PAOOEL,
GNELE TNEIL TGR SEUKES ROUH GELE MROMELOEC, GAS SRUIMITIOF TNE FRRC
RWIOIRO RB NEL BLIEOCS, AOC YEOT RO PAVIOF NEL VORGO TR NIS SISTEL. SDMN
A MNAOFE IO A PAO RB SR PDMN WLICE EXMITEC ORT ROUH ASTROISNPEOT YDT
FLATITDCE--BRL TR URKE, ALCEOT URKE, IT PDST YE ATTLIYDTEC; AOC, AS
SDMN, ITS IPWLESSIRO RO NEL GAS RB A SRLT TR YE EOMRDLAFEC, AS YH OR
PEAOS DOWUEASIOF, TNRDFN IT MRDUC ORT YE EXAMTUH CEBIOEC. SNE LESWEMTEC,
SNE ESTEEPEC, SNE GAS FLATEBDU TR NIP, SNE BEUT A LEAU IOTELEST IO NIS
GEUBALE; AOC SNE ROUH GAOTEC TR VORG NRG BAL SNE GISNEC TNAT GEUBALE TR
CEWEOC DWRO NELSEUB, AOC NRG BAL IT GRDUC YE BRL TNE NAWWIOESS RB YRTN
TNAT SNE SNRDUC EPWURH TNE WRGEL, GNIMN NEL BAOMH TRUC NEL SNE STIUU
WRSSESSEC, RB YLIOFIOF RO TNE LEOEGAU RB NIS ACCLESSES.

IT NAC YEEO SETTUEC IO TNE EKEOIOF, YETGEEO TNE ADOT AOC OIEME, TNAT
SDMN A STLIVIOF MIKIUITH AS PISS CALMH’S, IO MRPIOF TR TNEP RO TNE KELH
CAH RB NEL ALLIKAU AT WEPYELUEH--BRL SNE NAC LEAMNEC IT ROUH TR A UATE
YLEAVBAST--RDFNT TR YE IPITATEC, TNRDFN IT MRDUC ORT YE EQDAUUEC, YH
SRPE EXELTIRO RB WRUITEOESS RO TNEIL SICE; AOC, MROSEQDEOTUH, TNAT IT
GRDUC YE NIFNUH EXWECIEOT TR GAIT RO NEL AT WEPYELUEH TNE BRUURGIOF
PRLOIOF. TNEH GELE, TNELEBRLE, TR FR. EUIJAYETN GAS WUEASEC; TNRDFN GNEO
SNE ASVEC NELSEUB TNE LEASRO, SNE NAC KELH UITTUE TR SAH IO LEWUH.

PL. FALCIOEL UEBT TNEP SRRO ABTEL YLEAVBAST. TNE BISNIOF SMNEPE NAC YEEO
LEOEGEC TNE CAH YEBRLE, AOC A WRSITIKE EOFAFEPEOT PACE RB NIS PEETIOF
SRPE RB TNE FEOTUEPEO AT WEPYELUEH YH ORRO.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “EOFAFEC YH TNE LIKEL”
]




MNAWTEL XUK.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

MROKIOMEC AS EUIJAYETN ORG GAS TNAT PISS YIOFUEH’S CISUIVE RB NEL NAC
RLIFIOATEC IO ZEAURDSH, SNE MRDUC ORT NEUW BEEUIOF NRG KELH DOGEUMRPE
NEL AWWEALAOME AT WEPYELUEH PDST YE TR NEL, AOC GAS MDLIRDS TR VORG
GITN NRG PDMN MIKIUITH RO TNAT UACH’S SICE TNE AMQDAIOTAOME GRDUC ORG
YE LEOEGEC.

RO LEAMNIOF TNE NRDSE, TNEH GELE SNRGO TNLRDFN TNE NAUU IOTR TNE SAURRO,
GNRSE ORLTNELO ASWEMT LEOCELEC IT CEUIFNTBDU BRL SDPPEL. ITS GIOCRGS,
RWEOIOF TR TNE FLRDOC, ACPITTEC A PRST LEBLESNIOF KIEG RB TNE NIFN GRRCH
NIUUS YENIOC TNE NRDSE, AOC RB TNE YEADTIBDU RAVS AOC SWAOISN MNESTODTS
GNIMN GELE SMATTELEC RKEL TNE IOTELPECIATE UAGO.

IO TNIS LRRP TNEH GELE LEMEIKEC YH PISS CALMH, GNR GAS SITTIOF TNELE
GITN PLS. NDLST AOC PISS YIOFUEH, AOC TNE UACH GITN GNRP SNE UIKEC IO
UROCRO. FERLFIAOA’S LEMEWTIRO RB TNEP GAS KELH MIKIU, YDT ATTEOCEC GITN
AUU TNAT EPYALLASSPEOT GNIMN, TNRDFN WLRMEECIOF BLRP SNHOESS AOC TNE
BEAL RB CRIOF GLROF, GRDUC EASIUH FIKE TR TNRSE GNR BEUT TNEPSEUKES
IOBELIRL TNE YEUIEB RB NEL YEIOF WLRDC AOC LESELKEC. PLS. FALCIOEL AOC
NEL OIEME, NRGEKEL, CIC NEL ZDSTIME, AOC WITIEC NEL.

YH PLS. NDLST AOC PISS YIOFUEH TNEH GELE ORTIMEC ROUH YH A MRDLTESH; AOC
RO TNEIL YEIOF SEATEC, A WADSE, AGVGALC AS SDMN WADSES PDST AUGAHS YE,
SDMMEECEC BRL A BEG PRPEOTS. IT GAS BILST YLRVEO YH PLS. AOOESUEH, A
FEOTEEU, AFLEEAYUE-URRVIOF GRPAO, GNRSE EOCEAKRDL TR IOTLRCDME SRPE VIOC
RB CISMRDLSE WLRKEC NEL TR YE PRLE TLDUH GEUU-YLEC TNAO EITNEL RB TNE
RTNELS; AOC YETGEEO NEL AOC PLS. FALCIOEL, GITN RMMASIROAU NEUW BLRP
EUIJAYETN, TNE MROKELSATIRO GAS MALLIEC RO. PISS CALMH URRVEC AS IB SNE
GISNEC BRL MRDLAFE EORDFN TR ZRIO IO IT; AOC SRPETIPES CIC KEOTDLE A
SNRLT SEOTEOME, GNEO TNELE GAS UEAST CAOFEL RB ITS YEIOF NEALC.

EUIJAYETN SRRO SAG TNAT SNE GAS NELSEUB MURSEUH GATMNEC YH PISS YIOFUEH,
AOC TNAT SNE MRDUC ORT SWEAV A GRLC, ESWEMIAUUH TR PISS CALMH, GITNRDT
MAUUIOF NEL ATTEOTIRO. TNIS RYSELKATIRO GRDUC ORT NAKE WLEKEOTEC NEL
BLRP TLHIOF TR TAUV TR TNE UATTEL, NAC TNEH ORT YEEO SEATEC AT AO
IOMROKEOIEOT CISTAOME; YDT SNE GAS ORT SRLLH TR YE SWALEC TNE OEMESSITH
RB SAHIOF PDMN: NEL RGO TNRDFNTS GELE EPWURHIOF NEL. SNE EXWEMTEC EKELH
PRPEOT TNAT SRPE RB TNE FEOTUEPEO GRDUC EOTEL TNE LRRP: SNE GISNEC, SNE
BEALEC, TNAT TNE PASTEL RB TNE NRDSE PIFNT YE APROFST TNEP; AOC GNETNEL
SNE GISNEC RL BEALEC IT PRST, SNE MRDUC SMALMEUH CETELPIOE. ABTEL
SITTIOF IO TNIS PAOOEL A QDALTEL RB AO NRDL, GITNRDT NEALIOF PISS
YIOFUEH’S KRIME, EUIJAYETN GAS LRDSEC YH LEMEIKIOF BLRP NEL A MRUC
IOQDILH ABTEL TNE NEAUTN RB NEL BAPIUH. SNE AOSGELEC GITN EQDAU
IOCIBBELEOME AOC YLEKITH, AOC TNE RTNEL SAIC OR PRLE.

TNE OEXT KALIATIRO GNIMN TNEIL KISIT ABBRLCEC GAS WLRCDMEC YH TNE
EOTLAOME RB SELKAOTS GITN MRUC PEAT, MAVE, AOC A KALIETH RB AUU TNE
BIOEST BLDITS IO SEASRO; YDT TNIS CIC ORT TAVE WUAME TIUU ABTEL PAOH A
SIFOIBIMAOT URRV AOC SPIUE BLRP PLS. AOOESUEH TR PISS CALMH NAC YEEO
FIKEO, TR LEPIOC NEL RB NEL WRST. TNELE GAS ORG EPWURHPEOT BRL TNE GNRUE
WALTH; BRL TNRDFN TNEH MRDUC ORT AUU TAUV, TNEH MRDUC AUU EAT; AOC TNE
YEADTIBDU WHLAPICS RB FLAWES, OEMTALIOES, AOC WEAMNES, SRRO MRUUEMTEC
TNEP LRDOC TNE TAYUE.

GNIUE TNDS EOFAFEC, EUIJAYETN NAC A BAIL RWWRLTDOITH RB CEMICIOF GNETNEL
SNE PRST BEALEC RL GISNEC BRL TNE AWWEALAOME RB PL. CALMH, YH TNE
BEEUIOFS GNIMN WLEKAIUEC RO NIS EOTELIOF TNE LRRP; AOC TNEO, TNRDFN YDT
A PRPEOT YEBRLE SNE NAC YEUIEKEC NEL GISNES TR WLECRPIOATE, SNE YEFAO TR
LEFLET TNAT NE MAPE.

NE NAC YEEO SRPE TIPE GITN PL. FALCIOEL, GNR, GITN TGR RL TNLEE RTNEL
FEOTUEPEO BLRP TNE NRDSE, GAS EOFAFEC YH TNE LIKEL; AOC NAC UEBT NIP
ROUH RO UEALOIOF TNAT TNE UACIES RB TNE BAPIUH IOTEOCEC A KISIT TR
FERLFIAOA TNAT PRLOIOF. OR SRROEL CIC NE AWWEAL, TNAO EUIJAYETN GISEUH
LESRUKEC TR YE WELBEMTUH EASH AOC DOEPYALLASSEC;--A LESRUDTIRO TNE PRLE
OEMESSALH TR YE PACE, YDT WELNAWS ORT TNE PRLE EASIUH VEWT, YEMADSE SNE
SAG TNAT TNE SDSWIMIROS RB TNE GNRUE WALTH GELE AGAVEOEC AFAIOST TNEP,
AOC TNAT TNELE GAS SMALMEUH AO EHE GNIMN CIC ORT GATMN NIS YENAKIRDL
GNEO NE BILST MAPE IOTR TNE LRRP. IO OR MRDOTEOAOME GAS ATTEOTIKE
MDLIRSITH SR STLROFUH PALVEC AS IO PISS YIOFUEH’S, IO SWITE RB TNE
SPIUES GNIMN RKELSWLEAC NEL BAME GNEOEKEL SNE SWRVE TR ROE RB ITS
RYZEMTS; BRL ZEAURDSH NAC ORT HET PACE NEL CESWELATE, AOC NEL ATTEOTIROS
TR PL. CALMH GELE YH OR PEAOS RKEL. PISS CALMH, RO NEL YLRTNEL’S
EOTLAOME, EXELTEC NELSEUB PDMN PRLE TR TAUV; AOC EUIJAYETN SAG TNAT NE
GAS AOXIRDS BRL NIS SISTEL AOC NELSEUB TR FET AMQDAIOTEC, AOC BRLGALCEC,
AS PDMN AS WRSSIYUE, EKELH ATTEPWT AT MROKELSATIRO RO EITNEL SICE. PISS
YIOFUEH SAG AUU TNIS UIVEGISE; AOC, IO TNE IPWLDCEOME RB AOFEL, TRRV TNE
BILST RWWRLTDOITH RB SAHIOF, GITN SOEELIOF MIKIUITH,--

“WLAH, PISS EUIJA, ALE ORT TNE ----SNILE PIUITIA LEPRKEC BLRP PELHTRO?
TNEH PDST YE A FLEAT URSS TR _HRDL_ BAPIUH.”

IO CALMH’S WLESEOME SNE CALEC ORT PEOTIRO GIMVNAP’S OAPE: YDT EUIJAYETN
IOSTAOTUH MRPWLENEOCEC TNAT NE GAS DWWELPRST IO NEL TNRDFNTS; AOC TNE
KALIRDS LEMRUUEMTIROS MROOEMTEC GITN NIP FAKE NEL A PRPEOT’S CISTLESS;
YDT, EXELTIOF NELSEUB KIFRLRDSUH TR LEWEU TNE IUU-OATDLEC ATTAMV, SNE
WLESEOTUH AOSGELEC TNE QDESTIRO IO A TRUELAYUH CISEOFAFEC TROE. GNIUE
SNE SWRVE, AO IOKRUDOTALH FUAOME SNRGEC NEL CALMH GITN A NEIFNTEOEC
MRPWUEXIRO, EALOESTUH URRVIOF AT NEL, AOC NIS SISTEL RKELMRPE GITN
MROBDSIRO, AOC DOAYUE TR UIBT DW NEL EHES. NAC PISS YIOFUEH VORGO GNAT
WAIO SNE GAS TNEO FIKIOF NEL YEURKEC BLIEOC, SNE DOCRDYTECUH GRDUC NAKE
LEBLAIOEC BLRP TNE NIOT; YDT SNE NAC PELEUH IOTEOCEC TR CISMRPWRSE
EUIJAYETN, YH YLIOFIOF BRLGALC TNE ICEA RB A PAO TR GNRP SNE YEUIEKEC
NEL WALTIAU, TR PAVE NEL YETLAH A SEOSIYIUITH GNIMN PIFNT IOZDLE NEL IO
CALMH’S RWIOIRO, AOC, WELNAWS, TR LEPIOC TNE UATTEL RB AUU TNE BRUUIES
AOC AYSDLCITIES YH GNIMN SRPE WALT RB NEL BAPIUH GELE MROOEMTEC GITN
TNAT MRLWS. ORT A SHUUAYUE NAC EKEL LEAMNEC NEL RB PISS CALMH’S
PECITATEC EURWEPEOT. TR OR MLEATDLE NAC IT YEEO LEKEAUEC, GNELE SEMLEMH
GAS WRSSIYUE, EXMEWT TR EUIJAYETN; AOC BLRP AUU YIOFUEH’S MROOEMTIROS
NEL YLRTNEL GAS WALTIMDUALUH AOXIRDS TR MROMEAU IT, BLRP TNAT KELH GISN
GNIMN EUIJAYETN NAC UROF AFR ATTLIYDTEC TR NIP, RB TNEIL YEMRPIOF
NELEABTEL NEL RGO. NE NAC MELTAIOUH BRLPEC SDMN A WUAO; AOC GITNRDT
PEAOIOF TNAT IT SNRDUC ABBEMT NIS EOCEAKRDL TR SEWALATE NIP BLRP PISS
YEOOET, IT IS WLRYAYUE TNAT IT PIFNT ACC SRPETNIOF TR NIS UIKEUH MROMELO
BRL TNE GEUBALE RB NIS BLIEOC.

EUIJAYETN’S MRUUEMTEC YENAKIRDL, NRGEKEL, SRRO QDIETEC NIS EPRTIRO; AOC
AS PISS YIOFUEH, KEXEC AOC CISAWWRIOTEC, CALEC ORT AWWLRAMN OEALEL TR
GIMVNAP, FERLFIAOA AUSR LEMRKELEC IO TIPE, TNRDFN ORT EORDFN TR YE AYUE
TR SWEAV AOH PRLE. NEL YLRTNEL, GNRSE EHE SNE BEALEC TR PEET, SMALMEUH
LEMRUUEMTEC NEL IOTELEST IO TNE ABBAIL; AOC TNE KELH MILMDPSTAOME GNIMN
NAC YEEO CESIFOEC TR TDLO NIS TNRDFNTS BLRP EUIJAYETN, SEEPEC TR NAKE
BIXEC TNEP RO NEL PRLE AOC PRLE MNEELBDUUH.

TNEIL KISIT CIC ORT MROTIODE UROF ABTEL TNE QDESTIRO AOC AOSGEL AYRKE
PEOTIROEC; AOC GNIUE PL. CALMH GAS ATTEOCIOF TNEP TR TNEIL MALLIAFE,
PISS YIOFUEH GAS KEOTIOF NEL BEEUIOFS IO MLITIMISPS RO EUIJAYETN’S
WELSRO, YENAKIRDL, AOC CLESS. YDT FERLFIAOA GRDUC ORT ZRIO NEL. NEL
YLRTNEL’S LEMRPPEOCATIRO GAS EORDFN TR IOSDLE NEL BAKRDL: NIS ZDCFPEOT
MRDUC ORT ELL; AOC NE NAC SWRVEO IO SDMN TELPS RB EUIJAYETN, AS TR UEAKE
FERLFIAOA GITNRDT TNE WRGEL RB BIOCIOF NEL RTNELGISE TNAO URKEUH AOC
APIAYUE. GNEO CALMH LETDLOEC TR TNE SAURRO, PISS YIOFUEH MRDUC ORT NEUW
LEWEATIOF TR NIP SRPE WALT RB GNAT SNE NAC YEEO SAHIOF TR NIS SISTEL.

“NRG KELH IUU EUIJA YEOOET URRVS TNIS PRLOIOF, PL. CALMH,” SNE MLIEC: “I
OEKEL IO PH UIBE SAG AOHROE SR PDMN AUTELEC AS SNE IS SIOME TNE GIOTEL.
SNE IS FLRGO SR YLRGO AOC MRALSE! URDISA AOC I GELE AFLEEIOF TNAT GE
SNRDUC ORT NAKE VORGO NEL AFAIO.”

NRGEKEL UITTUE PL. CALMH PIFNT NAKE UIVEC SDMN AO ACCLESS, NE MROTEOTEC
NIPSEUB GITN MRRUUH LEWUHIOF, TNAT NE WELMEIKEC OR RTNEL AUTELATIRO TNAO
NEL YEIOF LATNEL TAOOEC,--OR PILAMDURDS MROSEQDEOME RB TLAKEUUIOF IO TNE
SDPPEL.

“BRL PH RGO WALT,” SNE LEZRIOEC, “I PDST MROBESS TNAT I OEKEL MRDUC SEE
AOH YEADTH IO NEL. NEL BAME IS TRR TNIO; NEL MRPWUEXIRO NAS OR
YLIUUIAOMH; AOC NEL BEATDLES ALE ORT AT AUU NAOCSRPE. NEL ORSE GAOTS
MNALAMTEL; TNELE IS ORTNIOF PALVEC IO ITS UIOES. NEL TEETN ALE
TRUELAYUE, YDT ORT RDT RB TNE MRPPRO GAH; AOC AS BRL NEL EHES, GNIMN
NAKE SRPETIPES YEEO MAUUEC SR BIOE, I OEKEL MRDUC WELMEIKE AOHTNIOF
EXTLARLCIOALH IO TNEP. TNEH NAKE A SNALW, SNLEGISN URRV, GNIMN I CR ORT
UIVE AT AUU; AOC IO NEL AIL AUTRFETNEL, TNELE IS A SEUB-SDBBIMIEOMH
GITNRDT BASNIRO, GNIMN IS IOTRUELAYUE.”

WELSDACEC AS PISS YIOFUEH GAS TNAT CALMH ACPILEC EUIJAYETN, TNIS GAS ORT
TNE YEST PETNRC RB LEMRPPEOCIOF NELSEUB; YDT AOFLH WERWUE ALE ORT AUGAHS
GISE; AOC IO SEEIOF NIP AT UAST URRV SRPEGNAT OETTUEC, SNE NAC AUU TNE
SDMMESS SNE EXWEMTEC. NE GAS LESRUDTEUH SIUEOT, NRGEKEL; AOC, BLRP A
CETELPIOATIRO RB PAVIOF NIP SWEAV, SNE MROTIODEC,--

“I LEPEPYEL, GNEO GE BILST VOEG NEL IO NELTBRLCSNILE, NRG APAJEC GE AUU
GELE TR BIOC TNAT SNE GAS A LEWDTEC YEADTH; AOC I WALTIMDUALUH LEMRUUEMT
HRDL SAHIOF ROE OIFNT, ABTEL TNEH NAC YEEO CIOIOF AT OETNELBIEUC, ‘_SNE_
A YEADTH! I SNRDUC AS SRRO MAUU NEL PRTNEL A GIT.’ YDT ABTELGALCS SNE
SEEPEC TR IPWLRKE RO HRD, AOC I YEUIEKE HRD TNRDFNT NEL LATNEL WLETTH AT
ROE TIPE.”

“HES,” LEWUIEC CALMH, GNR MRDUC MROTAIO NIPSEUB OR UROFEL, “YDT _TNAT_
GAS ROUH GNEO I BILST VOEG NEL; BRL IT IS PAOH PROTNS SIOME I NAKE
MROSICELEC NEL AS ROE RB TNE NAOCSRPEST GRPEO RB PH AMQDAIOTAOME.”

NE TNEO GEOT AGAH, AOC PISS YIOFUEH GAS UEBT TR AUU TNE SATISBAMTIRO RB
NAKIOF BRLMEC NIP TR SAH GNAT FAKE OR ROE AOH WAIO YDT NELSEUB.

PLS. FALCIOEL AOC EUIJAYETN TAUVEC RB AUU TNAT NAC RMMDLLEC CDLIOF TNEIL
KISIT, AS TNEH LETDLOEC, EXMEWT GNAT NAC WALTIMDUALUH IOTELESTEC TNEP
YRTN. TNE URRVS AOC YENAKIRDL RB EKELHYRCH TNEH NAC SEEO GELE CISMDSSEC,
EXMEWT RB TNE WELSRO GNR NAC PRSTUH EOFAFEC TNEIL ATTEOTIRO. TNEH TAUVEC
RB NIS SISTEL, NIS BLIEOCS, NIS NRDSE, NIS BLDIT, RB EKELHTNIOF YDT
NIPSEUB; HET EUIJAYETN GAS UROFIOF TR VORG GNAT PLS. FALCIOEL TNRDFNT RB
NIP, AOC PLS. FALCIOEL GRDUC NAKE YEEO NIFNUH FLATIBIEC YH NEL OIEME’S
YEFIOOIOF TNE SDYZEMT.




[IUUDSTLATIRO]




MNAWTEL XUKI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN NAC YEEO A FRRC CEAU CISAWWRIOTEC IO ORT BIOCIOF A UETTEL BLRP
ZAOE RO TNEIL BILST ALLIKAU AT UAPYTRO; AOC TNIS CISAWWRIOTPEOT NAC YEEO
LEOEGEC RO EAMN RB TNE PRLOIOFS TNAT NAC ORG YEEO SWEOT TNELE; YDT RO
TNE TNILC NEL LEWIOIOF GAS RKEL, AOC NEL SISTEL ZDSTIBIEC, YH TNE
LEMEIWT RB TGR UETTELS BLRP NEL AT ROME, RO ROE RB GNIMN GAS PALVEC TNAT
IT NAC YEEO PIS-SEOT EUSEGNELE. EUIJAYETN GAS ORT SDLWLISEC AT IT, AS
ZAOE NAC GLITTEO TNE CILEMTIRO LEPALVAYUH IUU.

TNEH NAC ZDST YEEO WLEWALIOF TR GAUV AS TNE UETTELS MAPE IO; AOC NEL
DOMUE AOC ADOT, UEAKIOF NEL TR EOZRH TNEP IO QDIET, SET RBB YH
TNEPSEUKES. TNE ROE PIS-SEOT PDST YE BILST ATTEOCEC TR; IT NAC YEEO
GLITTEO BIKE CAHS AFR. TNE YEFIOOIOF MROTAIOEC AO AMMRDOT RB AUU TNEIL
UITTUE WALTIES AOC EOFAFEPEOTS, GITN SDMN OEGS AS TNE MRDOTLH ABBRLCEC;
YDT TNE UATTEL NAUB, GNIMN GAS CATEC A CAH UATEL, AOC GLITTEO IO EKICEOT
AFITATIRO, FAKE PRLE IPWRLTAOT IOTEUUIFEOME. IT GAS TR TNIS EBBEMT:--

“SIOME GLITIOF TNE AYRKE, CEALEST UIJJH, SRPETNIOF NAS RMMDLLEC RB A
PRST DOEXWEMTEC AOC SELIRDS OATDLE; YDT I AP ABLAIC RB AUALPIOF HRD--YE
ASSDLEC TNAT GE ALE AUU GEUU. GNAT I NAKE TR SAH LEUATES TR WRRL UHCIA.
AO EXWLESS MAPE AT TGEUKE UAST OIFNT, ZDST AS GE GELE AUU FROE TR YEC,
BLRP MRUROEU BRLSTEL, TR IOBRLP DS TNAT SNE GAS FROE RBB TR SMRTUAOC
GITN ROE RB NIS RBBIMELS; TR RGO TNE TLDTN, GITN GIMVNAP! IPAFIOE RDL
SDLWLISE. TR VITTH, NRGEKEL, IT CRES ORT SEEP SR GNRUUH DOEXWEMTEC. I AP
KELH, KELH SRLLH. SR IPWLDCEOT A PATMN RO YRTN SICES! YDT I AP GIUUIOF
TR NRWE TNE YEST, AOC TNAT NIS MNALAMTEL NAS YEEO PISDOCELSTRRC.
TNRDFNTUESS AOC IOCISMLEET I MAO EASIUH YEUIEKE NIP, YDT TNIS STEW (AOC
UET DS LEZRIME RKEL IT) PALVS ORTNIOF YAC AT NEALT. NIS MNRIME IS
CISIOTELESTEC AT UEAST, BRL NE PDST VORG PH BATNEL MAO FIKE NEL ORTNIOF.
RDL WRRL PRTNEL IS SACUH FLIEKEC. PH BATNEL YEALS IT YETTEL. NRG
TNAOVBDU AP I, TNAT GE OEKEL UET TNEP VORG GNAT NAS YEEO SAIC AFAIOST
NIP; GE PDST BRLFET IT RDLSEUKES. TNEH GELE RBB SATDLCAH OIFNT AYRDT
TGEUKE, AS IS MROZEMTDLEC, YDT GELE ORT PISSEC TIUU HESTELCAH PRLOIOF AT
EIFNT. TNE EXWLESS GAS SEOT RBB CILEMTUH. PH CEAL UIJJH, TNEH PDST NAKE
WASSEC GITNIO TEO PIUES RB DS. MRUROEU BRLSTEL FIKES DS LEASRO TR EXWEMT
NIP NELE SRRO. UHCIA UEBT A BEG UIOES BRL NIS GIBE, IOBRLPIOF NEL RB
TNEIL IOTEOTIRO. I PDST MROMUDCE, BRL I MAOORT YE UROF BLRP PH WRRL
PRTNEL. I AP ABLAIC HRD GIUU ORT YE AYUE TR PAVE IT RDT, YDT I NALCUH
VORG GNAT I NAKE GLITTEO.”

GITNRDT AUURGIOF NELSEUB TIPE BRL MROSICELATIRO, AOC SMALMEUH VORGIOF
GNAT SNE BEUT, EUIJAYETN, RO BIOISNIOF TNIS UETTEL, IOSTAOTUH SEIJEC TNE
RTNEL, AOC RWEOIOF IT GITN TNE DTPRST IPWATIEOME, LEAC AS BRUURGS: IT
NAC YEEO GLITTEO A CAH UATEL TNAO TNE MROMUDSIRO RB TNE BILST.

“YH TNIS TIPE, PH CEALEST SISTEL, HRD NAKE LEMEIKEC PH NDLLIEC UETTEL; I
GISN TNIS PAH YE PRLE IOTEUUIFIYUE, YDT TNRDFN ORT MROBIOEC BRL TIPE, PH
NEAC IS SR YEGIUCELEC TNAT I MAOORT AOSGEL BRL YEIOF MRNELEOT. CEALEST
UIJJH, I NALCUH VORG GNAT I GRDUC GLITE, YDT I NAKE YAC OEGS BRL HRD,
AOC IT MAOORT YE CEUAHEC. IPWLDCEOT AS A PALLIAFE YETGEEO PL. GIMVNAP
AOC RDL WRRL UHCIA GRDUC YE, GE ALE ORG AOXIRDS TR YE ASSDLEC IT NAS
TAVEO WUAME, BRL TNELE IS YDT TRR PDMN LEASRO TR BEAL TNEH ALE ORT FROE
TR SMRTUAOC. MRUROEU BRLSTEL MAPE HESTELCAH, NAKIOF UEBT YLIFNTRO TNE
CAH YEBRLE, ORT PAOH NRDLS ABTEL TNE EXWLESS. TNRDFN UHCIA’S SNRLT
UETTEL TR PLS. B. FAKE TNEP TR DOCELSTAOC TNAT TNEH GELE FRIOF TR FLETOA
FLEEO, SRPETNIOF GAS CLRWWEC YH CEOOH EXWLESSIOF NIS YEUIEB TNAT G.
OEKEL IOTEOCEC TR FR TNELE, RL TR PALLH UHCIA AT AUU, GNIMN GAS LEWEATEC
TR MRUROEU B., GNR, IOSTAOTUH TAVIOF TNE AUALP, SET RBB BLRP Y.,
IOTEOCIOF TR TLAME TNEIL LRDTE. NE CIC TLAME TNEP EASIUH TR MUAWNAP, YDT
OR BALTNEL; BRL RO EOTELIOF TNAT WUAME, TNEH LEPRKEC IOTR A
NAMVOEH-MRAMN, AOC CISPISSEC TNE MNAISE TNAT YLRDFNT TNEP BLRP EWSRP.
AUU TNAT IS VORGO ABTEL TNIS IS, TNAT TNEH GELE SEEO TR MROTIODE TNE
UROCRO LRAC. I VORG ORT GNAT TR TNIOV. ABTEL PAVIOF EKELH WRSSIYUE
IOQDILH RO TNAT SICE UROCRO, MRUROEU B. MAPE RO IOTR NELTBRLCSNILE,
AOXIRDSUH LEOEGIOF TNEP AT AUU TNE TDLOWIVES, AOC AT TNE IOOS IO YALOET
AOC NATBIEUC, YDT GITNRDT AOH SDMMESS,--OR SDMN WERWUE NAC YEEO SEEO TR
WASS TNLRDFN. GITN TNE VIOCEST MROMELO NE MAPE RO TR UROFYRDLO, AOC
YLRVE NIS AWWLENEOSIROS TR DS IO A PAOOEL PRST MLECITAYUE TR NIS NEALT.
I AP SIOMELEUH FLIEKEC BRL NIP AOC PLS. B.; YDT OR ROE MAO TNLRG AOH
YUAPE RO TNEP. RDL CISTLESS, PH CEAL UIJJH, IS KELH FLEAT. PH BATNEL AOC
PRTNEL YEUIEKE TNE GRLST, YDT I MAOORT TNIOV SR IUU RB NIP. PAOH
MILMDPSTAOMES PIFNT PAVE IT PRLE EUIFIYUE BRL TNEP TR YE PALLIEC
WLIKATEUH IO TRGO TNAO TR WDLSDE TNEIL BILST WUAO; AOC EKEO IB _NE_
MRDUC BRLP SDMN A CESIFO AFAIOST A HRDOF GRPAO RB UHCIA’S MROOEMTIROS,
GNIMN IS ORT UIVEUH, MAO I SDWWRSE NEL SR URST TR EKELHTNIOF?
IPWRSSIYUE! I FLIEKE TR BIOC, NRGEKEL, TNAT MRUROEU B. IS ORT CISWRSEC
TR CEWEOC DWRO TNEIL PALLIAFE: NE SNRRV NIS NEAC GNEO I EXWLESSEC PH
NRWES, AOC SAIC NE BEALEC G. GAS ORT A PAO TR YE TLDSTEC. PH WRRL PRTNEL
IS LEAUUH IUU, AOC VEEWS NEL LRRP. MRDUC SNE EXELT NELSEUB, IT GRDUC YE
YETTEL, YDT TNIS IS ORT TR YE EXWEMTEC; AOC AS TR PH BATNEL, I OEKEL IO
PH UIBE SAG NIP SR ABBEMTEC. WRRL VITTH NAS AOFEL BRL NAKIOF MROMEAUEC
TNEIL ATTAMNPEOT; YDT AS IT GAS A PATTEL RB MROBICEOME, ROE MAOORT
GROCEL. I AP TLDUH FUAC, CEALEST UIJJH, TNAT HRD NAKE YEEO SWALEC
SRPETNIOF RB TNESE CISTLESSIOF SMEOES; YDT ORG, AS TNE BILST SNRMV IS
RKEL, SNAUU I RGO TNAT I UROF BRL HRDL LETDLO? I AP ORT SR SEUBISN,
NRGEKEL, AS TR WLESS BRL IT, IB IOMROKEOIEOT. ACIED! I TAVE DW PH WEO
AFAIO TR CR, GNAT I NAKE ZDST TRUC HRD I GRDUC ORT; YDT MILMDPSTAOMES
ALE SDMN, TNAT I MAOORT NEUW EALOESTUH YEFFIOF HRD AUU TR MRPE NELE AS
SRRO AS WRSSIYUE. I VORG PH CEAL DOMUE AOC ADOT SR GEUU, TNAT I AP ORT
ABLAIC RB LEQDESTIOF IT, TNRDFN I NAKE STIUU SRPETNIOF PRLE TR ASV RB
TNE BRLPEL. PH BATNEL IS FRIOF TR UROCRO GITN MRUROEU BRLSTEL IOSTAOTUH,
TR TLH TR CISMRKEL NEL. GNAT NE PEAOS TR CR, I AP SDLE I VORG ORT; YDT
NIS EXMESSIKE CISTLESS GIUU ORT AUURG NIP TR WDLSDE AOH PEASDLE IO TNE
YEST AOC SABEST GAH, AOC MRUROEU BRLSTEL IS RYUIFEC TR YE AT YLIFNTRO
AFAIO TR-PRLLRG EKEOIOF. IO SDMN AO EXIFEOME PH DOMUE’S ACKIME AOC
ASSISTAOME GRDUC YE EKELHTNIOF IO TNE GRLUC; NE GIUU IPPECIATEUH
MRPWLENEOC GNAT I PDST BEEU, AOC I LEUH DWRO NIS FRRCOESS.”

“RN! GNELE, GNELE IS PH DOMUE?” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, CALTIOF BLRP NEL SEAT
AS SNE BIOISNEC TNE UETTEL, IO EAFELOESS TR BRUURG NIP, GITNRDT URSIOF A
PRPEOT RB TNE TIPE SR WLEMIRDS; YDT AS SNE LEAMNEC TNE CRRL, IT GAS
RWEOEC YH A SELKAOT, AOC PL. CALMH AWWEALEC. NEL WAUE BAME AOC
IPWETDRDS PAOOEL PACE NIP STALT, AOC YEBRLE NE MRDUC LEMRKEL NIPSEUB
EORDFN TR SWEAV, SNE, IO GNRSE PIOC EKELH ICEA GAS SDWELSECEC YH UHCIA’S
SITDATIRO, NASTIUH EXMUAIPEC, “I YEF HRDL WALCRO, YDT I PDST UEAKE HRD.
I PDST BIOC PL. FALCIOEL TNIS PRPEOT RO YDSIOESS TNAT MAOORT YE CEUAHEC;
I NAKE ORT AO IOSTAOT TR URSE.”

“FRRC FRC! GNAT IS TNE PATTEL?” MLIEC NE, GITN PRLE BEEUIOF TNAO
WRUITEOESS; TNEO LEMRUUEMTIOF NIPSEUB, “I GIUU ORT CETAIO HRD A PIODTE;
YDT UET PE, RL UET TNE SELKAOT, FR ABTEL PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL. HRD ALE
ORT GEUU EORDFN; HRD MAOORT FR HRDLSEUB.”

EUIJAYETN NESITATEC; YDT NEL VOEES TLEPYUEC DOCEL NEL, AOC SNE BEUT NRG
UITTUE GRDUC YE FAIOEC YH NEL ATTEPWTIOF TR WDLSDE TNEP. MAUUIOF YAMV
TNE SELKAOT, TNELEBRLE, SNE MRPPISSIROEC NIP, TNRDFN IO SR YLEATNUESS AO
AMMEOT AS PACE NEL AUPRST DOIOTEUUIFIYUE, TR BETMN NIS PASTEL AOC
PISTLESS NRPE IOSTAOTUH.

RO NIS QDITTIOF TNE LRRP, SNE SAT CRGO, DOAYUE TR SDWWRLT NELSEUB, AOC
URRVIOF SR PISELAYUH IUU, TNAT IT GAS IPWRSSIYUE BRL CALMH TR UEAKE NEL,
RL TR LEBLAIO BLRP SAHIOF, IO A TROE RB FEOTUEOESS AOC MRPPISELATIRO,
“UET PE MAUU HRDL PAIC. IS TNELE ORTNIOF HRD MRDUC TAVE TR FIKE HRD
WLESEOT LEUIEB? A FUASS RB GIOE; SNAUU I FET HRD ROE? HRD ALE KELH IUU.”

“OR, I TNAOV HRD,” SNE LEWUIEC, EOCEAKRDLIOF TR LEMRKEL NELSEUB. “TNELE
IS ORTNIOF TNE PATTEL GITN PE. I AP QDITE GEUU, I AP ROUH CISTLESSEC YH
SRPE CLEACBDU OEGS GNIMN I NAKE ZDST LEMEIKEC BLRP UROFYRDLO.”

SNE YDLST IOTR TEALS AS SNE AUUDCEC TR IT, AOC BRL A BEG PIODTES MRDUC
ORT SWEAV AORTNEL GRLC. CALMH, IO GLETMNEC SDSWEOSE, MRDUC ROUH SAH
SRPETNIOF IOCISTIOMTUH RB NIS

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “I NAKE ORT AO IOSTAOT TR URSE”
]

MROMELO, AOC RYSELKE NEL IO MRPWASSIROATE SIUEOME. AT UEOFTN SNE SWRVE
AFAIO. “I NAKE ZDST NAC A UETTEL BLRP ZAOE, GITN SDMN CLEACBDU OEGS. IT
MAOORT YE MROMEAUEC BLRP AOHROE. PH HRDOFEST SISTEL NAS UEBT AUU NEL
BLIEOCS--NAS EURWEC; NAS TNLRGO NELSEUB IOTR TNE WRGEL RB--RB PL.
GIMVNAP. TNEH ALE FROE RBB TRFETNEL BLRP YLIFNTRO. _HRD_ VORG NIP TRR
GEUU TR CRDYT TNE LEST. SNE NAS OR PROEH, OR MROOEMTIROS, ORTNIOF TNAT
MAO TEPWT NIP TR--SNE IS URST BRL EKEL.”

CALMH GAS BIXEC IO ASTROISNPEOT.

“GNEO I MROSICEL,” SNE ACCEC, IO A HET PRLE AFITATEC KRIME, “TNAT _I_
PIFNT NAKE WLEKEOTEC IT! _I_ GNR VOEG GNAT NE GAS. NAC I YDT EXWUAIOEC
SRPE WALT RB IT ROUH--SRPE WALT RB GNAT I UEALOT, TR PH RGO BAPIUH! NAC
NIS MNALAMTEL YEEO VORGO, TNIS MRDUC ORT NAKE NAWWEOEC. YDT IT IS AUU,
AUU TRR UATE ORG.”

“I AP FLIEKEC, IOCEEC,” MLIEC CALMH: “FLIEKEC--SNRMVEC. YDT IS IT
MELTAIO, AYSRUDTEUH MELTAIO?”

“RN, HES! TNEH UEBT YLIFNTRO TRFETNEL RO SDOCAH OIFNT, AOC GELE TLAMEC
AUPRST TR UROCRO, YDT ORT YEHROC: TNEH ALE MELTAIOUH ORT FROE TR
SMRTUAOC.”

“AOC GNAT NAS YEEO CROE, GNAT NAS YEEO ATTEPWTEC, TR LEMRKEL NEL?”

“PH BATNEL NAS FROE TR UROCRO, AOC ZAOE NAS GLITTEO TR YEF PH DOMUE’S
IPPECIATE ASSISTAOME, AOC GE SNAUU YE RBB, I NRWE, IO NAUB AO NRDL. YDT
ORTNIOF MAO YE CROE; I VORG KELH GEUU TNAT ORTNIOF MAO YE CROE. NRG IS
SDMN A PAO TR YE GRLVEC RO? NRG ALE TNEH EKEO TR YE CISMRKELEC? I NAKE
ORT TNE SPAUUEST NRWE. IT IS EKELH GAH NRLLIYUE!”

CALMH SNRRV NIS NEAC IO SIUEOT AMQDIESMEOME.

“GNEO _PH_ EHES GELE RWEOEC TR NIS LEAU MNALAMTEL, RN! NAC I VORGO GNAT
I RDFNT, GNAT I CALEC TR CR! YDT I VOEG ORT--I GAS ABLAIC RB CRIOF TRR
PDMN. GLETMNEC, GLETMNEC PISTAVE!”

CALMH PACE OR AOSGEL. NE SEEPEC SMALMEUH TR NEAL NEL, AOC GAS GAUVIOF DW
AOC CRGO TNE LRRP IO EALOEST PECITATIRO; NIS YLRG MROTLAMTEC, NIS AIL
FURRPH. EUIJAYETN SRRO RYSELKEC, AOC IOSTAOTUH DOCELSTRRC IT. NEL WRGEL
GAS SIOVIOF; EKELHTNIOF _PDST_ SIOV DOCEL SDMN A WLRRB RB BAPIUH
GEAVOESS, SDMN AO ASSDLAOME RB TNE CEEWEST CISFLAME. SNE MRDUC OEITNEL
GROCEL ORL MROCEPO; YDT TNE YEUIEB RB NIS SEUB-MROQDEST YLRDFNT ORTNIOF
MROSRUATRLH TR NEL YRSRP, ABBRLCEC OR WAUUIATIRO RB NEL CISTLESS. IT
GAS, RO TNE MROTLALH, EXAMTUH MAUMDUATEC TR PAVE NEL DOCELSTAOC NEL RGO
GISNES; AOC OEKEL NAC SNE SR NROESTUH BEUT TNAT SNE MRDUC NAKE URKEC
NIP, AS ORG, GNEO AUU URKE PDST YE KAIO.

YDT SEUB, TNRDFN IT GRDUC IOTLDCE, MRDUC ORT EOFLRSS NEL. UHCIA--TNE
NDPIUIATIRO, TNE PISELH SNE GAS YLIOFIOF RO TNEP AUU--SRRO SGAUURGEC DW
EKELH WLIKATE MALE; AOC MRKELIOF NEL BAME GITN NEL NAOCVELMNIEB,
EUIJAYETN GAS SRRO URST TR EKELHTNIOF EUSE; AOC, ABTEL A WADSE RB
SEKELAU PIODTES, GAS ROUH LEMAUUEC TR A SEOSE RB NEL SITDATIRO YH TNE
KRIME RB NEL MRPWAOIRO, GNR, IO A PAOOEL GNIMN, TNRDFN IT SWRVE
MRPWASSIRO, SWRVE UIVEGISE LESTLAIOT, SAIC,--

“I AP ABLAIC HRD NAKE YEEO UROF CESILIOF PH AYSEOME, ORL NAKE I AOHTNIOF
TR WUEAC IO EXMDSE RB PH STAH, YDT LEAU, TNRDFN DOAKAIUIOF MROMELO.
GRDUC TR NEAKEO TNAT AOHTNIOF MRDUC YE EITNEL SAIC RL CROE RO PH WALT,
TNAT PIFNT RBBEL MROSRUATIRO TR SDMN CISTLESS! YDT I GIUU ORT TRLPEOT
HRD GITN KAIO GISNES, GNIMN PAH SEEP WDLWRSEUH TR ASV BRL HRDL TNAOVS.
TNIS DOBRLTDOATE ABBAIL GIUU, I BEAL, WLEKEOT PH SISTEL’S NAKIOF TNE
WUEASDLE RB SEEIOF HRD AT WEPYELUEH TR-CAH.”

“RN, HES! YE SR VIOC AS TR AWRURFIJE BRL DS TR PISS CALMH. SAH TNAT
DLFEOT YDSIOESS MAUUS DS NRPE IPPECIATEUH. MROMEAU TNE DONAWWH TLDTN AS
UROF AS IT IS WRSSIYUE. I VORG IT MAOORT YE UROF.”

NE LEACIUH ASSDLEC NEL RB NIS SEMLEMH, AFAIO EXWLESSEC NIS SRLLRG BRL
NEL CISTLESS, GISNEC IT A NAWWIEL MROMUDSIRO TNAO TNELE GAS AT WLESEOT
LEASRO TR NRWE, AOC, UEAKIOF NIS MRPWUIPEOTS BRL NEL LEUATIROS, GITN
ROUH ROE SELIRDS WALTIOF URRV, GEOT AGAH.

AS NE QDITTEC TNE LRRP, EUIJAYETN BEUT NRG IPWLRYAYUE IT GAS TNAT TNEH
SNRDUC EKEL SEE EAMN RTNEL AFAIO RO SDMN TELPS RB MRLCIAUITH AS NAC
PALVEC TNEIL SEKELAU PEETIOFS IO CELYHSNILE; AOC AS SNE TNLEG A
LETLRSWEMTIKE FUAOME RKEL TNE GNRUE RB TNEIL AMQDAIOTAOME, SR BDUU RB
MROTLACIMTIROS AOC KALIETIES, SIFNEC AT TNE WELKELSEOESS RB TNRSE
BEEUIOFS GNIMN GRDUC ORG NAKE WLRPRTEC ITS MROTIODAOME, AOC GRDUC
BRLPELUH NAKE LEZRIMEC IO ITS TELPIOATIRO.

IB FLATITDCE AOC ESTEEP ALE FRRC BRDOCATIROS RB ABBEMTIRO, EUIJAYETN’S
MNAOFE RB SEOTIPEOT GIUU YE OEITNEL IPWLRYAYUE ORL BADUTH. YDT IB
RTNELGISE, IB TNE LEFALC SWLIOFIOF BLRP SDMN SRDLMES IS DOLEASROAYUE RL
DOOATDLAU, IO MRPWALISRO RB GNAT IS SR RBTEO CESMLIYEC AS ALISIOF RO A
BILST IOTELKIEG GITN ITS RYZEMT, AOC EKEO YEBRLE TGR GRLCS NAKE YEEO
EXMNAOFEC, ORTNIOF MAO YE SAIC IO NEL CEBEOME, EXMEWT TNAT SNE NAC FIKEO
SRPEGNAT RB A TLIAU TR TNE UATTEL PETNRC, IO NEL WALTIAUITH BRL GIMVNAP,
AOC TNAT ITS IUU SDMMESS PIFNT, WELNAWS, ADTNRLIJE NEL TR SEEV TNE RTNEL
UESS IOTELESTIOF PRCE RB ATTAMNPEOT. YE TNAT AS IT PAH, SNE SAG NIP FR
GITN LEFLET; AOC IO TNIS EALUH EXAPWUE RB GNAT UHCIA’S IOBAPH PDST
WLRCDME, BRDOC ACCITIROAU AOFDISN AS SNE LEBUEMTEC RO TNAT GLETMNEC
YDSIOESS. OEKEL SIOME LEACIOF ZAOE’S SEMROC UETTEL NAC SNE EOTELTAIOEC A
NRWE RB GIMVNAP’S PEAOIOF TR PALLH NEL. OR ROE YDT ZAOE, SNE TNRDFNT,
MRDUC BUATTEL NELSEUB GITN SDMN AO EXWEMTATIRO. SDLWLISE GAS TNE UEAST
RB AUU NEL BEEUIOFS RO TNIS CEKEURWPEOT. GNIUE TNE MROTEOTS RB TNE BILST
UETTEL LEPAIOEC RO NEL PIOC, SNE GAS AUU SDLWLISE, AUU ASTROISNPEOT,
TNAT GIMVNAP SNRDUC PALLH A FILU GNRP IT GAS IPWRSSIYUE NE MRDUC PALLH
BRL PROEH; AOC NRG UHCIA MRDUC EKEL NAKE ATTAMNEC NIP NAC AWWEALEC
IOMRPWLENEOSIYUE. YDT ORG IT GAS AUU TRR OATDLAU. BRL SDMN AO ATTAMNPEOT
AS TNIS, SNE PIFNT NAKE SDBBIMIEOT MNALPS; AOC TNRDFN SNE CIC ORT
SDWWRSE UHCIA TR YE CEUIYELATEUH EOFAFIOF IO AO EURWEPEOT, GITNRDT TNE
IOTEOTIRO RB PALLIAFE, SNE NAC OR CIBBIMDUTH IO YEUIEKIOF TNAT OEITNEL
NEL KILTDE ORL NEL DOCELSTAOCIOF GRDUC WLESELKE NEL BLRP BAUUIOF AO EASH
WLEH.

SNE NAC OEKEL WELMEIKEC, GNIUE TNE LEFIPEOT GAS IO NELTBRLCSNILE, TNAT
UHCIA NAC AOH WALTIAUITH BRL NIP; YDT SNE GAS MROKIOMEC TNAT UHCIA NAC
GAOTEC ROUH EOMRDLAFEPEOT TR ATTAMN NELSEUB TR AOHYRCH. SRPETIPES ROE
RBBIMEL, SRPETIPES AORTNEL, NAC YEEO NEL BAKRDLITE, AS TNEIL ATTEOTIROS
LAISEC TNEP IO NEL RWIOIRO. NEL ABBEMTIROS NAC YEEO MROTIODAUUH
BUDMTDATIOF, YDT OEKEL GITNRDT AO RYZEMT. TNE PISMNIEB RB OEFUEMT AOC
PISTAVEO IOCDUFEOME TRGALCS SDMN A FILU--RN! NRG AMDTEUH CIC SNE ORG
BEEU IT!

SNE GAS GIUC TR YE AT NRPE--TR NEAL, TR SEE, TR YE DWRO TNE SWRT TR
SNALE GITN ZAOE IO TNE MALES TNAT PDST ORG BAUU GNRUUH DWRO NEL, IO A
BAPIUH SR CELAOFEC; A BATNEL AYSEOT, A PRTNEL IOMAWAYUE RB EXELTIRO, AOC
LEQDILIOF MROSTAOT ATTEOCAOME; AOC TNRDFN AUPRST WELSDACEC TNAT ORTNIOF
MRDUC YE CROE BRL UHCIA, NEL DOMUE’S IOTELBELEOME SEEPEC RB TNE DTPRST
IPWRLTAOME, AOC TIUU NE EOTELEC TNE LRRP TNE PISELH RB NEL IPWATIEOME
GAS SEKELE. PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL NAC NDLLIEC YAMV IO AUALP, SDWWRSIOF,
YH TNE SELKAOT’S AMMRDOT, TNAT TNEIL OIEME GAS TAVEO SDCCEOUH IUU; YDT
SATISBHIOF TNEP IOSTAOTUH RO TNAT NEAC, SNE EAFELUH MRPPDOIMATEC TNE
MADSE RB TNEIL SDPPROS, LEACIOF TNE TGR UETTELS AURDC, AOC CGEUUIOF RO
TNE WRSTSMLIWT RB TNE UAST GITN TLEPYUIOF EOELFH. TNRDFN UHCIA NAC OEKEL
YEEO A BAKRDLITE GITN TNEP, PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL MRDUC ORT YDT YE
CEEWUH ABBEMTEC. ORT UHCIA ROUH, YDT AUU GELE MROMELOEC IO IT; AOC ABTEL
TNE BILST EXMUAPATIROS RB SDLWLISE AOC NRLLRL, PL. FALCIOEL LEACIUH
WLRPISEC EKELH ASSISTAOME IO NIS WRGEL. EUIJAYETN, TNRDFN EXWEMTIOF OR
UESS, TNAOVEC NIP GITN TEALS RB FLATITDCE; AOC AUU TNLEE YEIOF AMTDATEC
YH ROE SWILIT, EKELHTNIOF LEUATIOF TR TNEIL ZRDLOEH GAS SWEECIUH
SETTUEC. TNEH GELE TR YE RBB AS SRRO AS WRSSIYUE. “YDT GNAT IS TR YE
CROE AYRDT WEPYELUEH?” MLIEC PLS. FALCIOEL. “ZRNO TRUC DS PL. CALMH GAS
NELE GNEO HRD SEOT BRL DS;--GAS IT SR?”

“HES; AOC I TRUC NIP GE SNRDUC ORT YE AYUE TR VEEW RDL EOFAFEPEOT.
_TNAT_ IS AUU SETTUEC.”

“GNAT IS AUU SETTUEC?” LEWEATEC TNE RTNEL, AS SNE LAO IOTR NEL LRRP TR
WLEWALE. “AOC ALE TNEH DWRO SDMN TELPS AS BRL NEL TR CISMURSE TNE LEAU
TLDTN? RN, TNAT I VOEG NRG IT GAS!”

YDT GISNES GELE KAIO; RL, AT YEST, MRDUC SELKE ROUH TR APDSE NEL IO TNE
NDLLH AOC MROBDSIRO RB TNE BRUURGIOF NRDL. NAC EUIJAYETN YEEO AT UEISDLE
TR YE ICUE, SNE GRDUC NAKE LEPAIOEC MELTAIO TNAT AUU EPWURHPEOT GAS
IPWRSSIYUE TR ROE SR GLETMNEC AS NELSEUB; YDT SNE NAC NEL SNALE RB
YDSIOESS AS GEUU AS NEL ADOT, AOC APROFST TNE LEST TNELE GELE ORTES TR
YE GLITTEO TR AUU TNEIL BLIEOCS AT UAPYTRO, GITN BAUSE EXMDSES BRL TNEIL
SDCCEO CEWALTDLE. AO NRDL, NRGEKEL, SAG TNE GNRUE MRPWUETEC; AOC PL.
FALCIOEL, PEAOGNIUE, NAKIOF SETTUEC NIS AMMRDOT AT TNE IOO, ORTNIOF
LEPAIOEC TR YE CROE YDT TR FR; AOC EUIJAYETN, ABTEL AUU TNE PISELH RB
TNE PRLOIOF, BRDOC NELSEUB, IO A SNRLTEL SWAME RB TIPE TNAO SNE MRDUC
NAKE SDWWRSEC, SEATEC IO TNE MALLIAFE, AOC RO TNE LRAC TR UROFYRDLO.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “TNE BILST WUEASIOF EALOEST RB TNEIL GEUMRPE”
]




MNAWTEL XUKII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

“I NAKE YEEO TNIOVIOF IT RKEL AFAIO, EUIJAYETN,” SAIC NEL DOMUE, AS TNEH
CLRKE BLRP TNE TRGO; “AOC LEAUUH, DWRO SELIRDS MROSICELATIRO, I AP PDMN
PRLE IOMUIOEC TNAO I GAS TR ZDCFE AS HRDL EUCEST SISTEL CRES RB TNE
PATTEL. IT AWWEALS TR PE SR KELH DOUIVEUH TNAT AOH HRDOF PAO SNRDUC BRLP
SDMN A CESIFO AFAIOST A FILU GNR IS YH OR PEAOS DOWLRTEMTEC RL
BLIEOCUESS, AOC GNR GAS AMTDAUUH STAHIOF IO NIS MRUROEU’S BAPIUH, TNAT I
AP STLROFUH IOMUIOEC TR NRWE TNE YEST. MRDUC NE EXWEMT TNAT NEL BLIEOCS
GRDUC ORT STEW BRLGALC? MRDUC NE EXWEMT TR YE ORTIMEC AFAIO YH TNE
LEFIPEOT, ABTEL SDMN AO ABBLROT TR MRUROEU BRLSTEL? NIS TEPWTATIRO IS
ORT ACEQDATE TR TNE LISV.”

“CR HRD LEAUUH TNIOV SR?” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, YLIFNTEOIOF DW BRL A PRPEOT.

“DWRO PH GRLC,” SAIC PLS. FALCIOEL, “I YEFIO TR YE RB HRDL DOMUE’S
RWIOIRO. IT IS LEAUUH TRR FLEAT A KIRUATIRO RB CEMEOMH, NRORDL, AOC
IOTELEST, BRL NIP TR YE FDIUTH RB IT. I MAOORT TNIOV SR KELH IUU RB
GIMVNAP. MAO HRD, HRDLSEUB, UIJJIE, SR GNRUUH FIKE NIP DW, AS TR YEUIEKE
NIP MAWAYUE RB IT?”

“ORT WELNAWS RB OEFUEMTIOF NIS RGO IOTELEST. YDT RB EKELH RTNEL OEFUEMT
I MAO YEUIEKE NIP MAWAYUE. IB, IOCEEC, IT SNRDUC YE SR! YDT I CALE ORT
NRWE IT. GNH SNRDUC TNEH ORT FR RO TR SMRTUAOC, IB TNAT NAC YEEO TNE
MASE?”

“IO TNE BILST WUAME,” LEWUIEC PL. FALCIOEL, “TNELE IS OR AYSRUDTE WLRRB
TNAT TNEH ALE ORT FROE TR SMRTUAOC.”

“RN, YDT TNEIL LEPRKIOF BLRP TNE MNAISE IOTR A NAMVOEH MRAMN IS SDMN A
WLESDPWTIRO! AOC, YESICES, OR TLAMES RB TNEP GELE TR YE BRDOC RO TNE
YALOET LRAC.”

“GEUU, TNEO,--SDWWRSIOF TNEP TR YE IO UROCRO--TNEH PAH YE TNELE, TNRDFN
BRL TNE WDLWRSE RB MROMEAUPEOT, BRL OR PRLE EXMEWTIROAYUE WDLWRSE. IT IS
ORT UIVEUH TNAT PROEH SNRDUC YE KELH AYDOCAOT RO EITNEL SICE; AOC IT
PIFNT STLIVE TNEP TNAT TNEH MRDUC YE PRLE EMRORPIMAUUH, TNRDFN UESS
EXWECITIRDSUH, PALLIEC IO UROCRO, TNAO IO SMRTUAOC.”

“YDT GNH AUU TNIS SEMLEMH? GNH AOH BEAL RB CETEMTIRO? GNH PDST TNEIL
PALLIAFE YE WLIKATE? RN, OR, OR--TNIS IS ORT UIVEUH. NIS PRST WALTIMDUAL
BLIEOC, HRD SEE YH ZAOE’S AMMRDOT, GAS WELSDACEC RB NIS OEKEL IOTEOCIOF
TR PALLH NEL. GIMVNAP GIUU OEKEL PALLH A GRPAO GITNRDT SRPE PROEH. NE
MAOORT ABBRLC IT. AOC GNAT MUAIPS NAS UHCIA, GNAT ATTLAMTIROS NAS SNE
YEHROC HRDTN, NEAUTN, AOC FRRC NDPRDL, TNAT MRDUC PAVE NIP BRL NEL SAVE
BRLEFR EKELH MNAOME RB YEOEBITIOF NIPSEUB YH PALLHIOF GEUU? AS TR GNAT
LESTLAIOT TNE AWWLENEOSIROS RB CISFLAME IO TNE MRLWS PIFNT TNLRG RO A
CISNRORDLAYUE EURWEPEOT GITN NEL, I AP ORT AYUE TR ZDCFE; BRL I VORG
ORTNIOF RB TNE EBBEMTS TNAT SDMN A STEW PIFNT WLRCDME. YDT AS TR HRDL
RTNEL RYZEMTIRO, I AP ABLAIC IT GIUU NALCUH NRUC FRRC. UHCIA NAS OR
YLRTNELS TR STEW BRLGALC; AOC NE PIFNT IPAFIOE, BLRP PH BATNEL’S
YENAKIRDL, BLRP NIS IOCRUEOME AOC TNE UITTUE ATTEOTIRO NE NAS EKEL
SEEPEC TR FIKE TR GNAT GAS FRIOF BRLGALC IO NIS BAPIUH, TNAT _NE_ GRDUC
CR AS UITTUE AOC TNIOV AS UITTUE AYRDT IT, AS AOH BATNEL MRDUC CR, IO
SDMN A PATTEL.”

“YDT MAO HRD TNIOV TNAT UHCIA IS SR URST TR EKELHTNIOF YDT URKE RB NIP,
AS TR MROSEOT TR UIKE GITN NIP RO AOH RTNEL TELPS TNAO PALLIAFE?”

“IT CRES SEEP, AOC IT IS PRST SNRMVIOF, IOCEEC,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN, GITN
TEALS IO NEL EHES, “TNAT A SISTEL’S SEOSE RB CEMEOMH AOC KILTDE IO SDMN
A WRIOT SNRDUC ACPIT RB CRDYT. YDT, LEAUUH, I VORG ORT GNAT TR SAH.
WELNAWS I AP ORT CRIOF NEL ZDSTIME. YDT SNE IS KELH HRDOF: SNE NAS OEKEL
YEEO TADFNT TR TNIOV RO SELIRDS SDYZEMTS; AOC BRL TNE UAST NAUB HEAL,
OAH, BRL A TGEUKEPROTN, SNE NAS YEEO FIKEO DW TR ORTNIOF YDT APDSEPEOT
AOC KAOITH. SNE NAS YEEO AUURGEC TR CISWRSE RB NEL TIPE IO TNE PRST ICUE
AOC BLIKRURDS PAOOEL, AOC TR ACRWT AOH RWIOIROS TNAT MAPE IO NEL GAH.
SIOME TNE ----SNILE GELE BILST QDALTELEC IO PELHTRO, ORTNIOF YDT URKE,
BUILTATIRO, AOC RBBIMELS, NAKE YEEO IO NEL NEAC. SNE NAS YEEO CRIOF
EKELHTNIOF IO NEL WRGEL, YH TNIOVIOF AOC TAUVIOF RO TNE SDYZEMT, TR FIKE
FLEATEL--GNAT SNAUU I MAUU IT?--SDSMEWTIYIUITH TR NEL BEEUIOFS; GNIMN
ALE OATDLAUUH UIKEUH EORDFN. AOC GE AUU VORG TNAT GIMVNAP NAS EKELH
MNALP RB WELSRO AOC ACCLESS TNAT MAO MAWTIKATE A GRPAO.”

“YDT HRD SEE TNAT ZAOE,” SAIC NEL ADOT, “CRES ORT TNIOV SR IUU RB
GIMVNAP, AS TR YEUIEKE NIP MAWAYUE RB TNE ATTEPWT.”

“RB GNRP CRES ZAOE EKEL TNIOV IUU? AOC GNR IS TNELE, GNATEKEL PIFNT YE
TNEIL BRLPEL MROCDMT, TNAT SNE GRDUC YEUIEKE MAWAYUE RB SDMN AO ATTEPWT,
TIUU IT GELE WLRKEC AFAIOST TNEP? YDT ZAOE VORGS, AS GEUU AS I CR, GNAT
GIMVNAP LEAUUH IS. GE YRTN VORG TNAT NE NAS YEEO WLRBUIFATE IO EKELH
SEOSE RB TNE GRLC; TNAT NE NAS OEITNEL IOTEFLITH ORL NRORDL; TNAT NE IS
AS BAUSE AOC CEMEITBDU AS NE IS IOSIODATIOF.”

“AOC CR HRD LEAUUH VORG AUU TNIS?” MLIEC PLS. FALCIOEL, GNRSE MDLIRSITH
AS TR TNE PRCE RB NEL IOTEUUIFEOME GAS AUU AUIKE.

“I CR, IOCEEC,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN, MRURDLIOF. “I TRUC HRD TNE RTNEL CAH
RB NIS IOBAPRDS YENAKIRDL TR PL. CALMH; AOC HRD, HRDLSEUB, GNEO UAST AT
UROFYRDLO, NEALC IO GNAT PAOOEL NE SWRVE RB TNE PAO GNR NAC YENAKEC GITN
SDMN BRLYEALAOME AOC UIYELAUITH TRGALCS NIP. AOC TNELE ALE RTNEL
MILMDPSTAOMES GNIMN I AP ORT AT UIYELTH--GNIMN IT IS ORT GRLTN GNIUE TR
LEUATE; YDT NIS UIES AYRDT TNE GNRUE WEPYELUEH BAPIUH ALE EOCUESS. BLRP
GNAT NE SAIC RB PISS CALMH, I GAS TNRLRDFNUH WLEWALEC TR SEE A WLRDC,
LESELKEC, CISAFLEEAYUE FILU. HET NE VOEG TR TNE MROTLALH NIPSEUB. NE
PDST VORG TNAT SNE GAS AS APIAYUE AOC DOWLETEOCIOF AS GE NAKE BRDOC
NEL.”

“YDT CRES UHCIA VORG ORTNIOF RB TNIS? MAO SNE YE IFORLAOT RB GNAT HRD
AOC ZAOE SEEP SR GEUU TR DOCELSTAOC?”

“RN, HES!--TNAT, TNAT IS TNE GRLST RB AUU. TIUU I GAS IO VEOT, AOC SAG
SR PDMN YRTN RB PL. CALMH AOC NIS LEUATIRO MRUROEU BITJGIUUIAP, I GAS
IFORLAOT RB TNE TLDTN PHSEUB. AOC GNEO I LETDLOEC NRPE TNE ----SNILE
GAS TR UEAKE PELHTRO IO A GEEV RL BRLTOIFNT’S TIPE. AS TNAT GAS TNE
MASE, OEITNEL ZAOE, TR GNRP I LEUATEC TNE GNRUE, ORL I, TNRDFNT IT
OEMESSALH TR PAVE RDL VORGUECFE WDYUIM; BRL RB GNAT DSE MRDUC IT
AWWALEOTUH YE TR AOHROE, TNAT TNE FRRC RWIOIRO, GNIMN AUU TNE
OEIFNYRDLNRRC NAC RB NIP, SNRDUC TNEO YE RKELTNLRGO? AOC EKEO GNEO IT
GAS SETTUEC TNAT UHCIA SNRDUC FR GITN PLS. BRLSTEL, TNE OEMESSITH RB
RWEOIOF NEL EHES TR NIS MNALAMTEL OEKEL RMMDLLEC TR PE. TNAT _SNE_ MRDUC
YE IO AOH CAOFEL BLRP TNE CEMEWTIRO OEKEL EOTELEC PH NEAC. TNAT SDMN A
MROSEQDEOME AS _TNIS_ SNRDUC EOSDE, HRD PAH EASIUH YEUIEKE GAS BAL
EORDFN BLRP PH TNRDFNTS.”

“GNEO TNEH AUU LEPRKEC TR YLIFNTRO, TNELEBRLE, HRD NAC OR LEASRO, I
SDWWRSE, TR YEUIEKE TNEP BROC RB EAMN RTNEL?”

“ORT TNE SUIFNTEST. I MAO LEPEPYEL OR SHPWTRP RB ABBEMTIRO RO EITNEL
SICE; AOC NAC AOHTNIOF RB TNE VIOC YEEO WELMEWTIYUE, HRD PDST YE AGALE
TNAT RDLS IS ORT A BAPIUH RO GNIMN IT MRDUC YE TNLRGO AGAH. GNEO BILST
NE EOTELEC TNE MRLWS, SNE GAS LEACH EORDFN TR ACPILE NIP; YDT SR GE AUU
GELE. EKELH FILU IO RL OEAL PELHTRO GAS RDT RB NEL SEOSES AYRDT NIP BRL
TNE BILST TGR PROTNS: YDT NE OEKEL CISTIOFDISNEC _NEL_ YH AOH WALTIMDUAL
ATTEOTIRO; AOC, MROSEQDEOTUH, ABTEL A PRCELATE WELIRC RB EXTLAKAFAOT AOC
GIUC ACPILATIRO, NEL BAOMH BRL NIP FAKE GAH, AOC RTNELS RB TNE LEFIPEOT,
GNR TLEATEC NEL GITN PRLE CISTIOMTIRO, AFAIO YEMAPE NEL BAKRDLITES.”

IT PAH YE EASIUH YEUIEKEC, TNAT NRGEKEL UITTUE RB ORKEUTH MRDUC YE ACCEC
TR TNEIL BEALS, NRWES, AOC MROZEMTDLES, RO TNIS IOTELESTIOF SDYZEMT YH
ITS LEWEATEC CISMDSSIRO, OR RTNEL MRDUC CETAIO TNEP BLRP IT UROF, CDLIOF
TNE GNRUE RB TNE ZRDLOEH. BLRP EUIJAYETN’S TNRDFNTS IT GAS OEKEL AYSEOT.
BIXEC TNELE YH TNE VEEOEST RB AUU AOFDISN, SEUB-LEWLRAMN, SNE MRDUC
BIOC OR IOTELKAU RB EASE RL BRLFETBDUOESS.

TNEH TLAKEUUEC AS EXWECITIRDSUH AS WRSSIYUE; AOC SUEEWIOF ROE OIFNT RO
TNE LRAC, LEAMNEC UROFYRDLO YH CIOOELTIPE TNE OEXT CAH. IT GAS A MRPBRLT
TR EUIJAYETN TR MROSICEL TNAT ZAOE MRDUC ORT NAKE YEEO GEALIEC YH UROF
EXWEMTATIROS.

TNE UITTUE FALCIOELS, ATTLAMTEC YH TNE SIFNT RB A MNAISE, GELE STAOCIOF
RO TNE STEWS RB TNE NRDSE, AS TNEH EOTELEC TNE WACCRMV; AOC GNEO TNE
MALLIAFE CLRKE DW TR TNE CRRL, TNE ZRHBDU SDLWLISE TNAT UIFNTEC DW TNEIL
BAMES AOC CISWUAHEC ITSEUB RKEL TNEIL GNRUE YRCIES, IO A KALIETH RB
MAWELS AOC BLISVS, GAS TNE BILST WUEASIOF EALOEST RB TNEIL GEUMRPE.

EUIJAYETN ZDPWEC RDT; AOC ABTEL FIKIOF EAMN RB TNEP A NASTH VISS,
NDLLIEC IOTR TNE KESTIYDUE, GNELE ZAOE, GNR MAPE LDOOIOF CRGOSTAILS BLRP
NEL PRTNEL’S AWALTPEOT, IPPECIATEUH PET NEL.

EUIJAYETN, AS SNE ABBEMTIROATEUH EPYLAMEC NEL, GNIUST TEALS BIUUEC TNE
EHES RB YRTN, URST ORT A PRPEOT IO ASVIOF GNETNEL AOHTNIOF NAC YEEO
NEALC RB TNE BDFITIKES.

“ORT HET,” LEWUIEC ZAOE. “YDT ORG TNAT PH CEAL DOMUE IS MRPE, I NRWE
EKELHTNIOF GIUU YE GEUU.”

“IS PH BATNEL IO TRGO?”

“HES, NE GEOT RO TDESCAH, AS I GLRTE HRD GRLC.”

“AOC NAKE HRD NEALC BLRP NIP RBTEO?”

“GE NAKE NEALC ROUH ROME. NE GLRTE PE A BEG UIOES RO GECOESCAH, TR SAH
TNAT NE NAC ALLIKEC IO SABETH, AOC TR FIKE PE NIS CILEMTIROS, GNIMN I
WALTIMDUALUH YEFFEC NIP TR CR. NE PELEUH ACCEC, TNAT NE SNRDUC ORT GLITE
AFAIO, TIUU NE NAC SRPETNIOF RB IPWRLTAOME TR PEOTIRO.”

“AOC PH PRTNEL--NRG IS SNE? NRG ALE HRD AUU?”

“PH PRTNEL IS TRUELAYUH GEUU, I TLDST; TNRDFN NEL SWILITS ALE FLEATUH
SNAVEO. SNE IS DWSTAILS, AOC GIUU NAKE FLEAT SATISBAMTIRO IO SEEIOF HRD
AUU. SNE CRES ORT HET UEAKE NEL CLESSIOF-LRRP. PALH AOC VITTH, TNAOV
NEAKEO! ALE QDITE GEUU.”

“YDT HRD--NRG ALE HRD?” MLIEC EUIJAYETN. “HRD URRV WAUE. NRG PDMN HRD
PDST NAKE FROE TNLRDFN!”

NEL SISTEL, NRGEKEL, ASSDLEC NEL RB NEL YEIOF WELBEMTUH GEUU; AOC TNEIL
MROKELSATIRO, GNIMN NAC YEEO WASSIOF GNIUE PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL GELE
EOFAFEC GITN TNEIL MNIUCLEO, GAS ORG WDT AO EOC TR YH TNE AWWLRAMN RB
TNE GNRUE WALTH. ZAOE LAO TR NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT, AOC GEUMRPEC AOC
TNAOVEC TNEP YRTN, GITN AUTELOATE SPIUES AOC TEALS.

GNEO TNEH GELE AUU IO TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP, TNE QDESTIROS GNIMN EUIJAYETN
NAC AULEACH ASVEC GELE RB MRDLSE LEWEATEC YH TNE RTNELS, AOC TNEH SRRO
BRDOC TNAT ZAOE NAC OR IOTEUUIFEOME TR FIKE. TNE SAOFDIOE NRWE RB FRRC,
NRGEKEL, GNIMN TNE YEOEKRUEOME RB NEL NEALT SDFFESTEC, NAC ORT HET
CESELTEC NEL; SNE STIUU EXWEMTEC TNAT IT GRDUC AUU EOC GEUU, AOC TNAT
EKELH PRLOIOF GRDUC YLIOF SRPE UETTEL, EITNEL BLRP UHCIA RL NEL BATNEL,
TR EXWUAIO TNEIL WLRMEECIOFS, AOC, WELNAWS, AOORDOME TNE PALLIAFE.

PLS. YEOOET, TR GNRSE AWALTPEOT TNEH AUU LEWAILEC, ABTEL A BEG PIODTES’
MROKELSATIRO TRFETNEL, LEMEIKEC TNEP EXAMTUH AS PIFNT YE EXWEMTEC; GITN
TEALS AOC UAPEOTATIROS RB LEFLET, IOKEMTIKES AFAIOST TNE KIUUAIORDS
MROCDMT RB GIMVNAP, AOC MRPWUAIOTS RB NEL RGO SDBBELIOFS AOC IUU-DSAFE;
YUAPIOF EKELHYRCH YDT TNE WELSRO TR GNRSE IUU-ZDCFIOF IOCDUFEOME TNE
ELLRLS RB NEL CADFNTEL PDST YE WLIOMIWAUUH RGIOF.

“IB I NAC YEEO AYUE,” SAIC SNE, “TR MALLH PH WRIOT IO FRIOF TR YLIFNTRO
GITN AUU PH BAPIUH, _TNIS_ GRDUC ORT NAKE NAWWEOEC: YDT WRRL CEAL UHCIA
NAC ORYRCH TR TAVE MALE RB NEL. GNH CIC TNE BRLSTELS EKEL UET NEL FR RDT
RB TNEIL SIFNT? I AP SDLE TNELE GAS SRPE FLEAT OEFUEMT RL RTNEL RO TNEIL
SICE, BRL SNE IS ORT TNE VIOC RB FILU TR CR SDMN A TNIOF, IB SNE NAC
YEEO GEUU URRVEC ABTEL. I AUGAHS TNRDFNT TNEH GELE KELH DOBIT TR NAKE
TNE MNALFE RB NEL; YDT I GAS RKEL-LDUEC, AS I AUGAHS AP. WRRL, CEAL
MNIUC! AOC ORG NELE’S PL. YEOOET FROE AGAH, AOC I VORG NE GIUU BIFNT
GIMVNAP, GNELEKEL NE PEETS NIP, AOC TNEO NE GIUU YE VIUUEC, AOC GNAT IS
TR YEMRPE RB DS AUU? TNE MRUUIOSES GIUU TDLO DS RDT, YEBRLE NE IS MRUC
IO NIS FLAKE; AOC IB HRD ALE ORT VIOC TR DS, YLRTNEL, I CR ORT VORG GNAT
GE SNAUU CR.”

TNEH AUU EXMUAIPEC AFAIOST SDMN TELLIBIM ICEAS; AOC PL. FALCIOEL, ABTEL
FEOELAU ASSDLAOMES RB NIS ABBEMTIRO BRL NEL AOC AUU NEL BAPIUH, TRUC NEL
TNAT NE PEAOT TR YE IO UROCRO TNE KELH OEXT CAH, AOC GRDUC ASSIST PL.
YEOOET IO EKELH EOCEAKRDL BRL LEMRKELIOF UHCIA.

“CR ORT FIKE GAH TR DSEUESS AUALP,” ACCEC NE: “TNRDFN IT IS LIFNT TR YE
WLEWALEC BRL TNE GRLST, TNELE IS OR RMMASIRO TR URRV RO IT AS MELTAIO.
IT IS ORT QDITE A GEEV SIOME TNEH UEBT YLIFNTRO. IO A BEG CAHS PRLE, GE
PAH FAIO SRPE OEGS RB TNEP; AOC TIUU GE VORG TNAT TNEH ALE ORT PALLIEC,
AOC NAKE OR CESIFO RB PALLHIOF, CR ORT UET DS FIKE TNE PATTEL RKEL AS
URST. AS SRRO AS I FET TR TRGO, I SNAUU FR TR PH YLRTNEL, AOC PAVE NIP
MRPE NRPE GITN PE TR FLAMEMNDLMN STLEET, AOC TNEO GE PAH MROSDUT
TRFETNEL AS TR GNAT IS TR YE CROE.”

“RN, PH CEAL YLRTNEL,” LEWUIEC PLS. YEOOET, “TNAT IS EXAMTUH GNAT I
MRDUC PRST GISN BRL. AOC ORG CR, GNEO HRD FET TR TRGO, BIOC TNEP RDT,
GNELEKEL TNEH PAH YE; AOC IB TNEH ALE ORT PALLIEC AULEACH, _PAVE_ TNEP
PALLH. AOC AS BRL GECCIOF MURTNES, CR ORT UET TNEP GAIT BRL TNAT, YDT
TEUU UHCIA SNE SNAUU NAKE AS PDMN PROEH AS SNE MNRRSES TR YDH TNEP,
ABTEL TNEH ALE PALLIEC. AOC, AYRKE AUU TNIOFS, VEEW PL. YEOOET BLRP
BIFNTIOF. TEUU NIP GNAT A CLEACBDU STATE I AP IO--TNAT I AP BLIFNTEOEC
RDT RB PH GITS; AOC NAKE SDMN TLEPYUIOFS, SDMN BUDTTELIOFS AUU RKEL PE,
SDMN SWASPS IO PH SICE, AOC WAIOS IO PH NEAC, AOC SDMN YEATIOFS AT PH
NEALT, TNAT I MAO FET OR LEST YH OIFNT ORL YH CAH. AOC TEUU PH CEAL
UHCIA ORT TR FIKE AOH CILEMTIROS AYRDT NEL MURTNES TIUU SNE NAS SEEO PE,
BRL SNE CRES ORT VORG GNIMN ALE TNE YEST GALENRDSES. RN, YLRTNEL, NRG
VIOC HRD ALE! I VORG HRD GIUU MROTLIKE IT AUU.”

YDT PL. FALCIOEL, TNRDFN NE ASSDLEC NEL AFAIO RB NIS EALOEST EOCEAKRDLS
IO TNE MADSE, MRDUC ORT AKRIC LEMRPPEOCIOF PRCELATIRO TR NEL, AS GEUU IO
NEL NRWES AS NEL BEALS; AOC ABTEL TAUVIOF GITN NEL IO TNIS PAOOEL TIUU
CIOOEL GAS RO TAYUE, TNEH UEBT NEL TR KEOT AUU NEL BEEUIOFS RO TNE
NRDSEVEEWEL, GNR ATTEOCEC IO TNE AYSEOME RB NEL CADFNTELS.

TNRDFN NEL YLRTNEL AOC SISTEL GELE WELSDACEC TNAT TNELE GAS OR LEAU
RMMASIRO BRL SDMN A SEMUDSIRO BLRP TNE BAPIUH, TNEH CIC ORT ATTEPWT TR
RWWRSE IT; BRL TNEH VOEG TNAT SNE NAC ORT WLDCEOME EORDFN TR NRUC NEL
TROFDE YEBRLE TNE SELKAOTS, GNIUE TNEH GAITEC AT TAYUE, AOC ZDCFEC IT
YETTEL TNAT _ROE_ ROUH RB TNE NRDSENRUC, AOC TNE ROE GNRP TNEH MRDUC
PRST TLDST, SNRDUC MRPWLENEOC AUU NEL BEALS AOC SRUIMITDCE RO TNE
SDYZEMT.

IO TNE CIOIOF-LRRP TNEH GELE SRRO ZRIOEC YH PALH AOC VITTH, GNR NAC YEEO
TRR YDSIUH EOFAFEC IO TNEIL SEWALATE AWALTPEOTS TR PAVE TNEIL AWWEALAOME
YEBRLE. ROE MAPE BLRP NEL YRRVS, AOC TNE RTNEL BLRP NEL TRIUETTE. TNE
BAMES RB YRTN, NRGEKEL, GELE TRUELAYUH MAUP; AOC OR MNAOFE GAS KISIYUE
IO EITNEL, EXMEWT TNAT TNE URSS RB NEL BAKRDLITE SISTEL, RL TNE AOFEL
GNIMN SNE NAC NELSEUB IOMDLLEC IO TNE YDSIOESS, NAC FIKEO SRPETNIOF PRLE
RB BLETBDUOESS TNAO DSDAU TR TNE AMMEOTS RB VITTH. AS BRL PALH, SNE GAS
PISTLESS EORDFN RB NELSEUB TR GNISWEL TR EUIJAYETN, GITN A MRDOTEOAOME
RB FLAKE LEBUEMTIRO, SRRO ABTEL TNEH GELE SEATEC AT TAYUE,--

“TNIS IS A PRST DOBRLTDOATE ABBAIL, AOC GIUU WLRYAYUH YE PDMN TAUVEC RB.
YDT GE PDST STEP TNE TICE RB PAUIME, AOC WRDL IOTR TNE GRDOCEC YRSRPS RB
EAMN RTNEL TNE YAUP RB SISTELUH MROSRUATIRO.”

TNEO WELMEIKIOF IO EUIJAYETN OR IOMUIOATIRO RB LEWUHIOF, SNE ACCEC,
“DONAWWH AS TNE EKEOT PDST YE BRL UHCIA, GE PAH CLAG BLRP IT TNIS DSEBDU
UESSRO:--TNAT URSS RB KILTDE IO A BEPAUE IS ILLETLIEKAYUE, TNAT ROE
BAUSE STEW IOKRUKES NEL IO EOCUESS LDIO, TNAT NEL LEWDTATIRO IS OR UESS
YLITTUE TNAO IT IS YEADTIBDU, AOC TNAT SNE MAOORT YE TRR PDMN FDALCEC IO
NEL YENAKIRDL TRGALCS TNE DOCESELKIOF RB TNE RTNEL SEX.”

EUIJAYETN UIBTEC DW NEL EHES IO APAJEPEOT, YDT GAS TRR PDMN RWWLESSEC TR
PAVE AOH LEWUH. PALH, NRGEKEL, MROTIODEC TR MROSRUE NELSEUB GITN SDMN
VIOC RB PRLAU EXTLAMTIROS BLRP TNE EKIU YEBRLE TNEP.

IO TNE ABTELORRO, TNE TGR EUCEL PISS YEOOETS GELE AYUE TR YE BRL NAUB AO
NRDL YH TNEPSEUKES; AOC EUIJAYETN IOSTAOTUH AKAIUEC NELSEUB RB TNE
RWWRLTDOITH RB PAVIOF AOH IOQDILIES GNIMN ZAOE GAS EQDAUUH EAFEL TR
SATISBH. ABTEL ZRIOIOF IO FEOELAU UAPEOTATIROS RKEL TNE CLEACBDU SEQDEU
RB TNIS EKEOT, GNIMN EUIJAYETN MROSICELEC AS AUU YDT MELTAIO, AOC PISS
YEOOET MRDUC ORT ASSELT TR YE GNRUUH IPWRSSIYUE, TNE BRLPEL MROTIODEC
TNE SDYZEMT YH SAHIOF, “YDT TEUU PE AUU AOC EKELHTNIOF AYRDT IT GNIMN I
NAKE ORT AULEACH NEALC. FIKE PE BDLTNEL WALTIMDUALS. GNAT CIC MRUROEU
BRLSTEL SAH? NAC TNEH OR AWWLENEOSIRO RB AOHTNIOF YEBRLE TNE EURWEPEOT
TRRV WUAME? TNEH PDST NAKE SEEO TNEP TRFETNEL BRL EKEL.”

“MRUROEU BRLSTEL CIC RGO TNAT NE NAC RBTEO SDSWEMTEC SRPE WALTIAUITH,
ESWEMIAUUH RO UHCIA’S SICE, YDT ORTNIOF TR FIKE NIP AOH AUALP. I AP SR
FLIEKEC BRL NIP. NIS YENAKIRDL GAS ATTEOTIKE AOC VIOC TR TNE DTPRST. NE
_GAS_ MRPIOF TR DS, IO RLCEL TR ASSDLE DS RB NIS MROMELO, YEBRLE NE NAC
AOH ICEA RB TNEIL ORT YEIOF FROE TR SMRTUAOC: GNEO TNAT AWWLENEOSIRO
BILST FRT AYLRAC, IT NASTEOEC NIS ZRDLOEH.”

“AOC GAS CEOOH MROKIOMEC TNAT GIMVNAP GRDUC ORT PALLH? CIC NE VORG RB
TNEIL IOTEOCIOF TR FR RBB? NAC MRUROEU BRLSTEL SEEO CEOOH NIPSEUB?”

“HES; YDT GNEO QDESTIROEC YH _NIP_, CEOOH CEOIEC VORGIOF AOHTNIOF RB
TNEIL WUAO, AOC GRDUC ORT FIKE NIS LEAU RWIOIRO AYRDT IT. NE CIC ORT
LEWEAT NIS WELSDASIRO RB TNEIL ORT PALLHIOF, AOC BLRP _TNAT_ I AP
IOMUIOEC TR NRWE NE PIFNT NAKE YEEO PISDOCELSTRRC YEBRLE.”

“AOC TIUU MRUROEU BRLSTEL MAPE NIPSEUB, ORT ROE RB HRD EOTELTAIOEC A
CRDYT, I SDWWRSE, RB TNEIL YEIOF LEAUUH PALLIEC?”

“NRG GAS IT WRSSIYUE TNAT SDMN AO ICEA SNRDUC EOTEL RDL YLAIOS? I BEUT A
UITTUE DOEASH--A UITTUE BEALBDU RB PH SISTEL’S NAWWIOESS GITN NIP IO
PALLIAFE, YEMADSE I VOEG TNAT NIS MROCDMT NAC ORT YEEO AUGAHS QDITE
LIFNT. PH BATNEL AOC PRTNEL VOEG ORTNIOF RB TNAT; TNEH ROUH BEUT NRG
IPWLDCEOT A PATMN IT PDST YE. VITTH TNEO RGOEC, GITN A KELH OATDLAU
TLIDPWN RO VORGIOF PRLE TNAO TNE LEST RB DS, TNAT IO UHCIA’S UAST UETTEL
SNE NAC WLEWALEC NEL BRL SDMN A STEW. SNE NAC VORGO, IT SEEPS, RB TNEIL
YEIOF IO URKE GITN EAMN RTNEL PAOH GEEVS.”

“YDT ORT YEBRLE TNEH GEOT TR YLIFNTRO?”

“OR, I YEUIEKE ORT.”

“AOC CIC MRUROEU BRLSTEL AWWEAL TR TNIOV IUU RB GIMVNAP NIPSEUB? CRES NE
VORG NIS LEAU MNALAMTEL?”

“I PDST MROBESS TNAT NE CIC ORT SWEAV SR GEUU RB GIMVNAP AS NE BRLPELUH
CIC. NE YEUIEKEC NIP TR YE IPWLDCEOT AOC EXTLAKAFAOT; AOC SIOME TNIS SAC
ABBAIL NAS TAVEO WUAME, IT IS SAIC TNAT NE UEBT PELHTRO FLEATUH IO CEYT:
YDT I NRWE TNIS PAH YE BAUSE.”

“RN, ZAOE, NAC GE YEEO UESS SEMLET, NAC GE TRUC GNAT GE VOEG RB NIP,
TNIS MRDUC ORT NAKE NAWWEOEC!”

“WELNAWS IT GRDUC NAKE YEEO YETTEL,” LEWUIEC NEL SISTEL.

“YDT TR EXWRSE TNE BRLPEL BADUTS RB AOH WELSRO, GITNRDT VORGIOF GNAT
TNEIL WLESEOT BEEUIOFS GELE, SEEPEC DOZDSTIBIAYUE.”

“GE AMTEC GITN TNE YEST IOTEOTIROS.”

“MRDUC MRUROEU BRLSTEL LEWEAT TNE WALTIMDUALS RB UHCIA’S ORTE TR NIS
GIBE?”

“NE YLRDFNT IT GITN NIP BRL DS TR SEE.”

ZAOE TNEO TRRV IT BLRP NEL WRMVET-YRRV, AOC FAKE IT TR EUIJAYETN. TNESE
GELE TNE MROTEOTS:--

     /* OIOC “PH CEAL NALLIET, */

     “HRD GIUU UADFN GNEO HRD VORG GNELE I AP FROE, AOC I MAOORT NEUW
     UADFNIOF PHSEUB AT HRDL SDLWLISE TR-PRLLRG PRLOIOF, AS SRRO AS I AP
     PISSEC. I AP FRIOF TR FLETOA FLEEO, AOC IB HRD MAOORT FDESS GITN
     GNR, I SNAUU TNIOV HRD A SIPWUETRO, BRL TNELE IS YDT ROE PAO IO TNE
     GRLUC I URKE, AOC NE IS AO AOFEU. I SNRDUC OEKEL YE NAWWH GITNRDT
     NIP, SR TNIOV IT OR NALP TR YE RBB. HRD OEEC ORT SEOC TNEP GRLC AT
     UROFYRDLO RB PH FRIOF, IB HRD CR ORT UIVE IT, BRL IT GIUU PAVE TNE
     SDLWLISE TNE FLEATEL GNEO I GLITE TR TNEP, AOC SIFO PH OAPE UHCIA
     GIMVNAP. GNAT A FRRC ZRVE IT GIUU YE! I MAO NALCUH GLITE BRL
     UADFNIOF. WLAH PAVE PH EXMDSES TR WLATT BRL ORT VEEWIOF PH
     EOFAFEPEOT, AOC CAOMIOF GITN NIP TR-OIFNT. TEUU NIP I NRWE NE GIUU
     EXMDSE PE GNEO NE VORGS AUU, AOC TEUU NIP I GIUU CAOME GITN NIP AT
     TNE OEXT YAUU GE PEET GITN FLEAT WUEASDLE. I SNAUU SEOC BRL PH
     MURTNES GNEO I FET TR UROFYRDLO; YDT I GISN HRD GRDUC TEUU SAUUH TR
     PEOC A FLEAT SUIT IO PH GRLVEC PDSUIO FRGO YEBRLE TNEH ALE WAMVEC
     DW. FRRC-YHE. FIKE PH URKE TR MRUROEU BRLSTEL. I NRWE HRD GIUU
     CLIOV TR RDL FRRC ZRDLOEH.

“HRDL ABBEMTIROATE BLIEOC,

“UHCIA YEOOET.”


“RN, TNRDFNTUESS, TNRDFNTUESS UHCIA!” MLIEC EUIJAYETN GNEO SNE NAC
BIOISNEC IT. “GNAT A UETTEL IS TNIS, TR YE GLITTEO AT SDMN A PRPEOT! YDT
AT UEAST IT SNRGS TNAT _SNE_ GAS SELIRDS IO TNE RYZEMT RB NEL ZRDLOEH.
GNATEKEL NE PIFNT ABTELGALCS WELSDACE NEL TR, IT GAS ORT RO NEL SICE A
_SMNEPE_ RB IOBAPH. PH WRRL BATNEL! NRG NE PDST NAKE BEUT IT!”

“I OEKEL SAG AOHROE SR SNRMVEC. NE MRDUC ORT SWEAV A GRLC BRL BDUU TEO
PIODTES. PH PRTNEL GAS TAVEO IUU IPPECIATEUH, AOC TNE GNRUE NRDSE IO
SDMN MROBDSIRO!”

“RN, ZAOE,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, “GAS TNELE A SELKAOT YEUROFIOF TR IT GNR
CIC ORT VORG TNE GNRUE STRLH YEBRLE TNE EOC RB TNE CAH?”

“I CR ORT VORG: I NRWE TNELE GAS. YDT TR YE FDALCEC AT SDMN A TIPE IS
KELH CIBBIMDUT. PH PRTNEL GAS IO NHSTELIMS; AOC TNRDFN I EOCEAKRDLEC TR
FIKE NEL EKELH ASSISTAOME IO PH WRGEL, I AP ABLAIC I CIC ORT CR SR PDMN
AS I PIFNT NAKE CROE. YDT TNE NRLLRL RB GNAT PIFNT WRSSIYUH NAWWEO
AUPRST TRRV BLRP PE PH BAMDUTIES.”

“HRDL ATTEOCAOME DWRO NEL NAS YEEO TRR PDMN BRL HRD. HRD CR ORT URRV
GEUU. RN TNAT I NAC YEEO GITN HRD! HRD NAKE NAC EKELH MALE AOC AOXIETH
DWRO HRDLSEUB AUROE.”

“PALH AOC VITTH NAKE YEEO KELH VIOC, AOC GRDUC NAKE SNALEC IO EKELH
BATIFDE, I AP SDLE, YDT I CIC ORT TNIOV IT LIFNT BRL EITNEL RB TNEP.
VITTH IS SUIFNT AOC CEUIMATE, AOC PALH STDCIES SR PDMN TNAT NEL NRDLS RB
LEWRSE SNRDUC ORT YE YLRVEO IO RO. PH ADOT WNIUIWS MAPE TR UROFYRDLO RO
TDESCAH, ABTEL PH BATNEL GEOT AGAH; AOC GAS SR FRRC AS TR STAH TIUU
TNDLSCAH GITN PE. SNE GAS RB FLEAT DSE AOC MRPBRLT TR DS AUU, AOC UACH
UDMAS NAS YEEO KELH VIOC: SNE GAUVEC NELE RO GECOESCAH PRLOIOF TR
MROCRUE GITN DS, AOC RBBELEC NEL SELKIMES, RL AOH RB NEL CADFNTELS, IB
TNEH MRDUC YE RB DSE TR DS.”

“SNE NAC YETTEL NAKE STAHEC AT NRPE,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN: “WELNAWS SNE
_PEAOT_ GEUU, YDT, DOCEL SDMN A PISBRLTDOE AS TNIS, ROE MAOORT SEE TRR
UITTUE RB ROE’S OEIFNYRDLS. ASSISTAOME IS IPWRSSIYUE; MROCRUEOME,
IOSDBBELAYUE. UET TNEP TLIDPWN RKEL DS AT A CISTAOME, AOC YE SATISBIEC.”

SNE TNEO WLRMEECEC TR IOQDILE IOTR TNE PEASDLES GNIMN NEL BATNEL NAC
IOTEOCEC TR WDLSDE, GNIUE IO TRGO, BRL TNE LEMRKELH RB NIS CADFNTEL.

“NE PEAOT, I YEUIEKE,” LEWUIEC ZAOE, “TR FR TR EWSRP, TNE WUAME GNELE
TNEH UAST MNAOFEC NRLSES, SEE TNE WRSTIUIROS, AOC TLH IB AOHTNIOF MRDUC
YE PACE RDT BLRP TNEP. NIS WLIOMIWAU RYZEMT PDST YE TR CISMRKEL TNE
ODPYEL RB TNE NAMVOEH MRAMN GNIMN TRRV TNEP BLRP MUAWNAP. IT NAC MRPE
GITN A BALE BLRP UROCRO; AOC AS NE TNRDFNT TNE MILMDPSTAOME RB A
FEOTUEPAO AOC UACH’S LEPRKIOF BLRP ROE MALLIAFE IOTR AORTNEL PIFNT YE
LEPALVEC, NE PEAOT TR PAVE IOQDILIES AT MUAWNAP. IB NE MRDUC AOHNRG
CISMRKEL AT GNAT NRDSE TNE MRAMNPAO NAC YEBRLE SET CRGO NIS BALE, NE
CETELPIOEC TR PAVE IOQDILIES TNELE, AOC NRWEC IT PIFNT ORT YE IPWRSSIYUE
TR BIOC RDT TNE STAOC AOC ODPYEL RB TNE MRAMN. I CR ORT VORG RB AOH
RTNEL CESIFOS TNAT NE NAC BRLPEC; YDT NE GAS IO SDMN A NDLLH TR YE FROE,
AOC NIS SWILITS SR FLEATUH CISMRPWRSEC, TNAT I NAC CIBBIMDUTH IO BIOCIOF
RDT EKEO SR PDMN AS TNIS.”




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     TNE WRST
]




MNAWTEL XUKIII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TNE GNRUE WALTH GELE IO NRWES RB A UETTEL BLRP PL. YEOOET TNE OEXT
PRLOIOF, YDT TNE WRST MAPE IO GITNRDT YLIOFIOF A SIOFUE UIOE BLRP NIP.
NIS BAPIUH VOEG NIP TR YE, RO AUU MRPPRO RMMASIROS, A PRST OEFUIFEOT AOC
CIUATRLH MRLLESWROCEOT; YDT AT SDMN A TIPE TNEH NAC NRWEC BRL EXELTIRO.
TNEH GELE BRLMEC TR MROMUDCE, TNAT NE NAC OR WUEASIOF IOTEUUIFEOME TR
SEOC; YDT EKEO RB _TNAT_ TNEH GRDUC NAKE YEEO FUAC TR YE MELTAIO. PL.
FALCIOEL NAC GAITEC ROUH BRL TNE UETTELS YEBRLE NE SET RBB.

GNEO NE GAS FROE, TNEH GELE MELTAIO AT UEAST RB LEMEIKIOF MROSTAOT
IOBRLPATIRO RB GNAT GAS FRIOF RO; AOC TNEIL DOMUE WLRPISEC, AT WALTIOF,
TR WLEKAIU RO PL. YEOOET TR LETDLO TR UROFYRDLO AS SRRO AS NE MRDUC, TR
TNE FLEAT MROSRUATIRO RB NIS SISTEL, GNR MROSICELEC IT AS TNE ROUH
SEMDLITH BRL NEL NDSYAOC’S ORT YEIOF VIUUEC IO A CDEU.

PLS. FALCIOEL AOC TNE MNIUCLEO GELE TR LEPAIO IO NELTBRLCSNILE A BEG
CAHS UROFEL, AS TNE BRLPEL TNRDFNT NEL WLESEOME PIFNT YE SELKIMEAYUE TR
NEL OIEMES. SNE SNALEC IO TNEIL ATTEOCAOME RO PLS. YEOOET, AOC GAS A
FLEAT MRPBRLT TR TNEP IO TNEIL NRDLS RB BLEECRP. TNEIL RTNEL ADOT AUSR
KISITEC TNEP BLEQDEOTUH, AOC AUGAHS, AS SNE SAIC, GITN TNE CESIFO RB
MNEELIOF AOC NEALTEOIOF TNEP DW--TNRDFN, AS SNE OEKEL MAPE GITNRDT
LEWRLTIOF SRPE BLESN IOSTAOME RB GIMVNAP’S EXTLAKAFAOME RL ILLEFDUALITH,
SNE SEUCRP GEOT AGAH GITNRDT UEAKIOF TNEP PRLE CISWILITEC TNAO SNE BRDOC
TNEP.

AUU PELHTRO SEEPEC STLIKIOF TR YUAMVEO TNE PAO GNR, YDT TNLEE PROTNS
YEBRLE, NAC YEEO AUPRST AO AOFEU RB UIFNT. NE GAS CEMUALEC TR YE IO CEYT
TR EKELH TLACESPAO IO TNE WUAME, AOC NIS IOTLIFDES, AUU NRORDLEC GITN
TNE TITUE RB SECDMTIRO, NAC YEEO EXTEOCEC IOTR EKELH TLACESPAO’S BAPIUH.
EKELHYRCH CEMUALEC TNAT NE GAS TNE GIMVECEST HRDOF PAO IO TNE GRLUC; AOC
EKELHYRCH YEFAO TR BIOC RDT TNAT TNEH NAC AUGAHS CISTLDSTEC TNE
AWWEALAOME RB NIS FRRCOESS. EUIJAYETN, TNRDFN SNE CIC ORT MLECIT AYRKE
NAUB RB GNAT GAS SAIC, YEUIEKEC EORDFN TR PAVE NEL BRLPEL ASSDLAOME RB
NEL SISTEL’S LDIO STIUU PRLE MELTAIO; AOC EKEO ZAOE, GNR YEUIEKEC STIUU
UESS RB IT, YEMAPE AUPRST NRWEUESS, PRLE ESWEMIAUUH AS TNE TIPE GAS ORG
MRPE, GNEO, IB TNEH NAC FROE TR SMRTUAOC, GNIMN SNE NAC OEKEL YEBRLE
EOTILEUH CESWAILEC RB, TNEH PDST IO AUU WLRYAYIUITH NAKE FAIOEC SRPE
OEGS RB TNEP.

PL. FALCIOEL UEBT UROFYRDLO RO SDOCAH; RO TDESCAH, NIS GIBE LEMEIKEC A
UETTEL BLRP NIP: IT TRUC TNEP, TNAT RO NIS ALLIKAU NE NAC IPPECIATEUH
BRDOC RDT NIS YLRTNEL, AOC WELSDACEC NIP TR MRPE TR FLAMEMNDLMN STLEET.
TNAT PL. YEOOET NAC YEEO TR EWSRP AOC MUAWNAP, YEBRLE NIS ALLIKAU, YDT
GITNRDT FAIOIOF AOH SATISBAMTRLH IOBRLPATIRO; AOC TNAT NE GAS ORG
CETELPIOEC TR IOQDILE AT AUU TNE WLIOMIWAU NRTEUS IO TRGO, AS PL. YEOOET
TNRDFNT IT WRSSIYUE TNEH PIFNT NAKE FROE TR ROE RB TNEP, RO TNEIL BILST
MRPIOF TR UROCRO, YEBRLE TNEH WLRMDLEC URCFIOFS. PL. FALCIOEL NIPSEUB
CIC ORT EXWEMT AOH SDMMESS BLRP TNIS PEASDLE; YDT AS NIS YLRTNEL GAS
EAFEL IO IT, NE PEAOT TR ASSIST NIP IO WDLSDIOF IT. NE ACCEC, TNAT PL.
YEOOET SEEPEC GNRUUH CISIOMUIOEC AT WLESEOT TR UEAKE UROCRO, AOC
WLRPISEC TR GLITE AFAIO KELH SRRO. TNELE GAS AUSR A WRSTSMLIWT TR TNIS
EBBEMT:--

“I NAKE GLITTEO TR MRUROEU BRLSTEL TR CESILE NIP TR BIOC RDT, IB
WRSSIYUE, BLRP SRPE RB TNE HRDOF PAO’S IOTIPATES IO TNE LEFIPEOT,
GNETNEL GIMVNAP NAS AOH LEUATIROS RL MROOEMTIROS GNR GRDUC YE UIVEUH TR
VORG IO GNAT WALT RB TNE TRGO NE NAS ORG MROMEAUEC NIPSEUB. IB TNELE
GELE AOHROE TNAT ROE MRDUC AWWUH TR, GITN A WLRYAYIUITH RB FAIOIOF SDMN
A MUDE AS TNAT, IT PIFNT YE RB ESSEOTIAU MROSEQDEOME. AT WLESEOT GE NAKE
ORTNIOF TR FDICE DS. MRUROEU BRLSTEL GIUU, I CALE SAH, CR EKELHTNIOF IO
NIS WRGEL TR SATISBH DS RO TNIS NEAC. YDT, RO SEMROC TNRDFNTS, WELNAWS
UIJJH MRDUC TEUU DS GNAT LEUATIROS NE NAS ORG UIKIOF YETTEL TNAO AOH
RTNEL WELSRO.”

EUIJAYETN GAS AT OR URSS TR DOCELSTAOC BLRP GNEOME TNIS CEBELEOME BRL
NEL ADTNRLITH WLRMEECEC; YDT IT GAS ORT IO NEL WRGEL TR FIKE AOH
IOBRLPATIRO RB SR SATISBAMTRLH A OATDLE AS TNE MRPWUIPEOT CESELKEC.

SNE NAC OEKEL NEALC RB NIS NAKIOF NAC AOH LEUATIROS, EXMEWT A BATNEL
AOC PRTNEL, YRTN RB GNRP NAC YEEO CEAC PAOH HEALS. IT GAS WRSSIYUE,
NRGEKEL, TNAT SRPE RB NIS MRPWAOIROS IO TNE ----SNILE PIFNT YE AYUE TR
FIKE PRLE IOBRLPATIRO; AOC TNRDFN SNE GAS ORT KELH SAOFDIOE IO EXWEMTIOF
IT, TNE AWWUIMATIRO GAS A SRPETNIOF TR URRV BRLGALC TR.

EKELH CAH AT UROFYRDLO GAS ORG A CAH RB AOXIETH; YDT TNE PRST AOXIRDS
WALT RB EAMN GAS GNEO TNE WRST GAS EXWEMTEC. TNE ALLIKAU RB UETTELS GAS
TNE BILST FLAOC RYZEMT RB EKELH PRLOIOF’S IPWATIEOME. TNLRDFN UETTELS,
GNATEKEL RB FRRC RL YAC GAS TR YE TRUC GRDUC YE MRPPDOIMATEC; AOC EKELH
SDMMEECIOF CAH GAS EXWEMTEC TR YLIOF SRPE OEGS RB IPWRLTAOME.

YDT YEBRLE TNEH NEALC AFAIO BLRP PL. FALCIOEL, A UETTEL ALLIKEC BRL
TNEIL BATNEL, BLRP A CIBBELEOT QDALTEL, BLRP PL. MRUUIOS; GNIMN, AS ZAOE
NAC LEMEIKEC CILEMTIROS TR RWEO AUU TNAT MAPE BRL NIP IO NIS AYSEOME,
SNE AMMRLCIOFUH LEAC; AOC EUIJAYETN, GNR VOEG GNAT MDLIRSITIES NIS
UETTELS AUGAHS GELE, URRVEC RKEL NEL, AOC LEAC IT UIVEGISE. IT GAS AS
BRUURGS:--

     /* “PH CEAL SIL, */

     “I BEEU PHSEUB MAUUEC DWRO, YH RDL LEUATIROSNIW, AOC PH SITDATIRO
     IO UIBE, TR MROCRUE GITN HRD RO TNE FLIEKRDS ABBUIMTIRO HRD ALE ORG
     SDBBELIOF DOCEL, RB GNIMN GE GELE HESTELCAH IOBRLPEC YH A UETTEL
     BLRP NELTBRLCSNILE. YE ASSDLEC, PH CEAL SIL, TNAT PLS. MRUUIOS AOC
     PHSEUB SIOMELEUH SHPWATNIJE GITN HRD, AOC AUU HRDL LESWEMTAYUE
     BAPIUH, IO HRDL WLESEOT CISTLESS, GNIMN PDST YE RB TNE YITTELEST
     VIOC, YEMADSE WLRMEECIOF BLRP A MADSE GNIMN OR TIPE MAO LEPRKE. OR
     ALFDPEOTS SNAUU YE GAOTIOF RO PH WALT, TNAT MAO AUUEKIATE SR SEKELE
     A PISBRLTDOE; RL TNAT PAH MRPBRLT HRD, DOCEL A MILMDPSTAOME TNAT
     PDST YE, RB AUU RTNELS, PRST ABBUIMTIOF TR A WALEOT’S PIOC. TNE
     CEATN RB HRDL CADFNTEL GRDUC NAKE YEEO A YUESSIOF IO MRPWALISRO RB
     TNIS. AOC IT IS TNE PRLE TR YE UAPEOTEC, YEMADSE TNELE IS LEASRO TR
     SDWWRSE, AS PH CEAL MNALURTTE IOBRLPS PE, TNAT TNIS UIMEOTIRDSOESS
     RB YENAKIRDL IO HRDL

     [IUUDSTLATIRO:

“TR GNRP I NAKE LEUATEC TNE ABBAIL”

     [_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

     CADFNTEL NAS WLRMEECEC BLRP A BADUTH CEFLEE RB IOCDUFEOME; TNRDFN,
     AT TNE SAPE TIPE, BRL TNE MROSRUATIRO RB HRDLSEUB AOC PLS. YEOOET,
     I AP IOMUIOEC TR TNIOV TNAT NEL RGO CISWRSITIRO PDST YE OATDLAUUH
     YAC, RL SNE MRDUC ORT YE FDIUTH RB SDMN AO EORLPITH, AT SR EALUH AO
     AFE. NRGSREKEL TNAT PAH YE, HRD ALE FLIEKRDSUH TR YE WITIEC; IO
     GNIMN RWIOIRO I AP ORT ROUH ZRIOEC YH PLS. MRUUIOS, YDT UIVEGISE YH
     UACH MATNELIOE AOC NEL CADFNTEL, TR GNRP I NAKE LEUATEC TNE ABBAIL.
     TNEH AFLEE GITN PE IO AWWLENEOCIOF TNAT TNIS BAUSE STEW IO ROE
     CADFNTEL GIUU YE IOZDLIRDS TR TNE BRLTDOES RB AUU TNE RTNELS: BRL
     GNR, AS UACH MATNELIOE NELSEUB MROCESMEOCIOFUH SAHS, GIUU MROOEMT
     TNEPSEUKES GITN SDMN A BAPIUH? AOC TNIS MROSICELATIRO UEACS PE,
     PRLERKEL, TR LEBUEMT, GITN ADFPEOTEC SATISBAMTIRO, RO A MELTAIO
     EKEOT RB UAST ORKEPYEL; BRL NAC IT YEEO RTNELGISE, I PDST NAKE YEEO
     IOKRUKEC IO AUU HRDL SRLLRG AOC CISFLAME. UET PE ACKISE HRD, TNEO,
     PH CEAL SIL, TR MROSRUE HRDLSEUB AS PDMN AS WRSSIYUE, TR TNLRG RBB
     HRDL DOGRLTNH MNIUC BLRP HRDL ABBEMTIRO BRL EKEL, AOC UEAKE NEL TR
     LEAW TNE BLDITS RB NEL RGO NEIORDS RBBEOME.

“I AP, CEAL SIL,” ETM., ETM.

PL. FALCIOEL CIC ORT GLITE AFAIO, TIUU NE NAC LEMEIKEC AO AOSGEL BLRP
MRUROEU BRLSTEL; AOC TNEO NE NAC ORTNIOF RB A WUEASAOT OATDLE TR SEOC.
IT GAS ORT VORGO TNAT GIMVNAP NAC A SIOFUE LEUATIRO GITN GNRP NE VEWT DW
AOH MROOEMTIRO, AOC IT GAS MELTAIO TNAT NE NAC OR OEAL ROE UIKIOF. NIS
BRLPEL AMQDAIOTAOME NAC YEEO ODPELRDS; YDT SIOME NE NAC YEEO IO TNE
PIUITIA, IT CIC ORT AWWEAL TNAT NE GAS RO TELPS RB WALTIMDUAL BLIEOCSNIW
GITN AOH RB TNEP. TNELE GAS OR ROE, TNELEBRLE, GNR MRDUC YE WRIOTEC RDT
AS UIVEUH TR FIKE AOH OEGS RB NIP. AOC IO TNE GLETMNEC STATE RB NIS RGO
BIOAOMES, TNELE GAS A KELH WRGELBDU PRTIKE BRL SEMLEMH, IO ACCITIRO TR
NIS BEAL RB CISMRKELH YH UHCIA’S LEUATIROS; BRL IT NAC ZDST TLAOSWILEC
TNAT NE NAC UEBT FAPIOF CEYTS YENIOC NIP TR A KELH MROSICELAYUE APRDOT.
MRUROEU BRLSTEL YEUIEKEC TNAT PRLE TNAO A TNRDSAOC WRDOCS GRDUC YE
OEMESSALH TR MUEAL NIS EXWEOSES AT YLIFNTRO. NE RGEC A FRRC CEAU IO TNE
TRGO, YDT NIS CEYTS RB NRORDL GELE STIUU PRLE BRLPICAYUE. PL. FALCIOEL
CIC ORT ATTEPWT TR MROMEAU TNESE WALTIMDUALS BLRP TNE UROFYRDLO BAPIUH;
ZAOE NEALC TNEP GITN NRLLRL. “A FAPESTEL!” SNE MLIEC. “TNIS IS GNRUUH
DOEXWEMTEC; I NAC ORT AO ICEA RB IT.”

PL. FALCIOEL ACCEC, IO NIS UETTEL, TNAT TNEH PIFNT EXWEMT TR SEE TNEIL
BATNEL AT NRPE RO TNE BRUURGIOF CAH, GNIMN GAS SATDLCAH. LEOCELEC
SWILITUESS YH TNE IUU SDMMESS RB AUU TNEIL EOCEAKRDLS, NE NAC HIEUCEC TR
NIS YLRTNEL-IO-UAG’S EOTLEATH TNAT NE GRDUC LETDLO TR NIS BAPIUH AOC
UEAKE IT TR NIP TR CR GNATEKEL RMMASIRO PIFNT SDFFEST TR YE ACKISAYUE
BRL MROTIODIOF TNEIL WDLSDIT. GNEO PLS. YEOOET GAS TRUC RB TNIS, SNE CIC
ORT EXWLESS SR PDMN SATISBAMTIRO AS NEL MNIUCLEO EXWEMTEC, MROSICELIOF
GNAT NEL AOXIETH BRL NIS UIBE NAC YEEO YEBRLE.

“GNAT! IS NE MRPIOF NRPE, AOC GITNRDT WRRL UHCIA?” SNE MLIEC. “SDLE NE
GIUU ORT UEAKE UROCRO YEBRLE NE NAS BRDOC TNEP. GNR IS TR BIFNT GIMVNAP,
AOC PAVE NIP PALLH NEL, IB NE MRPES AGAH?”

AS PLS. FALCIOEL YEFAO TR GISN TR YE AT NRPE, IT GAS SETTUEC TNAT SNE
AOC NEL MNIUCLEO SNRDUC FR TR UROCRO AT TNE SAPE TIPE TNAT PL. YEOOET
MAPE BLRP IT. TNE MRAMN, TNELEBRLE, TRRV TNEP TNE BILST STAFE RB TNEIL
ZRDLOEH, AOC YLRDFNT ITS PASTEL YAMV TR UROFYRDLO.

PLS. FALCIOEL GEOT AGAH IO AUU TNE WELWUEXITH AYRDT EUIJAYETN AOC NEL
CELYHSNILE BLIEOC, TNAT NAC ATTEOCEC NEL BLRP TNAT WALT RB TNE GRLUC.
NIS OAPE NAC OEKEL YEEO KRUDOTALIUH PEOTIROEC YEBRLE TNEP YH NEL OIEME;
AOC TNE VIOC RB NAUB-EXWEMTATIRO GNIMN PLS. FALCIOEL NAC BRLPEC, RB
TNEIL YEIOF BRUURGEC YH A UETTEL BLRP NIP, NAC EOCEC IO ORTNIOF.
EUIJAYETN NAC LEMEIKEC OROE SIOME NEL LETDLO, TNAT MRDUC MRPE BLRP
WEPYELUEH.

TNE WLESEOT DONAWWH STATE RB TNE BAPIUH LEOCELEC AOH RTNEL EXMDSE BRL
TNE URGOESS RB NEL SWILITS DOOEMESSALH; ORTNIOF, TNELEBRLE, MRDUC YE
BAILUH MROZEMTDLEC BLRP _TNAT_,--TNRDFN EUIJAYETN, GNR GAS YH TNIS TIPE
TRUELAYUH GEUU AMQDAIOTEC GITN NEL RGO BEEUIOFS, GAS WELBEMTUH AGALE
TNAT, NAC SNE VORGO ORTNIOF RB CALMH, SNE MRDUC NAKE YRLOE TNE CLEAC RB
UHCIA’S IOBAPH SRPEGNAT YETTEL. IT GRDUC NAKE SWALEC NEL, SNE TNRDFNT,
ROE SUEEWUESS OIFNT RDT RB TGR.

GNEO PL. YEOOET ALLIKEC, NE NAC AUU TNE AWWEALAOME RB NIS DSDAU
WNIURSRWNIM MRPWRSDLE. NE SAIC AS UITTUE AS NE NAC EKEL YEEO IO TNE
NAYIT RB SAHIOF; PACE OR PEOTIRO RB TNE YDSIOESS TNAT NAC TAVEO NIP
AGAH; AOC IT GAS SRPE TIPE YEBRLE NIS CADFNTELS NAC MRDLAFE TR SWEAV RB
IT.

IT GAS ORT TIUU TNE ABTELORRO, GNEO NE ZRIOEC TNEP AT TEA, TNAT
EUIJAYETN KEOTDLEC TR IOTLRCDME TNE SDYZEMT; AOC TNEO, RO NEL YLIEBUH
EXWLESSIOF NEL SRLLRG BRL GNAT NE PDST NAKE EOCDLEC, NE LEWUIEC, “SAH
ORTNIOF RB TNAT. GNR SNRDUC SDBBEL YDT PHSEUB? IT NAS YEEO PH RGO CRIOF,
AOC I RDFNT TR BEEU IT.”

“HRD PDST ORT YE TRR SEKELE DWRO HRDLSEUB,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN.

“HRD PAH GEUU GALO PE AFAIOST SDMN AO EKIU. NDPAO OATDLE IS SR WLROE TR
BAUU IOTR IT! OR, UIJJH, UET PE ROME IO PH UIBE BEEU NRG PDMN I NAKE
YEEO TR YUAPE. I AP ORT ABLAIC RB YEIOF RKELWRGELEC YH TNE IPWLESSIRO.
IT GIUU WASS AGAH SRRO EORDFN.”

“CR HRD SDWWRSE TNEP TR YE IO UROCRO?”

“HES; GNELE EUSE MAO TNEH YE SR GEUU MROMEAUEC?”

“AOC UHCIA DSEC TR GAOT TR FR TR UROCRO,” ACCEC VITTH.

“SNE IS NAWWH, TNEO,” SAIC NEL BATNEL, CLIUH; “AOC NEL LESICEOME TNELE
GIUU WLRYAYUH YE RB SRPE CDLATIRO.”

TNEO, ABTEL A SNRLT SIUEOME, NE MROTIODEC, “UIJJH, I YEAL HRD OR
IUU-GIUU BRL YEIOF ZDSTIBIEC IO HRDL ACKIME TR PE UAST PAH, GNIMN,
MROSICELIOF TNE EKEOT, SNRGS SRPE FLEATOESS RB PIOC.”

TNEH GELE IOTELLDWTEC YH PISS YEOOET, GNR MAPE TR BETMN NEL PRTNEL’S
TEA.

“TNIS IS A WALACE,” MLIEC NE, “GNIMN CRES ROE FRRC; IT FIKES SDMN AO
EUEFAOME TR PISBRLTDOE! AORTNEL CAH I GIUU CR TNE SAPE; I GIUU SIT IO PH
UIYLALH, IO PH OIFNTMAW AOC WRGCELIOF FRGO, AOC FIKE AS PDMN TLRDYUE AS
I MAO,--RL WELNAWS I PAH CEBEL IT TIUU VITTH LDOS AGAH.”

“I AP ORT FRIOF TR LDO AGAH, WAWA,” SAIC VITTH, BLETBDUUH. “IB _I_
SNRDUC EKEL FR TR YLIFNTRO, I GRDUC YENAKE YETTEL TNAO UHCIA.”

“_HRD_ FR TR YLIFNTRO! I GRDUC ORT TLDST HRD SR OEAL IT AS EASTYRDLOE,
BRL BIBTH WRDOCS! OR, VITTH, I NAKE AT UEAST UEALOT TR YE MADTIRDS, AOC
HRD GIUU BEEU TNE EBBEMTS RB IT. OR RBBIMEL IS EKEL TR EOTEL PH NRDSE
AFAIO, ORL EKEO TR WASS TNLRDFN TNE KIUUAFE. YAUUS GIUU YE AYSRUDTEUH
WLRNIYITEC, DOUESS HRD STAOC DW GITN ROE RB HRDL SISTELS. AOC HRD ALE
OEKEL TR STIL RDT RB CRRLS, TIUU HRD MAO WLRKE TNAT HRD NAKE SWEOT TEO
PIODTES RB EKELH CAH IO A LATIROAU PAOOEL.”

VITTH, GNR TRRV AUU TNESE TNLEATS IO A SELIRDS UIFNT, YEFAO TR MLH.

FILU BRL TNE OEXT TEO HEALS, I GIUU TAVE HRD TR A LEKIEG AT TNE EOC RB
TNEP.”

TGR CAHS ABTEL PL. YEOOET’S LETDLO, AS ZAOE AOC EUIJAYETN GELE GAUVIOF

AYRDT.”
