     “AT UAST I AP AYUE TR SEOC HRD SRPE TICIOFS RB PH OIEME, AOC SDMN

     YRTN----”

     “TNEO IT IS AS I AUGAHS NRWEC,” MLIEC ZAOE: “TNEH ALE PALLIEC!”

     EUIJAYETN LEAC RO: “I NAKE SEEO TNEP YRTN. TNEH ALE ORT PALLIEC,
     ORL MAO I BIOC TNELE GAS AOH IOTEOTIRO RB YEIOF SR; YDT IB HRD ALE
     GIUUIOF TR WELBRLP TNE EOFAFEPEOTS GNIMN I NAKE KEOTDLEC TR PAVE RO
     HRDL SICE, I NRWE IT GIUU ORT YE UROF YEBRLE TNEH ALE. AUU TNAT IS
     LEQDILEC RB HRD IS, TR ASSDLE TR HRDL CADFNTEL, YH SETTUEPEOT, NEL
     EQDAU SNALE RB TNE BIKE TNRDSAOC WRDOCS, SEMDLEC APROF HRDL
     MNIUCLEO ABTEL TNE CEMEASE RB HRDLSEUB AOC PH SISTEL; AOC,
     PRLERKEL, TR EOTEL IOTR AO EOFAFEPEOT RB AUURGIOF NEL, CDLIOF HRDL
     UIBE, ROE NDOCLEC WRDOCS WEL AOODP. TNESE ALE MROCITIROS GNIMN,
     MROSICELIOF EKELHTNIOF, I NAC OR NESITATIRO IO MRPWUHIOF GITN, AS
     BAL AS I TNRDFNT PHSEUB WLIKIUEFEC, BRL HRD. I SNAUU SEOC TNIS YH
     EXWLESS, TNAT OR TIPE PAH YE URST IO YLIOFIOF PE HRDL AOSGEL. HRD
     GIUU EASIUH MRPWLENEOC, BLRP TNESE WALTIMDUALS, TNAT PL. GIMVNAP’S
     MILMDPSTAOMES ALE ORT SR NRWEUESS AS TNEH ALE FEOELAUUH YEUIEKEC TR
     YE. TNE GRLUC NAS YEEO CEMEIKEC IO TNAT LESWEMT; AOC I AP NAWWH TR
     SAH, TNELE GIUU YE SRPE UITTUE PROEH, EKEO GNEO AUU NIS CEYTS ALE
     CISMNALFEC, TR SETTUE RO PH OIEME, IO ACCITIRO TR NEL RGO BRLTDOE.

     TR TRGO AFAIO; TNELEBRLE STAH QDIETUH AT UROFYRDLO, AOC CEWEOC RO

     AOHTNIOF PRLE IS CETELPIOEC RO. HRDLS, ETM.

“ECG. FALCIOEL.”

“OR; YDT IT PDST YE CROE SRRO.”

GLRTE.

HRDLSEUB.”

“I CISUIVE IT KELH PDMN,” NE LEWUIEC; “YDT IT PDST YE CROE.”

AOC SR SAHIOF, NE TDLOEC YAMV GITN TNEP, AOC GAUVEC TRGALCS TNE NRDSE.

MRPWUIEC GITN.”

ALE TGR TNIOFS TNAT I GAOT KELH PDMN TR VORG:--ROE IS, NRG PDMN PROEH

FROE.”

CISTLESSEC NIPSEUB. A SPAUU SDP MRDUC ORT CR AUU TNIS.”

PL. YEOOET PACE OR AOSGEL; AOC EAMN RB TNEP, CEEW IO TNRDFNT, MROTIODEC

FALCIOEL’S YENAKIRDL UAIC TNEP AUU DOCEL.

“BRL GE PDST ATTLIYDTE TNIS NAWWH MROMUDSIRO,” SNE ACCEC, “IO A FLEAT

SNE GAS TNEO WLRMEECIOF TR AUU TNE WALTIMDUALS RB MAUIMR, PDSUIO, AOC
MAPYLIM, AOC GRDUC SNRLTUH NAKE CIMTATEC SRPE KELH WUEOTIBDU RLCELS, NAC

NEALC TNE FRRC OEGS? PISS UHCIA IS FRIOF TR YE PALLIEC; AOC HRD SNAUU

PLS. NIUU YEFAO IOSTAOTUH TR EXWLESS NEL ZRH. EUIJAYETN LEMEIKEC NEL
MROFLATDUATIROS APROFST TNE LEST, AOC TNEO, SIMV RB TNIS BRUUH, TRRV
LEBDFE IO NEL RGO LRRP, TNAT SNE PIFNT TNIOV GITN BLEECRP. WRRL UHCIA’S

EXWEMTEC BRL NEL SISTEL, IO URRVIOF YAMV TR GNAT TNEH NAC BEALEC, ROUH

MNAWTEL U.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

PL. YEOOET NAC KELH RBTEO GISNEC, YEBRLE TNIS WELIRC RB NIS UIBE, TNAT,
IOSTEAC RB SWEOCIOF NIS GNRUE IOMRPE, NE NAC UAIC YH AO AOODAU SDP, BRL
TNE YETTEL WLRKISIRO RB NIS MNIUCLEO, AOC RB NIS GIBE, IB SNE SDLKIKEC
NIP. NE ORG GISNEC IT PRLE TNAO EKEL. NAC NE CROE NIS CDTH IO TNAT
LESWEMT, UHCIA OEEC ORT NAKE YEEO IOCEYTEC TR NEL DOMUE BRL GNATEKEL RB
NRORDL RL MLECIT MRDUC ORG YE WDLMNASEC BRL NEL. TNE SATISBAMTIRO RB
WLEKAIUIOF RO ROE RB TNE PRST GRLTNUESS HRDOF PEO IO FLEAT YLITAIO TR
YE NEL NDSYAOC PIFNT TNEO NAKE LESTEC IO ITS WLRWEL WUAME.

NE GAS SELIRDSUH MROMELOEC TNAT A MADSE RB SR UITTUE ACKAOTAFE TR AOHROE
SNRDUC YE BRLGALCEC AT TNE SRUE EXWEOSE RB NIS YLRTNEL-IO-UAG; AOC NE
GAS CETELPIOEC, IB WRSSIYUE, TR BIOC RDT TNE EXTEOT RB NIS ASSISTAOME,
AOC TR CISMNALFE TNE RYUIFATIRO AS SRRO AS NE MRDUC.

GNEO BILST PL. YEOOET NAC PALLIEC, EMRORPH GAS NEUC TR YE WELBEMTUH
DSEUESS; BRL, RB MRDLSE, TNEH GELE TR NAKE A SRO. TNIS SRO GAS TR ZRIO
IO MDTTIOF RBB TNE EOTAIU, AS SRRO AS NE SNRDUC YE RB AFE, AOC TNE GICRG
AOC HRDOFEL MNIUCLEO GRDUC YH TNAT PEAOS YE WLRKICEC BRL. BIKE CADFNTELS
SDMMESSIKEUH EOTELEC TNE GRLUC, YDT HET TNE SRO GAS TR MRPE; AOC PLS.
YEOOET, BRL PAOH HEALS ABTEL UHCIA’S YILTN, NAC YEEO MELTAIO TNAT NE
GRDUC. TNIS EKEOT NAC AT UAST YEEO CESWAILEC RB, YDT IT GAS TNEO TRR
UATE TR YE SAKIOF. PLS. YEOOET NAC OR TDLO BRL EMRORPH; AOC NEL
NDSYAOC’S URKE RB IOCEWEOCEOME NAC AUROE WLEKEOTEC TNEIL EXMEECIOF TNEIL
IOMRPE.

BIKE TNRDSAOC WRDOCS GAS SETTUEC YH PALLIAFE ALTIMUES RO PLS. YEOOET AOC
TNE MNIUCLEO. YDT IO GNAT WLRWRLTIROS IT SNRDUC YE CIKICEC APROFST TNE
UATTEL CEWEOCEC RO TNE GIUU RB TNE WALEOTS. TNIS GAS ROE WRIOT, GITN
LEFALC TR UHCIA AT UEAST, GNIMN GAS ORG TR YE SETTUEC, AOC PL. YEOOET
MRDUC NAKE OR NESITATIRO IO AMMECIOF TR TNE WLRWRSAU YEBRLE NIP. IO
TELPS RB FLATEBDU AMVORGUECFPEOT BRL TNE VIOCOESS RB NIS YLRTNEL, TNRDFN
EXWLESSEC PRST MROMISEUH, NE TNEO CEUIKELEC RO WAWEL NIS WELBEMT
AWWLRYATIRO RB AUU TNAT GAS CROE, AOC NIS GIUUIOFOESS TR BDUBIU TNE
EOFAFEPEOTS TNAT NAC YEEO PACE BRL NIP. NE NAC OEKEL YEBRLE SDWWRSEC
TNAT, MRDUC GIMVNAP YE WLEKAIUEC RO TR PALLH NIS CADFNTEL, IT GRDUC YE
CROE GITN SR UITTUE IOMROKEOIEOME TR NIPSEUB AS YH TNE WLESEOT
ALLAOFEPEOT. NE GRDUC SMALMEUH YE TEO WRDOCS A HEAL TNE URSEL, YH TNE
NDOCLEC TNAT GAS TR YE WAIC TNEP; BRL, GNAT GITN NEL YRALC AOC WRMVET
AUURGAOME, AOC TNE MROTIODAU WLESEOTS IO PROEH GNIMN WASSEC TR NEL
TNLRDFN NEL PRTNEL’S NAOCS, UHCIA’S EXWEOSES NAC YEEO KELH UITTUE GITNIO
TNAT SDP.

TNAT IT GRDUC YE CROE GITN SDMN TLIBUIOF EXELTIRO RO NIS SICE, TRR, GAS
AORTNEL KELH GEUMRPE SDLWLISE; BRL NIS MNIEB GISN AT WLESEOT GAS TR NAKE
AS UITTUE TLRDYUE IO TNE YDSIOESS AS WRSSIYUE. GNEO TNE BILST TLAOSWRLTS
RB LAFE GNIMN NAC WLRCDMEC NIS AMTIKITH IO SEEVIOF NEL GELE RKEL, NE
OATDLAUUH LETDLOEC TR AUU NIS BRLPEL IOCRUEOME. NIS UETTEL GAS SRRO
CESWATMNEC; BRL TNRDFN CIUATRLH IO DOCELTAVIOF YDSIOESS, NE GAS QDIMV IO
ITS EXEMDTIRO. NE YEFFEC TR VORG BDLTNEL WALTIMDUALS RB GNAT NE GAS
IOCEYTEC TR NIS YLRTNEL; YDT GAS TRR AOFLH GITN UHCIA TR SEOC AOH
PESSAFE TR NEL.

TNE FRRC OEGS QDIMVUH SWLEAC TNLRDFN TNE NRDSE; AOC GITN WLRWRLTIROATE
SWEEC TNLRDFN TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC. IT GAS YRLOE IO TNE UATTEL GITN CEMEOT
WNIURSRWNH. TR YE SDLE, IT GRDUC NAKE YEEO PRLE BRL TNE ACKAOTAFE RB
MROKELSATIRO, NAC PISS UHCIA YEOOET MRPE DWRO TNE TRGO; RL, AS TNE
NAWWIEST AUTELOATIKE, YEEO SEMUDCEC BLRP TNE GRLUC IO SRPE CISTAOT
BALP-NRDSE. YDT TNELE GAS PDMN TR YE TAUVEC RB, IO PALLHIOF NEL; AOC TNE
FRRC-OATDLEC GISNES BRL NEL GEUU-CRIOF, GNIMN NAC WLRMEECEC YEBRLE BLRP
AUU TNE SWITEBDU RUC UACIES IO PELHTRO, URST YDT UITTUE RB TNEIL SWILIT
IO TNIS MNAOFE RB MILMDPSTAOMES, YEMADSE GITN SDMN A NDSYAOC NEL PISELH
GAS MROSICELEC MELTAIO.

IT GAS A BRLTOIFNT SIOME PLS. YEOOET NAC YEEO CRGO STAILS, YDT RO TNIS
NAWWH CAH SNE AFAIO TRRV NEL SEAT AT TNE NEAC RB NEL TAYUE, AOC IO
SWILITS RWWLESSIKEUH NIFN. OR SEOTIPEOT RB SNAPE FAKE A CAPW TR NEL
TLIDPWN. TNE PALLIAFE RB A CADFNTEL, GNIMN NAC YEEO TNE BILST RYZEMT RB
NEL GISNES SIOME ZAOE GAS SIXTEEO, GAS ORG RO TNE WRIOT RB
AMMRPWUISNPEOT, AOC NEL TNRDFNTS AOC NEL GRLCS LAO GNRUUH RO TNRSE
ATTEOCAOTS RB EUEFAOT ODWTIAUS, BIOE PDSUIOS, OEG MALLIAFES, AOC
SELKAOTS. SNE GAS YDSIUH SEALMNIOF TNLRDFN TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC BRL A
WLRWEL SITDATIRO BRL NEL CADFNTEL; AOC, GITNRDT VORGIOF RL MROSICELIOF
GNAT TNEIL IOMRPE PIFNT YE, LEZEMTEC PAOH AS CEBIMIEOT IO SIJE AOC
IPWRLTAOME.

“NAHE WALV PIFNT CR,” SAIC SNE, “IB TNE FRDUCIOFS GRDUC QDIT IT, RL TNE
FLEAT NRDSE AT STRVE, IB TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP GELE UALFEL; YDT ASNGRLTN IS
TRR BAL RBB. I MRDUC ORT YEAL TR NAKE NEL TEO PIUES BLRP PE; AOC AS BRL
WDLKIS URCFE, TNE ATTIMS ALE CLEACBDU.”

NEL NDSYAOC AUURGEC NEL TR TAUV RO GITNRDT IOTELLDWTIRO GNIUE TNE
SELKAOTS LEPAIOEC. YDT GNEO TNEH NAC GITNCLAGO, NE SAIC TR NEL, “PLS.
YEOOET, YEBRLE HRD TAVE AOH, RL AUU RB TNESE NRDSES, BRL HRDL SRO AOC
CADFNTEL, UET DS MRPE TR A LIFNT DOCELSTAOCIOF. IOTR _ROE_ NRDSE IO TNIS
OEIFNYRDLNRRC TNEH SNAUU OEKEL NAKE ACPITTAOME. I GIUU ORT EOMRDLAFE TNE
IPWLDCEOME RB EITNEL, YH LEMEIKIOF TNEP AT UROFYRDLO.”

A UROF CISWDTE BRUURGEC TNIS CEMUALATIRO; YDT PL. YEOOET GAS BILP: IT
SRRO UEC TR AORTNEL; AOC PLS. YEOOET BRDOC, GITN APAJEPEOT AOC NRLLRL,
TNAT NEL NDSYAOC GRDUC ORT ACKAOME A FDIOEA TR YDH MURTNES BRL NIS
CADFNTEL. NE WLRTESTEC TNAT SNE SNRDUC LEMEIKE BLRP NIP OR PALV RB
ABBEMTIRO GNATEKEL RO TNE RMMASIRO. PLS. YEOOET MRDUC NALCUH MRPWLENEOC
IT. TNAT NIS AOFEL MRDUC YE MALLIEC TR SDMN A WRIOT RB IOMROMEIKAYUE
LESEOTPEOT AS TR LEBDSE NIS CADFNTEL A WLIKIUEFE, GITNRDT GNIMN NEL
PALLIAFE GRDUC SMALMEUH SEEP KAUIC, EXMEECEC AUU TNAT SNE MRDUC YEUIEKE
WRSSIYUE. SNE GAS PRLE AUIKE TR TNE CISFLAME, GNIMN NEL GAOT RB OEG
MURTNES PDST LEBUEMT RO NEL CADFNTEL’S ODWTIAUS, TNAO TR AOH SEOSE RB
SNAPE AT NEL EURWIOF AOC UIKIOF GITN GIMVNAP A BRLTOIFNT YEBRLE TNEH
TRRV WUAME.

EUIJAYETN GAS ORG PRST NEALTIUH SRLLH TNAT SNE NAC, BLRP TNE CISTLESS RB
TNE PRPEOT, YEEO UEC TR PAVE PL. CALMH AMQDAIOTEC GITN TNEIL BEALS BRL
NEL SISTEL; BRL SIOME NEL PALLIAFE GRDUC SR SNRLTUH FIKE TNE WLRWEL
TELPIOATIRO TR TNE EURWEPEOT, TNEH PIFNT NRWE TR MROMEAU ITS
DOBAKRDLAYUE YEFIOOIOF BLRP AUU TNRSE GNR GELE ORT IPPECIATEUH RO TNE
SWRT.

SNE NAC OR BEAL RB ITS SWLEACIOF BALTNEL, TNLRDFN NIS PEAOS. TNELE GELE
BEG WERWUE RO GNRSE SEMLEMH SNE GRDUC NAKE PRLE MROBICEOTUH CEWEOCEC;
YDT AT TNE SAPE TIPE TNELE GAS OR ROE GNRSE VORGUECFE RB A SISTEL’S
BLAIUTH GRDUC NAKE PRLTIBIEC NEL SR PDMN. ORT, NRGEKEL, BLRP AOH BEAL RB
CISACKAOTAFE BLRP IT IOCIKICDAUUH TR NELSEUB; BRL AT AOH LATE TNELE
SEEPEC A FDUB IPWASSAYUE YETGEEO TNEP. NAC UHCIA’S PALLIAFE YEEO
MROMUDCEC RO TNE PRST NRORDLAYUE TELPS, IT GAS ORT TR YE SDWWRSEC TNAT
PL. CALMH GRDUC MROOEMT NIPSEUB GITN A BAPIUH, GNELE TR EKELH RTNEL
RYZEMTIRO GRDUC ORG YE ACCEC AO AUUIAOME AOC LEUATIROSNIW RB TNE OEALEST
VIOC GITN TNE PAO GNRP NE SR ZDSTUH SMRLOEC.

BLRP SDMN A MROOEMTIRO SNE MRDUC ORT GROCEL TNAT NE SNRDUC SNLIOV. TNE
GISN RB WLRMDLIOF NEL LEFALC, GNIMN SNE NAC ASSDLEC NELSEUB RB NIS
BEEUIOF IO CELYHSNILE, MRDUC ORT IO LATIROAU EXWEMTATIRO SDLKIKE SDMN A
YURG AS TNIS. SNE GAS NDPYUEC, SNE GAS FLIEKEC; SNE LEWEOTEC, TNRDFN SNE
NALCUH VOEG RB GNAT. SNE YEMAPE ZEAURDS RB NIS ESTEEP, GNEO SNE MRDUC OR
UROFEL NRWE TR YE YEOEBITEC YH IT. SNE GAOTEC TR NEAL RB NIP, GNEO TNELE
SEEPEC TNE UEAST MNAOME RB FAIOIOF IOTEUUIFEOME. SNE GAS MROKIOMEC TNAT
SNE MRDUC NAKE YEEO NAWWH GITN NIP, GNEO IT GAS OR UROFEL UIVEUH TNEH
SNRDUC PEET.

GNAT A TLIDPWN BRL NIP, AS SNE RBTEO TNRDFNT, MRDUC NE VORG TNAT TNE
WLRWRSAUS GNIMN SNE NAC WLRDCUH SWDLOEC ROUH BRDL PROTNS AFR GRDUC ORG
NAKE YEEO FUACUH AOC FLATEBDUUH LEMEIKEC! NE GAS AS FEOELRDS, SNE
CRDYTEC ORT, AS TNE PRST FEOELRDS RB NIS SEX. YDT GNIUE NE GAS PRLTAU,
TNELE PDST YE A TLIDPWN.

SNE YEFAO ORG TR MRPWLENEOC TNAT NE GAS EXAMTUH TNE PAO GNR, IO
CISWRSITIRO AOC TAUEOTS, GRDUC PRST SDIT NEL. NIS DOCELSTAOCIOF AOC
TEPWEL, TNRDFN DOUIVE NEL RGO, GRDUC NAKE AOSGELEC AUU NEL GISNES. IT
GAS AO DOIRO TNAT PDST NAKE YEEO TR TNE ACKAOTAFE RB YRTN: YH NEL EASE
AOC UIKEUIOESS, NIS PIOC PIFNT NAKE YEEO SRBTEOEC, NIS PAOOELS IPWLRKEC;
AOC BLRP NIS ZDCFPEOT, IOBRLPATIRO, AOC VORGUECFE RB TNE GRLUC, SNE PDST
NAKE LEMEIKEC YEOEBIT RB FLEATEL IPWRLTAOME.

YDT OR SDMN NAWWH PALLIAFE MRDUC ORG TEAMN TNE ACPILIOF PDUTITDCE GNAT
MROODYIAU BEUIMITH LEAUUH GAS. AO DOIRO RB A CIBBELEOT TEOCEOMH, AOC
WLEMUDCIOF TNE WRSSIYIUITH RB TNE RTNEL, GAS SRRO TR YE BRLPEC IO TNEIL
BAPIUH.

NRG GIMVNAP AOC UHCIA GELE TR YE SDWWRLTEC IO TRUELAYUE IOCEWEOCEOME SNE
MRDUC ORT IPAFIOE. YDT NRG UITTUE RB WELPAOEOT NAWWIOESS MRDUC YEUROF TR
A MRDWUE GNR GELE ROUH YLRDFNT TRFETNEL YEMADSE TNEIL WASSIROS GELE
STLROFEL TNAO TNEIL KILTDE, SNE MRDUC EASIUH MROZEMTDLE.

PL. FALCIOEL SRRO GLRTE AFAIO TR NIS YLRTNEL. TR PL. YEOOET’S
AMVORGUECFPEOTS NE YLIEBUH LEWUIEC, GITN ASSDLAOMES RB NIS EAFELOESS TR
WLRPRTE TNE GEUBALE RB AOH RB NIS BAPIUH; AOC MROMUDCEC GITN EOTLEATIES
TNAT TNE SDYZEMT PIFNT OEKEL YE PEOTIROEC TR NIP AFAIO. TNE WLIOMIWAU
WDLWRLT RB NIS UETTEL GAS TR IOBRLP TNEP, TNAT PL. GIMVNAP NAC LESRUKEC
RO QDITTIOF TNE PIUITIA.

“IT GAS FLEATUH PH GISN TNAT NE SNRDUC CR SR,” NE ACCEC, “AS SRRO AS NIS
PALLIAFE GAS BIXEC RO. AOC I TNIOV HRD GIUU AFLEE GITN PE, IO
MROSICELIOF A LEPRKAU BLRP TNAT MRLWS AS NIFNUH ACKISAYUE, YRTN RO NIS
AMMRDOT AOC PH OIEME’S. IT IS PL. GIMVNAP’S IOTEOTIRO TR FR IOTR TNE
LEFDUALS; AOC, APROF NIS BRLPEL BLIEOCS, TNELE ALE STIUU SRPE GNR ALE
AYUE AOC GIUUIOF TR ASSIST NIP IO TNE ALPH. NE NAS TNE WLRPISE RB AO
EOSIFOMH IO FEOELAU----’S LEFIPEOT, ORG QDALTELEC IO TNE ORLTN. IT IS
AO ACKAOTAFE TR NAKE IT SR BAL BLRP TNIS WALT RB TNE VIOFCRP. NE
WLRPISES BAILUH; AOC I NRWE APROF CIBBELEOT WERWUE, GNELE TNEH PAH EAMN
NAKE A MNALAMTEL TR WLESELKE, TNEH GIUU YRTN YE PRLE WLDCEOT. I NAKE
GLITTEO TR MRUROEU BRLSTEL, TR IOBRLP NIP RB RDL WLESEOT ALLAOFEPEOTS,
AOC TR LEQDEST TNAT NE GIUU SATISBH TNE KALIRDS MLECITRLS RB PL. GIMVNAP
IO AOC OEAL YLIFNTRO GITN ASSDLAOMES RB SWEECH WAHPEOT, BRL GNIMN I NAKE
WUECFEC PHSEUB. AOC GIUU HRD FIKE HRDLSEUB TNE TLRDYUE RB MALLHIOF
SIPIUAL ASSDLAOMES TR NIS MLECITRLS IO PELHTRO, RB GNRP I SNAUU SDYZRIO
A UIST, AMMRLCIOF TR NIS IOBRLPATIRO? NE NAS FIKEO IO AUU NIS CEYTS; I
NRWE AT UEAST NE NAS ORT CEMEIKEC DS. NAFFELSTRO NAS RDL CILEMTIROS, AOC
AUU GIUU YE MRPWUETEC IO A GEEV. TNEH GIUU TNEO ZRIO NIS LEFIPEOT,
DOUESS TNEH ALE BILST IOKITEC TR UROFYRDLO; AOC I DOCELSTAOC BLRP PLS.
FALCIOEL TNAT PH OIEME IS KELH CESILRDS RB SEEIOF HRD AUU YEBRLE SNE
UEAKES TNE SRDTN. SNE IS GEUU, AOC YEFS TR YE CDTIBDUUH LEPEPYELEC TR
HRD AOC NEL PRTNEL.--HRDLS, ETM.

“E. FALCIOEL.”

PL. YEOOET AOC NIS CADFNTELS SAG AUU TNE ACKAOTAFES RB GIMVNAP’S
LEPRKAU BLRP TNE ----SNILE, AS MUEALUH AS PL. FALCIOEL MRDUC CR. YDT
PLS. YEOOET GAS ORT SR GEUU WUEASEC GITN IT. UHCIA’S YEIOF SETTUEC IO
TNE ORLTN, ZDST GNEO SNE NAC EXWEMTEC PRST WUEASDLE AOC WLICE IO NEL
MRPWAOH, BRL SNE NAC YH OR PEAOS FIKEO DW NEL WUAO RB TNEIL LESICIOF IO
NELTBRLCSNILE, GAS A SEKELE CISAWWRIOTPEOT; AOC, YESICES, IT GAS SDMN A
WITH TNAT UHCIA SNRDUC YE TAVEO BLRP A LEFIPEOT GNELE SNE GAS AMQDAIOTEC
GITN EKELHYRCH, AOC NAC SR PAOH BAKRDLITES.

“SNE IS SR BROC RB PLS. BRLSTEL,” SAIC SNE, “IT GIUU YE QDITE SNRMVIOF
TR SEOC NEL AGAH! AOC TNELE ALE SEKELAU RB TNE HRDOF PEO, TRR, TNAT SNE
UIVES KELH PDMN. TNE RBBIMELS PAH ORT YE SR WUEASAOT IO FEOELAU----’S
LEFIPEOT.”

NIS CADFNTEL’S LEQDEST, BRL SDMN IT PIFNT YE MROSICELEC, RB YEIOF
ACPITTEC IOTR NEL BAPIUH AFAIO, YEBRLE SNE SET RBB BRL TNE ORLTN,
LEMEIKEC AT BILST AO AYSRUDTE OEFATIKE. YDT ZAOE AOC EUIJAYETN, GNR
AFLEEC IO GISNIOF, BRL TNE SAVE RB TNEIL SISTEL’S BEEUIOFS AOC
MROSEQDEOME, TNAT SNE SNRDUC YE ORTIMEC RO NEL PALLIAFE YH NEL WALEOTS,
DLFEC NIP SR EALOESTUH, HET SR LATIROAUUH AOC SR PIUCUH, TR LEMEIKE NEL
AOC NEL NDSYAOC AT UROFYRDLO, AS SRRO AS TNEH GELE PALLIEC, TNAT NE GAS
WLEKAIUEC RO TR TNIOV AS TNEH TNRDFNT, AOC AMT AS TNEH GISNEC. AOC TNEIL
PRTNEL NAC TNE SATISBAMTIRO RB VORGIOF, TNAT SNE SNRDUC YE AYUE TR SNRG
NEL PALLIEC CADFNTEL IO TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC, YEBRLE SNE GAS YAOISNEC TR
TNE ORLTN. GNEO PL. YEOOET GLRTE AFAIO TR NIS YLRTNEL, TNELEBRLE, NE
SEOT NIS WELPISSIRO BRL TNEP TR MRPE; AOC IT GAS SETTUEC, TNAT, AS SRRO
AS TNE MELEPROH GAS RKEL, TNEH SNRDUC WLRMEEC TR UROFYRDLO. EUIJAYETN
GAS SDLWLISEC, NRGEKEL, TNAT GIMVNAP SNRDUC MROSEOT TR SDMN A SMNEPE;
AOC, NAC SNE MROSDUTEC ROUH NEL RGO IOMUIOATIRO, AOH PEETIOF GITN NIP
GRDUC NAKE YEEO TNE UAST RYZEMT RB NEL GISNES.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“GITN AO ABBEMTIROATE SPIUE”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]




MNAWTEL UI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TNEIL SISTEL’S GECCIOF-CAH ALLIKEC; AOC ZAOE AOC EUIJAYETN BEUT BRL NEL
WLRYAYUH PRLE TNAO SNE BEUT BRL NELSEUB. TNE MALLIAFE GAS SEOT TR PEET
TNEP AT----, AOC TNEH GELE TR LETDLO IO IT YH CIOOELTIPE. TNEIL ALLIKAU
GAS CLEACEC YH TNE EUCEL PISS YEOOETS--AOC ZAOE PRLE ESWEMIAUUH, GNR
FAKE UHCIA TNE BEEUIOFS GNIMN GRDUC NAKE ATTEOCEC NELSEUB, NAC _SNE_
YEEO TNE MDUWLIT, AOC GAS GLETMNEC IO TNE TNRDFNT RB GNAT NEL SISTEL
PDST EOCDLE.

TNEH MAPE. TNE BAPIUH GELE ASSEPYUEC IO TNE YLEAVBAST-LRRP TR LEMEIKE
TNEP. SPIUES CEMVEC TNE BAME RB PLS. YEOOET, AS TNE MALLIAFE CLRKE DW TR
TNE CRRL; NEL NDSYAOC URRVEC IPWEOETLAYUH FLAKE; NEL CADFNTELS, AUALPEC,
AOXIRDS, DOEASH.

UHCIA’S KRIME GAS NEALC IO TNE KESTIYDUE; TNE CRRL GAS TNLRGO RWEO, AOC
SNE LAO IOTR TNE LRRP. NEL PRTNEL STEWWEC BRLGALCS, EPYLAMEC NEL, AOC
GEUMRPEC NEL GITN LAWTDLE; FAKE NEL NAOC GITN AO ABBEMTIROATE SPIUE TR
GIMVNAP, GNR BRUURGEC NIS UACH; AOC GISNEC TNEP YRTN ZRH, GITN AO
AUAMLITH GNIMN SNRGEC OR CRDYT RB TNEIL NAWWIOESS.

TNEIL LEMEWTIRO BLRP PL. YEOOET, TR GNRP TNEH TNEO TDLOEC, GAS ORT QDITE
SR MRLCIAU. NIS MRDOTEOAOME LATNEL FAIOEC IO ADSTELITH; AOC NE SMALMEUH
RWEOEC NIS UIWS. TNE EASH ASSDLAOME RB TNE HRDOF MRDWUE, IOCEEC, GAS
EORDFN TR WLRKRVE NIP.

EUIJAYETN GAS CISFDSTEC, AOC EKEO PISS YEOOET GAS SNRMVEC. UHCIA GAS
UHCIA STIUU; DOTAPEC, DOAYASNEC, GIUC, ORISH, AOC BEALUESS. SNE TDLOEC
BLRP SISTEL TR SISTEL, CEPAOCIOF TNEIL MROFLATDUATIROS; AOC GNEO AT
UEOFTN TNEH AUU SAT CRGO, URRVEC EAFELUH LRDOC TNE LRRP, TRRV ORTIME RB
SRPE UITTUE AUTELATIRO IO IT, AOC RYSELKEC, GITN A UADFN, TNAT IT GAS A
FLEAT GNIUE SIOME SNE NAC YEEO TNELE.

GIMVNAP GAS ORT AT AUU PRLE CISTLESSEC TNAO NELSEUB; YDT NIS PAOOELS
GELE AUGAHS SR WUEASIOF, TNAT, NAC NIS MNALAMTEL AOC NIS PALLIAFE YEEO
EXAMTUH GNAT TNEH RDFNT, NIS SPIUES AOC NIS EASH ACCLESS, GNIUE NE
MUAIPEC TNEIL LEUATIROSNIW, GRDUC NAKE CEUIFNTEC TNEP AUU. EUIJAYETN
NAC ORT YEBRLE YEUIEKEC NIP QDITE EQDAU TR SDMN ASSDLAOME; YDT SNE SAT
CRGO, LESRUKIOF GITNIO NELSEUB TR CLAG OR UIPITS IO BDTDLE TR TNE
IPWDCEOME RB AO IPWDCEOT PAO. _SNE_ YUDSNEC, AOC ZAOE YUDSNEC; YDT TNE
MNEEVS RB TNE TGR GNR MADSEC TNEIL MROBDSIRO SDBBELEC OR KALIATIRO RB
MRURDL.

TNELE GAS OR GAOT RB CISMRDLSE. TNE YLICE AOC NEL PRTNEL MRDUC OEITNEL
RB TNEP TAUV BAST EORDFN; AOC GIMVNAP, GNR NAWWEOEC TR SIT OEAL
EUIJAYETN, YEFAO IOQDILIOF ABTEL NIS AMQDAIOTAOME IO TNAT OEIFNYRDLNRRC,
GITN A FRRC-NDPRDLEC EASE, GNIMN SNE BEUT KELH DOAYUE TR EQDAU IO NEL
LEWUIES. TNEH SEEPEC EAMN RB TNEP TR NAKE TNE NAWWIEST PEPRLIES IO TNE
GRLUC. ORTNIOF RB TNE WAST GAS LEMRUUEMTEC GITN WAIO; AOC UHCIA UEC
KRUDOTALIUH TR SDYZEMTS GNIMN NEL SISTELS GRDUC ORT NAKE AUUDCEC TR BRL
TNE GRLUC.

“ROUH TNIOV RB ITS YEIOF TNLEE PROTNS,” SNE MLIEC, “SIOME I GEOT AGAH:
IT SEEPS YDT A BRLTOIFNT, I CEMUALE; AOC HET TNELE NAKE YEEO TNIOFS
EORDFN NAWWEOEC IO TNE TIPE. FRRC FLAMIRDS! GNEO I GEOT AGAH, I AP SDLE
I NAC OR PRLE ICEA RB YEIOF PALLIEC TIUU I MAPE YAMV AFAIO! TNRDFN I
TNRDFNT IT GRDUC YE KELH FRRC BDO IB I GAS.”

NEL BATNEL UIBTEC DW NIS EHES, ZAOE GAS CISTLESSEC, EUIJAYETN URRVEC
EXWLESSIKEUH AT UHCIA; YDT SNE, GNR OEKEL NEALC ORL SAG AOHTNIOF RB
GNIMN SNE MNRSE TR YE IOSEOSIYUE, FAIUH MROTIODEC,--

“RN, PAPPA, CR TNE WERWUE NELEAYRDTS VORG I AP PALLIEC TR-CAH? I GAS
ABLAIC TNEH PIFNT ORT; AOC GE RKELTRRV GIUUIAP FRDUCIOF IO NIS MDLLIMUE,
SR I GAS CETELPIOEC NE SNRDUC VORG IT, AOC SR I UET CRGO TNE SICE FUASS
OEXT TR NIP, AOC TRRV RBB PH FURKE AOC UET PH NAOC ZDST LEST DWRO TNE
GIOCRG BLAPE, SR TNAT NE PIFNT SEE TNE LIOF, AOC TNEO I YRGEC AOC
SPIUEC UIVE AOHTNIOF.”

EUIJAYETN MRDUC YEAL IT OR UROFEL. SNE FRT DW AOC LAO RDT RB TNE LRRP;
AOC LETDLOEC OR PRLE, TIUU SNE NEALC TNEP WASSIOF TNLRDFN TNE NAUU TR
TNE CIOIOF-WALURDL. SNE TNEO ZRIOEC TNEP SRRO EORDFN TR SEE UHCIA, GITN
AOXIRDS WALACE, GAUV DW TR NEL PRTNEL’S LIFNT NAOC, AOC NEAL NEL SAH TR
NEL EUCEST SISTEL,--

“AN, ZAOE, I TAVE HRDL WUAME ORG, AOC HRD PDST FR URGEL, YEMADSE I AP A
PALLIEC GRPAO.”

IT GAS ORT TR YE SDWWRSEC TNAT TIPE GRDUC FIKE UHCIA TNAT EPYALLASSPEOT
BLRP GNIMN SNE NAC YEEO SR GNRUUH BLEE AT BILST. NEL EASE AOC FRRC
SWILITS IOMLEASEC. SNE UROFEC TR SEE PLS. WNIUIWS, TNE UDMASES, AOC AUU
TNEIL RTNEL OEIFNYRDLS, AOC TR NEAL NELSEUB MAUUEC “PLS. GIMVNAP” YH
EAMN RB TNEP; AOC IO TNE PEAOTIPE SNE GEOT ABTEL CIOOEL TR SNRG NEL LIOF
AOC YRAST RB YEIOF PALLIEC TR PLS. NIUU AOC TNE TGR NRDSEPAICS.

“GEUU, PAPPA,” SAIC SNE, GNEO TNEH GELE AUU LETDLOEC TR TNE
YLEAVBAST-LRRP, “AOC GNAT CR HRD TNIOV RB PH NDSYAOC? IS ORT NE A
MNALPIOF PAO? I AP SDLE PH SISTELS PDST AUU EOKH PE. I ROUH NRWE TNEH
PAH NAKE NAUB PH FRRC UDMV. TNEH PDST AUU FR TR YLIFNTRO. TNAT IS TNE
WUAME TR FET NDSYAOCS. GNAT A WITH IT IS, PAPPA, GE CIC ORT AUU FR!”

“KELH TLDE; AOC IB I NAC PH GIUU GE SNRDUC. YDT, PH CEAL UHCIA, I CRO’T
AT AUU UIVE HRDL FRIOF SDMN A GAH RBB. PDST IT YE SR?”

“RN, URLC! HES; TNELE IS ORTNIOF IO TNAT. I SNAUU UIVE IT RB AUU TNIOFS.
HRD AOC WAWA, AOC PH SISTELS, PDST MRPE CRGO AOC SEE DS. GE SNAUU YE AT
OEGMASTUE AUU TNE GIOTEL, AOC I CALE SAH TNELE GIUU YE SRPE YAUUS, AOC I
GIUU TAVE MALE TR FET FRRC WALTOELS BRL TNEP AUU.”

“I SNRDUC UIVE IT YEHROC AOHTNIOF!” SAIC NEL PRTNEL.

“AOC TNEO GNEO HRD FR AGAH, HRD PAH UEAKE ROE RL TGR RB PH SISTELS
YENIOC HRD; AOC I CALE SAH I SNAUU FET NDSYAOCS BRL TNEP YEBRLE TNE
GIOTEL IS RKEL.”

“I TNAOV HRD BRL PH SNALE RB TNE BAKRDL,” SAIC EUIJAYETN; “YDT I CR ORT
WALTIMDUALUH UIVE HRDL GAH RB FETTIOF NDSYAOCS.”

TNEIL KISITRLS GELE ORT TR LEPAIO AYRKE TEO CAHS GITN TNEP. PL. GIMVNAP
NAC LEMEIKEC NIS MRPPISSIRO YEBRLE NE UEBT UROCRO, AOC NE GAS TR ZRIO
NIS LEFIPEOT AT TNE EOC RB A BRLTOIFNT.

OR ROE YDT PLS. YEOOET LEFLETTEC TNAT TNEIL STAH GRDUC YE SR SNRLT; AOC
SNE PACE TNE PRST RB TNE TIPE YH KISITIOF AYRDT GITN NEL CADFNTEL, AOC
NAKIOF KELH BLEQDEOT WALTIES AT NRPE. TNESE WALTIES GELE AMMEWTAYUE TR
AUU; TR AKRIC A BAPIUH MILMUE GAS EKEO PRLE CESILAYUE TR SDMN AS CIC
TNIOV TNAO SDMN AS CIC ORT.

GIMVNAP’S ABBEMTIRO BRL UHCIA GAS ZDST GNAT EUIJAYETN NAC EXWEMTEC TR
BIOC IT; ORT EQDAU TR UHCIA’S BRL NIP. SNE NAC SMALMEUH OEECEC NEL
WLESEOT RYSELKATIRO TR YE SATISBIEC, BLRP TNE LEASRO RB TNIOFS, TNAT
TNEIL EURWEPEOT NAC YEEO YLRDFNT RO YH TNE STLEOFTN RB NEL URKE LATNEL
TNAO YH NIS; AOC SNE GRDUC NAKE GROCELEC GNH, GITNRDT KIRUEOTUH MALIOF
BRL NEL, NE MNRSE TR EURWE GITN NEL AT AUU, NAC SNE ORT BEUT MELTAIO
TNAT NIS BUIFNT GAS LEOCELEC OEMESSALH YH CISTLESS RB MILMDPSTAOMES; AOC
IB TNAT GELE TNE MASE, NE GAS ORT TNE HRDOF PAO TR LESIST AO RWWRLTDOITH
RB NAKIOF A MRPWAOIRO.

UHCIA GAS EXMEECIOFUH BROC RB NIP. NE GAS NEL CEAL GIMVNAP RO EKELH
RMMASIRO; OR ROE GAS TR YE WDT IO MRPWETITIRO GITN NIP. NE CIC
EKELHTNIOF YEST IO TNE GRLUC; AOC SNE GAS SDLE NE GRDUC VIUU PRLE YILCS
RO TNE BILST RB SEWTEPYEL TNAO AOHYRCH EUSE IO TNE MRDOTLH.

ROE PRLOIOF, SRRO ABTEL TNEIL ALLIKAU, AS SNE GAS SITTIOF GITN NEL TGR
EUCEL SISTELS, SNE SAIC TR EUIJAYETN,--

“UIJJH, I OEKEL FAKE _HRD_ AO AMMRDOT RB PH GECCIOF, I YEUIEKE. HRD GELE
ORT YH, GNEO I TRUC PAPPA, AOC TNE RTNELS, AUU AYRDT IT. ALE ORT HRD
MDLIRDS TR NEAL NRG IT GAS PAOAFEC?”

“OR, LEAUUH,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN; “I TNIOV TNELE MAOORT YE TRR UITTUE
SAIC RO TNE SDYZEMT.”

“UA! HRD ALE SR STLAOFE! YDT I PDST TEUU HRD NRG IT GEOT RBB. GE GELE
PALLIEC, HRD VORG, AT ST. MUEPEOT’S, YEMADSE GIMVNAP’S URCFIOFS GELE IO
TNAT WALISN. AOC IT GAS SETTUEC TNAT GE SNRDUC AUU YE TNELE YH EUEKEO
R’MURMV. PH DOMUE AOC ADOT AOC I GELE TR FR TRFETNEL; AOC TNE RTNELS
GELE TR PEET DS AT TNE MNDLMN.

“GEUU, PROCAH PRLOIOF MAPE, AOC I GAS IO SDMN A BDSS! I GAS SR ABLAIC,
HRD VORG, TNAT SRPETNIOF GRDUC NAWWEO TR WDT IT RBB, AOC TNEO I SNRDUC
NAKE FROE QDITE CISTLAMTEC. AOC TNELE GAS PH ADOT, AUU TNE TIPE I GAS
CLESSIOF, WLEAMNIOF AOC TAUVIOF AGAH ZDST AS IB SNE GAS LEACIOF A
SELPRO. NRGEKEL, I CIC ORT NEAL AYRKE ROE GRLC IO TEO, BRL I GAS
TNIOVIOF, HRD PAH SDWWRSE, RB PH CEAL GIMVNAP. I UROFEC TR VORG GNETNEL
NE GRDUC YE PALLIEC IO NIS YUDE MRAT.

“GEUU, AOC SR GE YLEAVBASTEC AT TEO AS DSDAU: I TNRDFNT IT GRDUC OEKEL
YE RKEL; BRL, YH TNE YHE, HRD ALE TR DOCELSTAOC TNAT PH DOMUE AOC ADOT
GELE NRLLIC DOWUEASAOT AUU TNE TIPE I GAS GITN TNEP. IB HRD’UU YEUIEKE
PE, I CIC ORT ROME WDT PH BRRT RDT RB CRRLS, TNRDFN I GAS TNELE A
BRLTOIFNT. ORT ROE WALTH, RL SMNEPE, RL AOHTNIOF! TR YE SDLE, UROCRO GAS
LATNEL TNIO, YDT, NRGEKEL, TNE UITTUE TNEATLE GAS RWEO.

“GEUU, AOC SR, ZDST AS TNE MALLIAFE MAPE TR TNE CRRL, PH DOMUE GAS
MAUUEC AGAH DWRO YDSIOESS TR TNAT NRLLIC PAO PL. STROE. AOC TNEO, HRD
VORG, GNEO ROME TNEH FET TRFETNEL, TNELE IS OR EOC RB IT. GEUU, I GAS SR
BLIFNTEOEC I CIC ORT VORG GNAT TR CR, BRL PH DOMUE GAS TR FIKE PE AGAH;
AOC IB GE GELE YEHROC TNE NRDL GE MRDUC ORT YE PALLIEC AUU CAH. YDT,
UDMVIUH, NE MAPE YAMV AFAIO IO TEO PIODTES’ TIPE, AOC TNEO GE AUU SET
RDT. NRGEKEL, I LEMRUUEMTEC ABTELGALCS, TNAT IB NE _NAC_ YEEO WLEKEOTEC
FRIOF, TNE GECCIOF OEEC ORT YE WDT RBB, BRL PL. CALMH PIFNT NAKE CROE AS
GEUU.”

“PL. CALMH!” LEWEATEC EUIJAYETN, IO DTTEL APAJEPEOT.

“RN, HES! NE GAS TR MRPE TNELE GITN GIMVNAP, HRD VORG. YDT, FLAMIRDS PE!
I QDITE BRLFRT! I RDFNT ORT TR NAKE SAIC A GRLC AYRDT IT. I WLRPISEC
TNEP SR BAITNBDUUH! GNAT GIUU GIMVNAP SAH? IT GAS TR YE SDMN A SEMLET!”

“IB IT GAS TR YE A SEMLET,” SAIC ZAOE, “SAH ORT AORTNEL GRLC RO TNE
SDYZEMT. HRD PAH CEWEOC DWRO PH SEEVIOF OR BDLTNEL.”

“RN, MELTAIOUH,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, TNRDFN YDLOIOF GITN MDLIRSITH; “GE GIUU
ASV HRD OR QDESTIROS.”

“TNAOV HRD,” SAIC UHCIA; “BRL IB HRD CIC, I SNRDUC MELTAIOUH TEUU HRD
AUU, AOC TNEO GIMVNAP GRDUC YE SR AOFLH.”

RO SDMN EOMRDLAFEPEOT TR ASV, EUIJAYETN GAS BRLMEC TR WDT IT RDT RB NEL
WRGEL, YH LDOOIOF AGAH.

YDT TR UIKE IO IFORLAOME RO SDMN A WRIOT GAS IPWRSSIYUE; RL AT UEAST IT
GAS IPWRSSIYUE ORT TR TLH BRL IOBRLPATIRO. PL. CALMH NAC YEEO AT NEL
SISTEL’S GECCIOF. IT GAS EXAMTUH A SMEOE, AOC EXAMTUH APROF WERWUE,
GNELE NE NAC AWWALEOTUH UEAST TR CR, AOC UEAST TEPWTATIRO TR FR.
MROZEMTDLES AS TR TNE PEAOIOF RB IT, LAWIC AOC GIUC, NDLLIEC IOTR NEL
YLAIO; YDT SNE GAS SATISBIEC GITN OROE. TNRSE TNAT YEST WUEASEC NEL, AS
WUAMIOF NIS MROCDMT IO TNE ORYUEST UIFNT, SEEPEC PRST IPWLRYAYUE. SNE
MRDUC ORT YEAL SDMN SDSWEOSE; AOC NASTIUH SEIJIOF A SNEET RB WAWEL,
GLRTE A SNRLT UETTEL TR NEL ADOT, TR LEQDEST AO EXWUAOATIRO RB GNAT
UHCIA NAC CLRWWEC, IB IT GELE MRPWATIYUE GITN TNE SEMLEMH GNIMN NAC YEEO
IOTEOCEC.

“HRD PAH LEACIUH MRPWLENEOC,” SNE ACCEC, “GNAT PH MDLIRSITH PDST YE TR
VORG NRG A WELSRO DOMROOEMTEC GITN AOH RB DS, AOC, MRPWALATIKEUH
SWEAVIOF, A STLAOFEL TR RDL BAPIUH, SNRDUC NAKE YEEO APROFST HRD AT SDMN
A TIPE. WLAH GLITE IOSTAOTUH, AOC UET PE DOCELSTAOC IT--DOUESS IT IS,
BRL KELH MRFEOT LEASROS, TR LEPAIO IO TNE SEMLEMH GNIMN UHCIA SEEPS TR
TNIOV OEMESSALH; AOC TNEO I PDST EOCEAKRDL TR YE SATISBIEC GITN
IFORLAOME.”

“ORT TNAT I _SNAUU_, TNRDFN,” SNE ACCEC TR NELSEUB, AOC SNE BIOISNEC TNE
UETTEL; “AOC, PH CEAL ADOT, IB HRD CR ORT TEUU PE IO AO NRORDLAYUE
PAOOEL, I SNAUU MELTAIOUH YE LECDMEC TR TLIMVS AOC STLATAFEPS TR BIOC IT
RDT.”

ZAOE’S CEUIMATE SEOSE RB NRORDL GRDUC ORT AUURG NEL TR SWEAV TR
EUIJAYETN WLIKATEUH RB GNAT UHCIA NAC UET BAUU; EUIJAYETN GAS FUAC RB
IT:--TIUU IT AWWEALEC GNETNEL NEL IOQDILIES GRDUC LEMEIKE AOH
SATISBAMTIRO, SNE NAC LATNEL YE GITNRDT A MROBICAOTE.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“I AP SDLE SNE CIC ORT UISTEO.”
]




MNAWTEL UII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN NAC TNE SATISBAMTIRO RB LEMEIKIOF AO AOSGEL TR NEL UETTEL AS
SRRO AS SNE WRSSIYUH MRDUC. SNE GAS OR SRROEL IO WRSSESSIRO RB IT, TNAO
NDLLHIOF IOTR TNE UITTUE MRWSE, GNELE SNE GAS UEAST UIVEUH TR YE
IOTELLDWTEC, SNE SAT CRGO RO ROE RB TNE YEOMNES, AOC WLEWALEC TR YE
NAWWH; BRL TNE UEOFTN RB TNE UETTEL MROKIOMEC NEL TNAT IT CIC ORT
MROTAIO A CEOIAU.

     /* LIFNT “FLAMEMNDLMN STLEET, _SEWT. 6_. */

“PH CEAL OIEME,

     “I NAKE ZDST LEMEIKEC HRDL UETTEL, AOC SNAUU CEKRTE TNIS GNRUE
     PRLOIOF TR AOSGELIOF IT, AS I BRLESEE TNAT A _UITTUE_ GLITIOF GIUU
     ORT MRPWLISE GNAT I NAKE TR TEUU HRD. I PDST MROBESS PHSEUB
     SDLWLISEC YH HRDL AWWUIMATIRO; I CIC ORT EXWEMT IT BLRP _HRD_.
     CRO’T TNIOV PE AOFLH, NRGEKEL, BRL I ROUH PEAO TR UET HRD VORG,
     TNAT I NAC ORT IPAFIOEC SDMN IOQDILIES TR YE OEMESSALH RO _HRDL_
     SICE. IB HRD CR ORT MNRRSE TR DOCELSTAOC PE, BRLFIKE PH
     IPWELTIOEOME. HRDL DOMUE IS AS PDMN SDLWLISEC AS I AP; AOC ORTNIOF
     YDT TNE YEUIEB RB HRDL YEIOF A WALTH MROMELOEC GRDUC NAKE AUURGEC
     NIP TR AMT AS NE NAS CROE. YDT IB HRD ALE LEAUUH IOORMEOT AOC
     IFORLAOT, I PDST YE PRLE EXWUIMIT. RO TNE KELH CAH RB PH MRPIOF
     NRPE BLRP UROFYRDLO, HRDL DOMUE NAC A PRST DOEXWEMTEC KISITRL. PL.
     CALMH MAUUEC, AOC GAS SNDT DW GITN NIP SEKELAU NRDLS. IT GAS AUU
     RKEL YEBRLE I ALLIKEC; SR PH MDLIRSITH GAS ORT SR CLEACBDUUH LAMVEC
     AS _HRDLS_ SEEPS TR NAKE YEEO. NE MAPE TR TEUU PL. FALCIOEL TNAT NE
     NAC BRDOC RDT GNELE HRDL SISTEL AOC PL. GIMVNAP GELE, AOC TNAT NE
     NAC SEEO AOC TAUVEC GITN TNEP YRTN--GIMVNAP LEWEATECUH, UHCIA ROME.
     BLRP GNAT I MAO MRUUEMT, NE UEBT CELYHSNILE ROUH ROE CAH ABTEL
     RDLSEUKES, AOC MAPE TR TRGO GITN TNE LESRUDTIRO RB NDOTIOF BRL
     TNEP. TNE PRTIKE WLRBESSEC GAS NIS MROKIMTIRO RB ITS YEIOF RGIOF TR
     NIPSEUB TNAT GIMVNAP’S GRLTNUESSOESS NAC ORT YEEO SR GEUU VORGO AS
     TR PAVE IT IPWRSSIYUE BRL AOH HRDOF GRPAO RB MNALAMTEL TR URKE RL
     MROBICE IO NIP. NE FEOELRDSUH IPWDTEC TNE GNRUE TR NIS PISTAVEO
     WLICE, AOC MROBESSEC TNAT NE NAC YEBRLE TNRDFNT IT YEOEATN NIP TR
     UAH NIS WLIKATE AMTIROS RWEO TR TNE GRLUC. NIS MNALAMTEL GAS TR
     SWEAV BRL ITSEUB. NE MAUUEC IT, TNELEBRLE, NIS CDTH TR STEW
     BRLGALC, AOC EOCEAKRDL TR LEPECH AO EKIU GNIMN NAC YEEO YLRDFNT RO
     YH NIPSEUB. IB NE _NAC AORTNEL_ PRTIKE, I AP SDLE IT GRDUC OEKEL
     CISFLAME NIP. NE NAC YEEO SRPE CAHS IO TRGO YEBRLE NE GAS AYUE TR
     CISMRKEL TNEP; YDT NE NAC SRPETNIOF TR CILEMT NIS SEALMN, GNIMN GAS
     PRLE TNAO _GE_ NAC; AOC TNE MROSMIRDSOESS RB TNIS GAS AORTNEL
     LEASRO BRL NIS LESRUKIOF TR BRUURG DS. TNELE IS A UACH, IT SEEPS, A
     PLS. HRDOFE, GNR GAS SRPE TIPE AFR FRKELOESS TR PISS CALMH, AOC GAS
     CISPISSEC BLRP NEL MNALFE RO SRPE MADSE RB CISAWWLRYATIRO, TNRDFN
     NE CIC ORT SAH GNAT. SNE TNEO TRRV A UALFE NRDSE IO ECGALC STLEET,
     AOC NAS SIOME PAIOTAIOEC NELSEUB YH UETTIOF URCFIOFS. TNIS PLS.
     HRDOFE GAS, NE VOEG, IOTIPATEUH AMQDAIOTEC GITN GIMVNAP; AOC NE
     GEOT TR NEL BRL IOTEUUIFEOME RB NIP, AS SRRO AS NE FRT TR TRGO. YDT
     IT GAS TGR RL TNLEE CAHS YEBRLE NE MRDUC FET BLRP NEL GNAT NE
     GAOTEC. SNE GRDUC ORT YETLAH NEL TLDST, I SDWWRSE, GITNRDT YLIYELH
     AOC MRLLDWTIRO, BRL SNE LEAUUH CIC VORG GNELE NEL BLIEOC GAS TR YE
     BRDOC. GIMVNAP, IOCEEC, NAC FROE TR NEL RO TNEIL BILST ALLIKAU IO
     UROCRO; AOC NAC SNE YEEO AYUE TR LEMEIKE TNEP IOTR NEL NRDSE, TNEH
     GRDUC NAKE TAVEO DW TNEIL AYRCE GITN NEL. AT UEOFTN, NRGEKEL, RDL
     VIOC BLIEOC WLRMDLEC TNE GISNEC-BRL CILEMTIRO. TNEH GELE IO ----
     STLEET. NE SAG GIMVNAP, AOC ABTELGALCS IOSISTEC RO SEEIOF UHCIA.
     NIS BILST RYZEMT GITN NEL, NE AMVORGUECFEC, NAC YEEO TR WELSDACE
     NEL TR QDIT NEL WLESEOT CISFLAMEBDU SITDATIRO, AOC LETDLO TR NEL
     BLIEOCS AS SRRO AS TNEH MRDUC YE WLEKAIUEC RO TR LEMEIKE NEL,
     RBBELIOF NIS ASSISTAOME AS BAL AS IT GRDUC FR. YDT NE BRDOC UHCIA
     AYSRUDTEUH LESRUKEC RO LEPAIOIOF GNELE SNE GAS. SNE MALEC BRL OROE
     RB NEL BLIEOCS; SNE GAOTEC OR NEUW RB NIS; SNE GRDUC ORT NEAL RB
     UEAKIOF GIMVNAP. SNE GAS SDLE TNEH SNRDUC YE PALLIEC SRPE TIPE RL
     RTNEL, AOC IT CIC ORT PDMN SIFOIBH GNEO. SIOME SDMN GELE NEL
     BEEUIOFS, IT ROUH LEPAIOEC, NE TNRDFNT, TR SEMDLE AOC EXWECITE A
     PALLIAFE, GNIMN, IO NIS KELH BILST MROKELSATIRO GITN GIMVNAP, NE
     EASIUH UEALOT NAC OEKEL YEEO _NIS_ CESIFO. NE MROBESSEC NIPSEUB
     RYUIFEC TR UEAKE TNE LEFIPEOT RO AMMRDOT RB SRPE CEYTS RB NRORDL
     GNIMN GELE KELH WLESSIOF; AOC SMLDWUEC ORT TR UAH AUU TNE IUU
     MROSEQDEOMES RB UHCIA’S BUIFNT RO NEL RGO BRUUH AUROE. NE PEAOT TR
     LESIFO NIS MRPPISSIRO IPPECIATEUH; AOC AS TR NIS BDTDLE SITDATIRO,
     NE MRDUC MROZEMTDLE KELH UITTUE AYRDT IT. NE PDST FR SRPEGNELE, YDT
     NE CIC ORT VORG GNELE, AOC NE VOEG NE SNRDUC NAKE ORTNIOF TR UIKE
     RO. PL. CALMH ASVEC GNH NE CIC ORT PALLH HRDL SISTEL AT ROME.
     TNRDFN PL. YEOOET GAS ORT IPAFIOEC TR YE KELH LIMN, NE GRDUC NAKE
     YEEO AYUE TR CR SRPETNIOF BRL NIP, AOC NIS SITDATIRO PDST NAKE YEEO
     YEOEBITEC YH PALLIAFE. YDT NE BRDOC, IO LEWUH TR TNIS QDESTIRO,
     TNAT GIMVNAP STIUU MNELISNEC TNE NRWE RB PRLE EBBEMTDAUUH PAVIOF
     NIS BRLTDOE YH PALLIAFE, IO SRPE RTNEL MRDOTLH. DOCEL SDMN
     MILMDPSTAOMES, NRGEKEL, NE GAS ORT UIVEUH TR YE WLRRB AFAIOST TNE
     TEPWTATIRO RB IPPECIATE LEUIEB. TNEH PET SEKELAU TIPES, BRL TNELE
     GAS PDMN TR YE CISMDSSEC. GIMVNAP, RB MRDLSE, GAOTEC PRLE TNAO NE
     MRDUC FET; YDT AT UEOFTN GAS LECDMEC TR YE LEASROAYUE. EKELHTNIOF
     YEIOF SETTUEC YETGEEO _TNEP_, PL. CALMH’S OEXT STEW GAS TR PAVE
     HRDL DOMUE AMQDAIOTEC GITN IT, AOC NE BILST MAUUEC IO FLAMEMNDLMN
     STLEET TNE EKEOIOF YEBRLE I MAPE NRPE. YDT PL. FALCIOEL MRDUC ORT
     YE SEEO; AOC PL. CALMH BRDOC, RO BDLTNEL IOQDILH, TNAT HRDL BATNEL
     GAS STIUU GITN NIP, YDT GRDUC QDIT TRGO TNE OEXT PRLOIOF. NE CIC
     ORT ZDCFE HRDL BATNEL TR YE A WELSRO GNRP NE MRDUC SR WLRWELUH
     MROSDUT AS HRDL DOMUE, AOC TNELEBRLE LEACIUH WRSTWROEC SEEIOF NIP
     TIUU ABTEL TNE CEWALTDLE RB TNE BRLPEL. NE CIC ORT UEAKE NIS OAPE,
     AOC TIUU TNE OEXT CAH IT GAS ROUH VORGO TNAT A FEOTUEPAO NAC MAUUEC
     RO YDSIOESS. RO SATDLCAH NE MAPE AFAIO. HRDL BATNEL GAS FROE, HRDL
     DOMUE AT NRPE, AOC, AS I SAIC YEBRLE, TNEH NAC A FLEAT CEAU RB TAUV
     TRFETNEL. TNEH PET AFAIO RO SDOCAH, AOC TNEO _I_ SAG NIP TRR. IT
     GAS ORT AUU SETTUEC YEBRLE PROCAH: AS SRRO AS IT GAS, TNE EXWLESS
     GAS SEOT RBB TR UROFYRDLO. YDT RDL KISITRL GAS KELH RYSTIOATE. I
     BAOMH, UIJJH, TNAT RYSTIOAMH IS TNE LEAU CEBEMT RB NIS MNALAMTEL,
     ABTEL AUU. NE NAS YEEO AMMDSEC RB PAOH BADUTS AT CIBBELEOT TIPES;
     YDT _TNIS_ IS TNE TLDE ROE. ORTNIOF GAS TR YE CROE TNAT NE CIC ORT
     CR NIPSEUB; TNRDFN I AP SDLE (AOC I CR ORT SWEAV IT TR YE TNAOVEC,
     TNELEBRLE SAH ORTNIOF AYRDT IT) HRDL DOMUE GRDUC PRST LEACIUH NAKE
     SETTUEC TNE GNRUE. TNEH YATTUEC IT TRFETNEL BRL A UROF TIPE, GNIMN
     GAS PRLE TNAO EITNEL TNE FEOTUEPAO RL UACH MROMELOEC IO IT
     CESELKEC. YDT AT UAST HRDL DOMUE GAS BRLMEC TR HIEUC, AOC IOSTEAC
     RB YEIOF AUURGEC TR YE RB DSE TR NIS OIEME, GAS BRLMEC TR WDT DW
     GITN ROUH NAKIOF TNE WLRYAYUE MLECIT RB IT, GNIMN GEOT SRLEUH
     AFAIOST TNE FLAIO; AOC I LEAUUH YEUIEKE HRDL UETTEL TNIS PRLOIOF
     FAKE NIP FLEAT WUEASDLE, YEMADSE IT LEQDILEC AO EXWUAOATIRO TNAT
     GRDUC LRY NIP RB NIS YRLLRGEC BEATNELS, AOC FIKE TNE WLAISE GNELE
     IT GAS CDE. YDT, UIJJH, TNIS PDST FR OR BDLTNEL TNAO HRDLSEUB, RL
     ZAOE AT PRST. HRD VORG WLETTH GEUU, I SDWWRSE, GNAT NAS YEEO CROE
     BRL TNE HRDOF WERWUE. NIS CEYTS ALE TR YE WAIC, APRDOTIOF, I
     YEUIEKE, TR MROSICELAYUH PRLE TNAO A TNRDSAOC WRDOCS, AORTNEL
     TNRDSAOC IO ACCITIRO TR NEL RGO SETTUEC DWRO _NEL_, AOC NIS
     MRPPISSIRO WDLMNASEC. TNE LEASRO GNH AUU TNIS GAS TR YE CROE YH NIP
     AUROE, GAS SDMN AS I NAKE FIKEO AYRKE. IT GAS RGIOF TR NIP, TR NIS
     LESELKE AOC GAOT RB WLRWEL MROSICELATIRO, TNAT GIMVNAP’S MNALAMTEL
     NAC YEEO SR PISDOCELSTRRC, AOC MROSEQDEOTUH TNAT NE NAC YEEO
     LEMEIKEC AOC ORTIMEC AS NE GAS. WELNAWS TNELE GAS SRPE TLDTN IO
     _TNIS_; TNRDFN I CRDYT GNETNEL _NIS_ LESELKE, RL _AOHYRCH’S_
     LESELKE MAO YE AOSGELAYUE BRL TNE EKEOT. YDT IO SWITE RB AUU TNIS
     BIOE TAUVIOF, PH CEAL UIJJH, HRD PAH LEST WELBEMTUH ASSDLEC TNAT
     HRDL DOMUE GRDUC OEKEL NAKE HIEUCEC, IB GE NAC ORT FIKEO NIP MLECIT
     BRL _AORTNEL IOTELEST_ IO TNE ABBAIL. GNEO AUU TNIS GAS LESRUKEC
     RO, NE LETDLOEC AFAIO TR NIS BLIEOCS, GNR GELE STIUU STAHIOF AT
     WEPYELUEH; YDT IT GAS AFLEEC TNAT NE SNRDUC YE IO UROCRO ROME PRLE
     GNEO TNE GECCIOF TRRV WUAME, AOC AUU PROEH PATTELS GELE TNEO TR
     LEMEIKE TNE UAST BIOISN. I YEUIEKE I NAKE ORG TRUC HRD EKELHTNIOF.
     IT IS A LEUATIRO GNIMN HRD TEUU PE IS TR FIKE HRD FLEAT SDLWLISE; I
     NRWE AT UEAST IT GIUU ORT ABBRLC HRD AOH CISWUEASDLE. UHCIA MAPE TR
     DS, AOC GIMVNAP NAC MROSTAOT ACPISSIRO TR TNE NRDSE. _NE_ GAS
     EXAMTUH GNAT NE NAC YEEO GNEO I VOEG NIP IO NELTBRLCSNILE; YDT I
     GRDUC ORT TEUU HRD NRG UITTUE I GAS SATISBIEC GITN _NEL_ YENAKIRDL
     GNIUE SNE STAHEC GITN DS, IB I NAC ORT WELMEIKEC, YH ZAOE’S UETTEL
     UAST GECOESCAH, TNAT NEL MROCDMT RO MRPIOF NRPE GAS EXAMTUH RB A
     WIEME GITN IT, AOC TNELEBRLE GNAT I ORG TEUU HRD MAO FIKE HRD OR
     BLESN WAIO. I TAUVEC TR NEL LEWEATECUH IO TNE PRST SELIRDS PAOOEL,
     LEWLESEOTIOF TR NEL TNE GIMVECOESS RB GNAT SNE NAC CROE, AOC AUU
     TNE DONAWWIOESS SNE NAC YLRDFNT RO NEL BAPIUH. IB SNE NEALC PE, IT
     GAS YH FRRC UDMV, BRL I AP SDLE SNE CIC ORT UISTEO. I GAS SRPETIPES
     QDITE WLRKRVEC; YDT TNEO I LEMRUUEMTEC PH CEAL EUIJAYETN AOC ZAOE,
     AOC BRL TNEIL SAVES NAC WATIEOME GITN NEL. PL. CALMH GAS WDOMTDAU
     IO NIS LETDLO, AOC, AS UHCIA IPBRLPEC HRD, ATTEOCEC TNE GECCIOF. NE
     CIOEC GITN DS TNE OEXT CAH, AOC GAS TR UEAKE TRGO AFAIO RO
     GECOESCAH RL TNDLSCAH. GIUU HRD YE KELH AOFLH GITN PE, PH CEAL
     UIJJH, IB I TAVE TNIS RWWRLTDOITH RB SAHIOF (GNAT I GAS OEKEL YRUC
     EORDFN TR SAH YEBRLE) NRG PDMN I UIVE NIP? NIS YENAKIRDL TR DS NAS,
     IO EKELH LESWEMT, YEEO AS WUEASIOF AS GNEO GE GELE IO CELYHSNILE.
     NIS DOCELSTAOCIOF AOC RWIOIROS AUU WUEASE PE; NE GAOTS ORTNIOF YDT
     A UITTUE PRLE UIKEUIOESS, AOC _TNAT_, IB NE PALLH _WLDCEOTUH_, NIS
     GIBE PAH TEAMN NIP. I TNRDFNT NIP KELH SUH; NE NALCUH EKEL
     PEOTIROEC HRDL OAPE. YDT SUHOESS SEEPS TNE BASNIRO. WLAH BRLFIKE
     PE, IB I NAKE YEEO KELH WLESDPIOF, RL AT UEAST CR ORT WDOISN PE SR
     BAL AS TR EXMUDCE PE BLRP W. I SNAUU OEKEL YE QDITE NAWWH TIUU I
     NAKE YEEO AUU LRDOC TNE WALV. A URG WNAETRO GITN A OIME UITTUE WAIL
     RB WROIES GRDUC YE TNE KELH TNIOF. YDT I PDST GLITE OR PRLE. TNE
     MNIUCLEO NAKE YEEO GAOTIOF PE TNIS NAUB NRDL.

“HRDLS, KELH SIOMELEUH,

“P. FALCIOEL.”


TNE MROTEOTS RB TNIS UETTEL TNLEG EUIJAYETN IOTR A BUDTTEL RB SWILITS,
IO GNIMN IT GAS CIBBIMDUT TR CETELPIOE GNETNEL WUEASDLE RL WAIO YRLE TNE
FLEATEST SNALE. TNE KAFDE AOC DOSETTUEC SDSWIMIROS GNIMN DOMELTAIOTH NAC
WLRCDMEC, RB GNAT PL. CALMH PIFNT NAKE YEEO CRIOF TR BRLGALC NEL
SISTEL’S PATMN--GNIMN SNE NAC BEALEC TR EOMRDLAFE, AS AO EXELTIRO RB
FRRCOESS TRR FLEAT TR YE WLRYAYUE, AOC AT TNE SAPE TIPE CLEACEC TR YE
ZDST, BLRP TNE WAIO RB RYUIFATIRO--GELE WLRKEC YEHROC TNEIL FLEATEST
EXTEOT TR YE TLDE! NE NAC BRUURGEC TNEP WDLWRSEUH TR TRGO, NE NAC TAVEO
RO NIPSEUB AUU TNE TLRDYUE AOC PRLTIBIMATIRO ATTEOCAOT RO SDMN A
LESEALMN; IO GNIMN SDWWUIMATIRO NAC YEEO OEMESSALH TR A GRPAO GNRP NE
PDST AYRPIOATE AOC CESWISE, AOC GNELE NE GAS LECDMEC TR PEET, BLEQDEOTUH
PEET, LEASRO GITN, WELSDACE, AOC BIOAUUH YLIYE TNE PAO GNRP NE AUGAHS
PRST GISNEC TR AKRIC, AOC GNRSE KELH OAPE IT GAS WDOISNPEOT TR NIP TR
WLRORDOME. NE NAC CROE AUU TNIS BRL A FILU GNRP NE MRDUC OEITNEL LEFALC
ORL ESTEEP. NEL NEALT CIC GNISWEL TNAT NE NAC CROE IT BRL NEL. YDT IT
GAS A NRWE SNRLTUH MNEMVEC YH RTNEL MROSICELATIROS; AOC SNE SRRO BEUT
TNAT EKEO NEL KAOITH GAS IOSDBBIMIEOT, GNEO LEQDILEC TR CEWEOC RO NIS
ABBEMTIRO BRL NEL, BRL A GRPAO GNR NAC AULEACH LEBDSEC NIP, AS AYUE TR
RKELMRPE A SEOTIPEOT SR OATDLAU AS AYNRLLEOME AFAIOST LEUATIROSNIW GITN
GIMVNAP. YLRTNEL-IO-UAG RB GIMVNAP! EKELH VIOC RB WLICE PDST LEKRUT BLRP
TNE MROOEMTIRO. NE NAC, TR YE SDLE, CROE PDMN. SNE GAS ASNAPEC TR TNIOV
NRG PDMN. YDT NE NAC FIKEO A LEASRO BRL NIS IOTELBELEOME, GNIMN ASVEC OR
EXTLARLCIOALH STLETMN RB YEUIEB. IT GAS LEASROAYUE TNAT NE SNRDUC BEEU
NE NAC YEEO GLROF; NE NAC UIYELAUITH, AOC NE NAC TNE PEAOS RB EXELMISIOF
IT; AOC TNRDFN SNE GRDUC ORT WUAME NELSEUB AS NIS WLIOMIWAU IOCDMEPEOT,
SNE MRDUC WELNAWS YEUIEKE, TNAT LEPAIOIOF WALTIAUITH BRL NEL PIFNT
ASSIST NIS EOCEAKRDLS IO A MADSE GNELE NEL WEAME RB PIOC PDST YE
PATELIAUUH MROMELOEC. IT GAS WAIOBDU, EXMEECIOFUH WAIOBDU, TR VORG TNAT
TNEH GELE DOCEL RYUIFATIROS TR A WELSRO GNR MRDUC OEKEL LEMEIKE A
LETDLO. TNEH RGEC TNE LESTRLATIRO RB UHCIA, NEL MNALAMTEL, EKELHTNIOF TR
NIP. RN, NRG NEALTIUH CIC SNE FLIEKE RKEL EKELH DOFLAMIRDS SEOSATIRO SNE
NAC EKEL EOMRDLAFEC, EKELH SADMH SWEEMN SNE NAC EKEL CILEMTEC TRGALCS
NIP! BRL NELSEUB SNE GAS NDPYUEC; YDT SNE GAS WLRDC RB NIP,--WLRDC TNAT
IO A MADSE RB MRPWASSIRO AOC NRORDL NE NAC YEEO AYUE TR FET TNE YETTEL
RB NIPSEUB. SNE LEAC RKEL NEL ADOT’S MRPPEOCATIRO RB NIP AFAIO AOC
AFAIO. IT GAS NALCUH EORDFN; YDT IT WUEASEC NEL. SNE GAS EKEO SEOSIYUE
RB SRPE WUEASDLE, TNRDFN PIXEC GITN LEFLET, RO BIOCIOF NRG STEACBASTUH
YRTN SNE AOC NEL DOMUE NAC YEEO WELSDACEC TNAT ABBEMTIRO AOC MROBICEOME
SDYSISTEC YETGEEO PL. CALMH AOC NELSEUB.

SNE GAS LRDSEC BLRP NEL SEAT AOC NEL LEBUEMTIROS, YH SRPEROE’S AWWLRAMN;
AOC, YEBRLE SNE MRDUC STLIVE IOTR AORTNEL WATN, SNE GAS RKELTAVEO YH
GIMVNAP.

“I AP ABLAIC I IOTELLDWT HRDL SRUITALH LAPYUE, PH CEAL SISTEL?” SAIC NE,
AS NE ZRIOEC NEL.

“HRD MELTAIOUH CR,” SNE LEWUIEC GITN A SPIUE; “YDT IT CRES ORT BRUURG
TNAT TNE IOTELLDWTIRO PDST YE DOGEUMRPE.”

“I SNRDUC YE SRLLH, IOCEEC, IB IT GELE. _GE_ GELE AUGAHS FRRC BLIEOCS,
AOC ORG GE ALE YETTEL.”

“TLDE. ALE TNE RTNELS MRPIOF RDT?”

“I CR ORT VORG. PLS. YEOOET AOC UHCIA ALE FRIOF IO TNE MALLIAFE TR
PELHTRO. AOC SR, PH CEAL SISTEL, I BIOC, BLRP RDL DOMUE AOC ADOT, TNAT
HRD NAKE AMTDAUUH SEEO WEPYELUEH.”

SNE LEWUIEC IO TNE ABBILPATIKE.

“I AUPRST EOKH HRD TNE WUEASDLE, AOC HET I YEUIEKE IT GRDUC YE TRR PDMN
BRL PE, RL EUSE I MRDUC TAVE IT IO PH GAH TR OEGMASTUE. AOC HRD SAG TNE
RUC NRDSEVEEWEL, I SDWWRSE? WRRL LEHORUCS, SNE GAS AUGAHS KELH BROC RB
PE. YDT RB MRDLSE SNE CIC ORT PEOTIRO PH OAPE TR HRD.”

“HES, SNE CIC.”

“AOC GNAT CIC SNE SAH?”

“TNAT HRD GELE FROE IOTR TNE ALPH, AOC SNE GAS ABLAIC NAC--ORT TDLOEC
RDT GEUU. AT SDMN A CISTAOME AS _TNAT_, HRD VORG, TNIOFS ALE STLAOFEUH
PISLEWLESEOTEC.”

“MELTAIOUH,” NE LEWUIEC, YITIOF NIS UIWS. EUIJAYETN NRWEC SNE NAC
SIUEOMEC NIP; YDT NE SRRO ABTELGALCS SAIC,--

“I GAS SDLWLISEC TR SEE CALMH IO TRGO UAST PROTN. GE WASSEC EAMN RTNEL
SEKELAU TIPES. I GROCEL GNAT NE MAO YE CRIOF TNELE.”

“WELNAWS WLEWALIOF BRL NIS PALLIAFE GITN PISS CE YRDLFN,” SAIC
EUIJAYETN. “IT PDST YE SRPETNIOF WALTIMDUAL TR TAVE NIP TNELE AT TNIS
TIPE RB HEAL.”

“DOCRDYTECUH. CIC HRD SEE NIP GNIUE HRD GELE AT UAPYTRO? I TNRDFNT I
DOCELSTRRC BLRP TNE FALCIOELS TNAT HRD NAC.”

“HES; NE IOTLRCDMEC DS TR NIS SISTEL.”

“AOC CR HRD UIVE NEL?”

“KELH PDMN.”

“I NAKE NEALC, IOCEEC, TNAT SNE IS DOMRPPROUH IPWLRKEC GITNIO TNIS HEAL
RL TGR. GNEO I UAST SAG NEL, SNE GAS ORT KELH WLRPISIOF. I AP KELH FUAC
HRD UIVEC NEL. I NRWE SNE GIUU TDLO RDT GEUU.”

“I CALE SAH SNE GIUU; SNE NAS FRT RKEL TNE PRST TLHIOF AFE.”

“CIC HRD FR YH TNE KIUUAFE RB VHPWTRO?”

“I CR ORT LEMRUUEMT TNAT GE CIC.”

“I PEOTIRO IT YEMADSE IT IS TNE UIKIOF GNIMN I RDFNT TR NAKE NAC. A PRST
CEUIFNTBDU WUAME! EXMEUUEOT WALSROAFE-NRDSE! IT GRDUC NAKE SDITEC PE IO
EKELH LESWEMT.”

“NRG SNRDUC HRD NAKE UIVEC PAVIOF SELPROS?”

“EXMEECIOFUH GEUU. I SNRDUC NAKE MROSICELEC IT AS WALT RB PH CDTH, AOC
TNE EXELTIRO GRDUC SRRO NAKE YEEO ORTNIOF. ROE RDFNT ORT TR LEWIOE; YDT,
TR YE SDLE, IT GRDUC NAKE YEEO SDMN A TNIOF BRL PE! TNE QDIET, TNE
LETILEPEOT RB SDMN A UIBE, GRDUC NAKE AOSGELEC AUU PH ICEAS RB
NAWWIOESS! YDT IT GAS ORT TR YE. CIC HRD EKEL NEAL CALMH PEOTIRO TNE
MILMDPSTAOME GNEO HRD GELE IO VEOT?”

“I _NAKE_ NEALC BLRP ADTNRLITH, GNIMN I TNRDFNT _AS FRRC_, TNAT IT GAS
UEBT HRD MROCITIROAUUH ROUH, AOC AT TNE GIUU RB TNE WLESEOT WATLRO.”

“HRD NAKE! HES, TNELE GAS SRPETNIOF IO _TNAT_; I TRUC HRD SR BLRP TNE
BILST, HRD PAH LEPEPYEL.”

“I _CIC_ NEAL, TRR, TNAT TNELE GAS A TIPE GNEO SELPRO-PAVIOF GAS ORT SR
WAUATAYUE TR HRD AS IT SEEPS TR YE AT WLESEOT; TNAT HRD AMTDAUUH
CEMUALEC HRDL LESRUDTIRO RB OEKEL TAVIOF RLCELS, AOC TNAT TNE YDSIOESS
NAC YEEO MRPWLRPISEC AMMRLCIOFUH.”

“HRD CIC! AOC IT GAS ORT GNRUUH GITNRDT BRDOCATIRO. HRD PAH LEPEPYEL
GNAT I TRUC HRD RO TNAT WRIOT, GNEO BILST GE TAUVEC RB IT.”

TNEH GELE ORG AUPRST AT TNE CRRL RB TNE NRDSE, BRL SNE NAC GAUVEC BAST
TR FET LIC RB NIP; AOC DOGIUUIOF, BRL NEL SISTEL’S SAVE, TR WLRKRVE NIP,
SNE ROUH SAIC IO LEWUH, GITN A FRRC-NDPRDLEC SPIUE,--

“MRPE, PL. GIMVNAP, GE ALE YLRTNEL AOC SISTEL, HRD VORG. CR ORT UET DS
QDALLEU AYRDT TNE WAST. IO BDTDLE, I NRWE GE SNAUU YE AUGAHS RB ROE
PIOC.”

SNE NEUC RDT NEL NAOC: NE VISSEC IT GITN ABBEMTIROATE FAUUAOTLH, TNRDFN
NE NALCUH VOEG NRG TR URRV, AOC TNEH EOTELEC TNE NRDSE.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“PL. CALMH GITN NIP.”

MNAWTEL UIII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

PL. GIMVNAP GAS SR WELBEMTUH SATISBIEC GITN TNIS MROKELSATIRO, TNAT NE
OEKEL AFAIO CISTLESSEC NIPSEUB, RL WLRKRVEC NIS CEAL SISTEL EUIJAYETN,
YH IOTLRCDMIOF TNE SDYZEMT RB IT; AOC SNE GAS WUEASEC TR BIOC TNAT SNE
NAC SAIC EORDFN TR VEEW NIP QDIET.

TNE CAH RB NIS AOC UHCIA’S CEWALTDLE SRRO MAPE; AOC PLS. YEOOET GAS
BRLMEC TR SDYPIT TR A SEWALATIRO, GNIMN, AS NEL NDSYAOC YH OR PEAOS
EOTELEC IOTR NEL SMNEPE RB TNEIL AUU FRIOF TR OEGMASTUE, GAS UIVEUH TR
MROTIODE AT UEAST A TGEUKEPROTN.

“RN, PH CEAL UHCIA,” SNE MLIEC, “GNEO SNAUU GE PEET AFAIO?”

“RN, URLC! I CRO’T VORG. ORT TNESE TGR RL TNLEE HEALS, WELNAWS.”

“GLITE TR PE KELH RBTEO, PH CEAL.”

“AS RBTEO AS I MAO. YDT HRD VORG PALLIEC GRPEO NAKE OEKEL PDMN TIPE BRL
GLITIOF. PH SISTELS PAH GLITE TR _PE_. TNEH GIUU NAKE ORTNIOF EUSE TR
CR.”

PL. GIMVNAP’S ACIEDS GELE PDMN PRLE ABBEMTIROATE TNAO NIS GIBE’S. NE
SPIUEC, URRVEC NAOCSRPE, AOC SAIC PAOH WLETTH TNIOFS.

“NE IS AS BIOE A BEUURG,” SAIC PL. YEOOET, AS SRRO AS TNEH GELE RDT RB
TNE NRDSE, “AS EKEL I SAG. NE SIPWELS, AOC SPILVS, AOC PAVES URKE TR DS
AUU. I AP WLRCIFIRDSUH WLRDC RB NIP. I CEBH EKEO SIL GIUUIAP UDMAS
NIPSEUB TR WLRCDME A PRLE KAUDAYUE SRO-IO-UAG.”

TNE URSS RB NEL CADFNTEL PACE PLS. YEOOET KELH CDUU BRL SEKELAU CAHS.

“I RBTEO TNIOV,” SAIC SNE, “TNAT TNELE IS ORTNIOF SR YAC AS WALTIOF GITN
ROE’S BLIEOCS. ROE SEEPS SR BRLURLO GITNRDT TNEP.”

“TNIS IS TNE MROSEQDEOME, HRD SEE, PACAP, RB PALLHIOF A CADFNTEL,” SAIC
EUIJAYETN. “IT PDST PAVE HRD YETTEL SATISBIEC TNAT HRDL RTNEL BRDL ALE
SIOFUE.”

“IT IS OR SDMN TNIOF. UHCIA CRES ORT UEAKE PE YEMADSE SNE IS PALLIEC;
YDT ROUH YEMADSE NEL NDSYAOC’S LEFIPEOT NAWWEOS TR YE SR BAL RBB. IB
TNAT NAC YEEO OEALEL, SNE GRDUC ORT NAKE FROE SR SRRO.”

YDT TNE SWILITUESS MROCITIRO GNIMN TNIS EKEOT TNLEG NEL IOTR GAS SNRLTUH
LEUIEKEC, AOC NEL PIOC RWEOEC AFAIO TR TNE AFITATIRO RB NRWE, YH AO
ALTIMUE RB OEGS GNIMN TNEO YEFAO TR YE IO MILMDUATIRO. TNE NRDSEVEEWEL
AT OETNELBIEUC NAC LEMEIKEC RLCELS TR WLEWALE BRL TNE ALLIKAU RB NEL
PASTEL, GNR GAS MRPIOF CRGO IO A CAH RL TGR, TR SNRRT TNELE BRL SEKELAU
GEEVS. PLS. YEOOET GAS QDITE IO TNE BICFETS. SNE URRVEC AT ZAOE, AOC
SPIUEC, AOC SNRRV NEL NEAC, YH TDLOS.

“GEUU, GEUU, AOC SR PL. YIOFUEH IS MRPIOF CRGO, SISTEL,” (BRL PLS.
WNIUIWS BILST YLRDFNT NEL TNE OEGS). “GEUU, SR PDMN TNE YETTEL. ORT TNAT
I MALE AYRDT IT, TNRDFN. NE IS ORTNIOF TR DS, HRD VORG, AOC I AP SDLE I
OEKEL GAOT TR SEE NIP AFAIO. YDT, NRGEKEL, NE IS KELH GEUMRPE TR MRPE TR
OETNELBIEUC, IB NE UIVES IT. AOC GNR VORGS GNAT _PAH_ NAWWEO? YDT TNAT
IS ORTNIOF TR DS. HRD VORG, SISTEL, GE AFLEEC UROF AFR OEKEL TR PEOTIRO
A GRLC AYRDT IT. AOC SR, IT IS QDITE MELTAIO NE IS MRPIOF?”

“HRD PAH CEWEOC RO IT,” LEWUIEC TNE RTNEL, “BRL PLS. OIMNRUS GAS IO
PELHTRO UAST OIFNT: I SAG NEL WASSIOF YH, AOC GEOT RDT PHSEUB RO WDLWRSE
TR VORG TNE TLDTN RB IT; AOC SNE TRUC PE TNAT IT GAS MELTAIOUH TLDE. NE
MRPES CRGO RO TNDLSCAH, AT TNE UATEST, KELH UIVEUH RO GECOESCAH. SNE GAS
FRIOF TR TNE YDTMNEL’S, SNE TRUC PE, RO WDLWRSE TR RLCEL IO SRPE PEAT RO
GECOESCAH, AOC SNE NAS FRT TNLEE MRDWUE RB CDMVS ZDST BIT TR YE VIUUEC.”

PISS YEOOET NAC ORT YEEO AYUE TR NEAL RB NIS MRPIOF GITNRDT MNAOFIOF
MRURDL. IT GAS PAOH PROTNS SIOME SNE NAC PEOTIROEC NIS OAPE TR
EUIJAYETN; YDT ORG, AS SRRO AS TNEH GELE AUROE TRFETNEL, SNE SAIC,--

“I SAG HRD URRV AT PE TR-CAH, UIJJH, GNEO PH ADOT TRUC DS RB TNE WLESEOT
LEWRLT; AOC I VORG I AWWEALEC CISTLESSEC; YDT CRO’T IPAFIOE IT GAS BLRP
AOH SIUUH MADSE. I GAS ROUH MROBDSEC BRL TNE PRPEOT, YEMADSE I BEUT TNAT
I _SNRDUC_ YE URRVEC AT. I CR ASSDLE HRD TNAT TNE OEGS CRES ORT ABBEMT
PE EITNEL GITN WUEASDLE RL WAIO. I AP FUAC RB ROE TNIOF, TNAT NE MRPES
AUROE; YEMADSE GE SNAUU SEE TNE UESS RB NIP. ORT TNAT I AP ABLAIC RB
_PHSEUB_, YDT I CLEAC RTNEL WERWUE’S LEPALVS.”

EUIJAYETN CIC ORT VORG GNAT TR PAVE RB IT. NAC SNE ORT SEEO NIP IO
CELYHSNILE, SNE PIFNT NAKE SDWWRSEC NIP MAWAYUE RB MRPIOF TNELE GITN OR
RTNEL KIEG TNAO GNAT GAS AMVORGUECFEC; YDT SNE STIUU TNRDFNT NIP WALTIAU
TR ZAOE, AOC SNE GAKELEC AS TR TNE FLEATEL WLRYAYIUITH RB NIS MRPIOF
TNELE _GITN_ NIS BLIEOC’S WELPISSIRO, RL YEIOF YRUC EORDFN TR MRPE
GITNRDT IT.

“HET IT IS NALC,” SNE SRPETIPES TNRDFNT, “TNAT TNIS WRRL PAO MAOORT MRPE
TR A NRDSE, GNIMN NE NAS UEFAUUH NILEC, GITNRDT LAISIOF AUU TNIS
SWEMDUATIRO! I _GIUU_ UEAKE NIP TR NIPSEUB.”

IO SWITE RB GNAT NEL SISTEL CEMUALEC, AOC LEAUUH YEUIEKEC TR YE NEL
BEEUIOFS, IO TNE EXWEMTATIRO RB NIS ALLIKAU, EUIJAYETN MRDUC EASIUH
WELMEIKE TNAT NEL SWILITS GELE ABBEMTEC YH IT. TNEH GELE PRLE CISTDLYEC,
PRLE DOEQDAU, TNAO SNE NAC RBTEO SEEO TNEP.

TNE SDYZEMT GNIMN NAC YEEO SR GALPUH MAOKASSEC YETGEEO TNEIL WALEOTS,
AYRDT A TGEUKEPROTN AFR, GAS ORG YLRDFNT BRLGALC AFAIO.

“AS SRRO AS EKEL PL. YIOFUEH MRPES, PH CEAL,” SAIC PLS. YEOOET, “HRD
GIUU GAIT RO NIP, RB MRDLSE.”

“OR, OR. HRD BRLMEC PE IOTR KISITIOF NIP UAST HEAL, AOC WLRPISEC, IB I
GEOT TR SEE NIP, NE SNRDUC PALLH ROE RB PH CADFNTELS. YDT IT EOCEC IO
ORTNIOF, AOC I GIUU ORT YE SEOT RO A BRRU’S ELLAOC AFAIO.”

NIS GIBE LEWLESEOTEC TR NIP NRG AYSRUDTEUH OEMESSALH SDMN AO ATTEOTIRO
GRDUC YE BLRP AUU TNE OEIFNYRDLIOF FEOTUEPEO, RO NIS LETDLOIOF TR
OETNELBIEUC.

“’TIS AO _ETIQDETTE_ I CESWISE,” SAIC NE. “IB NE GAOTS RDL SRMIETH, UET
NIP SEEV IT. NE VORGS GNELE GE UIKE. I GIUU ORT SWEOC _PH_ NRDLS IO
LDOOIOF ABTEL PH OEIFNYRDLS EKELH TIPE TNEH FR AGAH AOC MRPE YAMV
AFAIO.”

“GEUU, AUU I VORG IS, TNAT IT GIUU YE AYRPIOAYUH LDCE IB HRD CR ORT GAIT
RO NIP. YDT, NRGEKEL, TNAT SNAO’T WLEKEOT PH ASVIOF NIP TR CIOE NELE, I
AP CETELPIOEC. GE PDST NAKE PLS. UROF AOC TNE FRDUCIOFS SRRO. TNAT GIUU
PAVE TNILTEEO GITN RDLSEUKES, SR TNELE GIUU YE ZDST LRRP AT TAYUE BRL
NIP.”

MROSRUEC YH TNIS LESRUDTIRO, SNE GAS TNE YETTEL AYUE TR YEAL NEL
NDSYAOC’S IOMIKIUITH; TNRDFN IT GAS KELH PRLTIBHIOF TR VORG TNAT NEL
OEIFNYRDLS PIFNT AUU SEE PL. YIOFUEH, IO MROSEQDEOME RB IT, YEBRLE
_TNEH_ CIC. AS TNE CAH RB NIS ALLIKAU CLEG OEAL,--

“I YEFIO TR YE SRLLH TNAT NE MRPES AT AUU,” SAIC ZAOE TR NEL SISTEL. “IT
GRDUC YE ORTNIOF; I MRDUC SEE NIP GITN WELBEMT IOCIBBELEOME; YDT I MAO
NALCUH YEAL TR NEAL IT TNDS WELWETDAUUH TAUVEC RB. PH PRTNEL PEAOS GEUU;
YDT SNE CRES ORT VORG, OR ROE MAO VORG, NRG PDMN I SDBBEL BLRP GNAT SNE
SAHS. NAWWH SNAUU I YE GNEO NIS STAH AT OETNELBIEUC IS RKEL!”

“I GISN I MRDUC SAH AOHTNIOF TR MRPBRLT HRD,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN; “YDT IT
IS GNRUUH RDT RB PH WRGEL. HRD PDST BEEU IT; AOC TNE DSDAU SATISBAMTIRO
RB WLEAMNIOF WATIEOME TR A SDBBELEL IS CEOIEC PE, YEMADSE HRD NAKE
AUGAHS SR PDMN.”

PL. YIOFUEH ALLIKEC. PLS. YEOOET, TNLRDFN TNE ASSISTAOME RB SELKAOTS,
MROTLIKEC TR NAKE TNE EALUIEST TICIOFS RB IT, TNAT TNE WELIRC RB AOXIETH
AOC BLETBDUOESS RO NEL SICE YE AS UROF AS IT MRDUC. SNE MRDOTEC TNE CAHS
TNAT PDST IOTELKEOE YEBRLE TNEIL IOKITATIRO MRDUC YE SEOT--NRWEUESS RB
SEEIOF NIP YEBRLE. YDT RO TNE TNILC PRLOIOF ABTEL NIS ALLIKAU IO
NELTBRLCSNILE, SNE SAG NIP BLRP NEL CLESSIOF-LRRP GIOCRG EOTEL TNE
WACCRMV, AOC LICE TRGALCS TNE NRDSE.

NEL CADFNTELS GELE EAFELUH MAUUEC TR WALTAVE RB NEL ZRH. ZAOE LESRUDTEUH
VEWT NEL WUAME AT TNE TAYUE; YDT EUIJAYETN, TR SATISBH NEL PRTNEL, GEOT
TR TNE GIOCRG--SNE URRVEC--SNE SAG PL. CALMH GITN NIP, AOC SAT CRGO
AFAIO YH NEL SISTEL.

“TNELE IS A FEOTUEPAO GITN NIP, PAPPA,” SAIC VITTH; “GNR MAO IT YE?”

“SRPE AMQDAIOTAOME RL RTNEL, PH CEAL, I SDWWRSE; I AP SDLE I CR ORT
VORG.”

“UA!” LEWUIEC VITTH, “IT URRVS ZDST UIVE TNAT PAO TNAT DSEC TR YE GITN
NIP YEBRLE. PL. GNAT’S NIS OAPE--TNAT TAUU, WLRDC PAO.”

“FRRC FLAMIRDS! PL. CALMH!--AOC SR IT CRES, I KRG. GEUU, AOH BLIEOC RB
PL. YIOFUEH’S GIUU AUGAHS YE GEUMRPE NELE, TR YE SDLE; YDT EUSE I PDST
SAH TNAT I NATE TNE KELH SIFNT RB NIP.”

ZAOE URRVEC AT EUIJAYETN GITN SDLWLISE AOC MROMELO. SNE VOEG YDT UITTUE
RB TNEIL PEETIOF IO CELYHSNILE, AOC TNELEBRLE BEUT BRL TNE AGVGALCOESS
GNIMN PDST ATTEOC NEL SISTEL, IO SEEIOF NIP AUPRST BRL TNE BILST TIPE
ABTEL LEMEIKIOF NIS EXWUAOATRLH UETTEL. YRTN SISTELS GELE DOMRPBRLTAYUE
EORDFN. EAMN BEUT BRL TNE RTNEL, AOC RB MRDLSE BRL TNEPSEUKES; AOC TNEIL
PRTNEL TAUVEC RO RB NEL CISUIVE RB PL. CALMH, AOC NEL LESRUDTIRO TR YE
MIKIU TR NIP ROUH AS PL. YIOFUEH’S BLIEOC, GITNRDT YEIOF NEALC YH EITNEL
RB TNEP. YDT EUIJAYETN NAC SRDLMES RB DOEASIOESS GNIMN MRDUC ORT HET YE
SDSWEMTEC YH ZAOE, TR GNRP SNE NAC OEKEL HET NAC MRDLAFE TR SNRG PLS.
FALCIOEL’S UETTEL, RL TR LEUATE NEL RGO MNAOFE RB SEOTIPEOT TRGALCS
NIP. TR ZAOE, NE MRDUC YE ROUH A PAO GNRSE WLRWRSAUS SNE NAC LEBDSEC,
AOC GNRSE PELITS SNE NAC DOCELKAUDEC; YDT TR NEL RGO PRLE EXTEOSIKE
IOBRLPATIRO, NE GAS TNE WELSRO TR GNRP TNE GNRUE BAPIUH GELE IOCEYTEC
BRL TNE BILST RB YEOEBITS, AOC GNRP SNE LEFALCEC NELSEUB GITN AO
IOTELEST, IB ORT QDITE SR TEOCEL, AT UEAST AS LEASROAYUE AOC ZDST, AS
GNAT ZAOE BEUT BRL YIOFUEH. NEL ASTROISNPEOT AT NIS MRPIOF--AT NIS
MRPIOF TR OETNELBIEUC, TR UROFYRDLO, AOC KRUDOTALIUH SEEVIOF NEL AFAIO,
GAS AUPRST EQDAU TR GNAT SNE NAC VORGO RO BILST GITOESSIOF NIS AUTELEC
YENAKIRDL IO CELYHSNILE.

TNE MRURDL GNIMN NAC YEEO CLIKEO BLRP NEL BAME LETDLOEC BRL NAUB A
PIODTE GITN AO ACCITIROAU FURG, AOC A SPIUE RB CEUIFNT ACCEC UDSTLE TR
NEL EHES, AS SNE TNRDFNT BRL TNAT SWAME RB TIPE TNAT NIS ABBEMTIRO AOC
GISNES PDST STIUU YE DOSNAVEO; YDT SNE GRDUC ORT YE SEMDLE.

“UET PE BILST SEE NRG NE YENAKES,” SAIC SNE; “IT GIUU TNEO YE EALUH
EORDFN BRL EXWEMTATIRO.”

SNE SAT IOTEOTUH AT GRLV, STLIKIOF TR YE MRPWRSEC, AOC GITNRDT CALIOF TR
UIBT DW NEL EHES, TIUU AOXIRDS MDLIRSITH MALLIEC TNEP TR TNE BAME RB NEL
SISTEL AS TNE SELKAOT GAS AWWLRAMNIOF TNE CRRL. ZAOE URRVEC A UITTUE
WAUEL TNAO DSDAU, YDT PRLE SECATE TNAO EUIJAYETN NAC EXWEMTEC. RO TNE
FEOTUEPEO’S AWWEALIOF, NEL MRURDL IOMLEASEC; HET SNE LEMEIKEC TNEP GITN
TRUELAYUE EASE, AOC GITN A WLRWLIETH RB YENAKIRDL EQDAUUH BLEE BLRP AOH
SHPWTRP RB LESEOTPEOT, RL AOH DOOEMESSALH MRPWUAISAOME.

EUIJAYETN SAIC AS UITTUE TR EITNEL AS MIKIUITH GRDUC AUURG, AOC SAT CRGO
AFAIO TR NEL GRLV, GITN AO EAFELOESS GNIMN IT CIC ORT RBTEO MRPPAOC. SNE
NAC KEOTDLEC ROUH ROE FUAOME AT CALMH. NE URRVEC SELIRDS AS DSDAU; AOC,
SNE TNRDFNT, PRLE AS NE NAC YEEO DSEC TR URRV IO NELTBRLCSNILE, TNAO AS
SNE NAC SEEO NIP AT WEPYELUEH. YDT, WELNAWS, NE MRDUC ORT IO NEL
PRTNEL’S WLESEOME YE GNAT NE GAS YEBRLE NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT. IT GAS A
WAIOBDU, YDT ORT AO IPWLRYAYUE, MROZEMTDLE.

YIOFUEH SNE NAC UIVEGISE SEEO BRL AO IOSTAOT, AOC IO TNAT SNRLT WELIRC
SAG NIP URRVIOF YRTN WUEASEC AOC EPYALLASSEC. NE GAS LEMEIKEC YH PLS.
YEOOET GITN A CEFLEE RB MIKIUITH GNIMN PACE NEL TGR CADFNTELS ASNAPEC,
ESWEMIAUUH GNEO MROTLASTEC GITN TNE MRUC AOC MELEPROIRDS WRUITEOESS RB
NEL MRDLTESH AOC ACCLESS RB NIS BLIEOC.

EUIJAYETN WALTIMDUALUH, GNR VOEG TNAT NEL PRTNEL RGEC TR TNE UATTEL TNE
WLESELKATIRO RB NEL BAKRDLITE CADFNTEL BLRP ILLEPECIAYUE IOBAPH, GAS
NDLT AOC CISTLESSEC TR A PRST WAIOBDU CEFLEE YH A CISTIOMTIRO SR IUU
AWWUIEC.

CALMH, ABTEL IOQDILIOF RB NEL NRG PL. AOC PLS. FALCIOEL CIC--A QDESTIRO
GNIMN SNE MRDUC ORT AOSGEL GITNRDT MROBDSIRO--SAIC SMALMEUH AOHTNIOF. NE
GAS ORT SEATEC YH NEL: WELNAWS TNAT GAS TNE LEASRO RB NIS SIUEOME; YDT
IT NAC ORT YEEO SR IO CELYHSNILE. TNELE NE NAC TAUVEC TR NEL BLIEOCS
GNEO NE MRDUC ORT TR NELSEUB. YDT ORG SEKELAU PIODTES EUAWSEC, GITNRDT
YLIOFIOF TNE SRDOC RB NIS KRIME; AOC GNEO RMMASIROAUUH, DOAYUE TR LESIST
TNE IPWDUSE RB MDLIRSITH, SNE LAISEC NEL EHES TR NIS BAME, SNE AS RBTEO
BRDOC NIP URRVIOF AT ZAOE AS AT NELSEUB, AOC BLEQDEOTUH RO OR RYZEMT YDT
TNE FLRDOC. PRLE TNRDFNTBDUOESS AOC UESS AOXIETH TR WUEASE, TNAO GNEO
TNEH UAST PET, GELE WUAIOUH EXWLESSEC. SNE GAS CISAWWRIOTEC, AOC AOFLH
GITN NELSEUB BRL YEIOF SR.

“MRDUC I EXWEMT IT TR YE RTNELGISE?” SAIC SNE. “HET GNH CIC NE MRPE?”

SNE GAS IO OR NDPRDL BRL MROKELSATIRO GITN AOHROE YDT NIPSEUB; AOC TR
NIP SNE NAC NALCUH MRDLAFE TR SWEAV.

SNE IOQDILEC ABTEL NIS SISTEL, YDT MRDUC CR OR PRLE.

“IT IS A UROF TIPE, PL. YIOFUEH, SIOME HRD GEOT AGAH,” SAIC PLS. YEOOET.

NE LEACIUH AFLEEC TR IT.

“I YEFAO TR YE ABLAIC HRD GRDUC OEKEL MRPE YAMV AFAIO. WERWUE _CIC_ SAH,
HRD PEAOT TR QDIT TNE WUAME EOTILEUH AT PIMNAEUPAS; YDT, NRGEKEL, I NRWE
IT IS ORT TLDE. A FLEAT PAOH MNAOFES NAKE NAWWEOEC IO TNE OEIFNYRDLNRRC
SIOME HRD GEOT AGAH. PISS UDMAS IS PALLIEC AOC SETTUEC: AOC ROE RB PH
RGO CADFNTELS. I SDWWRSE HRD NAKE NEALC RB IT; IOCEEC, HRD PDST NAKE
SEEO IT IO TNE WAWELS. IT GAS IO TNE ‘TIPES’ AOC TNE ‘MRDLIEL,’ I VORG;
TNRDFN IT GAS ORT WDT IO AS IT RDFNT TR YE. IT GAS ROUH SAIC, ‘UATEUH,
FERLFE GIMVNAP, ESQ., TR PISS UHCIA YEOOET,’ GITNRDT TNELE YEIOF A
SHUUAYUE SAIC RB NEL BATNEL, RL TNE WUAME GNELE SNE UIKEC, RL AOHTNIOF.
IT GAS PH YLRTNEL FALCIOEL’S CLAGIOF DW, TRR, AOC I GROCEL NRG NE MAPE
TR PAVE SDMN AO AGVGALC YDSIOESS RB IT. CIC HRD SEE IT?”

YIOFUEH LEWUIEC TNAT NE CIC, AOC PACE NIS MROFLATDUATIROS. EUIJAYETN
CALEC ORT UIBT DW NEL EHES. NRG PL. CALMH URRVEC, TNELEBRLE, SNE MRDUC
ORT TEUU.

“IT IS A CEUIFNTBDU TNIOF, TR YE SDLE, TR NAKE A CADFNTEL GEUU PALLIEC,”
MROTIODEC NEL PRTNEL; “YDT AT TNE SAPE TIPE, PL. YIOFUEH, IT IS KELH
NALC TR NAKE NEL TAVEO AGAH BLRP PE. TNEH ALE FROE CRGO TR OEGMASTUE, A
WUAME QDITE ORLTNGALC IT SEEPS, AOC TNELE TNEH ALE TR STAH, I CR ORT
VORG NRG UROF. NIS LEFIPEOT IS TNELE; BRL I SDWWRSE HRD NAKE NEALC RB
NIS UEAKIOF TNE ----SNILE, AOC RB NIS YEIOF FROE IOTR TNE LEFDUALS.
TNAOV NEAKEO! NE NAS _SRPE_ BLIEOCS, TNRDFN, WELNAWS, ORT SR PAOH AS NE
CESELKES.”

EUIJAYETN, GNR VOEG TNIS TR YE UEKEUUEC AT PL. CALMH, GAS IO SDMN PISELH
RB SNAPE TNAT SNE MRDUC NALCUH VEEW NEL SEAT. IT CLEG BLRP NEL, NRGEKEL,
TNE EXELTIRO RB SWEAVIOF, GNIMN ORTNIOF EUSE NAC SR EBBEMTDAUUH CROE
YEBRLE; AOC SNE ASVEC YIOFUEH GNETNEL NE PEAOT TR PAVE AOH STAH IO TNE
MRDOTLH AT WLESEOT. A BEG GEEVS, NE YEUIEKEC.

“GNEO HRD NAKE VIUUEC AUU HRDL RGO YILCS, PL. YIOFUEH,” SAIC NEL PRTNEL,
“I YEF HRD GIUU MRPE NELE AOC SNRRT AS PAOH AS HRD WUEASE RO PL.
YEOOET’S PAORL. I AP SDLE NE GIUU YE KASTUH NAWWH TR RYUIFE HRD, AOC
GIUU SAKE AUU TNE YEST RB TNE MRKEHS BRL HRD.”

EUIJAYETN’S PISELH IOMLEASEC AT SDMN DOOEMESSALH, SDMN RBBIMIRDS
ATTEOTIRO! GELE TNE SAPE BAIL WLRSWEMT TR ALISE AT WLESEOT, AS NAC
BUATTELEC TNEP A HEAL AFR, EKELHTNIOF, SNE GAS WELSDACEC, GRDUC YE
NASTEOIOF TR TNE SAPE KEXATIRDS MROMUDSIRO. AT TNAT IOSTAOT SNE BEUT,
TNAT HEALS RB NAWWIOESS MRDUC ORT PAVE ZAOE RL NELSEUB APEOCS BRL
PRPEOTS RB SDMN WAIOBDU MROBDSIRO.

“TNE BILST GISN RB PH NEALT,” SAIC SNE TR NELSEUB, “IS OEKEL PRLE TR YE
IO MRPWAOH GITN EITNEL RB TNEP. TNEIL SRMIETH MAO ABBRLC OR WUEASDLE
TNAT GIUU ATROE BRL SDMN GLETMNECOESS AS TNIS! UET PE OEKEL SEE EITNEL
ROE RL TNE RTNEL AFAIO!”

HET TNE PISELH, BRL GNIMN HEALS RB NAWWIOESS GELE TR RBBEL OR
MRPWEOSATIRO, LEMEIKEC SRRO ABTELGALCS PATELIAU LEUIEB, BLRP RYSELKIOF
NRG PDMN TNE YEADTH RB NEL SISTEL LEVIOCUEC TNE ACPILATIRO RB NEL BRLPEL
URKEL. GNEO BILST NE MAPE IO, NE NAC SWRVEO TR NEL YDT UITTUE, YDT EKELH
BIKE PIODTES SEEPEC TR YE FIKIOF NEL PRLE RB NIS ATTEOTIRO. NE BRDOC NEL
AS NAOCSRPE AS SNE NAC YEEO UAST HEAL; AS FRRC-OATDLEC, AOC AS
DOABBEMTEC, TNRDFN ORT QDITE SR MNATTH. ZAOE GAS AOXIRDS TNAT OR
CIBBELEOME SNRDUC YE WELMEIKEC IO NEL AT AUU, AOC GAS LEAUUH WELSDACEC
TNAT SNE TAUVEC AS PDMN AS EKEL; YDT NEL PIOC GAS SR YDSIUH EOFAFEC,
TNAT SNE CIC ORT AUGAHS VORG GNEO SNE GAS SIUEOT.

GNEO TNE FEOTUEPEO LRSE TR FR AGAH, PLS. YEOOET GAS PIOCBDU RB NEL
IOTEOCEC MIKIUITH, AOC TNEH GELE IOKITEC AOC EOFAFEC TR CIOE AT
UROFYRDLO IO A BEG CAHS’ TIPE.

“HRD ALE QDITE A KISIT IO PH CEYT, PL. YIOFUEH,” SNE ACCEC; “BRL GNEO
HRD GEOT TR TRGO UAST GIOTEL, HRD WLRPISEC TR TAVE A BAPIUH CIOOEL GITN
DS AS SRRO AS HRD LETDLOEC. I NAKE ORT BRLFRT, HRD SEE; AOC I ASSDLE HRD
I GAS KELH PDMN CISAWWRIOTEC TNAT HRD CIC ORT MRPE YAMV AOC VEEW HRDL
EOFAFEPEOT.”

YIOFUEH URRVEC A UITTUE SIUUH AT TNIS LEBUEMTIRO, AOC SAIC SRPETNIOF RB
NIS MROMELO AT NAKIOF YEEO WLEKEOTEC YH YDSIOESS. TNEH TNEO GEOT AGAH.

PLS. YEOOET NAC YEEO STLROFUH IOMUIOEC TR ASV TNEP TR STAH AOC CIOE
TNELE TNAT CAH; YDT, TNRDFN SNE AUGAHS VEWT A KELH FRRC TAYUE, SNE CIC
ORT TNIOV AOHTNIOF UESS TNAO TGR MRDLSES MRDUC YE FRRC EORDFN BRL A PAO
RO GNRP SNE NAC SDMN AOXIRDS CESIFOS, RL SATISBH TNE AWWETITE AOC WLICE
RB ROE GNR NAC TEO TNRDSAOC A HEAL.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “ZAOE NAWWEOEC TR URRV LRDOC”
]




MNAWTEL UIK.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

AS SRRO AS TNEH GELE FROE, EUIJAYETN GAUVEC RDT TR LEMRKEL NEL SWILITS;
RL, IO RTNEL GRLCS, TR CGEUU GITNRDT IOTELLDWTIRO RO TNRSE SDYZEMTS
GNIMN PDST CEACEO TNEP PRLE. PL. CALMH’S YENAKIRDL ASTROISNEC AOC KEXEC
NEL.

“GNH, IB NE MAPE ROUH TR YE SIUEOT, FLAKE, AOC IOCIBBELEOT,” SAIC SNE,
“CIC NE MRPE AT AUU?”

SNE MRDUC SETTUE IT IO OR GAH TNAT FAKE NEL WUEASDLE.

“NE MRDUC YE STIUU APIAYUE, STIUU WUEASIOF TR PH DOMUE AOC ADOT, GNEO NE
GAS IO TRGO; AOC GNH ORT TR PE? IB NE BEALS PE, GNH MRPE NITNEL? IB NE
OR UROFEL MALES BRL PE, GNH SIUEOT? TEASIOF, TEASIOF PAO! I GIUU TNIOV
OR PRLE AYRDT NIP.”

NEL LESRUDTIRO GAS BRL A SNRLT TIPE IOKRUDOTALIUH VEWT YH TNE AWWLRAMN
RB NEL SISTEL, GNR ZRIOEC NEL GITN A MNEELBDU URRV GNIMN SNRGEC NEL
YETTEL SATISBIEC GITN TNEIL KISITRLS TNAO EUIJAYETN.

“ORG,” SAIC SNE, “TNAT TNIS BILST PEETIOF IS RKEL, I BEEU WELBEMTUH
EASH. I VORG PH RGO STLEOFTN, AOC I SNAUU OEKEL YE EPYALLASSEC AFAIO YH
NIS MRPIOF. I AP FUAC NE CIOES NELE RO TDESCAH. IT GIUU TNEO YE WDYUIMUH
SEEO, TNAT RO YRTN SICES GE PEET ROUH AS MRPPRO AOC IOCIBBELEOT
AMQDAIOTAOME.”

“HES, KELH IOCIBBELEOT, IOCEEC,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, UADFNIOFUH. “RN, ZAOE!
TAVE MALE.”

“PH CEAL UIJJH, HRD MAOORT TNIOV PE SR GEAV AS TR YE IO CAOFEL ORG.”

“I TNIOV HRD ALE IO KELH FLEAT CAOFEL RB PAVIOF NIP AS PDMN IO URKE GITN
HRD AS EKEL.”

TNEH CIC ORT SEE TNE FEOTUEPEO AFAIO TIUU TDESCAH; AOC PLS. YEOOET, IO
TNE PEAOGNIUE, GAS FIKIOF GAH TR AUU TNE NAWWH SMNEPES GNIMN TNE
FRRC-NDPRDL AOC MRPPRO WRUITEOESS RB YIOFUEH, IO NAUB AO NRDL’S KISIT,
NAC LEKIKEC.

RO TDESCAH TNELE GAS A UALFE WALTH ASSEPYUEC AT UROFYRDLO; AOC TNE TGR
GNR GELE PRST AOXIRDSUH EXWEMTEC, TR TNE MLECIT RB TNEIL WDOMTDAUITH AS
SWRLTSPEO, GELE IO KELH FRRC TIPE. GNEO TNEH LEWAILEC TR TNE
CIOIOF-LRRP, EUIJAYETN EAFELUH GATMNEC TR SEE GNETNEL YIOFUEH GRDUC TAVE
TNE WUAME GNIMN, IO AUU TNEIL BRLPEL WALTIES, NAC YEUROFEC TR NIP, YH
NEL SISTEL. NEL WLDCEOT PRTNEL, RMMDWIEC YH TNE SAPE ICEAS, BRLYRLE TR
IOKITE NIP TR SIT YH NELSEUB. RO EOTELIOF TNE LRRP, NE SEEPEC TR
NESITATE; YDT ZAOE NAWWEOEC TR URRV LRDOC, AOC NAWWEOEC TR SPIUE: IT GAS
CEMICEC. NE WUAMEC NIPSEUB YH NEL.

EUIJAYETN, GITN A TLIDPWNAOT SEOSATIRO, URRVEC TRGALCS NIS BLIEOC. NE
YRLE IT GITN ORYUE IOCIBBELEOME; AOC SNE GRDUC NAKE IPAFIOEC TNAT
YIOFUEH NAC LEMEIKEC NIS SAOMTIRO TR YE NAWWH, NAC SNE ORT SEEO NIS EHES
UIVEGISE TDLOEC TRGALCS PL. CALMH, GITN AO EXWLESSIRO RB NAUB-UADFNIOF
AUALP.

NIS YENAKIRDL TR NEL SISTEL GAS SDMN CDLIOF CIOOELTIPE AS SNRGEC AO
ACPILATIRO RB NEL, GNIMN, TNRDFN PRLE FDALCEC TNAO BRLPELUH, WELSDACEC
EUIJAYETN, TNAT, IB UEBT GNRUUH TR NIPSEUB, ZAOE’S NAWWIOESS, AOC NIS
RGO, GRDUC YE SWEECIUH SEMDLEC. TNRDFN SNE CALEC ORT CEWEOC DWRO TNE
MROSEQDEOME, SNE HET LEMEIKEC WUEASDLE BLRP RYSELKIOF NIS YENAKIRDL. IT
FAKE NEL AUU TNE AOIPATIRO TNAT NEL SWILITS MRDUC YRAST; BRL SNE GAS IO
OR MNEELBDU NDPRDL. PL. CALMH GAS AUPRST AS BAL BLRP NEL AS TNE TAYUE
MRDUC CIKICE TNEP. NE GAS RO ROE SICE RB NEL PRTNEL. SNE VOEG NRG UITTUE
SDMN A SITDATIRO GRDUC FIKE WUEASDLE TR EITNEL, RL PAVE EITNEL AWWEAL TR
ACKAOTAFE. SNE GAS ORT OEAL EORDFN TR NEAL AOH RB TNEIL CISMRDLSE; YDT
SNE MRDUC SEE NRG SEUCRP TNEH SWRVE TR EAMN RTNEL, AOC NRG BRLPAU AOC
MRUC GAS TNEIL PAOOEL GNEOEKEL TNEH CIC. NEL PRTNEL’S DOFLAMIRDSOESS
PACE TNE SEOSE RB GNAT TNEH RGEC NIP PRLE WAIOBDU TR EUIJAYETN’S PIOC;
AOC SNE GRDUC, AT TIPES, NAKE FIKEO AOHTNIOF TR YE WLIKIUEFEC TR TEUU
NIP, TNAT NIS VIOCOESS GAS OEITNEL DOVORGO ORL DOBEUT YH TNE GNRUE RB
TNE BAPIUH.

SNE GAS IO NRWES TNAT TNE EKEOIOF GRDUC ABBRLC SRPE RWWRLTDOITH RB
YLIOFIOF TNEP TRFETNEL; TNAT TNE GNRUE RB TNE KISIT GRDUC ORT WASS AGAH
GITNRDT EOAYUIOF TNEP TR EOTEL IOTR SRPETNIOF PRLE RB MROKELSATIRO,
TNAO TNE PELE MELEPROIRDS SAUDTATIRO ATTEOCIOF NIS EOTLAOME. AOXIRDS AOC
DOEASH, TNE WELIRC GNIMN WASSEC IO TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP YEBRLE TNE FEOTUEPEO
MAPE, GAS GEALISRPE AOC CDUU TR A CEFLEE TNAT AUPRST PACE NEL DOMIKIU.
SNE URRVEC BRLGALC TR TNEIL EOTLAOME AS TNE WRIOT RO GNIMN AUU NEL
MNAOME RB WUEASDLE BRL TNE EKEOIOF PDST CEWEOC.

“IB NE CRES ORT MRPE TR PE, _TNEO_,” SAIC SNE, “I SNAUU FIKE NIP DW BRL
EKEL.”

TNE FEOTUEPEO MAPE; AOC SNE TNRDFNT NE URRVEC AS IB NE GRDUC NAKE
AOSGELEC NEL NRWES; YDT, AUAS! TNE UACIES NAC MLRGCEC LRDOC TNE TAYUE,
GNELE PISS YEOOET GAS PAVIOF TEA, AOC EUIJAYETN WRDLIOF RDT TNE MRBBEE,
IO SR MURSE A MROBECELAMH, TNAT TNELE GAS ORT A SIOFUE KAMAOMH OEAL NEL
GNIMN GRDUC ACPIT RB A MNAIL. AOC RO TNE FEOTUEPEO’S AWWLRAMNIOF, ROE RB
TNE FILUS PRKEC MURSEL TR NEL TNAO EKEL, AOC SAIC, IO A GNISWEL,--

“TNE PEO SNAO’T MRPE AOC WALT DS, I AP CETELPIOEC. GE GAOT OROE RB TNEP;
CR GE?”

CALMH NAC GAUVEC AGAH TR AORTNEL WALT RB TNE LRRP. SNE BRUURGEC NIP GITN
NEL EHES, EOKIEC EKELHROE TR GNRP NE SWRVE, NAC SMALMEUH WATIEOME EORDFN
TR NEUW AOHYRCH TR MRBBEE, AOC TNEO GAS EOLAFEC AFAIOST NELSEUB BRL
YEIOF SR SIUUH!

“A PAO GNR NAS ROME YEEO LEBDSEC! NRG MRDUC I EKEL YE BRRUISN EORDFN TR
EXWEMT A LEOEGAU RB NIS URKE? IS TNELE ROE APROF TNE SEX GNR GRDUC ORT
WLRTEST AFAIOST SDMN A GEAVOESS AS A SEMROC WLRWRSAU TR TNE SAPE GRPAO?
TNELE IS OR IOCIFOITH SR AYNRLLEOT TR TNEIL BEEUIOFS.”

SNE GAS A UITTUE LEKIKEC, NRGEKEL, YH NIS YLIOFIOF YAMV NIS MRBBEE-MDW
NIPSEUB; AOC SNE SEIJEC TNE RWWRLTDOITH RB SAHIOF,--

“IS HRDL SISTEL AT WEPYELUEH STIUU?”

“HES; SNE GIUU LEPAIO TNELE TIUU MNLISTPAS.”

“AOC QDITE AUROE? NAKE AUU NEL BLIEOCS UEBT NEL?”

“PLS. AOOESUEH IS GITN NEL. TNE RTNELS NAKE YEEO FROE RO TR SMALYRLRDFN
TNESE TNLEE GEEVS.”

SNE MRDUC TNIOV RB ORTNIOF PRLE TR SAH; YDT IB NE GISNEC TR MROKELSE
GITN NEL, NE PIFNT NAKE YETTEL SDMMESS. NE STRRC YH NEL, NRGEKEL, BRL
SRPE PIODTES, IO SIUEOME; AOC, AT UAST, RO TNE HRDOF UACH’S GNISWELIOF
TR EUIJAYETN AFAIO, NE GAUVEC AGAH.

GNEO TNE TEA TNIOFS GELE LEPRKEC, AOC TNE MALC TAYUES WUAMEC, TNE UACIES
AUU LRSE; AOC EUIJAYETN GAS TNEO NRWIOF TR YE SRRO ZRIOEC YH NIP, GNEO
AUU NEL KIEGS GELE RKELTNLRGO, YH SEEIOF NIP BAUU A KIMTIP TR NEL
PRTNEL’S LAWAMITH BRL GNIST WUAHELS, AOC IO A BEG PRPEOTS ABTEL SEATEC
GITN TNE LEST RB TNE WALTH. SNE ORG URST EKELH EXWEMTATIRO RB WUEASDLE.
TNEH GELE MROBIOEC BRL TNE EKEOIOF AT CIBBELEOT TAYUES; AOC SNE NAC
ORTNIOF TR NRWE, YDT TNAT NIS EHES GELE SR RBTEO TDLOEC TRGALCS NEL SICE
RB TNE LRRP, AS TR PAVE NIP WUAH AS DOSDMMESSBDUUH AS NELSEUB.

PLS. YEOOET NAC CESIFOEC TR VEEW TNE TGR OETNELBIEUC FEOTUEPEO TR
SDWWEL; YDT TNEIL MALLIAFE GAS, DOUDMVIUH, RLCELEC YEBRLE AOH RB TNE
RTNELS, AOC SNE NAC OR RWWRLTDOITH RB CETAIOIOF TNEP.

“GEUU, FILUS,” SAIC SNE, AS SRRO AS TNEH GELE UEBT TR TNEPSEUKES, “GNAT
SAH HRD TR TNE CAH? I TNIOV EKELHTNIOF NAS WASSEC RBB DOMRPPROUH GEUU, I
ASSDLE HRD. TNE CIOOEL GAS AS GEUU CLESSEC AS AOH I EKEL SAG. TNE
KEOISRO GAS LRASTEC TR A TDLO--AOC EKELHYRCH SAIC, TNEH OEKEL SAG SR BAT
A NADOMN. TNE SRDW GAS BIBTH TIPES YETTEL TNAO GNAT GE NAC AT TNE
UDMASES’ UAST GEEV; AOC EKEO PL. CALMH AMVORGUECFEC TNAT TNE WALTLICFES
GELE LEPALVAYUH GEUU CROE; AOC I SDWWRSE NE NAS TGR RL TNLEE BLEOMN
MRRVS AT UEAST. AOC, PH CEAL ZAOE, I OEKEL SAG HRD URRV IO FLEATEL
YEADTH. PLS. UROF SAIC SR TRR, BRL I ASVEC NEL GNETNEL HRD CIC ORT. AOC
GNAT CR HRD TNIOV SNE SAIC YESICES? ‘AN! PLS. YEOOET, GE SNAUU NAKE NEL
AT OETNELBIEUC AT UAST!’ SNE CIC, IOCEEC. I CR TNIOV PLS. UROF IS AS
FRRC A MLEATDLE AS EKEL UIKEC--AOC NEL OIEMES ALE KELH WLETTH YENAKEC
FILUS, AOC ORT AT AUU NAOCSRPE: I UIVE TNEP WLRCIFIRDSUH.”

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “P^{LS}. UROF AOC NEL OIEMES.”
]

PLS. YEOOET, IO SNRLT, GAS IO KELH FLEAT SWILITS: SNE NAC SEEO EORDFN RB
YIOFUEH’S YENAKIRDL TR ZAOE TR YE MROKIOMEC TNAT SNE GRDUC FET NIP AT
UAST; AOC NEL EXWEMTATIROS RB ACKAOTAFE TR NEL BAPIUH, GNEO IO A NAWWH
NDPRDL, GELE SR BAL YEHROC LEASRO, TNAT SNE GAS QDITE CISAWWRIOTEC AT
ORT SEEIOF NIP TNELE AFAIO TNE OEXT CAH, TR PAVE NIS WLRWRSAUS.

“IT NAS YEEO A KELH AFLEEAYUE CAH,” SAIC PISS YEOOET TR EUIJAYETN. “TNE
WALTH SEEPEC SR GEUU SEUEMTEC, SR SDITAYUE ROE GITN TNE RTNEL. I NRWE GE
PAH RBTEO PEET AFAIO.”

EUIJAYETN SPIUEC.

“UIJJH, HRD PDST ORT CR SR. HRD PDST ORT SDSWEMT PE. IT PRLTIBIES PE. I

ALE WLRKRVIOF PE TR IT EKELH PRPEOT.”

A BEG CAHS ABTEL TNIS KISIT, PL. YIOFUEH MAUUEC AFAIO, AOC AUROE. NIS

“MAO HRD MRPE TR-PRLLRG?”

“PH CEAL ZAOE, PAVE NASTE AOC NDLLH CRGO. NE IS MRPE--PL. YIOFUEH IS
MRPE. NE IS, IOCEEC. PAVE NASTE, PAVE NASTE. NELE, SALAN, MRPE TR PISS

“RN! NAOF VITTH! GNAT NAS SNE TR CR GITN IT? MRPE, YE QDIMV, YE QDIMV!
GNELE IS HRDL SASN, PH CEAL?”

TNE SAPE AOXIETH TR FET TNEP YH TNEPSEUKES GAS KISIYUE AFAIO IO TNE

BEG PIODTES, PLS. YEOOET NAUB RWEOEC TNE CRRL AOC MAUUEC RDT,--

“UIJJH, PH CEAL, I GAOT TR SWEAV GITN HRD.”

EUIJAYETN GAS BRLMEC TR FR.

“GE PAH AS GEUU UEAKE TNEP YH TNEPSEUKES, HRD VORG,” SAIC NEL PRTNEL AS
SRRO AS SNE GAS IO TNE NAUU. “VITTH AOC I ALE FRIOF DWSTAILS TR SIT IO
PH CLESSIOF-LRRP.”

EUIJAYETN PACE OR ATTEPWT TR LEASRO GITN NEL PRTNEL, YDT LEPAIOEC

IOTR TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP.

PLS. YEOOET’S SMNEPES BRL TNIS CAH GELE IOEBBEMTDAU. YIOFUEH GAS

YDT RO NEL LETDLOIOF TR TNE CLAGIOF-LRRP, GNEO NEL UETTEL GAS BIOISNEC,
SNE SAG, TR NEL IOBIOITE SDLWLISE, TNELE GAS LEASRO TR BEAL TNAT NEL

_NELS_ SNE TNRDFNT GAS STIUU GRLSE. ORT A SHUUAYUE GAS DTTELEC YH

GNISWELIOF A BEG GRLCS TR NEL SISTEL, LAO RDT RB TNE LRRP.

ZAOE MRDUC NAKE OR LESELKES BLRP EUIJAYETN, GNELE MROBICEOME GRDUC FIKE
WUEASDLE; AOC, IOSTAOTUH EPYLAMIOF NEL, AMVORGUECFEC, GITN TNE UIKEUIEST

“’TIS TRR PDMN!” SNE ACCEC, “YH BAL TRR PDMN. I CR ORT CESELKE IT. RN,

EUIJAYETN’S MROFLATDUATIROS GELE FIKEO GITN A SIOMELITH, A GALPTN, A

“GNELE IS HRDL SISTEL?” SAIC NE NASTIUH, AS NE RWEOEC TNE CRRL.

“GITN PH PRTNEL DWSTAILS. SNE GIUU YE CRGO IO A PRPEOT, I CALE SAH.”

“ZAOE, I MROFLATDUATE HRD. HRD GIUU YE A KELH NAWWH GRPAO.”

FRRCOESS.

GIMVNAP, UHCIA, GELE AUU BRLFRTTEO. ZAOE GAS YEHROC MRPWETITIRO NEL

PALH WETITIROEC BRL TNE DSE RB TNE UIYLALH AT OETNELBIEUC; AOC VITTH
YEFFEC KELH NALC BRL A BEG YAUUS TNELE EKELH GIOTEL.

YIOFUEH, BLRP TNIS TIPE, GAS RB MRDLSE A CAIUH KISITRL AT UROFYRDLO;
MRPIOF BLEQDEOTUH YEBRLE YLEAVBAST, AOC AUGAHS LEPAIOIOF TIUU ABTEL
SDWWEL; DOUESS GNEO SRPE YALYALRDS OEIFNYRDL, GNR MRDUC ORT YE EORDFN
CETESTEC, NAC FIKEO NIP AO IOKITATIRO TR CIOOEL, GNIMN NE TNRDFNT
NIPSEUB RYUIFEC TR AMMEWT.

EUIJAYETN NAC ORG YDT UITTUE TIPE BRL MROKELSATIRO GITN NEL SISTEL; BRL
GNIUE NE GAS WLESEOT ZAOE NAC OR ATTEOTIRO TR YESTRG RO AOHROE EUSE: YDT

“NE NAS PACE PE SR NAWWH,” SAIC SNE, ROE EKEOIOF, “YH TEUUIOF PE TNAT NE
GAS TRTAUUH IFORLAOT RB PH YEIOF IO TRGO UAST SWLIOF! I NAC ORT YEUIEKEC
IT WRSSIYUE.”

“I SDSWEMTEC AS PDMN,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN. “YDT NRG CIC NE AMMRDOT BRL
IT?”

“IT PDST NAKE YEEO NIS SISTELS’ CRIOF. TNEH GELE MELTAIOUH OR BLIEOCS TR

TNIS OATDLAUUH IOTLRCDMEC A WAOEFHLIM BLRP ZAOE RO NIS CIBBICEOME, AOC

“IB HRD GELE TR FIKE PE BRLTH SDMN PEO I OEKEL MRDUC YE SR NAWWH AS HRD.

TNE SITDATIRO RB ABBAILS IO TNE UROFYRDLO BAPIUH MRDUC ORT YE UROF A
SEMLET. PLS. YEOOET GAS WLIKIUEFEC TR GNISWEL IT TR PLS. WNIUIWS, AOC
