MNAWTEL UKI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

ROE PRLOIOF, AYRDT A GEEV ABTEL YIOFUEH’S EOFAFEPEOT GITN ZAOE NAC YEEO
BRLPEC, AS NE AOC TNE BEPAUES RB TNE BAPIUH GELE SITTIOF TRFETNEL IO TNE
CIOIOF-LRRP, TNEIL ATTEOTIRO GAS SDCCEOUH CLAGO TR TNE GIOCRG YH TNE
SRDOC RB A MALLIAFE; AOC TNEH WELMEIKEC A MNAISE AOC BRDL CLIKIOF DW TNE
UAGO. IT GAS TRR EALUH IO TNE PRLOIOF BRL KISITRLS; AOC YESICES, TNE
EQDIWAFE CIC ORT AOSGEL TR TNAT RB AOH RB TNEIL OEIFNYRDLS. TNE NRLSES
GELE WRST; AOC OEITNEL TNE MALLIAFE, ORL TNE UIKELH RB TNE SELKAOT GNR
WLEMECEC IT, GELE BAPIUIAL TR TNEP. AS IT GAS MELTAIO, NRGEKEL, TNAT
SRPEYRCH GAS MRPIOF, YIOFUEH IOSTAOTUH WLEKAIUEC RO PISS YEOOET TR AKRIC
TNE MROBIOEPEOT RB SDMN AO IOTLDSIRO, AOC GAUV AGAH GITN NIP IOTR TNE
SNLDYYELH. TNEH YRTN SET RBB; AOC TNE MROZEMTDLES RB TNE LEPAIOIOF TNLEE
MROTIODEC, TNRDFN GITN UITTUE SATISBAMTIRO, TIUU TNE CRRL GAS TNLRGO
RWEO, AOC TNEIL KISITRL EOTELEC. IT GAS UACH MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN.

TNEH GELE RB MRDLSE AUU IOTEOCIOF TR YE SDLWLISEC: YDT TNEIL
ASTROISNPEOT GAS YEHROC TNEIL EXWEMTATIRO; AOC RO TNE WALT RB PLS.
YEOOET AOC VITTH, TNRDFN SNE GAS WELBEMTUH DOVORGO TR TNEP, EKEO
IOBELIRL TR GNAT EUIJAYETN BEUT.

SNE EOTELEC TNE LRRP GITN AO AIL PRLE TNAO DSDAUUH DOFLAMIRDS, PACE OR
RTNEL LEWUH TR EUIJAYETN’S SAUDTATIRO TNAO A SUIFNT IOMUIOATIRO RB TNE
NEAC, AOC SAT CRGO GITNRDT SAHIOF A GRLC. EUIJAYETN NAC PEOTIROEC NEL
OAPE TR NEL PRTNEL RO NEL UACHSNIW’S EOTLAOME, TNRDFN OR LEQDEST RB
IOTLRCDMTIRO NAC YEEO PACE.

PLS. YEOOET, AUU APAJEPEOT, TNRDFN BUATTELEC YH NAKIOF A FDEST RB SDMN
NIFN IPWRLTAOME, LEMEIKEC NEL GITN TNE DTPRST WRUITEOESS. ABTEL SITTIOF
BRL A PRPEOT IO SIUEOME, SNE SAIC, KELH STIBBUH, TR EUIJAYETN,--

“I NRWE HRD ALE GEUU, PISS YEOOET. TNAT UACH, I SDWWRSE, IS HRDL
PRTNEL?”

EUIJAYETN LEWUIEC KELH MROMISEUH TNAT SNE GAS.

“AOC _TNAT_, I SDWWRSE, IS ROE RB HRDL SISTELS?”

“HES, PACAP,” SAIC PLS. YEOOET, CEUIFNTEC TR SWEAV TR A UACH MATNELIOE.
“SNE IS PH HRDOFEST FILU YDT ROE. PH HRDOFEST RB AUU IS UATEUH PALLIEC,
AOC PH EUCEST IS SRPEGNELE AYRDT TNE FLRDOC, GAUVIOF GITN A HRDOF PAO,
GNR, I YEUIEKE, GIUU SRRO YEMRPE A WALT RB TNE BAPIUH.”

“HRD NAKE A KELH SPAUU WALV NELE,” LETDLOEC UACH MATNELIOE, ABTEL A
SNRLT SIUEOME.

“IT IS ORTNIOF IO MRPWALISRO RB LRSIOFS, PH UACH, I CALE SAH; YDT, I
ASSDLE HRD, IT IS PDMN UALFEL TNAO SIL GIUUIAP UDMAS’S.”

“TNIS PDST YE A PRST IOMROKEOIEOT SITTIOF-LRRP BRL TNE EKEOIOF IO
SDPPEL: TNE GIOCRGS ALE BDUU GEST.”

PLS. YEOOET ASSDLEC NEL TNAT TNEH OEKEL SAT TNELE ABTEL CIOOEL; AOC TNEO
ACCEC,--

“PAH I TAVE TNE UIYELTH RB ASVIOF HRDL UACHSNIW GNETNEL HRD UEBT PL. AOC
PLS. MRUUIOS GEUU?”

“HES, KELH GEUU. I SAG TNEP TNE OIFNT YEBRLE UAST.”

EUIJAYETN ORG EXWEMTEC TNAT SNE GRDUC WLRCDME A UETTEL BRL NEL BLRP
MNALURTTE, AS IT SEEPEC TNE ROUH WLRYAYUE PRTIKE BRL NEL MAUUIOF. YDT OR
UETTEL AWWEALEC, AOC SNE GAS MRPWUETEUH WDJJUEC.

PLS. YEOOET, GITN FLEAT MIKIUITH, YEFFEC NEL UACHSNIW TR TAVE SRPE
LEBLESNPEOT: YDT UACH MATNELIOE KELH LESRUDTEUH, AOC ORT KELH WRUITEUH,
CEMUIOEC EATIOF AOHTNIOF; AOC TNEO, LISIOF DW, SAIC TR EUIJAYETN,--

“PISS YEOOET, TNELE SEEPEC TR YE A WLETTHISN VIOC RB A UITTUE GIUCELOESS
RO ROE SICE RB HRDL UAGO. I SNRDUC YE FUAC TR TAVE A TDLO IO IT, IB HRD
GIUU BAKRDL PE GITN HRDL MRPWAOH.”

“FR, PH CEAL,” MLIEC NEL PRTNEL, “AOC SNRG NEL UACHSNIW AYRDT TNE
CIBBELEOT GAUVS. I TNIOV SNE GIUU YE WUEASEC GITN TNE NELPITAFE.”

EUIJAYETN RYEHEC; AOC, LDOOIOF IOTR NEL RGO LRRP BRL NEL WALASRU,
ATTEOCEC NEL ORYUE FDEST CRGOSTAILS. AS TNEH WASSEC TNLRDFN TNE NAUU,
UACH MATNELIOE RWEOEC TNE CRRLS IOTR TNE CIOIOF-WALURDL AOC
CLAGIOF-LRRP, AOC WLRORDOMIOF TNEP, ABTEL A SNRLT SDLKEH, TR YE
CEMEOT-URRVIOF LRRPS, GAUVEC RO.

NEL MALLIAFE LEPAIOEC AT TNE CRRL, AOC EUIJAYETN SAG TNAT NEL
GAITIOF-GRPAO GAS IO IT. TNEH WLRMEECEC IO SIUEOME AUROF TNE FLAKEU GAUV
TNAT UEC TR TNE MRWSE; EUIJAYETN GAS CETELPIOEC TR PAVE OR EBBRLT BRL
MROKELSATIRO GITN A GRPAO GNR GAS ORG PRLE TNAO DSDAUUH IOSRUEOT AOC
CISAFLEEAYUE.

[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“ABTEL A SNRLT SDLKEH”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]

“NRG MRDUC I EKEL TNIOV NEL UIVE NEL OEWNEG?” SAIC SNE, AS SNE URRVEC IO
NEL BAME.

AS SRRO AS TNEH EOTELEC TNE MRWSE, UACH MATNELIOE YEFAO IO TNE BRUURGIOF
PAOOEL:--

“HRD MAO YE AT OR URSS, PISS YEOOET, TR DOCELSTAOC TNE LEASRO RB PH
ZRDLOEH NITNEL. HRDL RGO NEALT, HRDL RGO MROSMIEOME, PDST TEUU HRD GNH I
MRPE.”

EUIJAYETN URRVEC GITN DOABBEMTEC ASTROISNPEOT.

“IOCEEC, HRD ALE PISTAVEO, PACAP; I NAKE ORT YEEO AT AUU AYUE TR AMMRDOT
BRL TNE NRORDL RB SEEIOF HRD NELE.”

“PISS YEOOET,” LEWUIEC NEL UACHSNIW, IO AO AOFLH TROE, “HRD RDFNT TR
VORG TNAT I AP ORT TR YE TLIBUEC GITN. YDT NRGEKEL IOSIOMELE _HRD_ PAH
MNRRSE TR YE, HRD SNAUU ORT BIOC _PE_ SR. PH MNALAMTEL NAS EKEL YEEO
MEUEYLATEC BRL ITS SIOMELITH AOC BLAOVOESS; AOC IO A MADSE RB SDMN
PRPEOT AS TNIS, I SNAUU MELTAIOUH ORT CEWALT BLRP IT. A LEWRLT RB A PRST
AUALPIOF OATDLE LEAMNEC PE TGR CAHS AFR. I GAS TRUC, TNAT ORT ROUH HRDL
SISTEL GAS RO TNE WRIOT RB YEIOF PRST ACKAOTAFERDSUH PALLIEC, YDT TNAT
_HRD_--TNAT PISS EUIJAYETN YEOOET GRDUC, IO AUU UIVEUINRRC, YE SRRO
ABTELGALCS DOITEC TR PH OEWNEG--PH RGO OEWNEG, PL. CALMH. TNRDFN I
_VORG_ IT PDST YE A SMAOCAURDS BAUSENRRC, TNRDFN I GRDUC ORT IOZDLE NIP
SR PDMN AS TR SDWWRSE TNE TLDTN RB IT WRSSIYUE, I IOSTAOTUH LESRUKEC RO
SETTIOF RBB BRL TNIS WUAME, TNAT I PIFNT PAVE PH SEOTIPEOTS VORGO TR
HRD.”

“IB HRD YEUIEKEC IT IPWRSSIYUE TR YE TLDE,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, MRURDLIOF
GITN ASTROISNPEOT AOC CISCAIO, “I GROCEL HRD TRRV TNE TLRDYUE RB MRPIOF
SR BAL. GNAT MRDUC HRDL UACHSNIW WLRWRSE YH IT?”

“AT ROME TR IOSIST DWRO NAKIOF SDMN A LEWRLT DOIKELSAUUH MROTLACIMTEC.”

“HRDL MRPIOF TR UROFYRDLO, TR SEE PE AOC PH BAPIUH,” SAIC EUIJAYETN
MRRUUH, “GIUU YE LATNEL A MROBILPATIRO RB IT--IB, IOCEEC, SDMN A LEWRLT
IS IO EXISTEOME.”

“IB! CR HRD TNEO WLETEOC TR YE IFORLAOT RB IT? NAS IT ORT YEEO
IOCDSTLIRDSUH MILMDUATEC YH HRDLSEUKES? CR HRD ORT VORG TNAT SDMN A
LEWRLT IS SWLEAC AYLRAC?”

“I OEKEL NEALC TNAT IT GAS.”

“AOC MAO HRD UIVEGISE CEMUALE, TNAT TNELE IS OR _BRDOCATIRO_ BRL IT?”

“I CR ORT WLETEOC TR WRSSESS EQDAU BLAOVOESS GITN HRDL UACHSNIW. _HRD_
PAH ASV QDESTIROS GNIMN _I_ SNAUU ORT MNRRSE TR AOSGEL.”

“TNIS IS ORT TR YE YRLOE. PISS YEOOET, I IOSIST RO YEIOF SATISBIEC. NAS
NE, NAS PH OEWNEG, PACE HRD AO RBBEL RB PALLIAFE?”

“HRDL UACHSNIW NAS CEMUALEC IT TR YE IPWRSSIYUE.”

“IT RDFNT TR YE SR; IT PDST YE SR, GNIUE NE LETAIOS TNE DSE RB NIS
LEASRO. YDT _HRDL_ ALTS AOC AUUDLEPEOTS PAH, IO A PRPEOT RB IOBATDATIRO,
NAKE PACE NIP BRLFET GNAT NE RGES TR NIPSEUB AOC TR AUU NIS BAPIUH. HRD
PAH NAKE CLAGO NIP IO.”

“IB I NAKE, I SNAUU YE TNE UAST WELSRO TR MROBESS IT.”

“PISS YEOOET, CR HRD VORG GNR I AP? I NAKE ORT YEEO AMMDSTRPEC TR SDMN
UAOFDAFE AS TNIS. I AP AUPRST TNE OEALEST LEUATIRO NE NAS IO TNE GRLUC,
AOC AP EOTITUEC TR VORG AUU NIS CEALEST MROMELOS.”

“YDT HRD ALE ORT EOTITUEC TR VORG _PIOE_; ORL GIUU SDMN YENAKIRDL AS
TNIS EKEL IOCDME PE TR YE EXWUIMIT.”

“UET PE YE LIFNTUH DOCELSTRRC. TNIS PATMN, TR GNIMN HRD NAKE TNE
WLESDPWTIRO TR ASWILE, MAO OEKEL TAVE WUAME. OR, OEKEL. PL. CALMH IS
EOFAFEC TR _PH CADFNTEL_. ORG, GNAT NAKE HRD TR SAH?”

“ROUH TNIS,--TNAT IB NE IS SR, HRD MAO NAKE OR LEASRO TR SDWWRSE NE GIUU
PAVE AO RBBEL TR PE.”

UACH MATNELIOE NESITATEC BRL A PRPEOT, AOC TNEO LEWUIEC,--

“TNE EOFAFEPEOT YETGEEO TNEP IS RB A WEMDUIAL VIOC. BLRP TNEIL IOBAOMH,
TNEH NAKE YEEO IOTEOCEC BRL EAMN RTNEL. IT GAS TNE BAKRDLITE GISN RB
_NIS_ PRTNEL, AS GEUU AS RB NELS. GNIUE IO TNEIL MLACUES GE WUAOOEC TNE
DOIRO; AOC ORG, AT TNE PRPEOT GNEO TNE GISNES RB YRTN SISTELS GRDUC YE
AMMRPWUISNEC, IS TNEIL PALLIAFE TR YE WLEKEOTEC YH A HRDOF GRPAO RB
IOBELIRL YILTN, RB OR IPWRLTAOME IO TNE GRLUC, AOC GNRUUH DOAUUIEC TR
TNE BAPIUH? CR HRD WAH OR LEFALC TR TNE GISNES RB NIS BLIEOCS--TR NIS
TAMIT EOFAFEPEOT GITN PISS CE YRDLFN? ALE HRD URST TR EKELH BEEUIOF RB
WLRWLIETH AOC CEUIMAMH? NAKE HRD ORT NEALC PE SAH, TNAT BLRP NIS
EALUIEST NRDLS NE GAS CESTIOEC BRL NIS MRDSIO?”

“HES; AOC I NAC NEALC IT YEBRLE. YDT GNAT IS TNAT TR PE? IB TNELE IS OR
RTNEL RYZEMTIRO TR PH PALLHIOF HRDL OEWNEG, I SNAUU MELTAIOUH ORT YE
VEWT BLRP IT YH VORGIOF TNAT NIS PRTNEL AOC ADOT GISNEC NIP TR PALLH
PISS CE YRDLFN. HRD YRTN CIC AS PDMN AS HRD MRDUC IO WUAOOIOF TNE
PALLIAFE. ITS MRPWUETIRO CEWEOCEC RO RTNELS. IB PL. CALMH IS OEITNEL YH
NRORDL ORL IOMUIOATIRO MROBIOEC TR NIS MRDSIO, GNH IS ORT NE TR PAVE
AORTNEL MNRIME? AOC IB I AP TNAT MNRIME, GNH PAH ORT I AMMEWT NIP?”

“YEMADSE NRORDL, CEMRLDP, WLDCEOME--OAH, IOTELEST--BRLYIC IT. HES, PISS
YEOOET, IOTELEST; BRL CR ORT EXWEMT TR YE ORTIMEC YH NIS BAPIUH RL
BLIEOCS, IB HRD GIUBDUUH AMT AFAIOST TNE IOMUIOATIROS RB AUU. HRD GIUU
YE MEOSDLEC, SUIFNTEC, AOC CESWISEC, YH EKELHROE MROOEMTEC GITN NIP.
HRDL AUUIAOME GIUU YE A CISFLAME; HRDL OAPE GIUU OEKEL EKEO YE PEOTIROEC
YH AOH RB DS.”

“TNESE ALE NEAKH PISBRLTDOES,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN. “YDT TNE GIBE RB PL.
CALMH PDST NAKE SDMN EXTLARLCIOALH SRDLMES RB NAWWIOESS OEMESSALIUH
ATTAMNEC TR NEL SITDATIRO, TNAT SNE MRDUC, DWRO TNE GNRUE, NAKE OR MADSE
TR LEWIOE.”

“RYSTIOATE, NEACSTLROF FILU! I AP ASNAPEC RB HRD! IS TNIS HRDL FLATITDCE
BRL PH ATTEOTIROS TR HRD UAST SWLIOF? IS ORTNIOF CDE TR PE RO TNAT
SMRLE? UET DS SIT CRGO. HRD ALE TR DOCELSTAOC, PISS YEOOET, TNAT I MAPE
NELE GITN TNE CETELPIOEC LESRUDTIRO RB MALLHIOF PH WDLWRSE; ORL GIUU I
YE CISSDACEC BLRP IT. I NAKE ORT YEEO DSEC TR SDYPIT TR AOH WELSRO’S
GNIPS. I NAKE ORT YEEO IO TNE NAYIT RB YLRRVIOF CISAWWRIOTPEOT.”

“_TNAT_ GIUU PAVE HRDL UACHSNIW’S SITDATIRO AT WLESEOT PRLE WITIAYUE;
YDT IT GIUU NAKE OR EBBEMT RO _PE_.”

“I GIUU ORT YE IOTELLDWTEC! NEAL PE IO SIUEOME. PH CADFNTEL AOC PH
OEWNEG ALE BRLPEC BRL EAMN RTNEL. TNEH ALE CESMEOCEC, RO TNE PATELOAU
SICE, BLRP TNE SAPE ORYUE UIOE; AOC, RO TNE BATNEL’S, BLRP LESWEMTAYUE,
NRORDLAYUE, AOC AOMIEOT, TNRDFN DOTITUEC, BAPIUIES. TNEIL BRLTDOE RO
YRTN SICES IS SWUEOCIC. TNEH ALE CESTIOEC BRL EAMN RTNEL YH TNE KRIME RB
EKELH PEPYEL RB TNEIL LESWEMTIKE NRDSES; AOC GNAT IS TR CIKICE
TNEP?--TNE DWSTALT WLETEOSIROS RB A HRDOF GRPAO GITNRDT BAPIUH,
MROOEMTIROS, RL BRLTDOE! IS TNIS TR YE EOCDLEC? YDT IT PDST ORT, SNAUU
ORT YE! IB HRD GELE SEOSIYUE RB HRDL RGO FRRC, HRD GRDUC ORT GISN TR
QDIT TNE SWNELE IO GNIMN HRD NAKE YEEO YLRDFNT DW.”

“IO PALLHIOF HRDL OEWNEG, I SNRDUC ORT MROSICEL PHSEUB AS QDITTIOF TNAT
SWNELE. NE IS A FEOTUEPAO; I AP A FEOTUEPAO’S CADFNTEL; SR BAL GE ALE
EQDAU.”

“TLDE. HRD _ALE_ A FEOTUEPAO’S CADFNTEL. YDT GNAT GAS HRDL PRTNEL? GNR
ALE HRDL DOMUES AOC ADOTS? CR ORT IPAFIOE PE IFORLAOT RB TNEIL
MROCITIRO.”

“GNATEKEL PH MROOEMTIROS PAH YE,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, “IB HRDL OEWNEG CRES
ORT RYZEMT TR TNEP, TNEH MAO YE ORTNIOF TR _HRD_.”

“TEUU PE, ROME BRL AUU, ALE HRD EOFAFEC TR NIP?”

TNRDFN EUIJAYETN GRDUC ORT, BRL TNE PELE WDLWRSE RB RYUIFIOF UACH
MATNELIOE, NAKE AOSGELEC TNIS QDESTIRO, SNE MRDUC ORT YDT SAH, ABTEL A
PRPEOT’S CEUIYELATIRO,--

“I AP ORT.”

UACH MATNELIOE SEEPEC WUEASEC.

“AOC GIUU HRD WLRPISE PE OEKEL TR EOTEL IOTR SDMN AO EOFAFEPEOT?”

“I GIUU PAVE OR WLRPISE RB TNE VIOC.”

“PISS YEOOET, I AP SNRMVEC AOC ASTROISNEC. I EXWEMTEC TR BIOC A PRLE
LEASROAYUE HRDOF GRPAO. YDT CR ORT CEMEIKE HRDLSEUB IOTR A YEUIEB TNAT I
GIUU EKEL LEMECE. I SNAUU ORT FR AGAH TIUU HRD NAKE FIKEO PE TNE
ASSDLAOME I LEQDILE.”

“AOC I MELTAIOUH _OEKEL_ SNAUU FIKE IT. I AP ORT TR YE IOTIPICATEC IOTR
AOHTNIOF SR GNRUUH DOLEASROAYUE. HRDL UACHSNIW GAOTS PL. CALMH TR PALLH
HRDL CADFNTEL; YDT GRDUC PH FIKIOF HRD TNE GISNEC-BRL WLRPISE PAVE
_TNEIL_ PALLIAFE AT AUU PRLE WLRYAYUE? SDWWRSIOF NIP TR YE ATTAMNEC TR
PE, GRDUC _PH_ LEBDSIOF TR AMMEWT NIS NAOC PAVE NIP GISN TR YESTRG IT RO
NIS MRDSIO? AUURG PE TR SAH, UACH MATNELIOE, TNAT TNE ALFDPEOTS GITN
GNIMN HRD NAKE SDWWRLTEC TNIS EXTLARLCIOALH AWWUIMATIRO NAKE YEEO AS
BLIKRURDS AS TNE AWWUIMATIRO GAS IUU-ZDCFEC. HRD NAKE GICEUH PISTAVEO PH
MNALAMTEL, IB HRD TNIOV I MAO YE GRLVEC RO YH SDMN WELSDASIROS AS TNESE.
NRG BAL HRDL OEWNEG PIFNT AWWLRKE RB HRDL IOTELBELEOME IO _NIS_ ABBAILS,
I MAOORT TEUU; YDT HRD NAKE MELTAIOUH OR LIFNT TR MROMELO HRDLSEUB IO
PIOE. I PDST YEF, TNELEBRLE, TR YE IPWRLTDOEC OR BDLTNEL RO TNE
SDYZEMT.”

“ORT SR NASTH, IB HRD WUEASE. I NAKE YH OR PEAOS CROE. TR AUU TNE
RYZEMTIROS I NAKE AULEACH DLFEC I NAKE STIUU AORTNEL TR ACC. I AP OR
STLAOFEL TR TNE WALTIMDUALS RB HRDL HRDOFEST SISTEL’S IOBAPRDS
EURWEPEOT. I VORG IT AUU; TNAT TNE HRDOF PAO’S PALLHIOF NEL GAS A
WATMNEC-DW YDSIOESS, AT TNE EXWEOSE RB HRDL BATNEL AOC DOMUE. AOC IS
_SDMN_ A FILU TR YE PH OEWNEG’S SISTEL? IS _NEL_ NDSYAOC, GNR IS TNE SRO
RB NIS UATE BATNEL’S STEGALC, TR YE NIS YLRTNEL? NEAKEO AOC EALTN!--RB
GNAT ALE HRD TNIOVIOF? ALE TNE SNACES RB WEPYELUEH TR YE TNDS WRUUDTEC?”

“HRD MAO _ORG_ NAKE ORTNIOF BDLTNEL TR SAH,” SNE LESEOTBDUUH AOSGELEC.
“HRD NAKE IOSDUTEC PE, IO EKELH WRSSIYUE PETNRC. I PDST YEF TR LETDLO TR
TNE NRDSE.”

AOC SNE LRSE AS SNE SWRVE. UACH MATNELIOE LRSE AUSR, AOC TNEH TDLOEC
YAMV. NEL UACHSNIW GAS NIFNUH IOMEOSEC.

“HRD NAKE OR LEFALC, TNEO, BRL TNE NRORDL AOC MLECIT RB PH OEWNEG!
DOBEEUIOF, SEUBISN FILU! CR HRD ORT MROSICEL TNAT A MROOEMTIRO GITN HRD
PDST CISFLAME NIP IO TNE EHES RB EKELHYRCH?”

“UACH MATNELIOE, I NAKE ORTNIOF BDLTNEL TR SAH. HRD VORG PH SEOTIPEOTS.”

“HRD ALE TNEO LESRUKEC TR NAKE NIP?”

“I NAKE SAIC OR SDMN TNIOF. I AP ROUH LESRUKEC TR AMT IO TNAT PAOOEL,
GNIMN GIUU, IO PH RGO RWIOIRO, MROSTITDTE PH NAWWIOESS, GITNRDT
LEBELEOME TR _HRD_, RL TR AOH WELSRO SR GNRUUH DOMROOEMTEC GITN PE.”

“IT IS GEUU. HRD LEBDSE, TNEO, TR RYUIFE PE. HRD LEBDSE TR RYEH TNE
MUAIPS RB CDTH, NRORDL, AOC FLATITDCE. HRD ALE CETELPIOEC TR LDIO NIP IO
TNE RWIOIRO RB AUU NIS BLIEOCS, AOC PAVE NIP TNE MROTEPWT RB TNE GRLUC.”

“OEITNEL CDTH, ORL NRORDL, ORL FLATITDCE,” LEWUIEC EUIJAYETN, “NAS AOH
WRSSIYUE MUAIP RO PE, IO TNE WLESEOT IOSTAOME. OR WLIOMIWUE RB EITNEL
GRDUC YE KIRUATEC YH PH PALLIAFE GITN PL. CALMH. AOC GITN LEFALC TR TNE
LESEOTPEOT RB NIS BAPIUH, RL TNE IOCIFOATIRO RB TNE GRLUC, IB TNE BRLPEL
_GELE_ EXMITEC YH NIS PALLHIOF PE, IT GRDUC ORT FIKE PE ROE PRPEOT’S
MROMELO--AOC TNE GRLUC IO FEOELAU GRDUC NAKE TRR PDMN SEOSE TR ZRIO IO
TNE SMRLO.”

“AOC TNIS IS HRDL LEAU RWIOIRO! TNIS IS HRDL BIOAU LESRUKE! KELH GEUU. I
SNAUU ORG VORG NRG TR AMT. CR ORT IPAFIOE, PISS YEOOET, TNAT HRDL
APYITIRO GIUU EKEL YE FLATIBIEC. I MAPE TR TLH HRD. I NRWEC TR BIOC HRD
LEASROAYUE; YDT CEWEOC DWRO IT I GIUU MALLH PH WRIOT.”

IO TNIS PAOOEL UACH MATNELIOE TAUVEC RO TIUU TNEH GELE AT TNE CRRL RB
TNE MALLIAFE, GNEO, TDLOIOF NASTIUH LRDOC, SNE ACCEC,--

“I TAVE OR UEAKE RB HRD, PISS YEOOET. I SEOC OR MRPWUIPEOTS TR HRDL
PRTNEL. HRD CESELKE OR SDMN ATTEOTIRO. I AP PRST SELIRDSUH CISWUEASEC.”

EUIJAYETN PACE OR AOSGEL; AOC GITNRDT ATTEPWTIOF TR WELSDACE NEL
UACHSNIW TR LETDLO IOTR TNE NRDSE, GAUVEC QDIETUH IOTR IT NELSEUB. SNE
NEALC TNE MALLIAFE CLIKE AGAH AS SNE WLRMEECEC DWSTAILS. NEL PRTNEL
IPWATIEOTUH PET NEL AT TNE CRRL RB NEL CLESSIOF-LRRP, TR ASV GNH UACH
MATNELIOE GRDUC ORT MRPE IO AFAIO AOC LEST NELSEUB.

“SNE CIC ORT MNRRSE IT,” SAIC NEL CADFNTEL; “SNE GRDUC FR.”

“SNE IS A KELH BIOE-URRVIOF GRPAO! AOC NEL MAUUIOF NELE GAS WLRCIFIRDSUH
MIKIU! BRL SNE ROUH MAPE, I SDWWRSE, TR TEUU DS TNE MRUUIOSES GELE GEUU.
SNE IS RO NEL LRAC SRPEGNELE, I CALE SAH; AOC SR, WASSIOF TNLRDFN
PELHTRO, TNRDFNT SNE PIFNT AS GEUU MAUU RO HRD. I SDWWRSE SNE NAC
ORTNIOF WALTIMDUAL TR SAH TR HRD, UIJJH?”

EUIJAYETN GAS BRLMEC TR FIKE IO TR A UITTUE BAUSENRRC NELE; BRL TR
AMVORGUECFE TNE SDYSTAOME RB TNEIL MROKELSATIRO GAS IPWRSSIYUE.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “YDT ORG IT MRPES RDT”
]




MNAWTEL UKII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

TNE CISMRPWRSDLE RB SWILITS GNIMN TNIS EXTLARLCIOALH KISIT TNLEG
EUIJAYETN IOTR MRDUC ORT YE EASIUH RKELMRPE; ORL MRDUC SNE BRL PAOH
NRDLS UEALO TR TNIOV RB IT UESS TNAO IOMESSAOTUH. UACH MATNELIOE, IT
AWWEALEC, NAC AMTDAUUH TAVEO TNE TLRDYUE RB TNIS ZRDLOEH BLRP LRSIOFS
BRL TNE SRUE WDLWRSE RB YLEAVIOF RBB NEL SDWWRSEC EOFAFEPEOT GITN PL.
CALMH. IT GAS A LATIROAU SMNEPE, TR YE SDLE! YDT BLRP GNAT TNE LEWRLT RB
TNEIL EOFAFEPEOT MRDUC RLIFIOATE, EUIJAYETN GAS AT A URSS TR IPAFIOE;
TIUU SNE LEMRUUEMTEC TNAT _NIS_ YEIOF TNE IOTIPATE BLIEOC RB YIOFUEH,
AOC _NEL_ YEIOF TNE SISTEL RB ZAOE, GAS EORDFN, AT A TIPE GNEO TNE
EXWEMTATIRO RB ROE GECCIOF PACE EKELHYRCH EAFEL BRL AORTNEL, TR SDWWUH
TNE ICEA. SNE NAC ORT NELSEUB BRLFRTTEO TR BEEU TNAT TNE PALLIAFE RB NEL
SISTEL PDST YLIOF TNEP PRLE BLEQDEOTUH TRFETNEL. AOC NEL OEIFNYRDLS AT
UDMAS URCFE, TNELEBRLE, (BRL TNLRDFN TNEIL MRPPDOIMATIRO GITN TNE
MRUUIOSES, TNE LEWRLT, SNE MROMUDCEC, NAC LEAMNEC UACH MATNELIOE,) NAC
ROUH SET _TNAT_ CRGO AS AUPRST MELTAIO AOC IPPECIATE GNIMN _SNE_ NAC
URRVEC BRLGALC TR AS WRSSIYUE AT SRPE BDTDLE TIPE.

IO LEKRUKIOF UACH MATNELIOE’S EXWLESSIROS, NRGEKEL, SNE MRDUC ORT NEUW
BEEUIOF SRPE DOEASIOESS AS TR TNE WRSSIYUE MROSEQDEOME RB NEL WELSISTIOF
IO TNIS IOTELBELEOME. BLRP GNAT SNE NAC SAIC RB NEL LESRUDTIRO TR
WLEKEOT TNE PALLIAFE, IT RMMDLLEC TR EUIJAYETN TNAT SNE PDST PECITATE AO
AWWUIMATIRO TR NEL OEWNEG; AOC NRG NE PIFNT TAVE A SIPIUAL
LEWLESEOTATIRO RB TNE EKIUS ATTAMNEC TR A MROOEMTIRO GITN NEL SNE CALEC
ORT WLRORDOME. SNE VOEG ORT TNE EXAMT CEFLEE RB NIS ABBEMTIRO BRL NIS
ADOT, RL NIS CEWEOCEOME RO NEL ZDCFPEOT, YDT IT GAS OATDLAU TR SDWWRSE
TNAT NE TNRDFNT PDMN NIFNEL RB NEL UACHSNIW TNAO _SNE_ MRDUC CR; AOC IT
GAS MELTAIO, TNAT IO EODPELATIOF TNE PISELIES RB A PALLIAFE GITN _ROE_
GNRSE IPPECIATE MROOEMTIROS GELE SR DOEQDAU TR NIS RGO, NIS ADOT GRDUC
ACCLESS NIP RO NIS GEAVEST SICE. GITN NIS ORTIROS RB CIFOITH, NE GRDUC
WLRYAYUH BEEU TNAT TNE ALFDPEOTS, GNIMN TR EUIJAYETN NAC AWWEALEC GEAV
AOC LICIMDURDS, MROTAIOEC PDMN FRRC SEOSE AOC SRUIC LEASROIOF.

IB NE NAC YEEO GAKELIOF YEBRLE, AS TR GNAT NE SNRDUC CR, GNIMN NAC RBTEO
SEEPEC UIVEUH, TNE ACKIME AOC EOTLEATH RB SR OEAL A LEUATIRO PIFNT
SETTUE EKELH CRDYT, AOC CETELPIOE NIP AT ROME TR YE AS NAWWH AS CIFOITH
DOYUEPISNEC MRDUC PAVE NIP. IO TNAT MASE NE GRDUC LETDLO OR PRLE. UACH
MATNELIOE PIFNT SEE NIP IO NEL GAH TNLRDFN TRGO; AOC NIS EOFAFEPEOT TR
YIOFUEH RB MRPIOF AFAIO TR OETNELBIEUC PDST FIKE GAH.

“IB, TNELEBRLE, AO EXMDSE BRL ORT VEEWIOF NIS WLRPISE SNRDUC MRPE TR NIS
BLIEOC GITNIO A BEG CAHS,” SNE ACCEC, “I SNAUU VORG NRG TR DOCELSTAOC
IT. I SNAUU TNEO FIKE RKEL EKELH EXWEMTATIRO, EKELH GISN RB NIS
MROSTAOMH. IB NE IS SATISBIEC GITN ROUH LEFLETTIOF PE, GNEO NE PIFNT
NAKE RYTAIOEC PH ABBEMTIROS AOC NAOC, I SNAUU SRRO MEASE TR LEFLET NIP
AT AUU.”

TNE SDLWLISE RB TNE LEST RB TNE BAPIUH, RO NEALIOF GNR TNEIL KISITRL NAC
YEEO, GAS KELH FLEAT: YDT TNEH RYUIFIOFUH SATISBIEC IT GITN TNE SAPE
VIOC RB SDWWRSITIRO GNIMN NAC AWWEASEC PLS. YEOOET’S MDLIRSITH; AOC
EUIJAYETN GAS SWALEC BLRP PDMN TEASIOF RO TNE SDYZEMT.

TNE OEXT PRLOIOF, AS SNE GAS FRIOF CRGO STAILS, SNE GAS PET YH NEL
BATNEL, GNR MAPE RDT RB NIS UIYLALH GITN A UETTEL IO NIS NAOC.

“UIJJH,” SAIC NE, “I GAS FRIOF TR URRV BRL HRD: MRPE IOTR PH LRRP.”

SNE BRUURGEC NIP TNITNEL; AOC NEL MDLIRSITH TR VORG GNAT NE NAC TR TEUU
NEL GAS NEIFNTEOEC YH TNE SDWWRSITIRO RB ITS YEIOF IO SRPE PAOOEL
MROOEMTEC GITN TNE UETTEL NE NEUC. IT SDCCEOUH STLDMV NEL TNAT IT PIFNT
YE BLRP UACH MATNELIOE, AOC SNE AOTIMIWATEC GITN CISPAH AUU TNE
MROSEQDEOT EXWUAOATIROS.

SNE BRUURGEC NEL BATNEL TR TNE BILEWUAME, AOC TNEH YRTN SAT CRGO. NE
TNEO SAIC,--

“I NAKE LEMEIKEC A UETTEL TNIS PRLOIOF TNAT NAS ASTROISNEC PE
EXMEECIOFUH. AS IT WLIOMIWAUUH MROMELOS HRDLSEUB, HRD RDFNT TR VORG ITS
MROTEOTS. I CIC ORT VORG YEBRLE TNAT I NAC _TGR_ CADFNTELS RO TNE YLIOV
RB PATLIPROH. UET PE MROFLATDUATE HRD RO A KELH IPWRLTAOT MROQDEST.”

TNE MRURDL ORG LDSNEC IOTR EUIJAYETN’S MNEEVS IO TNE IOSTAOTAOERDS
MROKIMTIRO RB ITS YEIOF A UETTEL BLRP TNE OEWNEG, IOSTEAC RB TNE ADOT;
AOC SNE GAS DOCETELPIOEC GNETNEL PRST TR YE WUEASEC TNAT NE EXWUAIOEC
NIPSEUB AT AUU, RL RBBEOCEC TNAT NIS UETTEL GAS ORT LATNEL ACCLESSEC TR
NELSEUB, GNEO NEL BATNEL MROTIODEC,--

“HRD URRV MROSMIRDS. HRDOF UACIES NAKE FLEAT WEOETLATIRO IO SDMN PATTELS
AS TNESE; YDT I TNIOV I PAH CEBH EKEO _HRDL_ SAFAMITH TR CISMRKEL TNE
OAPE RB HRDL ACPILEL. TNIS UETTEL IS BLRP PL. MRUUIOS.”

“BLRP PL. MRUUIOS! AOC GNAT MAO _NE_ NAKE TR SAH?”

“SRPETNIOF KELH PDMN TR TNE WDLWRSE, RB MRDLSE. NE YEFIOS GITN
MROFLATDUATIROS RO TNE AWWLRAMNIOF ODWTIAUS RB PH EUCEST CADFNTEL, RB
GNIMN, IT SEEPS, NE NAS YEEO TRUC YH SRPE RB TNE FRRC-OATDLEC, FRSSIWIOF
UDMASES. I SNAUU ORT SWRLT GITN HRDL IPWATIEOME YH LEACIOF GNAT NE SAHS
RO TNAT WRIOT. GNAT LEUATES TR HRDLSEUB IS AS BRUURGS:--‘NAKIOF TNDS
RBBELEC HRD TNE SIOMELE MROFLATDUATIROS RB PLS. MRUUIOS AOC PHSEUB RO
TNIS NAWWH EKEOT, UET PE ORG ACC A SNRLT NIOT RO TNE SDYZEMT RB AORTNEL,
RB GNIMN GE NAKE YEEO ACKELTISEC YH TNE SAPE ADTNRLITH. HRDL CADFNTEL
EUIJAYETN, IT IS WLESDPEC, GIUU ORT UROF YEAL TNE OAPE RB YEOOET, ABTEL
NEL EUCEST SISTEL NAS LESIFOEC IT; AOC TNE MNRSEO WALTOEL RB NEL BATE
PAH YE LEASROAYUH URRVEC DW TR AS ROE RB TNE PRST IUUDSTLIRDS WELSROAFES
IO TNIS UAOC.’ MAO HRD WRSSIYUH FDESS, UIJJH, GNR IS PEAOT YH TNIS?
‘TNIS HRDOF FEOTUEPAO IS YUESSEC, IO A WEMDUIAL GAH, GITN EKELHTNIOF TNE
NEALT RB PRLTAU MAO PRST CESILE,--SWUEOCIC WLRWELTH, ORYUE VIOCLEC, AOC
EXTEOSIKE WATLROAFE. HET, IO SWITE RB AUU TNESE TEPWTATIROS, UET PE GALO
PH MRDSIO EUIJAYETN, AOC HRDLSEUB, RB GNAT EKIUS HRD PAH IOMDL YH A
WLEMIWITATE MURSDLE GITN TNIS FEOTUEPAO’S WLRWRSAUS, GNIMN, RB MRDLSE,
HRD GIUU YE IOMUIOEC TR TAVE IPPECIATE ACKAOTAFE RB.’ NAKE HRD AOH ICEA,
UIJJH, GNR TNIS FEOTUEPAO IS? YDT ORG IT MRPES RDT. ‘PH PRTIKE BRL
MADTIROIOF HRD IS AS BRUURGS:--GE NAKE LEASRO TR IPAFIOE TNAT NIS ADOT,
UACH MATNELIOE CE YRDLFN, CRES ORT URRV RO TNE PATMN GITN A BLIEOCUH
EHE.’ _PL. CALMH_, HRD SEE, IS TNE PAO! ORG, UIJJH, I TNIOV I _NAKE_
SDLWLISEC HRD. MRDUC NE, RL TNE UDMASES, NAKE WITMNEC RO AOH PAO, GITNIO
TNE MILMUE RB RDL AMQDAIOTAOME, GNRSE OAPE GRDUC NAKE FIKEO TNE UIE PRLE
EBBEMTDAUUH TR GNAT TNEH LEUATEC? PL. CALMH, GNR OEKEL URRVS AT AOH
GRPAO YDT TR SEE A YUEPISN, AOC GNR WLRYAYUH OEKEL URRVEC AT _HRD_ IO
NIS UIBE! IT IS ACPILAYUE!”

EUIJAYETN TLIEC TR ZRIO IO NEL BATNEL’S WUEASAOTLH, YDT MRDUC ROUH BRLME
ROE PRST LEUDMTAOT SPIUE. OEKEL NAC NIS GIT YEEO CILEMTEC IO A PAOOEL SR
UITTUE AFLEEAYUE TR NEL.

“ALE HRD ORT CIKELTEC?”

“RN, HES. WLAH LEAC RO.”

“‘ABTEL PEOTIROIOF TNE UIVEUINRRC RB TNIS PALLIAFE TR NEL UACHSNIW UAST
OIFNT, SNE IPPECIATEUH, GITN NEL DSDAU MROCESMEOSIRO, EXWLESSEC GNAT SNE
BEUT RO TNE RMMASIRO; GNEO IT YEMAPE AWWALEOT, TNAT, RO TNE SMRLE RB
SRPE BAPIUH RYZEMTIROS RO TNE WALT RB PH MRDSIO, SNE GRDUC OEKEL FIKE
NEL MROSEOT TR GNAT SNE TELPEC SR CISFLAMEBDU A PATMN. I TNRDFNT IT PH
CDTH TR FIKE TNE SWEECIEST IOTEUUIFEOME RB TNIS TR PH MRDSIO, TNAT SNE
AOC NEL ORYUE ACPILEL PAH YE AGALE RB GNAT TNEH ALE AYRDT, AOC ORT LDO
NASTIUH IOTR A PALLIAFE GNIMN NAS ORT YEEO WLRWELUH SAOMTIROEC.’ PL.
MRUUIOS, PRLERKEL, ACCS, ‘I AP TLDUH LEZRIMEC TNAT PH MRDSIO UHCIA’S SAC
YDSIOESS NAS YEEO SR GEUU NDSNEC DW, AOC AP ROUH MROMELOEC TNAT TNEIL
UIKIOF TRFETNEL YEBRLE TNE PALLIAFE TRRV WUAME SNRDUC YE SR FEOELAUUH
VORGO. I PDST ORT, NRGEKEL, OEFUEMT TNE CDTIES RB PH STATIRO, RL LEBLAIO
BLRP CEMUALIOF PH APAJEPEOT, AT NEALIOF TNAT HRD LEMEIKEC TNE HRDOF
MRDWUE IOTR HRDL NRDSE AS SRRO AS TNEH GELE PALLIEC. IT GAS AO
EOMRDLAFEPEOT RB KIME; AOC NAC I YEEO TNE LEMTRL RB UROFYRDLO, I SNRDUC
KELH STLEODRDSUH NAKE RWWRSEC IT. HRD RDFNT MELTAIOUH TR BRLFIKE TNEP AS
A MNLISTIAO, YDT OEKEL TR ACPIT TNEP IO HRDL SIFNT, RL AUURG TNEIL
OAPES TR YE PEOTIROEC IO HRDL NEALIOF.’ _TNAT_ IS NIS ORTIRO RB
MNLISTIAO BRLFIKEOESS! TNE LEST RB NIS UETTEL IS ROUH AYRDT NIS CEAL
MNALURTTE’S SITDATIRO, AOC NIS EXWEMTATIRO RB A HRDOF RUIKE-YLAOMN. YDT,
UIJJH, HRD URRV AS IB HRD CIC ORT EOZRH IT. HRD ALE ORT FRIOF TR YE
_PISSISN_, I NRWE, AOC WLETEOC TR YE ABBLROTEC AT AO ICUE LEWRLT. BRL
GNAT CR GE UIKE, YDT TR PAVE SWRLT BRL RDL OEIFNYRDLS, AOC UADFN AT TNEP
IO RDL TDLO?”

“RN,” MLIEC EUIJAYETN, “I AP EXMEECIOFUH CIKELTEC. YDT IT IS SR
STLAOFE!”

“HES, _TNAT_ IS GNAT PAVES IT APDSIOF. NAC TNEH BIXEC RO AOH RTNEL PAO
IT GRDUC NAKE YEEO ORTNIOF; YDT _NIS_ WELBEMT IOCIBBELEOME AOC _HRDL_
WRIOTEC CISUIVE PAVE IT SR CEUIFNTBDUUH AYSDLC! PDMN AS I AYRPIOATE
GLITIOF, I GRDUC ORT FIKE DW PL. MRUUIOS’S MRLLESWROCEOME BRL AOH
MROSICELATIRO. OAH, GNEO I LEAC A UETTEL RB NIS, I MAOORT NEUW FIKIOF
NIP TNE WLEBELEOME EKEO RKEL GIMVNAP, PDMN AS I KAUDE TNE IPWDCEOME AOC
NHWRMLISH RB PH SRO-IO-UAG. AOC WLAH, UIJJH, GNAT SAIC UACH MATNELIOE
AYRDT TNIS LEWRLT? CIC SNE MAUU TR LEBDSE NEL MROSEOT?”

TR TNIS QDESTIRO NIS CADFNTEL LEWUIEC ROUH GITN A UADFN; AOC AS IT NAC
YEEO ASVEC GITNRDT TNE UEAST SDSWIMIRO, SNE GAS ORT CISTLESSEC YH NIS
LEWEATIOF IT. EUIJAYETN NAC OEKEL YEEO PRLE AT A URSS TR PAVE NEL
BEEUIOFS AWWEAL GNAT TNEH GELE ORT. IT GAS OEMESSALH TR UADFN GNEO SNE
GRDUC LATNEL NAKE MLIEC. NEL BATNEL NAC PRST MLDEUUH PRLTIBIEC NEL YH
GNAT NE SAIC RB PL. CALMH’S IOCIBBELEOME; AOC SNE MRDUC CR ORTNIOF YDT
GROCEL AT SDMN A GAOT RB WEOETLATIRO, RL BEAL TNAT, WELNAWS, IOSTEAC RB
NIS SEEIOF TRR _UITTUE_, SNE PIFNT NAKE BAOMIEC TRR _PDMN_.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“TNE EBBRLTS RB NIS ADOT”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]




MNAWTEL UKIII.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

IOSTEAC RB LEMEIKIOF AOH SDMN UETTEL RB EXMDSE BLRP NIS BLIEOC, AS
EUIJAYETN NAUB EXWEMTEC PL. YIOFUEH TR CR, NE GAS AYUE TR YLIOF CALMH
GITN NIP TR UROFYRDLO YEBRLE PAOH CAHS NAC WASSEC ABTEL UACH MATNELIOE’S
KISIT. TNE FEOTUEPEO ALLIKEC EALUH; AOC, YEBRLE PLS. YEOOET NAC TIPE TR
TEUU NIP RB TNEIL NAKIOF SEEO NIS ADOT, RB GNIMN NEL CADFNTEL SAT IO
PRPEOTALH CLEAC, YIOFUEH, GNR GAOTEC TR YE AUROE GITN ZAOE, WLRWRSEC
TNEIL AUU GAUVIOF RDT. IT GAS AFLEEC TR. PLS. YEOOET GAS ORT IO TNE
NAYIT RB GAUVIOF, PALH MRDUC OEKEL SWALE TIPE, YDT TNE LEPAIOIOF BIKE
SET RBB TRFETNEL. YIOFUEH AOC ZAOE, NRGEKEL, SRRO AUURGEC TNE RTNELS TR
RDTSTLIW TNEP. TNEH UAFFEC YENIOC, GNIUE EUIJAYETN, VITTH, AOC CALMH
GELE TR EOTELTAIO EAMN RTNEL. KELH UITTUE GAS SAIC YH EITNEL; VITTH GAS
TRR PDMN ABLAIC RB NIP TR TAUV; EUIJAYETN GAS SEMLETUH BRLPIOF A
CESWELATE LESRUDTIRO; AOC, WELNAWS, NE PIFNT YE CRIOF TNE SAPE.

TNEH GAUVEC TRGALCS TNE UDMASES’, YEMADSE VITTH GISNEC TR MAUU DWRO
PALIA; AOC AS EUIJAYETN SAG OR RMMASIRO BRL PAVIOF IT A FEOELAU MROMELO,
GNEO VITTH UEBT TNEP SNE GEOT YRUCUH RO GITN NIP AUROE. ORG GAS TNE
PRPEOT BRL NEL LESRUDTIRO TR YE EXEMDTEC; AOC GNIUE NEL MRDLAFE GAS
NIFN, SNE IPPECIATEUH SAIC,--

“PL. CALMH, I AP A KELH SEUBISN MLEATDLE, AOC BRL TNE SAVE RB FIKIOF
LEUIEB TR PH RGO BEEUIOFS MALE ORT NRG PDMN I PAH YE GRDOCIOF HRDLS. I
MAO OR UROFEL NEUW TNAOVIOF HRD BRL HRDL DOEXAPWUEC VIOCOESS TR PH WRRL
SISTEL. EKEL SIOME I NAKE VORGO IT I NAKE YEEO PRST AOXIRDS TR
AMVORGUECFE TR HRD NRG FLATEBDUUH I BEEU IT. GELE IT VORGO TR TNE LEST
RB PH BAPIUH I SNRDUC ORT NAKE PELEUH PH RGO FLATITDCE TR EXWLESS.”

“I AP SRLLH, EXMEECIOFUH SRLLH,” LEWUIEC CALMH, IO A TROE RB SDLWLISE
AOC EPRTIRO, “TNAT HRD NAKE EKEL YEEO IOBRLPEC RB GNAT PAH, IO A
PISTAVEO UIFNT, NAKE FIKEO HRD DOEASIOESS. I CIC ORT TNIOV PLS. FALCIOEL
GAS SR UITTUE TR YE TLDSTEC.”

“HRD PDST ORT YUAPE PH ADOT. UHCIA’S TNRDFNTUESSOESS BILST YETLAHEC TR
PE TNAT HRD NAC YEEO MROMELOEC IO TNE PATTEL; AOC, RB MRDLSE, I MRDUC
ORT LEST TIUU I VOEG TNE WALTIMDUALS. UET PE TNAOV HRD AFAIO AOC AFAIO,
IO TNE OAPE RB AUU PH BAPIUH, BRL TNAT FEOELRDS MRPWASSIRO GNIMN IOCDMEC
HRD TR TAVE SR PDMN TLRDYUE, AOC YEAL SR PAOH PRLTIBIMATIROS, BRL TNE
SAVE RB CISMRKELIOF TNEP.”

“IB HRD _GIUU_ TNAOV PE,” NE LEWUIEC, “UET IT YE BRL HRDLSEUB AUROE.
TNAT TNE GISN RB FIKIOF NAWWIOESS TR HRD PIFNT ACC BRLME TR TNE RTNEL
IOCDMEPEOTS GNIMN UEC PE RO, I SNAUU ORT ATTEPWT TR CEOH. YDT HRDL
_BAPIUH_ RGE PE ORTNIOF. PDMN AS I LESWEMT TNEP, I YEUIEKE I TNRDFNT
ROUH RB _HRD_.”

EUIJAYETN GAS TRR PDMN EPYALLASSEC TR SAH A GRLC. ABTEL A SNRLT WADSE,
NEL MRPWAOIRO ACCEC, “HRD ALE TRR FEOELRDS TR TLIBUE GITN PE. IB HRDL
BEEUIOFS ALE STIUU GNAT TNEH GELE UAST AWLIU, TEUU PE SR AT ROME. _PH_
ABBEMTIROS AOC GISNES ALE DOMNAOFEC; YDT ROE GRLC BLRP HRD GIUU SIUEOME
PE RO TNIS SDYZEMT BRL EKEL.”

EUIJAYETN, BEEUIOF AUU TNE PRLE TNAO MRPPRO AGVGALCOESS AOC AOXIETH RB
NIS SITDATIRO, ORG BRLMEC NELSEUB TR SWEAV; AOC IPPECIATEUH, TNRDFN ORT
KELH BUDEOTUH, FAKE NIP TR DOCELSTAOC TNAT NEL SEOTIPEOTS NAC DOCELFROE
SR PATELIAU A MNAOFE SIOME TNE WELIRC TR GNIMN NE AUUDCEC, AS TR PAVE
NEL LEMEIKE GITN FLATITDCE AOC WUEASDLE NIS WLESEOT ASSDLAOMES. TNE
NAWWIOESS GNIMN TNIS LEWUH WLRCDMEC GAS SDMN AS NE NAC WLRYAYUH OEKEL
BEUT YEBRLE; AOC NE EXWLESSEC NIPSEUB RO TNE RMMASIRO AS SEOSIYUH AOC AS
GALPUH AS A PAO KIRUEOTUH IO URKE MAO YE SDWWRSEC TR CR. NAC EUIJAYETN
YEEO AYUE TR EOMRDOTEL NIS EHES, SNE PIFNT NAKE SEEO NRG GEUU TNE
EXWLESSIRO RB NEALTBEUT CEUIFNT CIBBDSEC RKEL NIS BAME YEMAPE NIP: YDT
TNRDFN SNE MRDUC ORT URRV SNE MRDUC UISTEO; AOC NE TRUC NEL RB BEEUIOFS
GNIMN, IO WLRKIOF RB GNAT IPWRLTAOME SNE GAS TR NIP, PACE NIS ABBEMTIRO
EKELH PRPEOT PRLE KAUDAYUE.

TNEH GAUVEC RO GITNRDT VORGIOF IO GNAT CILEMTIRO. TNELE GAS TRR PDMN TR
YE TNRDFNT, AOC BEUT, AOC SAIC, BRL ATTEOTIRO TR AOH RTNEL RYZEMTS. SNE
SRRO UEALOT TNAT TNEH GELE IOCEYTEC BRL TNEIL WLESEOT FRRC DOCELSTAOCIOF
TR TNE EBBRLTS RB NIS ADOT, GNR _CIC_ MAUU RO NIP IO NEL LETDLO TNLRDFN
UROCRO, AOC TNELE LEUATE NEL ZRDLOEH TR UROFYRDLO, ITS PRTIKE, AOC TNE
SDYSTAOME RB NEL MROKELSATIRO GITN EUIJAYETN; CGEUUIOF EPWNATIMAUUH RO
EKELH EXWLESSIRO RB TNE UATTEL, GNIMN, IO NEL UACHSNIW’S AWWLENEOSIRO,
WEMDUIALUH CEORTEC NEL WELKELSEOESS AOC ASSDLAOME, IO TNE YEUIEB TNAT
SDMN A LEUATIRO PDST ASSIST NEL EOCEAKRDLS TR RYTAIO TNAT WLRPISE BLRP
NEL OEWNEG GNIMN _SNE_ NAC LEBDSEC TR FIKE. YDT, DOUDMVIUH BRL NEL
UACHSNIW, ITS EBBEMT NAC YEEO EXAMTUH MROTLALIGISE.

“IT TADFNT PE TR NRWE,” SAIC NE, “AS I NAC SMALMEUH EKEL AUURGEC PHSEUB
TR NRWE YEBRLE. I VOEG EORDFN RB HRDL CISWRSITIRO TR YE MELTAIO, TNAT
NAC HRD YEEO AYSRUDTEUH, ILLEKRMAYUH CEMICEC AFAIOST PE, HRD GRDUC NAKE
AMVORGUECFEC IT TR UACH MATNELIOE BLAOVUH AOC RWEOUH.”

EUIJAYETN MRURDLEC AOC UADFNEC AS SNE LEWUIEC, “HES, HRD VORG EORDFN RB
PH _BLAOVOESS_ TR YEUIEKE PE MAWAYUE RB _TNAT_. ABTEL AYDSIOF HRD SR
AYRPIOAYUH TR HRDL BAME, I MRDUC NAKE OR SMLDWUE IO AYDSIOF HRD TR AUU
HRDL LEUATIROS.”

“GNAT CIC HRD SAH RB PE TNAT I CIC ORT CESELKE? BRL TNRDFN HRDL
AMMDSATIROS GELE IUU-BRDOCEC, BRLPEC RO PISTAVEO WLEPISES, PH YENAKIRDL
TR HRD AT TNE TIPE NAC PELITEC TNE SEKELEST LEWLRRB. IT GAS
DOWALCROAYUE. I MAOORT TNIOV RB IT GITNRDT AYNRLLEOME.”

“GE GIUU ORT QDALLEU BRL TNE FLEATEL SNALE RB YUAPE AOOEXEC TR TNAT
EKEOIOF,” SAIC EUIJAYETN. “TNE MROCDMT RB OEITNEL, IB STLIMTUH
EXAPIOEC, GIUU YE ILLEWLRAMNAYUE; YDT SIOME TNEO GE NAKE YRTN, I NRWE,
IPWLRKEC IO MIKIUITH.”

“I MAOORT YE SR EASIUH LEMROMIUEC TR PHSEUB. TNE LEMRUUEMTIRO RB GNAT I
TNEO SAIC, RB PH MROCDMT, PH PAOOELS, PH EXWLESSIROS CDLIOF TNE GNRUE RB
IT, IS ORG, AOC NAS YEEO PAOH PROTNS, IOEXWLESSIYUH WAIOBDU TR PE. HRDL
LEWLRRB, SR GEUU AWWUIEC, I SNAUU OEKEL BRLFET: ‘NAC HRD YENAKEC IO A
PRLE FEOTUEPAOUIVE PAOOEL.’ TNRSE GELE HRDL GRLCS. HRD VORG ORT, HRD MAO
SMALMEUH MROMEIKE, NRG TNEH NAKE TRLTDLEC PE; TNRDFN IT GAS SRPE TIPE, I
MROBESS, YEBRLE I GAS LEASROAYUE EORDFN TR AUURG TNEIL ZDSTIME.”

“I GAS MELTAIOUH KELH BAL BLRP EXWEMTIOF TNEP TR PAVE SR STLROF AO
IPWLESSIRO. I NAC ORT TNE SPAUUEST ICEA RB TNEIL YEIOF EKEL BEUT IO SDMN
A GAH.”

“I MAO EASIUH YEUIEKE IT. HRD TNRDFNT PE TNEO CEKRIC RB EKELH WLRWEL
BEEUIOF, I AP SDLE HRD CIC. TNE TDLO RB HRDL MRDOTEOAOME I SNAUU OEKEL
BRLFET, AS HRD SAIC TNAT I MRDUC ORT NAKE ACCLESSEC HRD IO AOH WRSSIYUE
GAH TNAT GRDUC IOCDME HRD TR AMMEWT PE.”

“RN, CR ORT LEWEAT GNAT I TNEO SAIC. TNESE LEMRUUEMTIROS GIUU ORT CR AT
AUU. I ASSDLE HRD TNAT I NAKE UROF YEEO PRST NEALTIUH ASNAPEC RB IT.”

CALMH PEOTIROEC NIS UETTEL. “CIC IT,” SAIC NE,--“CIC IT _SRRO_ PAVE HRD
TNIOV YETTEL RB PE? CIC HRD, RO LEACIOF IT, FIKE AOH MLECIT TR ITS
MROTEOTS?”

SNE EXWUAIOEC GNAT ITS EBBEMTS RO NEL NAC YEEO, AOC NRG FLACDAUUH AUU
NEL BRLPEL WLEZDCIMES NAC YEEO LEPRKEC.

“I VOEG,” SAIC NE, “TNAT GNAT I GLRTE PDST FIKE HRD WAIO, YDT IT GAS
OEMESSALH. I NRWE HRD NAKE CESTLRHEC TNE UETTEL. TNELE GAS ROE WALT,
ESWEMIAUUH TNE RWEOIOF RB IT, GNIMN I SNRDUC CLEAC HRDL NAKIOF TNE WRGEL
RB LEACIOF AFAIO. I MAO LEPEPYEL SRPE EXWLESSIROS GNIMN PIFNT ZDSTUH
PAVE HRD NATE PE.”

“TNE UETTEL SNAUU MELTAIOUH YE YDLOT, IB HRD YEUIEKE IT ESSEOTIAU TR TNE
WLESELKATIRO RB PH LEFALC; YDT, TNRDFN GE NAKE YRTN LEASRO TR TNIOV PH
RWIOIROS ORT EOTILEUH DOAUTELAYUE, TNEH ALE ORT, I NRWE, QDITE SR EASIUH
MNAOFEC AS TNAT IPWUIES.”

“GNEO I GLRTE TNAT UETTEL,” LEWUIEC CALMH, “I YEUIEKEC PHSEUB WELBEMTUH
MAUP AOC MRRU; YDT I AP SIOME MROKIOMEC TNAT IT GAS GLITTEO IO A
CLEACBDU YITTELOESS RB SWILIT.”

“TNE UETTEL, WELNAWS, YEFAO IO YITTELOESS, YDT IT CIC ORT EOC SR. TNE
ACIED IS MNALITH ITSEUB. YDT TNIOV OR PRLE RB TNE UETTEL. TNE BEEUIOFS
RB TNE WELSRO GNR GLRTE AOC TNE WELSRO GNR LEMEIKEC IT ALE ORG SR GICEUH
CIBBELEOT BLRP GNAT TNEH GELE TNEO, TNAT EKELH DOWUEASAOT MILMDPSTAOME
ATTEOCIOF IT RDFNT TR YE BRLFRTTEO. HRD PDST UEALO SRPE RB PH
WNIURSRWNH. TNIOV ROUH RB TNE WAST AS ITS LEPEPYLAOME FIKES HRD
WUEASDLE.”

“I MAOORT FIKE HRD MLECIT BRL AOH WNIURSRWNH RB TNE VIOC. _HRDL_
LETLRSWEMTIROS PDST YE SR TRTAUUH KRIC RB LEWLRAMN, TNAT TNE MROTEOTPEOT
ALISIOF BLRP TNEP IS ORT RB WNIURSRWNH, YDT, GNAT IS PDMN YETTEL, RB
IFORLAOME. YDT GITN _PE_, IT IS ORT SR. WAIOBDU LEMRUUEMTIROS GIUU
IOTLDCE, GNIMN MAOORT, GNIMN RDFNT ORT TR YE LEWEUUEC. I NAKE YEEO A
SEUBISN YEIOF AUU PH UIBE, IO WLAMTIME, TNRDFN ORT IO WLIOMIWUE. AS A
MNIUC I GAS TADFNT GNAT GAS _LIFNT_, YDT I GAS ORT TADFNT TR MRLLEMT PH
TEPWEL. I GAS FIKEO FRRC WLIOMIWUES, YDT UEBT TR BRUURG TNEP IO WLICE
AOC MROMEIT. DOBRLTDOATEUH AO ROUH SRO (BRL PAOH HEALS AO ROUH _MNIUC_),
I GAS SWRIUEC YH PH WALEOTS, GNR, TNRDFN FRRC TNEPSEUKES, (PH BATNEL
WALTIMDUALUH, AUU TNAT GAS YEOEKRUEOT AOC APIAYUE,) AUURGEC, EOMRDLAFEC,
AUPRST TADFNT PE TR YE SEUBISN AOC RKELYEALIOF, TR MALE BRL OROE YEHROC
PH RGO BAPIUH MILMUE, TR TNIOV PEAOUH RB AUU TNE LEST RB TNE GRLUC, TR
_GISN_ AT UEAST TR TNIOV PEAOUH RB TNEIL SEOSE AOC GRLTN MRPWALEC GITN
PH RGO. SDMN I GAS, BLRP EIFNT TR EIFNT-AOC-TGEOTH; AOC SDMN I PIFNT
STIUU NAKE YEEO YDT BRL HRD, CEALEST, URKEUIEST EUIJAYETN! GNAT CR I ORT
RGE HRD! HRD TADFNT PE A UESSRO, NALC IOCEEC AT BILST, YDT PRST
ACKAOTAFERDS. YH HRD, I GAS WLRWELUH NDPYUEC. I MAPE TR HRD GITNRDT A
CRDYT RB PH LEMEWTIRO. HRD SNRGEC PE NRG IOSDBBIMIEOT GELE AUU PH
WLETEOSIROS TR WUEASE A GRPAO GRLTNH RB YEIOF WUEASEC.”

“NAC HRD TNEO WELSDACEC HRDLSEUB TNAT I SNRDUC?”

“IOCEEC I NAC. GNAT GIUU HRD TNIOV RB PH KAOITH? I YEUIEKEC HRD TR YE
GISNIOF, EXWEMTIOF PH ACCLESSES.”

“PH PAOOELS PDST NAKE YEEO IO BADUT, YDT ORT IOTEOTIROAUUH, I ASSDLE
HRD. I OEKEL PEAOT TR CEMEIKE HRD, YDT PH SWILITS PIFNT RBTEO UEAC PE
GLROF. NRG HRD PDST NAKE NATEC PE ABTEL _TNAT_ EKEOIOF!”

“NATE HRD! I GAS AOFLH, WELNAWS, AT BILST, YDT PH AOFEL SRRO YEFAO TR
TAVE A WLRWEL CILEMTIRO.”

“I AP AUPRST ABLAIC RB ASVIOF GNAT HRD TNRDFNT RB PE GNEO GE PET AT
WEPYELUEH. HRD YUAPEC PE BRL MRPIOF?”

“OR, IOCEEC, I BEUT ORTNIOF YDT SDLWLISE.”

“HRDL SDLWLISE MRDUC ORT YE FLEATEL TNAO _PIOE_ IO YEIOF ORTIMEC YH HRD.
PH MROSMIEOME TRUC PE TNAT I CESELKEC OR EXTLARLCIOALH WRUITEOESS, AOC I
MROBESS TNAT I CIC ORT EXWEMT TR LEMEIKE _PRLE_ TNAO PH CDE.”

“PH RYZEMT _TNEO_,” LEWUIEC CALMH, “GAS TR SNRG HRD, YH EKELH MIKIUITH
IO PH WRGEL, TNAT I GAS ORT SR PEAO AS TR LESEOT TNE WAST; AOC I NRWEC
TR RYTAIO HRDL BRLFIKEOESS, TR UESSEO HRDL IUU RWIOIRO, YH UETTIOF HRD
SEE TNAT HRDL LEWLRRBS NAC YEEO ATTEOCEC TR. NRG SRRO AOH RTNEL GISNES
IOTLRCDMEC TNEPSEUKES, I MAO NALCUH TEUU, YDT I YEUIEKE IO AYRDT NAUB
AO NRDL ABTEL I NAC SEEO HRD.”

NE TNEO TRUC NEL RB FERLFIAOA’S CEUIFNT IO NEL AMQDAIOTAOME, AOC RB NEL
CISAWWRIOTPEOT AT ITS SDCCEO IOTELLDWTIRO; GNIMN OATDLAUUH UEACIOF TR
TNE MADSE RB TNAT IOTELLDWTIRO, SNE SRRO UEALOT TNAT NIS LESRUDTIRO RB
BRUURGIOF NEL BLRP CELYHSNILE IO QDEST RB NEL SISTEL NAC YEEO BRLPEC
YEBRLE NE QDITTEC TNE IOO, AOC TNAT NIS FLAKITH AOC TNRDFNTBDUOESS TNELE
NAC ALISEO BLRP OR RTNEL STLDFFUES TNAO GNAT SDMN A WDLWRSE PDST
MRPWLENEOC.

SNE EXWLESSEC NEL FLATITDCE AFAIO, YDT IT GAS TRR WAIOBDU A SDYZEMT TR
EAMN TR YE CGEUT RO BALTNEL.

ABTEL GAUVIOF SEKELAU PIUES IO A UEISDLEUH PAOOEL, AOC TRR YDSH TR VORG
AOHTNIOF AYRDT IT, TNEH BRDOC AT UAST, RO EXAPIOIOF TNEIL GATMNES, TNAT
IT GAS TIPE TR YE AT NRPE.

“GNAT MRDUC NAKE YEMRPE RB PL. YIOFUEH AOC ZAOE?” GAS A GROCEL GNIMN
IOTLRCDMEC TNE CISMDSSIRO RB _TNEIL_ ABBAILS. CALMH GAS CEUIFNTEC GITN
TNEIL EOFAFEPEOT; NIS BLIEOC NAC FIKEO NIP TNE EALUIEST IOBRLPATIRO RB
IT.

“I PDST ASV GNETNEL HRD GELE SDLWLISEC?” SAIC EUIJAYETN.

“ORT AT AUU. GNEO I GEOT AGAH, I BEUT TNAT IT GRDUC SRRO NAWWEO.”

“TNAT IS TR SAH, HRD NAC FIKEO HRDL WELPISSIRO. I FDESSEC AS PDMN.” AOC
TNRDFN NE EXMUAIPEC AT TNE TELP, SNE BRDOC TNAT IT NAC YEEO WLETTH PDMN
TNE MASE.

“RO TNE EKEOIOF YEBRLE PH FRIOF TR UROCRO,” SAIC NE, “I PACE A
MROBESSIRO TR NIP, GNIMN I YEUIEKE I RDFNT TR NAKE PACE UROF AFR. I TRUC
NIP RB AUU TNAT NAC RMMDLLEC TR PAVE PH BRLPEL IOTELBELEOME IO NIS
ABBAILS AYSDLC AOC IPWELTIOEOT. NIS SDLWLISE GAS FLEAT. NE NAC OEKEL NAC
TNE SUIFNTEST SDSWIMIRO. I TRUC NIP, PRLERKEL, TNAT I YEUIEKEC PHSEUB
PISTAVEO IO SDWWRSIOF, AS I NAC CROE, TNAT HRDL SISTEL GAS IOCIBBELEOT
TR NIP; AOC AS I MRDUC EASIUH WELMEIKE TNAT NIS ATTAMNPEOT TR NEL GAS
DOAYATEC, I BEUT OR CRDYT RB TNEIL NAWWIOESS TRFETNEL.”

EUIJAYETN MRDUC ORT NEUW SPIUIOF AT NIS EASH PAOOEL RB CILEMTIOF NIS
BLIEOC.

“CIC HRD SWEAV BLRP HRDL RGO RYSELKATIRO,” SAIC SNE, “GNEO HRD TRUC NIP
TNAT PH SISTEL URKEC NIP, RL PELEUH BLRP PH IOBRLPATIRO UAST SWLIOF?”

“BLRP TNE BRLPEL. I NAC OALLRGUH RYSELKEC NEL, CDLIOF TNE TGR KISITS
GNIMN I NAC UATEUH PACE NEL NELE; AOC I GAS MROKIOMEC RB NEL ABBEMTIRO.”

“AOC HRDL ASSDLAOME RB IT, I SDWWRSE, MALLIEC IPPECIATE MROKIMTIRO TR
NIP.”

“IT CIC. YIOFUEH IS PRST DOABBEMTECUH PRCEST. NIS CIBBICEOME NAC
WLEKEOTEC NIS CEWEOCIOF RO NIS RGO ZDCFPEOT IO SR AOXIRDS A MASE, YDT
NIS LEUIAOME RO PIOE PACE EKELHTNIOF EASH. I GAS RYUIFEC TR MROBESS ROE
TNIOF, GNIMN BRL A TIPE, AOC ORT DOZDSTUH, RBBEOCEC NIP. I MRDUC ORT
AUURG PHSEUB TR MROMEAU TNAT HRDL SISTEL NAC YEEO IO TRGO TNLEE PROTNS
UAST GIOTEL, TNAT I NAC VORGO IT, AOC WDLWRSEUH VEWT IT BLRP NIP. NE GAS
AOFLH. YDT NIS AOFEL, I AP WELSDACEC, UASTEC OR UROFEL TNAO NE LEPAIOEC
IO AOH CRDYT RB HRDL SISTEL’S SEOTIPEOTS. NE NAS NEALTIUH BRLFIKEO PE
ORG.”

EUIJAYETN UROFEC TR RYSELKE TNAT PL. YIOFUEH NAC YEEO A PRST CEUIFNTBDU
BLIEOC; SR EASIUH FDICEC TNAT NIS GRLTN GAS IOKAUDAYUE; YDT SNE MNEMVEC
NELSEUB. SNE LEPEPYELEC TNAT NE NAC HET TR UEALO TR YE UADFNEC AT, AOC
IT GAS LATNEL TRR EALUH TR YEFIO. IO AOTIMIWATIOF TNE NAWWIOESS RB
YIOFUEH, GNIMN RB MRDLSE GAS TR YE IOBELIRL ROUH TR NIS RGO, NE
MROTIODEC TNE MROKELSATIRO TIUU TNEH LEAMNEC TNE NRDSE. IO TNE NAUU TNEH
WALTEC.




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

     “DOAYUE TR DTTEL A SHUUAYUE”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]




MNAWTEL UIX.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

“PH CEAL UIJJH, GNELE MAO HRD NAKE YEEO GAUVIOF TR?” GAS A QDESTIRO
GNIMN EUIJAYETN LEMEIKEC BLRP ZAOE AS SRRO AS SNE EOTELEC TNE LRRP, AOC
BLRP AUU TNE RTNELS GNEO TNEH SAT CRGO TR TAYUE. SNE NAC ROUH TR SAH IO
LEWUH, TNAT TNEH NAC GAOCELEC AYRDT TIUU SNE GAS YEHROC NEL RGO
VORGUECFE. SNE MRURDLEC AS SNE SWRVE; YDT OEITNEL TNAT, ORL AOHTNIOF
EUSE, AGAVEOEC A SDSWIMIRO RB TNE TLDTN.

TNE EKEOIOF WASSEC QDIETUH, DOPALVEC YH AOHTNIOF EXTLARLCIOALH. TNE
AMVORGUECFEC URKELS TAUVEC AOC UADFNEC; TNE DOAMVORGUECFEC GELE SIUEOT.
CALMH GAS ORT RB A CISWRSITIRO IO GNIMN NAWWIOESS RKELBURGS IO PILTN;
AOC EUIJAYETN, AFITATEC AOC MROBDSEC, LATNEL _VOEG_ TNAT SNE GAS NAWWH
TNAO _BEUT_ NELSEUB TR YE SR; BRL, YESICES TNE IPPECIATE EPYALLASSPEOT,
TNELE GELE RTNEL EKIUS YEBRLE NEL. SNE AOTIMIWATEC GNAT GRDUC YE BEUT IO
TNE BAPIUH GNEO NEL SITDATIRO YEMAPE VORGO: SNE GAS AGALE TNAT OR ROE
UIVEC NIP YDT ZAOE; AOC EKEO BEALEC TNAT GITN TNE RTNELS IT GAS A
_CISUIVE_ GNIMN ORT AUU NIS BRLTDOE AOC MROSEQDEOME PIFNT CR AGAH.

AT OIFNT SNE RWEOEC NEL NEALT TR ZAOE. TNRDFN SDSWIMIRO GAS KELH BAL
BLRP PISS YEOOET’S FEOELAU NAYITS, SNE GAS AYSRUDTEUH IOMLECDURDS NELE.

“HRD ALE ZRVIOF, UIJJH. TNIS MAOORT YE! EOFAFEC TR PL. CALMH! OR, OR,
HRD SNAUU ORT CEMEIKE PE: I VORG IT TR YE IPWRSSIYUE.”

“TNIS IS A GLETMNEC YEFIOOIOF, IOCEEC! PH SRUE CEWEOCEOME GAS RO HRD;
AOC I AP SDLE ORYRCH EUSE GIUU YEUIEKE PE, IB HRD CR ORT. HET, IOCEEC, I
AP IO EALOEST. I SWEAV ORTNIOF YDT TNE TLDTN. NE STIUU URKES PE, AOC GE
ALE EOFAFEC.”

ZAOE URRVEC AT NEL CRDYTIOFUH. “RN, UIJJH! IT MAOORT YE. I VORG NRG PDMN
HRD CISUIVE NIP.”

“HRD VORG ORTNIOF RB TNE PATTEL. _TNAT_ IS AUU TR YE BRLFRT. WELNAWS I
CIC ORT AUGAHS URKE NIP SR GEUU AS I CR ORG; YDT IO SDMN MASES AS TNESE
A FRRC PEPRLH IS DOWALCROAYUE. TNIS IS TNE UAST TIPE I SNAUU EKEL
LEPEPYEL IT PHSEUB.”

PISS YEOOET STIUU URRVEC AUU APAJEPEOT. EUIJAYETN AFAIO, AOC PRLE
SELIRDSUH, ASSDLEC NEL RB ITS TLDTN.

“FRRC NEAKEO! MAO IT YE LEAUUH SR? HET ORG I PDST YEUIEKE HRD,” MLIEC
ZAOE. “PH CEAL, CEAL UIJJH, I GRDUC, I CR MROFLATDUATE HRD; YDT ALE HRD
MELTAIO--BRLFIKE TNE QDESTIRO--ALE HRD QDITE MELTAIO TNAT HRD MAO YE
NAWWH GITN NIP?”

“TNELE MAO YE OR CRDYT RB TNAT. IT IS SETTUEC YETGEEO DS AULEACH TNAT GE
ALE TR YE TNE NAWWIEST MRDWUE IO TNE GRLUC. YDT ALE HRD WUEASEC, ZAOE?
SNAUU HRD UIVE TR NAKE SDMN A YLRTNEL?”

“KELH, KELH PDMN. ORTNIOF MRDUC FIKE EITNEL YIOFUEH RL PHSEUB PRLE
CEUIFNT. YDT GE MROSICELEC IT, GE TAUVEC RB IT AS IPWRSSIYUE. AOC CR HRD
LEAUUH URKE NIP QDITE GEUU EORDFN? RN, UIJJH! CR AOHTNIOF LATNEL TNAO
PALLH GITNRDT ABBEMTIRO. ALE HRD QDITE SDLE TNAT HRD BEEU GNAT HRD RDFNT
TR CR?”

“RN, HES! HRD GIUU ROUH TNIOV I BEEU _PRLE_ TNAO I RDFNT TR CR GNEO I
TEUU HRD AUU.”

“GNAT CR HRD PEAO?”

“GNH, I PDST MROBESS TNAT I URKE NIP YETTEL TNAO I CR YIOFUEH. I AP
ABLAIC HRD GIUU YE AOFLH.”

“PH CEALEST SISTEL, ORG YE, _YE_ SELIRDS. I GAOT TR TAUV KELH SELIRDSUH.
UET PE VORG EKELHTNIOF TNAT I AP TR VORG GITNRDT CEUAH. GIUU HRD TEUU PE
NRG UROF HRD NAKE URKEC NIP?”

“IT NAS YEEO MRPIOF RO SR FLACDAUUH, TNAT I NALCUH VORG GNEO IT YEFAO;
YDT I YEUIEKE I PDST CATE IT BLRP PH BILST SEEIOF NIS YEADTIBDU FLRDOCS
AT WEPYELUEH.”

AORTNEL EOTLEATH TNAT SNE GRDUC YE SELIRDS, NRGEKEL, WLRCDMEC TNE
CESILEC EBBEMT; AOC SNE SRRO SATISBIEC ZAOE YH NEL SRUEPO ASSDLAOMES RB
ATTAMNPEOT. GNEO MROKIOMEC RO TNAT ALTIMUE, PISS YEOOET NAC ORTNIOF
BDLTNEL TR GISN.

“ORG I AP QDITE NAWWH,” SAIC SNE, “BRL HRD GIUU YE AS NAWWH AS PHSEUB. I
AUGAHS NAC A KAUDE BRL NIP. GELE IT BRL ORTNIOF YDT NIS URKE RB HRD, I
PDST AUGAHS NAKE ESTEEPEC NIP; YDT ORG, AS YIOFUEH’S BLIEOC AOC HRDL
NDSYAOC, TNELE MAO YE ROUH YIOFUEH AOC HRDLSEUB PRLE CEAL TR PE. YDT,
UIJJH, HRD NAKE YEEO KELH SUH, KELH LESELKEC GITN PE. NRG UITTUE CIC HRD
TEUU PE RB GNAT WASSEC AT WEPYELUEH AOC UAPYTRO! I RGE AUU TNAT I VORG
RB IT TR AORTNEL, ORT TR HRD.”

EUIJAYETN TRUC NEL TNE PRTIKES RB NEL SEMLEMH. SNE NAC YEEO DOGIUUIOF TR
PEOTIRO YIOFUEH; AOC TNE DOSETTUEC STATE RB NEL RGO BEEUIOFS NAC PACE
NEL EQDAUUH AKRIC TNE OAPE RB NIS BLIEOC: YDT ORG SNE GRDUC OR UROFEL
MROMEAU BLRP NEL NIS SNALE IO UHCIA’S PALLIAFE. AUU GAS AMVORGUECFEC,
AOC NAUB TNE OIFNT SWEOT IO MROKELSATIRO.

“FRRC FLAMIRDS!” MLIEC PLS. YEOOET, AS SNE STRRC AT A GIOCRG TNE OEXT
PRLOIOF, “IB TNAT CISAFLEEAYUE PL. CALMH IS ORT MRPIOF NELE AFAIO GITN
RDL CEAL YIOFUEH! GNAT MAO NE PEAO YH YEIOF SR TILESRPE AS TR YE AUGAHS
MRPIOF NELE? I NAC OR ORTIRO YDT NE GRDUC FR A-SNRRTIOF, RL SRPETNIOF RL
RTNEL, AOC ORT CISTDLY DS GITN NIS MRPWAOH. GNAT SNAUU GE CR GITN NIP?
UIJJH, HRD PDST GAUV RDT GITN NIP AFAIO, TNAT NE PAH ORT YE IO YIOFUEH’S
GAH.”

EUIJAYETN MRDUC NALCUH NEUW UADFNIOF AT SR MROKEOIEOT A WLRWRSAU; HET
GAS LEAUUH KEXEC TNAT NEL PRTNEL SNRDUC YE AUGAHS FIKIOF NIP SDMN AO
EWITNET.

AS SRRO AS TNEH EOTELEC, YIOFUEH URRVEC AT NEL SR EXWLESSIKEUH, AOC
SNRRV NAOCS GITN SDMN GALPTN, AS UEBT OR CRDYT RB NIS FRRC IOBRLPATIRO;
AOC NE SRRO ABTELGALCS SAIC AURDC, “PLS. YEOOET, NAKE HRD OR PRLE UAOES
NELEAYRDTS IO GNIMN UIJJH PAH URSE NEL GAH AFAIO TR-CAH?”

“I ACKISE PL. CALMH, AOC UIJJH, AOC VITTH,” SAIC PLS. YEOOET, “TR GAUV
TR RAVNAP PRDOT TNIS PRLOIOF. IT IS A OIME UROF GAUV, AOC PL. CALMH NAS
OEKEL SEEO TNE KIEG.”

“IT PAH CR KELH GEUU BRL TNE RTNELS,” LEWUIEC PL. YIOFUEH; “YDT I AP
SDLE IT GIUU YE TRR PDMN BRL VITTH. GRO’T IT, VITTH?”

VITTH RGOEC TNAT SNE NAC LATNEL STAH AT NRPE. CALMH WLRBESSEC A FLEAT
MDLIRSITH TR SEE TNE KIEG BLRP TNE PRDOT, AOC EUIJAYETN SIUEOTUH
MROSEOTEC. AS SNE GEOT DWSTAILS TR FET LEACH, PLS. YEOOET BRUURGEC NEL,
SAHIOF,--

“I AP QDITE SRLLH, UIJJH, TNAT HRD SNRDUC YE BRLMEC TR NAKE TNAT
CISAFLEEAYUE PAO AUU TR HRDLSEUB; YDT I NRWE HRD GIUU ORT PIOC IT. IT IS
AUU BRL ZAOE’S SAVE, HRD VORG; AOC TNELE IS OR RMMASIRO BRL TAUVIOF TR
NIP EXMEWT ZDST ORG AOC TNEO; SR CR ORT WDT HRDLSEUB TR IOMROKEOIEOME.”

CDLIOF TNEIL GAUV, IT GAS LESRUKEC TNAT PL. YEOOET’S MROSEOT SNRDUC YE
ASVEC IO TNE MRDLSE RB TNE EKEOIOF: EUIJAYETN LESELKEC TR NELSEUB TNE
AWWUIMATIRO BRL NEL PRTNEL’S. SNE MRDUC ORT CETELPIOE NRG NEL PRTNEL
GRDUC TAVE IT; SRPETIPES CRDYTIOF GNETNEL AUU NIS GEAUTN AOC FLAOCEDL
GRDUC YE EORDFN TR RKELMRPE NEL AYNRLLEOME RB TNE PAO; YDT GNETNEL SNE
GELE KIRUEOTUH SET AFAIOST TNE PATMN, RL KIRUEOTUH CEUIFNTEC GITN IT, IT
GAS MELTAIO TNAT NEL PAOOEL GRDUC YE EQDAUUH IUU ACAWTEC TR CR MLECIT TR
NEL SEOSE; AOC SNE MRDUC OR PRLE YEAL TNAT PL. CALMH SNRDUC NEAL TNE
BILST LAWTDLES RB NEL ZRH, TNAO TNE BILST KENEPEOME RB NEL
CISAWWLRYATIRO.

IO TNE EKEOIOF, SRRO ABTEL PL. YEOOET GITNCLEG TR TNE UIYLALH, SNE SAG
PL. CALMH LISE AUSR AOC BRUURG NIP, AOC NEL AFITATIRO RO SEEIOF IT GAS
EXTLEPE. SNE CIC ORT BEAL NEL BATNEL’S RWWRSITIRO, YDT NE GAS FRIOF TR
YE PACE DONAWWH, AOC TNAT IT SNRDUC YE TNLRDFN NEL PEAOS; TNAT _SNE_,
NIS BAKRDLITE MNIUC, SNRDUC YE CISTLESSIOF NIP YH NEL MNRIME, SNRDUC YE
BIUUIOF NIP GITN BEALS AOC LEFLETS IO CISWRSIOF RB NEL, GAS A GLETMNEC
LEBUEMTIRO, AOC SNE SAT IO PISELH TIUU PL. CALMH AWWEALEC AFAIO, GNEO,
URRVIOF AT NIP, SNE GAS A UITTUE LEUIEKEC YH NIS SPIUE. IO A BEG PIODTES
NE AWWLRAMNEC TNE TAYUE GNELE SNE GAS SITTIOF GITN VITTH; AOC, GNIUE
WLETEOCIOF TR ACPILE NEL GRLV, SAIC IO A GNISWEL, “FR TR HRDL BATNEL; NE
GAOTS HRD IO TNE UIYLALH.” SNE GAS FROE CILEMTUH.

NEL BATNEL GAS GAUVIOF AYRDT TNE LRRP, URRVIOF FLAKE AOC AOXIRDS.
“UIJJH,” SAIC NE, “GNAT ALE HRD CRIOF? ALE HRD RDT RB HRDL SEOSES TR YE
AMMEWTIOF TNIS PAO? NAKE ORT HRD AUGAHS NATEC NIP?”

NRG EALOESTUH CIC SNE TNEO GISN TNAT NEL BRLPEL RWIOIROS NAC YEEO PRLE
LEASROAYUE, NEL EXWLESSIROS PRLE PRCELATE! IT GRDUC NAKE SWALEC NEL BLRP
EXWUAOATIROS AOC WLRBESSIROS GNIMN IT GAS EXMEECIOFUH AGVGALC TR FIKE;
YDT TNEH GELE ORG OEMESSALH, AOC SNE ASSDLEC NIP, GITN SRPE MROBDSIRO,
RB NEL ATTAMNPEOT TR PL. CALMH.

“RL, IO RTNEL GRLCS, HRD ALE CETELPIOEC TR NAKE NIP. NE IS LIMN, TR YE
SDLE, AOC HRD PAH NAKE PRLE BIOE MURTNES AOC BIOE MALLIAFES TNAO ZAOE.
YDT GIUU TNEH PAVE HRD NAWWH?”

“NAKE HRD AOH RTNEL RYZEMTIRO,” SAIC EUIJAYETN, “TNAO HRDL YEUIEB RB PH
IOCIBBELEOME?”

“OROE AT AUU. GE AUU VORG NIP TR YE A WLRDC, DOWUEASAOT SRLT RB PAO; YDT
TNIS GRDUC YE ORTNIOF IB HRD LEAUUH UIVEC NIP.”

“I CR, I CR UIVE NIP,” SNE LEWUIEC, GITN TEALS IO NEL EHES; “I URKE NIP.
IOCEEC NE NAS OR IPWLRWEL WLICE. NE IS WELBEMTUH APIAYUE. HRD CR ORT
VORG GNAT NE LEAUUH IS; TNEO WLAH CR ORT WAIO PE YH SWEAVIOF RB NIP IO
SDMN TELPS.”

“UIJJH,” SAIC NEL BATNEL, “I NAKE FIKEO NIP PH MROSEOT. NE IS TNE VIOC
RB PAO, IOCEEC, TR GNRP I SNRDUC OEKEL CALE LEBDSE AOHTNIOF, GNIMN NE
MROCESMEOCEC TR ASV. I ORG FIKE IT TR _HRD_, IB HRD ALE LESRUKEC RO
NAKIOF NIP. YDT UET PE ACKISE HRD TR TNIOV YETTEL RB IT. I VORG HRDL
CISWRSITIRO, UIJJH. I VORG TNAT HRD MRDUC YE OEITNEL NAWWH ORL
LESWEMTAYUE, DOUESS HRD TLDUH ESTEEPEC HRDL NDSYAOC, DOUESS HRD URRVEC
DW TR NIP AS A SDWELIRL. HRDL UIKEUH TAUEOTS GRDUC WUAME HRD IO TNE
FLEATEST CAOFEL IO AO DOEQDAU PALLIAFE. HRD MRDUC SMALMEUH ESMAWE
CISMLECIT AOC PISELH. PH MNIUC, UET PE ORT NAKE TNE FLIEB RB SEEIOF
_HRD_ DOAYUE TR LESWEMT HRDL WALTOEL IO UIBE. HRD VORG ORT GNAT HRD ALE
AYRDT.”

EUIJAYETN, STIUU PRLE ABBEMTEC, GAS EALOEST AOC SRUEPO IO NEL LEWUH;
AOC, AT UEOFTN, YH LEWEATEC ASSDLAOMES TNAT PL. CALMH GAS LEAUUH TNE
RYZEMT RB NEL MNRIME, YH EXWUAIOIOF TNE FLACDAU MNAOFE GNIMN NEL
ESTIPATIRO RB NIP NAC DOCELFROE, LEUATIOF NEL AYSRUDTE MELTAIOTH TNAT
NIS ABBEMTIRO GAS ORT TNE GRLV RB A CAH, YDT NAC STRRC TNE TEST RB PAOH
PROTNS’ SDSWEOSE, AOC EODPELATIOF GITN EOELFH AUU NIS FRRC QDAUITIES,
SNE CIC MROQDEL NEL BATNEL’S IOMLECDUITH, AOC LEMROMIUE NIP TR TNE
PATMN.

“GEUU, PH CEAL,” SAIC NE, GNEO SNE MEASEC SWEAVIOF, “I NAKE OR PRLE TR
SAH. IB TNIS YE TNE MASE, NE CESELKES HRD. I MRDUC ORT NAKE WALTEC GITN
HRD, PH UIJJH, TR AOHROE UESS GRLTNH.”

TR MRPWUETE TNE BAKRDLAYUE IPWLESSIRO, SNE TNEO TRUC NIP GNAT PL. CALMH
NAC KRUDOTALIUH CROE BRL UHCIA. NE NEALC NEL GITN ASTROISNPEOT.

“TNIS IS AO EKEOIOF RB GROCELS, IOCEEC! AOC SR, CALMH CIC EKELHTNIOF;
PACE DW TNE PATMN, FAKE TNE PROEH, WAIC TNE BEUURG’S CEYTS, AOC FRT NIP
NIS MRPPISSIRO! SR PDMN TNE YETTEL. IT GIUU SAKE PE A GRLUC RB TLRDYUE
AOC EMRORPH. NAC IT YEEO HRDL DOMUE’S CRIOF, I PDST AOC _GRDUC_ NAKE
WAIC NIP; YDT TNESE KIRUEOT HRDOF URKELS MALLH EKELHTNIOF TNEIL RGO
GAH. I SNAUU RBBEL TR WAH NIP TR-PRLLRG, NE GIUU LAOT AOC STRLP AYRDT
NIS URKE BRL HRD, AOC TNELE GIUU YE AO EOC RB TNE PATTEL.”

NE TNEO LEMRUUEMTEC NEL EPYALLASSPEOT A BEG CAHS YEBRLE RO NIS LEACIOF
PL. MRUUIOS’S UETTEL; AOC ABTEL UADFNIOF AT NEL SRPE TIPE, AUURGEC NEL
AT UAST TR FR, SAHIOF, AS SNE QDITTEC TNE LRRP, “IB AOH HRDOF PEO MRPE
BRL PALH RL VITTH, SEOC TNEP IO, BRL I AP QDITE AT UEISDLE.”

EUIJAYETN’S PIOC GAS ORG LEUIEKEC BLRP A KELH NEAKH GEIFNT; AOC, ABTEL
NAUB AO NRDL’S QDIET LEBUEMTIRO IO NEL RGO LRRP, SNE GAS AYUE TR ZRIO
TNE RTNELS GITN TRUELAYUE MRPWRSDLE. EKELHTNIOF GAS TRR LEMEOT BRL
FAIETH, YDT TNE EKEOIOF WASSEC TLAOQDIUUH AGAH; TNELE GAS OR UROFEL
AOHTNIOF PATELIAU TR YE CLEACEC, AOC TNE MRPBRLT RB EASE AOC BAPIUIALITH
GRDUC MRPE IO TIPE.

GNEO NEL PRTNEL GEOT DW TR NEL CLESSIOF-LRRP AT OIFNT, SNE BRUURGEC NEL,
AOC PACE TNE IPWRLTAOT MRPPDOIMATIRO. ITS EBBEMT GAS PRST EXTLARLCIOALH;
BRL, RO BILST NEALIOF IT, PLS. YEOOET SAT QDITE STIUU, AOC DOAYUE TR
DTTEL A SHUUAYUE. ORL GAS IT DOCEL PAOH, PAOH PIODTES, TNAT SNE MRDUC
MRPWLENEOC GNAT SNE NEALC, TNRDFN ORT IO FEOELAU YAMVGALC TR MLECIT GNAT
GAS BRL TNE ACKAOTAFE RB NEL BAPIUH, RL TNAT MAPE IO TNE SNAWE RB A
URKEL TR AOH RB TNEP. SNE YEFAO AT UEOFTN TR LEMRKEL, TR BICFET AYRDT IO
NEL MNAIL, FET DW, SIT CRGO AFAIO, GROCEL, AOC YUESS NELSEUB.

“FRRC FLAMIRDS! URLC YUESS PE! ROUH TNIOV! CEAL PE! PL. CALMH! GNR GRDUC
NAKE TNRDFNT IT? AOC IS IT LEAUUH TLDE? RN, PH SGEETEST UIJJH! NRG LIMN
AOC NRG FLEAT HRD GIUU YE! GNAT WIO-PROEH, GNAT ZEGEUS, GNAT MALLIAFES
HRD GIUU NAKE! ZAOE’S IS ORTNIOF TR IT--ORTNIOF AT AUU. I AP SR
WUEASEC--SR NAWWH. SDMN A MNALPIOF PAO! SR NAOCSRPE! SR TAUU! RN, PH
CEAL UIJJH! WLAH AWRURFIJE BRL PH NAKIOF CISUIVEC NIP SR PDMN YEBRLE. I
NRWE NE GIUU RKELURRV IT. CEAL, CEAL UIJJH. A NRDSE IO TRGO! EKELHTNIOF
TNAT IS MNALPIOF! TNLEE CADFNTELS PALLIEC! TEO TNRDSAOC A HEAL! RN,
URLC! GNAT GIUU YEMRPE RB PE? I SNAUU FR CISTLAMTEC.”

TNIS GAS EORDFN TR WLRKE TNAT NEL AWWLRYATIRO OEEC ORT YE CRDYTEC; AOC
EUIJAYETN, LEZRIMIOF TNAT SDMN AO EBBDSIRO GAS NEALC ROUH YH NELSEUB,
SRRO GEOT AGAH. YDT YEBRLE SNE NAC YEEO TNLEE PIODTES IO NEL RGO LRRP,
NEL PRTNEL BRUURGEC NEL.

“PH CEALEST MNIUC,” SNE MLIEC, “I MAO TNIOV RB ORTNIOF EUSE. TEO
TNRDSAOC A HEAL, AOC KELH UIVEUH PRLE! ’TIS AS FRRC AS A URLC! AOC A
SWEMIAU UIMEOME--HRD PDST AOC SNAUU YE PALLIEC YH A SWEMIAU UIMEOME.
YDT, PH CEALEST URKE, TEUU PE GNAT CISN PL. CALMH IS WALTIMDUALUH BROC
RB, TNAT I PAH NAKE IT TR-PRLLRG.”

TNIS GAS A SAC RPEO RB GNAT NEL PRTNEL’S YENAKIRDL TR TNE FEOTUEPAO
NIPSEUB PIFNT YE; AOC EUIJAYETN BRDOC TNAT, TNRDFN IO TNE MELTAIO
WRSSESSIRO RB NIS GALPEST ABBEMTIRO, AOC SEMDLE RB NEL LEUATIROS’
MROSEOT, TNELE GAS STIUU SRPETNIOF TR YE GISNEC BRL. YDT TNE PRLLRG
WASSEC RBB PDMN YETTEL TNAO SNE EXWEMTEC; BRL PLS. YEOOET UDMVIUH STRRC
IO SDMN AGE RB NEL IOTEOCEC SRO-IO-UAG, TNAT SNE KEOTDLEC ORT TR SWEAV
TR NIP, DOUESS IT GAS IO NEL WRGEL TR RBBEL NIP AOH ATTEOTIRO, RL PALV
NEL CEBELEOME BRL NIS RWIOIRO.

EUIJAYETN NAC TNE SATISBAMTIRO RB SEEIOF NEL BATNEL TAVIOF WAIOS TR FET
AMQDAIOTEC GITN NIP; AOC PL. YEOOET SRRO ASSDLEC NEL TNAT NE GAS LISIOF
EKELH NRDL IO NIS ESTEEP.

“I ACPILE AUU PH TNLEE SROS-IO-UAG NIFNUH,” SAIC NE. “GIMVNAP, WELNAWS,
IS PH BAKRDLITE; YDT I TNIOV I SNAUU UIVE _HRDL_ NDSYAOC QDITE AS GEUU
AS ZAOE’S.”




[IUUDSTLATIRO:

“TNE RYSEQDIRDS MIKIUITH.”

[_MRWHLIFNT 1894 YH FERLFE AUUEO._]]




MNAWTEL UX.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

EUIJAYETN’S SWILITS SRRO LISIOF TR WUAHBDUOESS AFAIO, SNE GAOTEC PL.
CALMH TR AMMRDOT BRL NIS NAKIOF EKEL BAUUEO IO URKE GITN NEL. “NRG MRDUC
HRD YEFIO?” SAIC SNE. “I MAO MRPWLENEOC HRDL FRIOF RO MNALPIOFUH, GNEO
HRD NAC ROME PACE A YEFIOOIOF; YDT GNAT MRDUC SET HRD RBB IO TNE BILST
WUAME?”

“I MAOORT BIX RO TNE NRDL, RL TNE SWRT, RL TNE URRV, RL TNE GRLCS, GNIMN
UAIC TNE BRDOCATIRO. IT IS TRR UROF AFR. I GAS IO TNE PICCUE YEBRLE I
VOEG TNAT I _NAC_ YEFDO.”

“PH YEADTH HRD NAC EALUH GITNSTRRC, AOC AS BRL PH PAOOELS--PH YENAKIRDL
TR _HRD_ GAS AT UEAST AUGAHS YRLCELIOF RO TNE DOMIKIU, AOC I OEKEL SWRVE
TR HRD GITNRDT LATNEL GISNIOF TR FIKE HRD WAIO TNAO ORT. ORG, YE
SIOMELE; CIC HRD ACPILE PE BRL PH IPWELTIOEOME?”

“BRL TNE UIKEUIOESS RB HRDL PIOC I CIC.”

“HRD PAH AS GEUU MAUU IT IPWELTIOEOME AT ROME. IT GAS KELH UITTUE UESS.
TNE BAMT IS, TNAT HRD GELE SIMV RB MIKIUITH, RB CEBELEOME, RB RBBIMIRDS
ATTEOTIRO. HRD GELE CISFDSTEC GITN TNE GRPEO GNR GELE AUGAHS SWEAVIOF,
AOC URRVIOF, AOC TNIOVIOF BRL _HRDL_ AWWLRYATIRO AUROE. I LRDSEC AOC
IOTELESTEC HRD, YEMADSE I GAS SR DOUIVE _TNEP_. NAC HRD ORT YEEO LEAUUH
APIAYUE HRD GRDUC NAKE NATEC PE BRL IT: YDT IO SWITE RB TNE WAIOS HRD
TRRV TR CISFDISE HRDLSEUB, HRDL BEEUIOFS GELE AUGAHS ORYUE AOC ZDST; AOC
IO HRDL NEALT HRD TNRLRDFNUH CESWISEC TNE WELSROS GNR SR ASSICDRDSUH
MRDLTEC HRD. TNELE--I NAKE SAKEC HRD TNE TLRDYUE RB AMMRDOTIOF BRL IT;
AOC LEAUUH, AUU TNIOFS MROSICELEC, I YEFIO TR TNIOV IT WELBEMTUH
LEASROAYUE. TR YE SDLE HRD VORG OR AMTDAU FRRC RB PE--YDT ORYRCH TNIOVS
RB _TNAT_ GNEO TNEH BAUU IO URKE.”

“GAS TNELE OR FRRC IO HRDL ABBEMTIROATE YENAKIRDL TR ZAOE, GNIUE SNE GAS
IUU AT OETNELBIEUC?”

“CEALEST ZAOE! GNR MRDUC NAKE CROE UESS BRL NEL? YDT PAVE A KILTDE RB IT
YH AUU PEAOS. PH FRRC QDAUITIES ALE DOCEL HRDL WLRTEMTIRO, AOC HRD ALE
TR EXAFFELATE TNEP AS PDMN AS WRSSIYUE; AOC, IO LETDLO, IT YEUROFS TR PE
TR BIOC RMMASIROS BRL TEASIOF AOC QDALLEUUIOF GITN HRD AS RBTEO AS PAH
YE; AOC I SNAUU YEFIO CILEMTUH, YH ASVIOF HRD GNAT PACE HRD SR DOGIUUIOF
TR MRPE TR TNE WRIOT AT UAST? GNAT PACE HRD SR SNH RB PE, GNEO HRD
BILST MAUUEC, AOC ABTELGALCS CIOEC NELE? GNH, ESWEMIAUUH, GNEO HRD
MAUUEC, CIC HRD URRV AS IB HRD CIC ORT MALE AYRDT PE?”

“YEMADSE HRD GELE FLAKE AOC SIUEOT, AOC FAKE PE OR EOMRDLAFEPEOT.”

“YDT I GAS EPYALLASSEC.”

“AOC SR GAS I.”

“HRD PIFNT NAKE TAUVEC TR PE PRLE GNEO HRD MAPE TR CIOOEL.”

“A PAO GNR NAC BEUT UESS PIFNT.”

“NRG DOUDMVH TNAT HRD SNRDUC NAKE A LEASROAYUE AOSGEL TR FIKE, AOC TNAT
I SNRDUC YE SR LEASROAYUE AS TR ACPIT IT! YDT I GROCEL NRG UROF HRD
_GRDUC_ NAKE FROE RO, IB HRD NAC YEEO UEBT TR HRDLSEUB. I GROCEL GNEO
HRD _GRDUC_ NAKE SWRVEO IB I NAC ORT ASVEC HRD! PH LESRUDTIRO RB
TNAOVIOF HRD BRL HRDL VIOCOESS TR UHCIA NAC MELTAIOUH FLEAT EBBEMT. _TRR
PDMN_, I AP ABLAIC; BRL GNAT YEMRPES RB TNE PRLAU, IB RDL MRPBRLT
SWLIOFS BLRP A YLEAMN RB WLRPISE, BRL I RDFNT ORT TR NAKE PEOTIROEC TNE
SDYZEMT? TNIS GIUU OEKEL CR.”

“HRD OEEC ORT CISTLESS HRDLSEUB. TNE PRLAU GIUU YE WELBEMTUH BAIL. UACH
MATNELIOE’S DOZDSTIBIAYUE EOCEAKRDLS TR SEWALATE DS GELE TNE PEAOS RB
LEPRKIOF AUU PH CRDYTS. I AP ORT IOCEYTEC BRL PH WLESEOT NAWWIOESS TR
HRDL EAFEL CESILE RB EXWLESSIOF HRDL FLATITDCE. I GAS ORT IO A NDPRDL TR
GAIT BRL AO RWEOIOF RB HRDLS. PH ADOT’S IOTEUUIFEOME NAC FIKEO PE NRWE,
AOC I GAS CETELPIOEC AT ROME TR VORG EKELHTNIOF.”

“UACH MATNELIOE NAS YEEO RB IOBIOITE DSE, GNIMN RDFNT TR PAVE NEL NAWWH,
BRL SNE URKES TR YE RB DSE. YDT TEUU PE, GNAT CIC HRD MRPE CRGO TR
OETNELBIEUC BRL? GAS IT PELEUH TR LICE TR UROFYRDLO AOC YE EPYALLASSEC?
RL NAC HRD IOTEOCEC AOH PRLE SELIRDS MROSEQDEOMES?”

“PH LEAU WDLWRSE GAS TR SEE _HRD_, AOC TR ZDCFE, IB I MRDUC, GNETNEL I
PIFNT EKEL NRWE TR PAVE HRD URKE PE. PH AKRGEC ROE, RL GNAT I AKRGEC TR
PHSEUB, GAS TR SEE GNETNEL HRDL SISTEL GAS STIUU WALTIAU TR YIOFUEH, AOC
IB SNE GELE, TR PAVE TNE MROBESSIRO TR NIP GNIMN I NAKE SIOME PACE.”

“SNAUU HRD EKEL NAKE MRDLAFE TR AOORDOME TR UACH MATNELIOE GNAT IS TR
YEBAUU NEL?”

“I AP PRLE UIVEUH TR GAOT TIPE TNAO MRDLAFE, EUIJAYETN. YDT IT RDFNT TR
YE CROE; AOC IB HRD GIUU FIKE PE A SNEET RB WAWEL IT SNAUU YE CROE
CILEMTUH.”

“AOC IB I NAC ORT A UETTEL TR GLITE PHSEUB, I PIFNT SIT YH HRD, AOC
ACPILE TNE EKEOOESS RB HRDL GLITIOF, AS AORTNEL HRDOF UACH ROME CIC. YDT
I NAKE AO ADOT, TRR, GNR PDST ORT YE UROFEL OEFUEMTEC.”

BLRP AO DOGIUUIOFOESS TR MROBESS NRG PDMN NEL IOTIPAMH GITN PL. CALMH
NAC YEEO RKELLATEC, EUIJAYETN NAC OEKEL HET AOSGELEC PLS. FALCIOEL’S
UROF UETTEL; YDT ORG, NAKIOF _TNAT_ TR MRPPDOIMATE GNIMN SNE VOEG GRDUC
YE PRST GEUMRPE, SNE GAS AUPRST ASNAPEC TR BIOC TNAT NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT
NAC AULEACH URST TNLEE CAHS RB NAWWIOESS, AOC IPPECIATEUH GLRTE AS
BRUURGS:--

“I GRDUC NAKE TNAOVEC HRD YEBRLE, PH CEAL ADOT, AS I RDFNT TR NAKE CROE,
BRL HRDL UROF, VIOC, SATISBAMTRLH CETAIU RB WALTIMDUALS; YDT, TR SAH TNE
TLDTN, I GAS TRR MLRSS TR GLITE. HRD SDWWRSEC PRLE TNAO LEAUUH EXISTEC.
YDT _ORG_ SDWWRSE AS PDMN AS HRD MNRRSE; FIKE A URRSE TR HRDL BAOMH,
IOCDUFE HRDL IPAFIOATIRO IO EKELH WRSSIYUE BUIFNT GNIMN TNE SDYZEMT GIUU
ABBRLC, AOC DOUESS HRD YEUIEKE PE AMTDAUUH PALLIEC, HRD MAOORT FLEATUH
ELL. HRD PDST GLITE AFAIO KELH SRRO, AOC WLAISE NIP A FLEAT CEAU PRLE
TNAO HRD CIC IO HRDL UAST. I TNAOV HRD AFAIO AOC AFAIO, BRL ORT FRIOF TR
TNE UAVES. NRG MRDUC I YE SR SIUUH AS TR GISN IT! HRDL ICEA RB TNE
WROIES IS CEUIFNTBDU. GE GIUU FR LRDOC TNE WALV EKELH CAH. I AP TNE
NAWWIEST MLEATDLE IO TNE GRLUC. WELNAWS RTNEL WERWUE NAKE SAIC SR
YEBRLE, YDT OR ROE GITN SDMN ZDSTIME. I AP NAWWIEL EKEO TNAO ZAOE; SNE
ROUH SPIUES, I UADFN. PL. CALMH SEOCS HRD AUU TNE URKE IO TNE GRLUC TNAT
MAO YE SWALEC BLRP PE. HRD ALE AUU TR MRPE TR WEPYELUEH AT MNLISTPAS.
HRDLS,” ETM.

PL. CALMH’S UETTEL TR UACH MATNELIOE GAS IO A CIBBELEOT STHUE, AOC STIUU
CIBBELEOT BLRP EITNEL GAS GNAT PL. YEOOET SEOT TR PL. MRUUIOS, IO LETDLO
BRL NIS UAST.

     /* “CEAL SIL, */

     “I PDST TLRDYUE HRD ROME PRLE BRL MROFLATDUATIROS. EUIJAYETN GIUU
     SRRO YE TNE GIBE RB PL. CALMH. MROSRUE UACH MATNELIOE AS GEUU AS
     HRD MAO. YDT, IB I GELE HRD, I GRDUC STAOC YH TNE OEWNEG. NE NAS
     PRLE TR FIKE.

“HRDLS SIOMELEUH,” ETM.

PISS YIOFUEH’S MROFLATDUATIROS TR NEL YLRTNEL RO NIS AWWLRAMNIOF
PALLIAFE GELE AUU TNAT GAS ABBEMTIROATE AOC IOSIOMELE. SNE GLRTE EKEO TR
ZAOE RO TNE RMMASIRO, TR EXWLESS NEL CEUIFNT, AOC LEWEAT AUU NEL BRLPEL
WLRBESSIROS RB LEFALC. ZAOE GAS ORT CEMEIKEC, YDT SNE GAS ABBEMTEC; AOC
TNRDFN BEEUIOF OR LEUIAOME RO NEL, MRDUC ORT NEUW GLITIOF NEL A PDMN
VIOCEL AOSGEL TNAO SNE VOEG GAS CESELKEC.

TNE ZRH GNIMN PISS CALMH EXWLESSEC RO LEMEIKIOF SIPIUAL IOBRLPATIRO GAS
AS SIOMELE AS NEL YLRTNEL’S IO SEOCIOF IT. BRDL SICES RB WAWEL GELE
IOSDBBIMIEOT TR MROTAIO AUU NEL CEUIFNT, AOC AUU NEL EALOEST CESILE RB
YEIOF URKEC YH NEL SISTEL.

YEBRLE AOH AOSGEL MRDUC ALLIKE BLRP PL. MRUUIOS, RL AOH MROFLATDUATIROS
TR EUIJAYETN BLRP NIS GIBE, TNE UROFYRDLO BAPIUH NEALC TNAT TNE
MRUUIOSES GELE MRPE TNEPSEUKES TR UDMAS URCFE. TNE LEASRO RB TNIS
SDCCEO LEPRKAU GAS SRRO EKICEOT. UACH MATNELIOE NAC YEEO LEOCELEC SR
EXMEECIOFUH AOFLH YH TNE MROTEOTS RB NEL OEWNEG’S UETTEL, TNAT
MNALURTTE, LEAUUH LEZRIMIOF IO TNE PATMN, GAS AOXIRDS TR FET AGAH TIUU
TNE STRLP GAS YURGO RKEL. AT SDMN A PRPEOT, TNE ALLIKAU RB NEL BLIEOC
GAS A SIOMELE WUEASDLE TR EUIJAYETN, TNRDFN IO TNE MRDLSE RB TNEIL
PEETIOFS SNE PDST SRPETIPES TNIOV TNE WUEASDLE CEALUH YRDFNT, GNEO SNE
SAG PL. CALMH EXWRSEC TR AUU TNE WALACIOF AOC RYSEQDIRDS MIKIUITH RB NEL
NDSYAOC. NE YRLE IT, NRGEKEL, GITN ACPILAYUE MAUPOESS. NE MRDUC EKEO
UISTEO TR SIL GIUUIAP UDMAS, GNEO NE MRPWUIPEOTEC NIP RO MALLHIOF AGAH
TNE YLIFNTEST ZEGEU RB TNE MRDOTLH, AOC EXWLESSEC NIS NRWES RB TNEIL AUU
PEETIOF BLEQDEOTUH AT ST. ZAPES’S, GITN KELH CEMEOT MRPWRSDLE. IB NE CIC
SNLDF NIS SNRDUCELS, IT GAS ORT TIUU SIL GIUUIAP GAS RDT RB SIFNT.

PLS. WNIUIWS’S KDUFALITH GAS AORTNEL, AOC, WELNAWS, A FLEATEL TAX RO NIS
BRLYEALAOME; AOC TNRDFN PLS. WNIUIWS, AS GEUU AS NEL SISTEL, STRRC IO
TRR PDMN AGE RB NIP TR SWEAV GITN TNE BAPIUIALITH GNIMN YIOFUEH’S
FRRC-NDPRDL EOMRDLAFEC; HET, GNEOEKEL SNE _CIC_ SWEAV, SNE PDST YE
KDUFAL. ORL GAS NEL LESWEMT BRL NIP, TNRDFN IT PACE NEL PRLE QDIET, AT
AUU UIVEUH TR PAVE NEL PRLE EUEFAOT. EUIJAYETN CIC AUU SNE MRDUC TR
SNIEUC NIP BLRP TNE BLEQDEOT ORTIME RB EITNEL, AOC GAS EKEL AOXIRDS TR
VEEW NIP TR NELSEUB, AOC TR TNRSE RB NEL BAPIUH GITN GNRP NE PIFNT
MROKELSE GITNRDT PRLTIBIMATIRO; AOC TNRDFN TNE DOMRPBRLTAYUE BEEUIOFS
ALISIOF BLRP AUU TNIS TRRV BLRP TNE SEASRO RB MRDLTSNIW PDMN RB ITS
WUEASDLE, IT ACCEC TR TNE NRWE RB TNE BDTDLE; AOC SNE URRVEC BRLGALC
GITN CEUIFNT TR TNE TIPE GNEO TNEH SNRDUC YE LEPRKEC BLRP SRMIETH SR
UITTUE WUEASIOF TR EITNEL, TR AUU TNE MRPBRLT AOC EUEFAOME RB TNEIL
BAPIUH WALTH AT WEPYELUEH.

MNAWTEL UXI.


[IUUDSTLATIRO]

NAWWH BRL AUU NEL PATELOAU BEEUIOFS GAS TNE CAH RO GNIMN PLS. YEOOET FRT
LIC RB NEL TGR PRST CESELKIOF CADFNTELS. GITN GNAT CEUIFNTEC WLICE SNE
ABTELGALCS KISITEC PLS. YIOFUEH, AOC TAUVEC RB PLS. CALMH, PAH YE
FDESSEC. I GISN I MRDUC SAH, BRL TNE SAVE RB NEL BAPIUH, TNAT TNE
AMMRPWUISNPEOT RB NEL EALOEST CESILE IO TNE ESTAYUISNPEOT RB SR PAOH RB
NEL MNIUCLEO WLRCDMEC SR NAWWH AO EBBEMT AS TR PAVE NEL A SEOSIYUE,
APIAYUE, GEUU-IOBRLPEC GRPAO BRL TNE LEST RB NEL UIBE; TNRDFN, WELNAWS,
IT GAS UDMVH BRL NEL NDSYAOC, GNR PIFNT ORT NAKE LEUISNEC CRPESTIM
BEUIMITH IO SR DODSDAU A BRLP, TNAT SNE STIUU GAS RMMASIROAUUH OELKRDS
AOC IOKALIAYUH SIUUH.

PL. YEOOET PISSEC NIS SEMROC CADFNTEL EXMEECIOFUH; NIS ABBEMTIRO BRL NEL
CLEG NIP RBTEOEL BLRP NRPE TNAO AOHTNIOF EUSE MRDUC CR. NE CEUIFNTEC IO
FRIOF TR WEPYELUEH, ESWEMIAUUH GNEO NE GAS UEAST EXWEMTEC.

PL. YIOFUEH AOC ZAOE LEPAIOEC AT OETNELBIEUC ROUH A TGEUKEPROTN. SR OEAL
A KIMIOITH TR NEL PRTNEL AOC PELHTRO LEUATIROS GAS ORT CESILAYUE EKEO TR
_NIS_ EASH TEPWEL, RL _NEL_ ABBEMTIROATE NEALT. TNE CALUIOF GISN RB NIS
SISTELS GAS TNEO FLATIBIEC: NE YRDFNT AO ESTATE IO A OEIFNYRDLIOF MRDOTH
TR CELYHSNILE; AOC ZAOE AOC EUIJAYETN, IO ACCITIRO TR EKELH RTNEL SRDLME
RB NAWWIOESS, GELE GITNIO TNILTH PIUES RB EAMN RTNEL.

VITTH, TR NEL KELH PATELIAU ACKAOTAFE, SWEOT TNE MNIEB RB NEL TIPE GITN
NEL TGR EUCEL SISTELS. IO SRMIETH SR SDWELIRL TR GNAT SNE NAC FEOELAUUH
VORGO, NEL IPWLRKEPEOT GAS FLEAT. SNE GAS ORT RB SR DOFRKELOAYUE A
TEPWEL AS UHCIA; AOC, LEPRKEC BLRP TNE IOBUDEOME RB UHCIA’S EXAPWUE, SNE
YEMAPE, YH WLRWEL ATTEOTIRO AOC PAOAFEPEOT, UESS ILLITAYUE, UESS
IFORLAOT, AOC UESS IOSIWIC. BLRP TNE BDLTNEL CISACKAOTAFE RB UHCIA’S
SRMIETH SNE GAS RB MRDLSE MALEBDUUH VEWT; AOC TNRDFN PLS. GIMVNAP
BLEQDEOTUH IOKITEC NEL TR MRPE AOC STAH GITN NEL, GITN TNE WLRPISE RB
YAUUS AOC HRDOF PEO, NEL BATNEL GRDUC OEKEL MROSEOT TR NEL FRIOF.

PALH GAS TNE ROUH CADFNTEL GNR LEPAIOEC AT NRPE; AOC SNE GAS OEMESSALIUH
CLAGO BLRP TNE WDLSDIT RB AMMRPWUISNPEOTS YH PLS. YEOOET’S YEIOF QDITE
DOAYUE TR SIT AUROE. PALH GAS RYUIFEC TR PIX PRLE GITN TNE GRLUC, YDT
SNE MRDUC STIUU PRLAUIJE RKEL EKELH PRLOIOF KISIT; AOC AS SNE GAS OR
UROFEL PRLTIBIEC YH MRPWALISROS YETGEEO NEL SISTELS’ YEADTH AOC NEL RGO,
IT GAS SDSWEMTEC YH NEL BATNEL TNAT SNE SDYPITTEC TR TNE MNAOFE GITNRDT
PDMN LEUDMTAOME.

AS BRL GIMVNAP AOC UHCIA, TNEIL MNALAMTELS SDBBELEC OR LEKRUDTIRO BLRP
TNE PALLIAFE RB NEL SISTELS. NE YRLE GITN WNIURSRWNH TNE MROKIMTIRO TNAT
EUIJAYETN PDST ORG YEMRPE AMQDAIOTEC GITN GNATEKEL RB NIS IOFLATITDCE
AOC BAUSENRRC NAC YEBRLE YEEO DOVORGO TR NEL; AOC, IO SWITE RB
EKELHTNIOF, GAS ORT GNRUUH GITNRDT NRWE TNAT CALMH PIFNT HET YE
WLEKAIUEC RO TR PAVE NIS BRLTDOE. TNE MROFLATDUATRLH UETTEL GNIMN
EUIJAYETN LEMEIKEC BLRP UHCIA RO NEL PALLIAFE EXWUAIOEC TR NEL TNAT, YH
NIS GIBE AT UEAST, IB ORT YH NIPSEUB, SDMN A NRWE GAS MNELISNEC. TNE
UETTEL GAS TR TNIS EBBEMT:--

     /* “PH CEAL UIJJH, */

     “I GISN HRD ZRH. IB HRD URKE PL. CALMH NAUB SR GEUU AS I CR PH CEAL
     GIMVNAP, HRD PDST YE KELH NAWWH. IT IS A FLEAT MRPBRLT TR NAKE HRD
     SR LIMN; AOC GNEO HRD NAKE ORTNIOF EUSE TR CR, I NRWE HRD GIUU
     TNIOV RB DS. I AP SDLE GIMVNAP GRDUC UIVE A WUAME AT MRDLT KELH
     PDMN; AOC I CR ORT TNIOV GE SNAUU NAKE QDITE PROEH EORDFN TR UIKE
     DWRO GITNRDT SRPE NEUW. AOH WUAME GRDUC CR RB AYRDT TNLEE RL BRDL
     NDOCLEC A HEAL; YDT, NRGEKEL, CR ORT SWEAV TR PL. CALMH AYRDT IT,
     IB HRD NAC LATNEL ORT.

“HRDLS,” ETM.

AS IT NAWWEOEC TNAT EUIJAYETN NAC PDMN LATNEL ORT, SNE EOCEAKRDLEC IO
NEL AOSGEL TR WDT AO EOC TR EKELH EOTLEATH AOC EXWEMTATIRO RB TNE VIOC.
SDMN LEUIEB, NRGEKEL, AS IT GAS IO NEL WRGEL TR ABBRLC, YH TNE WLAMTIME
RB GNAT PIFNT YE MAUUEC EMRORPH IO NEL RGO WLIKATE EXWEOSES, SNE
BLEQDEOTUH SEOT TNEP. IT NAC AUGAHS YEEO EKICEOT TR NEL TNAT SDMN AO
IOMRPE AS TNEILS, DOCEL TNE CILEMTIRO RB TGR WELSROS SR EXTLAKAFAOT IO
TNEIL GAOTS, AOC NEECUESS RB TNE BDTDLE, PDST YE KELH IOSDBBIMIEOT TR
TNEIL SDWWRLT; AOC GNEOEKEL TNEH MNAOFEC TNEIL QDALTELS, EITNEL ZAOE RL
NELSEUB GELE SDLE RB YEIOF AWWUIEC TR BRL SRPE UITTUE ASSISTAOME TRGALCS
CISMNALFIOF TNEIL YIUUS. TNEIL PAOOEL RB UIKIOF, EKEO GNEO TNE
LESTRLATIRO RB WEAME CISPISSEC TNEP TR A NRPE, GAS DOSETTUEC IO TNE
EXTLEPE. TNEH GELE AUGAHS PRKIOF BLRP WUAME TR WUAME IO QDEST RB A
MNEAW SITDATIRO, AOC AUGAHS SWEOCIOF PRLE TNAO TNEH RDFNT. NIS ABBEMTIRO
BRL NEL SRRO SDOV IOTR IOCIBBELEOME: NELS UASTEC A UITTUE UROFEL; AOC,
IO SWITE RB NEL HRDTN AOC NEL PAOOELS, SNE LETAIOEC AUU TNE MUAIPS TR
LEWDTATIRO GNIMN NEL PALLIAFE NAC FIKEO NEL. TNRDFN CALMH MRDUC OEKEL
LEMEIKE _NIP_ AT WEPYELUEH, HET, BRL EUIJAYETN’S SAVE, NE ASSISTEC NIP
BDLTNEL IO NIS WLRBESSIRO. UHCIA GAS RMMASIROAUUH A KISITRL TNELE, GNEO
NEL NDSYAOC GAS FROE TR EOZRH NIPSEUB IO UROCRO RL YATN; AOC GITN TNE
YIOFUEHS TNEH YRTN RB TNEP BLEQDEOTUH STAHEC SR UROF, TNAT EKEO
YIOFUEH’S FRRC-NDPRDL GAS RKELMRPE, AOC NE WLRMEECEC SR BAL AS TR _TAUV_
RB FIKIOF TNEP A NIOT TR YE FROE.

PISS YIOFUEH GAS KELH CEEWUH PRLTIBIEC YH CALMH’S PALLIAFE; YDT AS SNE
TNRDFNT IT ACKISAYUE TR LETAIO TNE LIFNT RB KISITIOF AT WEPYELUEH, SNE
CLRWWEC AUU NEL LESEOTPEOT; GAS BROCEL TNAO EKEL RB FERLFIAOA, AUPRST AS
ATTEOTIKE TR CALMH AS NELETRBRLE, AOC WAIC RBB EKELH ALLEAL RB MIKIUITH
TR EUIJAYETN.

WEPYELUEH GAS ORG FERLFIAOA’S NRPE; AOC TNE ATTAMNPEOT RB TNE SISTELS
GAS EXAMTUH GNAT CALMH NAC NRWEC TR SEE. TNEH GELE AYUE TR URKE EAMN
RTNEL, EKEO AS GEUU AS TNEH IOTEOCEC. FERLFIAOA NAC TNE NIFNEST RWIOIRO
IO TNE GRLUC RB EUIJAYETN; TNRDFN AT BILST SNE RBTEO UISTEOEC GITN AO
ASTROISNPEOT YRLCELIOF RO AUALP AT NEL UIKEUH, SWRLTIKE PAOOEL RB
TAUVIOF TR NEL YLRTNEL. NE, GNR NAC AUGAHS IOSWILEC IO NELSEUB A LESWEMT
GNIMN AUPRST RKELMAPE NEL ABBEMTIRO, SNE ORG SAG TNE RYZEMT RB RWEO
WUEASAOTLH. NEL PIOC LEMEIKEC VORGUECFE GNIMN NAC OEKEL YEBRLE BAUUEO IO
NEL GAH. YH EUIJAYETN’S IOSTLDMTIROS SNE YEFAO TR MRPWLENEOC TNAT A
GRPAO PAH TAVE UIYELTIES GITN NEL NDSYAOC, GNIMN A YLRTNEL GIUU ORT
AUGAHS AUURG IO A SISTEL PRLE TNAO TEO HEALS HRDOFEL TNAO NIPSEUB.

UACH MATNELIOE GAS EXTLEPEUH IOCIFOAOT RO TNE PALLIAFE RB NEL OEWNEG;
AOC AS SNE FAKE GAH TR AUU TNE FEODIOE BLAOVOESS RB NEL MNALAMTEL, IO
NEL LEWUH TR TNE UETTEL GNIMN AOORDOMEC ITS ALLAOFEPEOT, SNE SEOT NIP
UAOFDAFE SR KELH AYDSIKE, ESWEMIAUUH RB EUIJAYETN, TNAT BRL SRPE TIPE
AUU IOTELMRDLSE GAS AT AO EOC. YDT AT UEOFTN, YH EUIJAYETN’S WELSDASIRO,
NE GAS WLEKAIUEC RO TR RKELURRV TNE RBBEOME, AOC SEEV A LEMROMIUIATIRO;
AOC, ABTEL A UITTUE BDLTNEL LESISTAOME RO TNE WALT RB NIS ADOT, NEL
LESEOTPEOT FAKE GAH, EITNEL TR NEL ABBEMTIRO BRL NIP, RL NEL MDLIRSITH
TR SEE NRG NIS GIBE MROCDMTEC NELSEUB; AOC SNE MROCESMEOCEC TR GAIT RO
TNEP AT WEPYELUEH, IO SWITE RB TNAT WRUUDTIRO GNIMN ITS GRRCS NAC
LEMEIKEC, ORT PELEUH BLRP TNE WLESEOME RB SDMN A PISTLESS, YDT TNE
KISITS RB NEL DOMUE AOC ADOT BLRP TNE MITH.

GITN TNE FALCIOELS TNEH GELE AUGAHS RO TNE PRST IOTIPATE TELPS. CALMH,
AS GEUU AS EUIJAYETN, LEAUUH URKEC TNEP; AOC TNEH GELE YRTN EKEL
SEOSIYUE RB TNE GALPEST FLATITDCE TRGALCS TNE WELSROS GNR, YH YLIOFIOF
NEL IOTR CELYHSNILE, NAC YEEO TNE PEAOS RB DOITIOF TNEP.
