            *** EOC RB TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF EYRRV WLICE AOC WLEZDCIME ***
        

    

DWCATEC ECITIROS GIUU LEWUAME TNE WLEKIRDS ROE—TNE RUC ECITIROS GIUU
YE LEOAPEC.

MLEATIOF TNE GRLVS BLRP WLIOT ECITIROS ORT WLRTEMTEC YH D.S. MRWHLIFNT
UAG PEAOS TNAT OR ROE RGOS A DOITEC STATES MRWHLIFNT IO TNESE GRLVS,
SR TNE BRDOCATIRO (AOC HRD!) MAO MRWH AOC CISTLIYDTE IT IO TNE DOITEC
STATES GITNRDT WELPISSIRO AOC GITNRDT WAHIOF MRWHLIFNT
LRHAUTIES. SWEMIAU LDUES, SET BRLTN IO TNE FEOELAU TELPS RB DSE WALT
RB TNIS UIMEOSE, AWWUH TR MRWHIOF AOC CISTLIYDTIOF WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLVS TR WLRTEMT TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™
MROMEWT AOC TLACEPALV. WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF IS A LEFISTELEC TLACEPALV,
AOC PAH ORT YE DSEC IB HRD MNALFE BRL AO EYRRV, EXMEWT YH BRUURGIOF
TNE TELPS RB TNE TLACEPALV UIMEOSE, IOMUDCIOF WAHIOF LRHAUTIES BRL DSE
RB TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF TLACEPALV. IB HRD CR ORT MNALFE AOHTNIOF BRL
MRWIES RB TNIS EYRRV, MRPWUHIOF GITN TNE TLACEPALV UIMEOSE IS KELH
EASH. HRD PAH DSE TNIS EYRRV BRL OEALUH AOH WDLWRSE SDMN AS MLEATIRO
RB CELIKATIKE GRLVS, LEWRLTS, WELBRLPAOMES AOC LESEALMN. WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF EYRRVS PAH YE PRCIBIEC AOC WLIOTEC AOC FIKEO AGAH—HRD PAH
CR WLAMTIMAUUH AOHTNIOF IO TNE DOITEC STATES GITN EYRRVS ORT WLRTEMTEC
YH D.S. MRWHLIFNT UAG. LECISTLIYDTIRO IS SDYZEMT TR TNE TLACEPALV
UIMEOSE, ESWEMIAUUH MRPPELMIAU LECISTLIYDTIRO.


STALT: BDUU UIMEOSE

TNE BDUU WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF UIMEOSE

WUEASE LEAC TNIS YEBRLE HRD CISTLIYDTE RL DSE TNIS GRLV

TR WLRTEMT TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ PISSIRO RB WLRPRTIOF TNE BLEE
CISTLIYDTIRO RB EUEMTLROIM GRLVS, YH DSIOF RL CISTLIYDTIOF TNIS GRLV
(RL AOH RTNEL GRLV ASSRMIATEC IO AOH GAH GITN TNE WNLASE “WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF”), HRD AFLEE TR MRPWUH GITN AUU TNE TELPS RB TNE BDUU
WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ UIMEOSE AKAIUAYUE GITN TNIS BIUE RL ROUIOE AT
GGG.FDTEOYELF.RLF/UIMEOSE.

SEMTIRO 1. FEOELAU TELPS RB DSE AOC LECISTLIYDTIOF WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™
EUEMTLROIM GRLVS

1.A. YH LEACIOF RL DSIOF AOH WALT RB TNIS WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™
EUEMTLROIM GRLV, HRD IOCIMATE TNAT HRD NAKE LEAC, DOCELSTAOC, AFLEE TR
AOC AMMEWT AUU TNE TELPS RB TNIS UIMEOSE AOC IOTEUUEMTDAU WLRWELTH
(TLACEPALV/MRWHLIFNT) AFLEEPEOT. IB HRD CR ORT AFLEE TR AYICE YH AUU
TNE TELPS RB TNIS AFLEEPEOT, HRD PDST MEASE DSIOF AOC LETDLO RL
CESTLRH AUU MRWIES RB WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLVS IO HRDL
WRSSESSIRO. IB HRD WAIC A BEE BRL RYTAIOIOF A MRWH RB RL AMMESS TR A
WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLV AOC HRD CR ORT AFLEE TR YE YRDOC
YH TNE TELPS RB TNIS AFLEEPEOT, HRD PAH RYTAIO A LEBDOC BLRP TNE WELSRO
RL EOTITH TR GNRP HRD WAIC TNE BEE AS SET BRLTN IO WALAFLAWN 1.E.8.

1.Y. “WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF” IS A LEFISTELEC TLACEPALV. IT PAH ROUH YE
DSEC RO RL ASSRMIATEC IO AOH GAH GITN AO EUEMTLROIM GRLV YH WERWUE GNR
AFLEE TR YE YRDOC YH TNE TELPS RB TNIS AFLEEPEOT. TNELE ALE A BEG
TNIOFS TNAT HRD MAO CR GITN PRST WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLVS
EKEO GITNRDT MRPWUHIOF GITN TNE BDUU TELPS RB TNIS AFLEEPEOT. SEE
WALAFLAWN 1.M YEURG. TNELE ALE A URT RB TNIOFS HRD MAO CR GITN WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLVS IB HRD BRUURG TNE TELPS RB TNIS
AFLEEPEOT AOC NEUW WLESELKE BLEE BDTDLE AMMESS TR WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™
EUEMTLROIM GRLVS. SEE WALAFLAWN 1.E YEURG.

1.M. TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF UITELALH ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO (“TNE
BRDOCATIRO” RL WFUAB), RGOS A MRPWIUATIRO MRWHLIFNT IO TNE MRUUEMTIRO
RB WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLVS. OEALUH AUU TNE IOCIKICDAU
GRLVS IO TNE MRUUEMTIRO ALE IO TNE WDYUIM CRPAIO IO TNE DOITEC
STATES. IB AO IOCIKICDAU GRLV IS DOWLRTEMTEC YH MRWHLIFNT UAG IO TNE
DOITEC STATES AOC HRD ALE URMATEC IO TNE DOITEC STATES, GE CR ORT
MUAIP A LIFNT TR WLEKEOT HRD BLRP MRWHIOF, CISTLIYDTIOF, WELBRLPIOF,
CISWUAHIOF RL MLEATIOF CELIKATIKE GRLVS YASEC RO TNE GRLV AS UROF AS
AUU LEBELEOMES TR WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF ALE LEPRKEC. RB MRDLSE, GE NRWE
TNAT HRD GIUU SDWWRLT TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ PISSIRO RB WLRPRTIOF
BLEE AMMESS TR EUEMTLROIM GRLVS YH BLEEUH SNALIOF WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™
GRLVS IO MRPWUIAOME GITN TNE TELPS RB TNIS AFLEEPEOT BRL VEEWIOF TNE
WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ OAPE ASSRMIATEC GITN TNE GRLV. HRD MAO EASIUH
MRPWUH GITN TNE TELPS RB TNIS AFLEEPEOT YH VEEWIOF TNIS GRLV IO TNE
SAPE BRLPAT GITN ITS ATTAMNEC BDUU WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ UIMEOSE GNEO
HRD SNALE IT GITNRDT MNALFE GITN RTNELS.

1.C. TNE MRWHLIFNT UAGS RB TNE WUAME GNELE HRD ALE URMATEC AUSR FRKELO
GNAT HRD MAO CR GITN TNIS GRLV. MRWHLIFNT UAGS IO PRST MRDOTLIES ALE
IO A MROSTAOT STATE RB MNAOFE. IB HRD ALE RDTSICE TNE DOITEC STATES,
MNEMV TNE UAGS RB HRDL MRDOTLH IO ACCITIRO TR TNE TELPS RB TNIS
AFLEEPEOT YEBRLE CRGOURACIOF, MRWHIOF, CISWUAHIOF, WELBRLPIOF,
CISTLIYDTIOF RL MLEATIOF CELIKATIKE GRLVS YASEC RO TNIS GRLV RL AOH
RTNEL WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ GRLV. TNE BRDOCATIRO PAVES OR
LEWLESEOTATIROS MROMELOIOF TNE MRWHLIFNT STATDS RB AOH GRLV IO AOH
MRDOTLH RTNEL TNAO TNE DOITEC STATES.

1.E. DOUESS HRD NAKE LEPRKEC AUU LEBELEOMES TR WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF:

1.E.1. TNE BRUURGIOF SEOTEOME, GITN AMTIKE UIOVS TR, RL RTNEL
IPPECIATE AMMESS TR, TNE BDUU WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ UIMEOSE PDST AWWEAL
WLRPIOEOTUH GNEOEKEL AOH MRWH RB A WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ GRLV (AOH GRLV
RO GNIMN TNE WNLASE “WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF” AWWEALS, RL GITN GNIMN TNE
WNLASE “WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF” IS ASSRMIATEC) IS AMMESSEC, CISWUAHEC,
WELBRLPEC, KIEGEC, MRWIEC RL CISTLIYDTEC:

    TNIS EYRRV IS BRL TNE DSE RB AOHROE AOHGNELE IO TNE DOITEC STATES AOC PRST
    RTNEL WALTS RB TNE GRLUC AT OR MRST AOC GITN AUPRST OR LESTLIMTIROS
    GNATSREKEL. HRD PAH MRWH IT, FIKE IT AGAH RL LE-DSE IT DOCEL TNE TELPS
    RB TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF UIMEOSE IOMUDCEC GITN TNIS EYRRV RL ROUIOE
    AT GGG.FDTEOYELF.RLF. IB HRD
    ALE ORT URMATEC IO TNE DOITEC STATES, HRD GIUU NAKE TR MNEMV TNE UAGS
    RB TNE MRDOTLH GNELE HRD ALE URMATEC YEBRLE DSIOF TNIS EYRRV.
  
1.E.2. IB AO IOCIKICDAU WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLV IS
CELIKEC BLRP TEXTS ORT WLRTEMTEC YH D.S. MRWHLIFNT UAG (CRES ORT
MROTAIO A ORTIME IOCIMATIOF TNAT IT IS WRSTEC GITN WELPISSIRO RB TNE
MRWHLIFNT NRUCEL), TNE GRLV MAO YE MRWIEC AOC CISTLIYDTEC TR AOHROE IO
TNE DOITEC STATES GITNRDT WAHIOF AOH BEES RL MNALFES. IB HRD ALE
LECISTLIYDTIOF RL WLRKICIOF AMMESS TR A GRLV GITN TNE WNLASE “WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF” ASSRMIATEC GITN RL AWWEALIOF RO TNE GRLV, HRD PDST MRPWUH
EITNEL GITN TNE LEQDILEPEOTS RB WALAFLAWNS 1.E.1 TNLRDFN 1.E.7 RL
RYTAIO WELPISSIRO BRL TNE DSE RB TNE GRLV AOC TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™
TLACEPALV AS SET BRLTN IO WALAFLAWNS 1.E.8 RL 1.E.9.

1.E.3. IB AO IOCIKICDAU WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLV IS WRSTEC
GITN TNE WELPISSIRO RB TNE MRWHLIFNT NRUCEL, HRDL DSE AOC CISTLIYDTIRO
PDST MRPWUH GITN YRTN WALAFLAWNS 1.E.1 TNLRDFN 1.E.7 AOC AOH
ACCITIROAU TELPS IPWRSEC YH TNE MRWHLIFNT NRUCEL. ACCITIROAU TELPS
GIUU YE UIOVEC TR TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ UIMEOSE BRL AUU GRLVS
WRSTEC GITN TNE WELPISSIRO RB TNE MRWHLIFNT NRUCEL BRDOC AT TNE
YEFIOOIOF RB TNIS GRLV.

1.E.4. CR ORT DOUIOV RL CETAMN RL LEPRKE TNE BDUU WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™
UIMEOSE TELPS BLRP TNIS GRLV, RL AOH BIUES MROTAIOIOF A WALT RB TNIS
GRLV RL AOH RTNEL GRLV ASSRMIATEC GITN WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™.

1.E.5. CR ORT MRWH, CISWUAH, WELBRLP, CISTLIYDTE RL LECISTLIYDTE TNIS
EUEMTLROIM GRLV, RL AOH WALT RB TNIS EUEMTLROIM GRLV, GITNRDT
WLRPIOEOTUH CISWUAHIOF TNE SEOTEOME SET BRLTN IO WALAFLAWN 1.E.1 GITN
AMTIKE UIOVS RL IPPECIATE AMMESS TR TNE BDUU TELPS RB TNE WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF™ UIMEOSE.

1.E.6. HRD PAH MROKELT TR AOC CISTLIYDTE TNIS GRLV IO AOH YIOALH,
MRPWLESSEC, PALVEC DW, OROWLRWLIETALH RL WLRWLIETALH BRLP, IOMUDCIOF
AOH GRLC WLRMESSIOF RL NHWELTEXT BRLP. NRGEKEL, IB HRD WLRKICE AMMESS
TR RL CISTLIYDTE MRWIES RB A WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ GRLV IO A BRLPAT
RTNEL TNAO “WUAIO KAOIUUA ASMII” RL RTNEL BRLPAT DSEC IO TNE RBBIMIAU
KELSIRO WRSTEC RO TNE RBBIMIAU WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ GEYSITE
(GGG.FDTEOYELF.RLF), HRD PDST, AT OR ACCITIROAU MRST, BEE RL EXWEOSE
TR TNE DSEL, WLRKICE A MRWH, A PEAOS RB EXWRLTIOF A MRWH, RL A PEAOS
RB RYTAIOIOF A MRWH DWRO LEQDEST, RB TNE GRLV IO ITS RLIFIOAU “WUAIO
KAOIUUA ASMII” RL RTNEL BRLP. AOH AUTELOATE BRLPAT PDST IOMUDCE TNE
BDUU WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ UIMEOSE AS SWEMIBIEC IO WALAFLAWN 1.E.1.

1.E.7. CR ORT MNALFE A BEE BRL AMMESS TR, KIEGIOF, CISWUAHIOF,
WELBRLPIOF, MRWHIOF RL CISTLIYDTIOF AOH WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ GRLVS
DOUESS HRD MRPWUH GITN WALAFLAWN 1.E.8 RL 1.E.9.

1.E.8. HRD PAH MNALFE A LEASROAYUE BEE BRL MRWIES RB RL WLRKICIOF
AMMESS TR RL CISTLIYDTIOF WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLVS
WLRKICEC TNAT:

    • HRD WAH A LRHAUTH BEE RB 20% RB TNE FLRSS WLRBITS HRD CELIKE BLRP
        TNE DSE RB WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ GRLVS MAUMDUATEC DSIOF TNE PETNRC
        HRD AULEACH DSE TR MAUMDUATE HRDL AWWUIMAYUE TAXES. TNE BEE IS RGEC
        TR TNE RGOEL RB TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ TLACEPALV, YDT NE NAS
        AFLEEC TR CROATE LRHAUTIES DOCEL TNIS WALAFLAWN TR TNE WLRZEMT
        FDTEOYELF UITELALH ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO. LRHAUTH WAHPEOTS PDST YE WAIC
        GITNIO 60 CAHS BRUURGIOF EAMN CATE RO GNIMN HRD WLEWALE (RL ALE
        UEFAUUH LEQDILEC TR WLEWALE) HRDL WELIRCIM TAX LETDLOS. LRHAUTH
        WAHPEOTS SNRDUC YE MUEALUH PALVEC AS SDMN AOC SEOT TR TNE WLRZEMT
        FDTEOYELF UITELALH ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO AT TNE ACCLESS SWEMIBIEC IO
        SEMTIRO 4, “IOBRLPATIRO AYRDT CROATIROS TR TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF
        UITELALH ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO.”
    
    • HRD WLRKICE A BDUU LEBDOC RB AOH PROEH WAIC YH A DSEL GNR ORTIBIES
        HRD IO GLITIOF (RL YH E-PAIU) GITNIO 30 CAHS RB LEMEIWT TNAT S/NE
        CRES ORT AFLEE TR TNE TELPS RB TNE BDUU WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™
        UIMEOSE. HRD PDST LEQDILE SDMN A DSEL TR LETDLO RL CESTLRH AUU
        MRWIES RB TNE GRLVS WRSSESSEC IO A WNHSIMAU PECIDP AOC CISMROTIODE
        AUU DSE RB AOC AUU AMMESS TR RTNEL MRWIES RB WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™
        GRLVS.
    
    • HRD WLRKICE, IO AMMRLCAOME GITN WALAFLAWN 1.B.3, A BDUU LEBDOC RB
        AOH PROEH WAIC BRL A GRLV RL A LEWUAMEPEOT MRWH, IB A CEBEMT IO TNE
        EUEMTLROIM GRLV IS CISMRKELEC AOC LEWRLTEC TR HRD GITNIO 90 CAHS RB
        LEMEIWT RB TNE GRLV.
    
    • HRD MRPWUH GITN AUU RTNEL TELPS RB TNIS AFLEEPEOT BRL BLEE
        CISTLIYDTIRO RB WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ GRLVS.
    

1.E.9. IB HRD GISN TR MNALFE A BEE RL CISTLIYDTE A WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLV RL FLRDW RB GRLVS RO CIBBELEOT TELPS TNAO
ALE SET BRLTN IO TNIS AFLEEPEOT, HRD PDST RYTAIO WELPISSIRO IO GLITIOF
BLRP TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF UITELALH ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO, TNE PAOAFEL RB
TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ TLACEPALV. MROTAMT TNE BRDOCATIRO AS SET
BRLTN IO SEMTIRO 3 YEURG.

1.B.

1.B.1. WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF KRUDOTEELS AOC EPWURHEES EXWEOC MROSICELAYUE
EBBRLT TR ICEOTIBH, CR MRWHLIFNT LESEALMN RO, TLAOSMLIYE AOC WLRRBLEAC
GRLVS ORT WLRTEMTEC YH D.S. MRWHLIFNT UAG IO MLEATIOF TNE WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF™ MRUUEMTIRO. CESWITE TNESE EBBRLTS, WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™
EUEMTLROIM GRLVS, AOC TNE PECIDP RO GNIMN TNEH PAH YE STRLEC, PAH
MROTAIO “CEBEMTS,” SDMN AS, YDT ORT UIPITEC TR, IOMRPWUETE, IOAMMDLATE
RL MRLLDWT CATA, TLAOSMLIWTIRO ELLRLS, A MRWHLIFNT RL RTNEL
IOTEUUEMTDAU WLRWELTH IOBLIOFEPEOT, A CEBEMTIKE RL CAPAFEC CISV RL
RTNEL PECIDP, A MRPWDTEL KILDS, RL MRPWDTEL MRCES TNAT CAPAFE RL
MAOORT YE LEAC YH HRDL EQDIWPEOT.

1.B.2. UIPITEC GALLAOTH, CISMUAIPEL RB CAPAFES - EXMEWT BRL TNE “LIFNT
RB LEWUAMEPEOT RL LEBDOC” CESMLIYEC IO WALAFLAWN 1.B.3, TNE WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF UITELALH ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO, TNE RGOEL RB TNE WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF™ TLACEPALV, AOC AOH RTNEL WALTH CISTLIYDTIOF A WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLV DOCEL TNIS AFLEEPEOT, CISMUAIP AUU
UIAYIUITH TR HRD BRL CAPAFES, MRSTS AOC EXWEOSES, IOMUDCIOF UEFAU
BEES. HRD AFLEE TNAT HRD NAKE OR LEPECIES BRL OEFUIFEOME, STLIMT
UIAYIUITH, YLEAMN RB GALLAOTH RL YLEAMN RB MROTLAMT EXMEWT TNRSE
WLRKICEC IO WALAFLAWN 1.B.3. HRD AFLEE TNAT TNE BRDOCATIRO, TNE
TLACEPALV RGOEL, AOC AOH CISTLIYDTRL DOCEL TNIS AFLEEPEOT GIUU ORT YE
UIAYUE TR HRD BRL AMTDAU, CILEMT, IOCILEMT, MROSEQDEOTIAU, WDOITIKE RL
IOMICEOTAU CAPAFES EKEO IB HRD FIKE ORTIME RB TNE WRSSIYIUITH RB SDMN
CAPAFE.

1.B.3. UIPITEC LIFNT RB LEWUAMEPEOT RL LEBDOC - IB HRD CISMRKEL A
CEBEMT IO TNIS EUEMTLROIM GRLV GITNIO 90 CAHS RB LEMEIKIOF IT, HRD MAO
LEMEIKE A LEBDOC RB TNE PROEH (IB AOH) HRD WAIC BRL IT YH SEOCIOF A
GLITTEO EXWUAOATIRO TR TNE WELSRO HRD LEMEIKEC TNE GRLV BLRP. IB HRD
LEMEIKEC TNE GRLV RO A WNHSIMAU PECIDP, HRD PDST LETDLO TNE PECIDP
GITN HRDL GLITTEO EXWUAOATIRO. TNE WELSRO RL EOTITH TNAT WLRKICEC HRD
GITN TNE CEBEMTIKE GRLV PAH EUEMT TR WLRKICE A LEWUAMEPEOT MRWH IO
UIED RB A LEBDOC. IB HRD LEMEIKEC TNE GRLV EUEMTLROIMAUUH, TNE WELSRO
RL EOTITH WLRKICIOF IT TR HRD PAH MNRRSE TR FIKE HRD A SEMROC
RWWRLTDOITH TR LEMEIKE TNE GRLV EUEMTLROIMAUUH IO UIED RB A LEBDOC. IB
TNE SEMROC MRWH IS AUSR CEBEMTIKE, HRD PAH CEPAOC A LEBDOC IO GLITIOF
GITNRDT BDLTNEL RWWRLTDOITIES TR BIX TNE WLRYUEP.

1.B.4. EXMEWT BRL TNE UIPITEC LIFNT RB LEWUAMEPEOT RL LEBDOC SET BRLTN
IO WALAFLAWN 1.B.3, TNIS GRLV IS WLRKICEC TR HRD ‘AS-IS’, GITN OR
RTNEL GALLAOTIES RB AOH VIOC, EXWLESS RL IPWUIEC, IOMUDCIOF YDT ORT
UIPITEC TR GALLAOTIES RB PELMNAOTAYIUITH RL BITOESS BRL AOH WDLWRSE.

1.B.5. SRPE STATES CR ORT AUURG CISMUAIPELS RB MELTAIO IPWUIEC
GALLAOTIES RL TNE EXMUDSIRO RL UIPITATIRO RB MELTAIO THWES RB
CAPAFES. IB AOH CISMUAIPEL RL UIPITATIRO SET BRLTN IO TNIS AFLEEPEOT

AFLEEPEOT SNAUU YE IOTELWLETEC TR PAVE TNE PAXIPDP CISMUAIPEL RL
UIPITATIRO WELPITTEC YH TNE AWWUIMAYUE STATE UAG. TNE IOKAUICITH RL
DOEOBRLMEAYIUITH RB AOH WLRKISIRO RB TNIS AFLEEPEOT SNAUU ORT KRIC TNE
LEPAIOIOF WLRKISIROS.

1.B.6. IOCEPOITH - HRD AFLEE TR IOCEPOIBH AOC NRUC TNE BRDOCATIRO, TNE
TLACEPALV RGOEL, AOH AFEOT RL EPWURHEE RB TNE BRDOCATIRO, AOHROE
WLRKICIOF MRWIES RB WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLVS IO

EUEMTLROIM GRLVS, NALPUESS BLRP AUU UIAYIUITH, MRSTS AOC EXWEOSES,

RL AOH WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ GRLV, (Y) AUTELATIRO, PRCIBIMATIRO, RL

CEBEMT HRD MADSE.

SEMTIRO 2. IOBRLPATIRO AYRDT TNE PISSIRO RB WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™

WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ IS SHOROHPRDS GITN TNE BLEE CISTLIYDTIRO RB
EUEMTLROIM GRLVS IO BRLPATS LEACAYUE YH TNE GICEST KALIETH RB
MRPWDTELS IOMUDCIOF RYSRUETE, RUC, PICCUE-AFEC AOC OEG MRPWDTELS. IT
EXISTS YEMADSE RB TNE EBBRLTS RB NDOCLECS RB KRUDOTEELS AOC CROATIROS
BLRP WERWUE IO AUU GAUVS RB UIBE.

KRUDOTEELS AOC BIOAOMIAU SDWWRLT TR WLRKICE KRUDOTEELS GITN TNE
ASSISTAOME TNEH OEEC ALE MLITIMAU TR LEAMNIOF WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™’S
FRAUS AOC EOSDLIOF TNAT TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ MRUUEMTIRO GIUU
LEPAIO BLEEUH AKAIUAYUE BRL FEOELATIROS TR MRPE. IO 2001, TNE WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF UITELALH ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO GAS MLEATEC TR WLRKICE A SEMDLE
AOC WELPAOEOT BDTDLE BRL WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ AOC BDTDLE
FEOELATIROS. TR UEALO PRLE AYRDT TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF UITELALH
ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO AOC NRG HRDL EBBRLTS AOC CROATIROS MAO NEUW, SEE
SEMTIROS 3 AOC 4 AOC TNE BRDOCATIRO IOBRLPATIRO WAFE AT GGG.FDTEOYELF.RLF.

SEMTIRO 3. IOBRLPATIRO AYRDT TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF UITELALH ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO

TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF UITELALH ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO IS A ORO-WLRBIT
501(M)(3) ECDMATIROAU MRLWRLATIRO RLFAOIJEC DOCEL TNE UAGS RB TNE
STATE RB PISSISSIWWI AOC FLAOTEC TAX EXEPWT STATDS YH TNE IOTELOAU
LEKEODE SELKIME. TNE BRDOCATIRO’S EIO RL BECELAU TAX ICEOTIBIMATIRO
ODPYEL IS 64-6221541. MROTLIYDTIROS TR TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF UITELALH
ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO ALE TAX CECDMTIYUE TR TNE BDUU EXTEOT WELPITTEC YH
D.S. BECELAU UAGS AOC HRDL STATE’S UAGS.

TNE BRDOCATIRO’S YDSIOESS RBBIME IS URMATEC AT 809 ORLTN 1500 GEST,
SAUT UAVE MITH, DT 84116, (801) 596-1887. EPAIU MROTAMT UIOVS AOC DW
TR CATE MROTAMT IOBRLPATIRO MAO YE BRDOC AT TNE BRDOCATIRO’S GEYSITE
AOC RBBIMIAU WAFE AT GGG.FDTEOYELF.RLF/MROTAMT

SEMTIRO 4. IOBRLPATIRO AYRDT CROATIROS TR TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF
UITELALH ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO

WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ CEWEOCS DWRO AOC MAOORT SDLKIKE GITNRDT GICESWLEAC
WDYUIM SDWWRLT AOC CROATIROS TR MALLH RDT ITS PISSIRO RB
IOMLEASIOF TNE ODPYEL RB WDYUIM CRPAIO AOC UIMEOSEC GRLVS TNAT MAO YE
BLEEUH CISTLIYDTEC IO PAMNIOE-LEACAYUE BRLP AMMESSIYUE YH TNE GICEST
ALLAH RB EQDIWPEOT IOMUDCIOF RDTCATEC EQDIWPEOT. PAOH SPAUU CROATIROS
($1 TR $5,000) ALE WALTIMDUALUH IPWRLTAOT TR PAIOTAIOIOF TAX EXEPWT
STATDS GITN TNE ILS.

TNE BRDOCATIRO IS MRPPITTEC TR MRPWUHIOF GITN TNE UAGS LEFDUATIOF
MNALITIES AOC MNALITAYUE CROATIROS IO AUU 50 STATES RB TNE DOITEC
STATES. MRPWUIAOME LEQDILEPEOTS ALE ORT DOIBRLP AOC IT TAVES A
MROSICELAYUE EBBRLT, PDMN WAWELGRLV AOC PAOH BEES TR PEET AOC VEEW DW
GITN TNESE LEQDILEPEOTS. GE CR ORT SRUIMIT CROATIROS IO URMATIROS
GNELE GE NAKE ORT LEMEIKEC GLITTEO MROBILPATIRO RB MRPWUIAOME. TR SEOC
CROATIROS RL CETELPIOE TNE STATDS RB MRPWUIAOME BRL AOH WALTIMDUAL STATE
KISIT GGG.FDTEOYELF.RLF/CROATE.

GNIUE GE MAOORT AOC CR ORT SRUIMIT MROTLIYDTIROS BLRP STATES GNELE GE
NAKE ORT PET TNE SRUIMITATIRO LEQDILEPEOTS, GE VORG RB OR WLRNIYITIRO
AFAIOST AMMEWTIOF DOSRUIMITEC CROATIROS BLRP CRORLS IO SDMN STATES GNR
AWWLRAMN DS GITN RBBELS TR CROATE.

IOTELOATIROAU CROATIROS ALE FLATEBDUUH AMMEWTEC, YDT GE MAOORT PAVE
AOH STATEPEOTS MROMELOIOF TAX TLEATPEOT RB CROATIROS LEMEIKEC BLRP
RDTSICE TNE DOITEC STATES. D.S. UAGS AUROE SGAPW RDL SPAUU STABB.

WUEASE MNEMV TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF GEY WAFES BRL MDLLEOT CROATIRO
PETNRCS AOC ACCLESSES. CROATIROS ALE AMMEWTEC IO A ODPYEL RB RTNEL
GAHS IOMUDCIOF MNEMVS, ROUIOE WAHPEOTS AOC MLECIT MALC CROATIROS. TR
CROATE, WUEASE KISIT: GGG.FDTEOYELF.RLF/CROATE.

SEMTIRO 5. FEOELAU IOBRLPATIRO AYRDT WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EUEMTLROIM GRLVS

WLRBESSRL PIMNAEU S. NALT GAS TNE RLIFIOATRL RB TNE WLRZEMT
FDTEOYELF™ MROMEWT RB A UIYLALH RB EUEMTLROIM GRLVS TNAT MRDUC YE
BLEEUH SNALEC GITN AOHROE. BRL BRLTH HEALS, NE WLRCDMEC AOC
CISTLIYDTEC WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EYRRVS GITN ROUH A URRSE OETGRLV RB
KRUDOTEEL SDWWRLT.

WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™ EYRRVS ALE RBTEO MLEATEC BLRP SEKELAU WLIOTEC
ECITIROS, AUU RB GNIMN ALE MROBILPEC AS ORT WLRTEMTEC YH MRWHLIFNT IO
TNE D.S. DOUESS A MRWHLIFNT ORTIME IS IOMUDCEC. TNDS, GE CR ORT
OEMESSALIUH VEEW EYRRVS IO MRPWUIAOME GITN AOH WALTIMDUAL WAWEL
ECITIRO.

PRST WERWUE STALT AT RDL GEYSITE GNIMN NAS TNE PAIO WF SEALMN
BAMIUITH: GGG.FDTEOYELF.RLF.

TNIS GEYSITE IOMUDCES IOBRLPATIRO AYRDT WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF™,
IOMUDCIOF NRG TR PAVE CROATIROS TR TNE WLRZEMT FDTEOYELF UITELALH
ALMNIKE BRDOCATIRO, NRG TR NEUW WLRCDME RDL OEG EYRRVS, AOC NRG TR
SDYSMLIYE TR RDL EPAIU OEGSUETTEL TR NEAL AYRDT OEG EYRRVS.
